%%%% TITLE

\title[Bicombing MCG and Teich via stable cubical intervals]{Bicombing the mapping class group and Teichm\"uller space via stable cubical intervals}



 
 
 \author{Matthew Gentry Durham}
 \address{Department of Mathematics and Statistics, CUNY Hunter College, New York, NY }
 \email{matthew.durham@hunter.edu}
 

\newwrite\markfile
\immediate\openout\markfile=boxpositions_teichmuller.txt

\newcommand{\markbox}[2]{%
  \setbox0=\hbox{#2}%
  \immediate\write\markfile{#1:pwhd:\the\value{page}:\the\wd0:\the\ht0:\the\dp0}%
  \pdfsavepos
  \write\markfile{#1:spxy:\the\value{page}:\the\pdflastxpos:\the\pdflastypos:}%
  #2% 
  \pdfsavepos
  \write\markfile{#1:epxy:\the\value{page}:\the\pdflastxpos:\the\pdflastypos:}%
}

\begin{document}
\begin{abstract}
  In this mostly expository article, we provide a new account of our proof with Minsky and Sisto that mapping class groups and Teichm\"uller spaces admit bicombings.  More generally, we explain how the hierarchical hull of a pair of points in any colorable hierarchically hyperbolic space is quasi-isometric to a finite CAT(0) cube complex of bounded dimension, with the added property that perturbing the pair of points results in a uniformly bounded change to the cubical structure.  Our approach is simplified and new in many aspects.
  
\end{abstract}


\maketitle


\section{Introduction} \label{sec:intro}

The \markbox{0}{recent} \markbox{1}{infusion} \markbox{2}{of} \markbox{3}{techniques} \markbox{4}{from} \markbox{5}{cube} \markbox{6}{complexes} \markbox{7}{into} \markbox{8}{the} \markbox{9}{study} \markbox{10}{of} \markbox{11}{mapping} \markbox{12}{class} \markbox{13}{groups} \markbox{14}{of} \markbox{15}{finite-type} \markbox{16}{surfaces} \markbox{17}{has} \markbox{18}{had} \markbox{19}{dramatic} \markbox{20}{consequences,} \markbox{21}{including} \markbox{22}{toward} \markbox{23}{our} \markbox{24}{ability} \markbox{25}{to} \markbox{26}{control} \markbox{27}{top-dimensional} \markbox{28}{quasi-isometrically} \markbox{29}{embedded} \markbox{30}{flats} \cite{HHS_quasi}, \markbox{31}{build} \markbox{32}{bicombings} \cite{DMS_bary, HHP}, \markbox{33}{and} \markbox{34}{understand} \markbox{35}{their} \markbox{36}{geometry} \markbox{37}{at} \markbox{38}{infinity} \cite{DZ22, Ham_boundary, Dur_infcube}, \markbox{39}{among} \markbox{40}{others} \cite{ABD, Petyt_quasicube, DZ22, zalloum2025effective}.

The \markbox{41}{central} \markbox{42}{result} \markbox{43}{facilitating} \markbox{44}{most} \markbox{45}{of} \markbox{46}{the} \markbox{47}{above} \markbox{48}{work} \markbox{49}{was} \markbox{50}{the} \markbox{51}{\emph{cubical model theorem}} \markbox{52}{of} \markbox{53}{Behrstock--Hagen--Sisto} \cite{HHS_quasi}.  \markbox{54}{It} \markbox{55}{says,} \markbox{56}{roughly,} \markbox{57}{that} \markbox{58}{the} \markbox{59}{coarse} \markbox{60}{convex} \markbox{61}{hull} \markbox{62}{of} \markbox{63}{a} \markbox{64}{finite} \markbox{65}{set} \markbox{66}{of} \markbox{67}{points} \markbox{68}{in} \markbox{69}{the} \markbox{70}{mapping} \markbox{71}{class} \markbox{72}{group} \markbox{73}{is} \markbox{74}{quasi-isometrically} \markbox{75}{approximated} \markbox{76}{by} \markbox{77}{a} \markbox{78}{CAT(0)} \markbox{79}{cube} \markbox{80}{complex,} \markbox{81}{which} \markbox{82}{is} \markbox{83}{a} \markbox{84}{higher} \markbox{85}{dimensional} \markbox{86}{analogue} \markbox{87}{of} \markbox{88}{Gromov's} \markbox{89}{tree} \markbox{90}{approximation} \markbox{91}{theorem} \markbox{92}{for} \markbox{93}{hyperbolic} \markbox{94}{spaces.}  \markbox{95}{The} \markbox{96}{cubical} \markbox{97}{model} \markbox{98}{theorem} \markbox{99}{was} \markbox{100}{later} \markbox{101}{generalized} \markbox{102}{by} \markbox{103}{Bowditch} \cite{Bowditch_hulls} \markbox{104}{(to} \markbox{105}{certain} \markbox{106}{coarse} \markbox{107}{median} \markbox{108}{spaces)} \markbox{109}{and} \markbox{110}{the} \markbox{111}{author} \cite{Dur_infcube} \markbox{112}{(to} \markbox{113}{allow} \markbox{114}{for} \markbox{115}{points} \markbox{116}{at} \markbox{117}{infinity).}  \markbox{118}{All} \markbox{119}{versions} \markbox{120}{hold} \markbox{121}{in} \markbox{122}{the} \markbox{123}{broader} \markbox{124}{context} \markbox{125}{of} \markbox{126}{hierarchically} \markbox{127}{hyperbolic} \markbox{128}{spaces} \cite{HHS_I}, \markbox{129}{a} \markbox{130}{framework} \markbox{131}{for} \markbox{132}{studying} \markbox{133}{a} \markbox{134}{wide} \markbox{135}{variety} \markbox{136}{of} \markbox{137}{spaces} \markbox{138}{with} \markbox{139}{blended} \markbox{140}{negative} \markbox{141}{and} \markbox{142}{positive} \markbox{143}{curvature,} \markbox{144}{e.g.} Teichm\"uller \markbox{145}{spaces} \cite{Brock, Rafi:hypteich, Dur:augmented}, \markbox{146}{that} \markbox{147}{built} \markbox{148}{off} \markbox{149}{the} \markbox{150}{seminal} \markbox{151}{work} \markbox{152}{of} \markbox{153}{Masur--Minsky} \cite{MM99,MM00} \markbox{154}{on} \markbox{155}{the} \markbox{156}{mapping} \markbox{157}{class} \markbox{158}{group;} \markbox{159}{see} \markbox{160}{Section} \ref{sec:HHS}. 

The \markbox{161}{cubical} \markbox{162}{approximation} \markbox{163}{theorem} \markbox{164}{allows} \markbox{165}{one} \markbox{166}{to} \markbox{167}{build} \markbox{168}{any} \markbox{169}{number} \markbox{170}{of} \markbox{171}{cubically-defined} \markbox{172}{(and} \markbox{173}{hierarchically} \markbox{174}{well-behaved)} \markbox{175}{paths} \markbox{176}{between} \markbox{177}{a} \markbox{178}{pair} \markbox{179}{of} \markbox{180}{points} \markbox{181}{by} \markbox{182}{importing} \markbox{183}{them} \markbox{184}{from} \markbox{185}{the} \markbox{186}{cubical} \markbox{187}{model} \markbox{188}{of} \markbox{189}{their} \markbox{190}{hull.}  \markbox{191}{This} \markbox{192}{observation} \markbox{193}{was} \markbox{194}{at} \markbox{195}{the} \markbox{196}{core} \markbox{197}{of} \markbox{198}{two} \markbox{199}{recent} \markbox{200}{proofs} \markbox{201}{that} \markbox{202}{the} \markbox{203}{mapping} \markbox{204}{class} \markbox{205}{group} \markbox{206}{is} \markbox{207}{\emph{bicombable}}\footnote{Roughly, \markbox{208}{a} \markbox{209}{bicombing} \markbox{210}{on} \markbox{211}{a} \markbox{212}{metric} \markbox{213}{space} \markbox{214}{is} \markbox{215}{a} \markbox{216}{transitive} \markbox{217}{family} \markbox{218}{of} \markbox{219}{quasi-geodesic} \markbox{220}{paths} \markbox{221}{that} \markbox{222}{are} \markbox{223}{stable} \markbox{224}{under} \markbox{225}{small} \markbox{226}{perturbations} \markbox{227}{of} \markbox{228}{the} \markbox{229}{endpoints;} \markbox{230}{see} \markbox{231}{Definition} \ref{defn:bicombing}.}.  \markbox{232}{The} \markbox{233}{two} \markbox{234}{proofs,} \markbox{235}{due} \markbox{236}{to} \markbox{237}{Haettel--Hoda--Petyt} \cite{HHP} \markbox{238}{and} \markbox{239}{Minsky,} \markbox{240}{Sisto,} \markbox{241}{and} \markbox{242}{the} \markbox{243}{author} \cite{DMS_bary}, \markbox{244}{are} \markbox{245}{very} \markbox{246}{different} \markbox{247}{but} \markbox{248}{both} \markbox{249}{depend} \markbox{250}{crucially} \markbox{251}{on} \markbox{252}{this} \markbox{253}{cubical} \markbox{254}{model} \markbox{255}{machinery.}  \markbox{256}{See} \markbox{257}{also} \markbox{258}{a} \markbox{259}{recent} \markbox{260}{elegant} \markbox{261}{proof} \markbox{262}{of} \markbox{263}{bicombability} \markbox{264}{using} \markbox{265}{wallspace} \markbox{266}{techniques} \markbox{267}{due} \markbox{268}{to} \markbox{269}{Petyt--Zalloum} \cite{PZ_walls}.

The \markbox{270}{purpose} \markbox{271}{of} \markbox{272}{this} \markbox{273}{paper} \markbox{274}{is} \markbox{275}{to} \markbox{276}{explain} \markbox{277}{a} \markbox{278}{new} \markbox{279}{proof} \markbox{280}{of} \markbox{281}{the} \markbox{282}{two-point} \markbox{283}{version} \markbox{284}{of} \markbox{285}{the} \markbox{286}{main} \markbox{287}{technical} \markbox{288}{result} \markbox{289}{of} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{290}{via} \markbox{291}{the} \markbox{292}{machinery} \markbox{293}{in} \cite{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{294}{which} \markbox{295}{we} \markbox{296}{state} \markbox{297}{here} \markbox{298}{informally} \markbox{299}{(see} \markbox{300}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}):

\begin{thmi}\label{thmi:main}
The \markbox{301}{hierarchical} \markbox{302}{hull} \markbox{303}{of} \markbox{304}{a} \markbox{305}{pair} \markbox{306}{of} \markbox{307}{points} \markbox{308}{in} \markbox{309}{a} \markbox{310}{colorable} \markbox{311}{HHS} \markbox{312}{can} \markbox{313}{be} \markbox{314}{stably} \markbox{315}{approximated} \markbox{316}{by} \markbox{317}{a} \markbox{318}{CAT(0)} \markbox{319}{cube} complex.
\end{thmi}

With \markbox{320}{this} \markbox{321}{tool} \markbox{322}{in} \markbox{323}{hand,} \markbox{324}{bicombability} \markbox{325}{is} \markbox{326}{a} \markbox{327}{straight-forward} \markbox{328}{application} \markbox{329}{of} \markbox{330}{cubical} \markbox{331}{techniques} \markbox{332}{essentially} \markbox{333}{via} \markbox{334}{the} \markbox{335}{arguments} \markbox{336}{in}  \cite[Sections \markbox{337}{5} \markbox{338}{and} 6]{DMS_bary}:

\begin{cori}\label{cori:semihyp}
Let \markbox{m339}{$S$} \markbox{340}{be} \markbox{341}{a} \markbox{342}{finite} \markbox{343}{type} \markbox{344}{surface.}  \markbox{345}{Then} \markbox{346}{its} \markbox{347}{mapping} \markbox{348}{class} \markbox{349}{group} \markbox{350}{and} Teichm\"uller \markbox{351}{space} \markbox{352}{with} \markbox{353}{the} Teichm\"uller \markbox{354}{metric} \markbox{355}{admit} \markbox{356}{bicombings} \markbox{357}{by} \markbox{358}{hierarchy} paths.
\end{cori}


\begin{remark}
One \markbox{359}{can} \markbox{360}{upgrade} \markbox{361}{both} \markbox{362}{of} \markbox{363}{these} \markbox{364}{statements} \markbox{365}{to} \markbox{366}{ensure} \markbox{367}{coarse} \markbox{368}{equivariance} \markbox{369}{in} \markbox{370}{the} \markbox{371}{presence} \markbox{372}{of} \markbox{373}{an} \markbox{374}{appropriate} \markbox{375}{group} \markbox{376}{action.}  \markbox{377}{In} \markbox{378}{particular,} \markbox{379}{in} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{380}{we} \markbox{381}{showed} \markbox{382}{that} \markbox{383}{the} \markbox{384}{bicombings} \markbox{385}{in} \markbox{386}{Corollary} \ref{cori:semihyp} \markbox{387}{are} \markbox{388}{coarsely} \markbox{389}{equivariant} \markbox{390}{with} \markbox{391}{respect} \markbox{392}{to} \markbox{393}{the} \markbox{394}{mapping} \markbox{395}{class} \markbox{396}{group} \markbox{397}{action,} \markbox{398}{and} \markbox{399}{that} \markbox{400}{the} \markbox{401}{mapping} \markbox{402}{class} \markbox{403}{group} \markbox{404}{is} \markbox{405}{\emph{semi-hyperbolic}} \markbox{406}{in} \markbox{407}{the} \markbox{408}{sense} \markbox{409}{of} \cite{AB95}.  \markbox{410}{This} \markbox{411}{equivariance} \markbox{412}{upgrade} \markbox{413}{is} \markbox{414}{relatively} \markbox{415}{straight-forward} \markbox{416}{once} \markbox{417}{one} \markbox{418}{has} \markbox{419}{the} \markbox{420}{bicombing,} \markbox{421}{but} \markbox{422}{we} \markbox{423}{have} \markbox{424}{omitted} \markbox{425}{it} \markbox{426}{since} \markbox{427}{it} \markbox{428}{adds} \markbox{429}{yet} \markbox{430}{another} \markbox{431}{layer} \markbox{432}{complexity} \markbox{433}{to} \markbox{434}{the} \markbox{435}{statements} \markbox{436}{and} \markbox{437}{proofs} \markbox{438}{in} \markbox{439}{an} \markbox{440}{already} \markbox{441}{technical} \markbox{442}{construction.}  \markbox{443}{We} \markbox{444}{point} \markbox{445}{the} \markbox{446}{reader} \markbox{447}{to} \cite[Remark 2]{DMS_bary} \markbox{448}{for} \markbox{449}{a} \markbox{450}{discussion} \markbox{451}{of} \markbox{452}{how} \markbox{453}{equivariance} \markbox{454}{works} \markbox{455}{for} \markbox{456}{this} \markbox{457}{construction.} 
\end{remark}

% More generally, these results hold in the context of \emph{hierarchically hyperbolic spaces} (HHSes), a framework for studying a wide variety of spaces with blended negative and positive curvature that built off the seminal work of Masur--Minsky \cite{MM99,MM00} on the mapping class group; see Section \ref{sec:HHS}.  In the HHS setting, the guiding philosophy is to study objects by projecting to a family of hyperbolic spaces and then use techniques from hyperbolic geometry.  The cubical model theorem is utilized similarly---one exports problems from the mapping class group to a family cube complexes and employs cubical techniques.


We \markbox{458}{have} \markbox{459}{several} \markbox{460}{motivations} \markbox{461}{for} \markbox{462}{writing} \markbox{463}{this} \markbox{464}{paper.}  \markbox{465}{First,} \markbox{466}{we} \markbox{467}{wanted} \markbox{468}{to} \markbox{469}{give} \markbox{470}{a} \markbox{471}{simplified} \markbox{472}{account} \markbox{473}{of} \markbox{474}{the} \markbox{475}{cubical} \markbox{476}{model} \markbox{477}{results} \markbox{478}{in} \cite{DMS_bary, DMS_FJ} \markbox{479}{in} \markbox{480}{less} \markbox{481}{generality.}  \markbox{482}{Roughly} \markbox{483}{speaking,} \markbox{484}{the} \markbox{485}{cubical} \markbox{486}{model} \markbox{487}{for} \markbox{488}{a} \markbox{489}{finite} \markbox{490}{subset} \markbox{m491}{$F$} \markbox{492}{of} \markbox{493}{an} \markbox{494}{HHS} \markbox{495}{from} \cite{HHS_quasi} \markbox{496}{is} \markbox{497}{produced} \markbox{498}{from} \markbox{499}{a} \markbox{500}{wallspace} \markbox{501}{on} \markbox{502}{a} \markbox{503}{family} \markbox{504}{of} \markbox{505}{trees} \markbox{506}{obtained} \markbox{507}{by} \markbox{508}{projecting} \markbox{m509}{$F$} \markbox{510}{to} \markbox{511}{each} \markbox{512}{of} \markbox{513}{the} \markbox{514}{hyperbolic} \markbox{515}{spaces} \markbox{516}{in} \markbox{517}{the} \markbox{518}{hierarchy.}  \markbox{519}{The} \markbox{520}{proof} \markbox{521}{of} \markbox{522}{bicombability} \markbox{523}{in} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{524}{proceeds} \markbox{525}{by} \markbox{526}{using} \markbox{527}{hyperbolic} \markbox{528}{geometry} \markbox{529}{techniques---culminating} \markbox{530}{in} \markbox{531}{the} \markbox{532}{Stable} \markbox{533}{Tree} \markbox{534}{Theorem} \cite[Theorem 3.2]{DMS_bary}---to \markbox{535}{produce} \markbox{536}{a} \markbox{537}{family} \markbox{538}{of} \markbox{539}{trees} \markbox{540}{which} \markbox{541}{is} \markbox{542}{coarsely} \markbox{543}{stable} \markbox{544}{under} \markbox{545}{bounded} \markbox{546}{perturbations} \markbox{547}{of} \markbox{m548}{$F$}.  \markbox{549}{In} \markbox{550}{this} \markbox{551}{paper,} \markbox{552}{we} \markbox{553}{simplify} \markbox{554}{a} \markbox{555}{number} \markbox{556}{of} \markbox{557}{aspects} \markbox{558}{of} \markbox{559}{this} \markbox{560}{initial} \markbox{561}{portion} \markbox{562}{of} \markbox{563}{the} \markbox{564}{argument} \markbox{565}{by} \markbox{566}{limiting} \markbox{567}{ourselves} \markbox{568}{to} \markbox{569}{modeling} \markbox{570}{only} \markbox{571}{a} \markbox{572}{pair} \markbox{573}{of} \markbox{574}{points} \markbox{575}{instead} \markbox{576}{of} \markbox{577}{arbitrary} \markbox{578}{collections} \markbox{579}{of} \markbox{580}{points} \markbox{581}{and} rays.

The \markbox{582}{second} \markbox{583}{motivation} \markbox{584}{is} \markbox{585}{to} \markbox{586}{explain} \markbox{587}{how} \markbox{588}{to} \markbox{589}{combine} \markbox{590}{the} \markbox{591}{stability} \markbox{592}{techniques} \markbox{593}{from} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{594}{with} \markbox{595}{the} \markbox{596}{new} \markbox{597}{cubical} \markbox{598}{model} \markbox{599}{construction} \markbox{600}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}\footnote{This \markbox{601}{construction} \markbox{602}{has} \markbox{603}{many} \markbox{604}{extra} \markbox{605}{benefits} \markbox{606}{as} \markbox{607}{compared} \markbox{608}{to} \markbox{609}{the} \markbox{610}{construction} \markbox{611}{from} \cite{HHS_quasi}.  \markbox{612}{We} \markbox{613}{point} \markbox{614}{interested} \markbox{615}{readers} \markbox{616}{to} \markbox{617}{the} \markbox{618}{in-depth} \markbox{619}{discussion} \markbox{620}{in} \markbox{621}{the} \markbox{622}{introduction} \markbox{623}{of} \cite{Dur_infcube}.}.  \markbox{624}{This} \markbox{625}{involves} \markbox{626}{a} \markbox{627}{new,} \markbox{628}{more} \markbox{629}{elementary} \markbox{630}{proof} \markbox{631}{of} \markbox{632}{the} \markbox{633}{key} \markbox{634}{Stable} \markbox{635}{Trees} \markbox{636}{Theorem} \markbox{637}{for} \markbox{638}{intervals;} \markbox{639}{see} \markbox{640}{Section} \ref{sec:stable intervals} \markbox{641}{below.}  \markbox{642}{Notably,} \markbox{643}{with} \markbox{644}{Minsky} \markbox{645}{and} \markbox{646}{Sisto,} \markbox{647}{we} \markbox{648}{recently} \cite{DMS_FJ} \markbox{649}{implemented} \markbox{650}{a} \markbox{651}{significant} \markbox{652}{expansion} \markbox{653}{of} \markbox{654}{the} \markbox{655}{techniques} \markbox{656}{from} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{657}{utilizing} \markbox{658}{the} \markbox{659}{framework} \markbox{660}{of} \cite{Dur_infcube}\footnote{The \markbox{661}{first} \markbox{662}{version} \markbox{663}{of} \markbox{664}{this} \markbox{665}{expository} \markbox{666}{article} \markbox{667}{appeared} \markbox{668}{before} \cite{DMS_FJ}, \markbox{669}{but} \markbox{670}{we} \markbox{671}{have} \markbox{672}{subsequently} \markbox{673}{adapted} \markbox{674}{it} \markbox{675}{to} \markbox{676}{account} \markbox{677}{for} \markbox{678}{that} paper.}.  \markbox{679}{This} \markbox{680}{allowed} \markbox{681}{us} \markbox{682}{to} \markbox{683}{build} \markbox{684}{an} \markbox{685}{asymptotically} \markbox{686}{CAT(0)} \markbox{687}{metric} \cite{Kar_asymp} \markbox{688}{on} \markbox{689}{any} \markbox{690}{colorable} \markbox{691}{HHS,} \markbox{692}{construct} \markbox{693}{a} \markbox{m694}{$\calZ$}-boundary \markbox{695}{(in} \markbox{696}{the} \markbox{697}{sense} \markbox{698}{of} \cite{bestvina1996local, Dra:BM_formula}) \markbox{699}{for} \markbox{700}{any} \markbox{701}{colorable} \markbox{702}{HHG} \markbox{703}{(see} \markbox{704}{also} \cite{hamenstadt2025z} \markbox{705}{for} \markbox{706}{mapping} \markbox{707}{class} \markbox{708}{groups),} \markbox{709}{and} \markbox{710}{establish} \markbox{711}{the} \markbox{712}{Farrell--Jones} \markbox{713}{Conjecture} \cite{farrell1993isomorphism} \markbox{714}{for} \markbox{715}{many} \markbox{716}{HHGs,} \markbox{717}{including} \markbox{718}{extra-large} \markbox{719}{type} \markbox{720}{Artin} \markbox{721}{groups.}  \markbox{722}{This} \markbox{723}{paper} \markbox{724}{can} \markbox{725}{be} \markbox{726}{seen} \markbox{727}{as} \markbox{728}{explaining} \markbox{729}{the} \markbox{730}{simplest} \markbox{731}{possible} \markbox{732}{case} \markbox{733}{of} \markbox{734}{the} \markbox{735}{main} \markbox{736}{technical} \markbox{737}{construction} \markbox{738}{in} \cite{DMS_FJ}.

Unsurprisingly, \markbox{739}{combining} \markbox{740}{the} \markbox{741}{work} \markbox{742}{in} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{743}{and} \cite{Dur_infcube} \markbox{744}{involves} \markbox{745}{an} \markbox{746}{exposition} \markbox{747}{of} \markbox{748}{both,} \markbox{749}{though} \markbox{750}{we} \markbox{751}{have} \markbox{752}{mostly} \markbox{753}{focused} \markbox{754}{on} \markbox{755}{where} \markbox{756}{they} \markbox{757}{meet.}  \markbox{758}{We} \markbox{759}{summarize} \markbox{760}{the} \markbox{761}{main} \markbox{762}{features} \markbox{763}{of} \markbox{764}{this} \markbox{765}{(mostly)} \markbox{766}{expository} \markbox{767}{paper} \markbox{768}{as} follows:

\begin{itemize}
\item {} We \markbox{769}{give} \markbox{770}{an} \markbox{771}{exposition} \markbox{772}{of} \markbox{773}{the} \markbox{774}{basic} \markbox{775}{cubical} \markbox{776}{model} \markbox{777}{construction} \markbox{778}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{779}{which} \markbox{780}{is} \markbox{781}{significantly} \markbox{782}{simplified} \markbox{783}{from} \markbox{784}{the} \markbox{785}{much} \markbox{786}{more} \markbox{787}{general} \markbox{788}{setting} \markbox{789}{considered} \markbox{790}{therein,} \markbox{791}{(i.e.,} \markbox{792}{which} \markbox{793}{allows} \markbox{794}{for} \markbox{795}{modeling} \markbox{796}{points} \markbox{797}{at} infinity).

\item {} We \markbox{798}{explain} \markbox{799}{how} \markbox{800}{to} \markbox{801}{combine} \markbox{802}{the} \markbox{803}{stability} \markbox{804}{techniques} \markbox{805}{from} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{806}{with} \markbox{807}{the} \markbox{808}{cubical} \markbox{809}{model} \markbox{810}{construction} \markbox{811}{of} \cite{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{812}{In} \markbox{813}{particular,} \markbox{814}{this} \markbox{815}{involves} \markbox{816}{defining} \markbox{817}{a} \markbox{818}{refined} \markbox{819}{notion} \markbox{820}{of} \markbox{821}{a} \markbox{822}{\emph{stable decomposition}} \markbox{823}{(Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}), \markbox{824}{and} \markbox{825}{giving} \markbox{826}{a} \markbox{827}{new} \markbox{828}{proof} \markbox{829}{of} \markbox{830}{the} \markbox{831}{Stable} \markbox{832}{Trees} \markbox{833}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{834}{for} \markbox{835}{intervals.}  \markbox{836}{We} \markbox{837}{note} \markbox{838}{that} \markbox{839}{these} \markbox{840}{stable} \markbox{841}{decompositions} \markbox{842}{also} \markbox{843}{appear} \markbox{844}{in} \cite{DMS_FJ}.

\item {} Using \markbox{845}{the} \markbox{846}{above,} \markbox{847}{we} \markbox{848}{prove} \markbox{849}{bicombability} \markbox{850}{of} \markbox{851}{mapping} \markbox{852}{class} \markbox{853}{groups} \markbox{854}{(and} \markbox{855}{HHSes)} \markbox{856}{via} \markbox{857}{the} \markbox{858}{stable} \markbox{859}{cubulation} \markbox{860}{techniques} \markbox{861}{from} \cite{DMS_bary}, \markbox{862}{while} \markbox{863}{restricting} \markbox{864}{ourselves} \markbox{865}{to} \markbox{866}{the} \markbox{867}{simplified} \markbox{868}{setting} \markbox{869}{of} \markbox{870}{cubical} \markbox{871}{models} \markbox{872}{for} \markbox{873}{pairs} \markbox{874}{of} \markbox{875}{points.}  \markbox{876}{Notably,} \markbox{877}{the} \markbox{878}{bicombing} \markbox{879}{construction} \markbox{880}{from} \cite{HHP} \markbox{881}{also} \markbox{882}{depends} \markbox{883}{on} \markbox{884}{the} \markbox{885}{cubical} \markbox{886}{models} \markbox{887}{(from} \cite{HHS_quasi}), \markbox{888}{so} \markbox{889}{one} \markbox{890}{can} \markbox{891}{also} \markbox{892}{see} \markbox{893}{this} \markbox{894}{paper} \markbox{895}{as} \markbox{896}{supplying} \markbox{897}{an} \markbox{898}{exposition} \markbox{899}{for} \markbox{900}{some} \markbox{901}{of} \markbox{902}{the} \markbox{903}{underlying} \markbox{904}{technology} \markbox{905}{of} \markbox{906}{their} construction.

\item {} By \markbox{907}{focusing} \markbox{908}{on} \markbox{909}{the} \markbox{910}{bicombing} \markbox{911}{result} \markbox{912}{(Corollary} \ref{cori:semihyp}), \markbox{913}{we} \markbox{914}{are} \markbox{915}{able} \markbox{916}{significantly} \markbox{917}{simplifly} \markbox{918}{the} \markbox{919}{endgame} \markbox{920}{of} \markbox{921}{the} \markbox{922}{path} \markbox{923}{construction.}  \markbox{924}{In} \markbox{925}{particular,} \markbox{926}{we} \markbox{927}{utilize} \markbox{928}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{929}{paths} \cite{NibloReeves} \markbox{930}{in} \markbox{931}{the} \markbox{932}{cubical} \markbox{933}{model} \markbox{934}{instead} \markbox{935}{of} \markbox{936}{the} \markbox{937}{more} \markbox{938}{elaborate} \markbox{939}{version} \markbox{940}{of} \markbox{941}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{942}{contractions} \markbox{943}{from} \markbox{944}{our} \markbox{945}{work} \markbox{946}{with} \markbox{947}{Minsky} \markbox{948}{and} \markbox{949}{Sisto} \cite[Section 5]{DMS_bary}.
\end{itemize}

\subsection{Background reading}

Our \markbox{950}{main} \markbox{951}{focus} \markbox{952}{in} \markbox{953}{this} \markbox{954}{article} \markbox{955}{is} \markbox{956}{explaining} \markbox{957}{how} \markbox{958}{to} \markbox{959}{adapt} \markbox{960}{the} \markbox{961}{stable} \markbox{962}{cubulation} \markbox{963}{techniques} \markbox{964}{from} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{965}{to} \markbox{966}{the}  \markbox{967}{cubical} \markbox{968}{model} \markbox{969}{setup} \markbox{970}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{971}{which} \markbox{972}{we} \markbox{973}{note} \markbox{974}{is} \markbox{975}{done} \markbox{976}{in} \markbox{977}{much} \markbox{978}{more} \markbox{979}{general} \markbox{980}{setting} \markbox{981}{in} \cite{DMS_FJ}.  \markbox{982}{As} \markbox{983}{such,} \markbox{984}{the} \markbox{985}{reader} \markbox{986}{will} \markbox{987}{benefit} \markbox{988}{from} \markbox{989}{a} \markbox{990}{variety} \markbox{991}{of} \markbox{992}{contextual} \markbox{993}{information} \markbox{994}{and} \markbox{995}{motivation} \markbox{996}{in} \markbox{997}{and} \markbox{998}{around} \markbox{999}{cube} \markbox{1000}{complexes} \markbox{1001}{and} \markbox{1002}{HHSes.}  \markbox{1003}{We} \markbox{1004}{provide} \markbox{1005}{some} \markbox{1006}{suggested} \markbox{1007}{reading} \markbox{1008}{in} \markbox{1009}{the} \markbox{1010}{list} below:
\begin{itemize}
	\item  {} See \markbox{1011}{Sisto's} \markbox{1012}{notes} \cite{Sisto_HHS} \markbox{1013}{and} \markbox{1014}{the} \markbox{1015}{background} \markbox{1016}{in} \markbox{1017}{Casals-Ruiz--Hagen--Kazachkov} \cite{CRHK} \markbox{1018}{for} \markbox{1019}{an} \markbox{1020}{introduction} \markbox{1021}{to} \markbox{1022}{HHSes.}  \markbox{1023}{While} \markbox{1024}{we} \markbox{1025}{do} \markbox{1026}{give} \markbox{1027}{a} \markbox{1028}{proof} \markbox{1029}{of} \markbox{1030}{the} \markbox{1031}{harder} \markbox{1032}{bound} \markbox{1033}{of} \markbox{1034}{the} \markbox{1035}{Distance} \markbox{1036}{Formula} \markbox{1037}{in} \markbox{1038}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF lower bound}, \markbox{1039}{we} \markbox{1040}{expect} \markbox{1041}{the} \markbox{1042}{reader} \markbox{1043}{to} \markbox{1044}{be} \markbox{1045}{familiar} \markbox{1046}{with} \markbox{1047}{the} \markbox{1048}{general} framework.
	\item  {} See \markbox{1049}{Farb--Margalit} \cite{FM_primer} \markbox{1050}{for} \markbox{1051}{an} \markbox{1052}{introduction} \markbox{1053}{to} \markbox{1054}{mapping} \markbox{1055}{class} \markbox{1056}{groups,} \markbox{1057}{and} \cite[Section 11]{HHS_II} \markbox{1058}{and} \markbox{1059}{there} \markbox{1060}{references} \markbox{1061}{therein} \markbox{1062}{(particular,} \markbox{1063}{Masur--Minsky's} \markbox{1064}{work} \cite{MM99, MM00}) \markbox{1065}{for} \markbox{1066}{its} \markbox{1067}{hierarchically} \markbox{1068}{hyperbolic} \markbox{1069}{structure.}  \markbox{1070}{Similarly,} \markbox{1071}{see} \markbox{1072}{Rafi} \cite{Rafi:combo, Rafi:hypteich} \markbox{1073}{and} \markbox{1074}{the} \markbox{1075}{author} \cite{Dur:augmented} \markbox{1076}{for} \markbox{1077}{the} \markbox{1078}{hierarchical} \markbox{1079}{structure} \markbox{1080}{on} Teichm\"uller \markbox{1081}{space} \markbox{1082}{with} \markbox{1083}{the} Teichm\"uller metric.
	\item {} For \markbox{1084}{an} \markbox{1085}{introduction} \markbox{1086}{to} \markbox{1087}{bicombings} \markbox{1088}{and} \markbox{1089}{semihyperbolicity,} \markbox{1090}{see} \markbox{1091}{Alonso--Bridson} \cite{AB95}.

\end{itemize}

\subsection{Structure of the paper}

The \markbox{1115}{paper} \markbox{1116}{begins} \markbox{1117}{with} \markbox{1118}{a} \markbox{1119}{high-level} \markbox{1120}{discussion} \markbox{1121}{of} \markbox{1122}{the} \markbox{1123}{endgame} \markbox{1124}{for} \markbox{1125}{the} \markbox{1126}{bicombing} \markbox{1127}{construction} \markbox{1128}{using} \markbox{1129}{cubical} \markbox{1130}{approximation} \markbox{1131}{techniques.}  \markbox{1132}{In} \markbox{1133}{particular,} \markbox{1134}{in} \markbox{1135}{Section} \ref{sec:endgame}, \markbox{1136}{we} \markbox{1137}{will} \markbox{1138}{extract} \markbox{1139}{the} \markbox{1140}{key} \markbox{1141}{facts} \markbox{1142}{that} \markbox{1143}{we} \markbox{1144}{prove} \markbox{1145}{about} \markbox{1146}{colorable} \markbox{1147}{hierarchically} \markbox{1148}{hyperbolic} \markbox{1149}{spaces,} \markbox{1150}{namely} \markbox{1151}{the} \markbox{1152}{Stable} \markbox{1153}{Cubes} \markbox{1154}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes} \markbox{1155}{and} \markbox{1156}{Stable} \markbox{1157}{Moves} \markbox{1158}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable moves}, \markbox{1159}{to} \markbox{1160}{build} \markbox{1161}{a} \markbox{1162}{bicombing} \markbox{1163}{on} \markbox{1164}{any} \markbox{1165}{metric} \markbox{1166}{space} \markbox{1167}{possessing} \markbox{1168}{the} \markbox{1169}{properties} \markbox{1170}{described} \markbox{1171}{in} \markbox{1172}{the} \markbox{1173}{former.}  \markbox{1174}{This} \markbox{1175}{includes} \markbox{1176}{the} \markbox{1177}{much} \markbox{1178}{simplified} \markbox{1179}{construction} \markbox{1180}{of} \markbox{1181}{the} \markbox{1182}{bicombing} \markbox{1183}{paths} \markbox{1184}{themselves} \markbox{1185}{via} \markbox{1186}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{1187}{paths} \markbox{1188}{in} \markbox{1189}{Subsection} \ref{sec:NR stability}.

With \markbox{1190}{this} \markbox{1191}{setup} \markbox{1192}{as} \markbox{1193}{motivation,} \markbox{1194}{we} \markbox{1195}{then} \markbox{1196}{proceed} \markbox{1197}{to} \markbox{1198}{describe} \markbox{1199}{the} \markbox{1200}{cubical} \markbox{1201}{model} \markbox{1202}{construction} \markbox{1203}{for} \markbox{1204}{HHSes.}  \markbox{1205}{Sections} \ref{sec:interval systems} \markbox{1206}{through} \ref{sec:cubulation} \markbox{1207}{explain} \markbox{1208}{the} \markbox{1209}{interval} \markbox{1210}{version} \markbox{1211}{of} \markbox{1212}{the} \markbox{1213}{cubical} \markbox{1214}{model} \markbox{1215}{theorem} \markbox{1216}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{1217}{The} \markbox{1218}{heart} \markbox{1219}{of} \markbox{1220}{the} \markbox{1221}{paper} \markbox{1222}{is} \markbox{1223}{in} \markbox{1224}{Sections} \ref{sec:controlling domains} \markbox{1225}{and} \ref{sec:stable intervals}, \markbox{1226}{where} \markbox{1227}{we} \markbox{1228}{explain} \markbox{1229}{how} \markbox{1230}{to} \markbox{1231}{build} \markbox{1232}{the} \markbox{1233}{stabilized} \markbox{1234}{family} \markbox{1235}{of} \markbox{1236}{intervals} \markbox{1237}{which} \markbox{1238}{serve} \markbox{1239}{as} \markbox{1240}{input,} \markbox{1241}{as} \markbox{1242}{well} \markbox{1243}{as} \markbox{1244}{in} \markbox{1245}{Section} \ref{sec:stable cubes}, \markbox{1246}{where} \markbox{1247}{we} \markbox{1248}{see} \markbox{1249}{how} \markbox{1250}{to} \markbox{1251}{plug} \markbox{1252}{this} \markbox{1253}{stabilized} \markbox{1254}{input} \markbox{1255}{into} \markbox{1256}{the} \markbox{1257}{cubulation} machine.

\section{Beginning at the end} \label{sec:endgame}

The \markbox{1401}{purpose} \markbox{1402}{of} \markbox{1403}{this} \markbox{1404}{section} \markbox{1405}{is} \markbox{1406}{to} \markbox{1407}{prove} \markbox{1408}{the} \markbox{1409}{main} \markbox{1410}{consequence} \markbox{1411}{of} \markbox{1412}{the} \markbox{1413}{technical} \markbox{1414}{results} \markbox{1415}{we} \markbox{1416}{will} \markbox{1417}{spend} \markbox{1418}{the} \markbox{1419}{rest} \markbox{1420}{of} \markbox{1421}{the} \markbox{1422}{paper} \markbox{1423}{establishing.}  \markbox{1424}{That} \markbox{1425}{is,} \markbox{1426}{we} \markbox{1427}{will} \markbox{1428}{begin} \markbox{1429}{by} \markbox{1430}{explaining} \markbox{1431}{how} \markbox{1432}{the} \markbox{1433}{Stable} \markbox{1434}{Cubical} \markbox{1435}{Intervals} \markbox{1436}{Theorem} \ref{thmi:main}  \markbox{1437}{(Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}) \markbox{1438}{is} \markbox{1439}{enough} \markbox{1440}{to} \markbox{1441}{prove} \markbox{1442}{bicombability} \markbox{1443}{of} \markbox{1444}{the} \markbox{1445}{mapping} \markbox{1446}{class} \markbox{1447}{groups} \markbox{1448}{and} \markbox{1449}{colorably} \markbox{1450}{hierarchically} \markbox{1451}{hyperbolic} \markbox{1452}{spaces,} \markbox{1453}{more} generally.

We \markbox{1454}{begin} \markbox{1455}{with} \markbox{1456}{a} \markbox{1457}{brief} \markbox{1458}{primer} \markbox{1459}{on} \markbox{1460}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1461}{cube} \markbox{1462}{complexes} \markbox{1463}{and} \markbox{1464}{a} \markbox{1465}{discussion} \markbox{1466}{of} \markbox{1467}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{1468}{paths} \markbox{1469}{and} \markbox{1470}{their} \markbox{1471}{stability} \markbox{1472}{under} \markbox{1473}{hyperplane} \markbox{1474}{deletions.}  \markbox{1475}{In} \markbox{1476}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:stable cubes, early}, \markbox{1477}{we} \markbox{1478}{give} \markbox{1479}{a} \markbox{1480}{precise} \markbox{1481}{version} \markbox{1482}{of} \markbox{1483}{our} \markbox{1484}{stable} \markbox{1485}{cubulations} \markbox{1486}{result} \markbox{1487}{along} \markbox{1488}{with} \markbox{1489}{its} \markbox{1490}{associated} \markbox{1491}{path-building} \markbox{1492}{construction.}  \markbox{1493}{In} \markbox{1494}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:semihyp}, \markbox{1495}{we} \markbox{1496}{then} \markbox{1497}{define} \markbox{1498}{and} \markbox{1499}{discuss} \markbox{1500}{bicombings.}  \markbox{1501}{In} \markbox{1502}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:building bicombing}, \markbox{1503}{we} \markbox{1504}{explain} \markbox{1505}{how} \markbox{1506}{to} \markbox{1507}{put} \markbox{1508}{these} \markbox{1509}{parts} \markbox{1510}{together} \markbox{1511}{to} \markbox{1512}{give} \markbox{1513}{a} \markbox{1514}{bicombing} \markbox{1515}{for} \markbox{1516}{any} \markbox{1517}{metric} \markbox{1518}{space} \markbox{1519}{satisfying} \markbox{1520}{some} \markbox{1521}{version} \markbox{1522}{of} \markbox{1523}{our} \markbox{1524}{stable} \markbox{1525}{cubulations} setup.

\subsection{Wall spaces, cube complexes, and hyperplane deletions}\label{subsec:CCC background}


%@@@@Adapt to median setup

This \markbox{1526}{subsection} \markbox{1527}{includes} \markbox{1528}{a} \markbox{1529}{quick} \markbox{1530}{set} \markbox{1531}{of} \markbox{1532}{definitions} \markbox{1533}{and} \markbox{1534}{references} \markbox{1535}{for} \markbox{1536}{readers} \markbox{1537}{unfamiliar} \markbox{1538}{with} \markbox{1539}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1540}{cube} complexes.

Our \markbox{1541}{approach} \markbox{1542}{here} \markbox{1543}{follows} \markbox{1544}{most} \markbox{1545}{closely} \markbox{1546}{Roller's} \markbox{1547}{approach} \cite{Roller} \markbox{1548}{to} \markbox{1549}{Sageev's} \markbox{1550}{cubulation} \markbox{1551}{machine} \cite{Sageev:cubulation}, \markbox{1552}{which} \markbox{1553}{uses} \markbox{1554}{the} \markbox{1555}{notion} \markbox{1556}{of} \markbox{1557}{wall-space} \markbox{1558}{as} \markbox{1559}{introduced} \markbox{1560}{by} \markbox{1561}{Haglund-Paulin} \cite{HP_wallspace}.  \markbox{1562}{See} \markbox{1563}{Sageev's} \markbox{1564}{notes} \cite{Sageev:pcmi}, \markbox{1565}{as} \markbox{1566}{well} \markbox{1567}{as} \markbox{1568}{Hruska-Wise} \cite{HW_CCC}, \markbox{1569}{for} \markbox{1570}{excellent} \markbox{1571}{expositions} \markbox{1572}{on} \markbox{1573}{this} \markbox{1574}{subject.}  \markbox{1575}{We} \markbox{1576}{note} \markbox{1577}{that} \markbox{1578}{we} \markbox{1579}{will} \markbox{1580}{later} \markbox{1581}{take} \markbox{1582}{an} \markbox{1583}{approach} \markbox{1584}{using} \markbox{1585}{medians} \markbox{1586}{in} \markbox{1587}{Section} \ref{sec:cubulation}.  

A \markbox{1588}{\emph{cube complex}} \markbox{1589}{is} \markbox{1590}{a} \markbox{1591}{CW} \markbox{1592}{complex} \markbox{1593}{obtained} \markbox{1594}{by} \markbox{1595}{gluing} \markbox{1596}{a} \markbox{1597}{collection} \markbox{1598}{of} \markbox{1599}{unit} \markbox{1600}{Euclidean} \markbox{1601}{cubes} \markbox{1602}{of} \markbox{1603}{various} \markbox{1604}{dimensions} \markbox{1605}{along} \markbox{1606}{their} \markbox{1607}{faces} \markbox{1608}{by} \markbox{1609}{a} \markbox{1610}{collection} \markbox{1611}{of} \markbox{1612}{(Euclidean)} \markbox{1613}{isometries.}  \markbox{1614}{A} \markbox{1615}{cube} \markbox{1616}{complex} \markbox{m1617}{$\Sigma$} \markbox{1618}{is} \markbox{1619}{\emph{non-positively curved}} \markbox{1620}{when} \markbox{1621}{it} \markbox{1622}{satisfies} \markbox{1623}{Gromov's} \markbox{1624}{link} \markbox{1625}{condition,} \markbox{1626}{and} \markbox{1627}{every} \markbox{1628}{non-positively} \markbox{1629}{curved} \markbox{1630}{simply} \markbox{1631}{connected} \markbox{1632}{cube} \markbox{1633}{complex} \markbox{1634}{admits} \markbox{1635}{a} \markbox{1636}{unique} \markbox{1637}{CAT(0)} metric.

A \markbox{1638}{\emph{hyperplane}} \markbox{1639}{in} \markbox{1640}{a} \markbox{1641}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1642}{cube} \markbox{1643}{complex} \markbox{m1644}{$\Sigma$} \markbox{1645}{is} \markbox{1646}{a} \markbox{1647}{connected} \markbox{1648}{subspace} \markbox{1649}{whose} \markbox{1650}{intersection} \markbox{1651}{with} \markbox{1652}{each} \markbox{1653}{cube} \markbox{m1654}{$\sigma = [0,1]^{n}$} \markbox{1655}{is} \markbox{1656}{either} \markbox{m1657}{$\emptyset$} \markbox{1658}{or} \markbox{1659}{the} \markbox{1660}{subspace} \markbox{1661}{obtained} \markbox{1662}{by} \markbox{1663}{restricting} \markbox{1664}{exactly} \markbox{1665}{one} \markbox{1666}{coordinate} \markbox{1667}{to} \markbox{m1668}{$\frac{1}{2}$}.  \markbox{1669}{In} \markbox{1670}{particular,} \markbox{1671}{every} \markbox{1672}{hyperplane} \markbox{1673}{partitions} \markbox{m1674}{$\Sigma$}.  \markbox{1675}{This} \markbox{1676}{motivates} \markbox{1677}{the} \markbox{1678}{definition} \markbox{1679}{of} \markbox{1680}{a} \markbox{1681}{half-spaces} \markbox{1682}{and} \markbox{1683}{pocsets,} \markbox{1684}{following} \markbox{1685}{Roller} \cite{Roller}.

\begin{definition}[Pocset]\label{defn:pocset}
Let \markbox{m1686}{$(\Sigma,<)$} \markbox{1687}{be} \markbox{1688}{a} \markbox{1689}{partially-ordered} \markbox{1690}{set.}  \markbox{1691}{A} \markbox{1692}{\emph{pocset}} \markbox{1693}{structure} \markbox{1694}{on} \markbox{m1695}{$\Sigma$} \markbox{1696}{has} \markbox{1697}{the} \markbox{1698}{additional} \markbox{1699}{structure} \markbox{1700}{of} \markbox{1701}{an} \markbox{1702}{order-reversing} \markbox{1703}{involution} \markbox{m1704}{$A \mapsto A^*$} satisfying
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m1705}{$A \neq A^*$} \markbox{1706}{and} \markbox{m1707}{$A, A^*$} \markbox{1708}{are} \markbox{m1709}{$<$}-incomparable;
\item {} \markbox{m1710}{$A < B \implies B^* < A^*$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item {} Given \markbox{m1711}{$A<B$}, \markbox{1712}{the} \markbox{1713}{\emph{interval}} \markbox{1714}{between} \markbox{m1715}{$A$} \markbox{1716}{and} \markbox{m1717}{$B$} \markbox{1718}{is} \markbox{m1719}{$[A,B] = \{C|A<C<B\}$}.
\item {} The \markbox{1720}{pocset} \markbox{m1721}{$(\Sigma,<)$} \markbox{1722}{is} \markbox{1723}{\emph{locally finite}} \markbox{1724}{if} \markbox{1725}{every} \markbox{1726}{interval} \markbox{1727}{is} finite.
\item {} Given \markbox{m1728}{$A,B \in \Sigma$}, \markbox{1729}{we} \markbox{1730}{say} \markbox{m1731}{$A$} \markbox{1732}{is} \markbox{1733}{\emph{transverse}} \markbox{1734}{to} \markbox{m1735}{$B$} \markbox{1736}{if} \markbox{1737}{none} \markbox{1738}{of} \markbox{m1739}{$A<B, A<B^*, A^*<B, A^*<B^*$} \markbox{1740}{holds.}  \markbox{1741}{The} \markbox{1742}{pocset} \markbox{m1743}{$(\Sigma,<)$} \markbox{1744}{has} \markbox{1745}{\emph{finite width}} \markbox{1746}{if} \markbox{1747}{the} \markbox{1748}{maximal} \markbox{1749}{size} \markbox{1750}{of} \markbox{1751}{a} \markbox{1752}{pairwise} \markbox{1753}{transverse} \markbox{1754}{subset} \markbox{1755}{is} finite.

\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

In \markbox{1756}{a} \markbox{1757}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1758}{cube} \markbox{1759}{complex,} \markbox{1760}{every} \markbox{1761}{vertex} \markbox{1762}{is} \markbox{1763}{contained} \markbox{1764}{in} \markbox{1765}{exactly} \markbox{1766}{one} \markbox{1767}{half-space} \markbox{1768}{associated} \markbox{1769}{to} \markbox{1770}{each} \markbox{1771}{hyperplane.}  \markbox{1772}{The} \markbox{1773}{following} \markbox{1774}{notion} \markbox{1775}{abstracts} \markbox{1776}{the} \markbox{1777}{combinatorial} \markbox{1778}{structure} \markbox{1779}{of} \markbox{1780}{such} \markbox{1781}{a} \markbox{1782}{family} \markbox{1783}{of} half-spaces:

\begin{definition}[Ultrafilters \markbox{1784}{and} \markbox{1785}{the} DCC]\label{defn:ultrafilter}
Given \markbox{1786}{a} \markbox{1787}{locally} \markbox{1788}{finite} \markbox{1789}{pocset} \markbox{m1790}{$(\Sigma, <)$}, \markbox{1791}{an} \markbox{1792}{\emph{ultrafilter}} \markbox{m1793}{$\alpha$} \markbox{1794}{on} \markbox{m1795}{$\Sigma$} \markbox{1796}{is} \markbox{1797}{a} \markbox{1798}{subset} \markbox{1799}{of} \markbox{m1800}{$\Sigma$} satisfying
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} (Choice) \markbox{1801}{Exactly} \markbox{1802}{one} \markbox{1803}{element} \markbox{1804}{of} \markbox{1805}{each} \markbox{1806}{pair} \markbox{m1807}{$\{A,A^*\}$} \markbox{1808}{is} \markbox{1809}{an} \markbox{1810}{element} \markbox{1811}{of} \markbox{m1812}{$\alpha$};
\item {} (Consistency) \markbox{m1813}{$A \in \alpha$} \markbox{1814}{and} \markbox{m1815}{$A< B \implies B \in \alpha$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item {} An \markbox{1816}{ultrafilter} \markbox{m1817}{$\alpha$} \markbox{1818}{satisfies} \markbox{1819}{the} \markbox{1820}{\emph{descending chain condition}} \markbox{1821}{(DCC)} \markbox{1822}{if} \markbox{1823}{every} \markbox{1824}{descending} \markbox{1825}{chain} \markbox{1826}{of} \markbox{1827}{elements} terminates.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

We \markbox{1828}{can} \markbox{1829}{now} \markbox{1830}{define} \markbox{1831}{the} \markbox{1832}{dual} \markbox{1833}{cube} \markbox{1834}{complex} \markbox{1835}{to} \markbox{1836}{a} \markbox{1837}{locally} \markbox{1838}{finite,} \markbox{1839}{discrete,} \markbox{1840}{finite-width} pocset:

\begin{definition}[Dual \markbox{1841}{cube} complex]\label{defn:dual CCC}
Given \markbox{1842}{a} \markbox{1843}{locally} \markbox{1844}{finite,} \markbox{1845}{discrete,} \markbox{1846}{finite-width} \markbox{1847}{pocset} \markbox{m1848}{$(\Sigma,<)$}, \markbox{1849}{we} \markbox{1850}{define} \markbox{1851}{a} \markbox{1852}{CW} \markbox{1853}{complex} \markbox{m1854}{$X(\Sigma)$} \markbox{1855}{as} follows:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} The \markbox{m1856}{$0$}-cells \markbox{m1857}{$X^{(0)}$} \markbox{1858}{of} \markbox{m1859}{$X$} \markbox{1860}{are} \markbox{1861}{the} \markbox{1862}{DCC} \markbox{1863}{ultrafilters} \markbox{1864}{on} \markbox{m1865}{$(\Sigma, <)$}.
\item {} Two \markbox{m1866}{$0$}-cells \markbox{m1867}{$\alpha, \beta$} \markbox{1868}{are} \markbox{1869}{connected} \markbox{1870}{by} \markbox{1871}{an} \markbox{1872}{edge} \markbox{1873}{in} \markbox{m1874}{$X^{(1)}$} \markbox{1875}{if} \markbox{1876}{and} \markbox{1877}{only} \markbox{1878}{if} \markbox{m1879}{$|\alpha \triangle \beta| = 2$}, \markbox{1880}{i.e.} \markbox{m1881}{$\alpha = (\beta - \{A\}) \cup \{A^*\}$} \markbox{1882}{for} \markbox{1883}{some} \markbox{m1884}{$A \in \Sigma$}.
\item {} Define \markbox{m1885}{$X^{(n)}$} \markbox{1886}{inductively} \markbox{1887}{by} \markbox{1888}{adding} \markbox{1889}{an} \markbox{m1890}{$n$}-cube \markbox{1891}{whenever} \markbox{1892}{the} \markbox{1893}{boundary} \markbox{1894}{of} \markbox{1895}{one} \markbox{1896}{appears} \markbox{1897}{in} \markbox{1898}{the} \markbox{m1899}{$X^{(n-1)}$}-skeleton.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}


The \markbox{1900}{following} \markbox{1901}{is} \markbox{1902}{a} \markbox{1903}{theorem} \markbox{1904}{of} \markbox{1905}{Roller} \cite{Roller}, \markbox{1906}{building} \markbox{1907}{on} \markbox{1908}{Sageev} \cite{Sageev:cubulation}:

\begin{theorem}[Sageev's machine]\label{thm:Sageev}
Given \markbox{1909}{a} \markbox{1910}{locally} \markbox{1911}{finite,} \markbox{1912}{finite-width} \markbox{1913}{pocset} \markbox{m1914}{$(\Sigma,<)$}, \markbox{1915}{the} \markbox{1916}{CW} \markbox{1917}{complex} \markbox{m1918}{$X(\Sigma)$} \markbox{1919}{is} \markbox{1920}{a} \markbox{1921}{finite} \markbox{1922}{dimensional} \markbox{1923}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1924}{cube} \markbox{1925}{complex,} \markbox{1926}{where} \markbox{1927}{the} \markbox{1928}{dimension} \markbox{1929}{is} \markbox{1930}{equal} \markbox{1931}{to} \markbox{1932}{the} \markbox{1933}{width} \markbox{1934}{of} \markbox{m1935}{$(\Sigma, <)$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item {} We \markbox{1936}{call} \markbox{m1937}{$X(\Sigma)$} \markbox{1938}{the} \markbox{1939}{\emph{dual cube complex}} \markbox{1940}{to} \markbox{m1941}{$(\Sigma, <)$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{theorem}

We \markbox{1942}{note} \markbox{1943}{that} \markbox{1944}{the} \markbox{1945}{dual} \markbox{1946}{cube} \markbox{1947}{complex} \markbox{1948}{to} \markbox{1949}{the} \markbox{1950}{pocset} \markbox{1951}{coming} \markbox{1952}{from} \markbox{1953}{the} \markbox{1954}{hyperplanes} \markbox{1955}{of} \markbox{1956}{a} \markbox{1957}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1958}{cube} \markbox{1959}{complex} \markbox{1960}{is} \markbox{1961}{(isomorphic} \markbox{1962}{to)} \markbox{1963}{that} \markbox{1964}{cube} complex.

The \markbox{1965}{following} \markbox{1966}{lemma} \markbox{1967}{is} \markbox{1968}{useful} \markbox{1969}{for} \markbox{1970}{obtaining} \markbox{1971}{isomorphisms} \markbox{1972}{between} \markbox{1973}{cube} \markbox{1974}{complexes} \markbox{1975}{whose} \markbox{1976}{wall-spaces} \markbox{1977}{we} \markbox{1978}{can} \markbox{1979}{directly} \markbox{1980}{compare.}  \markbox{1981}{Its} \markbox{1982}{proof} \markbox{1983}{is} \markbox{1984}{an} \markbox{1985}{exercise} \markbox{1986}{in} \markbox{1987}{the} \markbox{1988}{basics} \markbox{1989}{of} \markbox{1990}{CAT(0)} \markbox{1991}{cube} \markbox{1992}{complexes} \markbox{1993}{which} \markbox{1994}{we} \markbox{1995}{leave} \markbox{1996}{to} \markbox{1997}{the} reader.

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:halfspaces_bijection}
 \markbox{1998}{Let} \markbox{m1999}{$\calW$}, \markbox{m2000}{$\calW'$} \markbox{2001}{be} \markbox{2002}{wallspaces,} \markbox{2003}{and} \markbox{2004}{let} \markbox{m2005}{$\iota:\calH_{\calW} \to \calH_{\calW'}$} \markbox{2006}{be} \markbox{2007}{a} \markbox{2008}{bijection} \markbox{2009}{of} \markbox{2010}{their} \markbox{2011}{half-spaces,} \markbox{2012}{which} preserves
 \markbox{2013}{complements} \markbox{2014}{and} \markbox{2015}{disjointness.}  \markbox{2016}{Then} \markbox{m2017}{$\iota$} \markbox{2018}{induces} \markbox{2019}{a} \markbox{2020}{cubical} isomorphism
\markbox{m2021}{$h:\calD(\calW)\to \calD(\calW')$}
between \markbox{2022}{the} \markbox{2023}{corresponding} \markbox{2024}{dual} \markbox{2025}{CAT(0)} \markbox{2026}{cube} complexes.
\end{lemma}

Finally, \markbox{2027}{in} \markbox{2028}{our} \markbox{2029}{stable} \markbox{2030}{cubulations} \markbox{2031}{theorem,} \markbox{2032}{we} \markbox{2033}{will} \markbox{2034}{want} \markbox{2035}{to} \markbox{2036}{realize} \markbox{2037}{maps} \markbox{2038}{between} \markbox{2039}{certain} \markbox{2040}{cube} \markbox{2041}{complexes} \markbox{2042}{as} \markbox{2043}{a} \markbox{2044}{sort} \markbox{2045}{of} \markbox{2046}{collapsing} \markbox{2047}{of} \markbox{2048}{a} \markbox{2049}{controlled} \markbox{2050}{piece} \markbox{2051}{of} \markbox{2052}{their} \markbox{2053}{combinatorial} \markbox{2054}{data.}  \markbox{2055}{The} \markbox{2056}{right} \markbox{2057}{notion} \markbox{2058}{here} \markbox{2059}{is} \markbox{2060}{of} \markbox{2061}{a} \markbox{2062}{\emph{hyperplane deletion}}.  \markbox{2063}{The} \markbox{2064}{motivating} \markbox{2065}{example} \markbox{2066}{is} \markbox{2067}{where} \markbox{2068}{one} \markbox{2069}{has} \markbox{2070}{a} \markbox{2071}{wall-space} \markbox{m2072}{$\calW(\calH)$} \markbox{2073}{on} \markbox{2074}{some} \markbox{2075}{set} \markbox{2076}{of} \markbox{2077}{walls} \markbox{m2078}{$\calH$}, \markbox{2079}{and} \markbox{2080}{one} \markbox{2081}{removes} \markbox{2082}{some} \markbox{2083}{collection} \markbox{2084}{of} \markbox{2085}{the} \markbox{2086}{walls} \markbox{m2087}{$\calH - \calG$}, \markbox{2088}{to} \markbox{2089}{obtain} \markbox{2090}{a} \markbox{2091}{\emph{restriction map}} \markbox{m2092}{$\calD(\calW(\calH)) \to \calD(\calW(\calH- \calG))$} \markbox{2093}{between} \markbox{2094}{their} \markbox{2095}{dual} \markbox{2096}{cube} \markbox{2097}{complexes} \markbox{2098}{in} \markbox{2099}{the} \markbox{2100}{sense} \markbox{2101}{of} \cite{CapraceSageev}.  \markbox{2102}{This} \markbox{2103}{map} \markbox{2104}{collapses} \markbox{2105}{the} \markbox{2106}{carriers} \markbox{2107}{of} \markbox{2108}{the} \markbox{2109}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2110}{in} \markbox{m2111}{$\calG$} \markbox{2112}{(recall} \markbox{2113}{that} \markbox{2114}{a} \markbox{2115}{carrier} \markbox{2116}{of} \markbox{2117}{a} \markbox{2118}{hyperplane} \markbox{m2119}{$\hh$} \markbox{2120}{is} \markbox{2121}{naturally} \markbox{2122}{isomorphic} \markbox{2123}{to} \markbox{m2124}{$\hh \times [0,1]$}).










\subsection{Stable cubes and stable moves}\label{subsec:stable cubes, early}

We \markbox{2125}{will} \markbox{2126}{prove} \markbox{2127}{Corollary} \ref{cori:semihyp} \markbox{2128}{in} \markbox{2129}{an} \markbox{2130}{ostensibly} \markbox{2131}{more} \markbox{2132}{general} \markbox{2133}{framework} \markbox{2134}{than} \markbox{2135}{that} \markbox{2136}{of} \markbox{2137}{(colorable)} HHSes\footnote{We \markbox{2138}{actually} \markbox{2139}{suspect} \markbox{2140}{that} \markbox{2141}{coarse} \markbox{2142}{median} \markbox{2143}{spaces} \markbox{2144}{satisfying} \markbox{2145}{some} \markbox{2146}{version} \markbox{2147}{of} \markbox{2148}{the} \markbox{2149}{property} \markbox{2150}{in} \markbox{2151}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes} \markbox{2152}{will} \markbox{2153}{be} \markbox{2154}{HHSes,} \markbox{2155}{though} \markbox{2156}{it} \markbox{2157}{is} \markbox{2158}{unclear} \markbox{2159}{to} \markbox{2160}{us} \markbox{2161}{what} \markbox{2162}{exactly} \markbox{2163}{the} \markbox{2164}{right} \markbox{2165}{property} \markbox{2166}{is,} \markbox{2167}{e.g.} \markbox{2168}{perhaps} \markbox{2169}{a} \markbox{2170}{factor} \markbox{2171}{system} \markbox{2172}{in} \markbox{2173}{the} \markbox{2174}{sense} \markbox{2175}{of} \cite{HHS_I}.}.  \markbox{2176}{That} \markbox{2177}{is,} \markbox{2178}{we} \markbox{2179}{only} \markbox{2180}{need} \markbox{2181}{a} \markbox{2182}{metric} \markbox{2183}{space} \markbox{2184}{which} \markbox{2185}{satisfies} \markbox{2186}{the} \markbox{2187}{following} \markbox{2188}{definitions.}  \markbox{2189}{The} \markbox{2190}{first} \markbox{2191}{is} \markbox{2192}{effectively} \markbox{2193}{a} \markbox{2194}{weak} \markbox{2195}{two-point} \markbox{2196}{version} \markbox{2197}{of} \markbox{2198}{the} \markbox{2199}{cubical} \markbox{2200}{model} \markbox{2201}{property} \markbox{2202}{for} \markbox{2203}{HHSes} \markbox{2204}{from} \cite{HHS_quasi}, \markbox{2205}{proven} \markbox{2206}{in} \markbox{2207}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC} \markbox{2208}{in} \markbox{2209}{this} paper.

\begin{definition}[Weak \markbox{2210}{local} quasi-cubicality]\label{defn:lqc pair}

Let \markbox{m2211}{$X$} \markbox{2212}{be} \markbox{2213}{a} \markbox{2214}{metric} \markbox{2215}{space.}  \markbox{2216}{A} \markbox{m2217}{$B_0$}-\markbox{2218}{\emph{cubical model}} \markbox{2219}{for} \markbox{2220}{a} \markbox{2221}{pair} \markbox{m2222}{$a,b \in X$} \markbox{2223}{is} \markbox{2224}{a} \markbox{2225}{CAT(0)} \markbox{2226}{cube} \markbox{2227}{complex} \markbox{m2228}{$\calQ$} \markbox{2229}{of} \markbox{2230}{dimension} \markbox{2231}{at} \markbox{2232}{most} \markbox{m2233}{$B_0$} \markbox{2234}{satisfying} \markbox{2235}{the} following:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} There \markbox{2236}{is} \markbox{2237}{a} \markbox{m2238}{$(B_0,B_0)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{2239}{embedding} \markbox{m2240}{$\hO:\calQ \to X$} \markbox{2241}{(the} \markbox{2242}{\emph{cubical model map}}),
\item {} There \markbox{2243}{are} \markbox{2244}{two} \markbox{2245}{\emph{distinguished vertices}} \markbox{m2246}{$\ha,\hb \in \calQ$} \markbox{2247}{so} \markbox{2248}{that} \markbox{2249}{any} \markbox{m2250}{$\ell^{\infty}$}-geodesic \markbox{m2251}{$\gamma \subset \calQ$} \markbox{2252}{between} \markbox{m2253}{$\ha,\hb$} \markbox{2254}{is} \markbox{2255}{sent} \markbox{2256}{to} \markbox{2257}{a} \markbox{m2258}{$(B_0,B_0)$}-quasi-geodesic \markbox{m2259}{$\hO(\gamma) \subset X$} \markbox{2260}{between} \markbox{m2261}{$a,b$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item {} We \markbox{2262}{say} \markbox{m2263}{$X$} \markbox{2264}{is} \markbox{m2265}{$B_0$}-\markbox{2266}{\emph{weakly locally quasi-cubical}} \markbox{2267}{(wLQC)} \markbox{2268}{if} \markbox{2269}{there} \markbox{2270}{exists} \markbox{m2271}{$B_0>0$} \markbox{2272}{so} \markbox{2273}{that} \markbox{2274}{any} \markbox{2275}{pair} \markbox{m2276}{$a,b\in X$} \markbox{2277}{admits} \markbox{2278}{a} \markbox{m2279}{$B_0$}-cubical model.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

 \markbox{2280}{While} \markbox{2281}{CAT(0)} \markbox{2282}{cube} \markbox{2283}{complexes} \markbox{2284}{have} \markbox{2285}{many} \markbox{2286}{standard} \markbox{2287}{metrics} \markbox{2288}{(all} \markbox{2289}{of} \markbox{2290}{which} \markbox{2291}{are} \markbox{2292}{quasi-isometric),} \markbox{2293}{the} \markbox{2294}{convenient} \markbox{2295}{one} \markbox{2296}{for} \markbox{2297}{us} \markbox{2298}{is} \markbox{2299}{the} \markbox{m2300}{$\ell^{\infty}$}-metric, \markbox{2301}{which,} \markbox{2302}{for} \markbox{2303}{vertices} \markbox{2304}{in} \markbox{2305}{a} \markbox{2306}{single} \markbox{2307}{unit} \markbox{2308}{cube,} \markbox{2309}{is} \markbox{2310}{just} \markbox{2311}{the} \markbox{m2312}{$\sup$}-metric. 

The \markbox{2313}{next} \markbox{2314}{definition} \markbox{2315}{is} \markbox{2316}{extracted} \markbox{2317}{from} \markbox{2318}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes} \markbox{2319}{below.}  \markbox{2320}{This} \markbox{2321}{property} \markbox{2322}{holds} \markbox{2323}{for} \markbox{2324}{colorable} \markbox{2325}{hierarchically} \markbox{2326}{hyperbolic} \markbox{2327}{spaces,} \markbox{2328}{e.g.,} \markbox{2329}{the} \markbox{2330}{mapping} \markbox{2331}{class} \markbox{2332}{group} \markbox{2333}{and} Teichm\"uller \markbox{2334}{space;} \markbox{2335}{see} \cite[Theorem 4.1]{DMS_bary} \markbox{2336}{for} \markbox{2337}{the} \markbox{2338}{original,} \markbox{2339}{more} \markbox{2340}{general} \markbox{2341}{version,} \markbox{2342}{and} \cite[Theorem 9.1]{DMS_FJ} \markbox{2343}{for} \markbox{2344}{the} \markbox{2345}{state-of-the-art.}  \markbox{2346}{Part} \markbox{2347}{of} \markbox{2348}{our} \markbox{2349}{purpose} \markbox{2350}{here} \markbox{2351}{for} \markbox{2352}{extracting} \markbox{2353}{it} \markbox{2354}{from} \markbox{2355}{the} \markbox{2356}{HHS} \markbox{2357}{setting} \markbox{2358}{is} \markbox{2359}{to} \markbox{2360}{highlight} \markbox{2361}{the} \markbox{2362}{structure} \markbox{2363}{of} \markbox{2364}{the} endgame.


\begin{definition}[Stable \markbox{2365}{weak} \markbox{2366}{local} quasicubicality]\label{defn:stable cubes}
We \markbox{2367}{say} \markbox{2368}{that} \markbox{2369}{a} \markbox{2370}{metric} \markbox{2371}{space} \markbox{m2372}{$X$} \markbox{2373}{is} \markbox{2374}{\emph{$B_0$-stably wLQC}} \markbox{2375}{if} \markbox{2376}{there} \markbox{2377}{is} \markbox{2378}{a} \markbox{m2379}{$B_0$} \markbox{2380}{so} \markbox{2381}{that} \markbox{2382}{the} \markbox{2383}{following} \markbox{2384}{holds:}  

\begin{itemize}
\item {} For \markbox{2385}{any} \markbox{m2386}{$a,b, a',b' \in X$} \markbox{2387}{with} \markbox{m2388}{$d_X(a,a') \leq 1$} \markbox{2389}{and} \markbox{m2390}{$d_X(b,b')\leq 1$}, \markbox{2391}{there} \markbox{2392}{exist} \markbox{m2393}{$B_0$}-cubical \markbox{2394}{models} \markbox{m2395}{$\calQ, \calQ_0$} \markbox{2396}{and} \markbox{m2397}{$\calQ',\calQ'_0$} \markbox{2398}{for} \markbox{m2399}{$a,b$} \markbox{2400}{and} \markbox{m2401}{$a',b'$} \markbox{2402}{so} \markbox{2403}{that} \markbox{2404}{the} \markbox{2405}{following} \markbox{2406}{diagram} \markbox{2407}{commutes} \markbox{2408}{up} \markbox{2409}{to} \markbox{2410}{additive} \markbox{2411}{error} \markbox{m2412}{$B_0$}:
\begin{equation}\label{Phi diagram, early}
  \begin{tikzcd}
   \calQ \arrow[ddrr,"\hO", bend left=40] \arrow[dr,"\Delta_0 \hspace{.075in}" left] &  \\
    &\calQ_{0} \arrow[dr,"\hO_0 \hspace{.2in}" below]\arrow[dd, "I_0"] \\
    & & X\\
    & \calQ'_{0} \arrow[ur,"\hO'_0"] \\
    \calQ'\arrow[uurr,"\hspace{.2in} \vspace{.1in} \hO'" below, bend right=40] \arrow[ur,"\Delta'_0"] & \\
  \end{tikzcd}
  \end{equation}
 \item {} In \markbox{2413}{the} above,
  \begin{enumerate}
  \item  {} \markbox{m2414}{$\hO, \hO_0, \hO', \hO'_0$} \markbox{2415}{are} \markbox{2416}{cubical} \markbox{2417}{model} \markbox{2418}{maps} \markbox{2419}{and} \markbox{2420}{hence} \markbox{m2421}{$(B_0,B_0)$}-quasi-isometric embeddings,
  \item {} the \markbox{2422}{map} \markbox{m2423}{$I_0$} \markbox{2424}{is} \markbox{2425}{a} \markbox{2426}{cubical} isomorphism,
  \item {} the \markbox{2427}{maps} \markbox{m2428}{$\Delta_0, \Delta'_0$} \markbox{2429}{are} \markbox{2430}{induced} \markbox{2431}{by} \markbox{2432}{deleting} \markbox{2433}{at} \markbox{2434}{most} \markbox{m2435}{$B_0$}-many \markbox{2436}{hyperplanes,} and
  \item {} \markbox{m2437}{$\Delta_0, \Delta'_0$} \markbox{2438}{take} \markbox{2439}{the} \markbox{2440}{distinguished} \markbox{2441}{vertices} \markbox{2442}{associated} \markbox{2443}{to} \markbox{m2444}{$a,b$} \markbox{2445}{and} \markbox{m2446}{$a',b'$} \markbox{2447}{in} \markbox{m2448}{$\calQ,\calQ'$} \markbox{2449}{to} \markbox{2450}{those} \markbox{2451}{in} \markbox{m2452}{$\calQ_0,\calQ'_0$}, respectively.
  \end{enumerate}
  \end{itemize}
\end{definition}

Requirement \markbox{2453}{(4)} \markbox{2454}{says} \markbox{2455}{that} \markbox{2456}{the} \markbox{2457}{way} \markbox{2458}{that} \markbox{2459}{the} \markbox{2460}{cube} \markbox{2461}{complexes} \markbox{m2462}{$\calQ,\calQ_0$} \markbox{2463}{model} \markbox{m2464}{$a,b$} \markbox{2465}{align,} \markbox{2466}{and} \markbox{2467}{similarly} \markbox{2468}{for} \markbox{m2469}{$\calQ', \calQ'_0$} \markbox{2470}{and} \markbox{m2471}{$a',b'$}.  \markbox{2472}{Note} \markbox{2473}{that} \markbox{2474}{if} \markbox{m2475}{$X$} \markbox{2476}{satisfies} \markbox{2477}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes} \markbox{2478}{then} \markbox{2479}{it} \markbox{2480}{satisfies} \markbox{2481}{Definition} \ref{defn:lqc pair}.  

\begin{remark}
Theorems \ref{thm:Q CCC} \markbox{2482}{and} \ref{thm:stable cubes} \markbox{2483}{actually} \markbox{2484}{provide} \markbox{2485}{a} \markbox{2486}{lot} \markbox{2487}{more} \markbox{2488}{information} \markbox{2489}{about} \markbox{2490}{these} \markbox{2491}{cubical} \markbox{2492}{models.}  \markbox{2493}{In} \markbox{2494}{particular,} \markbox{2495}{if} \markbox{m2496}{$\calX$} \markbox{2497}{is} \markbox{2498}{an} \markbox{2499}{HHS} \markbox{2500}{and} \markbox{m2501}{$a,b \in \calX$}, \markbox{2502}{then} \markbox{2503}{the} \markbox{2504}{cube} \markbox{2505}{complexes} \markbox{m2506}{$\calQ$} \markbox{2507}{and} \markbox{m2508}{$\calQ_0$} \markbox{2509}{above} \markbox{2510}{model} \markbox{2511}{the} \markbox{2512}{\emph{hierarchical hull}} \markbox{2513}{of} \markbox{m2514}{$a,b$} \markbox{2515}{(Definition} \ref{defn:hier hull}), \markbox{2516}{which} \markbox{2517}{is} \markbox{2518}{a} \markbox{2519}{coarsely} \markbox{2520}{convex} \markbox{2521}{subspace} \markbox{2522}{which} \markbox{2523}{encodes} \markbox{2524}{the} \markbox{2525}{hierarchical} \markbox{2526}{geometry} \markbox{2527}{between} \markbox{m2528}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{2529}{Moreover,} \markbox{2530}{the} \markbox{2531}{combinatorial} \markbox{2532}{geometry} \markbox{2533}{of} \markbox{2534}{the} \markbox{2535}{cube} \markbox{2536}{complex} \markbox{2537}{encodes} \markbox{2538}{essentially} \markbox{2539}{all} \markbox{2540}{of} \markbox{2541}{this} \markbox{2542}{hierarchical} \markbox{2543}{data.}  \markbox{2544}{See} \markbox{2545}{the} \markbox{2546}{introduction} \markbox{2547}{of} \cite{Dur_infcube} \markbox{2548}{for} \markbox{2549}{a} \markbox{2550}{detailed} discussion.
\end{remark}

\subsection{Stable moves}\label{sec:NR stability}

In \markbox{2551}{this} \markbox{2552}{subsection,} \markbox{2553}{we} \markbox{2554}{establish} \markbox{2555}{the} \markbox{2556}{key} \markbox{2557}{path-building} \markbox{2558}{portion} \markbox{2559}{of} \markbox{2560}{our} \markbox{2561}{bicombing} \markbox{2562}{construction,} \markbox{2563}{namely} \markbox{2564}{the} \markbox{2565}{Stable} \markbox{2566}{Moves} \markbox{2567}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable moves}.  \markbox{2568}{This} \markbox{2569}{involves} \markbox{2570}{proving} \markbox{2571}{that} \markbox{2572}{a} \markbox{2573}{well-studied} \markbox{2574}{family} \markbox{2575}{of} \markbox{2576}{paths} \markbox{2577}{in} \markbox{2578}{a} \markbox{2579}{cube} \markbox{2580}{complex} \markbox{2581}{due} \markbox{2582}{to} \markbox{2583}{Niblo--Reeves} \cite{NibloReeves} \markbox{2584}{behaves} \markbox{2585}{well} \markbox{2586}{under} \markbox{2587}{hyperplane} \markbox{2588}{deletion.}  \markbox{2589}{These} \markbox{2590}{paths} \markbox{2591}{were} \markbox{2592}{at} \markbox{2593}{the} \markbox{2594}{center} \markbox{2595}{of} \markbox{2596}{their} \markbox{2597}{construction} \markbox{2598}{of} \markbox{2599}{a} \markbox{2600}{biautomatic} \markbox{2601}{structure} \markbox{2602}{on} \markbox{2603}{an} \markbox{2604}{CAT(0)} \markbox{2605}{cubical} \markbox{2606}{group,} \markbox{2607}{and} \markbox{2608}{so} \markbox{2609}{it} \markbox{2610}{is} \markbox{2611}{quite} \markbox{2612}{agreeable} \markbox{2613}{that} \markbox{2614}{they} \markbox{2615}{play} \markbox{2616}{a} \markbox{2617}{central} \markbox{2618}{role} \markbox{2619}{in} \markbox{2620}{our} \markbox{2621}{construction} \markbox{2622}{of} \markbox{2623}{a} \markbox{2624}{bicombing} \markbox{2625}{for} \markbox{2626}{our} \markbox{2627}{sort} \markbox{2628}{of} \markbox{2629}{quasi-cubical} \markbox{2630}{spaces.}  \markbox{2631}{While} \markbox{2632}{we} \markbox{2633}{have} \markbox{2634}{maintained} \markbox{2635}{some} \markbox{2636}{of} \markbox{2637}{the} \markbox{2638}{structure} \markbox{2639}{and} \markbox{2640}{terminology} \markbox{2641}{from} \markbox{2642}{our} \markbox{2643}{work} \markbox{2644}{with} \markbox{2645}{Minsky} \markbox{2646}{and} \markbox{2647}{Sisto} \markbox{2648}{in} \cite[Section 5]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{2649}{our} \markbox{2650}{limited} \markbox{2651}{setting} \markbox{2652}{allows} \markbox{2653}{for} \markbox{2654}{a} \markbox{2655}{much} \markbox{2656}{simpler} \markbox{2657}{path} construction.

Let \markbox{m2658}{$X$} \markbox{2659}{be} \markbox{2660}{a} \markbox{2661}{finite} \markbox{2662}{CAT(0)} \markbox{2663}{cube} \markbox{2664}{complex} \markbox{2665}{with} \markbox{m2666}{$X = \hull_X(a,b)$} \markbox{2667}{the} \markbox{2668}{cubical} hull\footnote{The  \markbox{2669}{assumption} \markbox{2670}{that} \markbox{m2671}{$X = \hull_X(a,b)$} \markbox{2672}{is} \markbox{2673}{not} \markbox{2674}{necessary,} \markbox{2675}{but} \markbox{2676}{is} \markbox{2677}{convenient} \markbox{2678}{for} \markbox{2679}{our} purposes.} \markbox{2680}{of} \markbox{m2681}{$a,b \in X^0$}.  \markbox{2682}{Set} \markbox{m2683}{$\calH = \calH(a,b)$} \markbox{2684}{to} \markbox{2685}{be} \markbox{2686}{the} \markbox{2687}{set} \markbox{2688}{of} \markbox{2689}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2690}{in} \markbox{m2691}{$X$} \markbox{2692}{separating} \markbox{m2693}{$a,b$}, \markbox{2694}{so} \markbox{2695}{that} \markbox{m2696}{$X = \calX(\calH)$} \markbox{2697}{is} \markbox{2698}{the} \markbox{2699}{dual} \markbox{2700}{cube} \markbox{2701}{complex} \markbox{2702}{to} \markbox{m2703}{$\calH$}.  \markbox{2704}{Recall} \markbox{2705}{that} \markbox{2706}{we} \markbox{2707}{can} \markbox{2708}{think} \markbox{2709}{of} \markbox{2710}{vertices} \markbox{2711}{of} \markbox{m2712}{$X$} \markbox{2713}{as} \markbox{2714}{coherent} \markbox{2715}{orientations} \markbox{2716}{on} \markbox{2717}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2718}{in} \markbox{m2719}{$\calH$}.

\begin{definition}
Let \markbox{m2720}{$p \in X^0$}.  \markbox{2721}{A} \markbox{2722}{hyperplane} \markbox{m2723}{$\hh \in \calH$} \markbox{2724}{is} \markbox{2725}{\emph{transitional}}, \markbox{2726}{denoted} \markbox{m2727}{$\hh \in T(p,\calH)$}, if
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m2728}{$\hh$} \markbox{2729}{separates} \markbox{m2730}{$p$} \markbox{2731}{from} \markbox{m2732}{$b$}, and
\item {} \markbox{m2733}{$p$} \markbox{2734}{is} \markbox{2735}{\emph{adjacent}} \markbox{2736}{to} \markbox{m2737}{$\hh$}, \markbox{2738}{i.e.} \markbox{m2739}{$\hh$} \markbox{2740}{crosses} \markbox{2741}{some} \markbox{2742}{cube} \markbox{2743}{of} \markbox{2744}{which} \markbox{m2745}{$p$} \markbox{2746}{is} \markbox{2747}{a} vertex.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

We \markbox{2748}{note} \markbox{2749}{that} \markbox{2750}{there} \markbox{2751}{is} \markbox{2752}{a} \markbox{2753}{natural} \markbox{2754}{partial} \markbox{2755}{order} \markbox{m2756}{$\prec$} \markbox{2757}{on} \markbox{m2758}{$\calH$}, \markbox{2759}{where} \markbox{m2760}{$\hh \prec \hh'$} \markbox{2761}{when} \markbox{m2762}{$\hh$} \markbox{2763}{separates} \markbox{m2764}{$\hh'$} \markbox{2765}{from} \markbox{m2766}{$a$}, \markbox{2767}{or} \markbox{2768}{equivalently} \markbox{m2769}{$\hh'$} \markbox{2770}{separates} \markbox{m2771}{$\hh$} \markbox{2772}{from} \markbox{m2773}{$b$}.  \markbox{2774}{In} \markbox{2775}{our} \markbox{2776}{special} \markbox{2777}{setting} \markbox{2778}{with} \markbox{m2779}{$X = \hull_X(a,b)$}, \markbox{2780}{every} \markbox{2781}{vertex} \markbox{m2782}{$p \in X^0$} \markbox{2783}{occurs} \markbox{2784}{on} \markbox{2785}{some} \markbox{m2786}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic \markbox{2787}{from} \markbox{m2788}{$a$} \markbox{2789}{to} \markbox{m2790}{$b$}.  \markbox{2791}{The} \markbox{2792}{property} \markbox{2793}{of} \markbox{2794}{transitionality} \markbox{2795}{for} \markbox{m2796}{$\hh \in T(p,\calH)$} \markbox{2797}{is} \markbox{2798}{encoding} \markbox{2799}{that} \markbox{m2800}{$\hh$} \markbox{2801}{is} \markbox{2802}{minimal} \markbox{2803}{in} \markbox{2804}{the} \markbox{2805}{partial} \markbox{2806}{order} \markbox{2807}{on} \markbox{m2808}{$\calH(p,b) \subset \calH$}.

The \markbox{2809}{following} \markbox{2810}{lemma} \markbox{2811}{says} \markbox{2812}{that} \markbox{2813}{minimal} \markbox{2814}{elements} \markbox{2815}{in} \markbox{2816}{the} \markbox{2817}{partial} \markbox{2818}{order} \markbox{2819}{must} cross:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:trans cross}
If \markbox{m2820}{$\hh_1,\hh_2 \in T(p,\calH)$}, \markbox{2821}{then} \markbox{m2822}{$\hh_1$} \markbox{2823}{crosses} \markbox{m2824}{$\hh_2$}.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}
If \markbox{m2825}{$\hh_1$} \markbox{2826}{and} \markbox{m2827}{$\hh_2$} \markbox{2828}{do} \markbox{2829}{not} \markbox{2830}{cross,} \markbox{2831}{then,} \markbox{2832}{without} \markbox{2833}{loss} \markbox{2834}{of} \markbox{2835}{generality,} \markbox{2836}{there} \markbox{2837}{is} \markbox{2838}{a} \markbox{2839}{half-space} \markbox{2840}{of} \markbox{m2841}{$\hh_2$} \markbox{2842}{containing} \markbox{m2843}{$a, \hh_1$}.  \markbox{2844}{On} \markbox{2845}{the} \markbox{2846}{other} \markbox{2847}{hand,} \markbox{m2848}{$p$} \markbox{2849}{is} \markbox{2850}{adjacent} \markbox{2851}{to} \markbox{m2852}{$\hh_2$}.  \markbox{2853}{This} \markbox{2854}{implies} \markbox{2855}{that} \markbox{m2856}{$p,a$} \markbox{2857}{are} \markbox{2858}{in} \markbox{2859}{different} \markbox{2860}{half-spaces} \markbox{2861}{of} \markbox{m2862}{$\hh_1$}, \markbox{2863}{which} \markbox{2864}{is} \markbox{2865}{a} contradiction.
\end{proof}

With \markbox{2866}{this} \markbox{2867}{lemma,} \markbox{2868}{we} \markbox{2869}{can} \markbox{2870}{define} \markbox{2871}{our} \markbox{2872}{\emph{Niblo--Reeves}} \markbox{2873}{paths} \markbox{m2874}{$p_0=a, p_1, \dots, p_n = b$} \markbox{2875}{as} \markbox{2876}{follows} \cite{NibloReeves}:

\begin{itemize}
\item {} Let \markbox{m2877}{$p_0 = a$}.
\item {} By \markbox{2878}{Lemma} \ref{lem:trans cross}, \markbox{m2879}{$p_0$} \markbox{2880}{is} \markbox{2881}{the} \markbox{2882}{corner} \markbox{2883}{of} \markbox{2884}{a} \markbox{2885}{unique} \markbox{2886}{cube} \markbox{m2887}{$C_0$} \markbox{2888}{for} \markbox{2889}{which} \markbox{2890}{the} \markbox{2891}{set} \markbox{2892}{of} \markbox{2893}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2894}{that} \markbox{2895}{cross} \markbox{m2896}{$C_0$} \markbox{2897}{is} \markbox{2898}{precisely} \markbox{m2899}{$T(p,\calH)$}.  \markbox{2900}{Set} \markbox{m2901}{$p_1$} \markbox{2902}{to} \markbox{2903}{be} \markbox{2904}{the} \markbox{2905}{diagonally} \markbox{2906}{opposite} \markbox{2907}{corner} \markbox{2908}{of} \markbox{m2909}{$C_0$}.  \markbox{2910}{Equivalently,} \markbox{m2911}{$p_1$} \markbox{2912}{is} \markbox{2913}{obtained} \markbox{2914}{from} \markbox{m2915}{$p_0$} \markbox{2916}{by} \markbox{2917}{flipping} \markbox{2918}{orientations} \markbox{2919}{on} \markbox{2920}{the} \markbox{2921}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2922}{in} \markbox{m2923}{$T(p,\calH)$}.
\item {} Define \markbox{m2924}{$p_i$} \markbox{2925}{for} \markbox{m2926}{$i \geq 1$} \markbox{2927}{recursively} \markbox{2928}{with} \markbox{m2929}{$p_i$} \markbox{2930}{in} \markbox{2931}{place} \markbox{2932}{of} \markbox{m2933}{$p_0$}.
\end{itemize}



Thus, \markbox{2934}{at} \markbox{2935}{each} \markbox{2936}{step} \markbox{m2937}{$p_i \mapsto p_{i+1}$}, \markbox{2938}{the} \markbox{2939}{path} \markbox{2940}{crosses} \markbox{2941}{the} \markbox{2942}{set} \markbox{2943}{of} \markbox{m2944}{$\prec$}-minimal \markbox{2945}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2946}{in} \markbox{m2947}{$\calH(p_i,b)$}.  \markbox{2948}{The} \markbox{2949}{following} \markbox{2950}{proposition} \markbox{2951}{states} \markbox{2952}{the} \markbox{2953}{basic} \markbox{2954}{properties} \markbox{2955}{of} \markbox{2956}{the} \markbox{2957}{Niblo--Reeves} paths:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:NR basics}
Continuing \markbox{2958}{with} \markbox{2959}{the} \markbox{2960}{above} \markbox{2961}{notation,} \markbox{2962}{the} \markbox{2963}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} There \markbox{2964}{exists} \markbox{2965}{some} \markbox{m2966}{$n$} \markbox{2967}{so} \markbox{2968}{that} \markbox{m2969}{$p_n=b$}.
\item {} For \markbox{2970}{all} \markbox{m2971}{$0 \leq i \leq n$}, \markbox{2972}{we} \markbox{2973}{have} \markbox{m2974}{$d^{\infty}_X(p_{i}, p_{i+1}) =1$}.
\item {} Any \markbox{2975}{path} \markbox{2976}{obtained} \markbox{2977}{by} \markbox{2978}{concatenating} \markbox{m2979}{$\ell^1$}-geodesics \markbox{2980}{between} \markbox{m2981}{$p_i, p_{i+1}$} \markbox{2982}{for} \markbox{m2983}{$0 \leq i < n$} \markbox{2984}{is} \markbox{2985}{an} \markbox{m2986}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic.
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
For \markbox{2987}{(1),} \markbox{2988}{observe} \markbox{2989}{that} \markbox{2990}{the} \markbox{2991}{sequence} \markbox{m2992}{$p_i$} \markbox{2993}{only} \markbox{2994}{crosses} \markbox{2995}{hyperplanes} \markbox{2996}{separating} \markbox{m2997}{$a$} \markbox{2998}{from} \markbox{m2999}{$b$}.  \markbox{3000}{Each} \markbox{3001}{step} \markbox{m3002}{$p_i \mapsto p_{i+1}$} \markbox{3003}{of} \markbox{3004}{the} \markbox{3005}{sequence} \markbox{3006}{crosses} \markbox{3007}{the} \markbox{3008}{collection} \markbox{3009}{of} \markbox{m3010}{$\prec$}-minimal \markbox{3011}{hyperplanes} \markbox{3012}{in} \markbox{m3013}{$\calH(p_i, b)\subset \calH$}.  \markbox{3014}{Now} \markbox{3015}{(1)} \markbox{3016}{is} \markbox{3017}{equivalent} \markbox{3018}{to} \markbox{3019}{the} \markbox{3020}{claim} \markbox{3021}{that} \markbox{m3022}{$\calH = \bigcup_i \calH(p_i,b)$}, \markbox{3023}{which} \markbox{3024}{is} \markbox{3025}{to} \markbox{3026}{say} \markbox{3027}{that} \markbox{3028}{this} \markbox{3029}{process} \markbox{3030}{exhausts} \markbox{3031}{the} \markbox{3032}{set} \markbox{3033}{of} \markbox{3034}{hyperplanes} \markbox{3035}{separating} \markbox{m3036}{$a$} \markbox{3037}{and} \markbox{m3038}{$b$}, \markbox{3039}{which} \markbox{3040}{is} \markbox{3041}{clear} \markbox{3042}{because} \markbox{m3043}{$\calH$} \markbox{3044}{is} finite.

Item \markbox{3045}{(2)} \markbox{3046}{is} \markbox{3047}{by} \markbox{3048}{construction,} \markbox{3049}{since} \markbox{m3050}{$p_i$} \markbox{3051}{and} \markbox{m3052}{$p_{i+1}$} \markbox{3053}{are} \markbox{3054}{opposite} \markbox{3055}{corners} \markbox{3056}{of} \markbox{3057}{a} cube.

Finally, \markbox{3058}{item} \markbox{3059}{(3)} \markbox{3060}{follows} \markbox{3061}{from} \markbox{3062}{the} \markbox{3063}{fact} \markbox{3064}{that} \markbox{m3065}{$\calH(p_i, b) \subset \calH(p_{i+1},b)$} \markbox{3066}{with} \markbox{m3067}{$\calH(p_{i+1},b) - \calH(p_i, b) = \calH(p_i,p_{i+1})$}.  \markbox{3068}{Hence} \markbox{3069}{if} \markbox{m3070}{$\hh \in T(p_i,b)$}, \markbox{3071}{then} \markbox{m3072}{$\hh$} \markbox{3073}{does} \markbox{3074}{not} \markbox{3075}{separate} \markbox{m3076}{$p_i$} \markbox{3077}{from} \markbox{m3078}{$p_j$} \markbox{3079}{for} \markbox{m3080}{$j<i$}.  \markbox{3081}{This} \markbox{3082}{says} \markbox{3083}{that} \markbox{3084}{the} \markbox{3085}{sequence} \markbox{m3086}{$\{p_i\}$} \markbox{3087}{does} \markbox{3088}{not} \markbox{3089}{cross} \markbox{3090}{any} \markbox{3091}{hyperplane} \markbox{3092}{twice,} \markbox{3093}{and} \markbox{3094}{it} \markbox{3095}{follows} \markbox{3096}{that} \markbox{3097}{the} \markbox{3098}{concatenation} \markbox{3099}{of} \markbox{3100}{the} \markbox{m3101}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic \markbox{3102}{segments} \markbox{3103}{will} \markbox{3104}{not} \markbox{3105}{either,} \markbox{3106}{making} \markbox{3107}{it} \markbox{3108}{an} \markbox{m3109}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic.
\end{proof}

The \markbox{3110}{following} \markbox{3111}{is} \markbox{3112}{a} \markbox{3113}{useful} \markbox{3114}{observation} \markbox{3115}{about} \markbox{3116}{this} construction:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:NR iso}
Let \markbox{m3117}{$\Phi:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{3118}{be} \markbox{3119}{an} \markbox{3120}{isomorphism} \markbox{3121}{of} \markbox{3122}{cube} \markbox{3123}{complexes.}  \markbox{3124}{If} \markbox{m3125}{$\gamma$} \markbox{3126}{is} \markbox{3127}{the} \markbox{3128}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3129}{path} \markbox{3130}{between} \markbox{m3131}{$a,b \in \calQ^0$}, \markbox{3132}{then} \markbox{m3133}{$\Phi(\gamma)$} \markbox{3134}{is} \markbox{3135}{the} \markbox{3136}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3137}{path} \markbox{3138}{between} \markbox{m3139}{$\Phi(a), \Phi(b) \in \left(\calQ'\right)^{0}$}.
\end{proposition}

We \markbox{3140}{can} \markbox{3141}{now} \markbox{3142}{state} \markbox{3143}{the} \markbox{3144}{main} \markbox{3145}{result} \markbox{3146}{of} \markbox{3147}{this} subsection.

\begin{theorem}[Stable moves]\label{thm:stable moves}
Suppose \markbox{3148}{that} \markbox{m3149}{$\hh \in \calH$} \markbox{3150}{is} \markbox{3151}{hyperplane,} \markbox{3152}{and} \markbox{3153}{let} \markbox{m3154}{$\Delta_{\hh}:\calD(\calH) \to \calD(\calH - \{\hh\})$} \markbox{3155}{denote} \markbox{3156}{the} \markbox{3157}{hyperplane} \markbox{3158}{collapse} \markbox{3159}{map.}  \markbox{3160}{Set} \markbox{m3161}{$\Delta_{\hh}(a) = a'$} \markbox{3162}{and} \markbox{m3163}{$\Delta_{\hh}(b) =b'$}.  \markbox{3164}{Let} \markbox{m3165}{$p_0,\dots,p_n$} \markbox{3166}{denote} \markbox{3167}{the} \markbox{3168}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3169}{path} \markbox{3170}{in} \markbox{m3171}{$X = \calD(\calH)$}  \markbox{3172}{between} \markbox{m3173}{$a,b$} \markbox{3174}{and} \markbox{m3175}{$p'_0, \dots, p'_m$} \markbox{3176}{the} \markbox{3177}{path} \markbox{3178}{between} \markbox{m3179}{$a',b'$} \markbox{3180}{in} \markbox{m3181}{$\calD(\calH- \{\hh\})$}.  \markbox{3182}{Then} \markbox{3183}{the} \markbox{3184}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} We \markbox{3185}{have} \markbox{m3186}{$n \leq m+1$}.
\item {} For \markbox{3187}{all} \markbox{m3188}{$1 \leq i \leq n$}, \markbox{3189}{we} \markbox{3190}{have} \markbox{m3191}{$d^{\infty}_{\calD(\calH - \{\hh\})}(\Delta_{\hh}(p_i), p'_i) \leq 1$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

In \markbox{3192}{other} \markbox{3193}{words,} \markbox{3194}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3195}{paths} \markbox{3196}{are} \markbox{3197}{stable} \markbox{3198}{under} \markbox{3199}{hyperplane} \markbox{3200}{deletion} maps.

The \markbox{3201}{following} \markbox{3202}{notation} \markbox{3203}{will} \markbox{3204}{be} \markbox{3205}{useful} \markbox{3206}{for} us:

\begin{definition}
Let \markbox{m3207}{$\hh' \in \calH$}.  \markbox{3208}{We} \markbox{3209}{set} \markbox{m3210}{$t_{\hh'}(a, \calH)$}, \markbox{3211}{called} \markbox{3212}{the} \markbox{3213}{\emph{transition index}} \markbox{3214}{of} \markbox{m3215}{$\hh'$}, \markbox{3216}{to} \markbox{3217}{be} \markbox{3218}{the} \markbox{3219}{index} \markbox{m3220}{$i$} \markbox{3221}{at} \markbox{3222}{which} \markbox{m3223}{$\hh' \in \calH(p_i, p_{i+1})$}.  \markbox{3224}{Similarly,} \markbox{3225}{if} \markbox{m3226}{$\hh' \in \calH - \{\hh\}$}, \markbox{3227}{we} \markbox{3228}{define} \markbox{m3229}{$t_{\hh'}(a', \calH - \{\hh\})$} \markbox{3230}{to} \markbox{3231}{be} \markbox{3232}{the} \markbox{3233}{index} \markbox{m3234}{$i$} \markbox{3235}{so} \markbox{3236}{that} \markbox{m3237}{$\hh' \in \calH(p'_i, p'_{i+1})$}.
\end{definition} 

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:move control}
If \markbox{m3238}{$\hh' \in \calH - \{\hh\}$}, \markbox{3239}{then} \markbox{m3240}{$t_{\hh'}(a,\calH) = t_{\hh'}(a', \calH - \{\hh\}) + \delta$} \markbox{3241}{for} \markbox{m3242}{$\delta \in \{0,1\}$}.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}
This \markbox{3243}{is} \markbox{3244}{essentially} \cite[Lemma 5.12]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{3245}{though} \markbox{3246}{the} \markbox{3247}{proof} \markbox{3248}{is} \markbox{3249}{basically} \markbox{3250}{immediate} \markbox{3251}{in} \markbox{3252}{our} \markbox{3253}{setting.}  \markbox{3254}{Note} \markbox{3255}{that} \markbox{3256}{the} \markbox{3257}{transition} \markbox{3258}{index} \markbox{m3259}{$t_{\hh} = d_{\infty}(a, \hh) + \frac{1}{2}$}.  \markbox{3260}{Since} \markbox{3261}{the} \markbox{m3262}{$\ell^{\infty}$} \markbox{3263}{distance} \markbox{3264}{between} \markbox{m3265}{$a'$} \markbox{3266}{and} \markbox{m3267}{$\hh'$} \markbox{3268}{measures} \markbox{3269}{the} \markbox{3270}{maximal} \markbox{3271}{length} \markbox{3272}{of} \markbox{3273}{a} \markbox{3274}{chain} \markbox{3275}{of} \markbox{3276}{hyperplanes} \markbox{3277}{separating} \markbox{3278}{them} \markbox{3279}{(plus} \markbox{m3280}{$\frac{1}{2}$}), \markbox{3281}{that} \markbox{3282}{distance} \markbox{3283}{can} \markbox{3284}{be} \markbox{3285}{at} \markbox{3286}{most} \markbox{m3287}{$1$} \markbox{3288}{more} \markbox{3289}{than} \markbox{m3290}{$d_{\infty}(a,\hh)$}.  \markbox{3291}{This} \markbox{3292}{completes} \markbox{3293}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

\begin{proof}[Proof \markbox{3294}{of} \markbox{3295}{the} \markbox{3296}{Stable} \markbox{3297}{Moves} \markbox{3298}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable moves}]
Suppose \markbox{m3299}{$\hh_1, \hh_2$} \markbox{3300}{separate} \markbox{m3301}{$\Delta_{\hh}(p_i)$} \markbox{3302}{and} \markbox{m3303}{$p'_i$} \markbox{3304}{in} \markbox{m3305}{$X' = \calD(\calH - \{\hh\})$} \markbox{3306}{but} \markbox{3307}{do} \markbox{3308}{not} \markbox{3309}{cross,} \markbox{3310}{since} \markbox{3311}{we} \markbox{3312}{are} \markbox{3313}{done} \markbox{3314}{if} \markbox{3315}{all} \markbox{3316}{such} \markbox{3317}{hyperplanes} cross.
