Without \markbox{3318}{loss} \markbox{3319}{of} \markbox{3320}{generality,} \markbox{3321}{we} \markbox{3322}{may} \markbox{3323}{assume} \markbox{3324}{that} \markbox{m3325}{$\hh_1$} \markbox{3326}{separates} \markbox{m3327}{$\Delta_{\hh}(p_i)$} \markbox{3328}{from} \markbox{m3329}{$\hh_2$}.  \markbox{3330}{Let} \markbox{m3331}{$j = t_{\hh_1}(a',\calH - \{\hh\})$}.  \markbox{3332}{Then} \markbox{m3333}{$j < t_{\hh_2}(a',\calH - \{\hh\}) < i$}, \markbox{3334}{with} \markbox{3335}{the} \markbox{3336}{latter} \markbox{3337}{inequality} \markbox{3338}{following} \markbox{3339}{because} \markbox{m3340}{$p'_{i+1}$} \markbox{3341}{has} \markbox{3342}{already} \markbox{3343}{crossed} \markbox{m3344}{$\hh_2$} \markbox{3345}{(and} \markbox{m3346}{$\hh_1$}).  \markbox{3347}{Thus} \markbox{m3348}{$j + 1 < i$}.

But \markbox{3349}{then} \markbox{m3350}{$t_{\hh_1}(a, \calH) \leq t_{\hh_1}(a', \calH - \{\hh\}) + 1 = j+1 < i$}, \markbox{3351}{which} \markbox{3352}{says} \markbox{3353}{that} \markbox{m3354}{$\hh_1$} \markbox{3355}{separates} \markbox{m3356}{$p_i$} \markbox{3357}{from} \markbox{m3358}{$a$}, \markbox{3359}{which} \markbox{3360}{is} \markbox{3361}{a} contradiction.
\end{proof}


\subsection{Bicombings}\label{subsec:semihyp}

Our \markbox{3362}{ultimate} \markbox{3363}{goal} \markbox{3364}{is} \markbox{3365}{to} \markbox{3366}{prove} \markbox{3367}{that} \markbox{3368}{mapping} \markbox{3369}{class} \markbox{3370}{groups} \markbox{3371}{and} Teichm\"uller \markbox{3372}{spaces} \markbox{3373}{admits} \markbox{3374}{bicombings} \markbox{3375}{(Theorem} \ref{thmi:main}).  \markbox{3376}{Roughly,} \markbox{3377}{a} \markbox{3378}{bicombing} \markbox{3379}{on} \markbox{3380}{a} \markbox{3381}{space} \markbox{m3382}{$X$} \markbox{3383}{is} \markbox{3384}{a} \markbox{3385}{family} \markbox{3386}{of} \markbox{3387}{uniform} \markbox{3388}{quasi-geodesic} \markbox{3389}{paths} \markbox{3390}{that} \markbox{3391}{is} \markbox{3392}{transitive} \markbox{3393}{(i.e.,} \markbox{3394}{connects} \markbox{3395}{any} \markbox{3396}{pair} \markbox{3397}{of} \markbox{3398}{points} \markbox{3399}{of} \markbox{m3400}{$X$}), \markbox{3401}{and} \markbox{3402}{for} \markbox{3403}{which} \markbox{3404}{paths} \markbox{3405}{in} \markbox{3406}{the} \markbox{3407}{family} \markbox{3408}{between} \markbox{3409}{pairs} \markbox{3410}{of} \markbox{3411}{endpoints} \markbox{3412}{that} \markbox{3413}{are} \markbox{3414}{close} \markbox{3415}{to} \markbox{3416}{each} \markbox{3417}{other} \markbox{3418}{uniformly} \markbox{3419}{fellow-travel} \markbox{3420}{in} \markbox{3421}{a} \markbox{3422}{parameterized} \markbox{3423}{fashion.}   \markbox{3424}{The} \markbox{3425}{notion} \markbox{3426}{of} \markbox{3427}{bicombing} \markbox{3428}{was} \markbox{3429}{first} \markbox{3430}{introduced} \markbox{3431}{by} \markbox{3432}{Thurston} \markbox{3433}{in} \markbox{3434}{the} \markbox{3435}{context} \markbox{3436}{of} \markbox{3437}{algorithmic} \markbox{3438}{problems} \markbox{3439}{in} \markbox{3440}{groups.}  \markbox{3441}{It} \markbox{3442}{is} \markbox{3443}{a} \markbox{3444}{straightforward} \markbox{3445}{but} \markbox{3446}{informative} \markbox{3447}{exercise} \markbox{3448}{to} \markbox{3449}{prove} \markbox{3450}{that} \markbox{3451}{geodesics} \markbox{3452}{in} \markbox{3453}{hyperbolic} \markbox{3454}{and} \markbox{3455}{CAT(0)} \markbox{3456}{spaces} \markbox{3457}{satisfy} \markbox{3458}{this} \markbox{3459}{property,} \markbox{3460}{and} \markbox{3461}{this} \markbox{3462}{is} \markbox{3463}{precisely} \markbox{3464}{what} \markbox{3465}{the} \markbox{3466}{definition} \markbox{3467}{is} \markbox{3468}{intended} \markbox{3469}{to} generalize.

\smallskip
The \markbox{3470}{following} \markbox{3471}{definition} \markbox{3472}{is} \markbox{3473}{essentially} \markbox{3474}{from} \cite{AB95}, \markbox{3475}{as} \markbox{3476}{restated} \markbox{3477}{in} \cite[Definition 6.4]{DMS_bary}:  

\begin{definition}[Bicombings]\label{defn:bicombing}
A \markbox{3478}{\emph{discrete, bounded, quasi-geodesic bicombing}} \markbox{3479}{of} \markbox{3480}{a} \markbox{3481}{metric} \markbox{3482}{space} \markbox{m3483}{$X$} \markbox{3484}{consists} \markbox{3485}{of} \markbox{3486}{a} \markbox{3487}{family} \markbox{3488}{of} \markbox{3489}{discrete} \markbox{3490}{paths} \markbox{m3491}{$\{\Gamma_{x,y}\}_{x,y \in X}$} \markbox{3492}{and} \markbox{3493}{a} \markbox{3494}{constant} \markbox{m3495}{$\zeta>0$} \markbox{3496}{satisfying} \markbox{3497}{the} following:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{3498}{\emph{Quasi-geodesic}}: \markbox{3499}{For} \markbox{3500}{any} \markbox{m3501}{$x,y \in X$} \markbox{3502}{with} \markbox{m3503}{$d = d_{X}(x,y)$}, \markbox{3504}{there} \markbox{3505}{exists} \markbox{m3506}{$n_{x,y} \leq d\zeta + \zeta$} \markbox{3507}{so} \markbox{3508}{that} \markbox{3509}{the} \markbox{3510}{path} \markbox{m3511}{$\Gamma_{x,y}:\{0, \dots, n_{x,y}\} \rightarrow X$} \markbox{3512}{is} \markbox{3513}{a} \markbox{m3514}{$(\zeta,\zeta)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{3515}{embedding} \markbox{3516}{with} \markbox{m3517}{$\Gamma_{x,y}(0)=x$} \markbox{3518}{and} \markbox{m3519}{$\Gamma_{x,y}(n_{x,y}) = y$}; and
\item {} \markbox{3520}{\emph{Fellow-traveling}}: \markbox{3521}{If} \markbox{m3522}{$x',y' \in X$} \markbox{3523}{and} \markbox{m3524}{$d_X(x,x'), d_X(y,y') \leq 1$}, \markbox{3525}{then} \markbox{3526}{for} \markbox{3527}{all} \markbox{m3528}{$t \in \{0, \dots, \max\{n_{x,y}, n_{x',y'}\}\}$}, \markbox{3529}{we} have
$$d_X(\Gamma_{x,y}(t), \Gamma_{x',y'}(t)) \leq \zeta.$$
\end{enumerate}


For \markbox{3530}{our} \markbox{3531}{purposes,} \markbox{3532}{the} \markbox{3533}{fellow-traveling} \markbox{3534}{condition} \markbox{3535}{in} \markbox{3536}{item} \markbox{3537}{(2)} \markbox{3538}{is} \markbox{3539}{the} \markbox{3540}{key} \markbox{3541}{challenge.}  \markbox{3542}{At} \markbox{3543}{this} \markbox{3544}{point,} \markbox{3545}{there} \markbox{3546}{are} \markbox{3547}{many} \markbox{3548}{constructions} \markbox{3549}{of} \markbox{3550}{uniform} \markbox{3551}{quasigeodesics} \markbox{3552}{in} \markbox{3553}{mapping} \markbox{3554}{class} groups.


\end{definition}

\subsection{Building the bicombing}\label{subsec:building bicombing}

We \markbox{3555}{are} \markbox{3556}{now} \markbox{3557}{ready} \markbox{3558}{to} \markbox{3559}{define} \markbox{3560}{the} \markbox{3561}{bicombing.}  \markbox{3562}{Let} \markbox{m3563}{$X$} \markbox{3564}{be} \markbox{m3565}{$B_0$}-stably \markbox{3566}{wLQC} \markbox{3567}{(Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes}).  \markbox{3568}{For} \markbox{3569}{any} \markbox{m3570}{$a,b \in X$}, \markbox{3571}{let} \markbox{m3572}{$\calQ$} \markbox{3573}{be} \markbox{3574}{a} \markbox{3575}{CAT(0)} \markbox{3576}{cube} \markbox{3577}{complex} \markbox{3578}{provided} \markbox{3579}{by} \markbox{3580}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes} \markbox{3581}{and} \markbox{m3582}{$\ha,\hb\in \calQ$} \markbox{3583}{the} \markbox{3584}{distinguished} \markbox{3585}{vertices} \markbox{3586}{associated} \markbox{3587}{to} \markbox{m3588}{$a,b$}.

We \markbox{3589}{can} \markbox{3590}{define} \markbox{3591}{a} \markbox{3592}{family} \markbox{3593}{of} \markbox{3594}{paths} \markbox{m3595}{$\{\Gamma_{a,b}\}_{a,b \in X}$} \markbox{3596}{by} \markbox{3597}{taking} \markbox{m3598}{$\Gamma_{a,b}$} \markbox{3599}{to} \markbox{3600}{be} \markbox{3601}{the} \markbox{3602}{image} \markbox{3603}{under} \markbox{3604}{the} \markbox{3605}{quasi-isometry} \markbox{m3606}{$\hO:\calQ \to X$} \markbox{3607}{of} \markbox{3608}{the} \markbox{3609}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3610}{path} \markbox{3611}{between} \markbox{m3612}{$\ha,\hb$}.  \markbox{3613}{By} \markbox{3614}{Definition} \ref{defn:lqc pair}, \markbox{3615}{this} \markbox{3616}{is} \markbox{3617}{a} \markbox{3618}{uniform} \markbox{m3619}{$(B_0,B_0)$}-quasi-geodesic \markbox{3620}{between} \markbox{m3621}{$a,b$}.

\begin{theorem}\label{thm:bicombing}
The \markbox{3622}{family} \markbox{3623}{of} \markbox{3624}{paths} \markbox{m3625}{$\{\Gamma_{a,b}\}_{a,b \in X}$} \markbox{3626}{forms} \markbox{3627}{a} \markbox{3628}{discrete} \markbox{3629}{bounded} \markbox{3630}{quasi-geodesic} \markbox{3631}{bicombing} \markbox{3632}{on} \markbox{m3633}{$X$}.
\end{theorem}

\begin{figure}
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=.8\textwidth]{figures/bicombing_example.pdf}
    \caption{Stable Moves: A simple example of how Niblo--Reeves paths behave under hyperplane collapses.  In each cube complex, the red vertices correspond to $a,b$.  The orange hyperplanes are collapsed when passing to $\calQ_0 = \calQ'_0$.  The Niblo--Reeves path in $\calQ_0$ between $a,b$ travels in a straight line between the red vertices.  The Niblo--Reeves paths in $\calQ$ (blue) and $\calQ'$ (purple) descend to paths which are close to it the Niblo--Reeves path in $\calQ_0$, and hence close to each other.  This example is a modified version of \cite[Figure 25]{DMS_bary}.}
    \label{fig:bicoming_example}
\end{figure}


\begin{proof}
We \markbox{3634}{need} \markbox{3635}{to} \markbox{3636}{confirm} \markbox{3637}{the} \markbox{3638}{properties} \markbox{3639}{in} \markbox{3640}{Definition} \ref{defn:bicombing}.  \markbox{3641}{The} \markbox{3642}{paths} \markbox{3643}{are} \markbox{3644}{clearly} \markbox{3645}{discrete} \markbox{3646}{and} \markbox{3647}{are} \markbox{m3648}{$(B_0,B_0)$}-quasi-geodesics \markbox{3649}{by} \markbox{3650}{assumption.}  \markbox{3651}{So} \markbox{3652}{we} \markbox{3653}{need} \markbox{3654}{to} \markbox{3655}{show} \markbox{3656}{that} \markbox{3657}{they} \markbox{3658}{satisfy} \markbox{3659}{the} \markbox{3660}{fellow-traveling} \markbox{3661}{property} \markbox{3662}{in} \markbox{3663}{item} \markbox{3664}{(2)} \markbox{3665}{of} \markbox{3666}{that} \markbox{3667}{definition.}  \markbox{3668}{This} \markbox{3669}{is} \markbox{3670}{a} \markbox{3671}{direct} \markbox{3672}{application} \markbox{3673}{of} \markbox{3674}{the} \markbox{3675}{properties} \markbox{3676}{in} \markbox{3677}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes} \markbox{3678}{and} \markbox{3679}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable moves}.

Let \markbox{m3680}{$\ha,\hb \in \calQ$} \markbox{3681}{and} \markbox{m3682}{$\ha_0,\hb_0 \in \calQ_0$} \markbox{3683}{be} \markbox{3684}{the} \markbox{3685}{distinguished} \markbox{3686}{vertices} \markbox{3687}{associated} \markbox{3688}{to} \markbox{m3689}{$a,b$}, \markbox{3690}{and} \markbox{3691}{the} \markbox{3692}{same} \markbox{3693}{for} \markbox{m3694}{$\ha',\hb' \in \calQ'$} \markbox{3695}{and} \markbox{m3696}{$\ha'_0,\hb'_0 \in \calQ'_0$} \markbox{3697}{with} \markbox{m3698}{$a',b'$}, \markbox{3699}{respectively.}  \markbox{3700}{Note} \markbox{3701}{that} \markbox{m3702}{$\Delta_0(\ha) = \ha_0$}, \markbox{3703}{etc,} \markbox{3704}{by} \markbox{3705}{item} \markbox{3706}{(4)} \markbox{3707}{of} \markbox{3708}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes}.  \markbox{3709}{Let} \markbox{m3710}{$\Lambda, \Lambda_0, \Lambda',\Lambda'_0$} \markbox{3711}{be} \markbox{3712}{the} \markbox{3713}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3714}{paths} \markbox{3715}{in} \markbox{m3716}{$\calQ,\calQ_0,\calQ',\calQ'_0$} \markbox{3717}{connecting} \markbox{3718}{the} \markbox{3719}{respective} \markbox{3720}{pairs} \markbox{m3721}{$(\ha,\hb), (\ha_0,\hb_0), (\ha',\hb'), (\ha'_0,\hb'_0)$} \markbox{3722}{in} \markbox{3723}{their} \markbox{3724}{respective} \markbox{3725}{cube} \markbox{3726}{complexes} \markbox{m3727}{$\calQ,\calQ_0,\calQ',\calQ'_0$}.  \markbox{3728}{So} \markbox{3729}{in} \markbox{3730}{our} \markbox{3731}{notation,} \markbox{m3732}{$\Gamma_{a,b} = \hO(\Lambda)$} \markbox{3733}{and} \markbox{m3734}{$\Gamma_{a',b'} = \hO'(\Lambda')$}.  \markbox{3735}{We} \markbox{3736}{have} \markbox{3737}{the} \markbox{3738}{following} estimate
\begin{eqnarray}
d_X(\Gamma_{a,b}(i), \Gamma_{a',b'}(i)) &=& d_X(\hO(\Lambda(i)), \hO'(\Lambda'(i)))\\
&\leq& d_X(\hO_0 \circ \Delta_0(\Lambda(i)), \hO'_0 \circ \Delta'_0 (\Lambda'(i))) + 2B_0\\
&\leq& d_X(\hO_0(\Lambda_0(i)), \hO'_0(\Lambda'_0(i))) + 4B_0\\
&\leq& d_X(\hO'_0 \circ I_0(\Lambda_0(i)), \hO'_0(\Lambda'_0(i))) + 5B_0\\
&=& d_X(\hO'_0(\Lambda'_0(i)), \hO'_0(\Lambda'_0(i)))\\
&=& 5B_0.
\end{eqnarray}
In \markbox{3739}{the} \markbox{3740}{above,} \markbox{3741}{(3)} \markbox{3742}{follows} \markbox{3743}{from} \markbox{3744}{commutativity} \markbox{3745}{of} \markbox{3746}{the} \markbox{3747}{top} \markbox{3748}{and} \markbox{3749}{bottom} \markbox{3750}{triangles} \markbox{3751}{in} \markbox{3752}{diagram} \ref{Phi diagram, early}, \markbox{3753}{(4)} \markbox{3754}{follows} \markbox{3755}{from} \markbox{3756}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable moves}, \markbox{3757}{(5)} \markbox{3758}{follows} \markbox{3759}{from} \markbox{3760}{commutativity} \markbox{3761}{the} \markbox{3762}{middle} \markbox{3763}{triangle} \markbox{3764}{of} \markbox{3765}{diagram} \ref{Phi diagram, early}, \markbox{3766}{and} \markbox{3767}{(6)} \markbox{3768}{follows} \markbox{3769}{from} \markbox{3770}{the} \markbox{3771}{fact} \markbox{3772}{that} \markbox{3773}{the} \markbox{3774}{cubical} \markbox{3775}{isomorphism} \markbox{m3776}{$I_0:\calQ_0 \to \calQ'_0$} \markbox{3777}{identifies} \markbox{3778}{the} \markbox{3779}{paths} \markbox{m3780}{$\Lambda_0$} \markbox{3781}{and} \markbox{m3782}{$\Lambda'_0$}, \markbox{3783}{i.e.} \markbox{m3784}{$\Lambda_0(i) = \Lambda'_0(i)$} \markbox{3785}{for} \markbox{3786}{each} \markbox{m3787}{$i$} \markbox{3788}{(Proposition} \ref{prop:NR iso}).  \markbox{3789}{This} \markbox{3790}{completes} \markbox{3791}{the} proof.


\end{proof}

With \markbox{3792}{this} \markbox{3793}{in} \markbox{3794}{hand,} \markbox{3795}{we} \markbox{3796}{can} \markbox{3797}{prove} \markbox{3798}{our} \markbox{3799}{bicombing} result:

\begin{proof}[Proof \markbox{3800}{of} \markbox{3801}{Corollary} \ref{cori:semihyp}]
Mapping \markbox{3802}{class} \markbox{3803}{groups} \markbox{3804}{and} Teichm\"uller \markbox{3805}{spaces} \markbox{3806}{of} \markbox{3807}{finite} \markbox{3808}{type} \markbox{3809}{surfaces} \markbox{3810}{are} \markbox{3811}{colorable} \markbox{3812}{HHSes} \markbox{3813}{(see} \markbox{3814}{Section} \ref{sec:HHS} \markbox{3815}{for} \markbox{3816}{references),} \markbox{3817}{so} \markbox{3818}{they} \markbox{3819}{are} \markbox{3820}{stably} \markbox{3821}{weakly} \markbox{3822}{locally} \markbox{3823}{quasi-cubical} \markbox{3824}{by} \markbox{3825}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}.  \markbox{3826}{Hence} \markbox{3827}{Theorem} \ref{thm:bicombing} \markbox{3828}{provides} \markbox{3829}{a} \markbox{3830}{bicombing} \markbox{3831}{by} \markbox{3832}{pushing} \markbox{3833}{forward} \markbox{3834}{the} \markbox{3835}{Niblo--Reeves} \markbox{3836}{path} \markbox{3837}{in} \markbox{3838}{an} \markbox{3839}{appropriate} \markbox{3840}{cubical} \markbox{3841}{model} \markbox{3842}{to} \markbox{3843}{the} \markbox{3844}{respective} \markbox{3845}{space.}  \markbox{3846}{Any} \markbox{3847}{such} \markbox{m3848}{$\ell^{\infty}$}-geodesic \markbox{3849}{can} \markbox{3850}{be} \markbox{3851}{completed} \markbox{3852}{to} \markbox{3853}{an} \markbox{m3854}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic \markbox{3855}{by} \markbox{3856}{connecting} \markbox{3857}{vertices} \markbox{3858}{via} \markbox{m3859}{$\ell^1$}-geodesic \markbox{3860}{segments} \markbox{3861}{as} \markbox{3862}{in} \markbox{3863}{Proposition} \ref{prop:NR basics}.  \markbox{3864}{But} \markbox{3865}{now} \markbox{3866}{Proposition} \ref{prop:cubical hp} \markbox{3867}{says} \markbox{3868}{that} \markbox{3869}{the} \markbox{3870}{images} \markbox{3871}{of} \markbox{3872}{these} \markbox{3873}{paths} \markbox{3874}{are} \markbox{3875}{hierarchy} \markbox{3876}{paths} \markbox{3877}{(Definition} \ref{defn:hp}).  \markbox{3878}{This} \markbox{3879}{completes} \markbox{3880}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}\label{rem:no medians}
A \markbox{3881}{reader} \markbox{3882}{familiar} \markbox{3883}{with} \markbox{3884}{both} \cite{HHS_quasi} \markbox{3885}{and} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{3886}{will} \markbox{3887}{note} \markbox{3888}{that} \markbox{3889}{one} \markbox{3890}{usually} \markbox{3891}{uses} \markbox{3892}{the} \markbox{3893}{fact} \markbox{3894}{that} \markbox{3895}{the} \markbox{3896}{cubical} \markbox{3897}{model} \markbox{3898}{maps} \markbox{3899}{are} \markbox{3900}{\emph{quasi-median}} \markbox{3901}{maps} \markbox{3902}{to} \markbox{3903}{get} \markbox{3904}{this} \markbox{3905}{last} \markbox{3906}{hierarchy} \markbox{3907}{path} \markbox{3908}{property.}  \markbox{3909}{However,} \markbox{3910}{we} \markbox{3911}{have} \markbox{3912}{avoided} \markbox{3913}{discussions} \markbox{3914}{of} \markbox{3915}{median} \markbox{3916}{structures} \markbox{3917}{in} \markbox{3918}{this} \markbox{3919}{paper} \markbox{3920}{because} \markbox{3921}{they} \markbox{3922}{are} \markbox{3923}{unnecessary} \markbox{3924}{for} \markbox{3925}{our} \markbox{3926}{purposes.}  \markbox{3927}{See} \cite[Section 15]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{3928}{for} \markbox{3929}{how} \markbox{3930}{our} \markbox{3931}{cubical} \markbox{3932}{model} \markbox{3933}{construction} \markbox{3934}{works} \markbox{3935}{with} medians.
\end{remark}


\section{A brief primer on HHSes}\label{sec:HHS}

Hierarchically \markbox{3936}{hyperbolic} \markbox{3937}{spaces} \markbox{3938}{were} \markbox{3939}{introduced} \markbox{3940}{by} \markbox{3941}{Behrstock--Hagen--Sisto} \markbox{3942}{in} \cite{HHS_I, HHS_II}, \markbox{3943}{building} \markbox{3944}{off} \markbox{3945}{of} \markbox{3946}{work} \markbox{3947}{of} \markbox{3948}{Masur--Minsky} \cite{MM99,MM00} \markbox{3949}{on} \markbox{3950}{the} \markbox{3951}{mapping} \markbox{3952}{class} \markbox{3953}{group,} \markbox{3954}{among} \markbox{3955}{others} \cite{Brock, Rafi:combo, Rafi:hypteich, Dur:augmented, EMR:rank}.

For \markbox{3956}{our} \markbox{3957}{purposes,} \markbox{3958}{we} \markbox{3959}{will} \markbox{3960}{introduce} \markbox{3961}{the} \markbox{3962}{basic} \markbox{3963}{foundational} \markbox{3964}{concepts} \markbox{3965}{that} \markbox{3966}{we} \markbox{3967}{need.}  \markbox{3968}{It} \markbox{3969}{turns} \markbox{3970}{out} \markbox{3971}{that} \markbox{3972}{the} \markbox{3973}{cubical} \markbox{3974}{model} \markbox{3975}{construction} \markbox{3976}{is} \markbox{3977}{a} \markbox{3978}{foundational-level} \markbox{3979}{construction,} \markbox{3980}{as} \markbox{3981}{one} \markbox{3982}{can} \markbox{3983}{use} \markbox{3984}{it} \markbox{3985}{to} \markbox{3986}{prove} \markbox{3987}{key} \markbox{3988}{facts} \markbox{3989}{like} \markbox{3990}{the} \markbox{3991}{Distance} \markbox{3992}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}; \markbox{3993}{see} \markbox{3994}{Bowditch} \cite{Bowditch_hulls} \markbox{3995}{and} \cite{Dur_infcube}.

The \markbox{3996}{following} \markbox{3997}{is} \markbox{3998}{a} \markbox{3999}{complete} \markbox{4000}{list} \markbox{4001}{(at} \markbox{4002}{the} \markbox{4003}{time} \markbox{4004}{of} \markbox{4005}{writing)} \markbox{4006}{of} \markbox{4007}{the} \markbox{4008}{spaces} \markbox{4009}{known} \markbox{4010}{to} \markbox{4011}{be} \markbox{4012}{hierarchically} \markbox{4013}{hyperbolic.}  \markbox{4014}{With} \markbox{4015}{the} \markbox{4016}{exception} \markbox{4017}{of} \markbox{4018}{some} \markbox{4019}{cubical} \markbox{4020}{examples,} \markbox{4021}{all} \markbox{4022}{of} \markbox{4023}{them} \markbox{4024}{are} \markbox{4025}{colorable} \markbox{4026}{(Definition} \ref{defn:colorable}), \markbox{4027}{and} \markbox{4028}{so} \markbox{4029}{our} \markbox{4030}{main} \markbox{4031}{results} \markbox{4032}{Theorem} \ref{thmi:main} \markbox{4033}{and} \markbox{4034}{Corollary} \ref{cori:semihyp} apply:

\begin{itemize}
\item {} Hyperbolic spaces.
\item {} Mapping \markbox{4035}{class} \markbox{4036}{groups} \cite{MM99, MM00, Aougab_hyp, HHS_I} \markbox{4037}{and} Teichm\"uller \markbox{4038}{spaces,} \markbox{4039}{with} \markbox{4040}{both} \markbox{4041}{the} Teichm\"uller \cite{Rafi:combo, Dur:augmented} \markbox{4042}{and} \markbox{4043}{Weil-Petersson} \markbox{4044}{metrics} \cite{Brock}.
\item {} Many \cite{HS:cubical}, \markbox{4045}{but} \markbox{4046}{not} \markbox{4047}{all} \cite{shepherd2025cubulation}, \markbox{4048}{CAT(0)} \markbox{4049}{cubical} \markbox{4050}{groups,}  \markbox{4051}{including} \markbox{4052}{all} \markbox{4053}{right-angled} \markbox{4054}{Artin} \markbox{4055}{and} \markbox{4056}{Coxeter} \markbox{4057}{groups} \cite{HHS_I}.
\item {} Fundamental \markbox{4058}{groups} \markbox{4059}{of} \markbox{4060}{closed} \markbox{4061}{3-manifolds} \markbox{4062}{without} \markbox{4063}{Nil} \markbox{4064}{or} \markbox{4065}{Sol} \markbox{4066}{summands} \cite{HHS_II, hagen2022equivariant}.
\item {} Quotients \markbox{4067}{of} \markbox{4068}{mapping} \markbox{4069}{class} \markbox{4070}{groups} \markbox{4071}{by} \markbox{4072}{large} \markbox{4073}{powers} \markbox{4074}{of} \markbox{4075}{Dehn} \markbox{4076}{twists} \cite{behrstock2024combinatorial} \markbox{4077}{and} \markbox{4078}{pseudo-Anosovs} \cite{HHS:asdim}.
\item {} Surface \markbox{4079}{group} \markbox{4080}{extensions} \markbox{4081}{of} \markbox{4082}{Veech} \markbox{4083}{groups} \cite{DDLS1, DDLS2, bongiovanni2024extensions} \markbox{4084}{and} \markbox{4085}{multicurve} \markbox{4086}{stabilizers} \cite{russell2021extensions} \markbox{4087}{of} \markbox{4088}{mapping} \markbox{4089}{class} groups.
\item  {} The \markbox{4090}{genus-2} \markbox{4091}{handlebody} \markbox{4092}{group} \cite{chesser2022stable}.
\item {} Artin \markbox{4093}{groups} \markbox{4094}{of} \markbox{4095}{extra-large} \markbox{4096}{type} \cite{MMS:Artin}.
\item {} Many \markbox{4097}{free-by-cyclic} \markbox{4098}{groups} \cite{bongiovanni2025characterizing}.
\item {} Admissible \markbox{4099}{curve} \markbox{4100}{graphs} \cite{calderon2024hierarchical}.
\item {} The \markbox{4101}{class} \markbox{4102}{of} \markbox{4103}{HHSes} \markbox{4104}{is} \markbox{4105}{closed} \markbox{4106}{under} \markbox{4107}{products} \markbox{4108}{and} \markbox{4109}{appropriate} \markbox{4110}{combinations} \cite{HHS_II}, \markbox{4111}{including} \markbox{4112}{graph} \markbox{4113}{products} \cite{BR:graph_prods} \markbox{4114}{and} \markbox{4115}{graph} \markbox{4116}{braid} \markbox{4117}{groups}  \cite{berlyne2021hierarchical}.
\end{itemize}

We \markbox{4118}{note} \markbox{4119}{that} \markbox{4120}{there} \markbox{4121}{are} \markbox{4122}{non-colorable} \markbox{4123}{cubical} \markbox{4124}{HHSes} \cite{Hagen:non-col} \markbox{4125}{and} \markbox{4126}{non-HHS} \markbox{4127}{cubical} \markbox{4128}{groups} \cite{shepherd2025cubulation}.  \markbox{4129}{CAT(0)} \markbox{4130}{cube} \markbox{4131}{complexes} \markbox{4132}{are} \markbox{4133}{obviously} \markbox{4134}{locally} \markbox{4135}{modeled} \markbox{4136}{by} \markbox{4137}{cube} \markbox{4138}{complexes} \markbox{4139}{and,} \markbox{4140}{moreover,} \markbox{4141}{are} \markbox{4142}{bicombable} \cite{NibloReeves}, \markbox{4143}{so} \markbox{4144}{they} \markbox{4145}{are} \markbox{4146}{not} \markbox{4147}{of} \markbox{4148}{interest} \markbox{4149}{in} \markbox{4150}{this} \markbox{4151}{paper} \markbox{4152}{in} \markbox{4153}{any} event.

\subsection{Basic setup of an HHS}\label{subsec:basic HHS}

Roughly, \markbox{4154}{a} \markbox{4155}{\emph{hierarchically hyperbolic}} \markbox{4156}{structure} \markbox{4157}{is} \markbox{4158}{a} \markbox{4159}{pair} \markbox{m4160}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{4161}{where} \markbox{m4162}{$\calX$} \markbox{4163}{is} \markbox{4164}{a} \markbox{4165}{uniformly} \markbox{4166}{quasigeodesic} \markbox{4167}{metric} \markbox{4168}{space} \markbox{4169}{and} \markbox{m4170}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{4171}{is} \markbox{4172}{an} \markbox{4173}{index} \markbox{4174}{set} \markbox{4175}{for} \markbox{4176}{a} \markbox{4177}{family} \markbox{4178}{of} \markbox{4179}{uniformly} \markbox{4180}{hyperbolic} \markbox{4181}{spaces} \markbox{m4182}{$\{\calC(U)\}_{U \in \mathfrak S}$}.  \markbox{4183}{The} \markbox{4184}{ambient} \markbox{4185}{space} \markbox{m4186}{$\calX$} \markbox{4187}{admits} \markbox{4188}{a} \markbox{4189}{family} \markbox{4190}{of} \markbox{4191}{uniformly} \markbox{4192}{coarsely} \markbox{4193}{Lipschitz} \markbox{4194}{projections} \markbox{m4195}{$\pi_U:\calX \to \calC(U)$}, \markbox{4196}{and} \markbox{4197}{those} \markbox{4198}{projections,} \markbox{4199}{along} \markbox{4200}{with} \markbox{4201}{certain} \markbox{4202}{relations} \markbox{4203}{on} \markbox{4204}{the} \markbox{4205}{family} \markbox{m4206}{$\mathfrak S$}, \markbox{4207}{largely} \markbox{4208}{control} \markbox{4209}{the} \markbox{4210}{coarse} \markbox{4211}{geometry} \markbox{4212}{of} \markbox{m4213}{$\calX$}.

The \markbox{4214}{following} \markbox{4215}{extracts} \markbox{4216}{some} \markbox{4217}{of} \markbox{4218}{the} \markbox{4219}{properties} \markbox{4220}{we} \markbox{4221}{need} \markbox{4222}{from} \markbox{4223}{the} \markbox{4224}{axiomatic} \markbox{4225}{setup} \cite{HHS_II}, \markbox{4226}{see} \cite{Sisto_HHS} \markbox{4227}{for} \markbox{4228}{a} discussion.


\begin{enumerate}

\item {} For \markbox{4229}{each} \markbox{m4230}{$U \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4231}{there} \markbox{4232}{exist} \markbox{4233}{an} \markbox{m4234}{$\ES$}-hyperbolic \markbox{4235}{space} \markbox{m4236}{$\calC(U
)$} \markbox{4237}{and} \markbox{4238}{a} \markbox{m4239}{$\ES$}-coarsely \markbox{4240}{surjective} \markbox{m4241}{$(\ES,\ES)$}-coarsely \markbox{4242}{Lipschitz} \markbox{4243}{map} \markbox{m4244}{$\pi_U: \calX \rightarrow \calC(U),$} \markbox{4245}{with} \markbox{m4246}{$\ES$} \markbox{4247}{independent} \markbox{4248}{of} \markbox{m4249}{$U$}.

    \item {} The \markbox{4250}{set} \markbox{m4251}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{4252}{has} \markbox{4253}{the} \markbox{4254}{following} relations:
    \begin{itemize}
        \item {} It \markbox{4255}{is} \markbox{4256}{equipped} \markbox{4257}{with} \markbox{4258}{a} \markbox{4259}{partial} \markbox{4260}{order} \markbox{m4261}{$\nest$} \markbox{4262}{called} \markbox{4263}{\emph{nesting}}. \markbox{4264}{If} \markbox{m4265}{$\mathfrak S \neq \emptyset,$} \markbox{4266}{the} \markbox{4267}{set} \markbox{m4268}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{4269}{contains} \markbox{4270}{a} \markbox{4271}{unique} \markbox{m4272}{$\nest$}-maximal \markbox{4273}{element} \markbox{m4274}{$S.$}
        
        \item {} It \markbox{4275}{has} \markbox{4276}{a} \markbox{4277}{symmetric,} \markbox{4278}{anti-reflexive} \markbox{4279}{relation} \markbox{m4280}{$\perp$} \markbox{4281}{called} \markbox{4282}{\emph{orthogonality}}. \markbox{4283}{If} \markbox{m4284}{$U \nest V$}, \markbox{4285}{then} \markbox{m4286}{$U,V$} \markbox{4287}{are} \markbox{4288}{not} \markbox{4289}{related} \markbox{4290}{via} \markbox{m4291}{$\perp$}. \markbox{4292}{Furthermore,} \markbox{4293}{domains} \markbox{4294}{have} \markbox{4295}{\emph{orthogonal containers}}: \markbox{4296}{if} \markbox{m4297}{$U \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4298}{and} \markbox{4299}{there} \markbox{4300}{is} \markbox{4301}{a} \markbox{4302}{domain} \markbox{4303}{orthogonal} \markbox{4304}{to} \markbox{m4305}{$U$} \markbox{4306}{then} \markbox{4307}{there} \markbox{4308}{is} \markbox{4309}{a} \markbox{4310}{domain} \markbox{m4311}{$W$} \markbox{4312}{such} \markbox{4313}{that} \markbox{m4314}{$V \nest W$} \markbox{4315}{whenever} \markbox{m4316}{$V \perp U.$}
        
        \item {} For \markbox{4317}{any} \markbox{4318}{distinct} \markbox{m4319}{$ U, V \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4320}{unrelated} \markbox{4321}{via} \markbox{m4322}{$\perp, \nest$}, \markbox{4323}{then} \markbox{4324}{we} \markbox{4325}{say} \markbox{m4326}{$U,V$} \markbox{4327}{are} \markbox{4328}{\emph{transverse}} \markbox{4329}{and} \markbox{4330}{write} \markbox{m4331}{$U  \pitchfork V.$} 
     
        \end{itemize}
          
        \item {} There \markbox{4332}{exists} \markbox{4333}{an} \markbox{4334}{integer} \markbox{4335}{called} \markbox{4336}{the} \markbox{4337}{\emph{complexity}} \markbox{4338}{of} \markbox{m4339}{$\calX$} \markbox{4340}{and} \markbox{4341}{denoted} \markbox{m4342}{$\xi(\mathfrak S)$} \markbox{4343}{such} \markbox{4344}{that} \markbox{4345}{whenever} \markbox{m4346}{$U_1,U_2,\cdots U_n$} \markbox{4347}{is} \markbox{4348}{a} \markbox{4349}{collection} \markbox{4350}{of} \markbox{4351}{pairwise} \markbox{4352}{non-transverse} \markbox{4353}{domains,} \markbox{4354}{then} \markbox{m4355}{$n \leq \xi(\mathfrak S).$}
        
        \item {} If \markbox{m4356}{$U  \sqsubset V$} \markbox{4357}{or} \markbox{m4358}{$U  \pitchfork V,$} \markbox{4359}{then} \markbox{4360}{there} \markbox{4361}{exists} \markbox{4362}{a} \markbox{4363}{set} \markbox{m4364}{$\rho^U_V$} \markbox{4365}{of} \markbox{4366}{diameter} \markbox{4367}{at} \markbox{4368}{most} \markbox{m4369}{$\ES$} \markbox{4370}{in} \markbox{m4371}{$\calC(V)$}.
        
        \item {} If \markbox{m4372}{$U  \sqsubset V$}, \markbox{4373}{there} \markbox{4374}{is} \markbox{4375}{a} \markbox{4376}{map} \markbox{m4377}{$\rho^V_U:\calC(V) \rightarrow \calC(U)$}, \markbox{4378}{called} \markbox{4379}{the} \markbox{4380}{\emph{relative projection}} \markbox{4381}{of} \markbox{m4382}{$U$} \markbox{4383}{to} \markbox{m4384}{$V$} \markbox{4385}{which} \markbox{4386}{satisfies} \markbox{4387}{the} \markbox{4388}{following:} \markbox{4389}{For} \markbox{m4390}{$x \in \calX$} \markbox{4391}{with} \markbox{m4392}{$d_{ V}(\pi_V(x),\rho^U_V)>\ES,$} \markbox{4393}{we} \markbox{4394}{have} \markbox{m4395}{$\pi_U(x) \underset{\ES}{\asymp} \rho^V_U(\pi_V(x)).$}

        
        


\end{enumerate}

For \markbox{4396}{two} \markbox{4397}{points} \markbox{m4398}{$x,y \in \calX,$} \markbox{4399}{it} \markbox{4400}{is} \markbox{4401}{standard} \markbox{4402}{to} \markbox{4403}{use} \markbox{m4404}{$d_U(x,y)$} \markbox{4405}{to} \markbox{4406}{denote} \markbox{m4407}{$d_{\calC(U)}(\pi_U(x), \pi_U(y)),$} \markbox{4408}{and} \markbox{4409}{similarly} \markbox{4410}{for} \markbox{4411}{subsets} \markbox{4412}{of} \markbox{m4413}{$\calX.$} \markbox{4414}{For} \markbox{4415}{a} \markbox{4416}{subset} \markbox{m4417}{$A \subseteq \calX,$} \markbox{4418}{we} \markbox{4419}{will} \markbox{4420}{also} \markbox{4421}{use} \markbox{m4422}{$\diam_U(A)$} \markbox{4423}{to} \markbox{4424}{denote} \markbox{4425}{the} \markbox{4426}{diameter} \markbox{4427}{of} \markbox{4428}{the} \markbox{4429}{set} \markbox{m4430}{$\pi_U(A) \subset \calC(U)$}.

\subsection{Basic HHS facts}

We \markbox{4431}{now} \markbox{4432}{collect} \markbox{4433}{some} \markbox{4434}{useful} \markbox{4435}{facts} \markbox{4436}{about} \markbox{4437}{HHSes} \markbox{4438}{from} \markbox{4439}{various} \markbox{4440}{places.} \medskip

The \markbox{4441}{following} \markbox{4442}{definition} \markbox{4443}{from} \cite{Beh:thesis, BKMM:qirigid, HHS_II}, \markbox{4444}{will} \markbox{4445}{be} \markbox{4446}{important} \markbox{4447}{for} \markbox{4448}{us.}  \markbox{4449}{The} \markbox{4450}{idea} \markbox{4451}{here} \markbox{4452}{is} \markbox{4453}{that} \markbox{4454}{we} \markbox{4455}{want} \markbox{4456}{to} \markbox{4457}{combine} \markbox{4458}{all} \markbox{4459}{of} \markbox{4460}{the} \markbox{4461}{projections} \markbox{m4462}{$\pi_U:\calX \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{4463}{for} \markbox{4464}{each} \markbox{m4465}{$U \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4466}{into} \markbox{4467}{a} \markbox{4468}{global} \markbox{4469}{projection} \markbox{m4470}{$\Pi:\calX \to \prod_U \calC(U)$}.  \markbox{4471}{The} \markbox{4472}{following} \markbox{4473}{definition} \markbox{4474}{uses} \markbox{4475}{the} \markbox{4476}{relations} \markbox{4477}{on} \markbox{m4478}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{4479}{to} \markbox{4480}{constrain} \markbox{4481}{tuples} \markbox{4482}{in} \markbox{m4483}{$\prod_U \calC(U)$}.

\begin{definition}[Consistent tuple]\label{defn:consistency}
Let \markbox{m4484}{$\kappa\geq 0$} \markbox{4485}{and} \markbox{4486}{let} \markbox{m4487}{$(b_U)\in\prod_{U\in\mathfrak S}2^{\calC(U)}$} \markbox{4488}{be} \markbox{4489}{a} \markbox{4490}{tuple} \markbox{4491}{such} \markbox{4492}{that} \markbox{4493}{for} \markbox{4494}{each} \markbox{m4495}{$U\in\mathfrak S$}, 
the \markbox{m4496}{$U$}--coordinate  \markbox{m4497}{$b_U$} \markbox{4498}{has} \markbox{4499}{diameter} \markbox{m4500}{$\leq\kappa$}.  \markbox{4501}{Then} \markbox{m4502}{$(b_U)$} \markbox{4503}{is} \markbox{4504}{\textbf{\em $\kappa$--consistent}} \markbox{4505}{if} \markbox{4506}{for} \markbox{4507}{all} 
\markbox{m4508}{$V,W\in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{4509}{we} \markbox{4510}{have} $$\min\{\dist_V(b_V,\rho^W_V),\dist_W(b_W,\rho^V_W)\}\leq\kappa$$ \markbox{4511}{whenever} \markbox{m4512}{$V\pitchfork W$} \markbox{4513}{and} 
$$\min\{\dist_W(x,\rho^V_W),\diam_V(b_V\cup\rho^W_V)\}\leq\kappa$$ \markbox{4514}{whenever} \markbox{m4515}{$V\nest W$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item {} We \markbox{4516}{refer} \markbox{4517}{to} \markbox{4518}{the} \markbox{4519}{above} \markbox{4520}{inequalities} \markbox{4521}{as} \markbox{4522}{the} \markbox{4523}{\emph{consistency inequalities}}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}




\medskip


The \markbox{4524}{following} \markbox{4525}{is} \markbox{4526}{a} \markbox{4527}{key} \markbox{4528}{fact} \markbox{4529}{for} \markbox{4530}{us.}  \markbox{4531}{It} \markbox{4532}{says} \markbox{4533}{that} \markbox{4534}{the} \markbox{4535}{image} \markbox{4536}{of} \markbox{m4537}{$\Pi:\calX \to \prod_U \calC(U)$} \markbox{4538}{consists} \markbox{4539}{of} \markbox{4540}{uniformly} \markbox{4541}{consistent} tuples:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:base consistency}
There \markbox{4542}{exists} \markbox{m4543}{$\theta = \theta(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{4544}{so} \markbox{4545}{that} \markbox{4546}{if} \markbox{m4547}{$x \in \calX$}, \markbox{4548}{then} \markbox{4549}{the} \markbox{4550}{tuple} \markbox{m4551}{$(\pi_U(x)) \in \prod_{U \in \mathfrak S} \calC(U)$} \markbox{4552}{is} \markbox{m4553}{$\theta$}-consistent.
\end{lemma}


On \markbox{4554}{the} \markbox{4555}{other} \markbox{4556}{hand,} \markbox{4557}{we} \markbox{4558}{would} \markbox{4559}{like} \markbox{4560}{to} \markbox{4561}{know} \markbox{4562}{whether} \markbox{4563}{all} \markbox{4564}{consistent} \markbox{4565}{tuples} \markbox{4566}{in} \markbox{m4567}{$\prod_U \calC(U)$} \markbox{4568}{essentially} \markbox{4569}{come} \markbox{4570}{from} \markbox{m4571}{$\calX$}.  \markbox{4572}{That} \markbox{4573}{is} \markbox{4574}{the} \markbox{4575}{content} \markbox{4576}{of} \markbox{4577}{the} \markbox{4578}{following} \markbox{4579}{Realization} \markbox{4580}{Theorem.}  \markbox{4581}{In} \markbox{4582}{particular,} \markbox{4583}{says} \markbox{4584}{that} \markbox{4585}{any} \markbox{4586}{tuple} \markbox{4587}{satisfying} \markbox{4588}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency} \markbox{4589}{can} \markbox{4590}{be} \markbox{4591}{coarsely} \markbox{4592}{realized} \markbox{4593}{via} \markbox{4594}{a} \markbox{4595}{point} \markbox{4596}{in} \markbox{m4597}{$\calX$}.  \markbox{4598}{It} \markbox{4599}{is} \cite[Theorem 4.3]{BKMM:qirigid} \markbox{4600}{for} \markbox{4601}{mapping} \markbox{4602}{class} \markbox{4603}{groups,} \cite[Theorem 3.2]{EMR:rank} \markbox{4604}{for} Teichm\"uller \markbox{4605}{space} \markbox{4606}{with} \markbox{4607}{the} Teichm\"uller \markbox{4608}{metric,} \markbox{4609}{and} \cite[Theorem 3.1]{HHS_II} \markbox{4610}{for} \markbox{4611}{the} \markbox{4612}{general} \markbox{4613}{HHS} case:

\begin{theorem}[Realization]\label{thm:realization}
For \markbox{4614}{each} \markbox{m4615}{$\kappa \geq 1$} \markbox{4616}{there} \markbox{4617}{exists} \markbox{m4618}{$\theta_e, \theta_u \geq 0$} \markbox{4619}{such} \markbox{4620}{that} \markbox{4621}{the} \markbox{4622}{following} \markbox{4623}{holds.}  \markbox{4624}{Let} \markbox{m4625}{$\mathbf{b} = (b_U)_{U \in \mathfrak S} \in \prod_{U \in \mathfrak S} 2^{\calC(U)}$} \markbox{4626}{be} \markbox{m4627}{$\kappa$}-consistent.

Then \markbox{4628}{there} \markbox{4629}{exists} \markbox{m4630}{$x \in X$} \markbox{4631}{so} \markbox{4632}{that} \markbox{m4633}{$d_U(b_U, \pi_W(x)) \leq \theta_e$} \markbox{4634}{for} \markbox{4635}{all} \markbox{m4636}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{4637}{Moreover,} \markbox{m4638}{$x$} \markbox{4639}{is} \markbox{4640}{\emph{coarsely unique}} \markbox{4641}{in} \markbox{4642}{the} \markbox{4643}{sense} \markbox{4644}{that} 
$$\diam_{\calX} \{x \in \calX| d_W(b_W, \pi_W(x)) \leq \theta_e \textrm{ for all } U \in \mathfrak S\} < \theta_u.$$
\end{theorem}

\begin{remark}
Notably, \markbox{4645}{the} \markbox{4646}{proof} \markbox{4647}{of} \markbox{4648}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization} \markbox{4649}{in} \cite{HHS_II} \markbox{4650}{does} \markbox{4651}{not} \markbox{4652}{involve} \markbox{4653}{the} \markbox{4654}{hyperbolicity} \markbox{4655}{of} \markbox{4656}{the} \markbox{4657}{associated} \markbox{4658}{spaces} \markbox{m4659}{$\{\calC(U)\}_{U \in \mathfrak S}$}, \markbox{4660}{and} \markbox{4661}{actually} \markbox{4662}{follows} \markbox{4663}{from} \markbox{4664}{a} \markbox{4665}{weak} \markbox{4666}{form} \markbox{4667}{which} \markbox{4668}{is} \markbox{4669}{axiomatized} \markbox{4670}{into} \markbox{4671}{the} \markbox{4672}{HHS} \markbox{4673}{setup.}  \markbox{4674}{In} \markbox{4675}{this} \markbox{4676}{sense,} \markbox{4677}{realization} \markbox{4678}{is} \markbox{4679}{a} \markbox{4680}{purely} \markbox{4681}{hierarchical} \markbox{4682}{fact} \markbox{4683}{which} \markbox{4684}{plays} \markbox{4685}{a} \markbox{4686}{similar} \markbox{4687}{role} \markbox{4688}{to} \markbox{4689}{the} \markbox{4690}{existence} \markbox{4691}{of} \markbox{4692}{a} \markbox{4693}{coarse} \markbox{4694}{median} \markbox{4695}{in} \markbox{4696}{Bowditch's} \markbox{4697}{analysis} \cite{Bowditch_hulls}.


\end{remark}

Perhaps \markbox{4698}{the} \markbox{4699}{main} \markbox{4700}{technique} \markbox{4701}{in} \markbox{4702}{HHSes} \markbox{4703}{is} \markbox{4704}{taking} \markbox{4705}{an} \markbox{4706}{object} \markbox{4707}{in} \markbox{4708}{the} \markbox{4709}{ambient} \markbox{4710}{space} \markbox{m4711}{$\calX$} \markbox{4712}{and} \markbox{4713}{projecting} \markbox{4714}{it} \markbox{4715}{to} \markbox{4716}{all} \markbox{4717}{of} \markbox{4718}{the} \markbox{4719}{hyperbolic} \markbox{4720}{spaces,} \markbox{4721}{doing} \markbox{4722}{hyperbolic} \markbox{4723}{geometry,} \markbox{4724}{and} \markbox{4725}{then} \markbox{4726}{reassembling} \markbox{4727}{the} \markbox{4728}{pieces} \markbox{4729}{via} \markbox{4730}{hierarchical} \markbox{4731}{tools} \markbox{4732}{like} \markbox{4733}{the} \markbox{4734}{Realization} \markbox{4735}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization}.  \markbox{4736}{Toward} \markbox{4737}{that} \markbox{4738}{end,} \markbox{4739}{and} \markbox{4740}{recognizing} \markbox{4741}{that} \markbox{4742}{HHSes} \markbox{4743}{are} \markbox{4744}{fundamentally} \markbox{4745}{coarse} \markbox{4746}{spaces,} \markbox{4747}{we} \markbox{4748}{will} \markbox{4749}{usually} \markbox{4750}{want} \markbox{4751}{to} \markbox{4752}{restrict} \markbox{4753}{ourselves} \markbox{4754}{to} \markbox{4755}{the} \markbox{4756}{\emph{relevant}} \markbox{4757}{collection} \markbox{4758}{of} \markbox{4759}{hyperbolic} \markbox{4760}{spaces} \markbox{4761}{to} \markbox{4762}{which} \markbox{4763}{an} \markbox{4764}{object} \markbox{4765}{has} \markbox{4766}{a} \markbox{4767}{sufficiently} \markbox{4768}{large} projection.

\begin{definition}[Relevant domains] \label{defn:relevant}
Given \markbox{4769}{a} \markbox{4770}{subset} \markbox{m4771}{$A \subset \calX$} \markbox{4772}{and} \markbox{m4773}{$K > 0$}, \markbox{4774}{we} \markbox{4775}{say} \markbox{4776}{that} \markbox{m4777}{$U \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4778}{is} \markbox{m4779}{$K$}-\markbox{4780}{\emph{relevant}} \markbox{4781}{for} \markbox{m4782}{$A$} \markbox{4783}{if} \markbox{m4784}{$\diam_U(A) \geq K$}.  \markbox{4785}{We} \markbox{4786}{denote} \markbox{4787}{the} \markbox{4788}{set} \markbox{4789}{of} \markbox{m4790}{$K$}-relevant \markbox{4791}{domains} \markbox{4792}{for} \markbox{m4793}{$A$} \markbox{4794}{by} \markbox{m4795}{$\Rel_K(A)$}.
\end{definition}


The \markbox{4796}{following} \markbox{4797}{Passing-Up} \markbox{4798}{lemma} \markbox{4799}{is} \markbox{4800}{a} \markbox{4801}{foundational} \markbox{4802}{fact} \markbox{4803}{about} \markbox{4804}{HHSes;} \markbox{4805}{in} \markbox{4806}{fact,} \markbox{4807}{it} \markbox{4808}{can} \markbox{4809}{be} \markbox{4810}{taken} \markbox{4811}{to} \markbox{4812}{be} \markbox{4813}{an} \markbox{4814}{axiom} \cite[Proposition 4.15]{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{4815}{Roughly} \markbox{4816}{speaking,} \markbox{4817}{the} \markbox{4818}{passing-up} \markbox{4819}{lemma} \markbox{4820}{says} \markbox{4821}{that} \markbox{4822}{if} \markbox{m4823}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{4824}{have} \markbox{4825}{a} \markbox{4826}{large} \markbox{4827}{number} \markbox{4828}{of} \markbox{4829}{lower} \markbox{4830}{complexity} \markbox{4831}{relevant} \markbox{4832}{domains,} \markbox{4833}{then} \markbox{4834}{there} \markbox{4835}{must} \markbox{4836}{be} \markbox{4837}{some} \markbox{4838}{higher} \markbox{4839}{complexity} \markbox{4840}{relevant} \markbox{4841}{domain} \markbox{4842}{containing} \markbox{4843}{at} \markbox{4844}{least} \markbox{4845}{one} \markbox{4846}{of} \markbox{4847}{them,} \markbox{4848}{thereby} \markbox{4849}{allowing} \markbox{4850}{us} \markbox{4851}{to} \markbox{4852}{``pass} \markbox{4853}{up''} \markbox{4854}{the} \markbox{m4855}{$\nest$}-lattice.

\begin{lemma}[Passing-up]\label{lem:passing-up}
Let \markbox{m4856}{$\calX$} \markbox{4857}{be} \markbox{4858}{an} \markbox{4859}{HHS} \markbox{4860}{with} \markbox{4861}{constant} \markbox{m4862}{$\ES$}.  \markbox{4863}{For} \markbox{4864}{every} \markbox{m4865}{$D>0$} \markbox{4866}{there} \markbox{4867}{is} \markbox{4868}{an} \markbox{4869}{integer} \markbox{m4870}{$PU=PU(D)>0$} \markbox{4871}{such} \markbox{4872}{that} \markbox{4873}{if} \markbox{m4874}{$V \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4875}{and} \markbox{m4876}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{4877}{satisfy} \markbox{m4878}{$d_{U_i}(x,y)>\ES$} \markbox{4879}{for} \markbox{4880}{a} \markbox{4881}{collection} \markbox{4882}{of} \markbox{4883}{domains} \markbox{m4884}{$\{U_i\}_{i=1}^{PU}$} \markbox{4885}{with} \markbox{4886}{each} \markbox{m4887}{$U_i \in \mathfrak S_V$}, \markbox{4888}{then} \markbox{4889}{there} \markbox{4890}{exists} \markbox{m4891}{$W \in \mathfrak S_V$} \markbox{4892}{and} \markbox{m4893}{$i$} \markbox{4894}{with} \markbox{m4895}{$U_i \sqsubsetneq W$} \markbox{4896}{such} \markbox{4897}{that} \markbox{m4898}{$d_W(x,y)>D.$}
\end{lemma}

As \markbox{4899}{an} \markbox{4900}{example} \markbox{4901}{of} \markbox{4902}{how} \markbox{4903}{this} \markbox{4904}{lemma} \markbox{4905}{is} \markbox{4906}{foundational,} \markbox{4907}{we} \markbox{4908}{observe} \markbox{4909}{the} \markbox{4910}{following} \markbox{4911}{corollary.}  \markbox{4912}{The} \markbox{4913}{original} \markbox{4914}{proof} \markbox{4915}{is} \markbox{4916}{embedded} \markbox{4917}{in} \markbox{4918}{the} \markbox{4919}{proof} \markbox{4920}{of} \markbox{4921}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization} \markbox{4922}{in} \cite[Theorem 3.1]{HHS_II}, \markbox{4923}{but} \markbox{4924}{not} \markbox{4925}{explicitly} \markbox{4926}{stated.}  \markbox{4927}{We} \markbox{4928}{give} \markbox{4929}{a} \markbox{4930}{proof} \markbox{4931}{for} completeness:

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:rel sets are finite}
For \markbox{4932}{any} \markbox{m4933}{$x,y \in \calX$}, \markbox{4934}{the} \markbox{4935}{set} \markbox{m4936}{$\Rel_{\ES}(x,y)$} \markbox{4937}{is} finite.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Let \markbox{m4938}{$C$} \markbox{4939}{be} \markbox{4940}{the} \markbox{4941}{coarse} \markbox{4942}{Lipschitz} \markbox{4943}{constant} \markbox{4944}{for} \markbox{4945}{all} \markbox{4946}{of} \markbox{4947}{the} \markbox{4948}{projections} \markbox{m4949}{$\pi_U$} \markbox{4950}{for} \markbox{m4951}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{4952}{and} \markbox{4953}{set} \markbox{m4954}{$D > C d_{\calX}(x,y) + C$}.  \markbox{4955}{If} \markbox{m4956}{$\# \Rel_{\ES}(x,y) > P(D)$}, \markbox{4957}{then} \markbox{4958}{the} \markbox{4959}{Passing-Up} \markbox{4960}{Lemma} \ref{lem:passing-up} \markbox{4961}{provides} \markbox{4962}{a} \markbox{4963}{domain} \markbox{m4964}{$W \in \mathfrak S$} \markbox{4965}{with} \markbox{m4966}{$d_W(x,y)>D$}, \markbox{4967}{which} \markbox{4968}{is} impossible.
\end{proof}

Another \markbox{4969}{fundamental} \markbox{4970}{fact} \markbox{4971}{about} \markbox{4972}{HHSes} \markbox{4973}{is} \markbox{4974}{the} \markbox{4975}{following} \markbox{4976}{distance} \markbox{4977}{formula,} \markbox{4978}{which} \markbox{4979}{originated} \markbox{4980}{in} \markbox{4981}{work} \markbox{4982}{of} \markbox{4983}{Masur-Minsky} \cite{MM00}, \markbox{4984}{and} \markbox{4985}{found} \markbox{4986}{various} \markbox{4987}{iterations} \markbox{4988}{elsewhere} \cite{Brock, Rafi:combo, Dur:augmented, kim2014geometry} \markbox{4989}{before} \markbox{4990}{being} \markbox{4991}{generalized} \markbox{4992}{to} \markbox{4993}{all} \markbox{4994}{HHSes} \markbox{4995}{in} \cite{HHS_II}.  \markbox{4996}{See} \cite[Theorem 4.5]{HHS_II} \markbox{4997}{for} \markbox{4998}{a} \markbox{4999}{proof} \markbox{5000}{from} \markbox{5001}{the} \markbox{5002}{now-standard} \markbox{5003}{HHS} \markbox{5004}{setup,} \markbox{5005}{and} \markbox{5006}{also} \cite[Theorem 1.2]{Bowditch_hulls} \markbox{5007}{and} \cite[Corollary C]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{5008}{from} \markbox{5009}{proofs} \markbox{5010}{using} \markbox{5011}{cubical} \markbox{5012}{model} \markbox{5013}{techniques,} \markbox{5014}{which} \markbox{5015}{we} \markbox{5016}{also} \markbox{5017}{recover} \markbox{5018}{here} \markbox{5019}{below} \markbox{5020}{in} \markbox{5021}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF lower bound}.

\begin{theorem}[Distance formula]\label{thm:DF}
There \markbox{5022}{exists} \markbox{m5023}{$K_0 = K_0(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{5024}{so} \markbox{5025}{that} \markbox{5026}{if} \markbox{m5027}{$K>K_0$} \markbox{5028}{and} \markbox{m5029}{$x,y \in \calX$}, then
$$d_{\calX}(x,y) \asymp \sum_{U \in \mathfrak S} [d_U(x,y)]_K$$
where \markbox{5030}{the} \markbox{5031}{coarse} \markbox{5032}{equality} \markbox{m5033}{$\asymp$} \markbox{5034}{depends} \markbox{5035}{only} \markbox{5036}{on} \markbox{m5037}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{5038}{and} \markbox{m5039}{$K$}.
\end{theorem}

Philosophically \markbox{5040}{(for} \markbox{5041}{our} \markbox{5042}{purposes),} \markbox{5043}{the} \markbox{5044}{distance} \markbox{5045}{formula} \markbox{5046}{says} \markbox{5047}{that} \markbox{5048}{if} \markbox{5049}{we} \markbox{5050}{want} \markbox{5051}{to} \markbox{5052}{understand} \markbox{5053}{how} \markbox{5054}{to} \markbox{5055}{move} \markbox{5056}{between} \markbox{5057}{two} \markbox{5058}{points} \markbox{5059}{in} \markbox{5060}{an} \markbox{5061}{HHS,} \markbox{5062}{it} \markbox{5063}{should} \markbox{5064}{be} \markbox{5065}{enough} \markbox{5066}{to} \markbox{5067}{focus} \markbox{5068}{on} \markbox{5069}{the} \markbox{5070}{set} \markbox{5071}{of} \markbox{5072}{relevant} \markbox{5073}{domains} \markbox{5074}{between} \markbox{5075}{them.} 

The \markbox{5076}{next} \markbox{5077}{definition} \markbox{5078}{is} \markbox{5079}{of} \markbox{5080}{a} \markbox{5081}{special} \markbox{5082}{kind} \markbox{5083}{of} \markbox{5084}{path} \markbox{5085}{in} \markbox{5086}{an} \markbox{5087}{HHS.}  \markbox{5088}{The} \markbox{5089}{proof} \markbox{5090}{of} \markbox{5091}{their} \markbox{5092}{existence} \markbox{5093}{is} \markbox{5094}{always} \markbox{5095}{tied} \markbox{5096}{up} \markbox{5097}{in} \markbox{5098}{the} \markbox{5099}{proof} \markbox{5100}{of} \markbox{5101}{the} \markbox{5102}{more} \markbox{5103}{difficult} \markbox{5104}{bound} \markbox{5105}{of} \markbox{5106}{the} \markbox{5107}{distance} \markbox{5108}{formula,} \markbox{5109}{as} \markbox{5110}{is} \markbox{5111}{the} \markbox{5112}{case} \markbox{5113}{in} \markbox{5114}{this} \markbox{5115}{paper} \markbox{5116}{in} \markbox{5117}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:HP and DF}.  \markbox{5118}{Otherwise,} \markbox{5119}{we} \markbox{5120}{will} \markbox{5121}{not} \markbox{5122}{need} \markbox{5123}{this} notion.

\begin{definition}\label{defn:hp}
A \markbox{5124}{path} \markbox{m5125}{$\gamma:I \to \calX$} \markbox{5126}{in} \markbox{5127}{an} \markbox{5128}{HHS} \markbox{m5129}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{5130}{is} \markbox{5131}{a} \markbox{m5132}{$L$}-\markbox{5133}{\emph{hierarchy path}} \markbox{5134}{if} \markbox{5135}{its} \markbox{5136}{projection} \markbox{m5137}{$\pi_U(\gamma) \subset \calC(U)$} \markbox{5138}{is} \markbox{5139}{an} \markbox{5140}{unparameterized} \markbox{m5141}{$(L,L)$}-quasi-geodesic \markbox{5142}{for} \markbox{5143}{each} \markbox{m5144}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}.
\end{definition}

We \markbox{5145}{end} \markbox{5146}{this} \markbox{5147}{subsection} \markbox{5148}{with} \markbox{5149}{a} \markbox{5150}{basic} \markbox{5151}{observation,} \markbox{5152}{which} \markbox{5153}{generalizes} \markbox{5154}{the} \markbox{5155}{observation} \markbox{5156}{that} \markbox{5157}{if} \markbox{5158}{two} \markbox{5159}{subsurfaces} \markbox{m5160}{$U,V$} \markbox{5161}{are} \markbox{5162}{not} \markbox{5163}{transverse,} \markbox{5164}{then} \markbox{5165}{their} \markbox{5166}{boundary} \markbox{5167}{curves} \markbox{5168}{must} \markbox{5169}{be} \markbox{5170}{disjoint} \markbox{5171}{up} \markbox{5172}{to} isotopy.

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:rho control}
Suppose \markbox{5173}{that} \markbox{m5174}{$U,V,W \in \Rel_{K_0}(a,b)$} \markbox{5175}{for} \markbox{m5176}{$a,b \in \calX$}.
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} If \markbox{m5177}{$U, V \nest W$} \markbox{5178}{and} \markbox{m5179}{$U,V$} \markbox{5180}{are} \markbox{5181}{not} \markbox{5182}{transverse,} \markbox{5183}{then} \markbox{m5184}{$d_W(\rho^U_W, \rho^V_W) < \ES$}.
\item {} If \markbox{m5185}{$U \pitchfork V$} \markbox{5186}{and} \markbox{m5187}{$W \nest V$} \markbox{5188}{with} \markbox{m5189}{$W,U$} \markbox{5190}{not} \markbox{5191}{orthogonal,} \markbox{5192}{then} \markbox{m5193}{$d_U(\rho^V_W, \rho^W_U)<\ES$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{lemma}

Finally, \markbox{5194}{we} \markbox{5195}{end} \markbox{5196}{with} \markbox{5197}{a} \markbox{5198}{key} \markbox{5199}{HHS} \markbox{5200}{axiom,} \markbox{5201}{originally} \markbox{5202}{proven} \markbox{5203}{for} \markbox{5204}{mapping} \markbox{5205}{class} \markbox{5206}{groups} \markbox{5207}{in} \cite[Theorem 3.1]{MM_II}:

\begin{axiom}[Bounded \markbox{5208}{geodesic} image]\label{ax:BGIA}  \markbox{5209}{If} \markbox{m5210}{$U  \sqsubset V$} \markbox{5211}{and} \markbox{m5212}{$\gamma \in \calC(V)$} \markbox{5213}{is} \markbox{5214}{a} \markbox{5215}{geodesic} \markbox{5216}{with} \markbox{m5217}{$d_{V}(\rho^U_V,\gamma)>\ES$}, \markbox{5218}{then} diam\markbox{m5219}{$(\rho^V_U(\gamma))\leq \ES.$} \markbox{5220}{Furthermore,} \markbox{5221}{for} \markbox{5222}{any} \markbox{m5223}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{5224}{and} \markbox{5225}{any} \markbox{5226}{geodesic} \markbox{m5227}{$\gamma$} \markbox{5228}{connecting} \markbox{m5229}{$\pi_V(x),\pi_V(y)$}, \markbox{5230}{if} \markbox{m5231}{$d_{V}(\rho^U_V,\gamma)>\ES$}, \markbox{5232}{then} \markbox{m5233}{$d(\pi_U(x), \pi_U(y)) \leq \ES.$}
\end{axiom} 

\subsection{Hierarchical hulls and related basic facts}

In \markbox{5234}{our} \markbox{5235}{HHS} \markbox{5236}{setup,} \markbox{5237}{the} \markbox{5238}{basic} \markbox{5239}{object} \markbox{5240}{we} \markbox{5241}{will} \markbox{5242}{want} \markbox{5243}{to} \markbox{5244}{consider} \markbox{5245}{is} \markbox{5246}{the} \markbox{5247}{following} \markbox{5248}{hierarchical} \markbox{5249}{notion} \markbox{5250}{of} \markbox{5251}{a} \markbox{5252}{coarse} \markbox{5253}{convex} \markbox{5254}{hull.}  \markbox{5255}{These} \markbox{5256}{\emph{hierarchical hulls}} \markbox{5257}{are} \markbox{5258}{built} \markbox{5259}{out} \markbox{5260}{of} \markbox{5261}{consistent} \markbox{5262}{tuples} \markbox{5263}{of} \markbox{5264}{points} \markbox{5265}{whose} \markbox{5266}{coordinates} \markbox{5267}{are} \markbox{5268}{contained} \markbox{5269}{in} \markbox{5270}{the} \markbox{5271}{hyperbolic} \markbox{5272}{hulls} \markbox{5273}{in} \markbox{5274}{each} \markbox{5275}{domain.}  \markbox{5276}{More} \markbox{5277}{specifically,} \markbox{5278}{given} \markbox{5279}{a} \markbox{5280}{pair} \markbox{5281}{of} \markbox{5282}{points} \markbox{m5283}{$x,y \in \calX$}, \markbox{5284}{for} \markbox{5285}{each,} \markbox{m5286}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{5287}{we} \markbox{5288}{set} \markbox{m5289}{$H_U = \hull_U(\pi_U(\{x,y\}))$}, \markbox{5290}{where} \markbox{m5291}{$\hull_U$} \markbox{5292}{denotes} \markbox{5293}{the} \markbox{5294}{hyperbolic} \markbox{5295}{hull} \markbox{5296}{in} \markbox{m5297}{$\calC(U)$}.

\begin{definition}[Hierarchical hull]\label{defn:hier hull}
Given \markbox{5298}{a} \markbox{5299}{constant} \markbox{m5300}{$\theta>0$}, \markbox{5301}{we} \markbox{5302}{define} \markbox{5303}{the} \markbox{5304}{\emph{$\theta$-hull}} \markbox{5305}{of} \markbox{m5306}{$x,y$} \markbox{5307}{to} \markbox{5308}{be} \markbox{5309}{all} \markbox{m5310}{$z \in \calX$} \markbox{5311}{so} \markbox{5312}{that} \markbox{m5313}{$d_U(z, H_U)<\theta$} \markbox{5314}{for} \markbox{5315}{all} \markbox{m5316}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item {} We \markbox{5317}{denote} \markbox{5318}{the} \markbox{m5319}{$\theta$}-hull \markbox{5320}{of} \markbox{m5321}{$x,y$} \markbox{5322}{by} \markbox{m5323}{$H_{\theta} = \hull_{\theta}(x,y)$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

One \markbox{5324}{of} \markbox{5325}{the} \markbox{5326}{key} \markbox{5327}{facts} \markbox{5328}{about} \markbox{5329}{hierarchical} \markbox{5330}{hulls} \markbox{5331}{is} \markbox{5332}{that} \markbox{5333}{they} \markbox{5334}{are} \markbox{5335}{\emph{hierarchically quasiconvex}} \cite[Lemma 6.2]{HHS_II}, \markbox{5336}{see} \cite{russell2023convexity} \markbox{5337}{for} \markbox{5338}{more} \markbox{5339}{on} \markbox{5340}{convexity} \markbox{5341}{in} \markbox{5342}{HHSes.}  \markbox{5343}{We} \markbox{5344}{do} \markbox{5345}{not} \markbox{5346}{need} \markbox{5347}{this} \markbox{5348}{definition} \markbox{5349}{for} \markbox{5350}{our} \markbox{5351}{purposes,} \markbox{5352}{but} \markbox{5353}{we} \markbox{5354}{do} \markbox{5355}{need} \markbox{5356}{the} \markbox{5357}{following} consequence:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:gate retract}
For \markbox{5358}{any} \markbox{m5359}{$\theta>0$}, \markbox{5360}{there} \markbox{5361}{exists} \markbox{5362}{is} \markbox{5363}{a} \markbox{m5364}{$(J,J)$}-coarse \markbox{5365}{Lipschitz} \markbox{5366}{retract} \markbox{m5367}{$\gate_{H_{\theta}}:\calX \to H_{\theta}$}, \markbox{5368}{where} \markbox{m5369}{$J = J(\theta, \mathfrak S)>0$} .
\end{lemma}

In \markbox{5370}{the} \markbox{5371}{above} \markbox{5372}{lemma,} \markbox{5373}{the} \markbox{5374}{map} \markbox{m5375}{$\gate_{H_{\theta}}: \calX \to H_{\theta}$} \markbox{5376}{is} \markbox{5377}{a} \markbox{5378}{hierarchical} \markbox{5379}{analogue} \markbox{5380}{of} \markbox{5381}{a} \markbox{5382}{cubical} \markbox{5383}{gate} \markbox{5384}{map.}  \markbox{5385}{When} \markbox{m5386}{$z \in \calX$}, \markbox{5387}{the} \markbox{5388}{point} \markbox{m5389}{$\gate_{H_{\theta}}(z) \in H_{\theta}$} \markbox{5390}{is} \markbox{5391}{defined} \markbox{5392}{by} \markbox{5393}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{5394}{closest-point} \markbox{5395}{projection} \markbox{5396}{of} \markbox{m5397}{$\pi_U(z)$} \markbox{5398}{to} \markbox{m5399}{$H_U$} \markbox{5400}{and} \markbox{5401}{then} \markbox{5402}{applying} \markbox{5403}{the} \markbox{5404}{Realization} \markbox{5405}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization}; \markbox{5406}{see} \cite[Proposition 6.3]{HHS_II} \markbox{5407}{and} \markbox{5408}{the} \markbox{5409}{surrounding} \markbox{5410}{text} \markbox{5411}{for} details.







\subsection{Consequences of the Passing-up Lemma \ref{lem:passing-up}}

The \markbox{5412}{following} \markbox{5413}{statements} \markbox{5414}{are} \markbox{5415}{useful} \markbox{5416}{for} \markbox{5417}{the} \markbox{5418}{sort} \markbox{5419}{of} \markbox{5420}{distance} \markbox{5421}{formula} \markbox{5422}{related} \markbox{5423}{hierarchical} \markbox{5424}{accounting} \markbox{5425}{that} \markbox{5426}{we} \markbox{5427}{need} \markbox{5428}{to} \markbox{5429}{do} \markbox{5430}{the} \markbox{5431}{proof} \markbox{5432}{of} \markbox{5433}{the} \markbox{5434}{cubical} \markbox{5435}{model} \markbox{5436}{theorem.}  \markbox{5437}{The} \markbox{5438}{first} \markbox{5439}{says} \markbox{5440}{that} \markbox{5441}{any} \markbox{5442}{given} \markbox{5443}{relevant} \markbox{5444}{domain} \markbox{5445}{for} \markbox{5446}{a} \markbox{5447}{pair} \markbox{m5448}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{5449}{can} \markbox{5450}{only} \markbox{5451}{nest} \markbox{5452}{into} \markbox{5453}{boundedly-many} \markbox{5454}{other} \markbox{5455}{relevant} \markbox{5456}{domains} \markbox{5457}{for} \markbox{m5458}{$x,y$}.  \markbox{5459}{It} \markbox{5460}{first} \markbox{5461}{appeared} \markbox{5462}{in} \cite[Lemma 2.15]{DMS_bary}; \markbox{5463}{see} \cite[Lemma 11.13]{CRHK} \markbox{5464}{for} \markbox{5465}{a} \markbox{5466}{different} \markbox{5467}{proof} \markbox{5468}{and} \cite[Lemma 4.8]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{5469}{for} \markbox{5470}{a} \markbox{5471}{version} \markbox{5472}{that} \markbox{5473}{allows} \markbox{m5474}{$x,y$} \markbox{5475}{to} \markbox{5476}{be} \markbox{5477}{at} infinity.

\begin{lemma}[Covering]\label{lem:covering}
For \markbox{5478}{any} \markbox{5479}{HHS} \markbox{m5480}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$}, \markbox{5481}{there} \markbox{5482}{exists} \markbox{m5483}{$N = N(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{5484}{so} \markbox{5485}{that} \markbox{5486}{the} \markbox{5487}{following} \markbox{5488}{holds.}  \markbox{5489}{For} \markbox{5490}{any} \markbox{m5491}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{5492}{and} \markbox{5493}{all} \markbox{m5494}{$U \in \Rel_{50\ES}(x,y)$}, \markbox{5495}{there} \markbox{5496}{are} \markbox{5497}{at} \markbox{5498}{most} \markbox{m5499}{$N$} \markbox{5500}{domains} \markbox{m5501}{$V \in \Rel_{50\ES}(x,y)$} \markbox{5502}{so} \markbox{5503}{that} \markbox{m5504}{$U \nest V$}.
\end{lemma}

Another \markbox{5505}{consequence} \markbox{5506}{of} \markbox{5507}{Lemma} \ref{lem:passing-up} \markbox{5508}{is} \markbox{5509}{the} \markbox{5510}{following} \markbox{5511}{distance} \markbox{5512}{formula} \markbox{5513}{type} \markbox{5514}{statement,} \markbox{5515}{which} \markbox{5516}{is} \markbox{5517}{a} \markbox{5518}{less} \markbox{5519}{general} \markbox{5520}{version} \markbox{5521}{of} \cite[Proposition 4.14]{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{5522}{Roughly,} \markbox{5523}{it} \markbox{5524}{says} \markbox{5525}{that} \markbox{5526}{the} \markbox{5527}{number} \markbox{5528}{of} \markbox{5529}{medium-sized} \markbox{5530}{relevant} \markbox{5531}{domains} \markbox{5532}{for} \markbox{5533}{a} \markbox{5534}{pair} \markbox{m5535}{$x,y$} \markbox{5536}{can} \markbox{5537}{be} \markbox{5538}{accounted} \markbox{5539}{for} \markbox{5540}{(i.e.,} \markbox{5541}{in} \markbox{5542}{terms} \markbox{5543}{of} \markbox{5544}{the} \markbox{5545}{domain} \markbox{5546}{projections)} \markbox{5547}{by} \markbox{5548}{large-sized} \markbox{5549}{domains} \markbox{5550}{higher} \markbox{5551}{up} \markbox{5552}{the} \markbox{5553}{hierarchy} \markbox{5554}{in} \markbox{5555}{a} \markbox{5556}{precise} \markbox{5557}{fashion.}  

\begin{proposition}[Bounding \markbox{5558}{large} containers] \label{prop:bounding containers}
Let \markbox{m5559}{$K_1 >50\ES$}, \markbox{m5560}{$K_2 \geq K_1+47\ES$}, \markbox{5561}{and} \markbox{m5562}{$x,y \in \calX$} \markbox{5563}{with} \markbox{m5564}{$\calU_1 = \Rel_{K_1}(x,y), \calU_2 = \Rel_{K_2}(x,y),$} \markbox{5565}{and} \markbox{m5566}{$\calV = \calU_1 - \calU_2$}.  \markbox{5567}{Then} \markbox{5568}{the} \markbox{5569}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
    \item {} For \markbox{5570}{all} \markbox{5571}{but} \markbox{m5572}{$PU(K_2)-1$} \markbox{5573}{domains} \markbox{m5574}{$V \in \calV$}, \markbox{5575}{there} \markbox{5576}{exists} \markbox{m5577}{$W \in \calU_2$} \markbox{5578}{with} \markbox{m5579}{$V \nest W$}.
    \item {} For \markbox{5580}{any} \markbox{m5581}{$W \in \calU_2$}, \markbox{5582}{if} \markbox{m5583}{$\calW = \{V \in \calV| V \nest W\}$} \markbox{5584}{then} \markbox{5585}{we} \markbox{5586}{have} \markbox{m5587}{$\#\calW \prec d_W(x,y)$} \markbox{5588}{with} \markbox{5589}{constants} \markbox{5590}{depending} \markbox{5591}{only} \markbox{5592}{on} \markbox{m5593}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{5594}{and} \markbox{m5595}{$K_2$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

The \markbox{5596}{above} \markbox{5597}{proposition} \markbox{5598}{is} \markbox{5599}{useful} \markbox{5600}{for} \markbox{5601}{proving} \markbox{5602}{the} \markbox{5603}{following} \markbox{5604}{slight} \markbox{5605}{generalization} \markbox{5606}{of} \markbox{5607}{the} \markbox{5608}{Distance} \markbox{5609}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}.  \markbox{5610}{It's} \markbox{5611}{useful} \markbox{5612}{for} \markbox{5613}{circumstances,} \markbox{5614}{such} \markbox{5615}{as} \markbox{5616}{in} \markbox{5617}{Section} \ref{subsec:Q qie}, \markbox{5618}{where} \markbox{5619}{we} \markbox{5620}{want} \markbox{5621}{to} \markbox{5622}{make} \markbox{5623}{distance} \markbox{5624}{formula-type} \markbox{5625}{arguments} \markbox{5626}{where} \markbox{5627}{the} \markbox{5628}{summands} \markbox{5629}{are} \markbox{5630}{only} \markbox{5631}{coarsely} \markbox{5632}{equal} \markbox{5633}{to} \markbox{5634}{the} \markbox{5635}{standard} \markbox{5636}{distance} \markbox{5637}{formula} \markbox{5638}{terms.}  \markbox{5639}{Probably} \markbox{5640}{the} \markbox{5641}{key} \markbox{5642}{example} \markbox{5643}{of} \markbox{5644}{this} \markbox{5645}{is} \markbox{5646}{when} \markbox{5647}{we} \markbox{5648}{want} \markbox{5649}{to} \markbox{5650}{replace} \markbox{m5651}{$d_U(x,y)$} \markbox{5652}{with} \markbox{m5653}{$d_{T_U}(x,y)$}, \markbox{5654}{where} \markbox{5655}{each} \markbox{m5656}{$T_U$} \markbox{5657}{is} \markbox{5658}{a} \markbox{5659}{uniform} \markbox{5660}{quasi-geodesic} \markbox{5661}{in} \markbox{m5662}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{5663}{between} \markbox{m5664}{$\pi_U(x)$} \markbox{5665}{and} \markbox{m5666}{$\pi_U(y)$}.  \markbox{5667}{This} \markbox{5668}{originally} \markbox{5669}{appeared} \markbox{5670}{in} \cite[Lemma 9.6]{Min_ELC} \markbox{5671}{for} \markbox{5672}{mapping} \markbox{5673}{class} \markbox{5674}{groups,} \markbox{5675}{and} \markbox{5676}{see} \cite[Theorem 2.9]{BHMS:kill_twists} \markbox{5677}{(which} \markbox{5678}{depends} \markbox{5679}{on} \markbox{5680}{the} \markbox{5681}{distance} \markbox{5682}{formula)} \markbox{5683}{and} \cite[Corollary 4.17]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{5684}{(which} \markbox{5685}{does} \markbox{5686}{not)} \markbox{5687}{for} \markbox{5688}{proofs} \markbox{5689}{in} \markbox{5690}{the} \markbox{5691}{HHS} setting.

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:DF replace}
Let \markbox{m5692}{$x,y \in \calX$}.  \markbox{5693}{Suppose} \markbox{5694}{that} \markbox{m5695}{$\sigma:\mathbb R_+ \to \mathbb R_+$} \markbox{5696}{is} \markbox{5697}{a} \markbox{5698}{function} \markbox{5699}{satisfying} 
$$\sigma(d_U(x,y)) \asymp d_U(x,y)$$
for \markbox{5700}{each} \markbox{m5701}{$U \in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{5702}{where} \markbox{5703}{the} \markbox{5704}{constants} \markbox{5705}{in} \markbox{m5706}{$\asymp$} \markbox{5707}{are} \markbox{5708}{independent} \markbox{5709}{of} \markbox{m5710}{$U$}.  \markbox{5711}{Then} \markbox{5712}{for} \markbox{5713}{any} \markbox{m5714}{$K_1>50\ES$}, \markbox{5715}{we} have
$$\sum_{U \in \calU} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_1} \asymp \sum_{U \in \calU} [\sigma(d_U(x,y))]_{K_1}$$
where \markbox{5716}{the} \markbox{5717}{constants} \markbox{5718}{in} \markbox{m5719}{$\asymp$} \markbox{5720}{depend} \markbox{5721}{only} \markbox{5722}{on} \markbox{m5723}{$\mathfrak S$}, \markbox{m5724}{$K_1$}, \markbox{5725}{and} \markbox{m5726}{$\sigma$}.
\end{corollary}











\section{From hierarchical hulls to collapsed interval systems} \label{sec:interval systems}

In \markbox{5727}{the} \markbox{5728}{next} \markbox{5729}{three} \markbox{5730}{sections,} \markbox{5731}{we} \markbox{5732}{will} \markbox{5733}{give} \markbox{5734}{an} \markbox{5735}{overview} \markbox{5736}{of} \markbox{5737}{the} \markbox{5738}{cubical} \markbox{5739}{model} \markbox{5740}{construction} \markbox{5741}{for} \markbox{5742}{the} \markbox{5743}{hierarchical} \markbox{5744}{hull} \markbox{5745}{of} \markbox{5746}{a} \markbox{5747}{pair} \markbox{5748}{of} \markbox{5749}{points} \markbox{5750}{in} \markbox{5751}{an} \markbox{5752}{HHS} \markbox{5753}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{5754}{The} \markbox{5755}{original} \markbox{5756}{construction} \markbox{5757}{is} \markbox{5758}{due} \markbox{5759}{to} \markbox{5760}{Behrstock-Hagen-Sisto} \cite{HHS_quasi}, \markbox{5761}{and} \markbox{5762}{see} \markbox{5763}{also} \markbox{5764}{Bowditch} \cite{Bowditch_hulls} \markbox{5765}{for} \markbox{5766}{a} \markbox{5767}{version} \markbox{5768}{in} \markbox{5769}{the} \markbox{5770}{more} \markbox{5771}{general} \markbox{5772}{setting} \markbox{5773}{of} \markbox{5774}{coarse} \markbox{5775}{median} \markbox{5776}{spaces} \markbox{5777}{satisfying} \markbox{5778}{HHS-like} axioms.

The \markbox{5779}{main} \markbox{5780}{goal} \markbox{5781}{of} \markbox{5782}{this} \markbox{5783}{section} \markbox{5784}{is} \markbox{5785}{to} \markbox{5786}{explain} \markbox{5787}{how} \markbox{5788}{to} \markbox{5789}{take} \markbox{5790}{a} \markbox{5791}{pair} \markbox{5792}{of} \markbox{5793}{points} \markbox{m5794}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{5795}{in} \markbox{5796}{an} \markbox{5797}{HHS} \markbox{m5798}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{5799}{and} \markbox{5800}{produce} \markbox{5801}{a} \markbox{5802}{family} \markbox{5803}{of} \markbox{5804}{intervals} \markbox{5805}{which} \markbox{5806}{encode} \markbox{5807}{the} \markbox{5808}{relevant} \markbox{5809}{hierarchical} \markbox{5810}{data} \markbox{5811}{in} \markbox{5812}{a} \markbox{5813}{fairly} \markbox{5814}{efficient} \markbox{5815}{manner.}  \markbox{5816}{Roughly,} \markbox{5817}{the} \markbox{5818}{result} \markbox{5819}{of} \markbox{5820}{this} \markbox{5821}{process} \markbox{5822}{is} \markbox{5823}{a} \markbox{5824}{collection} \markbox{5825}{of} \markbox{5826}{intervals} \markbox{m5827}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{5828}{equipped} \markbox{5829}{with} \markbox{5830}{a} \markbox{5831}{family} \markbox{5832}{of} \markbox{5833}{relative} \markbox{5834}{projections} \markbox{5835}{satisfying} \markbox{5836}{certain} \markbox{5837}{HHS-like} \markbox{5838}{properties,} \markbox{5839}{where} \markbox{5840}{the} \markbox{5841}{index} \markbox{5842}{set} \markbox{m5843}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b)$} \markbox{5844}{is} \markbox{5845}{the} \markbox{5846}{set} \markbox{5847}{of} \markbox{m5848}{$K$}-relevant \markbox{5849}{domains} \markbox{5850}{for} \markbox{m5851}{$a,b$} \markbox{5852}{(Definition} \ref{defn:relevant}).  \markbox{5853}{For} \markbox{5854}{any} \markbox{5855}{such} \markbox{5856}{collection} \markbox{5857}{of} \markbox{5858}{intervals,} \markbox{5859}{one} \markbox{5860}{can} \markbox{5861}{define} \markbox{5862}{a} \markbox{5863}{notion} \markbox{5864}{of} \markbox{m5865}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{5866}{(an} \markbox{5867}{exact} \markbox{5868}{form} \markbox{5869}{of} \markbox{5870}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency}), \markbox{5871}{which} \markbox{5872}{defines} \markbox{5873}{a} \markbox{5874}{special} \markbox{m5875}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{5876}{subset} \markbox{m5877}{$\calQ$} \markbox{5878}{of} \markbox{5879}{the} \markbox{5880}{product} \markbox{m5881}{$\prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_U$}.  \markbox{5882}{In} \markbox{5883}{Section} \ref{sec:hPsi qi} \markbox{5884}{below} \markbox{5885}{we} \markbox{5886}{will} \markbox{5887}{explain} \markbox{5888}{why} \markbox{5889}{this} \markbox{5890}{set} \markbox{m5891}{$\calQ$} \markbox{5892}{is} \markbox{5893}{quasi-isometric} \markbox{5894}{to} \markbox{5895}{the} \markbox{5896}{hierarchical} \markbox{5897}{hull} \markbox{5898}{of} \markbox{m5899}{$a,b$} \markbox{5900}{in} \markbox{m5901}{$\calX$}.  \markbox{5902}{Finally} \markbox{5903}{in} \markbox{5904}{Section} \ref{sec:cubulation}, \markbox{5905}{we} \markbox{5906}{will} \markbox{5907}{axiomatize} \markbox{5908}{the} \markbox{5909}{properties} \markbox{5910}{any} \markbox{5911}{such} \markbox{5912}{family} \markbox{5913}{of} \markbox{5914}{intervals} \markbox{5915}{satisfies,} \markbox{5916}{explain} \markbox{5917}{how} \markbox{5918}{it} \markbox{5919}{admits} \markbox{5920}{a} \markbox{5921}{natural} \markbox{5922}{wallspace} \markbox{5923}{structure,} \markbox{5924}{and} \markbox{5925}{show} \markbox{5926}{that} \markbox{5927}{the} \markbox{5928}{associated} \markbox{m5929}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{5930}{set} \markbox{m5931}{$\calQ$} \markbox{5932}{is} \markbox{5933}{isometric} \markbox{5934}{to} \markbox{5935}{the} \markbox{5936}{cubical} \markbox{5937}{dual} \markbox{5938}{of} \markbox{5939}{this} \markbox{5940}{wallspace.} 


\subsection{Basic setup of the section}

For \markbox{5941}{the} \markbox{5942}{rest} \markbox{5943}{of} \markbox{5944}{this} \markbox{5945}{section,} \markbox{5946}{we} \markbox{5947}{fix} \markbox{5948}{a} \markbox{5949}{constant} \markbox{m5950}{$K\geq K_0$}, \markbox{5951}{where} \markbox{m5952}{$K_0 = K_0(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{5953}{is} \markbox{5954}{the} \markbox{5955}{constant} \markbox{5956}{from} \markbox{5957}{the} \markbox{5958}{Distance} \markbox{5959}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}.  \markbox{5960}{In} \markbox{5961}{this} \markbox{5962}{section,} \markbox{5963}{we} \markbox{5964}{will} \markbox{5965}{be} \markbox{5966}{able} \markbox{5967}{to} \markbox{5968}{allow} \markbox{m5969}{$K$} \markbox{5970}{to} \markbox{5971}{be} \markbox{5972}{as} \markbox{5973}{large} \markbox{5974}{as} necessary.

Fix \markbox{5975}{also} \markbox{m5976}{$a, b\in \calX$}.  \markbox{5977}{Let} \markbox{m5978}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b) = \{U \in \mathfrak S| d_U(a,b)>K\}$} \markbox{5979}{denote} \markbox{5980}{their} \markbox{m5981}{$K$}-relevant \markbox{5982}{set.}  \markbox{5983}{To} \markbox{5984}{each} \markbox{m5985}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{5986}{let} \markbox{m5987}{$\phi_U:T_U\to \calC(U)$} \markbox{5988}{denote} \markbox{5989}{a} \markbox{m5990}{$(C,C)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{5991}{embedding} \markbox{5992}{of} \markbox{5993}{an} \markbox{5994}{interval} \markbox{5995}{between} \markbox{m5996}{$a_U$} \markbox{5997}{and} \markbox{m5998}{$b_U$}, \markbox{5999}{so} \markbox{6000}{that} \markbox{m6001}{$\phi_U(a_U) = \pi_U(a)$} \markbox{6002}{and} \markbox{m6003}{$\phi_U(b_U) = \pi_U(b)$}.  \markbox{6004}{Here} \markbox{6005}{we} \markbox{6006}{can} \markbox{6007}{assume} \markbox{6008}{that} \markbox{m6009}{$C=C(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{6010}{depends} \markbox{6011}{only} \markbox{6012}{on} \markbox{6013}{the} \markbox{6014}{ambient} \markbox{6015}{HHS.}  \markbox{6016}{Note} \markbox{6017}{that} \markbox{6018}{we} \markbox{6019}{are} \markbox{6020}{only} \markbox{6021}{taking} \markbox{6022}{a} \markbox{6023}{quasi-isometric} \markbox{6024}{embedding,} \markbox{6025}{instead} \markbox{6026}{of} \markbox{6027}{a} \markbox{6028}{geodesic,} \markbox{6029}{because} \markbox{6030}{that} \markbox{6031}{is} \markbox{6032}{the} \markbox{6033}{level} \markbox{6034}{of} \markbox{6035}{generality} \markbox{6036}{that} \markbox{6037}{we} \markbox{6038}{will} \markbox{6039}{require} later.

We \markbox{6040}{also} \markbox{6041}{set} \markbox{6042}{some} \markbox{6043}{terminology} \markbox{6044}{for} \markbox{m6045}{$a_U,b_U$}, \markbox{6046}{since} \markbox{6047}{they} \markbox{6048}{will} \markbox{6049}{play} \markbox{6050}{a} \markbox{6051}{distinguished} \markbox{6052}{role} \markbox{6053}{below.} 

\begin{definition}[Marked \markbox{6054}{points} \markbox{6055}{on} intervals] \label{defn:marked}
For \markbox{6056}{each} \markbox{m6057}{$U\in \calU$} \markbox{6058}{the} \markbox{6059}{points} \markbox{m6060}{$a_U, b_U \in T_U$} \markbox{6061}{are} \markbox{6062}{called} \markbox{6063}{\emph{marked points}}.
\end{definition}

We \markbox{6064}{note} \markbox{6065}{that} \markbox{6066}{in} \markbox{6067}{the} \markbox{6068}{basic} \markbox{6069}{construction} \markbox{6070}{explained} \markbox{6071}{in} \markbox{6072}{this} \markbox{6073}{section,} \markbox{6074}{marked} \markbox{6075}{points} \markbox{6076}{will} \markbox{6077}{always} \markbox{6078}{been} \markbox{6079}{the} \markbox{6080}{endpoints} \markbox{6081}{of} \markbox{6082}{the} \markbox{6083}{intervals} \markbox{m6084}{$T_U$}.  \markbox{6085}{This} \markbox{6086}{will} \markbox{6087}{also} \markbox{6088}{be} \markbox{6089}{true} \markbox{6090}{of} \markbox{6091}{our} \markbox{6092}{collapsed} \markbox{6093}{stable} \markbox{6094}{trees} \markbox{6095}{defined} \markbox{6096}{in} \markbox{6097}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:collapsed stable intervals}, \markbox{6098}{though} \markbox{6099}{not} \markbox{6100}{necessarily} \markbox{6101}{of} \markbox{6102}{the} \markbox{6103}{stable} \markbox{6104}{intervals} themselves.

The \markbox{6105}{discussion} \markbox{6106}{in} \markbox{6107}{this} \markbox{6108}{section} \markbox{6109}{closely} \markbox{6110}{follows} \cite[Sections \markbox{6111}{6} \markbox{6112}{and} 7]{Dur_infcube}. \markbox{6113}{Given} \markbox{6114}{the} \markbox{6115}{technical} \markbox{6116}{nature} \markbox{6117}{of} \markbox{6118}{this} \markbox{6119}{part,} \markbox{6120}{we} \markbox{6121}{will} \markbox{6122}{mostly} \markbox{6123}{state} \markbox{6124}{definitions} \markbox{6125}{and} \markbox{6126}{important} \markbox{6127}{properties,} \markbox{6128}{providing} \markbox{6129}{sketches} \markbox{6130}{where} \markbox{6131}{convenient} \markbox{6132}{but} \markbox{6133}{leaving} \markbox{6134}{the} \markbox{6135}{details} \markbox{6136}{for} \markbox{6137}{the} \markbox{6138}{reader} \markbox{6139}{to} verify.

\subsection{Reduced interval systems} \label{subsec:reduced interval systems}

Our \markbox{6140}{first} \markbox{6141}{goal} \markbox{6142}{is} \markbox{6143}{to} \markbox{6144}{push} \markbox{6145}{the} \markbox{6146}{hierarchical} \markbox{6147}{data} \markbox{6148}{associated} \markbox{6149}{to} \markbox{m6150}{$a,b$} \markbox{6151}{onto} \markbox{6152}{the} \markbox{6153}{family} \markbox{6154}{of} \markbox{6155}{intervals} \markbox{m6156}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$}.  \markbox{6157}{This} \markbox{6158}{involves} \markbox{6159}{producing} \markbox{6160}{a} \markbox{6161}{notion} \markbox{6162}{of} \markbox{6163}{relative} \markbox{6164}{projection} \markbox{6165}{between} \markbox{6166}{the} \markbox{6167}{intervals} \markbox{6168}{and} \markbox{6169}{verifying} \markbox{6170}{some} \markbox{6171}{HHS-like} \markbox{6172}{properties} \markbox{6173}{for} them.

These \markbox{6174}{\emph{interval projections}} \markbox{6175}{are} \markbox{6176}{defined} \markbox{6177}{simply} \markbox{6178}{by} \markbox{6179}{closest-point} \markbox{6180}{projecting} \markbox{6181}{the} \markbox{6182}{relative} \markbox{6183}{projections} \markbox{6184}{of} \markbox{m6185}{$(\calX,\mathfrak S)$} \markbox{6186}{to} \markbox{6187}{the} \markbox{6188}{images} \markbox{6189}{of} \markbox{m6190}{$\phi_U(T_U) \subset \calC(U)$} \markbox{6191}{then} \markbox{6192}{pulling} \markbox{6193}{back} \markbox{6194}{to} \markbox{m6195}{$T_U$} \markbox{6196}{via} \markbox{m6197}{$\phi^{-1}_U$}.  \markbox{6198}{We} \markbox{6199}{write} \markbox{m6200}{$\delta^V_U$}, \markbox{6201}{rather} \markbox{6202}{than} \markbox{m6203}{$\rho^V_U$}, \markbox{6204}{for} \markbox{6205}{the} \markbox{6206}{relative} \markbox{6207}{interval} \markbox{6208}{projections} \markbox{6209}{among} \markbox{6210}{the} \markbox{m6211}{$T_U$}.  \markbox{6212}{These} \markbox{6213}{interval} \markbox{6214}{projections} \markbox{6215}{are} \markbox{6216}{interval} \markbox{6217}{versions} \markbox{6218}{of} \markbox{6219}{the} \markbox{6220}{``tree} \markbox{6221}{projections''} \markbox{6222}{described} \markbox{6223}{in} \cite[Section 6]{Dur_infcube}.

The \markbox{6224}{following} \markbox{6225}{lemma,} \markbox{6226}{which} \markbox{6227}{summarizes} \markbox{6228}{the} \markbox{6229}{basic} \markbox{6230}{properties} \markbox{6231}{that} \markbox{6232}{we} \markbox{6233}{need,} \markbox{6234}{says} \markbox{6235}{that} \markbox{6236}{the} \markbox{m6237}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{6238}{behave} \markbox{6239}{in} \markbox{6240}{essentially} \markbox{6241}{the} \markbox{6242}{same} \markbox{6243}{way} \markbox{6244}{as} \markbox{6245}{the} \markbox{m6246}{$\rho^V_U$}.  \markbox{6247}{Its} \markbox{6248}{proof} \markbox{6249}{is} \markbox{6250}{an} \markbox{6251}{exercise} \markbox{6252}{in} \markbox{6253}{the} \markbox{6254}{definitions} \markbox{6255}{and} \markbox{6256}{the} \markbox{6257}{basic} \markbox{6258}{properties} \markbox{6259}{of} \markbox{6260}{an} \markbox{6261}{HHS;} \markbox{6262}{see} \cite[Lemma 6.13]{Dur_infcube}.

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:interval control}
For \markbox{6263}{any} \markbox{m6264}{$C>0$} \markbox{6265}{there} \markbox{6266}{exists} \markbox{m6267}{$R_C = R_C(C,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{6268}{so} \markbox{6269}{that} \markbox{6270}{the} \markbox{6271}{following} holds:

\begin{enumerate}
    \item {} If \markbox{m6272}{$U \pitchfork V \in \calU$}, \markbox{6273}{then} \markbox{6274}{both} \markbox{m6275}{$\delta^V_U \subset T_U$} \markbox{6276}{and} \markbox{m6277}{$\delta^U_V \subset T_V$} \markbox{6278}{are} \markbox{6279}{sets} \markbox{6280}{of} \markbox{6281}{diameter} \markbox{6282}{at} \markbox{6283}{most} \markbox{m6284}{$R_C$} \markbox{6285}{which} \markbox{6286}{are} \markbox{m6287}{$R_C$}-close \markbox{6288}{to} \markbox{6289}{a} \markbox{6290}{marked} \markbox{6291}{point} \markbox{6292}{of} \markbox{m6293}{$T_U,T_V$}, \markbox{6294}{respectively.}  \markbox{6295}{Moreover,} \markbox{m6296}{$d_U(\phi_U(\delta^V_U), \rho^V_U)<R_C$}, \markbox{6297}{and} \markbox{6298}{similarly} \markbox{6299}{for} \markbox{m6300}{$\delta^U_V$}.
    \item {} If \markbox{m6301}{$U \nest V \in \calU$}, \markbox{6302}{then} \markbox{m6303}{$\delta^U_V \subset T_V$} \markbox{6304}{has} \markbox{6305}{diameter} \markbox{6306}{bounded} \markbox{6307}{by} \markbox{m6308}{$R_C$}.  \markbox{6309}{Moreover,} \markbox{m6310}{$d_V(\phi_V(\delta^U_V), \rho^U_V)<R_C$}.
     \item {} If \markbox{m6311}{$U, V \nest W \in \calU$} \markbox{6312}{with} \markbox{m6313}{$U,V$} \markbox{6314}{not} \markbox{6315}{transverse,} \markbox{6316}{then} \markbox{m6317}{$\diam_{T_W}(\delta^U_W \cup \delta^V_W) < R_C$}.
    \item {} If \markbox{m6318}{$U \pitchfork V$} \markbox{6319}{and} \markbox{m6320}{$W \nest V$} \markbox{6321}{and} \markbox{m6322}{$W,U$} \markbox{6323}{not} \markbox{6324}{orthogonal,} \markbox{6325}{then} \markbox{m6326}{$\diam_{T_U}(\delta^V_U \cup \delta^W_U)<R_C$}.
    \item{} (Bounded \markbox{6327}{geodesic} \markbox{6328}{image)} \markbox{6329}{If} \markbox{m6330}{$U \nest V \in \calU$}, \markbox{6331}{then} \markbox{6332}{any} \markbox{6333}{component} \markbox{m6334}{$C \subset T_V - \calN_{R_C}(\delta^U_V)$} \markbox{6335}{satisfies} \markbox{m6336}{$\diam_{T_U}(\delta^V_U(C))<R_C$}.
  
\end{enumerate}

\end{lemma}
