It \markbox{6337}{will} \markbox{6338}{be} \markbox{6339}{useful} \markbox{6340}{for} \markbox{6341}{us} \markbox{6342}{to} \markbox{6343}{abstract} \markbox{6344}{the} \markbox{6345}{properties} \markbox{6346}{obtained} \markbox{6347}{for} \markbox{6348}{the} \markbox{6349}{intervals} \markbox{m6350}{$T_U$} \markbox{6351}{in} \markbox{6352}{the} \markbox{6353}{last} \markbox{6354}{subsection.}  \markbox{6355}{We} \markbox{6356}{are} \markbox{6357}{doing} \markbox{6358}{this} \markbox{6359}{so} \markbox{6360}{that} \markbox{6361}{we} \markbox{6362}{can} \markbox{6363}{later} \markbox{6364}{plug} \markbox{6365}{in} \markbox{6366}{the} \markbox{6367}{intervals} \markbox{6368}{produced} \markbox{6369}{by} \markbox{6370}{the} \markbox{6371}{Stable} \markbox{6372}{Interval} \markbox{6373}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{6374}{below} \markbox{6375}{directly} \markbox{6376}{into} \markbox{6377}{this} setup.

\begin{definition}[Interval system]\label{defn:interval axioms}
Given \markbox{m6378}{$R>0$}, \markbox{6379}{an} \markbox{m6380}{$R$}-\markbox{6381}{\emph{interval system}} \markbox{6382}{for} \markbox{m6383}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{6384}{and} \markbox{m6385}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b)$} \markbox{6386}{is} \markbox{6387}{the} \markbox{6388}{following} \markbox{6389}{set} \markbox{6390}{of} data:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} For \markbox{6391}{each} \markbox{m6392}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{6393}{we} \markbox{6394}{have} \markbox{6395}{an} \markbox{6396}{interval} \markbox{m6397}{$T_U$} \markbox{6398}{and} \markbox{6399}{a} \markbox{m6400}{$(R,R)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{6401}{embedding} \markbox{m6402}{$\phi_U:T_U \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{6403}{so} \markbox{6404}{that} \markbox{m6405}{$d^{Haus}_U(\phi_U(T_U), \hull_U(a,b))<R$}.
\item {} For \markbox{6406}{each} \markbox{m6407}{$U \in\calU$}, \markbox{6408}{there} \markbox{6409}{exists} \markbox{6410}{a} \markbox{6411}{marked} \markbox{6412}{point} \markbox{m6413}{$a_U \in T_U$} \markbox{6414}{with} \markbox{m6415}{$d_{\calC(U)}(\phi_U(a_U),\pi_U(a))<R$}, \markbox{6416}{and} \markbox{6417}{similarly} \markbox{6418}{for} \markbox{m6419}{$b$}.
\item {} There \markbox{6420}{are} \markbox{m6421}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{6422}{sets} \markbox{6423}{which} \markbox{6424}{satisfy} \markbox{6425}{the} \markbox{6426}{conclusions} \markbox{6427}{of} \markbox{6428}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control}.


\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}


\begin{remark}
When \markbox{6429}{stabilizing} \markbox{6430}{the} \markbox{6431}{construction} \markbox{6432}{of} \markbox{6433}{the} \markbox{6434}{cubical} \markbox{6435}{models} \markbox{6436}{in} \markbox{6437}{Section} \ref{sec:stable cubes}, \markbox{6438}{we} \markbox{6439}{will} \markbox{6440}{want} \markbox{6441}{to} \markbox{6442}{use} \markbox{6443}{the} \markbox{6444}{stable} \markbox{6445}{intervals} \markbox{6446}{provided} \markbox{6447}{by} \markbox{6448}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{6449}{below.}  \markbox{6450}{For} \markbox{6451}{these,} \markbox{6452}{we} \markbox{6453}{will} \markbox{6454}{induce} \markbox{6455}{an} \markbox{6456}{interval} \markbox{6457}{system} \markbox{6458}{structure} \markbox{6459}{by} \markbox{6460}{a} \markbox{6461}{slightly} \markbox{6462}{more} \markbox{6463}{careful} \markbox{6464}{construction} \markbox{6465}{than} \markbox{6466}{just} \markbox{6467}{working} \markbox{6468}{directly} \markbox{6469}{with} \markbox{6470}{Gromov} \markbox{6471}{trees,} \markbox{6472}{e.g.} \markbox{6473}{item} \markbox{6474}{(2)} \markbox{6475}{in} \markbox{6476}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{6477}{is} \markbox{6478}{immediate} \markbox{6479}{in} \markbox{6480}{that} \markbox{6481}{setting.}  \markbox{6482}{But} \markbox{6483}{the} \markbox{6484}{upshot} \markbox{6485}{is} \markbox{6486}{the} \markbox{6487}{same:} \markbox{6488}{the} \markbox{6489}{rest} \markbox{6490}{of} \markbox{6491}{the} \markbox{6492}{material} \markbox{6493}{in} \markbox{6494}{this} \markbox{6495}{section} \markbox{6496}{also} \markbox{6497}{holds} \markbox{6498}{for} \markbox{6499}{that} setup.
\end{remark}

\subsection{Interval consistency}

The \markbox{6500}{goal} \markbox{6501}{of} \markbox{6502}{this} \markbox{6503}{subsection} \markbox{6504}{is} \markbox{6505}{to} \markbox{6506}{define} \markbox{6507}{a} \markbox{6508}{map} \markbox{m6509}{$\Psi:\hull_{\calX}(a,b)\to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$} \markbox{6510}{and} \markbox{6511}{show} \markbox{6512}{that} \markbox{6513}{its} \markbox{6514}{image} \markbox{6515}{satisfies} \markbox{6516}{the} \markbox{6517}{appropriate} \markbox{6518}{analogue} \markbox{6519}{of} \markbox{6520}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency} \markbox{6521}{in} \markbox{6522}{this} \markbox{6523}{setting.}  \markbox{6524}{Toward} \markbox{6525}{that} \markbox{6526}{end,} \markbox{6527}{for} \markbox{6528}{any} \markbox{m6529}{$\alpha>0$}, \markbox{6530}{we} \markbox{6531}{set} \markbox{m6532}{$\calZ_{\alpha} \subset \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$} \markbox{6533}{to} \markbox{6534}{be} \markbox{6535}{the} \markbox{6536}{set} \markbox{6537}{of} \markbox{m6538}{$\alpha$}-consistent tuples.

We \markbox{6539}{can} \markbox{6540}{now} \markbox{6541}{define} \markbox{6542}{our} \markbox{6543}{map} \markbox{m6544}{$\Psi:H \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$} \markbox{6545}{for} \markbox{m6546}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}.  \markbox{6547}{Let} \markbox{m6548}{$x \in H$} \markbox{6549}{and} \markbox{6550}{for} \markbox{6551}{each} \markbox{m6552}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{6553}{let} \markbox{m6554}{$x_U$} \markbox{6555}{denote} \markbox{6556}{a} \markbox{6557}{choice} \markbox{6558}{of} \markbox{6559}{a} \markbox{6560}{point} \markbox{6561}{in} \markbox{m6562}{$\psi_U(x) = \phi_{U}^{-1}(p_U(\pi_U(x))) \subset T_U$}, \markbox{6563}{where} \markbox{m6564}{$p_U:\calC(U)\to \phi_U(T_U)$} \markbox{6565}{is} \markbox{6566}{closest} \markbox{6567}{point} \markbox{6568}{projection.}  \markbox{6569}{For} \markbox{6570}{each} \markbox{m6571}{$x \in H$}, \markbox{6572}{this} \markbox{6573}{defines} \markbox{6574}{a} \markbox{6575}{tuple} \markbox{m6576}{$(\psi_U(x)) = (x_U) \in \prod_{U \in \calU}T_U$}.  \markbox{6577}{That} \markbox{6578}{is,} \markbox{6579}{the} \markbox{6580}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{6581}{maps} \markbox{m6582}{$\psi_U:H \to T_U$} \markbox{6583}{combine} \markbox{6584}{to} \markbox{6585}{a} \markbox{6586}{global} \markbox{6587}{map} \markbox{m6588}{$\Psi:H \to \prod_U T_U$}.

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:interval consistency}
For \markbox{6589}{any} \markbox{m6590}{$R>0$}, \markbox{6591}{there} \markbox{6592}{exists} \markbox{m6593}{$\alpha_0 = \alpha_0(\mathfrak S,R)>0$} \markbox{6594}{so} \markbox{6595}{that} \markbox{6596}{if} \markbox{m6597}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{6598}{is} \markbox{6599}{an} \markbox{m6600}{$R$}-interval \markbox{6601}{system} \markbox{6602}{for} \markbox{m6603}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{6604}{and} \markbox{m6605}{$x \in \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}, \markbox{6606}{then} \markbox{m6607}{$\Psi(x) = (x_U)$} \markbox{6608}{is} \markbox{m6609}{$\alpha_0$}-consistent.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}

Let \markbox{m6610}{$x \in \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}.  \markbox{6611}{The} \markbox{6612}{corresponding} \markbox{6613}{tuple} \markbox{m6614}{$(\pi_U(x_U))$} \markbox{6615}{is} \markbox{m6616}{$O(\theta, \mathfrak S)$}-consistent \markbox{6617}{by} \markbox{6618}{Lemma} \ref{lem:base consistency}.  \markbox{6619}{Moreover,} \markbox{6620}{by} \markbox{6621}{definition} \markbox{6622}{of} \markbox{m6623}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{6624}{(Definition} \ref{defn:hier hull}), \markbox{6625}{we} \markbox{6626}{have} \markbox{m6627}{$d_U(\pi_U(x_U), H_U) < \theta$}, \markbox{6628}{where} \markbox{m6629}{$H_U = \hull_{\calC(U)}(a,b)$} \markbox{6630}{and} \markbox{m6631}{$\theta = \theta(\mathfrak S)>0$}.  \markbox{6632}{Hence} \markbox{m6633}{$d_U(\pi_U(x_U), \phi_U(T_U))<\theta'$} \markbox{6634}{for} \markbox{6635}{some} \markbox{m6636}{$\theta' = \theta'(\mathfrak S, \theta)>0$}.  \markbox{6637}{At} \markbox{6638}{this} \markbox{6639}{point,} \markbox{6640}{a} \markbox{6641}{straight-forward} \markbox{6642}{argument} \markbox{6643}{using} \markbox{6644}{the} \markbox{6645}{properties} \markbox{6646}{in} \markbox{6647}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control} \markbox{6648}{gives} \markbox{6649}{the} \markbox{6650}{required} \markbox{6651}{consistency} \markbox{6652}{constant} \markbox{m6653}{$\alpha_0 = \alpha_0(\mathfrak S, R)$}.  \markbox{6654}{We} \markbox{6655}{leave} \markbox{6656}{the} \markbox{6657}{details} \markbox{6658}{to} \markbox{6659}{the} reader.
\end{proof}



\subsection{Interval thickenings}\label{subsec:thickenings}

Our \markbox{6660}{next} \markbox{6661}{goal} \markbox{6662}{is} \markbox{6663}{to} \markbox{6664}{define} \markbox{6665}{a} \markbox{6666}{way} \markbox{6667}{of} \markbox{6668}{collapsing} \markbox{6669}{the} \markbox{6670}{relative} \markbox{6671}{projection} \markbox{6672}{data} \markbox{6673}{associated} \markbox{6674}{to} \markbox{6675}{intervals} \markbox{m6676}{$T_U$}, \markbox{6677}{i.e.} \markbox{6678}{the} \markbox{m6679}{$\delta^V_U$}, \markbox{6680}{in} \markbox{6681}{an} \markbox{6682}{interval} \markbox{6683}{system} \markbox{6684}{to} \markbox{6685}{remove} \markbox{6686}{coarseness} \markbox{6687}{from} \markbox{6688}{the} \markbox{6689}{setup.}  \markbox{6690}{The} \markbox{6691}{idea} \markbox{6692}{is} \markbox{6693}{that} \markbox{6694}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{6695}{roughly} \markbox{6696}{encodes} \markbox{6697}{the} \markbox{6698}{projection} \markbox{6699}{data} \markbox{6700}{up} \markbox{6701}{to} \markbox{6702}{a} \markbox{6703}{controlled} \markbox{6704}{error.}  \markbox{6705}{In} \markbox{6706}{slightly} \markbox{6707}{more} \markbox{6708}{detail,} \markbox{6709}{observe} \markbox{6710}{that} \markbox{6711}{each} \markbox{6712}{interval} \markbox{m6713}{$T_U$} \markbox{6714}{contains} \markbox{6715}{the} \markbox{6716}{relative} \markbox{6717}{projections} \markbox{m6718}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{6719}{for} \markbox{m6720}{$V \nest U$}.  \markbox{6721}{We} \markbox{6722}{would} \markbox{6723}{like} \markbox{6724}{to} \markbox{6725}{collect} \markbox{6726}{close-by} \markbox{6727}{relative} \markbox{6728}{projections} \markbox{6729}{into} \markbox{6730}{single} \markbox{6731}{intervals} \markbox{6732}{called} \markbox{6733}{\emph{cluster components}}, \markbox{6734}{so} \markbox{6735}{that} \markbox{6736}{we} \markbox{6737}{can} \markbox{6738}{later} \markbox{6739}{collapse} \markbox{6740}{them.}  \markbox{6741}{One} \markbox{6742}{complication} \markbox{6743}{is} \markbox{6744}{that} \markbox{6745}{the} \markbox{m6746}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{6747}{need} \markbox{6748}{not} \markbox{6749}{be} \markbox{6750}{subintervals} \markbox{6751}{of} \markbox{m6752}{$T_U$}, \markbox{6753}{so} \markbox{6754}{we} \markbox{6755}{need} \markbox{6756}{a} \markbox{6757}{couple} \markbox{6758}{of} \markbox{6759}{constants---one} \markbox{6760}{to} \markbox{6761}{determine} \markbox{6762}{what} \markbox{6763}{it} \markbox{6764}{means} \markbox{6765}{for} \markbox{6766}{relative} \markbox{6767}{projections} \markbox{6768}{to} \markbox{6769}{be} \markbox{6770}{``close'',} \markbox{6771}{and} \markbox{6772}{the} \markbox{6773}{other} \markbox{6774}{to} \markbox{6775}{guarantee} \markbox{6776}{that} \markbox{6777}{cluster} \markbox{6778}{components} \markbox{6779}{which} \markbox{6780}{are} \markbox{6781}{not} \markbox{6782}{close} \markbox{6783}{satisfy} \markbox{6784}{a} \markbox{6785}{minimum} \markbox{6786}{distance} bound.



We \markbox{6787}{will} \markbox{6788}{use} \markbox{6789}{the} \markbox{6790}{following} \markbox{6791}{slightly} \markbox{6792}{more} \markbox{6793}{abstract} \markbox{6794}{setup,} \markbox{6795}{as} \markbox{6796}{it} \markbox{6797}{will} \markbox{6798}{be} \markbox{6799}{useful} \markbox{6800}{later} \markbox{6801}{during} \markbox{6802}{our} \markbox{6803}{stabilization} process:

 \begin{definition}[Thickenings]\label{defn:thickening}
Let \markbox{m6804}{$T$} \markbox{6805}{be} \markbox{6806}{an} \markbox{6807}{interval} \markbox{6808}{with} \markbox{6809}{a} \markbox{6810}{decomposition} \markbox{m6811}{$T = A \cup B$} \markbox{6812}{into} \markbox{6813}{collections} \markbox{6814}{of} \markbox{6815}{segments.}  \markbox{6816}{Given} \markbox{m6817}{$r_1,r_2>0$}, \markbox{6818}{the} \markbox{m6819}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-\markbox{6820}{\emph{thickening}} \markbox{6821}{of} \markbox{m6822}{$T$} \markbox{6823}{\emph{along $B$}} \markbox{6824}{defines} \markbox{6825}{a} \markbox{6826}{decomposition} \markbox{m6827}{$T = \bT_e \cup \bT_c$} \markbox{6828}{into} \markbox{6829}{\emph{edge}} \markbox{m6830}{$\bT_e$} \markbox{6831}{and} \markbox{6832}{\emph{cluster}} \markbox{m6833}{$\bT_c$} \markbox{6834}{components} \markbox{6835}{as} follows:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} First, \markbox{6836}{take} \markbox{6837}{the} \markbox{m6838}{$r_1$}-neighborhoods \markbox{6839}{in} \markbox{m6840}{$T$} \markbox{6841}{of} \markbox{6842}{the} \markbox{6843}{components} \markbox{6844}{of} \markbox{m6845}{$B$}.  \markbox{6846}{Call} \markbox{6847}{the} \markbox{6848}{collection} \markbox{6849}{of} \markbox{6850}{these} \markbox{6851}{neighborhood} \markbox{m6852}{$\calB$}, \markbox{6853}{and} \markbox{6854}{their} \markbox{6855}{complement} \markbox{m6856}{$T - \calB = \calA$}.
\item {} Second, \markbox{6857}{connect} \markbox{6858}{any} \markbox{6859}{two} \markbox{6860}{subintervals} \markbox{6861}{in} \markbox{m6862}{$\calB$} \markbox{6863}{which} \markbox{6864}{come} \markbox{6865}{within} \markbox{m6866}{$r_2$} \markbox{6867}{of} \markbox{6868}{each} \markbox{6869}{other} \markbox{6870}{in} \markbox{m6871}{$T$} \markbox{6872}{by} \markbox{6873}{the} \markbox{6874}{geodesic} \markbox{6875}{between} \markbox{6876}{them.}  \markbox{6877}{Call} \markbox{6878}{the} \markbox{6879}{resulting} \markbox{6880}{collection} \markbox{6881}{of} \markbox{6882}{subintervals} \markbox{m6883}{$\bT_c$} \markbox{6884}{and} \markbox{6885}{set} \markbox{m6886}{$\bT_e = T- \bT_c$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}



In \markbox{6887}{our} \markbox{6888}{current} \markbox{6889}{context,} \markbox{6890}{we} \markbox{6891}{can} \markbox{6892}{take} \markbox{m6893}{$B$} \markbox{6894}{to} \markbox{6895}{be} \markbox{6896}{the} \markbox{6897}{collection} \markbox{6898}{of} \markbox{m6899}{$\delta^V_U \subset T_U$} \markbox{6900}{segments} \markbox{6901}{for} \markbox{m6902}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{6903}{along} \markbox{6904}{with} \markbox{6905}{the} \markbox{6906}{marked} \markbox{6907}{points} \markbox{m6908}{$a_U,b_U$} \markbox{6909}{on} \markbox{m6910}{$T_U$} \markbox{6911}{(Definition} \ref{defn:marked}).  \markbox{6912}{Thus} \markbox{6913}{a} \markbox{6914}{thickening} \markbox{6915}{of} \markbox{m6916}{$T_U$} \markbox{6917}{along} \markbox{6918}{this} \markbox{6919}{collection} \markbox{m6920}{$B$} \markbox{6921}{expands} \markbox{6922}{the} \markbox{m6923}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{6924}{segments} \markbox{6925}{and} \markbox{m6926}{$a_U,b_U$} \markbox{6927}{and} \markbox{6928}{combines} \markbox{6929}{nearby} \markbox{6930}{expansions.}  \markbox{6931}{For} \markbox{6932}{each} \markbox{m6933}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{6934}{we} \markbox{6935}{denote} \markbox{6936}{the} \markbox{6937}{resulting} \markbox{6938}{decomposition} \markbox{6939}{of} \markbox{6940}{the} \markbox{6941}{thickened} \markbox{6942}{interval} \markbox{6943}{by} \markbox{m6944}{$T_U = \bT^e_{U} \cup \bT^c_{U}$}.  \markbox{6945}{When} \markbox{6946}{we} \markbox{6947}{perform} \markbox{6948}{an} \markbox{m6949}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{6950}{to} \markbox{6951}{each} \markbox{6952}{interval} \markbox{6953}{in} \markbox{6954}{an} \markbox{6955}{interval} \markbox{6956}{system,} \markbox{6957}{we} \markbox{6958}{refer} \markbox{6959}{to} \markbox{6960}{the} \markbox{6961}{resulting} \markbox{6962}{collection} \markbox{6963}{of} \markbox{6964}{thickened} \markbox{6965}{intervals} \markbox{6966}{as} \markbox{6967}{a} \markbox{m6968}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-\markbox{6969}{\emph{thickening}} \markbox{6970}{of} \markbox{6971}{the} \markbox{6972}{interval} system.

\begin{remark}
In \markbox{6973}{our} \markbox{6974}{context,} \markbox{6975}{we} \markbox{6976}{will} \markbox{6977}{be} \markbox{6978}{able} \markbox{6979}{to} \markbox{6980}{control} \markbox{6981}{the} \markbox{6982}{constants} \markbox{m6983}{$r_1,r_2>0$} \markbox{6984}{in} \markbox{6985}{terms} \markbox{6986}{of} \markbox{6987}{the} \markbox{6988}{ambient} \markbox{6989}{HHS,} \markbox{6990}{and,} \markbox{6991}{importantly,} \markbox{6992}{we} \markbox{6993}{will} \markbox{6994}{be} \markbox{6995}{able} \markbox{6996}{to} \markbox{6997}{choose} \markbox{6998}{our} \markbox{6999}{largeness} \markbox{7000}{constant} \markbox{m7001}{$K$} \markbox{7002}{to} \markbox{7003}{be} \markbox{7004}{independent} \markbox{7005}{of} them.
\end{remark}





\subsection{Collapsed intervals and $0$-consistency} \label{subsec:collapsing}

Let \markbox{m7006}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{7007}{be} \markbox{7008}{an} \markbox{m7009}{$R$}-interval \markbox{7010}{system} \markbox{7011}{for} \markbox{m7012}{$a,b \in \calX$}.  \markbox{7013}{Fix} \markbox{m7014}{$r_i = r_i(R, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7015}{for} \markbox{m7016}{$i=1,2$} \markbox{7017}{to} \markbox{7018}{be} \markbox{7019}{determined} \markbox{7020}{soon.}  \markbox{7021}{For} \markbox{7022}{each} \markbox{m7023}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{7024}{let} \markbox{m7025}{$T_U = \bT^e_U \cup \bT^c_U$} \markbox{7026}{denote} \markbox{7027}{its} \markbox{m7028}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening, \markbox{7029}{as} \markbox{7030}{in} \markbox{7031}{Definition} \ref{defn:thickening}.

Let \markbox{m7032}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{7033}{denote} \markbox{7034}{the} \markbox{7035}{map} \markbox{7036}{which} \markbox{7037}{collapses} \markbox{7038}{each} \markbox{7039}{component} \markbox{7040}{of} \markbox{m7041}{$\bT^c_U$} \markbox{7042}{to} \markbox{7043}{a} \markbox{7044}{point,} \markbox{7045}{each} \markbox{7046}{of} \markbox{7047}{which} \markbox{7048}{we} \markbox{7049}{call} \markbox{7050}{a} \markbox{7051}{\emph{collapsed point}}.  \markbox{7052}{The} \markbox{7053}{resulting} \markbox{7054}{object} \markbox{m7055}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{7056}{is} \markbox{7057}{an} \markbox{7058}{interval.}  \markbox{7059}{Note} \markbox{7060}{that} \markbox{7061}{by} \markbox{7062}{construction} \markbox{m7063}{$a_U, b_U \in \bT^c_U$} \markbox{7064}{for} \markbox{7065}{each} \markbox{m7066}{$U \in \calU$}.  \markbox{7067}{Hence} \markbox{7068}{each} \markbox{7069}{of} \markbox{m7070}{$a_U,b_U$} \markbox{7071}{determines} \markbox{7072}{a} \markbox{7073}{\emph{marked point}} \markbox{m7074}{$\ha_U,\hb_U \in \hT_U$}, \markbox{7075}{and} \markbox{7076}{these} \markbox{7077}{marked} \markbox{7078}{points} \markbox{m7079}{$\ha_U,\hb_U$} \markbox{7080}{will} \markbox{7081}{be} \markbox{7082}{the} \markbox{7083}{endpoints} \markbox{7084}{of} \markbox{7085}{the} \markbox{7086}{(collapsed)} \markbox{7087}{interval} \markbox{m7088}{$\hT_U$}.  \markbox{7089}{Moreover,} \markbox{7090}{the} \markbox{7091}{decomposition} \markbox{m7092}{$T_U = \bT^e_U \cup \bT^c_U$} \markbox{7093}{descends} \markbox{7094}{to} \markbox{7095}{a} \markbox{7096}{decomposition} \markbox{m7097}{$\hT_U = \hT^e_U \cup \hT^c_U$}, \markbox{7098}{where} \markbox{7099}{the} \markbox{7100}{components} \markbox{7101}{of} \markbox{m7102}{$\hT^c_U$} \markbox{7103}{are} \markbox{7104}{the} \markbox{7105}{collapsed} \markbox{7106}{points} \markbox{7107}{corresponding} \markbox{7108}{to} \markbox{7109}{the} \markbox{7110}{components} \markbox{7111}{of} \markbox{m7112}{$\bT^c_U$}, \markbox{7113}{and} \markbox{7114}{the} \markbox{7115}{components} \markbox{7116}{of} \markbox{m7117}{$\hT^e_U$} \markbox{7118}{are} \markbox{7119}{isometric} \markbox{7120}{images} \markbox{7121}{of} \markbox{7122}{the} \markbox{7123}{components} \markbox{7124}{of} \markbox{m7125}{$\bT^e_U$}.

Combining \markbox{7126}{these} \markbox{m7127}{$q_U$} \markbox{7128}{maps} \markbox{7129}{with} \markbox{7130}{our} \markbox{7131}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{7132}{projections} \markbox{m7133}{$\psi_U:H \to T_U$}, \markbox{7134}{we} \markbox{7135}{get} \markbox{7136}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{7137}{maps} \markbox{m7138}{$\hpsi_U:H \to \hT_U$} \markbox{7139}{to} \markbox{7140}{the} \markbox{7141}{collapsed} \markbox{7142}{intervals,} \markbox{7143}{and} \markbox{7144}{hence} \markbox{7145}{combining} \markbox{7146}{these} \markbox{7147}{gives} \markbox{7148}{a} \markbox{7149}{global} \markbox{7150}{map} \markbox{m7151}{$\hPsi:H \to \prod_U \hT_U$}.

We \markbox{7152}{can} \markbox{7153}{define} \markbox{7154}{\emph{collapsed relative projections}} \markbox{m7155}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{7156}{in} \markbox{7157}{the} \markbox{7158}{obvious} \markbox{7159}{way,} \markbox{7160}{by} \markbox{7161}{composing} \markbox{7162}{with} \markbox{7163}{the} \markbox{7164}{quotient} \markbox{7165}{maps} \markbox{m7166}{$q_U$}.  \markbox{7167}{Similarly,} \markbox{7168}{consistency} \markbox{7169}{in} \markbox{7170}{this} \markbox{7171}{setting} \markbox{7172}{is} \markbox{7173}{the} \markbox{7174}{appropriate} \markbox{7175}{analogue} \markbox{7176}{of} \markbox{7177}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency}, \markbox{7178}{except} \markbox{7179}{now} \markbox{7180}{all} \markbox{7181}{coarseness} \markbox{7182}{has} \markbox{7183}{been} removed:

\begin{definition} \label{defn:Q defined}
A \markbox{7184}{tuple} \markbox{m7185}{$(\hx_U) \in \prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_U$} \markbox{7186}{is} \markbox{m7187}{$0$}-\markbox{7188}{\emph{consistent}} \markbox{7189}{if} \markbox{7190}{the} \markbox{7191}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} For \markbox{7192}{any} \markbox{m7193}{$U \pitchfork V \in \calU$}, \markbox{7194}{either} \markbox{m7195}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$} \markbox{7196}{or} \markbox{m7197}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V$}.
\item {} For \markbox{7198}{any} \markbox{m7199}{$U \nest V \in \calU$}, \markbox{7200}{either} \markbox{m7201}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V$} \markbox{7202}{or} \markbox{m7203}{$\hx_U \in \hd^V_U(\hx_V) \subset \hT_U$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item {} We \markbox{7204}{let} \markbox{m7205}{$\calQ$} \markbox{7206}{denote} \markbox{7207}{set} \markbox{7208}{of} \markbox{m7209}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{7210}{tuples} \markbox{7211}{in} \markbox{m7212}{$\prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_U$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}



We \markbox{7213}{can} \markbox{7214}{prove} \markbox{7215}{that} \markbox{m7216}{$\hPsi$} \markbox{7217}{has} \markbox{7218}{image} \markbox{7219}{in} \markbox{m7220}{$\calQ$}:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:hPsi defined}
For \markbox{7221}{any} \markbox{m7222}{$R>0$},  \markbox{7223}{there} \markbox{7224}{exists} \markbox{m7225}{$R_1 = R_1(R,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7226}{so} \markbox{7227}{that} \markbox{7228}{for} \markbox{7229}{any} \markbox{m7230}{$r_1 > R_1$} \markbox{7231}{and} \markbox{m7232}{$r_2>0$}, \markbox{7233}{if} \markbox{m7234}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{7235}{are} \markbox{7236}{the} \markbox{7237}{collapsed} \markbox{7238}{intervals} \markbox{7239}{associated} \markbox{7240}{to} \markbox{7241}{an} \markbox{m7242}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{7243}{of} \markbox{7244}{an} \markbox{m7245}{$R$}-interval \markbox{7246}{system} \markbox{7247}{for} \markbox{m7248}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{7249}{and} \markbox{m7250}{$x \in \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}, \markbox{7251}{then} \markbox{m7252}{$\hPsi(x) = (\hx_U) \in \calQ$}.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
We \markbox{7253}{need} \markbox{7254}{to} \markbox{7255}{prove} \markbox{m7256}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{7257}{of} \markbox{m7258}{$\hPsi(x)$} \markbox{7259}{as} \markbox{7260}{in} \markbox{7261}{Definition} \ref{defn:Q defined}.

First \markbox{7262}{suppose} \markbox{7263}{that} \markbox{m7264}{$U \pitchfork V \in \calU$}.  \markbox{7265}{Since} \markbox{m7266}{$\Psi(x) = (x_V)$} \markbox{7267}{is} \markbox{m7268}{$\alpha_0$}-consistent \markbox{7269}{by} \markbox{7270}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval consistency} \markbox{7271}{where} \markbox{m7272}{$\alpha_0=\alpha_0(R,\theta,\mathfrak S)>0$}, \markbox{7273}{we} \markbox{7274}{have,} \markbox{7275}{without} \markbox{7276}{loss} \markbox{7277}{of} \markbox{7278}{generality,} \markbox{7279}{that} \markbox{m7280}{$d_{T_U}(x_U, \delta^V_U)< \alpha_0$}.  \markbox{7281}{Hence} \markbox{m7282}{$q_U(x_U) = \hd^V_U$} \markbox{7283}{as} \markbox{7284}{long} \markbox{7285}{as} \markbox{m7286}{$r_1 > \alpha_0$}.  

Next \markbox{7287}{suppose} \markbox{7288}{that} \markbox{m7289}{$U \nest V \in \calU$}.  \markbox{7290}{If} \markbox{m7291}{$d_{T_V}(x_V, \delta^U_V)< \alpha_0 < r_1$}, \markbox{7292}{then} \markbox{m7293}{$q_V(x_V) = \hd^U_V$}, \markbox{7294}{and} \markbox{7295}{we} \markbox{7296}{are} \markbox{7297}{done.}  \markbox{7298}{Otherwise,} \markbox{7299}{we} \markbox{7300}{have} \markbox{m7301}{$\diam_{T_U}(x_U \cup \delta^V_U(x_V))<\alpha_0$} \markbox{7302}{while} \markbox{7303}{also} \markbox{m7304}{$d_{T_V}(x_V, \delta^U_V)>\alpha_0$}.  \markbox{7305}{By} \markbox{7306}{taking} \markbox{m7307}{$\alpha_0 > R$}, \markbox{7308}{we} \markbox{7309}{have} \markbox{7310}{that} \markbox{m7311}{$\diam_{T_U}(\delta^V_U(x_V)\cup f_U)< R$} \markbox{7312}{for} \markbox{7313}{some} \markbox{m7314}{$f \in \{a,b\}$} \markbox{7315}{by} \markbox{7316}{the} \markbox{7317}{BGI} \markbox{7318}{property} \markbox{7319}{in} \markbox{7320}{item} \markbox{7321}{(4)} \markbox{7322}{of} \markbox{7323}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms}.  \markbox{7324}{In} \markbox{7325}{particular,} \markbox{7326}{setting} \markbox{m7327}{$r_1>\alpha_0 + R$}, \markbox{7328}{then} \markbox{7329}{both} \markbox{m7330}{$x_U$} \markbox{7331}{and} \markbox{m7332}{$\delta^V_U(x_V)$} \markbox{7333}{are} \markbox{7334}{within} \markbox{m7335}{$\alpha_0 + R< r_1$} \markbox{7336}{of} \markbox{m7337}{$f_U$}, \markbox{7338}{and} \markbox{7339}{hence} \markbox{m7340}{$q_U(x_U) = q_V(\delta^V_U(x_V))$}.  \markbox{7341}{Finally,} \markbox{7342}{observe} \markbox{7343}{that} \markbox{m7344}{$q^{-1}_V(q_V(x_V))$} \markbox{7345}{is} \markbox{7346}{contained} \markbox{7347}{in} \markbox{7348}{the} \markbox{7349}{component} \markbox{7350}{of} \markbox{m7351}{$T_V - \mathcal{N}_{R}(\delta^U_V)$} \markbox{7352}{containing} \markbox{m7353}{$x_V$}, \markbox{7354}{and} \markbox{7355}{hence} \markbox{m7356}{$q_V(\delta^V_U(x_V)) = \hd^V_U(q_V(x_V))$}.  \markbox{7357}{This} \markbox{7358}{completes} \markbox{7359}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

\subsection{Controlling the collapsed intervals}

In \markbox{7360}{this} \markbox{7361}{subsection,} \markbox{7362}{we} \markbox{7363}{record} \markbox{7364}{the} \markbox{7365}{following} \markbox{7366}{technical} \markbox{7367}{lemma,} \markbox{7368}{which} \markbox{7369}{is} \markbox{7370}{in} \markbox{7371}{part} \markbox{7372}{a} \markbox{7373}{collapsed} \markbox{7374}{version} \markbox{7375}{of} \markbox{7376}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control}, \markbox{7377}{but} \markbox{7378}{also} \markbox{7379}{contains} \markbox{7380}{the} \markbox{7381}{conclusion} \markbox{7382}{of} \markbox{7383}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}.  \markbox{7384}{The} \markbox{7385}{statement} \markbox{7386}{and} \markbox{7387}{its} \markbox{7388}{proof} \markbox{7389}{are} \markbox{7390}{basically} \cite[Lemma 7.13]{Dur_infcube}.

\begin{lemma}[Collapsed \markbox{7391}{interval} control]\label{lem:collapsed interval control}
Let \markbox{m7392}{$R>0$} \markbox{7393}{and} \markbox{m7394}{$r_1 > R_1$} \markbox{7395}{for} \markbox{m7396}{$R_1 = R_1(R,\theta, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7397}{as} \markbox{7398}{in} \markbox{7399}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}.  \markbox{7400}{There} \markbox{7401}{exists} \markbox{m7402}{$R_2 = R_2(R,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7403}{so} \markbox{7404}{that} \markbox{7405}{for} \markbox{7406}{any} \markbox{m7407}{$r_2>R_2$}, \markbox{7408}{the} \markbox{7409}{following} \markbox{7410}{hold} \markbox{7411}{for} \markbox{7412}{any} \markbox{m7413}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{7414}{of} \markbox{7415}{an} \markbox{m7416}{$R$}-interval \markbox{7417}{system} \markbox{7418}{for} \markbox{m7419}{$a,b \in \calX$}: 
\begin{enumerate}
    \item {} For \markbox{7420}{any} \markbox{m7421}{$x \in H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}, \markbox{7422}{the} \markbox{7423}{tuple} \markbox{m7424}{$\hPsi(x) \in \calQ$} \markbox{7425}{is} \markbox{m7426}{$0$}-consistent.
    
    \item {} If \markbox{m7427}{$U \pitchfork V \in \calU$}, \markbox{7428}{then} \markbox{7429}{both} \markbox{m7430}{$\hd^V_U \in \hT_U$} \markbox{7431}{and} \markbox{m7432}{$\hd^U_V \in \hT_V$} \markbox{7433}{are} \markbox{7434}{in} \markbox{m7435}{$\{\ha_U, \hb_U\}$}.
    
    \item {} If \markbox{m7436}{$U \nest V \in \calU$}, \markbox{7437}{then} \markbox{m7438}{$\hd^U_V$} \markbox{7439}{coincides} \markbox{7440}{with} \markbox{7441}{a} \markbox{7442}{collapsed} point.
    
    \item {} For \markbox{7443}{any} \markbox{m7444}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{7445}{and} \markbox{7446}{any} \markbox{m7447}{$x,y \in H$}, \markbox{7448}{we} \markbox{7449}{have} \markbox{m7450}{$d_U(x,y) \asymp d_{T_U}(x_u,y_U)\geq d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U)$}, \markbox{7451}{with} \markbox{7452}{the} \markbox{7453}{constants} \markbox{7454}{in} \markbox{m7455}{$\asymp$} \markbox{7456}{depending} \markbox{7457}{only} \markbox{7458}{on} \markbox{m7459}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{7460}{and} \markbox{m7461}{$R$}.
  
    
    \item {} If \markbox{m7462}{$x,y \in H$} \markbox{7463}{and} \markbox{m7464}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{7465}{and} \markbox{m7466}{$\hpsi_U(x), \hpsi_U(y)$} \markbox{7467}{are} \markbox{7468}{distinct} \markbox{7469}{collapsed} \markbox{7470}{points,} \markbox{7471}{then} \markbox{m7472}{$d_U(x,y) > 50\ES$}.
    
    \item {} If \markbox{m7473}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{7474}{is} \markbox{m7475}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal, \markbox{7476}{then} \markbox{m7477}{$d_{\hT_U}(\ha_U,\hb_U) \succ K - 2r_1$}, \markbox{7478}{with} \markbox{7479}{the} \markbox{7480}{constants} \markbox{7481}{in} \markbox{m7482}{$\succ$} \markbox{7483}{depending} \markbox{7484}{only} \markbox{7485}{on} \markbox{m7486}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{7487}{and} \markbox{7488}{where} \markbox{m7489}{$K = K(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7490}{is} \markbox{7491}{chosen} \markbox{7492}{independent} \markbox{7493}{of} \markbox{7494}{the} setup.
    
    \item {} (Bounded \markbox{7495}{geodesic} \markbox{7496}{image)} \markbox{7497}{Suppose} \markbox{m7498}{$V \nest U$}, \markbox{m7499}{$C \subset \hT_U - \hd^V_U$} \markbox{7500}{is} \markbox{7501}{a} \markbox{7502}{component,} \markbox{7503}{then} \markbox{m7504}{$\hd^U_V(C)$} \markbox{7505}{is} \markbox{7506}{a} \markbox{7507}{point.}  \markbox{7508}{In} \markbox{7509}{particular,} \markbox{7510}{if} \markbox{m7511}{$f \in \{a,b\}$} \markbox{7512}{with} \markbox{m7513}{$\hf_U$} \markbox{7514}{contained} \markbox{7515}{in} \markbox{m7516}{$C$}, \markbox{7517}{then} \markbox{m7518}{$\hd^U_V(C) = \hf_V.$}

 \item {} If \markbox{m7519}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{7520}{then} \markbox{m7521}{$\{U \in \calU| \hx_U \notin \{\ha_U,\hb_U\}\}$} \markbox{7522}{is} \markbox{7523}{pairwise} \markbox{7524}{non-transverse,} \markbox{7525}{and} \markbox{7526}{hence} \markbox{7527}{has} \markbox{7528}{cardinality} \markbox{7529}{bounded} \markbox{7530}{in} \markbox{7531}{terms} \markbox{7532}{of} \markbox{m7533}{$\mathfrak S$}.
   
    
    \item {} If \markbox{m7534}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{7535}{then} \markbox{m7536}{$E(\hx) = \{U \in \calU| \hx_U \in \hT^e_U\}$} \markbox{7537}{is} \markbox{7538}{pairwise} orthogonal.
    
   
\end{enumerate}
\end{lemma}

\begin{remark}
Item \markbox{7539}{(5)} \markbox{7540}{is} \markbox{7541}{notably} \markbox{7542}{the} \markbox{7543}{first} \markbox{7544}{time} \markbox{7545}{that} \markbox{7546}{the} \markbox{7547}{constant} \markbox{m7548}{$r_2$} \markbox{7549}{from} \markbox{7550}{Definition} \ref{defn:thickening} \markbox{7551}{plays} \markbox{7552}{a} \markbox{7553}{substantial} \markbox{7554}{role.}  \markbox{7555}{This} \markbox{7556}{is} \markbox{7557}{important} \markbox{7558}{later} \markbox{7559}{in} \markbox{7560}{proving} \markbox{7561}{that} \markbox{7562}{the} \markbox{7563}{map} \markbox{m7564}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{7565}{between}  \markbox{m7566}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{7567}{set} \markbox{m7568}{$\calQ$} \markbox{7569}{and} \markbox{7570}{the} \markbox{7571}{hierarchical} \markbox{7572}{hull} \markbox{m7573}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{7574}{is} \markbox{7575}{a} \markbox{7576}{quasi-isometry.}  \markbox{7577}{Another} \markbox{7578}{notable} \markbox{7579}{statement} \markbox{7580}{is} \markbox{7581}{item} \markbox{7582}{(6),} \markbox{7583}{which} \markbox{7584}{is} \markbox{7585}{about} \markbox{m7586}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{7587}{domains,} \markbox{7588}{namely} \markbox{7589}{domains} \markbox{m7590}{$U$} \markbox{7591}{for} \markbox{7592}{which} \markbox{7593}{no} \markbox{m7594}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{7595}{has} \markbox{m7596}{$V \nest U$}.  \markbox{7597}{Here} \markbox{7598}{is} \markbox{7599}{where} \markbox{7600}{our} \markbox{7601}{largeness} \markbox{7602}{constant} \markbox{m7603}{$K$} \markbox{7604}{plays} \markbox{7605}{a} \markbox{7606}{crucial} \markbox{7607}{role.}  \markbox{7608}{In} \markbox{7609}{particular,} \markbox{7610}{since} \markbox{7611}{nothing} \markbox{7612}{nests} \markbox{7613}{into} \markbox{7614}{a} \markbox{m7615}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{7616}{domain} \markbox{m7617}{$U$}, \markbox{7618}{the} \markbox{7619}{map} \markbox{m7620}{$q_U: T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{7621}{only} \markbox{7622}{collapses} \markbox{7623}{the} \markbox{m7624}{$r_1$}-neighborhood \markbox{7625}{of} \markbox{7626}{each} \markbox{7627}{endpoint,} \markbox{7628}{and} \markbox{7629}{hence} \markbox{7630}{the} \markbox{7631}{diameter} \markbox{7632}{of} \markbox{m7633}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{7634}{is} \markbox{7635}{coarsely} \markbox{7636}{bounded} \markbox{7637}{below} \markbox{7638}{by} \markbox{m7639}{$K$}.  \markbox{7640}{This} \markbox{7641}{is} \markbox{7642}{also} \markbox{7643}{important} \markbox{7644}{for} \markbox{7645}{confirming} \markbox{7646}{that} \markbox{m7647}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{7648}{is} \markbox{7649}{a} \markbox{7650}{quasi-isometry;} \markbox{7651}{see} \markbox{7652}{Section} \ref{sec:hPsi qi} below.
\end{remark}

\begin{proof}
Item \markbox{7653}{(1)} \markbox{7654}{is}  \markbox{7655}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}.  \markbox{7656}{Item} \markbox{7657}{(2)follows} \markbox{7658}{from} \markbox{7659}{item} \markbox{7660}{(2)} \markbox{7661}{of} \markbox{7662}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{7663}{by} \markbox{7664}{choosing} \markbox{m7665}{$r_1>2R$}.  \markbox{7666}{Similarly,} \markbox{7667}{item} \markbox{7668}{(3)} \markbox{7669}{follows} \markbox{7670}{from} \markbox{7671}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{7672}{(namely,} \markbox{7673}{item} \markbox{7674}{(1)} \markbox{7675}{of} \markbox{7676}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control}) \markbox{7677}{by} \markbox{7678}{choosing} \markbox{m7679}{$r_1 > 2R$}.  

Item \markbox{7680}{(4)} \markbox{7681}{follows} \markbox{7682}{directly} \markbox{7683}{from} \markbox{7684}{the} \markbox{7685}{construction} \markbox{7686}{and} \markbox{7687}{item} \markbox{7688}{(3)} \markbox{7689}{of} \markbox{7690}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms}.

Item \markbox{7691}{(4)} \markbox{7692}{is} \markbox{7693}{an} \markbox{7694}{immediate} \markbox{7695}{consequence} \markbox{7696}{of} \markbox{7697}{the} \markbox{7698}{definition} \markbox{7699}{of} \markbox{7700}{the} \markbox{7701}{hull} \markbox{m7702}{$H$} \markbox{7703}{(Definition} \ref{defn:hier hull}) \markbox{7704}{and} \markbox{7705}{the} \markbox{7706}{construction} \markbox{7707}{in} \markbox{7708}{this} \markbox{7709}{subsection.}  \markbox{7710}{In} \markbox{7711}{particular,} \markbox{7712}{by} \markbox{7713}{assumption} \markbox{m7714}{$\phi_U:T_U \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{7715}{is} \markbox{7716}{an} \markbox{m7717}{$(R,R)$}-quasi-geodesic \markbox{7718}{between} \markbox{m7719}{$\pi_U(a), \pi_U(b)$}, \markbox{7720}{giving} \markbox{7721}{the} \markbox{7722}{coarse} \markbox{7723}{equality,} \markbox{7724}{while} \markbox{7725}{the} \markbox{7726}{inequality} \markbox{7727}{follows} \markbox{7728}{because} \markbox{m7729}{$q_U:T_U\to \hT_U$} \markbox{7730}{collapses} \markbox{7731}{subintervals} \markbox{7732}{and} \markbox{7733}{therefore} \markbox{7734}{is} \markbox{7735}{distance} non-increasing.


For \markbox{7736}{item} \markbox{7737}{(5),} \markbox{7738}{if} \markbox{m7739}{$\hpsi_U(x),\hpsi_U(y)$} \markbox{7740}{are} \markbox{7741}{in} \markbox{7742}{distinct} \markbox{7743}{clusters,} \markbox{7744}{then} \markbox{m7745}{$d_{T_U}(x,y) > r_2$}, \markbox{7746}{and} \markbox{7747}{hence} \markbox{m7748}{$d_U(x,y) \succ r_2$} \markbox{7749}{by} \markbox{7750}{item} \markbox{7751}{(4).}  \markbox{7752}{Hence} \markbox{7753}{choosing} \markbox{m7754}{$r_2$} \markbox{7755}{large} \markbox{7756}{enough} \markbox{7757}{gives} \markbox{7758}{the} \markbox{7759}{desired} \markbox{7760}{lower} bound.

For \markbox{7761}{item} \markbox{7762}{(6):} \markbox{7763}{When} \markbox{m7764}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{7765}{is} \markbox{m7766}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{7767}{with} \markbox{7768}{respect} \markbox{7769}{to} \markbox{m7770}{$\calU$}, \markbox{7771}{then} \markbox{m7772}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{7773}{only} \markbox{7774}{collapses} \markbox{7775}{the} \markbox{m7776}{$r_1$}-neighborhoods \markbox{7777}{of} \markbox{m7778}{$a_U,b_U$} \markbox{7779}{in} \markbox{m7780}{$T_U$}.  \markbox{7781}{Since} \markbox{m7782}{$d_U(a,b)>K$} \markbox{7783}{by} \markbox{7784}{assumption,} \markbox{7785}{it} \markbox{7786}{follows} \markbox{7787}{that} \markbox{m7788}{$d_{T_U}(a_U,b_U) \succ K$}, \markbox{7789}{while} \markbox{7790}{the} \markbox{7791}{map} \markbox{m7792}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{7793}{only} \markbox{7794}{collapses} \markbox{7795}{the} \markbox{m7796}{$r_1$}-neighborhoods \markbox{7797}{of} \markbox{m7798}{$a_U,b_U$}.  \markbox{7799}{Thus} \markbox{7800}{provided} \markbox{7801}{that} \markbox{m7802}{$K -2r_1 > r_2$} \markbox{7803}{(which} \markbox{7804}{we} \markbox{7805}{can} \markbox{7806}{arrange),} \markbox{7807}{the} \markbox{7808}{claim} follows.



For \markbox{7809}{item} \markbox{7810}{(7):} \markbox{7811}{By} \markbox{7812}{item} \markbox{7813}{(1),} \markbox{7814}{if} \markbox{m7815}{$\hf_U$} \markbox{7816}{is} \markbox{7817}{a} \markbox{7818}{marked} \markbox{7819}{point,} \markbox{7820}{then} \markbox{m7821}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{7822}{of} \markbox{m7823}{$(\hf_V) = \hPsi(f)$} \markbox{7824}{implies} \markbox{7825}{that} \markbox{m7826}{$\hd^U_V(\hf_U) = \hf_V$} \markbox{7827}{because} \markbox{m7828}{$d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U(f_U),f_V)<\alpha_0 < r_1$}, \markbox{7829}{where} \markbox{7830}{we} \markbox{7831}{note} \markbox{7832}{that} \markbox{m7833}{$\alpha_0 = \alpha_0(R, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{7834}{by} \markbox{7835}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval consistency}.  \markbox{7836}{On} \markbox{7837}{the} \markbox{7838}{other} \markbox{7839}{hand,} \markbox{7840}{since} \markbox{m7841}{$C \cap \hd^V_U = \emptyset$}, \markbox{7842}{we} \markbox{7843}{have} \markbox{m7844}{$d_{T_U}(q^{-1}_U(C), \delta^V_U)>R$}.  \markbox{7845}{Hence} \markbox{7846}{item} \markbox{7847}{(4)} \markbox{7848}{of} \markbox{7849}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{7850}{says} \markbox{7851}{that} \markbox{m7852}{$\diam_{T_V}(\delta^U_V(C))<R$}, \markbox{7853}{while} \markbox{7854}{also} \markbox{m7855}{$\delta^U_V(f_U) \subset \delta^V_U(C)$}.  \markbox{7856}{Hence} \markbox{m7857}{$d_{T_V}(\delta^U_V(C), f_V)<\alpha_0 + R<r_1$}, \markbox{7858}{where} \markbox{7859}{we} \markbox{7860}{guarantee} \markbox{7861}{the} \markbox{7862}{last} \markbox{7863}{inequality} \markbox{7864}{by} \markbox{7865}{increasing} \markbox{m7866}{$r_1$} \markbox{7867}{as} \markbox{7868}{necessary.}  \markbox{7869}{It} \markbox{7870}{follows} \markbox{7871}{then} \markbox{7872}{that} \markbox{m7873}{$\hd^U_V(C) = \hf_V$}, \markbox{7874}{as} claimed.



For \markbox{7875}{item} \markbox{7876}{(8):} \markbox{7877}{Suppose} \markbox{m7878}{$U, V$} \markbox{7879}{are} \markbox{7880}{transverse} \markbox{7881}{and} \markbox{m7882}{$\hx_U \notin  \{\ha_U, \hb_U\}$}.  \markbox{7883}{Since} \markbox{m7884}{$\hd^V_U \in \{\ha_U,\hb_U\}$} \markbox{7885}{by} \markbox{7886}{item} \markbox{7887}{(2)} \markbox{7888}{and} \markbox{7889}{hence} \markbox{m7890}{$\hx_U \neq \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{7891}{it} \markbox{7892}{follows} \markbox{7893}{from} \markbox{m7894}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{7895}{of} \markbox{m7896}{$\hx$} \markbox{7897}{that} \markbox{m7898}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V$}.  \markbox{7899}{Thus} \markbox{m7900}{$\hx_V \in \{\ha_V,\hb_V\}$} \markbox{7901}{and} \markbox{7902}{so} \markbox{7903}{the} \markbox{7904}{set} \markbox{7905}{in} \markbox{7906}{the} \markbox{7907}{statement} \markbox{7908}{of} \markbox{7909}{item} \markbox{7910}{(8)} \markbox{7911}{is} \markbox{7912}{pairwise} \markbox{7913}{non-transverse,} \markbox{7914}{and} \markbox{7915}{hence} \markbox{7916}{has} \markbox{7917}{bounded} \markbox{7918}{complexity} \markbox{7919}{by} \markbox{7920}{item} \markbox{7921}{(2)} \markbox{7922}{in} \markbox{7923}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:basic HHS}.

Finally, \markbox{7924}{for} \markbox{7925}{item} \markbox{7926}{(9):} \markbox{7927}{Recall} \markbox{7928}{that} \markbox{m7929}{$\hT^e_U = \hT_U - \hT^c_U$}, \markbox{7930}{where} \markbox{m7931}{$\hT^c_U$} \markbox{7932}{are} \markbox{7933}{the} \markbox{7934}{collapsed} \markbox{7935}{points.}  \markbox{7936}{Hence} \markbox{m7937}{$E(\hx)$} \markbox{7938}{is} \markbox{7939}{the} \markbox{7940}{set} \markbox{7941}{of} \markbox{7942}{domains} \markbox{7943}{where} \markbox{m7944}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{7945}{is} \markbox{7946}{not} \markbox{7947}{a} \markbox{7948}{collapsed} \markbox{7949}{point.}  \markbox{7950}{Supposing} \markbox{7951}{that} \markbox{m7952}{$U,V$} \markbox{7953}{are} \markbox{7954}{neither} \markbox{7955}{orthogonal} \markbox{7956}{nor} \markbox{7957}{(by} \markbox{7958}{item} \markbox{7959}{(8))} \markbox{7960}{transverse.}  \markbox{7961}{When} \markbox{m7962}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{7963}{and} \markbox{m7964}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{7965}{we} \markbox{7966}{are} \markbox{7967}{done} \markbox{7968}{by} \markbox{7969}{items} \markbox{7970}{(1)} \markbox{7971}{and} \markbox{7972}{(3).}  \markbox{7973}{When} \markbox{m7974}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{7975}{and} \markbox{m7976}{$\hx_U \neq \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{7977}{item} \markbox{7978}{(7)} \markbox{7979}{implies} \markbox{7980}{there} \markbox{7981}{is} \markbox{7982}{some} \markbox{m7983}{$f \in \{a,b\}$} \markbox{7984}{so} \markbox{7985}{that} \markbox{m7986}{$\hd^U_V(\hx_U) = \hf_V$}, \markbox{7987}{while} \markbox{m7988}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{7989}{says} \markbox{7990}{that} \markbox{m7991}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V(\hx_U)$}, \markbox{7992}{giving} \markbox{m7993}{$\hx_V = \hf_V$}.  \markbox{7994}{Hence} \markbox{7995}{if} \markbox{m7996}{$U$} \markbox{7997}{and} \markbox{m7998}{$V$} \markbox{7999}{are} \markbox{8000}{not} \markbox{8001}{orthogonal,} \markbox{8002}{then} \markbox{8003}{one} \markbox{8004}{of} \markbox{m8005}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{8006}{or} \markbox{m8007}{$\hx_V$} \markbox{8008}{must} \markbox{8009}{be} \markbox{8010}{a} \markbox{8011}{collapsed} \markbox{8012}{point,} \markbox{8013}{proving} \markbox{8014}{this} \markbox{8015}{item.}  \markbox{8016}{This} \markbox{8017}{completes} \markbox{8018}{the} proof.



\end{proof}














\section{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$ is a quasi-isometry} \label{sec:hPsi qi}

In \markbox{8019}{this} \markbox{8020}{section,} \markbox{8021}{we} \markbox{8022}{explain} \markbox{8023}{why} \markbox{8024}{the} \markbox{8025}{map} \markbox{m8026}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{8027}{(Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}) \markbox{8028}{between} \markbox{8029}{the} \markbox{8030}{hierarchical} \markbox{8031}{hull} \markbox{m8032}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{8033}{of} \markbox{8034}{a} \markbox{8035}{pair} \markbox{8036}{of} \markbox{8037}{points} \markbox{m8038}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{8039}{and} \markbox{8040}{the} \markbox{m8041}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{8042}{set} \markbox{8043}{associated} \markbox{8044}{to} \markbox{8045}{any} \markbox{8046}{sufficiently} \markbox{8047}{wide} \markbox{m8048}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{8049}{of} \markbox{8050}{an} \markbox{m8051}{$R$}-interval \markbox{8052}{system} \markbox{8053}{for} \markbox{m8054}{$a,b$} \markbox{8055}{is} \markbox{8056}{a} \markbox{8057}{quasi-isometry.}  \markbox{8058}{There} \markbox{8059}{are} \markbox{8060}{two} \markbox{8061}{main} \markbox{8062}{parts} \markbox{8063}{to} this:

\begin{enumerate}
\item {} Proving \markbox{8064}{that} \markbox{m8065}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{8066}{is} \markbox{8067}{a} \markbox{8068}{quasi-isometric} \markbox{8069}{embedding,} and
\item {} Proving \markbox{8070}{that} \markbox{m8071}{$\hPsi$} \markbox{8072}{is} \markbox{8073}{coarsely} \markbox{8074}{surjective.}  \markbox{8075}{This} \markbox{8076}{is} \markbox{8077}{accomplished} \markbox{8078}{by} \markbox{8079}{defining} \markbox{8080}{a} \markbox{8081}{coarse} \markbox{8082}{inverse} \markbox{m8083}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$}, \markbox{8084}{so} \markbox{8085}{that} \markbox{m8086}{$\hPsi \circ \hO$} \markbox{8087}{is} \markbox{8088}{coarsely} \markbox{8089}{the} \markbox{8090}{identity} \markbox{8091}{on} \markbox{m8092}{$\calQ$}.
\end{enumerate}

As \markbox{8093}{we} \markbox{8094}{shall} \markbox{8095}{see,} \markbox{8096}{these} \markbox{8097}{two} \markbox{8098}{results} \markbox{8099}{have} \markbox{8100}{fairly} \markbox{8101}{different} \markbox{8102}{flavors---(1)} \markbox{8103}{is} \markbox{8104}{essentially} \markbox{8105}{purely} \markbox{8106}{hierarchical,} \markbox{8107}{while} \markbox{8108}{(2)} \markbox{8109}{has} \markbox{8110}{distinctly} \markbox{8111}{cubical} \markbox{8112}{elements.}  \markbox{8113}{Item} \markbox{8114}{(1)} \markbox{8115}{essentially} \markbox{8116}{says} \markbox{8117}{that} \markbox{8118}{one} \markbox{8119}{can} \markbox{8120}{encode} \markbox{8121}{the} \markbox{8122}{distance} \markbox{8123}{formula} \markbox{8124}{in} \markbox{m8125}{$\calX$} \markbox{8126}{as} \markbox{8127}{the} \markbox{m8128}{$\ell^1$}-distance \markbox{8129}{in} \markbox{8130}{a} \markbox{8131}{product} \markbox{8132}{of} \markbox{8133}{intervals.}  \markbox{8134}{Its} \markbox{8135}{proof} \markbox{8136}{involves} \markbox{8137}{mostly} \markbox{8138}{distance} \markbox{8139}{formula-type} \markbox{8140}{arguments} \markbox{8141}{and} \markbox{8142}{we} \markbox{8143}{present} \markbox{8144}{it} \markbox{8145}{in} \markbox{8146}{full.}  \markbox{8147}{On} \markbox{8148}{the} \markbox{8149}{other} \markbox{8150}{hand,} \markbox{8151}{the} \markbox{8152}{proof} \markbox{8153}{of} \markbox{8154}{item} \markbox{8155}{(2),} \markbox{8156}{which} \markbox{8157}{is} \markbox{8158}{contained} \markbox{8159}{in} \cite[Sections 9--11]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{8160}{is} \markbox{8161}{rather} \markbox{8162}{involved} \markbox{8163}{and} \markbox{8164}{many} \markbox{8165}{of} \markbox{8166}{the} \markbox{8167}{details} \markbox{8168}{of} \markbox{8169}{the} \markbox{8170}{argument} \markbox{8171}{are} \markbox{8172}{not} \markbox{8173}{crucial} \markbox{8174}{to} \markbox{8175}{our} \markbox{8176}{expository} \markbox{8177}{purposes} \markbox{8178}{in} \markbox{8179}{this} \markbox{8180}{article.}  \markbox{8181}{Thus,} \markbox{8182}{in} \markbox{8183}{this} \markbox{8184}{section,} \markbox{8185}{we} \markbox{8186}{will} \markbox{8187}{mostly} \markbox{8188}{explain} \markbox{8189}{the} \markbox{8190}{basics} \markbox{8191}{of} \markbox{8192}{the} \markbox{8193}{construction,} \markbox{8194}{including} \markbox{8195}{the} \markbox{8196}{points} \markbox{8197}{where} \markbox{8198}{our} \markbox{8199}{simpler} \markbox{8200}{setting} \markbox{8201}{simplifies} \markbox{8202}{things} considerably.

The \markbox{8203}{one} \markbox{8204}{exception} \markbox{8205}{here} \markbox{8206}{is} \markbox{8207}{the} \markbox{8208}{Tree} \markbox{8209}{Trimming} \markbox{8210}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}, \markbox{8211}{which} \markbox{8212}{is} \markbox{8213}{a} \markbox{8214}{distance-formula} \markbox{8215}{like} \markbox{8216}{tool} \markbox{8217}{that} \markbox{8218}{we} \markbox{8219}{need} \markbox{8220}{both} \markbox{8221}{here} \markbox{8222}{and} \markbox{8223}{for} \markbox{8224}{our} \markbox{8225}{stability} \markbox{8226}{results} \markbox{8227}{in} \markbox{8228}{Section} \ref{sec:stable cubes}.  \markbox{8229}{We} \markbox{8230}{will} \markbox{8231}{discuss} \markbox{8232}{it} \markbox{8233}{in} \markbox{8234}{detail} \markbox{8235}{and} \markbox{8236}{present} \markbox{8237}{its} \markbox{8238}{proof} \markbox{8239}{in} \markbox{8240}{Appendix} \ref{app:TT}.

For \markbox{8241}{the} \markbox{8242}{rest} \markbox{8243}{of} \markbox{8244}{this} \markbox{8245}{section,} \markbox{8246}{fix} \markbox{m8247}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{8248}{and} \markbox{8249}{let} \markbox{m8250}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{8251}{to} \markbox{8252}{be} \markbox{8253}{their} \markbox{8254}{hierarchical} \markbox{8255}{hull.}  \markbox{8256}{Fix} \markbox{8257}{a} \markbox{8258}{largeness} \markbox{8259}{constant} \markbox{m8260}{$K$}, \markbox{8261}{which} \markbox{8262}{we} \markbox{8263}{will} \markbox{8264}{be} \markbox{8265}{able} \markbox{8266}{to} \markbox{8267}{control} \markbox{8268}{relative} \markbox{8269}{to} \markbox{8270}{all} \markbox{8271}{other} \markbox{8272}{involved} \markbox{8273}{constants,} \markbox{8274}{and} \markbox{8275}{set} \markbox{m8276}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b)$}.  \markbox{8277}{Finally,} \markbox{8278}{fix} \markbox{m8279}{$R>0$} \markbox{8280}{and} \markbox{8281}{an} \markbox{m8282}{$R$}-interval \markbox{8283}{system} \markbox{m8284}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{8285}{for} \markbox{m8286}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{8287}{Let} \markbox{m8288}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{8289}{denote} \markbox{8290}{the} \markbox{8291}{family} \markbox{8292}{of} \markbox{8293}{collapsed} \markbox{8294}{intervals} \markbox{8295}{corresponding} \markbox{8296}{to} \markbox{8297}{an} \markbox{m8298}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening, \markbox{8299}{where} \markbox{m8300}{$r_i = r_i(R,\theta,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{8301}{are} \markbox{8302}{provided} \markbox{8303}{by} \markbox{8304}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined} \markbox{8305}{and} \markbox{8306}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.

\subsection{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$ is a quasi-isometric embedding}\label{subsec:Q qie}

The \markbox{8307}{content} \markbox{8308}{of} \markbox{8309}{this} \markbox{8310}{subsection} \markbox{8311}{is} \markbox{8312}{roughly} \markbox{8313}{contained} \markbox{8314}{in} \cite[Section 8]{Dur_infcube}.  

Before \markbox{8315}{we} \markbox{8316}{state} \markbox{8317}{the} \markbox{8318}{result,} \markbox{8319}{we} \markbox{8320}{set} \markbox{8321}{some} \markbox{8322}{additional} \markbox{8323}{notation:} \markbox{8324}{For} \markbox{8325}{numbers} \markbox{m8326}{$A,B$}, \markbox{8327}{the} \markbox{8328}{notation} \markbox{m8329}{$[A]_B$} \markbox{8330}{means} \markbox{m8331}{$0$} \markbox{8332}{when} \markbox{m8333}{$A<B$} \markbox{8334}{and} \markbox{m8335}{$A$} \markbox{8336}{when} \markbox{m8337}{$A\geq B$}.  \markbox{8338}{For} \markbox{m8339}{$x \in H$} \markbox{8340}{and} \markbox{m8341}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{8342}{we} \markbox{8343}{will} write
\begin{itemize}
\item {} \markbox{m8344}{$x = \pi_U(x) \in \calC(U)$};
\item {} \markbox{m8345}{$x_U = \psi_U(x) \in T_U$};
\item {} \markbox{m8346}{$\hx_U = \hpsi_U(x) \in \hT_U$}.
\end{itemize}

\begin{theorem}\label{thm:Q distance estimate}
There \markbox{8347}{exists} \markbox{m8348}{$K_1 = K_1(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{8349}{so} \markbox{8350}{that} \markbox{8351}{for} \markbox{8352}{any} \markbox{m8353}{$K_2 \geq K_1$} \markbox{8354}{and} \markbox{8355}{any} \markbox{m8356}{$x, y \in H$}, \markbox{8357}{we} \markbox{8358}{have} that
$$d_{\calX}(a,b) \asymp \sum_{U \in \mathfrak S} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2} \asymp \sum_{U \in \calU} d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U)$$
where \markbox{8359}{the} \markbox{8360}{constants} \markbox{8361}{in} \markbox{m8362}{$\asymp$} \markbox{8363}{only} \markbox{8364}{depend} \markbox{8365}{on} \markbox{m8366}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{8367}{and} \markbox{8368}{the} \markbox{8369}{choice} \markbox{8370}{of} \markbox{m8371}{$K_2$}.
\end{theorem}

We \markbox{8372}{note} \markbox{8373}{that} \markbox{8374}{the} \markbox{8375}{left} \markbox{8376}{coarse} \markbox{8377}{equality} \markbox{8378}{of} \markbox{8379}{the} \markbox{8380}{above} \markbox{8381}{statement} \markbox{8382}{is} \markbox{8383}{simply} \markbox{8384}{the} \markbox{8385}{Distance} \markbox{8386}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}, \markbox{8387}{hence} \markbox{8388}{the} \markbox{8389}{content} \markbox{8390}{is} \markbox{8391}{the} \markbox{8392}{right} \markbox{8393}{coarse} \markbox{8394}{equality.}  \markbox{8395}{In} \markbox{8396}{fact,} \markbox{8397}{one} \markbox{8398}{can} \markbox{8399}{obtain} \markbox{8400}{the} \markbox{8401}{(more} \markbox{8402}{difficult)} \markbox{8403}{lower-bound} \markbox{8404}{in} \markbox{8405}{the} \markbox{8406}{distance} \markbox{8407}{formula} \markbox{8408}{by} \markbox{8409}{combining} \markbox{8410}{the} \markbox{8411}{above} \markbox{8412}{theorem} \markbox{8413}{with} \markbox{8414}{the} \markbox{8415}{construction} \markbox{8416}{of} \markbox{8417}{hierarchy} \markbox{8418}{paths} \markbox{8419}{via} \markbox{8420}{cubical} \markbox{8421}{models,} \markbox{8422}{as} \markbox{8423}{we} \markbox{8424}{do} \markbox{8425}{below} \markbox{8426}{in} \markbox{8427}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF lower bound}.

Before \markbox{8428}{beginning} \markbox{8429}{the} \markbox{8430}{discussion} \markbox{8431}{of} \markbox{8432}{the} \markbox{8433}{proof} \markbox{8434}{properly,} \markbox{8435}{we} \markbox{8436}{make} \markbox{8437}{a} \markbox{8438}{couple} \markbox{8439}{of} \markbox{8440}{simplifying} \markbox{8441}{observations,} \markbox{8442}{which} \markbox{8443}{are} \markbox{8444}{all} \markbox{8445}{basically} \markbox{8446}{distance} \markbox{8447}{formula-type} manipulations.

First, \markbox{8448}{note} \markbox{8449}{that} \markbox{8450}{if} \markbox{m8451}{$x,y \in H$} \markbox{8452}{and} \markbox{m8453}{$V \in \Rel_K(x,y)$} \markbox{8454}{but} \markbox{m8455}{$V \notin \calU$}, \markbox{8456}{then} \markbox{m8457}{$d_V(x,y) < K + \epsilon$} \markbox{8458}{for} \markbox{8459}{some} \markbox{m8460}{$\epsilon = \epsilon(\mathfrak S)>0$}.  \markbox{8461}{This} \markbox{8462}{is} \markbox{8463}{because} \markbox{m8464}{$\pi_V(x), \pi_V(y) \in \calN_{\theta}(\hull_V(a,b))$}.  \markbox{8465}{Hence} \markbox{8466}{by} \markbox{8467}{taking} \markbox{m8468}{$K_2 \geq K_1 > K + \epsilon$}, \markbox{8469}{we} \markbox{8470}{may} \markbox{8471}{increase} \markbox{8472}{the} \markbox{8473}{threshold} \markbox{8474}{to} \markbox{8475}{remove} \markbox{8476}{any} \markbox{8477}{extraneous} \markbox{8478}{domains.}  \markbox{8479}{That} is:
$$\sum_{U \in \mathfrak S} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2} = \sum_{U \in \calU} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2}.$$

We \markbox{8480}{next} \markbox{8481}{observe} \markbox{8482}{that} \markbox{8483}{for} \markbox{8484}{any} \markbox{m8485}{$x,y \in H$}, \markbox{8486}{item} \markbox{8487}{(4)} \markbox{8488}{of} \markbox{8489}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{8490}{implies} \markbox{8491}{that} \markbox{m8492}{$d_U(x,y) \asymp d_{T_U}(x_U, y_U)$}, \markbox{8493}{with} \markbox{8494}{constants} \markbox{8495}{depending} \markbox{8496}{only} \markbox{8497}{on} \markbox{m8498}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{8499}{Thus} \markbox{8500}{we} \markbox{8501}{can} \markbox{8502}{use} \markbox{8503}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF replace} \markbox{8504}{to} \markbox{8505}{replace} \markbox{8506}{the} \markbox{8507}{terms} \markbox{m8508}{$d_U(x,y)$} \markbox{8509}{with} \markbox{m8510}{$d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)$} \markbox{8511}{in} \markbox{8512}{the} \markbox{8513}{sum,} namely:

$$\sum_{U \in \calU} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2} \asymp \sum_{U \in \calU} [d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)]_{K_2}.$$

The \markbox{8514}{two} \markbox{8515}{bounds} \markbox{8516}{in} \markbox{8517}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q distance estimate} \markbox{8518}{are} \markbox{8519}{proven} \markbox{8520}{separately.}  \markbox{8521}{The} \markbox{8522}{upper} \markbox{8523}{bound} \markbox{8524}{only} \markbox{8525}{requires} \markbox{8526}{the} \markbox{8527}{basic} \markbox{8528}{details} \markbox{8529}{from} \markbox{8530}{the} \markbox{8531}{construction} \markbox{8532}{of} \markbox{8533}{the} \markbox{m8534}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{8535}{and} \markbox{8536}{some} \markbox{8537}{distance} \markbox{8538}{formula} \markbox{8539}{tools.}  \markbox{8540}{We} \markbox{8541}{have} \markbox{8542}{included} \markbox{8543}{the} \markbox{8544}{full} \markbox{8545}{proof} \markbox{8546}{of} \markbox{8547}{the} \markbox{8548}{proposition} \markbox{8549}{for} \markbox{8550}{clarity} \markbox{8551}{but} \markbox{8552}{also} \markbox{8553}{because} \markbox{8554}{it} \markbox{8555}{is} \markbox{8556}{used} \markbox{8557}{in} \markbox{8558}{proving} \markbox{8559}{the} \markbox{8560}{existence} \markbox{8561}{of} \markbox{8562}{hierarchy} \markbox{8563}{paths} \markbox{8564}{and} \markbox{8565}{the} \markbox{8566}{upper} \markbox{8567}{bound} \markbox{8568}{of} \markbox{8569}{the} \markbox{8570}{distance} \markbox{8571}{formula;} \markbox{8572}{moreover,} \markbox{8573}{the} \markbox{8574}{argument} \markbox{8575}{is} \markbox{8576}{similar} \markbox{8577}{to} \markbox{8578}{the} \markbox{8579}{proof} \markbox{8580}{of} \markbox{8581}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF replace}, \markbox{8582}{which} \markbox{8583}{actually} \markbox{8584}{implies} \markbox{8585}{the} proposition.

\begin{proposition}[Upper bound]\label{prop:upper bound}
There \markbox{8586}{exists} \markbox{m8587}{$K_1= K_1(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{8588}{so} \markbox{8589}{that} \markbox{8590}{for} \markbox{8591}{any} \markbox{m8592}{$K_2 >K_1$} \markbox{8593}{and} \markbox{8594}{any} \markbox{m8595}{$x, y \in H$} \markbox{8596}{we} have
\begin{equation}\label{eqn:upper}
    \sum_{U \in \calU} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2} \succ \sum_{U \in \calU} d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U)
\end{equation}
with \markbox{8597}{the} \markbox{8598}{constants} \markbox{8599}{in} \markbox{m8600}{$\succ$} \markbox{8601}{depending} \markbox{8602}{only} \markbox{8603}{on} \markbox{m8604}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{8605}{and} \markbox{m8606}{$K_2$}.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}

As \markbox{8607}{above,} \markbox{8608}{let} \markbox{m8609}{$K_1 \geq K + \epsilon$} \markbox{8610}{and} \markbox{8611}{set} \markbox{m8612}{$K_2 \geq K_1 + 100\ES$}.  \markbox{8613}{Let} \markbox{m8614}{$\calU_i = \Rel_{K_i}(x,y)$}, \markbox{8615}{so} \markbox{8616}{that} \markbox{m8617}{$\calU_2 \subset \calU_1 \subset \calU$}.  \markbox{8618}{If} \markbox{m8619}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{8620}{satisfies} \markbox{m8621}{$\hx_U = \hy_U$}, \markbox{8622}{then} \markbox{8623}{the} \markbox{8624}{corresponding} \markbox{8625}{term} \markbox{8626}{disappears} \markbox{8627}{on} \markbox{8628}{the} \markbox{8629}{right-hand} \markbox{8630}{side.}  \markbox{8631}{Hence} \markbox{8632}{it} \markbox{8633}{suffices} \markbox{8634}{to} \markbox{8635}{account} \markbox{8636}{for} \markbox{8637}{the} \markbox{8638}{domains} \markbox{8639}{in} \markbox{m8640}{$\calV = \{V \in \calU | d_V(x,y) < K_2 \textrm{ and } \hx_U \neq \hy_U\}$}, \markbox{8641}{which} \markbox{8642}{appear} \markbox{8643}{on} \markbox{8644}{the} \markbox{8645}{right-hand} \markbox{8646}{side} \markbox{8647}{(RHS)} \markbox{8648}{but} \markbox{8649}{not} \markbox{8650}{the} \markbox{8651}{left-hand} \markbox{8652}{side} \markbox{8653}{(LHS)} \markbox{8654}{of} \markbox{8655}{equation} \eqref{eqn:upper}.

For \markbox{8656}{this,} \markbox{8657}{item} \markbox{8658}{(9)} \markbox{8659}{of} \markbox{8660}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{8661}{says} \markbox{8662}{that} \markbox{m8663}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{8664}{is} \markbox{8665}{not} \markbox{8666}{contained} \markbox{8667}{in} \markbox{8668}{some} \markbox{8669}{cluster} \markbox{8670}{point} \markbox{8671}{of} \markbox{m8672}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{8673}{for} \markbox{8674}{only} \markbox{8675}{boundedly-many} \markbox{m8676}{$U$}, \markbox{8677}{and} \markbox{8678}{the} \markbox{8679}{same} \markbox{8680}{for} \markbox{m8681}{$\hy_U$}.  \markbox{8682}{(In} \markbox{8683}{fact,} \markbox{8684}{we} \markbox{8685}{can} \markbox{8686}{take} \markbox{m8687}{$\hx_U = \ha_U$} \markbox{8688}{and} \markbox{m8689}{$\hy_U = \hb_U$}, \markbox{8690}{be} \markbox{8691}{this} \markbox{8692}{will} \markbox{8693}{not} \markbox{8694}{simplify} \markbox{8695}{things.)} \markbox{8696}{This} \markbox{8697}{means} \markbox{8698}{that,} \markbox{8699}{up} \markbox{8700}{to} \markbox{8701}{ignoring} \markbox{8702}{a} \markbox{8703}{bounded} \markbox{8704}{collection} \markbox{8705}{of} \markbox{8706}{domains} \markbox{m8707}{$\calV' \subset \calV$}, \markbox{8708}{if} \markbox{m8709}{$V \in \calV - \calV'$} \markbox{8710}{then} \markbox{m8711}{$\hx_V$} \markbox{8712}{and} \markbox{m8713}{$\hy_V$} \markbox{8714}{are} \markbox{8715}{at} \markbox{8716}{distinct} \markbox{8717}{cluster} \markbox{8718}{points,} \markbox{8719}{and} \markbox{8720}{so} \markbox{m8721}{$d_V(x,y) > 50\ES$} \markbox{8722}{by} \markbox{8723}{item} \markbox{8724}{(5)} \markbox{8725}{of} \markbox{8726}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}, \markbox{8727}{i.e.,} \markbox{m8728}{$\calV-\calV' \subset \Rel_{50\ES}(x,y)$}, \markbox{8729}{while} \markbox{8730}{also} \markbox{m8731}{$d_{\hT_V}(\hx_V,\hy_V) \geq r_2 \geq 1$}.

One \markbox{8732}{finishes} \markbox{8733}{the} \markbox{8734}{proof} \markbox{8735}{with} \markbox{8736}{an} \markbox{8737}{application} \markbox{8738}{of} \markbox{8739}{Proposition} \ref{prop:bounding containers} \markbox{8740}{as} \markbox{8741}{follows.}  \markbox{8742}{Set} \markbox{m8743}{$\calU_i = \Rel_{K_i}(x,y)$} \markbox{8744}{and} \markbox{8745}{observe} \markbox{8746}{that} \markbox{m8747}{$\calV - \calV' \subset \calU_1 - \calU_2$}.  \markbox{8748}{Proposition} \ref{prop:bounding containers} \markbox{8749}{says} \markbox{8750}{that} \markbox{8751}{up} \markbox{8752}{to} \markbox{8753}{ignoring} \markbox{8754}{a} \markbox{8755}{subset} \markbox{m8756}{$\calV'' \subset \calV - \calV'$} \markbox{8757}{with} \markbox{m8758}{$\#\calV'' \leq P(K_2)$}, \markbox{8759}{for} \markbox{8760}{each} \markbox{m8761}{$V \in \calV_0 = \calV - (\calV' \cup \calV'')$} \markbox{8762}{there} \markbox{8763}{exists} \markbox{8764}{some} \markbox{8765}{domain} \markbox{m8766}{$W \in \calU_2$} \markbox{8767}{determining} \markbox{8768}{a} \markbox{8769}{term} \markbox{8770}{on} \markbox{8771}{the} \markbox{8772}{RHS} \markbox{8773}{with} \markbox{m8774}{$V \nest W$}.  \markbox{8775}{Moreover,} \markbox{8776}{it} \markbox{8777}{says} \markbox{8778}{that} \markbox{8779}{the} \markbox{8780}{set} \markbox{8781}{of} \markbox{8782}{domains} \markbox{m8783}{$\calW = \{V \in \calV| V\nest W\}$} \markbox{8784}{for} \markbox{8785}{which} \markbox{8786}{each} \markbox{8787}{such} \markbox{m8788}{$W$} \markbox{8789}{accounts} \markbox{8790}{in} \markbox{8791}{this} \markbox{8792}{way} \markbox{8793}{satisfies} \markbox{m8794}{$\#\calW \leq (1+A)\cdot d_W(x,y) + A$}, \markbox{8795}{for} \markbox{8796}{some} \markbox{m8797}{$A = A(K_2, \mathfrak S)>0$}.

Combining \markbox{8798}{these} \markbox{8799}{observations} \markbox{8800}{leads} \markbox{8801}{to} \markbox{8802}{the} computation
\begin{eqnarray*}
\sum_{U \in \calU_2} d_U(x,y) &=& \sum_{U \in \calU_2} d_U(x,y) + \sum_{V \in \calV - \calV'} d_V(x,y)+ \sum_{Z \in \calV'} d_Z(x,y)\\
&\leq& \sum_{U \in \calU_2} ((1+A)\cdot d_U(x,y)+A) + K_2 \cdot P(K_2)\\
&\leq& (1+2A)\cdot \sum_{U \in \calU_2} d_U(x,y) + K_2 \cdot P(K_2)
\end{eqnarray*}
where \markbox{8803}{the} \markbox{8804}{last} \markbox{8805}{inequality} \markbox{8806}{follows} \markbox{8807}{from} \markbox{8808}{the} \markbox{8809}{fact} \markbox{8810}{that} \markbox{m8811}{$d_U(x,y) > K_2$} \markbox{8812}{for} \markbox{8813}{each} \markbox{m8814}{$U \in \calU_2$}.  \markbox{8815}{This} \markbox{8816}{completes} \markbox{8817}{the} \markbox{8818}{proof.} 

\end{proof}


\begin{figure}[h]
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=.8\textwidth]{figures/lower_bound_interval.pdf}
    \caption{Proof of Proposition \ref{prop:lower bound}: The subcluster $C'$ isolates the portion of $C$ which intersects $[x_U,y_U]$ but avoids the $(\alpha_0+R)$-neighborhoods of $x_U$ and $y_U$.  The (pink) net of $\delta$-sets from $\nest_{\calU}$-minimal domains $V \nest U$ with $\delta^V_U \subset C'$ coarsely encodes the length of $C'$, with the BGIA property guaranteeing that $\hx_V = \ha_V$ and $\hy_V = \hb_V$ and hence $d_{\hT_V}(\hx_V,\hy_V) \geq K - B^2 - 2r_1$ for each such $V$.}
    \label{fig:subcluster}
\end{figure}

\begin{proposition}[Lower bound]\label{prop:lower bound}
There \markbox{8819}{exists} \markbox{m8820}{$K_1= K_1(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{8821}{so} \markbox{8822}{that} \markbox{8823}{for} \markbox{8824}{any} \markbox{m8825}{$K_2 >K_1$} \markbox{8826}{and} \markbox{8827}{any} \markbox{m8828}{$x, y \in H$} \markbox{8829}{we} have
\begin{equation}\label{eqn:lower}
    \sum_{U \in \calU} [d_U(x,y)]_{K_2} \prec \sum_{U \in \calU} d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U)
\end{equation}
with \markbox{8830}{the} \markbox{8831}{constants} \markbox{8832}{in} \markbox{m8833}{$\prec$} \markbox{8834}{depending} \markbox{8835}{only} \markbox{8836}{on} \markbox{m8837}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{8838}{and} \markbox{m8839}{$K_2$}.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}

Observe \markbox{8840}{that} \markbox{8841}{since} \markbox{m8842}{$d_U(x,y) \prec d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)$} \markbox{8843}{for} \markbox{8844}{each} \markbox{m8845}{$U$}, \markbox{8846}{it} \markbox{8847}{suffices} \markbox{8848}{by} \markbox{8849}{Corollary} \ref{cor:DF replace} \markbox{8850}{to} \markbox{8851}{show} \markbox{8852}{that} 
$$\sum_{U \in \calU} [d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)]_{K_2} \prec \sum_{U \in \calU} d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U).$$

For \markbox{8853}{this} \markbox{8854}{bound,} \markbox{8855}{there} \markbox{8856}{are} \markbox{8857}{possibly} \markbox{8858}{domains} \markbox{m8859}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{8860}{where} \markbox{m8861}{$d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U) > K_2$} \markbox{8862}{but} \markbox{8863}{there} \markbox{8864}{is} \markbox{8865}{a} \markbox{8866}{discrepancy} \markbox{m8867}{$d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U) > d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U)$}.  \markbox{8868}{Let} \markbox{m8869}{$\calW$} \markbox{8870}{denote} \markbox{8871}{the} \markbox{8872}{collection} \markbox{8873}{of} \markbox{8874}{such} domains.

Since \markbox{m8875}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{8876}{is} \markbox{8877}{obtained} \markbox{8878}{from} \markbox{m8879}{$T_U$} \markbox{8880}{by} \markbox{8881}{collapsing} \markbox{8882}{clusters,} \markbox{8883}{we} \markbox{8884}{need} \markbox{8885}{to} \markbox{8886}{analyze} \markbox{8887}{the} \markbox{8888}{clusters} \markbox{8889}{which} \markbox{8890}{separate} \markbox{m8891}{$x_U$} \markbox{8892}{from} \markbox{m8893}{$y_U$}, \markbox{8894}{i.e.} \markbox{8895}{those} \markbox{8896}{clusters} \markbox{m8897}{$C_1, \dots, C_n$} \markbox{8898}{which} \markbox{8899}{intersect,} \markbox{8900}{in} \markbox{8901}{that} \markbox{8902}{order,} \markbox{8903}{the} \markbox{8904}{geodesic} \markbox{m8905}{$[x_U,y_U]$} \markbox{8906}{in} \markbox{m8907}{$T_U$}.  \markbox{8908}{The} \markbox{8909}{proof} \markbox{8910}{is} \markbox{8911}{mainly} \markbox{8912}{a} \markbox{8913}{BGIA} \ref{ax:BGIA} \markbox{8914}{type} \markbox{8915}{argument} \markbox{8916}{along} \markbox{8917}{with} \markbox{8918}{an} \markbox{8919}{application} \markbox{8920}{of} \markbox{8921}{Proposition} \ref{prop:bounding containers} \markbox{8922}{and} \markbox{8923}{the} \markbox{8924}{Covering} \markbox{8925}{Lemma} \ref{lem:covering}.

Continuing \markbox{8926}{with} \markbox{8927}{the} \markbox{8928}{above} \markbox{8929}{notation,} \markbox{8930}{for} \markbox{8931}{each} \markbox{m8932}{$i$}, \markbox{8933}{let} \markbox{m8934}{$C'_i = C_i \cap [x_U,y_U]_{T_U} - \left(B_{\alpha_0 + R}(x_U) \cup B_{\alpha_0 + R}(y_U)\right)$}, \markbox{8935}{where} \markbox{m8936}{$\alpha_0 = \alpha(R, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{8937}{is} \markbox{8938}{the} \markbox{8939}{interval} \markbox{8940}{consistency} \markbox{8941}{constant} \markbox{8942}{provided} \markbox{8943}{by} \markbox{8944}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval consistency}; \markbox{8945}{see} \markbox{8946}{Figure} \ref{fig:subcluster}.

Observe \markbox{8947}{that} \markbox{8948}{for} \markbox{8949}{each} \markbox{m8950}{$i$}, \markbox{8951}{if} \markbox{8952}{we} \markbox{8953}{set} \markbox{m8954}{$\calV_i = \{V \in \calU|V \nest U \text{ and } \delta^V_U \subset C_i\}$} \markbox{8955}{then} \markbox{m8956}{$\{\delta^V_U| V \in \calV_i\}$} \markbox{8957}{is} \markbox{m8958}{$(r_2 + 2r_1)$}-dense \markbox{8959}{in} \markbox{m8960}{$C_i$}.  \markbox{8961}{Hence} \markbox{8962}{we} \markbox{8963}{can} \markbox{8964}{find} \markbox{8965}{a} \markbox{8966}{subcollection} \markbox{m8967}{$\calV_i'$} \markbox{8968}{so} that
\begin{itemize}
    \item {} Each \markbox{m8969}{$V \in \calV_i'$} \markbox{8970}{is} \markbox{m8971}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal;
    \item {} For \markbox{8972}{each} \markbox{m8973}{$V \in \calV'$}, \markbox{8974}{we} \markbox{8975}{have} \markbox{m8976}{$\delta^V_U \subset C_i'$};
    \item {} \markbox{m8977}{$\{\delta^V_U| V \in \calV_i\}$} \markbox{8978}{is} \markbox{8979}{a} \markbox{m8980}{$(2r_2+4r_1, r_2)$}-net \markbox{8981}{on} \markbox{m8982}{$C_i'$} \markbox{8983}{(see} \markbox{8984}{Definition} \ref{defn:net} below).
\end{itemize}

Note \markbox{8985}{that} \markbox{8986}{the} \markbox{8987}{increase} \markbox{8988}{in} \markbox{8989}{the} \markbox{8990}{net} \markbox{8991}{constants} \markbox{8992}{in} \markbox{8993}{the} \markbox{8994}{third} \markbox{8995}{item} \markbox{8996}{is} \markbox{8997}{required} \markbox{8998}{to} \markbox{8999}{guarantee} \markbox{9000}{the} \markbox{9001}{second} \markbox{9002}{item.}  \markbox{9003}{In} \markbox{9004}{particular,} \markbox{9005}{we} \markbox{9006}{have} \markbox{m9007}{$\#\calV_i \succ \diam_{T_U}(C_i') \geq \diam_{T_U}(C_i \cap [x_U,y_U])- 2(\alpha_0+R)$}, \markbox{9008}{where} \markbox{m9009}{$\#\calV_i$} \markbox{9010}{denotes} \markbox{9011}{the} \markbox{9012}{cardinality} \markbox{9013}{of} \markbox{m9014}{$\calV_i$}.

Let \markbox{m9015}{$V \in \calV_i'$}.  \markbox{9016}{Then,} \markbox{9017}{by} \markbox{9018}{construction,} \markbox{m9019}{$d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U, x_U)> \alpha + R$} \markbox{9020}{and} \markbox{m9021}{$d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U, y_U)>\alpha_0 + R$}.  \markbox{9022}{Hence,} \markbox{9023}{up} \markbox{9024}{to} \markbox{9025}{switching} \markbox{9026}{the} \markbox{9027}{roles} \markbox{9028}{of} \markbox{m9029}{$a$} \markbox{9030}{and} \markbox{m9031}{$b$}, \markbox{9032}{the} \markbox{9033}{BGI} \markbox{9034}{property} \markbox{9035}{(5)} \markbox{9036}{of} \markbox{9037}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control} \markbox{9038}{says} \markbox{9039}{that} \markbox{m9040}{$d_{T_V}(\delta^U_V(a_V),\delta^U_V(x_V))<R$} \markbox{9041}{and} \markbox{m9042}{$d_{T_V}(\delta^U_V(b_V),\delta^U_V(y_V))<R$}. 

Lemma \ref{lem:interval consistency} \markbox{9043}{says} \markbox{9044}{that} \markbox{9045}{the} \markbox{9046}{tuples} \markbox{m9047}{$(a_U), (b_U), (x_U), (y_U)$} \markbox{9048}{are} \markbox{9049}{all} \markbox{m9050}{$\alpha_0$}-consistent.  \markbox{9051}{Thus} \markbox{9052}{since} \markbox{m9053}{$d_{T_U}(a_U, \delta^V_U)>R + \alpha_0$} \markbox{9054}{and} \markbox{9055}{similarly} \markbox{9056}{for} \markbox{m9057}{$b_U,x_U,y_U$}, \markbox{m9058}{$\alpha_0$}-consistency \markbox{9059}{forces} \markbox{9060}{that} \markbox{m9061}{$d_{T_V}(a_V, \delta^U_V(a_U)) < \alpha_0$}, \markbox{9062}{and} \markbox{9063}{similarly} \markbox{9064}{for} \markbox{m9065}{$b_V,x_V,y_V$}.  \markbox{9066}{As} \markbox{9067}{such,} \markbox{9068}{we} \markbox{9069}{get} \markbox{9070}{that} \markbox{m9071}{$d_{T_V}(x_V,a_V) < \alpha_0 + R$} \markbox{9072}{and} \markbox{m9073}{$d_{T_V}(y_V,b_V) < \alpha_0 + R$}, \markbox{9074}{and} \markbox{9075}{so} \markbox{9076}{that} \markbox{m9077}{$d_{T_V}(x_V,y_V) \geq d_{T_V}(a_V,b_V) - 2\alpha_0 - 2R$}, \markbox{9078}{from} \markbox{9079}{which} \markbox{9080}{we} \markbox{9081}{can} \markbox{9082}{conclude} \markbox{9083}{that} \markbox{m9084}{$\ha_V = \hx_V$} \markbox{9085}{and} \markbox{m9086}{$\hb_V = \hy_V$} \markbox{9087}{by} \markbox{9088}{requiring} \markbox{m9089}{$r_1 > \alpha_0 + R$}.




On \markbox{9090}{the} \markbox{9091}{other} \markbox{9092}{hand,} \markbox{9093}{since} \markbox{9094}{each} \markbox{m9095}{$V \in \calV_i'$} \markbox{9096}{is} \markbox{m9097}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{9098}{and} \markbox{m9099}{$d_V(a,b) > K$}, \markbox{9100}{item} \markbox{9101}{(4)} \markbox{9102}{of} \markbox{9103}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{9104}{says} \markbox{9105}{that} \markbox{m9106}{$d_{\hT_V}(\hat{a}_V,\hat{b}_V) \succ K$}.  \markbox{9107}{Hence} \markbox{9108}{we} \markbox{9109}{obtain} \markbox{9110}{that} \markbox{m9111}{$d_{\hT_V}(\hx_V,\hy_V)  = d_{\hT_V}(\ha_V,\hb_V) \succ K$}.

Thus \markbox{9112}{for} \markbox{9113}{each} \markbox{m9114}{$U \in \calW$}, \markbox{9115}{we} have
\begin{eqnarray*}
d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U) & = & d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U) + \sum_{i=1}^n \diam_{T_U}(C_i \cap [x_U,y_U]_{T_U})\\
&\prec& d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U) + \sum_{i=1}^n \#\calV_i'\\
&\prec& d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U) + \sum_{i=1}^n \left(\sum_{V \in \calV_i'} d_{\hT_V}(\hx_V,\hy_V)\right).
\end{eqnarray*}

Finally, \markbox{9116}{the} \markbox{9117}{Covering} \markbox{9118}{Lemma} \ref{lem:covering} \markbox{9119}{says} \markbox{9120}{that} \markbox{9121}{any} \markbox{9122}{domain} \markbox{m9123}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{9124}{can} \markbox{9125}{nest} \markbox{9126}{into} \markbox{9127}{only} \markbox{9128}{boundedly-many} \markbox{9129}{domains} \markbox{9130}{in} \markbox{m9131}{$\calU$}, \markbox{9132}{with} \markbox{9133}{bounds} \markbox{9134}{determined} \markbox{9135}{by} \markbox{m9136}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{9137}{Hence,} \markbox{9138}{each} \markbox{m9139}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{9140}{domain} \markbox{m9141}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{9142}{must} \markbox{9143}{account} \markbox{9144}{for} \markbox{9145}{at} \markbox{9146}{most} \markbox{9147}{boundedly-many} \markbox{m9148}{$U \in \calW$} \markbox{9149}{in} \markbox{9150}{the} \markbox{9151}{above} \markbox{9152}{way.}  \markbox{9153}{Thus,} \markbox{9154}{using} \markbox{9155}{an} \markbox{9156}{argument} \markbox{9157}{similar} \markbox{9158}{to} \markbox{9159}{the} \markbox{9160}{end} \markbox{9161}{of} \markbox{9162}{the} \markbox{9163}{proof} \markbox{9164}{of} \markbox{9165}{Proposition} \ref{prop:upper bound}, \markbox{9166}{we} \markbox{9167}{can} \markbox{9168}{account} \markbox{9169}{for} \markbox{9170}{the} \markbox{9171}{distance} \markbox{9172}{lost} \markbox{9173}{by} \markbox{9174}{collapsing} \markbox{9175}{clusters} \markbox{9176}{in} \markbox{9177}{each} \markbox{9178}{domain} \markbox{9179}{in} \markbox{m9180}{$\calW$} \markbox{9181}{with} \markbox{9182}{these} \markbox{9183}{large} \markbox{m9184}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{9185}{domains} \markbox{9186}{by} \markbox{9187}{increasing} \markbox{9188}{the} \markbox{9189}{multiplicative} \markbox{9190}{constant} \markbox{9191}{for} \markbox{9192}{the} \markbox{9193}{estimate} \markbox{9194}{in} \markbox{9195}{equation} \eqref{eqn:upper} \markbox{9196}{by} \markbox{9197}{a} \markbox{9198}{bounded} \markbox{9199}{amount.}  \markbox{9200}{This} \markbox{9201}{completes} \markbox{9202}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

We \markbox{9203}{used} \markbox{9204}{the} \markbox{9205}{following} \markbox{9206}{definition} \markbox{9207}{in} \markbox{9208}{the} \markbox{9209}{above} proof:

\begin{definition}[Net]\label{defn:net}
Given \markbox{9210}{constants} \markbox{m9211}{$a,A\geq 0$}, \markbox{9212}{a} \markbox{m9213}{$(a,A)$}-\markbox{9214}{\emph{net}} \markbox{9215}{on} \markbox{9216}{a} \markbox{9217}{subspace} \markbox{m9218}{$Y \subset X$} \markbox{9219}{of} \markbox{9220}{a} \markbox{9221}{metric} \markbox{9222}{space} \markbox{9223}{is} \markbox{9224}{a} \markbox{9225}{collection} \markbox{m9226}{$Z \subset Y$} \markbox{9227}{of} \markbox{9228}{points} \markbox{9229}{so} that:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m9230}{$Z$} \markbox{9231}{is} \markbox{m9232}{$a$}-coarsely \markbox{9233}{dense} \markbox{9234}{in} \markbox{m9235}{$Y$}, \markbox{9236}{i.e.} \markbox{9237}{for} \markbox{9238}{every} \markbox{m9239}{$y \in Y$} \markbox{9240}{there} \markbox{9241}{is} \markbox{9242}{some} \markbox{m9243}{$z \in Z$} \markbox{9244}{with} \markbox{m9245}{$d(z,y)<a$}, and
\item {} For \markbox{9246}{any} \markbox{m9247}{$z,z' \in Z$}, \markbox{9248}{we} \markbox{9249}{have} \markbox{m9250}{$d_X(z,z') \geq A$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

In \markbox{9251}{particular,} \markbox{9252}{an} \markbox{m9253}{$(a,A)$}-net \markbox{m9254}{$Z$} \markbox{9255}{on} \markbox{m9256}{$Y$} \markbox{9257}{satisfies} \markbox{m9258}{$\#Z \asymp \diam(Y)$} \markbox{9259}{with} \markbox{9260}{the} \markbox{9261}{constants} \markbox{9262}{depending} \markbox{9263}{only} \markbox{9264}{on} \markbox{m9265}{$a,A$}.








\subsection{The map $\hO:\calQ \to H$ and honing clusters}\label{subsec:hO defined}

With \markbox{9266}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q distance estimate} \markbox{9267}{in} \markbox{9268}{hand,} \markbox{9269}{in} \markbox{9270}{order} \markbox{9271}{to} \markbox{9272}{prove} \markbox{9273}{that} \markbox{m9274}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{9275}{is} \markbox{9276}{a} \markbox{9277}{quasi-isometry,} \markbox{9278}{we} \markbox{9279}{need} \markbox{9280}{to} \markbox{9281}{explain} \markbox{9282}{why} \markbox{m9283}{$\hPsi$} \markbox{9284}{is} \markbox{9285}{coarsely} \markbox{9286}{surjective.}  \markbox{9287}{The} \markbox{9288}{proof} \markbox{9289}{of} \markbox{9290}{this} \markbox{9291}{fact} \markbox{9292}{is} \markbox{9293}{quite} \markbox{9294}{involved} \markbox{9295}{and} \markbox{9296}{beyond} \markbox{9297}{the} \markbox{9298}{scope} \markbox{9299}{of} \markbox{9300}{an} \markbox{9301}{expository} \markbox{9302}{paper.}  \markbox{9303}{As} \markbox{9304}{such,} \markbox{9305}{we} \markbox{9306}{will} \markbox{9307}{mostly} \markbox{9308}{present} \markbox{9309}{key} \markbox{9310}{ideas} \markbox{9311}{and} \markbox{9312}{not} \markbox{9313}{a} \markbox{9314}{full} \markbox{9315}{detailed} \markbox{9316}{proof} \markbox{9317}{because} \markbox{9318}{the} \markbox{9319}{proof} \markbox{9320}{is} \markbox{9321}{not} \markbox{9322}{greatly} \markbox{9323}{simplified} \markbox{9324}{versus} \markbox{9325}{the} \markbox{9326}{most} \markbox{9327}{general} \markbox{9328}{version,} \markbox{9329}{see} \cite[Sections 9--11]{Dur_infcube}.

In \markbox{9330}{this} \markbox{9331}{subsection,} \markbox{9332}{we} \markbox{9333}{will} \markbox{9334}{construct} \markbox{9335}{a} \markbox{9336}{map} \markbox{m9337}{$\Omega:\calQ \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$}, \markbox{9338}{and} \markbox{9339}{sketch} \markbox{9340}{why} \markbox{9341}{its} \markbox{9342}{image} \markbox{9343}{is} \markbox{m9344}{$\beta$}-consistent \markbox{9345}{for} \markbox{9346}{some} \markbox{m9347}{$\beta = \beta(\mathfrak S, R, r_1,r_2)>0$}.   \markbox{9348}{Upgrading} \markbox{9349}{this} \markbox{9350}{to} \markbox{9351}{a} \markbox{9352}{map} \markbox{m9353}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$} \markbox{9354}{involves} \markbox{9355}{standard} \markbox{9356}{HHS} \markbox{9357}{techniques.}  \markbox{9358}{In} \markbox{9359}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:tree trimming}, \markbox{9360}{we} \markbox{9361}{will} \markbox{9362}{prove} \markbox{9363}{our} \markbox{9364}{Tree} \markbox{9365}{Trimming} \markbox{9366}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming},
