\markbox{9367}{which} \markbox{9368}{is} \markbox{9369}{a} \markbox{9370}{useful} \markbox{9371}{distance} \markbox{9372}{formula-like} \markbox{9373}{tool} \markbox{9374}{that} \markbox{9375}{will} \markbox{9376}{allow} \markbox{9377}{us} \markbox{9378}{modify} \markbox{9379}{our} \markbox{9380}{collapsed} \markbox{9381}{interval} \markbox{9382}{setup} \markbox{9383}{while} \markbox{9384}{coarsely} \markbox{9385}{preserving} \markbox{9386}{the} \markbox{9387}{geometry} \markbox{9388}{of} \markbox{m9389}{$\calQ$}.  \markbox{9390}{This} \markbox{9391}{tool} \markbox{9392}{is} \markbox{9393}{a} \markbox{9394}{key} \markbox{9395}{ingredient} \markbox{9396}{in} \markbox{9397}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:upgrade to HHS}, \markbox{9398}{where} \markbox{9399}{we} \markbox{9400}{sketch} \markbox{9401}{why} \markbox{m9402}{$\hO$} \markbox{9403}{is} \markbox{9404}{a} \markbox{9405}{coarse} \markbox{9406}{inverse} \markbox{9407}{to} \markbox{m9408}{$\hPsi$}, \markbox{9409}{namely} \markbox{9410}{that} \markbox{m9411}{$d_{\calQ}(\hPsi \circ \hO(\hx), \hx)$} \markbox{9412}{is} \markbox{9413}{bounded} \markbox{9414}{independently} \markbox{9415}{of} \markbox{m9416}{$\hx \in \calQ$}.

We \markbox{9417}{can} \markbox{9418}{now} \markbox{9419}{set} \markbox{9420}{about} \markbox{9421}{defining} \markbox{9422}{the} \markbox{9423}{map} \markbox{m9424}{$\Omega:\calQ \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$}, \markbox{9425}{which} \markbox{9426}{is} \markbox{9427}{defined} \markbox{9428}{coordinate-wise.}  \markbox{9429}{To} \markbox{9430}{put} \markbox{9431}{things} \markbox{9432}{more} \markbox{9433}{precisely,} \markbox{9434}{we} \markbox{9435}{want} \markbox{9436}{to} \markbox{9437}{define} \markbox{m9438}{$\Omega$} \markbox{9439}{so} that:

\begin{itemize}
    \item {} For \markbox{9440}{each} \markbox{m9441}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{9442}{the} \markbox{9443}{tuple} \markbox{m9444}{$\Omega(\hx)$} \markbox{9445}{is} \markbox{m9446}{$\omega$}-consistent \markbox{9447}{for} \markbox{9448}{some} \markbox{m9449}{$\omega = \omega(\mathfrak S)>0$}, and
    \item {} when \markbox{m9450}{$\hx  = (\hx_U)\in \calQ$} \markbox{9451}{and} \markbox{m9452}{$(x_U) = \Omega(\hx)$}, \markbox{9453}{then} \markbox{m9454}{$q_U(x_U) = \hx_U$} \markbox{9455}{for} \markbox{9456}{each} \markbox{m9457}{$U \in \calU$}.
\end{itemize}


Unsurprisingly, \markbox{9458}{the} \markbox{9459}{cluster} \markbox{9460}{subintervals,} \markbox{9461}{which} \markbox{9462}{are} \markbox{9463}{collapsed} \markbox{9464}{under} \markbox{9465}{each} \markbox{m9466}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$}, \markbox{9467}{play} \markbox{9468}{a} \markbox{9469}{key} \markbox{9470}{role.}  \markbox{9471}{In} \markbox{9472}{particular,} \markbox{9473}{these} \markbox{9474}{cluster} \markbox{9475}{subintervals} \markbox{9476}{can} \markbox{9477}{have} \markbox{9478}{arbitrarily} \markbox{9479}{large} \markbox{9480}{diameter,} \markbox{9481}{and} \markbox{9482}{so} \markbox{9483}{if} \markbox{9484}{a} \markbox{9485}{coordinate} \markbox{m9486}{$\hx_U\in \hT_U$} \markbox{9487}{lies} \markbox{9488}{in} \markbox{9489}{a} \markbox{9490}{cluster} \markbox{9491}{point} \markbox{9492}{of} \markbox{m9493}{$\hT_U$}, \markbox{9494}{then} \markbox{9495}{its} \markbox{9496}{preimage} \markbox{m9497}{$q_U^{-1}(\hx_U)$} \markbox{9498}{is} \markbox{9499}{that} \markbox{9500}{whole} \markbox{9501}{cluster.}  \markbox{9502}{Choosing} \markbox{9503}{a} \markbox{9504}{point} \markbox{9505}{within} \markbox{9506}{that} \markbox{9507}{cluster} \markbox{9508}{then} \markbox{9509}{requires} \markbox{9510}{utilizing} \markbox{9511}{the} \markbox{9512}{coordinates} \markbox{9513}{for} \markbox{m9514}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{9515}{with} \markbox{m9516}{$\hd^V_U = \hx_U$}.  \markbox{9517}{We} \markbox{9518}{think} \markbox{9519}{of} \markbox{9520}{this} \markbox{9521}{process} \markbox{9522}{as} \markbox{9523}{\emph{honing}} \markbox{9524}{the} cluster.


\smallskip


\markbox{9525}{\textbf{\underline{Honing clusters}}}: \markbox{9526}{Let} \markbox{m9527}{$\hx = (\hx_U) \in \calQ$}.  \markbox{9528}{When} \markbox{m9529}{$U\in \calU$} \markbox{9530}{has} \markbox{m9531}{$\hx_U \in \hT^e_U$}, \markbox{9532}{then} \markbox{9533}{the} \markbox{9534}{definition} \markbox{9535}{is} \markbox{9536}{simple:} \markbox{m9537}{$x_U = q_U^{-1}(\hx_U)$}, \markbox{9538}{which} \markbox{9539}{is} \markbox{9540}{a} \markbox{9541}{unique} \markbox{9542}{point.}  \markbox{9543}{For} \markbox{9544}{the} \markbox{9545}{other} \markbox{9546}{domains,} \markbox{9547}{we} \markbox{9548}{need} \markbox{9549}{some} \markbox{9550}{more} setup.

\begin{remark}
    \markbox{9551}{The} \markbox{9552}{reader} \markbox{9553}{should} \markbox{9554}{be} \markbox{9555}{warned} \markbox{9556}{here} \markbox{9557}{that} \markbox{9558}{one} \markbox{9559}{has} \markbox{9560}{to} \markbox{9561}{deal} \markbox{9562}{with} \markbox{9563}{the} \markbox{9564}{case} \markbox{9565}{where} \markbox{9566}{all} \markbox{9567}{coordinates} \markbox{m9568}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{9569}{are} \markbox{9570}{contained} \markbox{9571}{in} \markbox{9572}{a} \markbox{9573}{collapsed} \markbox{9574}{point.}  \markbox{9575}{When} \markbox{9576}{this} \markbox{9577}{happens,} \markbox{9578}{there} \markbox{9579}{is} \markbox{9580}{not} \markbox{9581}{an} \markbox{9582}{obvious} \markbox{9583}{choice} \markbox{9584}{of} \markbox{9585}{collection} \markbox{9586}{of} \markbox{9587}{minimal} \markbox{9588}{domains} \markbox{9589}{to} \markbox{9590}{work} \markbox{9591}{with,} \markbox{9592}{and} \markbox{9593}{in} \markbox{9594}{order} \markbox{9595}{to} \markbox{9596}{determine} \markbox{9597}{coordinates} \markbox{9598}{back} \markbox{9599}{in} \markbox{9600}{the} \markbox{9601}{intervals} \markbox{m9602}{$T_U$}, \markbox{9603}{one} \markbox{9604}{must} \markbox{9605}{use} \markbox{9606}{all} \markbox{9607}{of} \markbox{9608}{the} \markbox{9609}{hierarchical} \markbox{9610}{data} \markbox{9611}{at} \markbox{9612}{hand.} 
\end{remark}

Suppose \markbox{9613}{that} \markbox{m9614}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9615}{and} \markbox{m9616}{$\hx_U \notin \hT^e_U$}.  \markbox{9617}{Let} \markbox{m9618}{$C$} \markbox{9619}{denote} \markbox{9620}{the} \markbox{9621}{cluster} \markbox{9622}{in} \markbox{m9623}{$T_U$} \markbox{9624}{so} \markbox{9625}{that} \markbox{m9626}{$q_U(C) = \hx_U$}.  \markbox{9627}{The} \markbox{9628}{first} \markbox{9629}{step} \markbox{9630}{is} \markbox{9631}{to} \markbox{9632}{associate} \markbox{9633}{a} \markbox{9634}{marked} \markbox{9635}{point} \markbox{m9636}{$l_V \in \{a,b\}$} \markbox{9637}{to} \markbox{9638}{each} \markbox{m9639}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{9640}{domain} \markbox{m9641}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{9642}{with} \markbox{m9643}{$\delta^V_U \subset C$}.  \markbox{9644}{We} \markbox{9645}{then} \markbox{9646}{use} \markbox{9647}{these} \markbox{m9648}{$l_V$} \markbox{9649}{to} \markbox{9650}{hone} \markbox{9651}{the} \markbox{9652}{clusters} \markbox{9653}{of} \markbox{9654}{the} \markbox{9655}{larger} \markbox{m9656}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9657}{in} \markbox{9658}{which} \markbox{9659}{such} \markbox{m9660}{$V$} \markbox{9661}{are} involved.

Suppose \markbox{9662}{then} \markbox{9663}{that} \markbox{m9664}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9665}{is} \markbox{m9666}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.  \markbox{9667}{Since} \markbox{m9668}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{9669}{has} \markbox{9670}{no} \markbox{9671}{internal} \markbox{9672}{cluster} \markbox{9673}{points,} \markbox{m9674}{$\hat{x}_U$} \markbox{9675}{is} \markbox{9676}{either} \markbox{9677}{a} \markbox{9678}{marked} \markbox{9679}{point---either} \markbox{m9680}{$\ha_U$} \markbox{9681}{or} \markbox{m9682}{$\hb_U$}---or \markbox{9683}{a} \markbox{9684}{point} \markbox{9685}{in} \markbox{m9686}{$\hT^e_U$}.  \markbox{9687}{If} \markbox{9688}{the} \markbox{9689}{former,} \markbox{9690}{let} \markbox{m9691}{$l_U$} \markbox{9692}{be} \markbox{9693}{the} \markbox{9694}{corresponding} \markbox{9695}{marked} \markbox{9696}{point---i.e.} \markbox{9697}{either} \markbox{m9698}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{9699}{If} \markbox{9700}{the} \markbox{9701}{latter,} \markbox{9702}{set} \markbox{m9703}{$l_U = \emptyset$}.  \markbox{9704}{We} \markbox{9705}{note} \markbox{9706}{that} \markbox{m9707}{$\ha_U \neq \hb_U$} \markbox{9708}{by} \markbox{9709}{construction} \markbox{9710}{when} \markbox{m9711}{$U$} \markbox{9712}{is} \markbox{m9713}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.

Now \markbox{9714}{suppose} \markbox{9715}{that} \markbox{m9716}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9717}{is} \markbox{9718}{not} \markbox{m9719}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.  \markbox{9720}{We} \markbox{9721}{have} \markbox{9722}{that} \markbox{9723}{either} \markbox{m9724}{$\hat{x}_U \in \hT^e_U$}, \markbox{9725}{in} \markbox{9726}{which} \markbox{9727}{case} \markbox{9728}{we} \markbox{9729}{set} \markbox{m9730}{$l_U = \emptyset$} \markbox{9731}{and} \markbox{m9732}{$x_U = q_U^{-1}(\hat{x}_U)$}.  \markbox{9733}{Otherwise,} \markbox{m9734}{$\hat{x}_U$} \markbox{9735}{is} \markbox{9736}{contained} \markbox{9737}{in} \markbox{9738}{a} \markbox{9739}{collapsed} \markbox{9740}{cluster} \markbox{m9741}{$q_U(C)$} \markbox{9742}{for} \markbox{9743}{the} \markbox{9744}{cluster} \markbox{m9745}{$C \subset T_U$}.  \markbox{9746}{Let} \markbox{m9747}{$\calB_{\min}(C)$} \markbox{9748}{denote} \markbox{9749}{the} \markbox{9750}{set} \markbox{9751}{of} \markbox{m9752}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{9753}{domains} \markbox{m9754}{$V\nest U$} \markbox{9755}{so} \markbox{9756}{that} \markbox{m9757}{$\delta^V_U \subset C$}.  \markbox{9758}{Observe} \markbox{9759}{that} \markbox{9760}{if} \markbox{m9761}{$\BM(C) = \emptyset$}, \markbox{9762}{then} \markbox{m9763}{$\diam_{T_U}(C)$} \markbox{9764}{is} \markbox{9765}{bounded} \markbox{9766}{in} \markbox{9767}{terms} \markbox{9768}{of} \markbox{m9769}{$r_1,r_2$} \markbox{9770}{and} \markbox{9771}{hence} \markbox{9772}{in} \markbox{9773}{terms} \markbox{9774}{of} \markbox{m9775}{$\mathfrak S$}.

We \markbox{9776}{now} \markbox{9777}{explain} \markbox{9778}{the} \markbox{9779}{honing} \markbox{9780}{process} \markbox{9781}{for} \markbox{9782}{domains} \markbox{9783}{in} \markbox{m9784}{$\BM(C)$}, \markbox{9785}{which} \markbox{9786}{will} \markbox{9787}{associate} \markbox{9788}{to} \markbox{m9789}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{9790}{a} \markbox{9791}{bounded} \markbox{9792}{diameter} \markbox{9793}{subset} \markbox{9794}{of} \markbox{9795}{the} \markbox{9796}{cluster} \markbox{m9797}{$C$} \markbox{9798}{in} \markbox{m9799}{$T_U$} \markbox{9800}{(Lemma} \ref{lem:bdd int total}).

Let \markbox{m9801}{$V \in \BM(C)$}.  \markbox{9802}{Then} \markbox{9803}{we} \markbox{9804}{set} 
$$C^V_U = \hull_C(C \cap (\calN_{r_2}(\delta^V_U) \cup l_V)),$$
which \markbox{9805}{is} \markbox{9806}{a} \markbox{9807}{subinterval} \markbox{9808}{of} \markbox{m9809}{$C$}, \markbox{9810}{see} \markbox{9811}{Figure} \ref{fig:C^V_U}.  \markbox{9812}{Finally,} \markbox{9813}{let} \markbox{m9814}{$B_U(\hx) = \bigcap_{V \in \BM(C)} C^V_U$} \markbox{9815}{be} \markbox{9816}{the} \markbox{9817}{total} \markbox{9818}{intersection} \markbox{9819}{of} \markbox{9820}{the} \markbox{m9821}{$C^V_U$}.

\begin{figure}
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=.8\textwidth]{figures/C_V_U_interval.pdf}
    \caption{The cluster $C$ (green) in $T_U$ is identified with $\hx_U$ in $\hT_U$.  Since $V \in \BM(C)$, its shadow $\delta^V_U$ (orange) avoids all branches of $T_U$.  The marked points and leaves $l_V$ (pink) chosen by $\hx_V$ determine the half-subtree $C^V_U$ (blue) of $C$ chosen by $V$.} 
    \label{fig:C^V_U}
\end{figure}



In \markbox{9822}{Lemma} \ref{lem:bdd int pair} \markbox{9823}{below,} \markbox{9824}{we} \markbox{9825}{prove} \markbox{9826}{that} \markbox{9827}{if} \markbox{m9828}{$V, W \in \BM(C)$}, \markbox{9829}{then} \markbox{m9830}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U \neq \emptyset$}.  \markbox{9831}{Since} \markbox{9832}{each} \markbox{m9833}{$C^V_U$} \markbox{9834}{is} \markbox{9835}{a} \markbox{9836}{subinterval,} \markbox{9837}{it} \markbox{9838}{follows} \markbox{9839}{from} \markbox{9840}{the} \markbox{9841}{Helly} \markbox{9842}{property} \markbox{9843}{for} \markbox{9844}{trees} \markbox{9845}{that} \markbox{m9846}{$B_U(x)$} \markbox{9847}{is} \markbox{9848}{nonempty.}  \markbox{9849}{Finally,} \markbox{9850}{in} \markbox{9851}{Lemma} \ref{lem:bdd int total} \markbox{9852}{we} \markbox{9853}{prove} \markbox{9854}{that} \markbox{9855}{this} \markbox{9856}{intersection} \markbox{9857}{has} \markbox{9858}{diameter} \markbox{9859}{bounded} \markbox{9860}{in} \markbox{9861}{terms} \markbox{9862}{of} \markbox{m9863}{$\mathfrak S$}.

Thus \markbox{9864}{we} \markbox{9865}{can} \markbox{9866}{define} \markbox{9867}{a} \markbox{9868}{tuple} \markbox{m9869}{$\Omega(\hx) = (x_U)_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{9870}{as} follows:
\begin{itemize}
    \item {} For \markbox{m9871}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9872}{with} \markbox{m9873}{$U \in E(\hx)$}, \markbox{9874}{we} \markbox{9875}{set} \markbox{m9876}{$x_U = q_U^{-1}(\hx_U)$}.
    \item {} For \markbox{m9877}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{9878}{with} \markbox{m9879}{$U \notin E(\hx)$} \markbox{9880}{and} \markbox{m9881}{$U \nest_{\calU}$}-minimal, \markbox{9882}{we} \markbox{9883}{let} \markbox{m9884}{$x_U$} \markbox{9885}{be} \markbox{9886}{any} \markbox{9887}{point} \markbox{9888}{in} \markbox{m9889}{$q_U^{-1}(\hx_U)$}.
    \item {} Otherwise, \markbox{9890}{we} \markbox{9891}{let} \markbox{m9892}{$x_U \in B_U(\hx)$}.
\end{itemize}

The \markbox{9893}{following} \markbox{9894}{is} \markbox{9895}{immediate} \markbox{9896}{from} \markbox{9897}{the} construction:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:B_U in cluster}
For \markbox{9898}{every} \markbox{m9899}{$\hx \in \calQ$} \markbox{9900}{and} \markbox{m9901}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{9902}{we} \markbox{9903}{have} \markbox{m9904}{$q_U(x_U) = \hx_U$}.
\end{lemma}


In \markbox{9905}{Proposition} \ref{prop:Q-consistent} \markbox{9906}{below,} \markbox{9907}{we} \markbox{9908}{prove} \markbox{9909}{that} \markbox{m9910}{$(x_U)$} \markbox{9911}{is} \markbox{9912}{a} \markbox{m9913}{$\omega$}-consistent \markbox{9914}{tuple} \markbox{9915}{for} \markbox{m9916}{$\omega = \omega(\mathfrak S)>0$}.

\begin{remark}[Cubical flavor]
The \markbox{9917}{process} \markbox{9918}{of} \markbox{9919}{cluster} \markbox{9920}{honing} \markbox{9921}{is} \markbox{9922}{one} \markbox{9923}{of} \markbox{9924}{the} \markbox{9925}{few} \markbox{9926}{places} \markbox{9927}{where} \markbox{9928}{one} \markbox{9929}{sees} \markbox{9930}{cubical-like} \markbox{9931}{features} \markbox{9932}{appearing} \markbox{9933}{in} \markbox{9934}{a} \markbox{9935}{non-explicitly} \markbox{9936}{cubical} \markbox{9937}{part} \markbox{9938}{of} \markbox{9939}{the} \markbox{9940}{construction.}  \markbox{9941}{In} \markbox{9942}{particular,} \markbox{9943}{it} \markbox{9944}{is} \markbox{9945}{crucial} \markbox{9946}{that} \markbox{9947}{the} \markbox{9948}{two} \markbox{9949}{endpoints} \markbox{m9950}{$\ha_V, \hb_V$} \markbox{9951}{for} \markbox{9952}{every} \markbox{m9953}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{m9954}{$V$} \markbox{9955}{are} \markbox{9956}{distinct} \markbox{9957}{in} \markbox{m9958}{$\hT_V$}.  \markbox{9959}{Hence} \markbox{m9960}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{9961}{domains} \markbox{9962}{determine} \markbox{9963}{a} \markbox{9964}{choice} \markbox{9965}{of} \markbox{9966}{endpoint} \markbox{9967}{between} \markbox{m9968}{$a,b$}, \markbox{9969}{like} \markbox{9970}{a} \markbox{9971}{wall} \markbox{9972}{choosing} \markbox{9973}{a} half-space.

When \markbox{m9974}{$U$} \markbox{9975}{is} \markbox{9976}{not} \markbox{m9977}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{9978}{and} \markbox{m9979}{$\hd^V_U = \hx_U$}, \markbox{9980}{then} \markbox{9981}{the} \markbox{9982}{coordinate} \markbox{m9983}{$\hx_V$} \markbox{9984}{either} \markbox{9985}{chooses} \markbox{9986}{neither} \markbox{9987}{endpoint} \markbox{9988}{of} \markbox{m9989}{$\hT_V$} \markbox{9990}{(if} \markbox{m9991}{$\hx_V \in \hT^e_V$}), \markbox{9992}{or} \markbox{9993}{chooses} \markbox{9994}{one} \markbox{9995}{of} \markbox{m9996}{$\ha_V,\hb_V$}.  \markbox{9997}{This} \markbox{9998}{choice} \markbox{9999}{then} \markbox{10000}{determines} \markbox{10001}{a} \markbox{10002}{sort} \markbox{10003}{of} \markbox{10004}{``half-interval''} \markbox{m10005}{$C^V_U$} \markbox{10006}{of} \markbox{m10007}{$C$}, \markbox{10008}{where} \markbox{10009}{we} \markbox{10010}{can} \markbox{10011}{think} \markbox{10012}{of} \markbox{m10013}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{10014}{as} \markbox{10015}{functioning} \markbox{10016}{like} \markbox{10017}{a} \markbox{10018}{hyperplane} \markbox{10019}{here.}  \markbox{10020}{In} \markbox{10021}{Lemmas} \ref{lem:bdd int pair} \markbox{10022}{and} \ref{lem:bdd int total} \markbox{10023}{below,} \markbox{10024}{we} \markbox{10025}{see} \markbox{10026}{that} \markbox{10027}{the} \markbox{10028}{intersection} \markbox{10029}{over} \markbox{10030}{all} \markbox{10031}{such} \markbox{10032}{``half-intervals''} \markbox{m10033}{$B_U = \bigcap_{V \in \BM(C)} C^V_U$} \markbox{10034}{is} \markbox{10035}{nonempty} \markbox{10036}{and} \markbox{10037}{has} \markbox{10038}{bounded} \markbox{10039}{diameter,} \markbox{10040}{and} \markbox{10041}{this} \markbox{10042}{ultra-filter-like} \markbox{10043}{behavior} \markbox{10044}{is} \markbox{10045}{forced} \markbox{10046}{by} \markbox{10047}{consistency} \markbox{10048}{of} \markbox{10049}{the} \markbox{10050}{tuple} \markbox{m10051}{$\hx$}.
\end{remark}

\begin{remark}[A warning]
    \markbox{10052}{The} \markbox{10053}{reader} \markbox{10054}{should} \markbox{10055}{be} \markbox{10056}{warned} \markbox{10057}{that} \markbox{10058}{one} \markbox{10059}{has} \markbox{10060}{to} \markbox{10061}{deal} \markbox{10062}{with} \markbox{10063}{the} \markbox{10064}{case} \markbox{10065}{of} \markbox{m10066}{$\hx \in \calQ$} \markbox{10067}{where} \markbox{m10068}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{10069}{is} \markbox{10070}{a} \markbox{10071}{cluster} \markbox{10072}{or} \markbox{10073}{endpoint} \markbox{10074}{for} \markbox{10075}{every} \markbox{10076}{coordinate} \markbox{m10077}{$U$}.  \markbox{10078}{While,} \markbox{10079}{as} \markbox{10080}{in} \markbox{10081}{the} \markbox{10082}{previous} \markbox{10083}{remark,} \markbox{10084}{such} \markbox{10085}{points} \markbox{10086}{determine} \markbox{10087}{unambiguous} \markbox{10088}{coordinates} \markbox{10089}{in} \markbox{m10090}{$T_U$} \markbox{10091}{for} \markbox{10092}{all} \markbox{m10093}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{10094}{domains} \markbox{m10095}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{10096}{there} \markbox{10097}{is} \markbox{10098}{no} \markbox{10099}{way} \markbox{10100}{to} \markbox{10101}{leverage} \markbox{10102}{this} \markbox{10103}{data} \markbox{10104}{alone} \markbox{10105}{into} \markbox{10106}{choosing} \markbox{10107}{coordinates} \markbox{10108}{in} \markbox{m10109}{$T_V$} \markbox{10110}{for} \markbox{10111}{domains} \markbox{m10112}{$V$} \markbox{10113}{higher} \markbox{10114}{up} \markbox{10115}{the} \markbox{m10116}{$\nest$}-lattice.  \markbox{10117}{One} \markbox{10118}{must} \markbox{10119}{utilize} \markbox{10120}{the} \markbox{10121}{full} \markbox{10122}{set} \markbox{10123}{of} \markbox{10124}{relations} \markbox{10125}{between} \markbox{10126}{all} \markbox{10127}{of} \markbox{10128}{the} domains.
\end{remark}






\subsection{Bounding intersections}

In \markbox{10129}{this} \markbox{10130}{subsection,} \markbox{10131}{we} \markbox{10132}{prove} \markbox{10133}{the} \markbox{10134}{supporting} \markbox{10135}{statements} \markbox{10136}{we} \markbox{10137}{need} \markbox{10138}{to} \markbox{10139}{define} \markbox{10140}{the} \markbox{10141}{map} \markbox{m10142}{$\Omega:\calQ \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$}.  \markbox{10143}{Again} \markbox{10144}{fix} \markbox{m10145}{$\hx \in \calQ$}.

The \markbox{10146}{first} \markbox{10147}{says} \markbox{10148}{that} \markbox{10149}{the} \markbox{m10150}{$C^V_U$} \markbox{10151}{for} \markbox{m10152}{$V \in \BM(C)$} \markbox{10153}{have} \markbox{10154}{pairwise} \markbox{10155}{nonempty} intersection:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:bdd int pair}
If \markbox{m10156}{$V, W \in \BM(C)$}, \markbox{10157}{then} \markbox{m10158}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U \neq \emptyset$}.  \markbox{10159}{Moreover,} \markbox{10160}{if} \markbox{m10161}{$d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U, \delta^W_U)>r_2$}, \markbox{10162}{then} \markbox{10163}{at} \markbox{10164}{least} \markbox{10165}{one} \markbox{10166}{of} \markbox{m10167}{$\delta^V_U \subset C^W_U$} \markbox{10168}{or} \markbox{m10169}{$\delta^W_U \subset C^V_U$} holds.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}[Sketch \markbox{10170}{of} proof]

We \markbox{10171}{provide} \markbox{10172}{a} \markbox{10173}{sketch} \markbox{10174}{of} \markbox{10175}{the} \markbox{10176}{proof,} \markbox{10177}{see} \cite[Lemma 9.9]{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{10178}{We} \markbox{10179}{shall} \markbox{10180}{observe} \markbox{10181}{item} \markbox{10182}{(1)} \markbox{10183}{during} \markbox{10184}{the} \markbox{10185}{course} \markbox{10186}{of} \markbox{10187}{the} \markbox{10188}{proof} \markbox{10189}{of} \markbox{10190}{the} sketch.

By \markbox{10191}{definition} \markbox{10192}{of} \markbox{m10193}{$C^V_U = \hull_C((\calN_{r_2}(\delta^V_U) \cup l_V)\cap C)$}, \markbox{10194}{we} \markbox{10195}{may} \markbox{10196}{assume} \markbox{10197}{that} \markbox{m10198}{$\calN_{r_2}(\delta^V_U) \cap \calN_{r_2}(\delta^W_U) = \emptyset$}, \markbox{10199}{and} \markbox{10200}{hence} \markbox{10201}{that} \markbox{m10202}{$V \pitchfork W$} \markbox{10203}{by} \markbox{10204}{item} \markbox{10205}{(3)} \markbox{10206}{of} \markbox{10207}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control}.  \markbox{10208}{The} \markbox{10209}{idea} \markbox{10210}{now} \markbox{10211}{is} \markbox{10212}{that} \markbox{m10213}{$\delta^V_U, \delta^W_U$} \markbox{10214}{must} \markbox{10215}{occur} \markbox{10216}{separately} \markbox{10217}{along} \markbox{10218}{the} \markbox{10219}{cluster} \markbox{m10220}{$C$}.  \markbox{10221}{Without} \markbox{10222}{loss} \markbox{10223}{of} \markbox{10224}{generality,} \markbox{10225}{we} \markbox{10226}{can} \markbox{10227}{assume} \markbox{10228}{that} \markbox{m10229}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{10230}{separates} \markbox{m10231}{$a_U$} \markbox{10232}{from} \markbox{m10233}{$\delta^W_U$}.  \markbox{10234}{One} \markbox{10235}{can} \markbox{10236}{then} \markbox{10237}{use} \markbox{10238}{the} \markbox{10239}{consistency} \markbox{10240}{of} \markbox{m10241}{$(\hx_U)$} \markbox{10242}{and} \markbox{10243}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control} \markbox{10244}{and} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{10245}{to} \markbox{10246}{show} \markbox{10247}{that} \markbox{10248}{at} \markbox{10249}{least} \markbox{10250}{one} \markbox{10251}{of} \markbox{m10252}{$l_V = b$} \markbox{10253}{or} \markbox{m10254}{$l_W = a$}, \markbox{10255}{which} \markbox{10256}{would} \markbox{10257}{force} \markbox{m10258}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U \neq \emptyset$}, \markbox{10259}{as} \markbox{10260}{required;} \markbox{10261}{see} \markbox{10262}{Figure} \ref{fig:cluster_int}.

\begin{figure}
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=.8\textwidth]{figures/cluster_int_interval.pdf}
    \caption{The impossible situation in which $V\pitchfork W \in \BM(C)$ choose non-intersecting sides $C^V_U$ (pink) and $C^W_U$ (blue) of $C$ (green).  This forces inconsistency of $\hx_V$ and $\hx_W$.} 
    \label{fig:cluster_int}
\end{figure}
\end{proof}

As \markbox{10263}{discussed} \markbox{10264}{above,} \markbox{10265}{we} \markbox{10266}{can} \markbox{10267}{define} \markbox{m10268}{$B_U = \bigcap_{V \in \BM(C)}C^V_U$} \markbox{10269}{and} \markbox{10270}{it} \markbox{10271}{must} \markbox{10272}{be} \markbox{10273}{non-empty} \markbox{10274}{by} \markbox{10275}{the} \markbox{10276}{Helly} \markbox{10277}{property} \markbox{10278}{for} \markbox{10279}{trees} \markbox{10280}{as} \markbox{10281}{long} \markbox{10282}{as} \markbox{m10283}{$\BM(C) \neq \emptyset$}.

\begin{remark}\label{rem:Helly}
The \markbox{10284}{Helly} \markbox{10285}{property} \markbox{10286}{for} \markbox{10287}{trees} \markbox{10288}{says} \markbox{10289}{that} \markbox{10290}{if} \markbox{10291}{one} \markbox{10292}{has} \markbox{10293}{a} \markbox{10294}{pairwise-intersecting} \markbox{10295}{collection} \markbox{10296}{of} \markbox{10297}{subtrees} \markbox{10298}{then} \markbox{10299}{the} \markbox{10300}{collection} \markbox{10301}{has} \markbox{10302}{nonempty} \markbox{10303}{total} \markbox{10304}{intersection.}  \markbox{10305}{In} \markbox{10306}{the} \markbox{10307}{general} \markbox{10308}{version} \markbox{10309}{of} \markbox{10310}{our} \markbox{10311}{current} \markbox{10312}{construction} \markbox{10313}{from} \cite{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{10314}{the} \markbox{10315}{trees} \markbox{10316}{and} \markbox{10317}{subtrees} \markbox{10318}{in} \markbox{10319}{question} \markbox{10320}{need} \markbox{10321}{not} \markbox{10322}{be} \markbox{10323}{finite} \markbox{10324}{diameter.}  \markbox{10325}{This} \markbox{10326}{is} \markbox{10327}{one} \markbox{10328}{place} \markbox{10329}{where} \markbox{10330}{the} \markbox{10331}{arguments} \markbox{10332}{in} \markbox{10333}{our} \markbox{10334}{current} \markbox{10335}{context} \markbox{10336}{are} \markbox{10337}{simpler} \markbox{10338}{than} \markbox{10339}{that} \markbox{10340}{considered} \markbox{10341}{in} \cite{Dur_infcube}.
\end{remark}

The \markbox{10342}{next} \markbox{10343}{lemma} \markbox{10344}{bounds} \markbox{10345}{the} \markbox{10346}{diameter} \markbox{10347}{of} \markbox{m10348}{$B_U$}:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:bdd int total}
There \markbox{10349}{exists} \markbox{m10350}{$B_1 = B_1(\mathfrak S,r_2)>0$} \markbox{10351}{such} \markbox{10352}{that} \markbox{10353}{for} \markbox{10354}{all} \markbox{m10355}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{10356}{we} \markbox{10357}{have} 
\markbox{m10358}{$\diam_{T_U}(B_U) < B_1$}.
\end{lemma}

\begin{proof}

If \markbox{m10359}{$B_U$} \markbox{10360}{is} \markbox{10361}{too} \markbox{10362}{wide} \markbox{10363}{(relative} \markbox{10364}{to} \markbox{m10365}{$r_2$}), \markbox{10366}{then} \markbox{10367}{we} \markbox{10368}{can} \markbox{10369}{find} \markbox{m10370}{$V, W \in \BM(C)$} \markbox{10371}{with} \markbox{m10372}{$\delta^V_U, \delta^W_U \subset B_U$} \markbox{10373}{and} \markbox{m10374}{$r'< d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U, \delta^W_U) < 2r'$} \markbox{10375}{for} \markbox{m10376}{$r' = r'(r_2)>0$}, \markbox{10377}{since} \markbox{10378}{the} \markbox{m10379}{$\delta$}-sets \markbox{10380}{for} \markbox{10381}{domains} \markbox{10382}{in} \markbox{m10383}{$\BM(C)$} \markbox{10384}{coarsely} \markbox{10385}{cover} \markbox{m10386}{$C$} \markbox{10387}{with} \markbox{10388}{coarseness} \markbox{10389}{depending} \markbox{10390}{only} \markbox{10391}{on} \markbox{m10392}{$r_2$}.  \markbox{10393}{By} \markbox{10394}{Lemma} \ref{lem:bdd int pair}, \markbox{10395}{we} \markbox{10396}{must} \markbox{10397}{have} \markbox{10398}{at} \markbox{10399}{least} \markbox{10400}{one} \markbox{10401}{of} \markbox{m10402}{$\delta^V_U \subset C^W_U$} \markbox{10403}{or} \markbox{m10404}{$\delta^W_U \subset C^V_U$}, \markbox{10405}{or} \markbox{10406}{possibly} \markbox{10407}{both.}  \markbox{10408}{In} \markbox{10409}{fact,} \markbox{10410}{both} \markbox{10411}{must} \markbox{10412}{hold,} \markbox{10413}{for} \markbox{10414}{if} \markbox{m10415}{$\delta^V_U \notin C^W_U$}, \markbox{10416}{then} \markbox{m10417}{$\delta^V_U \notin B_U$}, \markbox{10418}{which} \markbox{10419}{is} \markbox{10420}{impossible.}  \markbox{10421}{But} \markbox{10422}{then} \markbox{m10423}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U \subset \hull_C(\calN_{r_2}(\delta^V_U) \cup \calN_{r_2}(\delta^W_U))$}, \markbox{10424}{which} \markbox{10425}{has} \markbox{10426}{diameter} \markbox{10427}{bounded} \markbox{10428}{by} \markbox{m10429}{$2r' + 2r_2$} \markbox{10430}{since} \markbox{m10431}{$d_{T_U}(\delta^V_U, \delta^W_U) < 2r'$}.  \markbox{10432}{Since} \markbox{m10433}{$B_U \subset C^V_U \cap C^W_U$}, \markbox{10434}{this} \markbox{10435}{completes} \markbox{10436}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

We \markbox{10437}{are} \markbox{10438}{now} \markbox{10439}{in} \markbox{10440}{place} \markbox{10441}{to} \markbox{10442}{state} \markbox{10443}{the} \markbox{10444}{consistency} result:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:Q-consistent}
There \markbox{10445}{exist} \markbox{m10446}{$\alpha_{\omega}=\alpha_{\omega}(\mathfrak S,r_1,r_2,R)>0$} \markbox{10447}{and} \markbox{10448}{a} \markbox{10449}{map} \markbox{m10450}{$\Omega: \calQ \to \calY$} \markbox{10451}{so} \markbox{10452}{that} \markbox{10453}{for} \markbox{10454}{any} \markbox{m10455}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{10456}{the} \markbox{10457}{tuple} \markbox{m10458}{$\Omega(\hx)$} \markbox{10459}{is} \markbox{m10460}{$\alpha_{\omega}$}-consistent.  \markbox{10461}{Moreover,} \markbox{10462}{if} \markbox{m10463}{$\Omega(\hx) = (x_U)$}, \markbox{10464}{then} \markbox{m10465}{$q_U(x_U) = \hx_U$} \markbox{10466}{for} \markbox{10467}{each} \markbox{m10468}{$U \in \calU$}.
\end{proposition}

The \markbox{10469}{proof} \markbox{10470}{of} \markbox{10471}{this} \markbox{10472}{proposition} \markbox{10473}{is} \markbox{10474}{a} \markbox{10475}{somewhat} \markbox{10476}{elaborate} \markbox{10477}{exercise} \markbox{10478}{in} \markbox{10479}{the} \markbox{10480}{definition} \markbox{10481}{of} \markbox{m10482}{$\Omega$} \markbox{10483}{and} \markbox{10484}{the} \markbox{10485}{construction} \markbox{10486}{of} \markbox{10487}{the} \markbox{10488}{clusters,} \markbox{10489}{in} \markbox{10490}{which} \markbox{10491}{one} \markbox{10492}{utilizes} \markbox{10493}{many} \markbox{10494}{standard} \markbox{10495}{HHS-type} \markbox{10496}{arguments.}  \markbox{10497}{Unlike} \markbox{10498}{other} \markbox{10499}{proofs} \markbox{10500}{in} \markbox{10501}{this} \markbox{10502}{paper,} \markbox{10503}{the} \markbox{10504}{proof} \markbox{10505}{of} \markbox{10506}{this} \markbox{10507}{fact} \markbox{10508}{in} \markbox{10509}{our} \markbox{10510}{current} \markbox{10511}{setting} \markbox{10512}{is} \markbox{10513}{not} \markbox{10514}{substantially} \markbox{10515}{different} \markbox{10516}{from} \markbox{10517}{proof} \markbox{10518}{in} \markbox{10519}{the} \markbox{10520}{general} \markbox{10521}{case} \markbox{10522}{in} \cite[Subsection 9.5]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{10523}{beyond} \markbox{10524}{the} \markbox{10525}{need} \markbox{10526}{for} \markbox{10527}{working} \markbox{10528}{with} \markbox{m10529}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{10530}{\emph{bipartite domains}} \markbox{10531}{as} \markbox{10532}{defined} \markbox{10533}{in} \cite[Definition 9.2]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{10534}{instead} \markbox{10535}{of} \markbox{10536}{all} \markbox{m10537}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{10538}{domains.}  \markbox{10539}{Thus} \markbox{10540}{instead} \markbox{10541}{of} \markbox{10542}{repeating} \markbox{10543}{it} \markbox{10544}{here,} \markbox{10545}{we} \markbox{10546}{leave} \markbox{10547}{it} \markbox{10548}{to} \markbox{10549}{the} \markbox{10550}{interested} \markbox{10551}{reader} \markbox{10552}{to} \markbox{10553}{check} \markbox{10554}{the} details.

\subsection{Tree trimming}\label{subsec:tree trimming}

In \markbox{10555}{this} \markbox{10556}{subsection,} \markbox{10557}{we} \markbox{10558}{introduce} \markbox{10559}{a} \markbox{10560}{useful} \markbox{10561}{tool} \markbox{10562}{for} \markbox{10563}{modifying} \markbox{10564}{collapsed} \markbox{10565}{interval} \markbox{10566}{systems} \markbox{10567}{and} \markbox{10568}{their} \markbox{10569}{associated} \markbox{m10570}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{10571}{sets.}  \markbox{10572}{These} \markbox{10573}{``tree-trimming''} \markbox{10574}{techniques} \markbox{10575}{will} \markbox{10576}{allow} \markbox{10577}{us} \markbox{10578}{to} \markbox{10579}{perform} \markbox{10580}{controlled} \markbox{10581}{collapses} \markbox{10582}{of} \markbox{10583}{subintervals} \markbox{10584}{across} \markbox{10585}{the} \markbox{10586}{various} \markbox{10587}{collapsed} \markbox{10588}{intervals} \markbox{m10589}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{10590}{while} \markbox{10591}{coarsely} \markbox{10592}{preserving} \markbox{10593}{the} \markbox{10594}{associated} \markbox{m10595}{$\calQ$}-distance.  \markbox{10596}{We} \markbox{10597}{think} \markbox{10598}{of} \markbox{10599}{them} \markbox{10600}{as} \markbox{10601}{a} \markbox{10602}{more} \markbox{10603}{flexible} \markbox{10604}{version} \markbox{10605}{of} \markbox{10606}{the} \markbox{10607}{distance} \markbox{10608}{formula,} \markbox{10609}{as} \markbox{10610}{they} \markbox{10611}{allow} \markbox{10612}{us} \markbox{10613}{to} \markbox{10614}{modify} \markbox{10615}{distance} \markbox{10616}{terms} \markbox{10617}{instead} \markbox{10618}{of} \markbox{10619}{just} \markbox{10620}{throwing} \markbox{10621}{them} \markbox{10622}{out} \markbox{10623}{by} \markbox{10624}{increasing} \markbox{10625}{a} \markbox{10626}{threshold.}  \markbox{10627}{For} \markbox{10628}{our} \markbox{10629}{purposes,} \markbox{10630}{they} \markbox{10631}{will} \markbox{10632}{be} \markbox{10633}{used} \markbox{10634}{in} \markbox{10635}{two} \markbox{10636}{different} \markbox{10637}{ways:} \markbox{10638}{We} \markbox{10639}{will} \markbox{10640}{need} \markbox{10641}{them} \markbox{10642}{in} \markbox{10643}{the} \markbox{10644}{proof} \markbox{10645}{of} \markbox{10646}{coarse} \markbox{10647}{surjectivity} \markbox{10648}{of} \markbox{m10649}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$}, \markbox{10650}{and} \markbox{10651}{they} \markbox{10652}{will} \markbox{10653}{also} \markbox{10654}{be} \markbox{10655}{useful} \markbox{10656}{later} \markbox{10657}{in} \markbox{10658}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:tt cube} \markbox{10659}{to} \markbox{10660}{modify} \markbox{10661}{the} \markbox{10662}{cubical} \markbox{10663}{structure} \markbox{10664}{on} \markbox{m10665}{$\calQ$}.

The \markbox{10666}{main} \markbox{10667}{idea} \markbox{10668}{is} \markbox{10669}{simple:} \markbox{10670}{Given} \markbox{10671}{a} \markbox{10672}{family} \markbox{10673}{of} \markbox{10674}{subintervals} \markbox{m10675}{$\calB$} \markbox{10676}{across} \markbox{10677}{of} \markbox{10678}{the} \markbox{10679}{family} \markbox{10680}{of} \markbox{10681}{intervals} \markbox{m10682}{$\hT_U$}, \markbox{10683}{we} \markbox{10684}{want} \markbox{10685}{to} \markbox{10686}{collapse} \markbox{10687}{these} \markbox{10688}{subintervals} \markbox{m10689}{$\Delta_U:\hT_U \to \hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{10690}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{10691}{and} \markbox{10692}{then} \markbox{10693}{combine} \markbox{10694}{them} \markbox{10695}{into} \markbox{10696}{a} \markbox{10697}{global} \markbox{10698}{collapsing} \markbox{10699}{map} \markbox{m10700}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$}, \markbox{10701}{where} \markbox{m10702}{$\calQ'$} \markbox{10703}{is} \markbox{10704}{the} \markbox{m10705}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{10706}{set} \markbox{10707}{of} \markbox{m10708}{$\prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_{U,0}$}, \markbox{10709}{defined} \markbox{10710}{the} \markbox{10711}{same} \markbox{10712}{way} \markbox{10713}{as} \markbox{10714}{in} \markbox{10715}{Definition} \ref{defn:Q defined}.  \markbox{10716}{Formally,} \markbox{10717}{we} \markbox{10718}{use} \markbox{10719}{the} \markbox{10720}{following} definition:

\begin{definition}[Admissible \markbox{10721}{trimming} setup]\label{defn:trimming setup}
Given \markbox{m10722}{$B>0$}, \markbox{10723}{a} \markbox{m10724}{$B$}-\markbox{10725}{\emph{admissible trimming setup}} \markbox{10726}{is} \markbox{10727}{a} \markbox{10728}{collection} \markbox{10729}{of} \markbox{10730}{\emph{trimming intervals}} \markbox{m10731}{$\calB$} \markbox{10732}{in} \markbox{10733}{the} \markbox{10734}{various} \markbox{m10735}{$\hT_{U,e}$} \markbox{10736}{satisfying} \markbox{10737}{the} following:
\begin{itemize}
\item {} For \markbox{10738}{each} \markbox{10739}{component}  \markbox{m10740}{$E \in \pi_0(\hT_{U,e})$}, \markbox{10741}{there} \markbox{10742}{are} \markbox{10743}{at} \markbox{10744}{most} \markbox{m10745}{$B$}-many \markbox{10746}{components} \markbox{m10747}{$D \in \calB$} \markbox{10748}{with} \markbox{m10749}{$D \subset E$}.
\item {} For \markbox{10750}{each} \markbox{10751}{component} \markbox{m10752}{$D \in \calB$} \markbox{10753}{satisfies} \markbox{m10754}{$|D|<B$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

Given \markbox{10755}{a} \markbox{m10756}{$B$}-admissible \markbox{10757}{trimming} \markbox{10758}{setup} \markbox{m10759}{$\calB$} \markbox{10760}{on} \markbox{m10761}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in\calU}$}, \markbox{10762}{for} \markbox{10763}{each} \markbox{m10764}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{10765}{let} \markbox{m10766}{$\Delta_U:\hT_U \to \hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{10767}{denote} \markbox{10768}{the} \markbox{10769}{map} \markbox{10770}{which} \markbox{10771}{collapses} \markbox{10772}{each} \markbox{10773}{trimming} \markbox{10774}{interval} \markbox{10775}{in} \markbox{m10776}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{10777}{to} \markbox{10778}{a} \markbox{10779}{point.}  \markbox{10780}{These} \markbox{10781}{allow} \markbox{10782}{us} \markbox{10783}{to} \markbox{10784}{induce} \markbox{10785}{projection} \markbox{10786}{data} \markbox{10787}{on} \markbox{10788}{the} \markbox{m10789}{$\hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{10790}{as} \markbox{10791}{follows:} \markbox{10792}{For} \markbox{m10793}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{10794}{and} \markbox{m10795}{$V \pitchfork U$}, \markbox{10796}{we} \markbox{10797}{set} \markbox{m10798}{$(\hd^V_U)_0 = \Delta_U(\hd^V_U)$}, \markbox{10799}{and} \markbox{10800}{if} \markbox{m10801}{$U \nest V$}, \markbox{10802}{we} \markbox{10803}{set} \markbox{m10804}{$(\hd^V_U)_0 = \Delta_U \circ \hd^V_U \circ \Delta^{-1}_V$}.  \markbox{10805}{We} \markbox{10806}{let} \markbox{m10807}{$\Delta: \prod_{\calU} \hT_U \to \prod_{\calU} \hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{10808}{denote} \markbox{10809}{the} \markbox{10810}{product} map.


\begin{theorem}[Tree Trimming]\label{thm:tree trimming}
There \markbox{10811}{exists} \markbox{m10812}{$B_{tt} = B_{tt}(\mathfrak S, K)>0$} \markbox{10813}{so} \markbox{10814}{that} \markbox{10815}{for} \markbox{10816}{any} \markbox{m10817}{$B < B_{tt}$}, \markbox{10818}{there} \markbox{10819}{exists} \markbox{m10820}{$L =L(\mathfrak S, B)>0$} \markbox{10821}{so} \markbox{10822}{that} \markbox{10823}{the} \markbox{10824}{following} hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item {} We \markbox{10825}{have} \markbox{m10826}{$\Delta(\calQ) \subset \calQ'$}.
\item {} There \markbox{10827}{is} \markbox{10828}{a} \markbox{10829}{map} \markbox{m10830}{$\Xi:\calQ' \to \calQ$} \markbox{10831}{so} \markbox{10832}{that} \markbox{m10833}{$\Delta \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ'}$}.  \markbox{10834}{In} \markbox{10835}{particular,} \markbox{m10836}{$\Delta(\calQ) = \calQ'$}.
\item {} The \markbox{10837}{map} \markbox{m10838}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{10839}{is} \markbox{10840}{an} \markbox{m10841}{$(L,L)$}-quasi-isometry.
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

While \markbox{10842}{the} \markbox{10843}{statement} \markbox{10844}{is} \markbox{10845}{quite} \markbox{10846}{believable} \markbox{10847}{in} \markbox{10848}{light} \markbox{10849}{of} \markbox{10850}{the} \markbox{10851}{Distance} \markbox{10852}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}, \markbox{10853}{the} \markbox{10854}{proof} \markbox{10855}{of} \markbox{10856}{this} \markbox{10857}{theorem} \markbox{10858}{is} \markbox{10859}{quite} \markbox{10860}{involved.}  \markbox{10861}{While} \markbox{10862}{these} \markbox{10863}{ideas} \markbox{10864}{were} \markbox{10865}{first} \markbox{10866}{developed} \markbox{10867}{in} \markbox{10868}{greater} \markbox{10869}{generality} \markbox{10870}{in} \cite[Section 10]{Dur_infcube}---where \markbox{10871}{it} \markbox{10872}{also} \markbox{10873}{works} \markbox{10874}{when} \markbox{10875}{the} \markbox{10876}{underlying} \markbox{10877}{data} \markbox{10878}{involves} \markbox{10879}{more} \markbox{10880}{than} \markbox{10881}{two} \markbox{10882}{points} \markbox{10883}{and} \markbox{10884}{also} \markbox{10885}{hierarchy} \markbox{10886}{rays---the} \markbox{10887}{proof} \markbox{10888}{these} \markbox{10889}{is} \markbox{10890}{only} \markbox{10891}{slightly} \markbox{10892}{more} \markbox{10893}{involved} \markbox{10894}{than} \markbox{10895}{that} \markbox{10896}{required} \markbox{10897}{in} \markbox{10898}{our} \markbox{10899}{setting.}  \markbox{10900}{Moreover,} \markbox{10901}{many} \markbox{10902}{of} \markbox{10903}{the} \markbox{10904}{technicalities} \markbox{10905}{from} \markbox{10906}{dealing} \markbox{10907}{with} \markbox{10908}{rays} \markbox{10909}{are} \markbox{10910}{dealt} \markbox{10911}{with} \markbox{10912}{in} \markbox{10913}{separate} \markbox{10914}{arguments,} \markbox{10915}{so} \markbox{10916}{the} \markbox{10917}{interested} \markbox{10918}{reader} \markbox{10919}{is} \markbox{10920}{encouraged} \markbox{10921}{to} \markbox{10922}{see} \markbox{10923}{a} \markbox{10924}{full} \markbox{10925}{proof} there.

Instead, \markbox{10926}{we} \markbox{10927}{will} \markbox{10928}{present} \markbox{10929}{a} \markbox{10930}{short} \markbox{10931}{sketch} \markbox{10932}{below,} \markbox{10933}{which} \markbox{10934}{will} \markbox{10935}{hopefully} \markbox{10936}{provide} \markbox{10937}{enough} \markbox{10938}{intuition} \markbox{10939}{to} \markbox{10940}{make} \markbox{10941}{the} \markbox{10942}{statement} \markbox{10943}{believable.}  \markbox{10944}{We} \markbox{10945}{have} \markbox{10946}{included} \markbox{10947}{a} \markbox{10948}{proof} \markbox{10949}{of} \markbox{10950}{the} \markbox{10951}{stated} \markbox{10952}{version} \markbox{10953}{of} \markbox{10954}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming} \markbox{10955}{in} \markbox{10956}{Appendix} \ref{app:TT}.



\begin{proof}[Sketch \markbox{10957}{of} proof]
The \markbox{10958}{fact} \markbox{10959}{that} \markbox{m10960}{$\Delta(\calQ) \subset \calQ'$}, \markbox{10961}{namely} \markbox{10962}{that} \markbox{m10963}{$\Delta$} \markbox{10964}{preserves} \markbox{m10965}{$0$}-consistency, \markbox{10966}{is} \markbox{10967}{immediate} \markbox{10968}{from} \markbox{10969}{the} \markbox{10970}{fact} \markbox{10971}{that} \markbox{10972}{the} \markbox{m10973}{$\Delta_U$} \markbox{10974}{just} \markbox{10975}{collapse} \markbox{10976}{subintervals,} \markbox{10977}{so} \markbox{10978}{coordinates} \markbox{10979}{which} \markbox{10980}{were} \markbox{10981}{collapsed} \markbox{10982}{projections} \markbox{10983}{remain} \markbox{10984}{collapsed} \markbox{10985}{projections,} \markbox{10986}{showing} \markbox{10987}{item} (1).

Item \markbox{10988}{(2)} \markbox{10989}{is} \markbox{10990}{the} \markbox{10991}{most} \markbox{10992}{involved} \markbox{10993}{part.}  \markbox{10994}{For} \markbox{10995}{each} \markbox{m10996}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{10997}{let} \markbox{m10998}{$C_U = \Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$}.  \markbox{10999}{The} \markbox{11000}{goal} \markbox{11001}{is} \markbox{11002}{to} \markbox{11003}{pick,} \markbox{11004}{for} \markbox{11005}{each} \markbox{m11006}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{11007}{a} \markbox{11008}{point} \markbox{m11009}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{11010}{and} \markbox{11011}{then} \markbox{11012}{prove} \markbox{m11013}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{11014}{of} \markbox{11015}{the} \markbox{11016}{tuple} \markbox{m11017}{$\hx = (\hx_U)$}.  \markbox{11018}{Note} \markbox{11019}{that} \markbox{m11020}{$\Delta(\hx) =\hy$} \markbox{11021}{for} \markbox{11022}{such} \markbox{11023}{a} \markbox{11024}{tuple,} \markbox{11025}{by} construction.

The \markbox{11026}{proof} \markbox{11027}{is} \markbox{11028}{similar} \markbox{11029}{in} \markbox{11030}{spirit} \markbox{11031}{to} \markbox{11032}{the} \markbox{11033}{cluster-honing} \markbox{11034}{procedure} \markbox{11035}{from} \markbox{11036}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:hO defined}.  \markbox{11037}{The} \markbox{11038}{main} \markbox{11039}{difference} \markbox{11040}{is} \markbox{11041}{that} \markbox{11042}{the} \markbox{11043}{collapsing} \markbox{11044}{subintervals} \markbox{11045}{are} \markbox{11046}{not} \markbox{11047}{automatically} \markbox{11048}{associated} \markbox{11049}{to} \markbox{11050}{a} \markbox{11051}{collection} \markbox{11052}{of} \markbox{11053}{domains,} \markbox{11054}{and} \markbox{11055}{this} \markbox{11056}{is} \markbox{11057}{where} \markbox{11058}{the} \markbox{11059}{work} \markbox{11060}{lies.}  \markbox{11061}{The} \markbox{11062}{argument} \markbox{11063}{is} \markbox{11064}{inductive} \markbox{11065}{on} \markbox{11066}{level} \markbox{11067}{in} \markbox{11068}{the} \markbox{m11069}{$\nest$}-lattice \markbox{11070}{and} \markbox{11071}{requires} \markbox{11072}{a} \markbox{11073}{careful} \markbox{11074}{analysis} \markbox{11075}{of} \markbox{11076}{the} \markbox{11077}{construction} \markbox{11078}{and} \markbox{11079}{number} \markbox{11080}{of} \markbox{11081}{hierarchal} techniques.

Finally, \markbox{11082}{for} \markbox{11083}{item} \markbox{11084}{(3),} \markbox{11085}{since} \markbox{m11086}{$\Delta|_{\calQ}$} \markbox{11087}{is} \markbox{11088}{surjective} \markbox{11089}{and} \markbox{11090}{distance} \markbox{11091}{non-increasing,} \markbox{11092}{it} \markbox{11093}{suffices} \markbox{11094}{to} \markbox{11095}{prove} \markbox{11096}{that} \markbox{m11097}{$d_{\calQ} \prec d_{\calQ'}$}, \markbox{11098}{and} \markbox{11099}{for} \markbox{11100}{this} \markbox{11101}{it} \markbox{11102}{suffices} \markbox{11103}{to} \markbox{11104}{bound} \markbox{11105}{the} \markbox{11106}{distances} \markbox{11107}{in} \markbox{11108}{each} \markbox{m11109}{$U \in \calU$}.

Given \markbox{m11110}{$\hx, \hy \in \calQ$} \markbox{11111}{with} \markbox{m11112}{$\hx' = \Delta(\hx)$} \markbox{11113}{and} \markbox{m11114}{$\hy' = \Delta(\hy)$}, \markbox{11115}{the} \markbox{11116}{concern} \markbox{11117}{is} \markbox{11118}{that} \markbox{11119}{somehow} \markbox{11120}{one} \markbox{11121}{will} \markbox{11122}{have} \markbox{11123}{arbitrarily} \markbox{11124}{shrunk} \markbox{11125}{distances} \markbox{11126}{during} \markbox{11127}{the} \markbox{11128}{trimming} \markbox{11129}{process.}  \markbox{11130}{However,} \markbox{11131}{each} \markbox{11132}{edge} \markbox{11133}{component} \markbox{11134}{of} \markbox{m11135}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{11136}{through} \markbox{11137}{which} \markbox{11138}{the} \markbox{11139}{geodesic} \markbox{m11140}{$[\hx_U,\hy_U]$} \markbox{11141}{passes} \markbox{11142}{can} \markbox{11143}{only} \markbox{11144}{contain} \markbox{11145}{boundedly-many} \markbox{11146}{subintervals} \markbox{11147}{collapsed.}  \markbox{11148}{However,} \markbox{11149}{all} \markbox{11150}{but} \markbox{11151}{at} \markbox{11152}{most} \markbox{11153}{two} \markbox{11154}{of} \markbox{11155}{such} \markbox{11156}{edge} \markbox{11157}{components} \markbox{11158}{have} \markbox{11159}{endpoints} \markbox{11160}{which} \markbox{11161}{are} \markbox{11162}{cluster} \markbox{11163}{points} \markbox{11164}{labeled} \markbox{11165}{by} \markbox{m11166}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{11167}{for} \markbox{m11168}{$V$} \markbox{m11169}{$\nest$}-minimal.  \markbox{11170}{Since} \markbox{11171}{for} \markbox{11172}{such} \markbox{m11173}{$V$}, \markbox{11174}{the} \markbox{11175}{map} \markbox{m11176}{$\Delta_V:\hT_V \to \hT'_V$} \markbox{11177}{collapses} \markbox{11178}{subintervals} \markbox{11179}{of} \markbox{11180}{total} \markbox{11181}{diameter} \markbox{11182}{at} \markbox{11183}{most} \markbox{m11184}{$B^2$}, \markbox{11185}{we} \markbox{11186}{can} \markbox{11187}{use} \markbox{11188}{these} \markbox{m11189}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{11190}{domains} \markbox{11191}{to} \markbox{11192}{account} \markbox{11193}{for} \markbox{11194}{all} \markbox{11195}{information} \markbox{11196}{lost} \markbox{11197}{up} \markbox{11198}{the} hierarchy.

Making \markbox{11199}{this} \markbox{11200}{precise} \markbox{11201}{takes} \markbox{11202}{care} \markbox{11203}{and} \markbox{11204}{utilizes} \markbox{11205}{Proposition} \ref{prop:bounding containers}.  \markbox{11206}{The} \markbox{11207}{interested} \markbox{11208}{reader} \markbox{11209}{can} \markbox{11210}{see} \cite[Section 10]{Dur_infcube}. 
\end{proof}

\subsection{Converting to simplicial intervals}

One \markbox{11211}{application} \markbox{11212}{of} \markbox{11213}{the} \markbox{11214}{Tree} \markbox{11215}{Trimming} \markbox{11216}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming} \markbox{11217}{is} \markbox{11218}{that} \markbox{11219}{we} \markbox{11220}{can} \markbox{11221}{replace} \markbox{11222}{the} \markbox{11223}{family} \markbox{11224}{of} \markbox{11225}{collapsed} \markbox{11226}{intervals} \markbox{m11227}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{11228}{with} \markbox{11229}{a} \markbox{11230}{family} \markbox{11231}{of} \markbox{11232}{simplicial} \markbox{11233}{intervals,} \markbox{11234}{where} \markbox{11235}{the} \markbox{11236}{cluster} \markbox{11237}{and} \markbox{11238}{marked} \markbox{11239}{points} \markbox{11240}{lie} \markbox{11241}{at} \markbox{11242}{vertices.}  \markbox{11243}{The} \markbox{11244}{idea} \markbox{11245}{here} \markbox{11246}{is} \markbox{11247}{that} \markbox{11248}{one} \markbox{11249}{can} \markbox{11250}{trim} \markbox{11251}{each} \markbox{11252}{edge} \markbox{11253}{component} \markbox{m11254}{$E \subset \hT^e_U$} \markbox{11255}{to} \markbox{11256}{have} \markbox{11257}{a} \markbox{11258}{nonnegative} \markbox{11259}{integer} \markbox{11260}{length} \markbox{11261}{simply} \markbox{11262}{by} \markbox{11263}{collapsing} \markbox{11264}{some} \markbox{11265}{small} \markbox{11266}{segment} \markbox{11267}{of} \markbox{m11268}{$E$} \markbox{11269}{of} \markbox{11270}{length} \markbox{11271}{less} \markbox{11272}{than} \markbox{m11273}{$1$}.  \markbox{11274}{The} \markbox{11275}{family} \markbox{11276}{of} \markbox{11277}{such} \markbox{11278}{segments} \markbox{11279}{is} \markbox{11280}{an} \markbox{m11281}{$1$}-admissible \markbox{11282}{trimming} \markbox{11283}{setup,} \markbox{11284}{and} \markbox{11285}{this} \markbox{11286}{provides} \markbox{11287}{us} \markbox{11288}{a} \markbox{11289}{family} \markbox{11290}{of} \markbox{11291}{intervals} \markbox{m11292}{$\{\hT'_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{11293}{where} \markbox{m11294}{$\Delta_U:\hT_U\to \hT'_U$} \markbox{11295}{collapses} \markbox{11296}{these} \markbox{11297}{small} \markbox{11298}{segments,} \markbox{11299}{and} \markbox{m11300}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{11301}{combines} \markbox{11302}{these} \markbox{11303}{to} \markbox{11304}{a} \markbox{11305}{map} \markbox{11306}{between} \markbox{11307}{their} \markbox{m11308}{$0$}-consistent sets.

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:simplicial version}
Suppose \markbox{11309}{that} \markbox{m11310}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{11311}{are} \markbox{11312}{the} \markbox{11313}{collapsed} \markbox{11314}{intervals} \markbox{11315}{associated} \markbox{11316}{to} \markbox{11317}{an} \markbox{m11318}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{11319}{of} \markbox{11320}{an} \markbox{m11321}{$R$}-interval \markbox{11322}{system} \markbox{11323}{for} \markbox{m11324}{$a,b \in \calX$}.  \markbox{11325}{There} \markbox{11326}{exists} \markbox{m11327}{$L_{simp} = L_{simp}(R, \calX)>0$} \markbox{11328}{so} \markbox{11329}{that} \markbox{m11330}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{11331}{is} \markbox{11332}{an} \markbox{m11333}{$(L_{simp},L_{simp})$}-quasi-isometry.

\begin{itemize}
\item {} In \markbox{11334}{particular,} \markbox{11335}{up} \markbox{11336}{to} \markbox{11337}{a} \markbox{11338}{uniform} \markbox{11339}{quasi-isometry} \markbox{11340}{of} \markbox{m11341}{$\calQ$}, \markbox{11342}{we} \markbox{11343}{can} \markbox{11344}{assume} \markbox{11345}{that} \markbox{11346}{the} \markbox{11347}{collapsed} \markbox{11348}{intervals} \markbox{m11349}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{11350}{are} \markbox{11351}{all} \markbox{11352}{simplicial} \markbox{11353}{intervals} \markbox{11354}{with} \markbox{11355}{cluster} \markbox{11356}{and} \markbox{11357}{marked} \markbox{11358}{points} \markbox{11359}{at} \markbox{11360}{vertices.} 
\end{itemize}
\end{corollary}

See \cite[Subsection 10.1]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{11361}{for} \markbox{11362}{more} \markbox{11363}{discussion.}  \markbox{11364}{We} \markbox{11365}{note} \markbox{11366}{that} \markbox{11367}{the} \markbox{11368}{above} \markbox{11369}{corollary} \markbox{11370}{will} \markbox{11371}{not} \markbox{11372}{be} \markbox{11373}{used} \markbox{11374}{in} \markbox{11375}{the} \markbox{11376}{proof} \markbox{11377}{of} \markbox{11378}{the} \markbox{11379}{Main} \markbox{11380}{Theorem} \ref{thmi:main}, \markbox{11381}{because} \markbox{11382}{we} \markbox{11383}{will} \markbox{11384}{carefully} \markbox{11385}{construct} \markbox{11386}{stable} \markbox{11387}{intervals} \markbox{11388}{to} \markbox{11389}{be} \markbox{11390}{simplicial.}  \markbox{11391}{However,} \markbox{11392}{it} \markbox{11393}{is} \markbox{11394}{necessary} \markbox{11395}{for} \markbox{11396}{taking} \markbox{11397}{general} \markbox{11398}{intervals} \markbox{11399}{in} \markbox{11400}{each} \markbox{11401}{hyperbolic} \markbox{11402}{spaces} \markbox{11403}{and} \markbox{11404}{performing} \markbox{11405}{the} \markbox{11406}{above} \markbox{11407}{constructions} \markbox{11408}{to} \markbox{11409}{form} \markbox{11410}{a} \markbox{11411}{hierarchical} \markbox{11412}{family} \markbox{11413}{of} \markbox{11414}{intervals} \markbox{11415}{(see} \markbox{11416}{Definition} \ref{defn:HFI}, \markbox{11417}{which} \markbox{11418}{is} \markbox{11419}{necessary} \markbox{11420}{for} \markbox{11421}{our} \markbox{11422}{proof} \markbox{11423}{of} \markbox{11424}{the} \markbox{11425}{distance} \markbox{11426}{formula} \markbox{11427}{below} \markbox{11428}{(Corollary} \ref{cor:DF lower bound}).


\subsection{From $\Omega:\calQ \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$ to $\hO:\calQ \to H$} \label{subsec:upgrade to HHS}

We \markbox{11429}{return} \markbox{11430}{to} \markbox{11431}{our} \markbox{11432}{main} \markbox{11433}{task,} \markbox{11434}{namely} \markbox{11435}{defining} \markbox{11436}{a} \markbox{11437}{quasi-isometry} \markbox{m11438}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$}.  \markbox{11439}{So} \markbox{11440}{far,} \markbox{11441}{we} \markbox{11442}{have} \markbox{11443}{defined} \markbox{11444}{a} \markbox{11445}{map} \markbox{m11446}{$\Omega:\calQ \to \prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$}, \markbox{11447}{which} \markbox{11448}{was} \markbox{11449}{the} \markbox{11450}{bulk} \markbox{11451}{of} \markbox{11452}{the} \markbox{11453}{work.}  \markbox{11454}{Our} \markbox{11455}{next} \markbox{11456}{step} \markbox{11457}{is} \markbox{11458}{to} \markbox{11459}{upgrade} \markbox{11460}{this} \markbox{11461}{to} \markbox{11462}{a} \markbox{11463}{map} \markbox{m11464}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$}.  \markbox{11465}{Since} \markbox{11466}{this} \markbox{11467}{part} \markbox{11468}{of} \markbox{11469}{the} \markbox{11470}{argument} \markbox{11471}{mostly} \markbox{11472}{uses} \markbox{11473}{standard} \markbox{11474}{HHS} \markbox{11475}{techniques,} \markbox{11476}{we} \markbox{11477}{will} \markbox{11478}{just} \markbox{11479}{outline} \markbox{11480}{it,} \markbox{11481}{with} \markbox{11482}{appropriate} \markbox{11483}{citations} \markbox{11484}{to} \cite{Dur_infcube}.

For \markbox{11485}{each} \markbox{m11486}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{11487}{we} \markbox{11488}{first} \markbox{11489}{take} \markbox{11490}{our} \markbox{11491}{tuple} \markbox{m11492}{$\Omega(\hx) = (x_U) \subset \prod_{\calU} T_U$} \markbox{11493}{and} \markbox{11494}{push} \markbox{11495}{it} \markbox{11496}{forward} \markbox{11497}{to} \markbox{11498}{a} \markbox{11499}{tuple} \markbox{m11500}{$(y_U) \in \prod_{\calU} \calC(U)$} \markbox{11501}{by} \markbox{m11502}{$\phi_U(x_U) = y_U$}, \markbox{11503}{where} \markbox{m11504}{$\phi_U:T_U \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{11505}{are} \markbox{11506}{the} \markbox{11507}{maps} \markbox{11508}{provided} \markbox{11509}{by} \markbox{11510}{the} \markbox{m11511}{$R$}-interval \markbox{11512}{system} \markbox{11513}{structure} \markbox{11514}{(Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms}).  \markbox{11515}{These} \markbox{11516}{combine} \markbox{11517}{to} \markbox{11518}{define} \markbox{11519}{a} \markbox{11520}{map} \markbox{m11521}{$\Phi:\prod_{U \in \calU} T_U \to \prod_{U \in \calU} \calC(U)$}.  \markbox{11522}{By} \markbox{11523}{Proposition} \ref{prop:Q-consistent}, \markbox{11524}{there} \markbox{11525}{is} \markbox{11526}{some} \markbox{m11527}{$\alpha_{\omega} = \alpha_{\omega}(\mathfrak S, R,r_1,r_2)>0$} \markbox{11528}{so} \markbox{11529}{that} \markbox{11530}{the} \markbox{11531}{tuple} \markbox{m11532}{$\Omega(\hx) \in \prod_{U \in \calU}T_U$} \markbox{11533}{is} \markbox{m11534}{$\alpha_{\omega}$}-consistent.  \markbox{11535}{Using} \markbox{11536}{just} \markbox{11537}{the} \markbox{m11538}{$R$}-system \markbox{11539}{axioms} \markbox{11540}{and} \markbox{11541}{standard} \markbox{11542}{HHS} \markbox{11543}{techniques,} \cite[Proposition 6.17]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{11544}{implies} \markbox{11545}{that} \markbox{m11546}{$(y_U) \in \prod_{U \in \calU} \calC(U)$} \markbox{11547}{is} \markbox{11548}{consistent} \markbox{11549}{in} \markbox{11550}{the} \markbox{11551}{sense} \markbox{11552}{of} \markbox{11553}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency} \markbox{11554}{for} \markbox{11555}{some} \markbox{11556}{consistency} \markbox{11557}{constant} \markbox{11558}{depending} \markbox{11559}{only} \markbox{11560}{on} \markbox{m11561}{$\mathfrak S, \alpha_{\omega}$}. 

Since \markbox{m11562}{$d_V(a,b) < K$} \markbox{11563}{for} \markbox{11564}{all} \markbox{m11565}{$V \in \mathfrak S - \calU$}, \markbox{11566}{it} \markbox{11567}{follows} \markbox{11568}{that} \markbox{11569}{by} \markbox{11570}{choosing} \markbox{m11571}{$y_V \in \pi_V(a)$} \markbox{11572}{for} \markbox{11573}{all} \markbox{m11574}{$V \in \mathfrak S - \calU$}, \markbox{11575}{then} \markbox{11576}{the} \markbox{11577}{complete} \markbox{11578}{tuple} \markbox{m11579}{$(y_U) \in \prod_{U \in \mathfrak S} \calC(U)$} \markbox{11580}{is} \markbox{m11581}{$\beta$}-consistent \markbox{11582}{for} \markbox{m11583}{$\beta = \beta(\mathfrak S, R, K)>0$} \markbox{11584}{(as} \markbox{m11585}{$\alpha_{\omega}$} \markbox{11586}{only} \markbox{11587}{depended} \markbox{11588}{on} \markbox{m11589}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{11590}{and} \markbox{m11591}{$R$}).

Now \markbox{11592}{with} \markbox{11593}{a} \markbox{11594}{complete} \markbox{11595}{consistent} \markbox{11596}{tuple} \markbox{11597}{in} \markbox{11598}{hand,} \markbox{11599}{we} \markbox{11600}{can} \markbox{11601}{apply} \markbox{11602}{the} \markbox{11603}{Realization} \markbox{11604}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization} \markbox{11605}{to} \markbox{11606}{define} \markbox{11607}{a} \markbox{11608}{map} \markbox{m11609}{$\mathrm{Real}_{\beta}:\prod_{U \in \mathfrak S} \calC(U) \to \calX$} \markbox{11610}{which} \markbox{11611}{takes} \markbox{11612}{each} \markbox{m11613}{$\beta$}-consistent \markbox{11614}{tuple} \markbox{11615}{and} \markbox{11616}{produces} \markbox{11617}{a} \markbox{11618}{point} \markbox{m11619}{$x \in \calX$} \markbox{11620}{whose} \markbox{11621}{projections} \markbox{11622}{coarsely} \markbox{11623}{coincide} \markbox{11624}{with} \markbox{11625}{the} \markbox{11626}{tuple,} \markbox{11627}{with} \markbox{11628}{error} \markbox{11629}{depending} \markbox{11630}{on} \markbox{m11631}{$\beta, \mathfrak S$}.

Finally, \cite[Lemma 6.6]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{11632}{which} \markbox{11633}{depends} \markbox{11634}{on} \markbox{11635}{the} \markbox{11636}{more} \markbox{11637}{general} \markbox{11638}{fact} \cite[Proposition 6.3]{HHS_II}, \markbox{11639}{provides} \markbox{11640}{a} \markbox{m11641}{$(J,J)$}-coarse \markbox{11642}{retraction} \markbox{11643}{map} \markbox{m11644}{$\mathrm{ret}_H:\calX \to H$}, \markbox{11645}{where} \markbox{m11646}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{11647}{where} \markbox{m11648}{$J = J(\mathfrak S)>0$}.  \markbox{11649}{This} \markbox{11650}{map} \markbox{11651}{is} \markbox{11652}{just} \markbox{11653}{closest-point} \markbox{11654}{projection} \markbox{11655}{to} \markbox{m11656}{$\hull_U(a,b)$} \markbox{11657}{in} \markbox{11658}{each} \markbox{m11659}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{11660}{plus} \markbox{11661}{Theorem} \ref{thm:realization}. 

Combining \markbox{11662}{these,} \markbox{11663}{we} \markbox{11664}{get} \markbox{11665}{a} \markbox{11666}{map} \markbox{m11667}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$} \markbox{11668}{given} \markbox{11669}{by} \markbox{m11670}{$\hO = \mathrm{ret}_H \circ \mathrm{Real}_{\beta} \circ \Phi \circ \Omega$}.  \markbox{11671}{Our} \markbox{11672}{main} \markbox{11673}{goal} \markbox{11674}{is} \markbox{11675}{to} \markbox{11676}{show} \markbox{11677}{that} \markbox{m11678}{$\hPsi \circ \hO:\calQ \to \calQ$} \markbox{11679}{is} \markbox{11680}{coarsely} \markbox{11681}{the} \markbox{11682}{identity,} \markbox{11683}{where} \markbox{m11684}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{11685}{is} \markbox{11686}{the} \markbox{11687}{map} \markbox{11688}{defined} \markbox{11689}{in} \markbox{11690}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}.

Before \markbox{11691}{analyzing} \markbox{11692}{this} \markbox{11693}{total} \markbox{11694}{composition,} \markbox{11695}{we} \markbox{11696}{want} \markbox{11697}{to} \markbox{11698}{look} \markbox{11699}{at} \markbox{11700}{an} \markbox{11701}{intermediate} \markbox{11702}{step.}  \markbox{11703}{For} \markbox{11704}{convenience,} \markbox{11705}{if} \markbox{m11706}{$\alpha>0$}, \markbox{11707}{we} \markbox{11708}{let} \markbox{m11709}{$\calZ_{\alpha}$} \markbox{11710}{denote} \markbox{11711}{the} \markbox{11712}{collection} \markbox{11713}{of} \markbox{m11714}{$\alpha$}-consistent \markbox{11715}{tuples} \markbox{11716}{in} \markbox{m11717}{$\prod_{U \in \calU} T_U$}.  Define
$$\Phi_{\alpha}:\calZ_{\alpha} \to H$$ \markbox{11718}{by} \markbox{m11719}{$\mathrm{ret}_H \circ \mathrm{Real}_{\beta} \circ \Phi$}.

The \markbox{11720}{following} \markbox{11721}{proposition} \markbox{11722}{says} \markbox{11723}{that} \markbox{11724}{this} \markbox{11725}{map} \markbox{11726}{behaves} \markbox{11727}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{11728}{as} \markbox{11729}{one} \markbox{11730}{might} \markbox{11731}{expect} \markbox{11732}{upon} \markbox{11733}{composition} \markbox{11734}{with} \markbox{11735}{the} \markbox{11736}{coordinate} \markbox{11737}{maps} \markbox{m11738}{$\psi_U:\calX \to T_U$}, \markbox{11739}{which} \markbox{11740}{we} \markbox{11741}{recall} \markbox{11742}{are} \markbox{11743}{defined} \markbox{11744}{by} \markbox{m11745}{$\psi_U = \phi^{-1}_U\circ p_U \circ \pi_U$}, \markbox{11746}{where} \markbox{m11747}{$p_U:\calC(U) \to \phi_U(T_U)$} \markbox{11748}{is} \markbox{11749}{closest-point} \markbox{11750}{projection.}  

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:interval coordinate control}
There \markbox{11751}{exists} \markbox{m11752}{$D_1 = D_1(K, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{11753}{so} \markbox{11754}{that} \markbox{11755}{if} \markbox{m11756}{$x = (x_V) \in \calZ_{\alpha_{\omega}}$}, \markbox{11757}{then} \markbox{11758}{we} have
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m11759}{$d_{T_U}(x_U, \psi_U \circ \Phi_{\alpha_{\omega}}(x))<D_1$} \markbox{11760}{for} \markbox{11761}{all} \markbox{m11762}{$U \in \calU$}, and
\item {} \markbox{m11763}{$\#\{U \in \calU| d_{T_U}(x_U, \psi_U \circ \Phi_{\alpha_{\omega}}(x)) > 2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R\} < D_1$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item {} In \markbox{11764}{particular,} \markbox{11765}{by} \markbox{11766}{choosing} \markbox{m11767}{$L>2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$}, \markbox{11768}{we} get
$$\sum_{U \in \calU} [d_{T_U}(x_U, \psi_U \circ \Phi_{\alpha_{\omega}}(x)]_L < D_1^2.$$
\end{itemize}
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}[Sketch]
This \markbox{11769}{proposition} \markbox{11770}{is} \markbox{11771}{a} \markbox{11772}{special} \markbox{11773}{case} \markbox{11774}{of} \cite[Proposition 11.4]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{11775}{and} \markbox{11776}{the} \markbox{11777}{proof} \markbox{11778}{is} \markbox{11779}{almost} \markbox{11780}{entirely} \markbox{11781}{the} \markbox{11782}{same.}  \markbox{11783}{The} \markbox{11784}{proof} \markbox{11785}{of} \markbox{11786}{item} \markbox{11787}{(1)} \markbox{11788}{is} \markbox{11789}{a} \markbox{11790}{definition} \markbox{11791}{chase.}  \markbox{11792}{It} \markbox{11793}{is} \markbox{11794}{basically} \markbox{11795}{saying} \markbox{11796}{that} \markbox{11797}{consistency} \markbox{11798}{in} \markbox{11799}{the} \markbox{11800}{interval} \markbox{11801}{setting} \markbox{11802}{is} \markbox{11803}{roughly} \markbox{11804}{consistency} \markbox{11805}{in} \markbox{11806}{the} \markbox{11807}{hierarchical} \markbox{11808}{setting,} \markbox{11809}{and} \markbox{11810}{that} \markbox{11811}{flowing} \markbox{11812}{from} \markbox{11813}{the} \markbox{11814}{former} \markbox{11815}{to} \markbox{11816}{the} \markbox{11817}{latter} \markbox{11818}{and} \markbox{11819}{back} \markbox{11820}{only} \markbox{11821}{moves} \markbox{11822}{coordinates} \markbox{11823}{a} \markbox{11824}{bounded} amount.

On \markbox{11825}{the} \markbox{11826}{other} \markbox{11827}{hand,} \markbox{11828}{the} \markbox{11829}{proof} \markbox{11830}{of} \markbox{11831}{(2)---which} \markbox{11832}{says} \markbox{11833}{that} \markbox{11834}{only} \markbox{11835}{boundedly-many} \markbox{11836}{coordinates} \markbox{11837}{move} \markbox{11838}{more} \markbox{11839}{than} \markbox{11840}{a} \markbox{11841}{bounded} \markbox{11842}{amount---is} \markbox{11843}{more} \markbox{11844}{involved,} \markbox{11845}{but} \markbox{11846}{also} \markbox{11847}{fairly} \markbox{11848}{standard.}  \markbox{11849}{It} \markbox{11850}{uses} \markbox{11851}{a} \markbox{11852}{variation} \markbox{11853}{on} \markbox{11854}{the} \markbox{11855}{Passing-Up} \markbox{11856}{property} \markbox{11857}{from} \markbox{11858}{Lemma} \ref{lem:passing-up}, \markbox{11859}{and} \markbox{11860}{the} \markbox{11861}{BGI} \markbox{11862}{property} \markbox{11863}{from} \markbox{11864}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms}.  \markbox{11865}{Set} \markbox{m11866}{$\psi_U \circ \Phi_{\alpha_{\omega}}(x) = y = (y_U)$}.  \markbox{11867}{The} \markbox{11868}{idea} \markbox{11869}{here} \markbox{11870}{is} \markbox{11871}{that} \markbox{11872}{if} \markbox{11873}{there} \markbox{11874}{are} \markbox{11875}{too} \markbox{11876}{many} \markbox{11877}{coordinates} \markbox{11878}{where} \markbox{m11879}{$d_{T_U}(x_U, y_U) > 2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$}, \markbox{11880}{then} \markbox{11881}{we} \markbox{11882}{can} \markbox{11883}{force} \markbox{11884}{the} \markbox{11885}{existence} \markbox{11886}{of} \markbox{11887}{some} \markbox{11888}{coordinate} \markbox{m11889}{$T_W$} \markbox{11890}{where} \markbox{m11891}{$d_{T_W}(x_W,y_W)>D_1$}, \markbox{11892}{which} \markbox{11893}{is} \markbox{11894}{impossible} \markbox{11895}{by} (1).
\end{proof}

\subsection{The map $\hO:\calQ \to H$ and coarse surjectivity of $\hPsi$}

We \markbox{11896}{are} \markbox{11897}{ready} \markbox{11898}{to} \markbox{11899}{analyze} \markbox{11900}{the} \markbox{11901}{map} \markbox{m11902}{$\hO = \Phi_{\alpha_{\omega}} \circ \Omega:\calQ \to H$}.    \markbox{11903}{Since} \markbox{m11904}{$\hPsi(H) \subset \calQ$} \markbox{11905}{by} \markbox{11906}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined}, \markbox{11907}{we} \markbox{11908}{see} \markbox{11909}{that} \markbox{m11910}{$\hPsi \circ \hO:\calQ \to \calQ$}.  \markbox{11911}{We} \markbox{11912}{prove} \markbox{11913}{that} \markbox{11914}{this} \markbox{11915}{map} \markbox{11916}{is} \markbox{11917}{coarsely} \markbox{11918}{the} identity:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:coarse surjectivity}
There \markbox{11919}{exists} \markbox{m11920}{$M_0 = M_0(R, \mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{11921}{so} \markbox{11922}{that} \markbox{11923}{for} \markbox{11924}{any} \markbox{m11925}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{11926}{we} \markbox{11927}{have} \markbox{m11928}{$d_{\calQ}(\hx, \hPsi \circ \hO(\hx)) < M_0$}. 
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}[Sketch]
This \markbox{11929}{proposition} \markbox{11930}{is} \markbox{11931}{a} \markbox{11932}{special} \markbox{11933}{case} \markbox{11934}{of} \markbox{11935}{the} \markbox{11936}{proof} \markbox{11937}{contained} \markbox{11938}{in} \cite[Subsection 11.2]{Dur_infcube}.  \markbox{11939}{Since} \markbox{11940}{the} \markbox{11941}{details} \markbox{11942}{of} \markbox{11943}{the} \markbox{11944}{proof} \markbox{11945}{are} \markbox{11946}{very} \markbox{11947}{similar} \markbox{11948}{to} \markbox{11949}{the} \markbox{11950}{original,} \markbox{11951}{we} \markbox{11952}{will} \markbox{11953}{again} \markbox{11954}{only} \markbox{11955}{provide} \markbox{11956}{a} sketch.

Fix \markbox{m11957}{$\hx \in \calQ$} \markbox{11958}{and} \markbox{11959}{let} \markbox{m11960}{$\hy \in \hPsi \circ \hO(\hx)$}. \markbox{11961}{We} \markbox{11962}{will} \markbox{11963}{argue} \markbox{11964}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{11965}{since} \markbox{11966}{that} \markbox{11967}{is} \markbox{11968}{how} \markbox{11969}{the} \markbox{m11970}{$\ell^1$} \markbox{11971}{distance} \markbox{11972}{on} \markbox{m11973}{$\calQ$} \markbox{11974}{is} \markbox{11975}{defined.}  \markbox{11976}{The} \markbox{11977}{difference} \markbox{11978}{from} \markbox{11979}{the} \markbox{11980}{usual} \markbox{11981}{HHS} \markbox{11982}{style} \markbox{11983}{argument} \markbox{11984}{here} \markbox{11985}{is} \markbox{11986}{that} \markbox{m11987}{$d_{\calQ}$} \markbox{11988}{is} \markbox{11989}{an} \markbox{m11990}{$\ell^1$} \markbox{11991}{sum} \markbox{11992}{not} \markbox{11993}{involving} \markbox{11994}{a} \markbox{11995}{threshold.}  \markbox{11996}{To} \markbox{11997}{get} \markbox{11998}{around} \markbox{11999}{that} \markbox{12000}{issue,} \markbox{12001}{we} \markbox{12002}{will} \markbox{12003}{make} \markbox{12004}{an} \markbox{12005}{argument} \markbox{12006}{using} \markbox{12007}{Proposition} \ref{prop:interval coordinate control} \markbox{12008}{and} \markbox{12009}{Tree} \markbox{12010}{Trimming} \ref{thm:tree trimming} \markbox{12011}{as} \markbox{12012}{follows.}  \markbox{12013}{We} \markbox{12014}{show} \markbox{12015}{that} \markbox{12016}{all} \markbox{12017}{coordinate} \markbox{12018}{distances} \markbox{m12019}{$d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U, \hy_U)$} \markbox{12020}{are} \markbox{12021}{bounded} \markbox{12022}{in} \markbox{12023}{terms} \markbox{12024}{of} \markbox{m12025}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{12026}{and} \markbox{m12027}{$K$}, \markbox{12028}{with} \markbox{12029}{all} \markbox{12030}{but} \markbox{12031}{boundedly-many} \markbox{12032}{(in} \markbox{12033}{terms} \markbox{12034}{of} \markbox{m12035}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{12036}{being} \markbox{12037}{bounded} \markbox{12038}{in} \markbox{12039}{terms} \markbox{12040}{of} \markbox{m12041}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{12042}{We} \markbox{12043}{can} \markbox{12044}{then} \markbox{12045}{collapse} \markbox{12046}{the} \markbox{12047}{subintervals} \markbox{12048}{between} \markbox{m12049}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{12050}{and} \markbox{m12051}{$\hy_U$} \markbox{12052}{in} \markbox{12053}{the} \markbox{12054}{latter} \markbox{12055}{domains} \markbox{12056}{while} \markbox{12057}{only} \markbox{12058}{incurring} \markbox{12059}{a} \markbox{12060}{bounded} \markbox{12061}{error} \markbox{12062}{globally,} \markbox{12063}{resulting} \markbox{12064}{in} \markbox{12065}{images} \markbox{12066}{for} \markbox{m12067}{$\hx,\hy$} \markbox{12068}{which} \markbox{12069}{are} \markbox{12070}{bounded} \markbox{12071}{distance} \markbox{12072}{in} \markbox{12073}{the} \markbox{12074}{quotient,} \markbox{12075}{showing} \markbox{12076}{that} \markbox{m12077}{$\hx,\hy$} \markbox{12078}{were} \markbox{12079}{bounded} \markbox{12080}{distance} \markbox{12081}{in} \markbox{m12082}{$\calQ$}.

Let \markbox{m12083}{$\Omega(\hx) = (x_U)$} \markbox{12084}{and} \markbox{m12085}{$\Psi \circ \hO(\hx) = (y_U)$}, \markbox{12086}{and} \markbox{12087}{observe} \markbox{12088}{that} \markbox{12089}{since} \markbox{m12090}{$q\circ \Omega(\hx) = \hx$}, \markbox{12091}{the} \markbox{12092}{tuples} \markbox{m12093}{$(x_U), (y_U)$} \markbox{12094}{are} \markbox{12095}{exactly} \markbox{12096}{the} \markbox{12097}{type} \markbox{12098}{in} \markbox{12099}{the} \markbox{12100}{statement} \markbox{12101}{of} \markbox{12102}{Proposition} \ref{prop:interval coordinate control}.  \markbox{12103}{Moreover,} \markbox{12104}{since} \markbox{m12105}{$q \circ \Omega(\hy) = \hy$} \markbox{12106}{by} \markbox{12107}{construction,} \markbox{12108}{while} \markbox{m12109}{$q$} \markbox{12110}{is} \markbox{m12111}{$1$}-Lipschitz \markbox{12112}{by} \markbox{12113}{item} \markbox{12114}{(4)} \markbox{12115}{of} \markbox{12116}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}, \markbox{12117}{it} \markbox{12118}{will} \markbox{12119}{suffice} \markbox{12120}{to} \markbox{12121}{control} \markbox{12122}{the} \markbox{12123}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{12124}{distances} \markbox{12125}{of} \markbox{12126}{the} \markbox{m12127}{$d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)$} \markbox{12128}{in} \markbox{12129}{order} \markbox{12130}{to} \markbox{12131}{utilize} \markbox{12132}{the} \markbox{12133}{above} argument.

Let \markbox{m12134}{$\calV = \{U \in \calU| \hx_U \neq \hy_U\}$}.  \markbox{12135}{One} \markbox{12136}{proceeds} \markbox{12137}{inductively} \markbox{12138}{on} \markbox{12139}{the} \markbox{m12140}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-level.  \markbox{12141}{Let} \markbox{m12142}{$\calV_{min} \subset \calV$} \markbox{12143}{denote} \markbox{12144}{the} \markbox{m12145}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{12146}{domains} \markbox{12147}{in} \markbox{m12148}{$\calV$}.

By \markbox{12149}{item} \markbox{12150}{(8)} \markbox{12151}{of} \markbox{12152}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}, \markbox{12153}{for} \markbox{12154}{all} \markbox{12155}{but} \markbox{m12156}{$A$}-many \markbox{m12157}{$U \in \calV_{min}$} \markbox{12158}{with} \markbox{m12159}{$A = A(\mathfrak S)>0$}, \markbox{12160}{we} \markbox{12161}{have} \markbox{m12162}{$\hx_U,\hy_U \in \{\ha_U,\hb_U\}$}, \markbox{12163}{and} \markbox{12164}{hence} \markbox{12165}{for} \markbox{12166}{all} \markbox{12167}{but} \markbox{12168}{at} \markbox{12169}{most} \markbox{m12170}{$A$} \markbox{12171}{domains} \markbox{12172}{in} \markbox{m12173}{$\calV_{min}$}, \markbox{12174}{we} \markbox{12175}{have} \markbox{12176}{that} \markbox{m12177}{$\hx_U,\hy_U$} \markbox{12178}{are} \markbox{12179}{the} \markbox{12180}{(opposite)} \markbox{12181}{endpoints} \markbox{12182}{of} \markbox{m12183}{$\hT_U$}.  \markbox{12184}{By} \markbox{12185}{item} \markbox{12186}{(6)} \markbox{12187}{of} \markbox{12188}{that} \markbox{12189}{lemma,} \markbox{m12190}{$d_{T_U}(a_U,b_U) > d_{\hT_U}(\ha_U,\hb_U) \succ K$}, \markbox{12191}{while} \markbox{m12192}{$K$} \markbox{12193}{can} \markbox{12194}{be} \markbox{12195}{taken} \markbox{12196}{to} \markbox{12197}{be} \markbox{12198}{as} \markbox{12199}{much} \markbox{12200}{larger} \markbox{12201}{than} \markbox{m12202}{$2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$} \markbox{12203}{as} \markbox{12204}{we} \markbox{12205}{need,} \markbox{12206}{as} \markbox{m12207}{$\alpha_{\omega}$} \markbox{12208}{and} \markbox{m12209}{$R$} \markbox{12210}{depend} \markbox{12211}{only} \markbox{12212}{on} \markbox{m12213}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{12214}{Since} \markbox{12215}{Proposition} \ref{prop:interval coordinate control} \markbox{12216}{bounds} \markbox{12217}{the} \markbox{12218}{number} \markbox{12219}{of} \markbox{12220}{domains} \markbox{m12221}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{12222}{where} \markbox{m12223}{$d_{T_U}(x_U,y_U)> 2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$}, \markbox{12224}{we} \markbox{12225}{can} \markbox{12226}{conclude} \markbox{12227}{that} \markbox{m12228}{$\#\calV_{min} < D_1 + A$}.

Now \markbox{12229}{let} \markbox{m12230}{$\calV' \subset \calV - \calV_{min}$} \markbox{12231}{denote} \markbox{12232}{the} \markbox{12233}{set} \markbox{12234}{of} \markbox{12235}{non-minimal} \markbox{12236}{domains} \markbox{m12237}{$V$} \markbox{12238}{where} \markbox{m12239}{$\hx_V \neq \hy_V$} \markbox{12240}{and} \markbox{m12241}{$d_{T_V}(x_V,y_V) < 2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$}, \markbox{12242}{which} \markbox{12243}{we} \markbox{12244}{note} \markbox{12245}{only} \markbox{12246}{excludes} \markbox{12247}{boundedly-many} \markbox{12248}{domains} \markbox{12249}{by} \markbox{12250}{item} \markbox{12251}{(2)} \markbox{12252}{of} \markbox{12253}{Proposition} \ref{prop:interval coordinate control}.

Since \markbox{12254}{the} \markbox{12255}{maps} \markbox{m12256}{$q_V:T_V \to \hT_V$} \markbox{12257}{are} \markbox{m12258}{$1$}-Lipschitz \markbox{12259}{(item} \markbox{12260}{(4)} \markbox{12261}{of} \markbox{12262}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}), \markbox{12263}{we} \markbox{12264}{have} \markbox{m12265}{$d_{\hT_V}(\hx_V,\hy_V) < 2\alpha_{\omega} + 3R$}.  \markbox{12266}{The} \markbox{12267}{idea} \markbox{12268}{now} \markbox{12269}{is} \markbox{12270}{to} \markbox{12271}{use} \markbox{12272}{the} \markbox{12273}{Tree} \markbox{12274}{Trimming} \markbox{12275}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming} \markbox{12276}{to} \markbox{12277}{collapse} \markbox{12278}{the} \markbox{12279}{geodesics} \markbox{m12280}{$[\hx_V,\hy_V]$} \markbox{12281}{between} \markbox{m12282}{$\hx_V,\hy_V$} \markbox{12283}{in} \markbox{m12284}{$\hT_V$} \markbox{12285}{to} \markbox{12286}{points.}  \markbox{12287}{Each} \markbox{12288}{interval} \markbox{m12289}{$\hT_V$} \markbox{12290}{contains} \markbox{12291}{at} \markbox{12292}{most} \markbox{12293}{one} \markbox{12294}{such} \markbox{12295}{geodesic,} \markbox{12296}{and} \markbox{12297}{each} \markbox{12298}{such} \markbox{12299}{geodesic} \markbox{12300}{has} \markbox{12301}{a} \markbox{12302}{length} \markbox{12303}{bounded} \markbox{12304}{independently} \markbox{12305}{of} \markbox{m12306}{$K$}.  \markbox{12307}{Hence} \markbox{12308}{the} \markbox{12309}{set} \markbox{12310}{of} \markbox{12311}{such} \markbox{12312}{intervals} \markbox{12313}{across} \markbox{12314}{both} \markbox{m12315}{$\nest$}-minimal \markbox{12316}{and} \markbox{12317}{non-minimal} \markbox{12318}{domains} \markbox{12319}{with} \markbox{12320}{this} \markbox{12321}{distance} \markbox{12322}{bound} \markbox{12323}{is} \markbox{12324}{an} \markbox{12325}{admissible} \markbox{12326}{trimming} \markbox{12327}{set} \markbox{12328}{in} \markbox{12329}{the} \markbox{12330}{sense} \markbox{12331}{required} \markbox{12332}{for} \markbox{12333}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}.

If \markbox{12334}{we} \markbox{12335}{take} \markbox{m12336}{$\hT'_V$} \markbox{12337}{to} \markbox{12338}{be} \markbox{12339}{the} \markbox{12340}{interval} \markbox{12341}{obtained} \markbox{12342}{from} \markbox{m12343}{$\hT_V$} \markbox{12344}{post-trimming} \markbox{12345}{and} \markbox{m12346}{$\calQ'$} \markbox{12347}{the} \markbox{12348}{corresponding} \markbox{m12349}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{12350}{set,} \markbox{12351}{then} \markbox{12352}{the} \markbox{12353}{images} \markbox{m12354}{$\hx', \hy'$} \markbox{12355}{of} \markbox{m12356}{$\hx,\hy$} \markbox{12357}{now} \markbox{12358}{satisfy} \markbox{m12359}{$\hx'_V = \hy'_V$} \markbox{12360}{for} \markbox{12361}{all} \markbox{12362}{but} \markbox{12363}{boundedly-many} \markbox{m12364}{$V$}, \markbox{12365}{and} \markbox{12366}{the} \markbox{12367}{remaining} \markbox{12368}{distances} \markbox{12369}{are} \markbox{12370}{all} \markbox{12371}{bounded} \markbox{12372}{by} \markbox{12373}{some} \markbox{12374}{function} \markbox{12375}{of} \markbox{m12376}{$D_1$} \markbox{12377}{by} \markbox{12378}{item} \markbox{12379}{(1)} \markbox{12380}{of} \markbox{12381}{Proposition} \ref{prop:interval coordinate control}.  \markbox{12382}{In} \markbox{12383}{particular,} \markbox{m12384}{$d_{\calQ'}(\hx,\hy)$} \markbox{12385}{is} \markbox{12386}{bounded.}  \markbox{12387}{But} \markbox{12388}{the} \markbox{12389}{map} \markbox{m12390}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{12391}{is} \markbox{12392}{a} \markbox{12393}{uniform} \markbox{12394}{quasi-isometry,} \markbox{12395}{so} \markbox{12396}{that} \markbox{12397}{means} \markbox{12398}{that} \markbox{m12399}{$d_{\calQ}(\hx,\hy)$} \markbox{12400}{is} \markbox{12401}{also} \markbox{12402}{bounded,} \markbox{12403}{which} \markbox{12404}{is} \markbox{12405}{what} \markbox{12406}{we} \markbox{12407}{wanted.}  \markbox{12408}{We} \markbox{12409}{leave}
