\markbox{12410}{checking} \markbox{12411}{the} \markbox{12412}{details} \markbox{12413}{to} \markbox{12414}{the} reader.
\end{proof}

\section{Building a cube complex from a hierarchical family of intervals}\label{sec:cubulation}

The \markbox{12415}{goal} \markbox{12416}{of} \markbox{12417}{this} \markbox{12418}{section} \markbox{12419}{is} \markbox{12420}{to} \markbox{12421}{explain} \markbox{12422}{how} \markbox{12423}{to} \markbox{12424}{take} \markbox{12425}{a} \markbox{12426}{special} \markbox{12427}{collection} \markbox{12428}{of} \markbox{12429}{intervals} \markbox{12430}{satisfying} \markbox{12431}{certain} \markbox{12432}{HHS-like} \markbox{12433}{properties,} \markbox{12434}{and} \markbox{12435}{to} \markbox{12436}{produce} \markbox{12437}{from} \markbox{12438}{them} \markbox{12439}{a} \markbox{12440}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12441}{cube} \markbox{12442}{complex.}  \markbox{12443}{The} \markbox{12444}{details} \markbox{12445}{of} \markbox{12446}{this} \markbox{12447}{construction} \markbox{12448}{motivate} \markbox{12449}{the} \markbox{12450}{stabilization} \markbox{12451}{techniques} \markbox{12452}{we} \markbox{12453}{develop} \markbox{12454}{later} \markbox{12455}{in} \markbox{12456}{this} article.


\subsection{Hierarchical families of intervals}

In \markbox{12457}{this} \markbox{12458}{subsection,} \markbox{12459}{we} \markbox{12460}{axiomatize} \markbox{12461}{the} \markbox{12462}{properties} \markbox{12463}{we} \markbox{12464}{need} \markbox{12465}{from} \markbox{12466}{a} \markbox{12467}{family} \markbox{12468}{of} \markbox{12469}{intervals} \markbox{12470}{in} \markbox{12471}{order} \markbox{12472}{to} \markbox{12473}{build} \markbox{12474}{a} \markbox{12475}{cube} \markbox{12476}{complex.}  \markbox{12477}{The} \markbox{12478}{purpose} \markbox{12479}{of} \markbox{12480}{this} \markbox{12481}{axiomatization} \markbox{12482}{is} \markbox{12483}{to} \markbox{12484}{allow} \markbox{12485}{us} \markbox{12486}{to} \markbox{12487}{modify} \markbox{12488}{our} \markbox{12489}{construction} \markbox{12490}{in} \markbox{12491}{various} \markbox{12492}{ways} \markbox{12493}{while} \markbox{12494}{preserving} \markbox{12495}{the} \markbox{12496}{axioms,} \markbox{12497}{as} \markbox{12498}{any} \markbox{12499}{setup} \markbox{12500}{which} \markbox{12501}{satisfies} \markbox{12502}{the} \markbox{12503}{axioms} \markbox{12504}{produces} \markbox{12505}{a} \markbox{12506}{cube} \markbox{12507}{complex.}  \markbox{12508}{The} \markbox{12509}{properties} \markbox{12510}{themselves} \markbox{12511}{are} \markbox{12512}{motivated} \markbox{12513}{by} \markbox{12514}{the} \markbox{12515}{HHS} \markbox{12516}{axioms} \markbox{12517}{and} \markbox{12518}{the} \markbox{12519}{properties} \markbox{12520}{in} \markbox{12521}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.

\begin{definition}[Hierarchical \markbox{12522}{family} \markbox{12523}{of} intervals] \label{defn:HFI}
A \markbox{12524}{\emph{hierarchical family of intervals (HFI)}} \markbox{12525}{is} \markbox{12526}{the} \markbox{12527}{following} \markbox{12528}{collection} \markbox{12529}{of} \markbox{12530}{objects} \markbox{12531}{and} properties:

\begin{enumerate}
\item {} A \markbox{12532}{finite} \markbox{12533}{index} \markbox{12534}{set} \markbox{m12535}{$\calU$} \markbox{12536}{of} \markbox{12537}{\emph{domains}} \markbox{12538}{with} \markbox{12539}{\emph{relations}} \markbox{m12540}{$\nest, \pitchfork, \perp$} \markbox{12541}{so} that
\begin{itemize}
    \item {} \markbox{m12542}{$\nest$} \markbox{12543}{is} \markbox{12544}{anti-reflexive} \markbox{12545}{and} \markbox{12546}{anti-symmetric,} \markbox{12547}{and} \markbox{12548}{gives} \markbox{12549}{a} \markbox{12550}{partial} \markbox{12551}{order} \markbox{12552}{with} \markbox{12553}{a} \markbox{12554}{bound} \markbox{12555}{on} \markbox{12556}{the} \markbox{12557}{length} \markbox{12558}{of} chains;
    \item {} \markbox{m12559}{$\pitchfork$} \markbox{12560}{is} \markbox{12561}{symmetric} \markbox{12562}{and} anti-reflexive;
    \item {} There \markbox{12563}{is} \markbox{12564}{a} \markbox{12565}{unique} \markbox{m12566}{$\nest$}-maximal \markbox{12567}{element} \markbox{m12568}{$S$};
    \item {} Any \markbox{12569}{pair} \markbox{12570}{of} \markbox{12571}{domains} \markbox{m12572}{$U,V \in \calU$} \markbox{12573}{satisfies} \markbox{12574}{exactly} \markbox{12575}{one} \markbox{12576}{of} \markbox{12577}{the} \markbox{12578}{relations.} 
\end{itemize}
\item {} There \markbox{12579}{is} \markbox{12580}{a} \markbox{12581}{bound} \markbox{12582}{on} \markbox{12583}{the} \markbox{12584}{size} \markbox{12585}{of} \markbox{12586}{any} \markbox{12587}{pairwise} \markbox{m12588}{$\perp$}-comparable \markbox{12589}{subset} \markbox{12590}{of} \markbox{m12591}{$\calU$}. \label{item:finite dim}
\item {} To \markbox{12592}{each} \markbox{m12593}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{12594}{there} \markbox{12595}{is} \markbox{12596}{an} \markbox{12597}{associated} \markbox{12598}{finite} \markbox{12599}{simplicial} \markbox{12600}{interval} \markbox{m12601}{$\hT_U$}. \label{item:simplicial}
\item {} A \markbox{12602}{pair} \markbox{12603}{of} \markbox{12604}{labels} \markbox{m12605}{$F = \{x,y\}$} \markbox{12606}{which} \markbox{12607}{determined} \markbox{12608}{the} \markbox{12609}{endpoints,} \markbox{12610}{called} \markbox{12611}{\emph{marked points}} \markbox{m12612}{$\hx_U, \hy_U$}, \markbox{12613}{of} \markbox{12614}{the} \markbox{12615}{interval} \markbox{m12616}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{12617}{for} \markbox{12618}{each} \markbox{m12619}{$U \in \calU$}.
\item {} A \markbox{12620}{family} \markbox{12621}{of} \markbox{12622}{\emph{relative projections}} determining:
\begin{itemize}
    \item {} For \markbox{12623}{each} \markbox{m12624}{$U, V \in \calU$} \markbox{12625}{with} \markbox{m12626}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{12627}{or} \markbox{m12628}{$V \pitchfork U$}, \markbox{12629}{there} \markbox{12630}{is} \markbox{12631}{a} \markbox{12632}{vertex} \markbox{m12633}{$\hd^V_U \in \hT^{(0)}_U$} \markbox{12634}{called} \markbox{12635}{a} \markbox{12636}{\emph{cluster point}}.
 
\end{itemize}
    \item {} There \markbox{12637}{exist} \markbox{12638}{projection} \markbox{12639}{maps} \markbox{m12640}{$\hd^U_V: \hT_U \to \hT_V$} \markbox{12641}{when} \markbox{m12642}{$V \nest U$}, \markbox{12643}{satisfying} \markbox{12644}{the} \markbox{12645}{following} properties:\label{item:BGI HFI}
    \begin{enumerate}
    	\item {} (Consistency) \markbox{12646}{For} \markbox{12647}{each} \markbox{m12648}{$f \in F$}, \markbox{12649}{we} \markbox{12650}{have} \markbox{m12651}{$\hd^U_V(\hf_U) = \hf_V$}.
        \item {} (BGI) \markbox{12652}{If} \markbox{m12653}{$C \subset \hT_U - \hd^V_U$} \markbox{12654}{is} \markbox{12655}{a} \markbox{12656}{component,} \markbox{12657}{then} \markbox{m12658}{$\hd^U_V(C)$} \markbox{12659}{coincides} \markbox{12660}{with} \markbox{m12661}{$\hf_V$} \markbox{12662}{for} \markbox{m12663}{$f \in F$} \markbox{12664}{with} \markbox{m12665}{$\hf_U \in C$}. 
    \end{enumerate}

\item {} If \markbox{m12666}{$U,V,W \in \calU$} \markbox{12667}{with} \markbox{m12668}{$V,W \nest U$}, \markbox{m12669}{$V \pitchfork W$}, \markbox{12670}{and} \markbox{m12671}{$\hd^V_U \neq \hd^W_U$}, \markbox{12672}{then} \markbox{m12673}{$\hd^U_V(\hd^W_U) = \hd^W_V \in \hT_V$}. \label{item:delta control HFI}
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}
In \cite[Definition 12.1]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{12674}{the} \markbox{12675}{definition} \markbox{12676}{of} \markbox{12677}{a} \markbox{12678}{\emph{hierarchical family of trees}} \markbox{12679}{allows} \markbox{12680}{for} \markbox{12681}{the} \markbox{12682}{trees} \markbox{12683}{to} \markbox{12684}{have} \markbox{12685}{more} \markbox{12686}{than} \markbox{m12687}{$2$} \markbox{12688}{leaves.}  \markbox{12689}{This} \markbox{12690}{is} \markbox{12691}{only} \markbox{12692}{needed} \markbox{12693}{for} \markbox{12694}{modeling} \markbox{12695}{tuples} \markbox{12696}{of} \markbox{m12697}{$3$} \markbox{12698}{or} \markbox{12699}{more} points.
\end{remark}

The \markbox{12700}{following} \markbox{12701}{is} \markbox{12702}{an} \markbox{12703}{immediate} \markbox{12704}{consequence} \markbox{12705}{of} \markbox{12706}{our} \markbox{12707}{work} \markbox{12708}{in} \markbox{12709}{Section} \ref{sec:interval systems}, \markbox{12710}{especially} \markbox{12711}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:HHS to HFI}
Let \markbox{m12712}{$R>0$}, \markbox{m12713}{$r_1 > R_1=R_1(R,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{12714}{as} \markbox{12715}{in} \markbox{12716}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined} \markbox{12717}{and} \markbox{m12718}{$r_2 > R_2=R_2(R,\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{12719}{as} \markbox{12720}{in} \markbox{12721}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.  \markbox{12722}{For} \markbox{12723}{any} \markbox{m12724}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{12725}{of} \markbox{12726}{an} \markbox{m12727}{$R$}-interval \markbox{12728}{system} \markbox{12729}{for} \markbox{m12730}{$a,b \in \calX$}, \markbox{12731}{the} \markbox{12732}{associated} \markbox{12733}{family} \markbox{12734}{of} \markbox{12735}{collapsed} \markbox{12736}{intervals} \markbox{12737}{and} \markbox{12738}{their} \markbox{12739}{collapsed} \markbox{12740}{projections} \markbox{12741}{form} \markbox{12742}{a} \markbox{12743}{hierarchical} \markbox{12744}{family} \markbox{12745}{of} intervals.
\end{lemma}

As \markbox{12746}{above} \markbox{12747}{in} \markbox{12748}{Definition} \ref{defn:Q defined}, \markbox{12749}{we} \markbox{12750}{can} \markbox{12751}{define} \markbox{12752}{a} \markbox{m12753}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{12754}{subset} \markbox{12755}{of} \markbox{12756}{the} \markbox{12757}{product} \markbox{m12758}{$\prod_U \hT_U$}.  \markbox{12759}{Our} \markbox{12760}{next} \markbox{12761}{goal} \markbox{12762}{is} \markbox{12763}{the} \markbox{12764}{following} theorem:

\begin{theorem}\label{thm:Q CCC}
The \markbox{m12765}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{12766}{subset} \markbox{12767}{of} \markbox{12768}{an} \markbox{12769}{HFI} \markbox{12770}{is} \markbox{12771}{a} \markbox{12772}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12773}{cube} \markbox{12774}{complex.}  \markbox{12775}{Moreover,} \markbox{12776}{there} \markbox{12777}{is} \markbox{12778}{a} \markbox{12779}{bijective} \markbox{12780}{correspondence} \markbox{12781}{between} \markbox{12782}{its} \markbox{12783}{hyperplanes} \markbox{12784}{and} \markbox{12785}{the} \markbox{12786}{edges} \markbox{12787}{of} \markbox{12788}{the} \markbox{12789}{factors.} 
\end{theorem}
    

\subsection{Median graphs and dual cube complexes}

The \markbox{12790}{proof} \markbox{12791}{of} \markbox{12792}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC} \markbox{12793}{that} \markbox{12794}{we} \markbox{12795}{give} \markbox{12796}{here} \markbox{12797}{will} \markbox{12798}{use} \markbox{12799}{the} \markbox{12800}{notion} \markbox{12801}{of} \markbox{12802}{median} \markbox{12803}{spaces.}  \markbox{12804}{The} \markbox{12805}{connection} \markbox{12806}{between} \markbox{12807}{median} \markbox{12808}{graphs} \markbox{12809}{and} \markbox{12810}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12811}{cube} \markbox{12812}{complexes} \markbox{12813}{goes} \markbox{12814}{back} \markbox{12815}{to} \markbox{12816}{Roller's} \cite{Roller} \markbox{12817}{reframing} \markbox{12818}{of} \markbox{12819}{Sageev's} \markbox{12820}{construction} \cite{Sageev:cubulation}, \markbox{12821}{see} \markbox{12822}{also} \cite{CN05, Nica}.  \markbox{12823}{Notably,} \markbox{12824}{Chepoi} \cite[Theorem 6.1]{Che00} \markbox{12825}{showed} \markbox{12826}{that} \markbox{12827}{every} \markbox{12828}{median} \markbox{12829}{graph} \markbox{12830}{is} \markbox{12831}{the} \markbox{m12832}{$1$}-skeleton \markbox{12833}{of} \markbox{12834}{a} \markbox{12835}{unique} \markbox{12836}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12837}{cube} \markbox{12838}{complex.}  \markbox{12839}{Bowditch} \markbox{12840}{explains} \markbox{12841}{these} \markbox{12842}{connections} \markbox{12843}{in} \markbox{12844}{detail} \markbox{12845}{in} \cite[Section 11]{bowditch2022median}.

Let \markbox{m12846}{$X$} \markbox{12847}{be} \markbox{12848}{a} \markbox{12849}{space} \markbox{12850}{and} \markbox{m12851}{$\mm:X^3\to X$} \markbox{12852}{a} \markbox{12853}{ternary} \markbox{12854}{operator.}  \markbox{12855}{We} \markbox{12856}{call} \markbox{m12857}{$(X,\mm)$} \markbox{12858}{a} \markbox{12859}{\emph{median algebra}} \markbox{12860}{if} \markbox{12861}{for} \markbox{12862}{all} \markbox{m12863}{$a,b,c,d,e \in X$} \markbox{12864}{we} have
$$\mm(a,b,c) = \mm(b,a,c) = \mm(c,a,b), \hspace{.1in} \mm(a,a,b) = a, \hspace{.1in} \mm(a,b,\mm(c,d,e)) = \mm(\mm(a,b,c),\mm(a,b,d),e).$$


A \markbox{12865}{graph} \markbox{m12866}{$\Gamma$} \markbox{12867}{is} \markbox{12868}{\emph{median}} \markbox{12869}{if} \markbox{12870}{all} \markbox{12871}{choices} \markbox{12872}{of} \markbox{m12873}{$v_1,v_2,v_3 \in \Gamma^{(0)}$}, \markbox{12874}{there} \markbox{12875}{exists} \markbox{12876}{a} \markbox{12877}{unique} \markbox{12878}{point} \markbox{12879}{lying} \markbox{12880}{on} \markbox{12881}{some} \markbox{12882}{geodesic} \markbox{12883}{from} \markbox{m12884}{$v_i,v_j$} \markbox{12885}{for} \markbox{12886}{all} \markbox{m12887}{$i,j$}; \markbox{12888}{then} \markbox{m12889}{$\mm(v_1,v_2,v_3)$} \markbox{12890}{is} \markbox{12891}{that} \markbox{12892}{unique} point.

Given \markbox{m12893}{$a,b \in X$}, \markbox{12894}{the} \markbox{12895}{(median)} \markbox{12896}{\emph{interval}} \markbox{12897}{between} \markbox{m12898}{$a,b$} \markbox{12899}{is} \markbox{m12900}{$I(a,b) = \{x \in X| \hspace{.01in} \mm(a,x,b) = x\}$}.  \markbox{12901}{We} \markbox{12902}{say} \markbox{12903}{a} \markbox{12904}{median} \markbox{12905}{algebra} \markbox{m12906}{$(X, \mm)$} \markbox{12907}{is} \markbox{12908}{\emph{discrete}} \markbox{12909}{when} \markbox{m12910}{$I(a,b)$} \markbox{12911}{is} \markbox{12912}{finite} \markbox{12913}{for} \markbox{12914}{every} \markbox{m12915}{$a,b \in X$}.  \markbox{12916}{A} \markbox{12917}{\emph{subalgebra}} \markbox{12918}{is} \markbox{12919}{a} \markbox{12920}{subset} \markbox{m12921}{$S \subset X$} \markbox{12922}{which} \markbox{12923}{is} \markbox{12924}{closed} \markbox{12925}{under} \markbox{m12926}{$\mm$}.  \markbox{12927}{In} \markbox{12928}{particular,} \markbox{12929}{locally} \markbox{12930}{finite} \markbox{12931}{median} \markbox{12932}{graphs} \markbox{12933}{are} \markbox{12934}{discrete} \markbox{12935}{median} algebras.


Every \markbox{12936}{median} \markbox{12937}{algebra} \markbox{m12938}{$(X,\mm)$} \markbox{12939}{determines} \markbox{12940}{a} \markbox{12941}{graph} \markbox{12942}{called} \markbox{12943}{its} \markbox{12944}{\emph{adjacency graph}} \markbox{m12945}{$\Gamma(X)$} \markbox{12946}{as} \markbox{12947}{follows.}  \markbox{12948}{We} \markbox{12949}{say} \markbox{12950}{that} \markbox{m12951}{$a,b \in X$} \markbox{12952}{are} \markbox{12953}{\emph{adjacent}} \markbox{12954}{when} \markbox{m12955}{$I(a,b) = \emptyset$}.  \markbox{12956}{The} \markbox{12957}{vertices} \markbox{12958}{of} \markbox{m12959}{$\Gamma(X)$} \markbox{12960}{are} \markbox{12961}{the} \markbox{12962}{points} \markbox{12963}{of} \markbox{m12964}{$X$}, \markbox{12965}{with} \markbox{m12966}{$a,b \in X$} \markbox{12967}{connected} \markbox{12968}{by} \markbox{12969}{an} \markbox{12970}{edge} \markbox{12971}{in} \markbox{m12972}{$\Gamma(X)$} \markbox{12973}{exactly} \markbox{12974}{when} \markbox{m12975}{$a,b$} \markbox{12976}{are} \markbox{12977}{adjacent.}  \markbox{12978}{This} \markbox{12979}{graph} \markbox{12980}{is} \markbox{12981}{median} \markbox{12982}{exactly} \markbox{12983}{when} \markbox{m12984}{$(X,\mm)$} \markbox{12985}{is} \markbox{12986}{a} \markbox{12987}{discrete} \markbox{12988}{median} \markbox{12989}{algebra} \cite[Lemma 16.1.2]{bowditch2022median}.

Every \markbox{12990}{CAT(0)} \markbox{12991}{cube} \markbox{12992}{complex} \markbox{m12993}{$X$} \markbox{12994}{admits} \markbox{12995}{a} \markbox{12996}{canonical} \markbox{12997}{median} \markbox{12998}{structure} \markbox{12999}{as} \markbox{13000}{follows.}  \markbox{13001}{For} \markbox{13002}{any} \markbox{m13003}{$a,b \in X^{(0)}$}, \markbox{13004}{let} \markbox{m13005}{$J(a,b)$} \markbox{13006}{denote} \markbox{13007}{the} \markbox{13008}{set} \markbox{13009}{of} \markbox{m13010}{$\ell^1$}-geodesics \markbox{13011}{between} \markbox{m13012}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{13013}{Then} \markbox{13014}{given} \markbox{m13015}{$a,b,c \in X^{(0)}$}, \markbox{13016}{we} \markbox{13017}{have} \markbox{m13018}{$\mm(a,b,c) = J(a,b) \cap J(a,c) \cap J(b,c)$} \markbox{13019}{is} \markbox{13020}{a} \markbox{13021}{single} \markbox{13022}{point,} \markbox{13023}{and} \markbox{m13024}{$(X, \mm)$} \markbox{13025}{is} \markbox{13026}{a} \markbox{13027}{median} \markbox{13028}{structure} \markbox{13029}{with} \markbox{m13030}{$X^{(1)}$} \markbox{13031}{a} \markbox{13032}{median} \markbox{13033}{graph,} \markbox{13034}{with} \markbox{13035}{notably} \markbox{m13036}{$J(a,b) = I(a,b)$} \markbox{13037}{for} \markbox{13038}{all} \markbox{m13039}{$a, b \in X^{(0)}$}.  \markbox{13040}{Moreover,} \markbox{13041}{it} \markbox{13042}{is} \markbox{13043}{immediate} \markbox{13044}{that} \markbox{m13045}{$X^{(1)} = \Gamma(X^{(0)})$}, \markbox{13046}{since} \markbox{13047}{median} \markbox{13048}{adjacent} \markbox{13049}{vertices} \markbox{13050}{in} \markbox{m13051}{$X^{(0)}$} \markbox{13052}{are} \markbox{13053}{exactly} \markbox{13054}{those} \markbox{13055}{spanning} \markbox{13056}{an} \markbox{13057}{edge} \markbox{13058}{in} \markbox{m13059}{$X^{(1)}$}.

\begin{proof}[Proof \markbox{13060}{of} \markbox{13061}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC}]
   \markbox{13062}{First,} \markbox{13063}{observe} \markbox{13064}{that} \markbox{m13065}{$\calY = \prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_U$} \markbox{13066}{is} \markbox{13067}{a} \markbox{13068}{product} \markbox{13069}{of} \markbox{13070}{simplicial} \markbox{13071}{trees} \markbox{13072}{and} \markbox{13073}{hence} \markbox{13074}{a} \markbox{13075}{CAT(0)} \markbox{13076}{cube} complex.
   
   \markbox{13077}{Next,} \markbox{13078}{observe} \markbox{13079}{that} \markbox{m13080}{$\calQ \subset \calY$} \markbox{13081}{is} \markbox{13082}{a} \markbox{13083}{cubical} \markbox{13084}{subcomplex} \markbox{13085}{as} \markbox{13086}{follows.}  \markbox{13087}{For} \markbox{13088}{any} \markbox{m13089}{$\hx \in \calQ$}, \markbox{13090}{let} \markbox{m13091}{$C \subset \calY$} \markbox{13092}{be} \markbox{13093}{the} \markbox{13094}{minimal} \markbox{13095}{cube} \markbox{13096}{containing} \markbox{m13097}{$\hx$} \markbox{13098}{in} \markbox{13099}{its} \markbox{13100}{interior.}  \markbox{13101}{Presuming} \markbox{m13102}{$C$} \markbox{13103}{is} \markbox{13104}{not} \markbox{13105}{a} \markbox{13106}{vertex,} \markbox{13107}{minimality} \markbox{13108}{says} \markbox{13109}{that} \markbox{m13110}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{13111}{is} \markbox{13112}{in} \markbox{13113}{the} \markbox{13114}{interior} \markbox{13115}{of} \markbox{13116}{an} \markbox{13117}{edge} \markbox{13118}{in} \markbox{13119}{each} \markbox{13120}{of} \markbox{13121}{the} \markbox{13122}{defining} \markbox{13123}{coordinate} \markbox{13124}{intervals} \markbox{13125}{of} \markbox{m13126}{$C$}, \markbox{13127}{whose} \markbox{13128}{domain} \markbox{13129}{labels} \markbox{13130}{are} \markbox{13131}{pairwise} \markbox{13132}{orthogonal} \markbox{13133}{by} \markbox{13134}{item} \markbox{13135}{(9)} \markbox{13136}{of} \markbox{13137}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.  \markbox{13138}{This} \markbox{13139}{means} \markbox{13140}{that} \markbox{13141}{we} \markbox{13142}{can} \markbox{13143}{freely} \markbox{13144}{alter} \markbox{13145}{those} \markbox{13146}{coordinates} \markbox{13147}{of} \markbox{m13148}{$\hx$} \markbox{13149}{to} \markbox{13150}{be} \markbox{13151}{any} \markbox{13152}{choice} \markbox{13153}{of} \markbox{13154}{points} \markbox{13155}{in} \markbox{13156}{those} \markbox{13157}{edges,} \markbox{13158}{meaning} \markbox{m13159}{$C \subset \calQ$}.  \markbox{13160}{Hence} \markbox{m13161}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13162}{is} \markbox{13163}{a} \markbox{13164}{cubical} \markbox{13165}{subcomplex} \markbox{13166}{of} \markbox{m13167}{$\calY$}.

   \markbox{13168}{It} \markbox{13169}{is} \markbox{13170}{enough} \markbox{13171}{then} \markbox{13172}{to} \markbox{13173}{show} \markbox{13174}{that} \markbox{m13175}{$\calQ^{(0)} \subset \calY$} \markbox{13176}{is} \markbox{13177}{a} \markbox{13178}{discrete} \markbox{13179}{median} \markbox{13180}{subalgebra.}  \markbox{13181}{For} \markbox{13182}{once} \markbox{13183}{that} \markbox{13184}{is} \markbox{13185}{done,} \markbox{13186}{it} \markbox{13187}{will} \markbox{13188}{follow} \markbox{13189}{that} \markbox{m13190}{$\Gamma(\calQ)$} \markbox{13191}{is} \markbox{13192}{a} \markbox{13193}{median} \markbox{13194}{graph,} \markbox{13195}{but} \markbox{13196}{evidently} \markbox{m13197}{$\Gamma(\calQ) = \calQ^{(1)}$}, \markbox{13198}{as} \markbox{m13199}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13200}{is} \markbox{13201}{a} \markbox{13202}{cubical} \markbox{13203}{subcomplex} \markbox{13204}{of} \markbox{m13205}{$\calY$}.  \markbox{13206}{Since} \markbox{13207}{every} \markbox{13208}{median} \markbox{13209}{graph} \markbox{13210}{is} \markbox{13211}{the} \markbox{m13212}{$1$}-skeleton \markbox{13213}{of} \markbox{13214}{a} \markbox{13215}{unique} \markbox{13216}{CAT(0)} \markbox{13217}{cube} \markbox{13218}{complex} \cite[Theorem 6.1]{Che00}, \markbox{13219}{it} \markbox{13220}{follows} \markbox{13221}{that} \markbox{m13222}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13223}{must} \markbox{13224}{be} \markbox{13225}{that} \markbox{13226}{cube} \markbox{13227}{complex,} \markbox{13228}{completing} \markbox{13229}{the} proof.

   \markbox{13230}{The} \markbox{13231}{claim} \markbox{13232}{boils} \markbox{13233}{down} \markbox{13234}{to} \markbox{13235}{three} \markbox{13236}{exercises} \markbox{13237}{that} \markbox{13238}{we} \markbox{13239}{leave} \markbox{13240}{for} \markbox{13241}{the} reader:
   \begin{itemize}
       \item {} Any \markbox{13242}{(finite)} \markbox{13243}{product} \markbox{13244}{of} \markbox{13245}{median} \markbox{13246}{spaces} \markbox{13247}{admits} \markbox{13248}{the} \markbox{13249}{structure} \markbox{13250}{of} \markbox{13251}{a} \markbox{13252}{median} \markbox{13253}{space,} \markbox{13254}{where} \markbox{13255}{the} \markbox{13256}{median} \markbox{13257}{on} \markbox{13258}{the} \markbox{13259}{product} \markbox{13260}{is} \markbox{13261}{the} \markbox{13262}{tuple} \markbox{13263}{of} \markbox{13264}{medians} \markbox{13265}{in} \markbox{13266}{the} coordinates.
       \item {} For \markbox{13267}{any} \markbox{m13268}{$\ha,\hb,\hc \in \calQ^{(0)}$}, \markbox{13269}{we} \markbox{13270}{have} \markbox{m13271}{$\left(\mm_U(\ha_U,\hb_U,\hc_U)\right)_U \in \calQ$}.  \markbox{13272}{This} \markbox{13273}{can} \markbox{13274}{be} \markbox{13275}{proven} \markbox{13276}{using} \markbox{13277}{a} \markbox{13278}{basic} \markbox{13279}{consistency} \markbox{13280}{argument} \markbox{13281}{(see} \cite[Lemma 15.12]{Dur_infcube}).
       \item {} With \markbox{13282}{this} \markbox{13283}{median} \markbox{13284}{structure,} \markbox{m13285}{$a,b \in \calQ^{(0)}$} \markbox{13286}{are} \markbox{13287}{median} \markbox{13288}{adjacent} \markbox{13289}{exactly} \markbox{13290}{when} \markbox{13291}{they} \markbox{13292}{span} \markbox{13293}{an} \markbox{13294}{edge} \markbox{13295}{in} \markbox{m13296}{$\calQ^{(1)}$}.
   \end{itemize}

   \markbox{13297}{Finally,} \markbox{13298}{observe} \markbox{13299}{that} \markbox{13300}{the} \markbox{13301}{hyperplanes} \markbox{13302}{of} \markbox{m13303}{$\calY$} \markbox{13304}{are} \markbox{13305}{of} \markbox{13306}{the} \markbox{13307}{form} \markbox{m13308}{$\hh \times \prod_{V\neq U} \hT_V$} \markbox{13309}{for} \markbox{m13310}{$\hh$} \markbox{13311}{some} \markbox{13312}{hyperplane} \markbox{13313}{in} \markbox{m13314}{$\hT_U$}.  \markbox{13315}{Since} \markbox{m13316}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13317}{is} \markbox{13318}{a} \markbox{13319}{median} \markbox{13320}{subalgebra} \markbox{13321}{of} \markbox{m13322}{$\calY$}, \markbox{13323}{the} \markbox{13324}{hyperplanes} \markbox{13325}{of} \markbox{m13326}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13327}{are} \markbox{13328}{just} \markbox{13329}{hyperplanes} \markbox{13330}{of} \markbox{m13331}{$\calY$} \markbox{13332}{intersected} \markbox{13333}{with} \markbox{m13334}{$\calQ$}, \markbox{13335}{so} \markbox{13336}{the} \markbox{13337}{moreover} \markbox{13338}{statement} \markbox{13339}{follows.}  \markbox{13340}{This} \markbox{13341}{completes} \markbox{13342}{the} proof.
\end{proof}














\subsection{More tree trimming and hyperplane deletions}\label{subsec:tt cube}


In \markbox{13343}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:tree trimming}, \markbox{13344}{we} \markbox{13345}{introduced} \markbox{13346}{our} \markbox{13347}{tree} \markbox{13348}{trimming} \markbox{13349}{techniques,} \markbox{13350}{which} \markbox{13351}{allowed} \markbox{13352}{us} \markbox{13353}{to} \markbox{13354}{take} \markbox{13355}{a} \markbox{13356}{family} \markbox{13357}{of} \markbox{13358}{collapsed} \markbox{13359}{intervals} \markbox{13360}{and} \markbox{13361}{collapse} \markbox{13362}{a} \markbox{13363}{further} \markbox{13364}{family} \markbox{13365}{of} \markbox{13366}{subintervals} \markbox{13367}{while} \markbox{13368}{maintaining} \markbox{13369}{control} \markbox{13370}{over} \markbox{13371}{their} \markbox{13372}{associated} \markbox{m13373}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{13374}{subsets.}  \markbox{13375}{In} \markbox{13376}{this} \markbox{13377}{subsection,} \markbox{13378}{we} \markbox{13379}{need} \markbox{13380}{a} \markbox{13381}{further} \markbox{13382}{refinement} \markbox{13383}{applied} \markbox{13384}{to} \markbox{13385}{HFIs} \markbox{13386}{and} \markbox{13387}{their} \markbox{13388}{associated} \markbox{13389}{cube} complexes.

To \markbox{13390}{set} \markbox{13391}{up} \markbox{13392}{the} \markbox{13393}{statement,} \markbox{13394}{let} \markbox{m13395}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{13396}{be} \markbox{13397}{a} \markbox{13398}{hierarchical} \markbox{13399}{family} \markbox{13400}{of} \markbox{13401}{intervals,} \markbox{13402}{as} \markbox{13403}{in} \markbox{13404}{Definition} \ref{defn:HFI}.  \markbox{13405}{Fix} \markbox{13406}{a} \markbox{13407}{constant} \markbox{m13408}{$B>0$}, \markbox{13409}{which} \markbox{13410}{will} \markbox{13411}{control} \markbox{13412}{the} \markbox{13413}{size} \markbox{13414}{and} \markbox{13415}{number} \markbox{13416}{of} \markbox{13417}{subintervals} \markbox{13418}{we} \markbox{13419}{will} \markbox{13420}{collapse} \markbox{13421}{across} \markbox{13422}{all} \markbox{13423}{of} \markbox{13424}{the} \markbox{13425}{intervals.}  \markbox{13426}{In} \markbox{13427}{our} \markbox{13428}{applications,} \markbox{13429}{we} \markbox{13430}{will} \markbox{13431}{be} \markbox{13432}{able} \markbox{13433}{to} \markbox{13434}{control} \markbox{13435}{the} \markbox{13436}{size} \markbox{13437}{of} \markbox{m13438}{$B$}, \markbox{13439}{but} \markbox{13440}{notably} \markbox{13441}{not} \markbox{13442}{with} \markbox{13443}{respect} \markbox{13444}{to} \markbox{13445}{the} \markbox{13446}{largeness} \markbox{13447}{constant} \markbox{m13448}{$K$}, \markbox{13449}{unlike} \markbox{13450}{in} \markbox{13451}{the} \markbox{13452}{statement} \markbox{13453}{of} \markbox{13454}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}.

\begin{definition}[Admissible \markbox{13455}{simplicial} \markbox{13456}{trimming} setup]\label{defn:simplicial trimming setup}
Given \markbox{m13457}{$B>0$}, \markbox{13458}{a} \markbox{m13459}{$B$}-\markbox{13460}{\emph{admissible simplicial trimming setup}} \markbox{13461}{is} \markbox{13462}{a} \markbox{13463}{collection} \markbox{13464}{of} \markbox{13465}{\emph{trimming intervals}} \markbox{m13466}{$\calB$} \markbox{13467}{in} \markbox{13468}{the} \markbox{13469}{various} \markbox{m13470}{$\hT_{U,e}$} \markbox{13471}{satisfying} \markbox{13472}{the} following:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} For \markbox{13473}{each} \markbox{m13474}{$D \in \calB$} \markbox{13475}{with} \markbox{m13476}{$D \subset E \in \pi_0(\hT_{U,e})$}, \markbox{13477}{we} \markbox{13478}{have} \label{item:trimming integer}
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m13479}{$D$} \markbox{13480}{is} \markbox{13481}{a} \markbox{13482}{subinterval} \markbox{13483}{of} \markbox{m13484}{$E$} \markbox{13485}{with} \markbox{13486}{endpoints} \markbox{13487}{at} \markbox{13488}{vertices,} and
\item {} the \markbox{13489}{length} \markbox{m13490}{$l(D)$} \markbox{13491}{of} \markbox{m13492}{$D$} \markbox{13493}{is} \markbox{13494}{a} \markbox{13495}{positive} \markbox{13496}{integer} \markbox{13497}{whose} \markbox{13498}{length} \markbox{13499}{is} \markbox{13500}{bounded} \markbox{13501}{above} \markbox{13502}{by} \markbox{m13503}{$B$}.
\end{enumerate}
\item {} The \markbox{13504}{number} \markbox{13505}{of} \markbox{13506}{subintervals} \markbox{13507}{in} \markbox{m13508}{$\calB$} \markbox{13509}{is} \markbox{13510}{bounded} \markbox{13511}{by} \markbox{m13512}{$B$}, \markbox{13513}{that} \markbox{13514}{is} \markbox{m13515}{$\#\calB < B$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}
We \markbox{13516}{note} \markbox{13517}{that} \markbox{13518}{the} \markbox{13519}{conditions} \markbox{13520}{in} \markbox{13521}{Definition} \ref{defn:simplicial trimming setup} \markbox{13522}{guarantee} \markbox{13523}{that} \markbox{13524}{each} \markbox{13525}{quotient} \markbox{13526}{interval} \markbox{m13527}{$\hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{13528}{is} \markbox{13529}{a} \markbox{13530}{simplicial} \markbox{13531}{interval} \markbox{13532}{of} \markbox{13533}{the} \markbox{13534}{usual} \markbox{13535}{type} \markbox{13536}{we} \markbox{13537}{consider.}  \markbox{13538}{The} \markbox{13539}{requirement} \markbox{13540}{that} \markbox{13541}{each} \markbox{13542}{segment} \markbox{m13543}{$D \in \calB$} \markbox{13544}{has} \markbox{13545}{endpoints} \markbox{13546}{at} \markbox{13547}{vertices} \markbox{13548}{guarantees} \markbox{13549}{that} \markbox{13550}{when} \markbox{13551}{we} \markbox{13552}{collapse} \markbox{13553}{such} \markbox{13554}{a} \markbox{13555}{segment,} \markbox{13556}{then} \markbox{13557}{it} \markbox{13558}{only} \markbox{13559}{affects} \markbox{13560}{the} \markbox{13561}{interval-hyperplanes} \markbox{13562}{it} \markbox{13563}{contains,} \markbox{13564}{preserving} \markbox{13565}{those} \markbox{13566}{in} \markbox{13567}{its} complement.
\end{remark}

We \markbox{13568}{use} \markbox{13569}{the} \markbox{13570}{same} \markbox{13571}{associated} \markbox{13572}{notation} \markbox{13573}{as} \markbox{13574}{in} \markbox{13575}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:tree trimming}.  \markbox{13576}{Furthermore,} \markbox{13577}{we} \markbox{13578}{note} \markbox{13579}{that} \markbox{13580}{if} \markbox{m13581}{$\hT^e_U \subset \calB$}, \markbox{13582}{then} \markbox{m13583}{$\diam (\hT_U) < B^2$} \markbox{13584}{and} \markbox{m13585}{$\hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{13586}{is} \markbox{13587}{a} \markbox{13588}{point.}  \markbox{13589}{Let} \markbox{m13590}{$\calU_0 \subset \calU$} \markbox{13591}{denote} \markbox{13592}{the} \markbox{13593}{subset} \markbox{13594}{of} \markbox{13595}{domains} \markbox{13596}{for} \markbox{13597}{which} \markbox{m13598}{$\hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{13599}{is} \markbox{13600}{not} \markbox{13601}{a} \markbox{13602}{point.}  \markbox{13603}{By} \markbox{13604}{ignoring} \markbox{13605}{the} \markbox{13606}{domains} \markbox{13607}{in} \markbox{m13608}{$\calU - \calU_0$}, \markbox{13609}{we} \markbox{13610}{can} \markbox{13611}{consider} \markbox{13612}{the} \markbox{13613}{set} \markbox{13614}{of} \markbox{13615}{collapsed} \markbox{13616}{intervals} \markbox{m13617}{$\{\hT_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$}, \markbox{13618}{where} \markbox{13619}{we} \markbox{13620}{remove} \markbox{13621}{any} \markbox{13622}{labels} \markbox{m13623}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{13624}{from} \markbox{m13625}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{13626}{from} \markbox{13627}{any} \markbox{13628}{domain} \markbox{m13629}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{13630}{with} \markbox{m13631}{$V \in \calU - \calU_0$}.

The \markbox{13632}{following} \markbox{13633}{theorem} \markbox{13634}{expands} \markbox{13635}{on} \markbox{13636}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming} \markbox{13637}{in} \markbox{13638}{the} \markbox{13639}{HFI} setting:

\begin{theorem}\label{thm:simplicial tree trimming}
Let \markbox{m13640}{$B>0$} \markbox{13641}{and} \markbox{m13642}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{13643}{be} \markbox{13644}{an} \markbox{13645}{HFI.}  \markbox{13646}{For} \markbox{13647}{any} \markbox{m13648}{$B$}-admissible \markbox{13649}{simplicial} \markbox{13650}{trimming} \markbox{13651}{setup} \markbox{m13652}{$\calB$}, \markbox{13653}{the} \markbox{13654}{following} hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item {} The \markbox{13655}{collections} \markbox{m13656}{$\{\hT_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{13657}{and} \markbox{m13658}{$\{\hT_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$} \markbox{13659}{are} \markbox{13660}{HFIs.}  \markbox{13661}{We} \markbox{13662}{let} \markbox{m13663}{$\calQ', \calQ_0$} \markbox{13664}{denote} \markbox{13665}{their} \markbox{13666}{corresponding} \markbox{m13667}{$0$}-consistent subsets.
\item {} We \markbox{13668}{have} \markbox{m13669}{$\Delta(\calQ) = \calQ'$}, \markbox{13670}{where} \markbox{m13671}{$\Delta:\prod_U \hT_U \to \prod_U \hT'_U$} \markbox{13672}{is} \markbox{13673}{the} \markbox{13674}{global} \markbox{13675}{collapsing} map.
\item {} There \markbox{13676}{exists} \markbox{13677}{a} \markbox{13678}{map} \markbox{m13679}{$\Xi:\calQ' \to \calQ$} \markbox{13680}{with} \markbox{m13681}{$\Delta \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ'}$}.
\item {} The \markbox{13682}{map} \markbox{m13683}{$\Delta|_{\calQ}: \calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{13684}{is} \markbox{13685}{a} \markbox{m13686}{$(1, B^2)$}-quasi-isometry.
\item {} At \markbox{13687}{the} \markbox{13688}{level} \markbox{13689}{of} \markbox{13690}{cube} \markbox{13691}{complexes,} \markbox{13692}{the} \markbox{13693}{map} \markbox{m13694}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{13695}{is} \markbox{13696}{a} \markbox{13697}{hyperplane} \markbox{13698}{deletion} \markbox{13699}{map} \markbox{13700}{deleting} \markbox{13701}{at} \markbox{13702}{most} \markbox{m13703}{$B^2$}-many hyperplanes.
\end{enumerate}

\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
Item \markbox{13704}{(1)} \markbox{13705}{is} \markbox{13706}{straightforward,} \markbox{13707}{since} \markbox{13708}{we} \markbox{13709}{are} \markbox{13710}{just} \markbox{13711}{collapsing} \markbox{13712}{simplicial} \markbox{13713}{subintervals.}  \markbox{13714}{Items} \markbox{13715}{(2)--(3)} \markbox{13716}{follow} \markbox{13717}{from} \markbox{13718}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}, \markbox{13719}{where} \markbox{13720}{in} \markbox{13721}{the} \markbox{13722}{argument} \markbox{13723}{we} \markbox{13724}{just} \markbox{13725}{replace} \markbox{13726}{the} \markbox{13727}{HFI} \markbox{13728}{axioms} \markbox{13729}{(Definition} \ref{defn:HFI}) \markbox{13730}{with} \markbox{13731}{the} \markbox{13732}{appropriate} \markbox{13733}{properties} \markbox{13734}{from} \markbox{13735}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.  \markbox{13736}{The} \markbox{13737}{fact} \markbox{13738}{that} \markbox{m13739}{$\Delta$} \markbox{13740}{deletes} \markbox{13741}{at} \markbox{13742}{most} \markbox{m13743}{$B^2$}-many \markbox{13744}{hyperplanes} \markbox{13745}{from} \markbox{m13746}{$\prod_U \hT_U$}, \markbox{13747}{so} \markbox{13748}{item} \markbox{13749}{(5)} \markbox{13750}{follows} \markbox{13751}{from} \markbox{13752}{the} \markbox{13753}{``moreover''} \markbox{13754}{part} \markbox{13755}{of} \markbox{13756}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC}.  \markbox{13757}{Finally,} \markbox{13758}{item} \markbox{13759}{(4)} \markbox{13760}{follows} \markbox{13761}{immediately} \markbox{13762}{from} \markbox{13763}{item} \markbox{13764}{(5).}  \markbox{13765}{This} \markbox{13766}{completes} \markbox{13767}{the} proof.


\end{proof}







\subsection{Hierarchy paths and the distance formula}\label{subsec:HP and DF}

With \markbox{13768}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC} \markbox{13769}{in} \markbox{13770}{hand,} \markbox{13771}{we} \markbox{13772}{can} \markbox{13773}{make} \markbox{13774}{some} \markbox{13775}{observations} \markbox{13776}{about} \markbox{13777}{the} \markbox{13778}{cubical} \markbox{13779}{structure} \markbox{13780}{of} \markbox{m13781}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13782}{and} \markbox{13783}{how} \markbox{13784}{it} \markbox{13785}{relates} \markbox{13786}{to} \markbox{13787}{its} \markbox{13788}{hierarchical} \markbox{13789}{nature.}  \markbox{13790}{In} \markbox{13791}{particular,} \markbox{13792}{we} \markbox{13793}{get} \markbox{13794}{a} \markbox{13795}{proof} \markbox{13796}{of} \markbox{13797}{the} \markbox{13798}{(more} \markbox{13799}{difficult)} \markbox{13800}{lower} \markbox{13801}{bound} \markbox{13802}{of} \markbox{13803}{the} \markbox{13804}{Distance} \markbox{13805}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF} \markbox{13806}{and} \markbox{13807}{the} \markbox{13808}{existence} \markbox{13809}{of} \markbox{13810}{hierarchy} paths.

The \markbox{13811}{following} \markbox{13812}{lemma} \markbox{13813}{is} \cite[Lemma 14.7]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{13814}{and} \markbox{13815}{we} \markbox{13816}{have} \markbox{13817}{included} \markbox{13818}{its} \markbox{13819}{proof} \markbox{13820}{here} \markbox{13821}{for} completeness.


\begin{lemma}\label{lem:NR hp in Q}
Let \markbox{m13822}{$\hx,\hy \in \calQ$}.  \markbox{13823}{Let} \markbox{m13824}{$\gamma$} \markbox{13825}{be} \markbox{13826}{any} \markbox{13827}{combinatorial} \markbox{13828}{geodesic} \markbox{13829}{in} \markbox{m13830}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13831}{from} \markbox{m13832}{$\hx$} \markbox{13833}{to} \markbox{m13834}{$\hy$}.  \markbox{13835}{Then} \markbox{13836}{for} \markbox{13837}{all} \markbox{m13838}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{13839}{the} \markbox{13840}{projection} \markbox{m13841}{$\hpi_U(\gamma) \subset \hT_U$} \markbox{13842}{is} \markbox{13843}{an} \markbox{13844}{unparameterized} \markbox{13845}{geodesic} \markbox{13846}{between} \markbox{m13847}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{13848}{and} \markbox{m13849}{$\hy_U$}.
\end{lemma} 

\begin{proof}
Since \markbox{13850}{combinatorial} \markbox{13851}{geodesics} \markbox{13852}{do} \markbox{13853}{not} \markbox{13854}{cross} \markbox{13855}{a} \markbox{13856}{hyperplane} \markbox{13857}{twice} \markbox{13858}{and} \markbox{13859}{the} \markbox{13860}{restriction} \markbox{13861}{quotient} \markbox{m13862}{$\hpi_U:\calQ \to \hT_U$} \markbox{13863}{is} \markbox{m13864}{$1$}-Lipschitz, \markbox{13865}{it} \markbox{13866}{follows} \markbox{13867}{that} \markbox{m13868}{$\hpi_U(\gamma)$} \markbox{13869}{does} \markbox{13870}{not} \markbox{13871}{backtrack} \markbox{13872}{either.}  \markbox{13873}{This} \markbox{13874}{completes} \markbox{13875}{the} proof.





\end{proof}

This \markbox{13876}{lemma} \markbox{13877}{plays} \markbox{13878}{two} \markbox{13879}{roles:} \markbox{13880}{it's} \markbox{13881}{useful} \markbox{13882}{for} \markbox{13883}{proving} \markbox{13884}{that} \markbox{13885}{an} \markbox{13886}{isomorphism} \markbox{13887}{of} \markbox{13888}{HFIs} \markbox{13889}{induces} \markbox{13890}{an} \markbox{13891}{isomorphism} \markbox{13892}{of} \markbox{13893}{their} \markbox{13894}{cubical} \markbox{13895}{duals} \markbox{13896}{(Proposition} \ref{prop:HFI isomorphism}), \markbox{13897}{and,} \markbox{13898}{in} \markbox{13899}{the} \markbox{13900}{next} \markbox{13901}{proposition,} \markbox{13902}{we} \markbox{13903}{use} \markbox{13904}{it} \markbox{13905}{directly} \markbox{13906}{to} \markbox{13907}{show} \markbox{13908}{that} \markbox{13909}{combinatorial} \markbox{13910}{geodesics} \markbox{13911}{in} \markbox{13912}{a} \markbox{13913}{cubical} \markbox{13914}{model} \markbox{13915}{get} \markbox{13916}{sent} \markbox{13917}{to} \markbox{13918}{hierarchy} \markbox{13919}{paths} \markbox{13920}{(Definition} \ref{defn:hp}) \markbox{13921}{in} \markbox{13922}{the} \markbox{13923}{ambient} \markbox{13924}{HHS.}  \markbox{13925}{That} \markbox{13926}{is} \markbox{13927}{the} \markbox{13928}{content} \markbox{13929}{of} \markbox{13930}{the} \markbox{13931}{next} \markbox{13932}{proposition,} \markbox{13933}{which} \markbox{13934}{is} \markbox{13935}{simplified} \markbox{13936}{version} \markbox{13937}{of} \cite[Proposition 14.8]{Dur_infcube}:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:cubical hp}
Let \markbox{m13938}{$a,b \in \calX$}, \markbox{m13939}{$K \geq K_0$} \markbox{13940}{where} \markbox{m13941}{$K_0 = K_0(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{13942}{is} \markbox{13943}{from} \markbox{13944}{Theorem} \ref{thm:DF}, \markbox{m13945}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b)$}, \markbox{13946}{and} \markbox{13947}{let} \markbox{m13948}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$}.  \markbox{13949}{Let} \markbox{m13950}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{13951}{be} \markbox{13952}{any} \markbox{m13953}{$R$}-interval \markbox{13954}{system} \markbox{13955}{for} \markbox{m13956}{$a,b$} \markbox{13957}{and} \markbox{m13958}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{13959}{the} \markbox{13960}{HFI} \markbox{13961}{associated} \markbox{13962}{to} \markbox{13963}{any} \markbox{m13964}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{13965}{for} \markbox{m13966}{$r_1 \geq R_1, r_2 \geq R_2$}  \markbox{13967}{with} \markbox{m13968}{$r_1$} \markbox{13969}{a} \markbox{13970}{positive} \markbox{13971}{integer.}  \markbox{13972}{Let} \markbox{m13973}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13974}{be} \markbox{13975}{the} \markbox{13976}{corresponding} \markbox{m13977}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{13978}{set} \markbox{13979}{and} \markbox{m13980}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$} \markbox{13981}{the} \markbox{13982}{quasi-isometry} \markbox{13983}{constructed} \markbox{13984}{in} \markbox{13985}{Section} \ref{sec:hPsi qi}.
\begin{itemize}
\item {} If \markbox{m13986}{$\ha, \hb$} \markbox{13987}{are} \markbox{13988}{the} \markbox{13989}{points} \markbox{m13990}{$\calQ$} \markbox{13991}{corresponding} \markbox{13992}{to} \markbox{m13993}{$a, b$} \markbox{13994}{and} \markbox{m13995}{$\gamma$} \markbox{13996}{is} \markbox{13997}{a} \markbox{13998}{combinatorial} \markbox{13999}{geodesic} \markbox{14000}{between} \markbox{14001}{them,} \markbox{14002}{then} \markbox{m14003}{$\hO(\gamma) \subset H$} \markbox{14004}{is} \markbox{14005}{an} \markbox{m14006}{$(L_{hp},L_{hp})$}-hierarchy \markbox{14007}{path} \markbox{14008}{between} \markbox{m14009}{$a,b$} \markbox{14010}{for} \markbox{m14011}{$L_{hp} = L_{hp}(R,r_1,r_2,K, \mathfrak S)>0$}.
\end{itemize} 
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
The \markbox{14012}{following} \markbox{14013}{is} \markbox{14014}{a} \markbox{14015}{fairly} \markbox{14016}{complete} \markbox{14017}{sketch} \markbox{14018}{of} \markbox{14019}{the} \markbox{14020}{proof,} \markbox{14021}{which} \markbox{14022}{is} \markbox{14023}{simpler} \markbox{14024}{than} \markbox{14025}{the} \markbox{14026}{more} \markbox{14027}{general} \markbox{14028}{version} \markbox{14029}{from} \cite[Proposition 14.8]{Dur_infcube}.

Since \markbox{14030}{the} \markbox{14031}{map} \markbox{m14032}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$} \markbox{14033}{is} \markbox{14034}{effectively} \markbox{14035}{defined} \markbox{14036}{coordinate-wise,} \markbox{14037}{its} \markbox{14038}{enough} \markbox{14039}{to} \markbox{14040}{consider} \markbox{14041}{the} \markbox{14042}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{14043}{maps} \markbox{m14044}{$B_U:\hT_U \to T_U$} \markbox{14045}{as} \markbox{14046}{described} \markbox{14047}{in} \markbox{14048}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:hO defined}, \markbox{14049}{as} \markbox{14050}{the} \markbox{14051}{map} \markbox{m14052}{$\phi_U:T_U\to \calC(U)$} \markbox{14053}{is} \markbox{14054}{an} \markbox{m14055}{$(R,R)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{14056}{embedding} \markbox{14057}{by} \markbox{14058}{assumption.}  \markbox{14059}{For} \markbox{14060}{this,} \markbox{14061}{we} \markbox{14062}{can} \markbox{14063}{let} \markbox{m14064}{$\gamma_U$} \markbox{14065}{denote} \markbox{14066}{the} \markbox{14067}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{14068}{projection} \markbox{14069}{of} \markbox{m14070}{$\gamma$} \markbox{14071}{to} \markbox{14072}{each} \markbox{m14073}{$\hT_U$}, \markbox{14074}{and} \markbox{14075}{we} \markbox{14076}{want} \markbox{14077}{to} \markbox{14078}{show} \markbox{14079}{that} \markbox{m14080}{$B_U(\gamma_U)$} \markbox{14081}{is} \markbox{14082}{an} \markbox{14083}{unparameterized} \markbox{14084}{quasi-geodesic} \markbox{14085}{in} \markbox{m14086}{$T_U$}.

By \markbox{14087}{construction,} \markbox{m14088}{$B_U(\gamma_U) \subset [a_U,b_U] = T_U$}, \markbox{14089}{so} \markbox{14090}{it} \markbox{14091}{suffices} \markbox{14092}{to} \markbox{14093}{show} \markbox{14094}{that} \markbox{14095}{this} \markbox{14096}{path} \markbox{14097}{never} \markbox{14098}{backtracks} \markbox{14099}{an} \markbox{14100}{unbounded} \markbox{14101}{amount.}  \markbox{14102}{Proceeding} \markbox{14103}{by} \markbox{14104}{induction} \markbox{14105}{in} \markbox{14106}{the} \markbox{m14107}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-level \markbox{14108}{in} \markbox{m14109}{$\calU$}, \markbox{14110}{if} \markbox{m14111}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{14112}{is} \markbox{m14113}{$\nest$}-minimal, \markbox{14114}{then} \markbox{14115}{the} \markbox{14116}{amount} \markbox{14117}{of} \markbox{14118}{collapsing} \markbox{14119}{in} \markbox{m14120}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{14121}{is} \markbox{14122}{bounded} \markbox{14123}{by} \markbox{m14124}{$2r_1$}, \markbox{14125}{and} \markbox{14126}{we} \markbox{14127}{are} \markbox{14128}{done} \markbox{14129}{by} \markbox{14130}{Lemma} \ref{lem:NR hp in Q}.  \markbox{14131}{For} \markbox{14132}{non-minimal} \markbox{14133}{domains} \markbox{m14134}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{14135}{note} \markbox{14136}{that} \markbox{14137}{by} \markbox{14138}{Lemma} \ref{lem:NR hp in Q}, \markbox{14139}{backtracking} \markbox{14140}{in} \markbox{m14141}{$T_U$} \markbox{14142}{is} \markbox{14143}{only} \markbox{14144}{possible} \markbox{14145}{if} \markbox{m14146}{$\gamma_U(t), \gamma_U(s)$} \markbox{14147}{are} \markbox{14148}{at} \markbox{14149}{the} \markbox{14150}{same} \markbox{14151}{collapsed} \markbox{14152}{point} \markbox{14153}{corresponding} \markbox{14154}{to} \markbox{14155}{some} \markbox{14156}{cluster} \markbox{m14157}{$C$}.  \markbox{14158}{If} \markbox{14159}{there} \markbox{14160}{are} \markbox{14161}{times} \markbox{m14162}{$s < t$} \markbox{14163}{so} \markbox{14164}{that} \markbox{m14165}{$d_{T_U}(B_U(\gamma(s), b_U) - d_{T_U}(B_U(\gamma(s)),b_U) \gg 100r_2 + 100r_1$}, \markbox{14166}{then} \markbox{14167}{there} \markbox{14168}{is} \markbox{14169}{some} \markbox{m14170}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{14171}{domain} \markbox{m14172}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{14173}{with} \markbox{m14174}{$\hd^V_U = q_U(C)$} \markbox{14175}{for} \markbox{14176}{which} \markbox{m14177}{$B_U(\gamma_U(t))$} \markbox{14178}{is} \markbox{14179}{on} \markbox{14180}{the} \markbox{14181}{side} \markbox{14182}{of} \markbox{m14183}{$a_U$} \markbox{14184}{while} \markbox{m14185}{$B_U(\gamma_U(s))$} \markbox{14186}{is} \markbox{14187}{on} \markbox{14188}{the} \markbox{14189}{side} \markbox{14190}{of} \markbox{m14191}{$b_U$}, \markbox{14192}{with} \markbox{14193}{both} \markbox{m14194}{$(50r_2 + 50r_1)$}-away \markbox{14195}{from} \markbox{m14196}{$\delta^V_U$}.  \markbox{14197}{But} \markbox{14198}{then} \markbox{14199}{consistency} \markbox{14200}{and} \markbox{14201}{the} \markbox{14202}{BGI} \markbox{14203}{properties} \markbox{14204}{from} \markbox{14205}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control} \markbox{14206}{implies} \markbox{14207}{that} \markbox{m14208}{$B_V(\gamma_V(t)), a_V$} \markbox{14209}{and} \markbox{m14210}{$B_V(\gamma_V(s)),b_V$} \markbox{14211}{are} \markbox{m14212}{$R$}-close, \markbox{14213}{and} \markbox{14214}{so} \markbox{m14215}{$\gamma_V(t) = \ha_V$} \markbox{14216}{and} \markbox{m14217}{$\gamma_V(s) = \hb_V$}, \markbox{14218}{which} \markbox{14219}{contradicts} \markbox{14220}{the} \markbox{14221}{base} \markbox{14222}{case} \markbox{14223}{of} \markbox{14224}{this} \markbox{14225}{induction.}  \markbox{14226}{This} \markbox{14227}{completes} \markbox{14228}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}
     \markbox{14229}{Since} \markbox{14230}{the} \markbox{14231}{map} \markbox{m14232}{$\hO: \calQ \to \calX$} \markbox{14233}{is} \markbox{14234}{uniformly} \markbox{14235}{quasi-median} \cite[Section 15]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{14236}{one} \markbox{14237}{could} \markbox{14238}{alternatively} \markbox{14239}{use} \markbox{14240}{the} \markbox{14241}{fact} \markbox{14242}{that} \markbox{14243}{median} \markbox{14244}{paths} \markbox{14245}{in} \markbox{14246}{HHSes} \markbox{14247}{are} \markbox{14248}{hierarchy} \markbox{14249}{paths} \cite[Lemma 1.37]{HHS_quasi}.
\end{remark}

As \markbox{14250}{a} \markbox{14251}{consequence} \markbox{14252}{of} \markbox{14253}{Propositions} \ref{prop:cubical hp} \markbox{14254}{and} \ref{prop:lower bound}, \markbox{14255}{we} \markbox{14256}{obtain} \markbox{14257}{the} \markbox{14258}{lower} \markbox{14259}{bound} \markbox{14260}{of} \markbox{14261}{the} \markbox{14262}{Distance} \markbox{14263}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF}:

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:DF lower bound}
There \markbox{14264}{exists} \markbox{m14265}{$K_0 = K_0(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{14266}{such} \markbox{14267}{that} \markbox{14268}{for} \markbox{14269}{all} \markbox{m14270}{$K>K_0$} \markbox{14271}{and} \markbox{14272}{any} \markbox{m14273}{$x, y \in \calX$}, \markbox{14274}{we} have
$$\sum_{U \in \mathfrak S} \left[d_U(x,y)\right]_K \prec d_{\calX}(x,y).$$
\end{corollary}

\subsection{Isomorphisms of HFIs and their associated cube complexes}

In \markbox{14275}{this} \markbox{14276}{final} \markbox{14277}{subsection,} \markbox{14278}{we} \markbox{14279}{will} \markbox{14280}{discuss} \markbox{14281}{when} \markbox{14282}{two} \markbox{14283}{HFIs} \markbox{14284}{to} \markbox{14285}{determine} \markbox{14286}{isomorphic} \markbox{14287}{cube} \markbox{14288}{complexes.}  \markbox{14289}{This} \markbox{14290}{statement,} \markbox{14291}{while} \markbox{14292}{unsurprising,} \markbox{14293}{motivates} \markbox{14294}{what} \markbox{14295}{happens} \markbox{14296}{in} \markbox{14297}{the} \markbox{14298}{subsequent} \markbox{14299}{sections,} \markbox{14300}{hence} \markbox{14301}{its} \markbox{14302}{placement} here.

Let \markbox{m14303}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{14304}{and} \markbox{m14305}{$\{\hT'_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{14306}{be} \markbox{14307}{two} \markbox{14308}{HFIs} \markbox{14309}{over} \markbox{14310}{a} \markbox{14311}{common} \markbox{14312}{index} \markbox{14313}{set} \markbox{m14314}{$\calU$} \markbox{14315}{and} \markbox{14316}{common} \markbox{14317}{relations,} \markbox{14318}{i.e.} \markbox{m14319}{$U,V \in \calU$} \markbox{14320}{have} \markbox{14321}{the} \markbox{14322}{same} \markbox{14323}{relation} \markbox{14324}{in} \markbox{14325}{both} \markbox{14326}{HFIs.}  \markbox{14327}{Any} \markbox{14328}{family} \markbox{14329}{of} \markbox{14330}{maps} \markbox{m14331}{$i_U:\hT_U \to \hT'_U$} \markbox{14332}{induces} \markbox{14333}{a} \markbox{14334}{global} \markbox{14335}{map} \markbox{m14336}{$I:\prod_{U \in \calU} \hT_U \to \prod_{U \in \calU} \hT'_U$}, \markbox{14337}{where} \markbox{m14338}{$I((\hx_U)) = (i_U(\hx_U))$}.

The \markbox{14339}{following} \markbox{14340}{proposition,} \markbox{14341}{which} \markbox{14342}{is} \markbox{14343}{an} \markbox{14344}{interval} \markbox{14345}{version} \markbox{14346}{of} \cite[Proposition 14.12]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{14347}{gives} \markbox{14348}{sufficient} \markbox{14349}{conditions} \markbox{14350}{for} \markbox{14351}{the} \markbox{14352}{induced} \markbox{14353}{map} \markbox{14354}{to} \markbox{14355}{be} \markbox{14356}{an} \markbox{14357}{isometry} \markbox{m14358}{$I:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{14359}{which} \markbox{14360}{induces} \markbox{14361}{a} \markbox{14362}{cubical} \markbox{14363}{isomorphism} \markbox{14364}{between} \markbox{14365}{their} \markbox{14366}{dual} \markbox{14367}{cube} complexes.

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:HFI isomorphism}
Let \markbox{m14368}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{14369}{and} \markbox{m14370}{$\{\hT'_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{14371}{be} \markbox{14372}{two} \markbox{14373}{HFIs} \markbox{14374}{over} \markbox{14375}{a} \markbox{14376}{common} \markbox{14377}{index} \markbox{14378}{set} \markbox{m14379}{$\calU$} \markbox{14380}{with} \markbox{14381}{marked} \markbox{14382}{points} \markbox{m14383}{$F = \{a,b\}$}, \markbox{14384}{and} \markbox{14385}{let} \markbox{m14386}{$\calQ, \calQ'$} \markbox{14387}{be} \markbox{14388}{their} \markbox{14389}{corresponding} \markbox{m14390}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{14391}{sets.}  \markbox{14392}{Suppose} \markbox{14393}{that} \markbox{14394}{for} \markbox{14395}{each} \markbox{m14396}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{14397}{there} \markbox{14398}{is} \markbox{14399}{a} \markbox{14400}{simplicial} \markbox{14401}{isometry} \markbox{m14402}{$i_U:\hT_U \to \hT'_U$} \markbox{14403}{which} \markbox{14404}{also} satisfies:
\begin{enumerate}
	\item {} We \markbox{14405}{have} \markbox{m14406}{$i_U(\ha_U) = \ha'_U \in \hT'_U$} \markbox{14407}{and} \markbox{m14408}{$i_U(\hb_U) = \hb'_U \in \hT'_U$}.
	\item {} For \markbox{14409}{all} \markbox{m14410}{$V  \in \calU$} \markbox{14411}{with} \markbox{m14412}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{14413}{or} \markbox{m14414}{$V \pitchfork U$}, \markbox{14415}{we} \markbox{14416}{have} \markbox{m14417}{$i_U(\hd^V_U) = \left(\hd^V_U\right)'$}.
	\item {} For \markbox{14418}{all} \markbox{m14419}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{14420}{with} \markbox{m14421}{$U \nest V$} \markbox{14422}{and} \markbox{m14423}{$\hx_V \in \hT_V$}, \markbox{14424}{we} \markbox{14425}{have} \markbox{m14426}{$\left(\hd^V_U\right)'(i_V(\hx_V)) = i_U(\hd^V_U(\hx_V))$}.
\end{enumerate}
Then \markbox{14427}{the} \markbox{14428}{corresponding} \markbox{14429}{map} \markbox{14430}{induces} \markbox{14431}{a} \markbox{14432}{cubical} \markbox{14433}{isomorphism} \markbox{m14434}{$I:\calQ \to \calQ'$}.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}[Sketch \markbox{14435}{of} proof]


The \markbox{14436}{proof} \markbox{14437}{of} \markbox{14438}{this} \markbox{14439}{version} \markbox{14440}{below} \markbox{14441}{is} \markbox{14442}{the} \markbox{14443}{same} \markbox{14444}{as} \markbox{14445}{the} \markbox{14446}{original,} \markbox{14447}{which} \markbox{14448}{is,} \markbox{14449}{in} \markbox{14450}{turn,} \markbox{14451}{an} \markbox{14452}{exercise} \markbox{14453}{in} \markbox{14454}{the} \markbox{14455}{construction} \markbox{14456}{from} \markbox{14457}{this} \markbox{14458}{section} \markbox{14459}{plus} \markbox{14460}{Lemma} \ref{lem:NR hp in Q}.  \markbox{14461}{The} \markbox{14462}{main} \markbox{14463}{idea} \markbox{14464}{is} \markbox{14465}{that} \markbox{14466}{items} \markbox{14467}{in} \markbox{14468}{the} \markbox{14469}{statement} \markbox{14470}{guarantee} \markbox{14471}{that} \markbox{14472}{the} \markbox{14473}{global} \markbox{14474}{map} \markbox{m14475}{$I$} \markbox{14476}{induced} \markbox{14477}{from} \markbox{14478}{the} \markbox{14479}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{14480}{isometries} \markbox{14481}{preserves} \markbox{m14482}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{14483}{and} \markbox{14484}{distances,} \markbox{14485}{i.e.} \markbox{14486}{we} \markbox{14487}{have} \markbox{m14488}{$I:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{14489}{is} \markbox{14490}{an} \markbox{14491}{isometric} \markbox{14492}{embedding,} \markbox{14493}{with} \markbox{14494}{surjectivity} \markbox{14495}{following} \markbox{14496}{from} \markbox{14497}{a} \markbox{14498}{consistency} \markbox{14499}{argument.}  \markbox{14500}{Since} \markbox{14501}{the} \markbox{14502}{interval-wise} \markbox{14503}{maps} \markbox{14504}{respect} \markbox{14505}{the} \markbox{14506}{simplicial} \markbox{14507}{structure,} \markbox{14508}{we} \markbox{14509}{have} \markbox{14510}{that} \markbox{m14511}{$I$} \markbox{14512}{is} \markbox{14513}{also} \markbox{14514}{a} \markbox{14515}{cubical} \markbox{14516}{isomorphism} \markbox{14517}{via} \markbox{14518}{Lemma} \ref{lem:halfspaces_bijection}.  \markbox{14519}{We} \markbox{14520}{leave} \markbox{14521}{the} \markbox{14522}{details} \markbox{14523}{to} \markbox{14524}{the} reader.



\end{proof}
















\section{Controlling domains} \label{sec:controlling domains}

In \markbox{14525}{this} \markbox{14526}{section,} \markbox{14527}{we} \markbox{14528}{turn} \markbox{14529}{toward} \markbox{14530}{the} \markbox{14531}{proof} \markbox{14532}{of} \markbox{14533}{our} \markbox{14534}{main} \markbox{14535}{technical} \markbox{14536}{result,} \markbox{14537}{namely} \markbox{14538}{the} \markbox{14539}{Stable} \markbox{14540}{Cubical} \markbox{14541}{Interval} \markbox{14542}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}, \markbox{14543}{which} \markbox{14544}{is} \markbox{14545}{a} \markbox{14546}{stabilized} \markbox{14547}{version} \markbox{14548}{of} \markbox{14549}{the} \markbox{14550}{cubical} \markbox{14551}{model} \markbox{14552}{construction} \markbox{14553}{for} \markbox{14554}{a} \markbox{14555}{pair} \markbox{14556}{of} \markbox{14557}{points} \markbox{m14558}{$a,b$} \markbox{14559}{in} \markbox{14560}{any} \markbox{14561}{HHS} \markbox{m14562}{$\calX$}.  \markbox{14563}{The} \markbox{14564}{goal} \markbox{14565}{is} \markbox{14566}{to} \markbox{14567}{show} \markbox{14568}{that} \markbox{14569}{if} \markbox{14570}{we} \markbox{14571}{perturb} \markbox{m14572}{$a,b$} \markbox{14573}{a} \markbox{14574}{small} \markbox{14575}{amount} \markbox{14576}{to} \markbox{14577}{a} \markbox{14578}{pair} \markbox{14579}{of} \markbox{14580}{points} \markbox{m14581}{$a',b'$} \markbox{14582}{with} \markbox{m14583}{$d_{\calX}(a,a') \leq 1$} \markbox{14584}{and} \markbox{m14585}{$d_{\calX}(b,b') \leq 1$}, \markbox{14586}{then} \markbox{14587}{we} \markbox{14588}{can} \markbox{14589}{produce} \markbox{14590}{cubical} \markbox{14591}{models} \markbox{m14592}{$\calQ$} \markbox{14593}{for} \markbox{m14594}{$a,b$} \markbox{14595}{and} \markbox{m14596}{$\calQ'$} \markbox{14597}{for} \markbox{m14598}{$a',b'$} \markbox{14599}{which} \markbox{14600}{are} \markbox{14601}{isomorphic} \markbox{14602}{up} \markbox{14603}{to} \markbox{14604}{deleting} \markbox{14605}{boundedly-many} \markbox{14606}{hyperplanes.}  \markbox{14607}{Doing} \markbox{14608}{so} \markbox{14609}{requires} \markbox{14610}{carefully} \markbox{14611}{controlling} \markbox{14612}{the} \markbox{14613}{main} \markbox{14614}{inputs} \markbox{14615}{into} \markbox{14616}{the} \markbox{14617}{cubulation} \markbox{14618}{machine---namely} \markbox{14619}{the} \markbox{14620}{families} \markbox{14621}{of} \markbox{14622}{intervals} \markbox{14623}{we} \markbox{14624}{construct} \markbox{14625}{from} \markbox{14626}{the} \markbox{14627}{projections} \markbox{14628}{of} \markbox{14629}{the} points.

The \markbox{14630}{first} \markbox{14631}{step} \markbox{14632}{in} \markbox{14633}{the} \markbox{14634}{process} \markbox{14635}{involves} \markbox{14636}{explaining} \markbox{14637}{how} \markbox{14638}{to} \markbox{14639}{gain} \markbox{14640}{control} \markbox{14641}{over} \markbox{14642}{the} \markbox{14643}{set} \markbox{14644}{of} \markbox{14645}{relevant} \markbox{14646}{domains} \markbox{14647}{(Definition} \ref{defn:relevant}) \markbox{14648}{for} \markbox{14649}{a} \markbox{14650}{pair} \markbox{14651}{of} \markbox{14652}{points} \markbox{m14653}{$F = \{a,b\} \subset \calX$} \markbox{14654}{and} \markbox{14655}{its} \markbox{14656}{perturbation} \markbox{m14657}{$F' = \{a',b'\}$}  \markbox{14658}{as} \markbox{14659}{above.}  \markbox{14660}{In} \markbox{14661}{the} \markbox{14662}{next} \markbox{14663}{sections,} \markbox{14664}{we} \markbox{14665}{explain} \markbox{14666}{how} \markbox{14667}{to} \markbox{14668}{take} \markbox{14669}{this} \markbox{14670}{projection} \markbox{14671}{data} \markbox{14672}{to} \markbox{14673}{build} \markbox{14674}{a} \markbox{14675}{family} \markbox{14676}{of} \markbox{14677}{stable} \markbox{14678}{intervals} \markbox{14679}{that} \markbox{14680}{we} \markbox{14681}{can} \markbox{14682}{plug} \markbox{14683}{into} \markbox{14684}{the} \markbox{14685}{cubulation} machine.

The \markbox{14686}{main} \markbox{14687}{bit} \markbox{14688}{of} \markbox{14689}{work} \markbox{14690}{for} \markbox{14691}{this} \markbox{14692}{first} \markbox{14693}{part} \markbox{14694}{has} \markbox{14695}{already} \markbox{14696}{been} \markbox{14697}{done} \markbox{14698}{for} \markbox{14699}{us} \markbox{14700}{by} \markbox{14701}{Bestvina--Bromberg--Fujiwara} \cite{BBF} \markbox{14702}{and} \markbox{14703}{Bestvina--Bromberg--Fujiwara--Sisto} \cite{BBFS}.  \markbox{14704}{The} \markbox{14705}{work} \markbox{14706}{we} \markbox{14707}{did} \markbox{14708}{with} \markbox{14709}{Minsky} \markbox{14710}{and} \markbox{14711}{Sisto} \markbox{14712}{in} \cite{DMS_bary} \markbox{14713}{mostly} \markbox{14714}{adapts} \markbox{14715}{their} \markbox{14716}{setup} \markbox{14717}{to} \markbox{14718}{the} \markbox{14719}{HHS} \markbox{14720}{setting,} \markbox{14721}{and} \markbox{14722}{makes} \markbox{14723}{some} \markbox{14724}{straight-forward} \markbox{14725}{but} \markbox{14726}{important} observations.

In \cite[Subsections \markbox{14727}{2.3} \markbox{14728}{and} 2.4]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{14729}{we} \markbox{14730}{were} \markbox{14731}{dealing} \markbox{14732}{with} \markbox{14733}{the} \markbox{14734}{situation} \markbox{14735}{where} \markbox{m14736}{$F,F'$} \markbox{14737}{were} \markbox{14738}{finite} \markbox{14739}{sets} \markbox{14740}{of} \markbox{14741}{points} \markbox{14742}{with} \markbox{14743}{cardinality} \markbox{14744}{possibly} \markbox{14745}{larger} \markbox{14746}{than} \markbox{m14747}{$2$}.  \markbox{14748}{Nonetheless,} \markbox{14749}{all} \markbox{14750}{of} \markbox{14751}{the} \markbox{14752}{arguments} \markbox{14753}{there} \markbox{14754}{reduce} \markbox{14755}{to} \markbox{14756}{considering} \markbox{14757}{pairs} \markbox{14758}{of} \markbox{14759}{points,} \markbox{14760}{and} \markbox{14761}{so} \markbox{14762}{the} \markbox{14763}{proofs} \markbox{14764}{for} \markbox{14765}{our} \markbox{14766}{current} \markbox{14767}{setting} \markbox{14768}{are} \markbox{14769}{essentially} \markbox{14770}{the} \markbox{14771}{same.}  \markbox{14772}{As} \markbox{14773}{such,} \markbox{14774}{we} \markbox{14775}{will} \markbox{14776}{mainly} \markbox{14777}{explain} \markbox{14778}{the} \markbox{14779}{setup} \markbox{14780}{and} \markbox{14781}{key} \markbox{14782}{statements,} \markbox{14783}{only} \markbox{14784}{giving} \markbox{14785}{minimal} \markbox{14786}{sketches} \markbox{14787}{of} proofs.

\subsection{Colorability}

The \markbox{14788}{hierarchical} \markbox{14789}{setting} \markbox{14790}{in} \markbox{14791}{which} \cite{BBFS} \markbox{14792}{works} \markbox{14793}{is} \markbox{14794}{for} \markbox{14795}{the} \markbox{14796}{following} \markbox{14797}{class,} \markbox{14798}{which} \markbox{14799}{was} \markbox{14800}{first} \markbox{14801}{defined} \markbox{14802}{in} \cite[Definition 2.8]{DMS_bary} \markbox{14803}{and} \markbox{14804}{later} \markbox{14805}{used} \markbox{14806}{in} \cite{HP_proj,Petyt_quasicube}:

\begin{definition}[Colorable HHS]\label{defn:colorable}
We \markbox{14807}{say} \markbox{14808}{that} \markbox{14809}{an} HHS
\markbox{m14810}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{14811}{is} \markbox{14812}{\emph{colorable}} \markbox{14813}{if} \markbox{14814}{there} \markbox{14815}{exists} \markbox{14816}{a} \markbox{14817}{decomposition} of
\markbox{m14818}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{14819}{into} \markbox{14820}{finitely} \markbox{14821}{many} \markbox{14822}{families} \markbox{m14823}{$\mathfrak S_i$}, \markbox{14824}{so} \markbox{14825}{that} \markbox{14826}{each} \markbox{m14827}{$\mathfrak S_i$} is
pairwise-\markbox{m14828}{$\pitchfork$}.

\begin{itemize}
\item {} We \markbox{14829}{refer} \markbox{14830}{to} \markbox{14831}{the} \markbox{m14832}{$\mathfrak S_i$} \markbox{14833}{as} \markbox{14834}{\emph{BBF families}}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}
The \markbox{14835}{notion} \markbox{14836}{of} \markbox{14837}{colorability} \markbox{14838}{was} \markbox{14839}{inspired} \markbox{14840}{by} \markbox{14841}{work} \markbox{14842}{of} \markbox{14843}{Bestvina-Bromberg-Fujiwara} \cite{BBF}, \markbox{14844}{who} \markbox{14845}{proved} \markbox{14846}{that} \markbox{14847}{the} \markbox{14848}{curve} \markbox{14849}{graph} \markbox{14850}{is} \markbox{14851}{finitely-colorable.}  \markbox{14852}{As} \markbox{14853}{a} \markbox{14854}{consequence} \markbox{14855}{of} \markbox{14856}{this,} \markbox{14857}{the} \markbox{14858}{set} \markbox{14859}{of} \markbox{14860}{subsurfaces} \markbox{14861}{of} \markbox{14862}{a} \markbox{14863}{given} \markbox{14864}{finite-type} \markbox{14865}{surface} \markbox{m14866}{$S$} \markbox{14867}{can} \markbox{14868}{be} \markbox{14869}{decomposed} \markbox{14870}{into} \markbox{14871}{finitely-many} \markbox{14872}{families} \markbox{14873}{of} \markbox{14874}{pairwise-interlocking} \markbox{14875}{subsurfaces,} \markbox{14876}{which} \markbox{14877}{the} \markbox{14878}{above} \markbox{14879}{definition} \markbox{14880}{directly} \markbox{14881}{generalizes.}  \markbox{14882}{See} \cite[Subsection 2.3]{DMS_bary} \markbox{14883}{for} \markbox{14884}{a} \markbox{14885}{detailed} \markbox{14886}{discussion} \markbox{14887}{of} \markbox{14888}{this} connection.
\end{remark}

\subsection{Stable projections}

Our \markbox{14889}{next} \markbox{14890}{goal} \markbox{14891}{is} \markbox{14892}{to} \markbox{14893}{state} \markbox{14894}{a} \markbox{14895}{theorem} \markbox{14896}{which} \markbox{14897}{equips} \markbox{14898}{any} \markbox{14899}{colorable} \markbox{14900}{HHS} \markbox{14901}{with} \markbox{14902}{a} \markbox{14903}{set} \markbox{14904}{of} \markbox{14905}{projections} \markbox{14906}{which} \markbox{14907}{satisfy} \markbox{14908}{certain} \markbox{14909}{key} \markbox{14910}{stability} \markbox{14911}{properties.}  \markbox{14912}{We} \markbox{14913}{need} \markbox{14914}{some} \markbox{14915}{definitions} first.

Given \markbox{14916}{a} \markbox{14917}{pair} \markbox{14918}{of} \markbox{14919}{points} \markbox{m14920}{$F = \{x,y\} \subset \calX$} \markbox{14921}{and} \markbox{m14922}{$K>0$}, \markbox{14923}{we} \markbox{14924}{let} \markbox{m14925}{$\calU(F) = \Rel_K(F)$}.  \markbox{14926}{If} \markbox{m14927}{$V \in \calU(F)$}, \markbox{14928}{then} \markbox{14929}{we} \markbox{14930}{let} \markbox{m14931}{$\calU^V(F) = \{W \in \calU(F) | W \sqsubsetneq V\}$}.

The \markbox{14932}{following} \markbox{14933}{definition} \cite[Definition 2.13]{DMS_bary} \markbox{14934}{describes} \markbox{14935}{the} \markbox{14936}{domains} \markbox{14937}{we} \markbox{14938}{want} \markbox{14939}{to} \markbox{14940}{control} \markbox{14941}{when} \markbox{14942}{perturbing} \markbox{m14943}{$F$}:

\begin{definition}[Involved domains]\label{defn:involved}
Let \markbox{m14944}{$F = \{x,y\}, F' = \{x', y'\} \subset \calX$} \markbox{14945}{be} \markbox{14946}{so} \markbox{14947}{that} \markbox{m14948}{$d_{\calX}(x,x') \leq 1 $} \markbox{14949}{and} \markbox{m14950}{$d_{\calX}(y,y') \leq 1$}.  \markbox{14951}{For} \markbox{m14952}{$K>0$}, \markbox{14953}{we} \markbox{14954}{say} \markbox{14955}{that} \markbox{m14956}{$V \in \calU(F) \cup \calU(F')$} \markbox{14957}{is} \markbox{14958}{\emph{involved in the transition}} \markbox{14959}{between} \markbox{m14960}{$F$} \markbox{14961}{and} \markbox{m14962}{$F'$} \markbox{14963}{if} \markbox{14964}{one} \markbox{14965}{of} \markbox{14966}{the} \markbox{14967}{following} holds:

\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m14968}{$\pi_V(F) \neq \pi_V(F')$}.
\item {} \markbox{m14969}{$\calU^V(F) \neq \calU^V(F')$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

The \markbox{14970}{following,} \markbox{14971}{which} \markbox{14972}{combines} \markbox{14973}{the} \markbox{14974}{statements} \markbox{14975}{of} \cite[Theorem \markbox{14976}{2.9} \markbox{14977}{and} \markbox{14978}{Proposition} 2.14]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{14979}{states} \markbox{14980}{that,} \markbox{14981}{for} \markbox{14982}{any} \markbox{14983}{colorable} \markbox{14984}{HHS} \markbox{m14985}{$\calX$}, \markbox{14986}{we} \markbox{14987}{can} \markbox{14988}{replace} \markbox{14989}{its} \markbox{14990}{given} \markbox{14991}{projections} \markbox{14992}{with} \markbox{14993}{coarsely} \markbox{14994}{equivalent} \markbox{14995}{projections} \markbox{14996}{with} \markbox{14997}{which} \markbox{14998}{we} \markbox{14999}{can} \markbox{15000}{control} \markbox{15001}{involved} \markbox{15002}{domains} \markbox{15003}{up} \markbox{15004}{to} \markbox{15005}{a} \markbox{15006}{bounded} error:

\begin{theorem}\label{thm:controlling domains}
Let \markbox{m15007}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{15008}{be} \markbox{15009}{a} \markbox{15010}{colorable} \markbox{15011}{HHS} \markbox{15012}{with} \markbox{15013}{standard} \markbox{15014}{projections} \markbox{m15015}{$\hat{\pi}_{-}, \hat{\rho}^{-}_{-}$}.  \markbox{15016}{Then} \markbox{15017}{there} \markbox{15018}{exists} \markbox{m15019}{$\theta>0$} \markbox{15020}{and} \markbox{15021}{new} \markbox{15022}{projections} \markbox{m15023}{$\pi_{-}, \rho^{-}_{-}$} \markbox{15024}{with} \markbox{15025}{the} \markbox{15026}{same} \markbox{15027}{domains} \markbox{15028}{and} \markbox{15029}{ranges,} \markbox{15030}{respectively,} \markbox{15031}{such} \markbox{15032}{that} \markbox{15033}{the} \markbox{15034}{following} hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item {} The \markbox{15035}{new} \markbox{15036}{projections} \markbox{m15037}{$\pi_{-}, \rho^{-}_{-}$} \markbox{15038}{coarsely} \markbox{15039}{coincide} \markbox{15040}{with} \markbox{15041}{the} \markbox{15042}{old} \markbox{15043}{ones} \markbox{m15044}{$\hat{\pi}_{-}, \hat{\rho}^{-}_{-}$}.  \markbox{15045}{More} precisely:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} If \markbox{m15046}{$X,Y$} \markbox{15047}{lie} \markbox{15048}{in} \markbox{15049}{different} \markbox{m15050}{$\mathfrak S_j$} \markbox{15051}{and} \markbox{m15052}{$\hat{\rho}^X_Y$} \markbox{15053}{is} \markbox{15054}{defined,} \markbox{15055}{then} \markbox{m15056}{$\rho^X_Y = \hat{\rho}^X_Y$}.
\item {} If \markbox{m15057}{$X,Y \in \mathfrak S_j$}, \markbox{15058}{then} \markbox{m15059}{$d^{Haus}_{Y}(\rho^X_Y, \hat{\rho}^X_Y)<\theta.$}
\item {} If \markbox{m15060}{$x \in \calX$} \markbox{15061}{and} \markbox{m15062}{$Y \in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{15063}{then} \markbox{m15064}{$d^{Haus}_Y(\pi_Y(x),\hat{\pi}_Y(x))<\theta$}.
\end{enumerate}
\item {} There \markbox{15065}{exists} \markbox{m15066}{$K_0 = K_0(\calX)>0$} \markbox{15067}{and} \markbox{m15068}{$N_0(\calX)>0$} \markbox{15069}{so} \markbox{15070}{that} \markbox{15071}{if} \markbox{m15072}{$K>K_0$}, \markbox{15073}{then} \markbox{15074}{the} \markbox{15075}{following} \markbox{15076}{holds.}  \markbox{15077}{Let} \markbox{m15078}{$x,y,x',y' \in \calX$} \markbox{15079}{with} \markbox{m15080}{$d_{\calX}(x,x') \leq 1 $} \markbox{15081}{and} \markbox{m15082}{$d_{\calX}(y,y') \leq 1$}, \markbox{15083}{and} \markbox{15084}{let} \markbox{m15085}{$\calU = \Rel_K(\{x,y\})$} \markbox{15086}{and} \markbox{m15087}{$\calU' = \Rel_K(\{x',y'\})$} \markbox{15088}{be} \markbox{15089}{the} \markbox{15090}{relevant} \markbox{15091}{sets} \markbox{15092}{for} \markbox{15093}{the} \markbox{15094}{new} \markbox{15095}{projections} \markbox{m15096}{$\pi_-$}.  Then:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m15097}{$\#(\calU \triangle \calU') < N_0$}, \markbox{15098}{and} \markbox{15099}{if} \markbox{m15100}{$V \in \calU \triangle \calU'$}, \markbox{15101}{then} \markbox{m15102}{$d_V(x,y) \prec K$} \markbox{15103}{and} \markbox{m15104}{$d_V(x',y') \prec K$}. \label{item:bounded symdiff}
\item  {} There \markbox{15105}{are} \markbox{15106}{at} \markbox{15107}{most} \markbox{m15108}{$N_0$} \markbox{15109}{domains} \markbox{m15110}{$V \in \calU(F) \cup \calU(F')$} \markbox{15111}{involved} \markbox{15112}{in} \markbox{15113}{the} \markbox{15114}{transition} \markbox{15115}{between} \markbox{m15116}{$F$} \markbox{15117}{and} \markbox{m15118}{$F'$}. \label{item:bounded involved}
\end{enumerate}
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}[Sketch \markbox{15119}{of} proof]
The \markbox{15120}{existence} \markbox{15121}{of} \markbox{15122}{new} \markbox{15123}{projections} \markbox{15124}{satisfying} \markbox{15125}{the} \markbox{15126}{conditions} \markbox{15127}{of} \markbox{15128}{item} \markbox{15129}{(1)} \markbox{15130}{is} \markbox{15131}{essentially} \markbox{15132}{an} \markbox{15133}{immediate} \markbox{15134}{consequence} \markbox{15135}{of} \markbox{15136}{the} \markbox{15137}{construction} \markbox{15138}{in} \cite[Theorem 4.1]{BBFS}.  \markbox{15139}{Item} \markbox{15140}{(2),} \markbox{15141}{which} \markbox{15142}{regards} \markbox{15143}{stability} \markbox{15144}{of} \markbox{15145}{the} \markbox{15146}{relevant} \markbox{15147}{sets} \markbox{m15148}{$\calU, \calU'$}, \markbox{15149}{requires} \markbox{15150}{a} \markbox{15151}{bit} \markbox{15152}{more} \markbox{15153}{work,} \markbox{15154}{but} \markbox{15155}{the} \markbox{15156}{key} \markbox{15157}{ideas} \markbox{15158}{are} \markbox{15159}{as} follows:

Using \cite[Proposition 2.8]{HHS_II} \markbox{15160}{(which} \markbox{15161}{generalizes} \cite{CLM12, BKMM:qirigid, BBF}), \markbox{15162}{there} \markbox{15163}{is} \markbox{15164}{a} \markbox{15165}{partial} \markbox{15166}{order} \markbox{m15167}{$\prec$} \markbox{15168}{on} \markbox{m15169}{$\Rel(x,y)$}, \markbox{15170}{which} \markbox{15171}{becomes} \markbox{15172}{a} \markbox{15173}{total} \markbox{15174}{order} \markbox{15175}{on} \markbox{m15176}{$\Rel^i(x,y) = \Rel_K(x,y) \cap \mathfrak S_i$} \markbox{15177}{for} \markbox{15178}{each} \markbox{m15179}{$i$}.  \markbox{15180}{In} \markbox{15181}{particular,} \markbox{15182}{we} \markbox{15183}{can} \markbox{15184}{think} \markbox{15185}{of} \markbox{15186}{each} \markbox{m15187}{$\Rel^i(x,y)$} \markbox{15188}{as} \markbox{15189}{an} \markbox{15190}{interval} \markbox{m15191}{$X_1 \prec \cdots \prec X_n$}.  \markbox{15192}{One} \markbox{15193}{of} \markbox{15194}{the} \markbox{15195}{additional} \markbox{15196}{properties} \markbox{15197}{that} \markbox{15198}{the} \markbox{15199}{new} \markbox{15200}{projections} \markbox{m15201}{$\pi_{-}, \rho^{-}_{-}$} \markbox{15202}{satisfy} \markbox{15203}{(see} \cite[Theorem 2.9]{DMS_bary}) \markbox{15204}{is} \markbox{15205}{that} \markbox{15206}{if} \markbox{m15207}{$X \prec Y$} \markbox{15208}{along} \markbox{15209}{both} \markbox{m15210}{$\Rel(x,y)$} \markbox{15211}{and} \markbox{m15212}{$\Rel(x',y')$}, \markbox{15213}{then} \markbox{m15214}{$\pi_Y(x) = \pi_Y(x') = \rho^X_Y$} \markbox{15215}{and} \markbox{m15216}{$\pi_X(y) = \pi_X(y') = \rho^Y_X$}.  \markbox{15217}{Using} \markbox{15218}{this,} \markbox{15219}{one} \markbox{15220}{can} \markbox{15221}{show} \markbox{15222}{that} \markbox{m15223}{$\Rel(x,y)$} \markbox{15224}{and} \markbox{m15225}{$\Rel(x',y')$} \markbox{15226}{can} \markbox{15227}{only} \markbox{15228}{differ} \markbox{15229}{at} \markbox{15230}{their} \markbox{15231}{first} \markbox{15232}{or} \markbox{15233}{last} \markbox{15234}{elements} \markbox{15235}{in} \markbox{15236}{the} \markbox{15237}{order} \markbox{m15238}{$\prec$}.  \markbox{15239}{Hence} \markbox{m15240}{$\#\left(\Rel^i(x,y) \triangle \Rel^i(x',y')\right) \leq 4$}; \markbox{15241}{see} \cite[Lemma \markbox{15242}{2.11} \markbox{15243}{and} \markbox{15244}{Proposition} 2.12]{DMS_bary}.  \markbox{15245}{Since} \markbox{15246}{there} \markbox{15247}{are} \markbox{15248}{only} \markbox{15249}{boundedly-many} \markbox{15250}{BBF} \markbox{15251}{families} \markbox{m15252}{$\mathfrak S_i$}, \markbox{15253}{item} \eqref{item:bounded symdiff} \markbox{15254}{follows} easily.

A \markbox{15255}{similar} \markbox{15256}{argument} \markbox{15257}{can} \markbox{15258}{now} \markbox{15259}{be} \markbox{15260}{used} \markbox{15261}{to} \markbox{15262}{control} \markbox{15263}{the} \markbox{15264}{number} \markbox{15265}{of} \markbox{15266}{involved} \markbox{15267}{domains} \markbox{15268}{of} \markbox{15269}{type} \markbox{15270}{(1)} \markbox{15271}{of} \markbox{15272}{Definition} \ref{defn:involved}, \markbox{15273}{see} \markbox{15274}{the} \markbox{15275}{proof} \markbox{15276}{of} \cite[Proposition 2.14]{DMS_bary}.  \markbox{15277}{For} \markbox{15278}{involved} \markbox{15279}{domains} \markbox{15280}{of} \markbox{15281}{type} \markbox{15282}{(2),} \markbox{15283}{this} \markbox{15284}{is} \markbox{15285}{an} \markbox{15286}{immediate} \markbox{15287}{consequence} \markbox{15288}{of} \markbox{15289}{item} \eqref{item:bounded symdiff} \markbox{15290}{and} \markbox{15291}{the} \markbox{15292}{Covering} \markbox{15293}{Lemma} \ref{lem:covering}, \markbox{15294}{which} \markbox{15295}{bounds} \markbox{15296}{the} \markbox{15297}{number} \markbox{15298}{of} \markbox{15299}{domains} \markbox{m15300}{$W \in \calU$} \markbox{15301}{into} \markbox{15302}{which} \markbox{15303}{a} \markbox{15304}{given} \markbox{m15305}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{15306}{can} nest.
\end{proof}





\section{Stable Intervals}\label{sec:stable intervals}

With \markbox{15307}{the} \markbox{15308}{new} \markbox{15309}{HHS} \markbox{15310}{projections} \markbox{15311}{provided} \markbox{15312}{by} \markbox{15313}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains}, \markbox{15314}{we} \markbox{15315}{now} \markbox{15316}{turn} \markbox{15317}{toward} \markbox{15318}{converting} \markbox{15319}{stabilized} \markbox{15320}{projection} \markbox{15321}{data} \markbox{15322}{into} \markbox{15323}{stable} \markbox{15324}{families} \markbox{15325}{of} \markbox{15326}{intervals,} \markbox{15327}{in} \markbox{15328}{partivuvlar} \markbox{15329}{stabilizing} \markbox{15330}{the} \markbox{15331}{input} \markbox{15332}{into} \markbox{15333}{the} \markbox{15334}{cubical} \markbox{15335}{model} \markbox{15336}{construction} \markbox{15337}{from} \markbox{15338}{Section} \ref{sec:interval systems}.


Our \markbox{15339}{ultimate} \markbox{15340}{goal} \markbox{15341}{is} \markbox{15342}{to} \markbox{15343}{produce} \markbox{15344}{cubical} \markbox{15345}{models} \markbox{15346}{for} \markbox{15347}{pairs} \markbox{15348}{of} \markbox{15349}{nearby} \markbox{15350}{points} \markbox{15351}{that} \markbox{15352}{differ} \markbox{15353}{by} \markbox{15354}{a} \markbox{15355}{controlled} \markbox{15356}{number} \markbox{15357}{of} \markbox{15358}{hyperplane} \markbox{15359}{deletions} \markbox{15360}{(Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}). \markbox{15361}{Since} \markbox{15362}{the} \markbox{15363}{hyperplanes} \markbox{15364}{in} \markbox{15365}{the} \markbox{15366}{cubical} \markbox{15367}{models} \markbox{15368}{come} \markbox{15369}{from} \markbox{15370}{edges} \markbox{15371}{of} \markbox{15372}{the} \markbox{15373}{simplicial} \markbox{15374}{intervals} \markbox{15375}{in} \markbox{15376}{our} \markbox{15377}{HFIs} \markbox{15378}{(Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC}), \markbox{15379}{it} \markbox{15380}{will} \markbox{15381}{suffice} \markbox{15382}{to} \markbox{15383}{build} \markbox{15384}{HFIs} \markbox{15385}{where} \markbox{15386}{the} \markbox{15387}{intervals} \markbox{15388}{only} \markbox{15389}{differ} \markbox{15390}{by} \markbox{15391}{boundedly-many} \markbox{15392}{bounded-size} \markbox{15393}{collections} \markbox{15394}{of} \markbox{15395}{edges.}  \markbox{15396}{That} \markbox{15397}{is} \markbox{15398}{the} \markbox{15399}{content} \markbox{15400}{of} \markbox{15401}{the} \markbox{15402}{Stable} \markbox{15403}{Intervals} \markbox{15404}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.
