We \markbox{15405}{first} \markbox{15406}{explain} \markbox{15407}{the} \markbox{15408}{build-up} \markbox{15409}{to} \markbox{15410}{this} \markbox{15411}{theorem} \markbox{15412}{and} \markbox{15413}{defer} \markbox{15414}{the} \markbox{15415}{explicit} \markbox{15416}{statement.}  \markbox{15417}{We} \markbox{15418}{will} \markbox{15419}{work} \markbox{15420}{in} \markbox{15421}{the} \markbox{15422}{setting} \markbox{15423}{of} \markbox{15424}{a} \markbox{15425}{hyperbolic} \markbox{15426}{space} \markbox{15427}{with} \markbox{15428}{a} \markbox{15429}{hierarchical-like} \markbox{15430}{configuration.}  \markbox{15431}{The} \markbox{15432}{construction} \markbox{15433}{is} \markbox{15434}{a} \markbox{15435}{somewhat} \markbox{15436}{long} \markbox{15437}{and} \markbox{15438}{delicate} \markbox{15439}{exercise} \markbox{15440}{in} \markbox{15441}{hyperbolic} \markbox{15442}{geometry} \markbox{15443}{and} \markbox{15444}{we} \markbox{15445}{will} \markbox{15446}{mainly} \markbox{15447}{provide} \markbox{15448}{a} \markbox{15449}{detailed} sketch.

\subsection{Basic setup and assumptions}\label{subsec:stable setup}

For \markbox{15450}{the} \markbox{15451}{rest} \markbox{15452}{of} \markbox{15453}{this} \markbox{15454}{section,} \markbox{15455}{let} \markbox{15456}{us} \markbox{15457}{assume} \markbox{15458}{that} \markbox{m15459}{$\calZ$} \markbox{15460}{is} \markbox{15461}{a} \markbox{m15462}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic \markbox{15463}{geodesic} \markbox{15464}{space.}  \markbox{15465}{The} \markbox{15466}{first} \markbox{15467}{bit} \markbox{15468}{of} \markbox{15469}{notation} \markbox{15470}{we} \markbox{15471}{want} \markbox{15472}{to} \markbox{15473}{set} \markbox{15474}{is} \markbox{15475}{a} \markbox{15476}{choice} \markbox{15477}{of} \markbox{15478}{geodesic} \markbox{15479}{between} \markbox{15480}{any} \markbox{15481}{pair} \markbox{15482}{of} \markbox{15483}{points.}  \markbox{15484}{That} \markbox{15485}{is,} \markbox{15486}{for} \markbox{15487}{any} \markbox{m15488}{$x,y \in \calZ$}, \markbox{15489}{we} \markbox{15490}{fix} \markbox{15491}{(once} \markbox{15492}{and} \markbox{15493}{for} \markbox{15494}{all)} \markbox{15495}{a} \markbox{15496}{geodesic} \markbox{m15497}{$\lambda(x,y)$}.  \markbox{15498}{More} \markbox{15499}{generally,} \markbox{15500}{if} \markbox{m15501}{$C,C' \subset \calZ$} \markbox{15502}{are} \markbox{15503}{finite} \markbox{15504}{subsets,} \markbox{15505}{then} \markbox{15506}{we} \markbox{15507}{let} \markbox{m15508}{$\lambda(C,C')$} \markbox{15509}{denote} \markbox{15510}{a} \markbox{15511}{choice} \markbox{15512}{of} \markbox{15513}{geodesic} \markbox{15514}{between} \markbox{15515}{them} \markbox{15516}{whose} \markbox{15517}{length} \markbox{15518}{satisfies} \markbox{m15519}{$|\lambda(C,C')| = d_{\calZ}(C,C')$}, \markbox{15520}{and} \markbox{15521}{we} \markbox{15522}{require} \markbox{15523}{symmetry,} \markbox{15524}{namely} \markbox{m15525}{$\lambda(C,C') = \lambda(C',C)$}.

It \markbox{15526}{will} \markbox{15527}{also} \markbox{15528}{be} \markbox{15529}{necessary} \markbox{15530}{to} \markbox{15531}{perform} \markbox{15532}{a} \markbox{15533}{slight} \markbox{15534}{modification} \markbox{15535}{on} \markbox{15536}{the} \markbox{15537}{geodesic} \markbox{15538}{function} \markbox{m15539}{$\lambda$}, \markbox{15540}{so} \markbox{15541}{that} \markbox{15542}{its} \markbox{15543}{resulting} \markbox{15544}{length} \markbox{15545}{is} \markbox{15546}{an} \markbox{15547}{integer.}  \markbox{15548}{To} \markbox{15549}{fix} \markbox{15550}{this,} \markbox{15551}{we} \markbox{15552}{let} \markbox{m15553}{$\lambda_0(C,C')$} \markbox{15554}{denote} \markbox{15555}{the} \markbox{15556}{restriction} \markbox{15557}{of} \markbox{m15558}{$\lambda(C,C'):[0, d_{\calZ}(C,C')]\to \calZ$} \markbox{15559}{to} \markbox{15560}{the} \markbox{15561}{interval} \markbox{m15562}{$[0, \lfloor{d_{\calZ}(C,C')}\rfloor]$}.  \markbox{15563}{The} \markbox{15564}{effect} \markbox{15565}{of} \markbox{15566}{this} \markbox{15567}{is} \markbox{15568}{to} \markbox{15569}{trim} \markbox{m15570}{$\lambda(A,B)$} \markbox{15571}{so} \markbox{15572}{that} \markbox{15573}{it} \markbox{15574}{has} \markbox{15575}{positive} \markbox{15576}{integer} \markbox{15577}{length} \markbox{15578}{and} \markbox{15579}{their} \markbox{15580}{lengths} \markbox{15581}{satisfy} \markbox{m15582}{$l(\lambda(C,C')) -l(\lambda_0(C,C')) < 1$}.  \markbox{15583}{While} \markbox{15584}{not} \markbox{15585}{necessary,} \markbox{15586}{one} \markbox{15587}{could} \markbox{15588}{make} \markbox{15589}{this} \markbox{15590}{symmetric} \markbox{15591}{by} \markbox{15592}{trimming} \markbox{15593}{both} \markbox{15594}{the} \markbox{15595}{sides} \markbox{15596}{by} \markbox{15597}{half} \markbox{15598}{of} \markbox{m15599}{$l(\lambda(C,C')) -l(\lambda_0(C,C'))$}.  \markbox{15600}{In} \markbox{15601}{the} \markbox{15602}{course} \markbox{15603}{of} \markbox{15604}{the} \markbox{15605}{arguments,} \markbox{15606}{however,} \markbox{15607}{one} \markbox{15608}{can} \markbox{15609}{usually} \markbox{15610}{work} \markbox{15611}{with} \markbox{m15612}{$\lambda$} \markbox{15613}{instead} \markbox{15614}{of} \markbox{m15615}{$\lambda_0$}.

Now, \markbox{15616}{for} \markbox{15617}{the} \markbox{15618}{rest} \markbox{15619}{of} \markbox{15620}{this} \markbox{15621}{section,} \markbox{15622}{we} \markbox{15623}{fix} \markbox{15624}{a} \markbox{15625}{pair} \markbox{15626}{of} \markbox{15627}{points} \markbox{m15628}{$\{a,b\} \subset \calZ$}.  \markbox{15629}{Furthermore,} \markbox{15630}{let} \markbox{m15631}{$\calY \subset \calZ$} \markbox{15632}{be} \markbox{15633}{a} \markbox{15634}{finite} \markbox{15635}{(but} \markbox{15636}{possibly} \markbox{15637}{arbitrarily} \markbox{15638}{large)} \markbox{15639}{set} \markbox{15640}{of} \markbox{15641}{points} \markbox{15642}{of} \markbox{m15643}{$\calZ$} \markbox{15644}{and} \markbox{15645}{let} \markbox{m15646}{$\epsilon>0$} \markbox{15647}{so} \markbox{15648}{that} \markbox{m15649}{$d_{\calZ}(\lambda(a,b), y) < \epsilon/2$} \markbox{15650}{for} \markbox{15651}{all} \markbox{m15652}{$y \in \calY$}.  \markbox{15653}{We} \markbox{15654}{call} \markbox{15655}{such} \markbox{15656}{an} \markbox{15657}{arrangement} \markbox{m15658}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{15659}{an} \markbox{m15660}{$\epsilon$}-\markbox{15661}{\emph{setup}} \markbox{15662}{in} \markbox{m15663}{$\calZ$}.

In \markbox{15664}{the} \markbox{15665}{hierarchical} \markbox{15666}{setting,} \markbox{m15667}{$\calZ$} \markbox{15668}{will} \markbox{15669}{be} \markbox{15670}{one} \markbox{15671}{of} \markbox{15672}{the} \markbox{15673}{hyperbolic} \markbox{15674}{spaces} \markbox{m15675}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{15676}{for} \markbox{m15677}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{15678}{and} \markbox{15679}{the} \markbox{15680}{points} \markbox{m15681}{$\calY$} \markbox{15682}{will} \markbox{15683}{be} \markbox{15684}{the} \markbox{15685}{points} \markbox{15686}{in} \markbox{m15687}{$\rho^V_U$} \markbox{15688}{for} \markbox{m15689}{$V \nest U \in \calU$}.  \markbox{15690}{The} \markbox{15691}{proximity} \markbox{15692}{condition} \markbox{15693}{of} \markbox{15694}{the} \markbox{15695}{points} \markbox{15696}{in} \markbox{m15697}{$\calY$} \markbox{15698}{to} \markbox{m15699}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{15700}{comes} \markbox{15701}{from} \markbox{15702}{BGIA} \ref{ax:BGIA}.

\begin{notation}[\markbox{m15703}{$O(\epsilon)$}-notation]
In \markbox{15704}{this} \markbox{15705}{section,} \markbox{15706}{we} \markbox{15707}{will} \markbox{15708}{often} \markbox{15709}{want} \markbox{15710}{to} \markbox{15711}{get} \markbox{15712}{controlled} \markbox{15713}{bounds} \markbox{15714}{over} \markbox{15715}{various} \markbox{15716}{distance} \markbox{15717}{quantities,} \markbox{15718}{where} \markbox{15719}{the} \markbox{15720}{bounds} \markbox{15721}{will} \markbox{15722}{depend} \markbox{15723}{on} \markbox{15724}{our} \markbox{15725}{choice} \markbox{15726}{of} \markbox{m15727}{$\epsilon$} \markbox{15728}{and} \markbox{15729}{the} \markbox{15730}{hyperbolicity} \markbox{15731}{constant} \markbox{m15732}{$\delta$} \markbox{15733}{for} \markbox{m15734}{$\calZ$}.  \markbox{15735}{When} \markbox{15736}{a} \markbox{15737}{number} \markbox{m15738}{$A$} \markbox{15739}{is} \markbox{15740}{bounded} \markbox{15741}{above} \markbox{15742}{as} \markbox{15743}{a} \markbox{15744}{function} \markbox{15745}{of} \markbox{m15746}{$\epsilon, \delta$}, \markbox{15747}{we} \markbox{15748}{will} \markbox{15749}{simply} \markbox{15750}{write} 
$$A < O(\epsilon),$$
since \markbox{m15751}{$\delta$} \markbox{15752}{is} \markbox{15753}{given} \markbox{15754}{to} \markbox{15755}{us,} \markbox{15756}{while} \markbox{15757}{we} \markbox{15758}{need} \markbox{15759}{some} \markbox{15760}{flexibility} \markbox{15761}{to} \markbox{15762}{choose} \markbox{m15763}{$\epsilon$}.
\end{notation}

The \markbox{15764}{following} \markbox{15765}{lemma,} \markbox{15766}{which} \markbox{15767}{is} \markbox{15768}{essentially} \markbox{15769}{a} \markbox{15770}{consequence} \markbox{15771}{of} \markbox{15772}{the} \markbox{15773}{Morse} \markbox{15774}{Lemma} \markbox{15775}{for} \markbox{15776}{hyperbolic} \markbox{15777}{spaces,} \markbox{15778}{gives} \markbox{15779}{us} \markbox{15780}{control} \markbox{15781}{over} \markbox{15782}{how} \markbox{15783}{far} \markbox{m15784}{$\lambda(C,C')$} \markbox{15785}{can} \markbox{15786}{get} \markbox{15787}{from} \markbox{m15788}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{15789}{when} \markbox{m15790}{$C, C' \subset \calY$}, \markbox{15791}{and} \markbox{15792}{are} \markbox{15793}{thus} \markbox{m15794}{$\epsilon$}-close \markbox{15795}{to} \markbox{m15796}{$\lambda(a,b)$}:

\begin{lemma}[Fellow-traveling, \markbox{m15797}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic]\label{lem:Morse close}
Let \markbox{m15798}{$\calZ$} \markbox{15799}{be} \markbox{m15800}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic \markbox{15801}{and} \markbox{15802}{geodesic,} \markbox{15803}{and} \markbox{m15804}{$\gamma$} \markbox{15805}{a} \markbox{15806}{geodesic} \markbox{15807}{between} \markbox{m15808}{$a,b \in \calZ$}.  \markbox{15809}{For} \markbox{15810}{every} \markbox{m15811}{$\epsilon>0$} \markbox{15812}{there} \markbox{15813}{exists} \markbox{m15814}{$\epsilon'=O(\epsilon)>0$} \markbox{15815}{so} \markbox{15816}{that} \markbox{15817}{the} \markbox{15818}{following} holds:

\begin{itemize}
\item {} Suppose \markbox{m15819}{$\gamma'$} \markbox{15820}{is} \markbox{15821}{a} \markbox{15822}{geodesic} \markbox{15823}{connecting} \markbox{15824}{points} \markbox{m15825}{$x,y \in \calN_{\epsilon}(\gamma)$}, \markbox{15826}{and} \markbox{15827}{that} \markbox{m15828}{$x',y'$} \markbox{15829}{are} \markbox{15830}{closest} \markbox{15831}{points} \markbox{15832}{to} \markbox{m15833}{$x,y$} \markbox{15834}{on} \markbox{m15835}{$\gamma$}, \markbox{15836}{respectively.}  \markbox{15837}{Then} \markbox{15838}{any} \markbox{15839}{geodesic} \markbox{m15840}{$[x,y]$} \markbox{15841}{satisfies} \markbox{m15842}{$d_{\calZ}^{Haus}([x,y], [x',y']) < \epsilon'$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{lemma}

As \markbox{15843}{a} \markbox{15844}{consequence,} \markbox{15845}{if} \markbox{m15846}{$C, C' \subset \calY$} \markbox{15847}{are} \markbox{15848}{finite} \markbox{15849}{subsets,} \markbox{15850}{then} \markbox{m15851}{$\lambda(C,C') \subset \calN_{\epsilon'}(\lambda(a,b))$}.  \markbox{15852}{Finally,} \markbox{15853}{it} \markbox{15854}{will} \markbox{15855}{be} \markbox{15856}{convenient} \markbox{15857}{for} \markbox{15858}{us} \markbox{15859}{to} \markbox{15860}{assume} \markbox{15861}{that} \markbox{m15862}{$\epsilon' > \epsilon$}.



  
\subsection{Clusters and the cluster graph} \label{subsec:clusters}

Our \markbox{15863}{first} \markbox{15864}{goal} \markbox{15865}{is} \markbox{15866}{to} \markbox{15867}{group} \markbox{15868}{the} \markbox{15869}{points} \markbox{15870}{of} \markbox{m15871}{$\calY$} \markbox{15872}{into} \markbox{15873}{\emph{clusters}} \markbox{15874}{of} \markbox{15875}{nearby} \markbox{15876}{sets.}  \markbox{15877}{To} \markbox{15878}{that} \markbox{15879}{end,} \markbox{15880}{let} \markbox{m15881}{$E = E(\epsilon)> \epsilon$} \markbox{15882}{be} \markbox{15883}{sufficiently} \markbox{15884}{large,} \markbox{15885}{to} \markbox{15886}{be} \markbox{15887}{determined} below.

Let \markbox{m15888}{$\calC_E$} \markbox{15889}{denote} \markbox{15890}{the} \markbox{15891}{graph} \markbox{15892}{whose} \markbox{15893}{vertices} \markbox{15894}{are} \markbox{15895}{points} \markbox{15896}{of} \markbox{m15897}{$\calY \cup \{a,b\}$}, \markbox{15898}{with} \markbox{15899}{two} \markbox{15900}{points} \markbox{m15901}{$x,y \in \calY \cup \{a,b\}$} \markbox{15902}{connected} \markbox{15903}{by} \markbox{15904}{an} \markbox{15905}{edge} \markbox{15906}{exactly} \markbox{15907}{when} \markbox{m15908}{$d_{\calZ}(x,y) < E$}.  \markbox{15909}{The} \markbox{15910}{connected} \markbox{15911}{components} \markbox{15912}{of} \markbox{m15913}{$\calC_E$} \markbox{15914}{are} \markbox{15915}{called} \markbox{m15916}{$E$}-\markbox{15917}{\emph{clusters}}, \markbox{15918}{or} \markbox{15919}{simply} \markbox{15920}{\emph{clusters}} \markbox{15921}{when} \markbox{m15922}{$E$} \markbox{15923}{is} fixed.

For \markbox{15924}{any} \markbox{m15925}{$E$}-cluster \markbox{m15926}{$C$}, \markbox{15927}{let} \markbox{m15928}{$s(C) = \hull_{\lambda(a,b)}(p_{\lambda(a,b)}(C))$} \markbox{15929}{denote} \markbox{15930}{the} \markbox{15931}{hull} \markbox{15932}{(in} \markbox{m15933}{$\lambda(a,b)$}) \markbox{15934}{of} \markbox{15935}{the} \markbox{15936}{closest} \markbox{15937}{point} \markbox{15938}{projection} \markbox{15939}{of} \markbox{m15940}{$C$} \markbox{15941}{to} \markbox{m15942}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{15943}{The} \markbox{15944}{set} \markbox{m15945}{$s(C)$} \markbox{15946}{is} \markbox{15947}{called} \markbox{15948}{the} \markbox{15949}{\emph{shadow}} \markbox{15950}{of} \markbox{m15951}{$C$} \markbox{15952}{on} \markbox{m15953}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.

The \markbox{15954}{following} \markbox{15955}{lemma} \markbox{15956}{controls} \markbox{15957}{how} \markbox{15958}{shadows} \markbox{15959}{of} \markbox{15960}{clusters} \markbox{15961}{are} \markbox{15962}{arranged} \markbox{15963}{along} \markbox{m15964}{$\lambda(a,b)$}. \markbox{15965}{Its} \markbox{15966}{proof} \markbox{15967}{is} \markbox{15968}{straightforward} \markbox{15969}{(see} \cite[Lemma 3.6]{DMS_bary}), \markbox{15970}{so} \markbox{15971}{we} \markbox{15972}{leave} \markbox{15973}{it} \markbox{15974}{to} \markbox{15975}{the} \markbox{15976}{reader} \markbox{15977}{to} \markbox{15978}{check} (:

\begin{lemma} \label{lem:cluster arrangement}
If \markbox{m15979}{$E > 5\epsilon$} \markbox{15980}{and} \markbox{m15981}{$C \neq C'$} \markbox{15982}{are} \markbox{15983}{distinct} \markbox{m15984}{$E$}-clusters, \markbox{15985}{then} \markbox{m15986}{$s(C) \cap s(C') = \emptyset$}.
\end{lemma}




In \markbox{15987}{what} \markbox{15988}{follows,} \markbox{15989}{we} \markbox{15990}{will} \markbox{15991}{need} \markbox{15992}{to} \markbox{15993}{adjust} \markbox{15994}{the} \markbox{15995}{cluster} \markbox{15996}{constant} \markbox{m15997}{$E$} \markbox{15998}{a} \markbox{15999}{number} \markbox{16000}{of} \markbox{16001}{times,} \markbox{16002}{but} \markbox{16003}{we} \markbox{16004}{will} \markbox{16005}{usually} \markbox{16006}{omit} \markbox{16007}{the} \markbox{16008}{constant} \markbox{16009}{and} \markbox{16010}{refer} \markbox{16011}{to} \markbox{16012}{them} \markbox{16013}{simply} \markbox{16014}{as} clusters.

We \markbox{16015}{now} \markbox{16016}{can} \markbox{16017}{define} \markbox{16018}{our} \markbox{16019}{notion} \markbox{16020}{of} \markbox{16021}{cluster} \markbox{16022}{separation} \markbox{16023}{using} \markbox{16024}{Lemma} \ref{lem:Morse close}.  \markbox{16025}{The} \markbox{16026}{idea} \markbox{16027}{here} \markbox{16028}{is} \markbox{16029}{that} \markbox{16030}{clusters} \markbox{16031}{are} \markbox{m16032}{$\epsilon$}-close \markbox{16033}{to} \markbox{m16034}{$\lambda(a,b)$}, \markbox{16035}{and} \markbox{16036}{hence} \markbox{16037}{geodesics} \markbox{16038}{connecting} \markbox{16039}{them} \markbox{16040}{stay} \markbox{m16041}{$\epsilon'$}-close \markbox{16042}{to} \markbox{m16043}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{16044}{by} \markbox{16045}{Lemma} \ref{lem:Morse close}.

\begin{definition}
Let \markbox{m16046}{$C_1, C_2, C_3$} \markbox{16047}{be} \markbox{16048}{clusters.}  \markbox{16049}{Given} \markbox{m16050}{$\epsilon'>0$}, \markbox{16051}{we} \markbox{16052}{say} \markbox{m16053}{$C_2$} \markbox{m16054}{$\epsilon'$}-\markbox{16055}{\emph{separates}} \markbox{m16056}{$C_1$} \markbox{16057}{from} \markbox{m16058}{$C_3$} \markbox{16059}{if} \markbox{16060}{there} \markbox{16061}{exists} \markbox{16062}{a} \markbox{16063}{minimal} \markbox{16064}{length} \markbox{16065}{geodesic} \markbox{16066}{connecting} \markbox{m16067}{$C_1$} \markbox{16068}{to} \markbox{m16069}{$C_3$} \markbox{16070}{which} \markbox{16071}{passes} \markbox{16072}{within} \markbox{m16073}{$2\epsilon'$} \markbox{16074}{of} \markbox{m16075}{$C_2$}.

\begin{itemize}
\item {} Given \markbox{m16076}{$E>0$}, \markbox{16077}{the} \markbox{16078}{\emph{$E$-cluster separation graph}} \markbox{16079}{for} \markbox{m16080}{$(a,b; \calY)$}, \markbox{16081}{denoted} \markbox{m16082}{$\calG_E = \calG_{E,\epsilon'}(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{16083}{is} \markbox{16084}{defined} \markbox{16085}{as} \markbox{16086}{follows:} \markbox{16087}{The} \markbox{16088}{vertices} \markbox{16089}{of} \markbox{m16090}{$\calG_E$} \markbox{16091}{are} \markbox{16092}{clusters,} \markbox{16093}{and} \markbox{16094}{two} \markbox{16095}{vertices} \markbox{16096}{are} \markbox{16097}{connected} \markbox{16098}{by} \markbox{16099}{an} \markbox{16100}{edge} \markbox{16101}{if} \markbox{16102}{and} \markbox{16103}{only} \markbox{16104}{if} \markbox{16105}{they} \markbox{16106}{are} \markbox{16107}{not} \markbox{m16108}{$2\epsilon'$}-separated \markbox{16109}{by} \markbox{16110}{another} cluster.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}


The \markbox{16111}{following} \markbox{16112}{is} \markbox{16113}{essentially} \markbox{16114}{a} \markbox{16115}{consequence} \markbox{16116}{of} \markbox{16117}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster arrangement}.  \markbox{16118}{It} \markbox{16119}{states} \markbox{16120}{that} \markbox{16121}{the} \markbox{16122}{cluster} \markbox{16123}{graph} \markbox{16124}{is} \markbox{16125}{an} \markbox{16126}{interval} \markbox{16127}{with} \markbox{16128}{the} \markbox{16129}{order} \markbox{16130}{of} \markbox{16131}{vertices} \markbox{16132}{corresponding} \markbox{16133}{to} \markbox{16134}{the} \markbox{16135}{order} \markbox{16136}{of} \markbox{16137}{the} \markbox{16138}{cluster} \markbox{16139}{shadows} \markbox{16140}{along} \markbox{m16141}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{16142}{We} \markbox{16143}{omit} \markbox{16144}{its} \markbox{16145}{proof,} \markbox{16146}{which} \markbox{16147}{uses} \markbox{16148}{only} \markbox{16149}{hyperbolic} \markbox{16150}{geometry} \markbox{16151}{and} \markbox{16152}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster arrangement}.


\begin{proposition}\label{prop:cluster sep graph}
Let \markbox{m16153}{$\calZ$} \markbox{16154}{be} \markbox{m16155}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic, \markbox{m16156}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{16157}{a} \markbox{16158}{geodesic} \markbox{16159}{connecting} \markbox{m16160}{$a,b \in \calZ$}, \markbox{16161}{and} \markbox{m16162}{$\calY \subset \calZ$} \markbox{16163}{finite} \markbox{16164}{with} \markbox{m16165}{$\calY \subset \calN_{\epsilon}(\lambda(a,b))$}.  \markbox{16166}{Also} \markbox{16167}{let} \markbox{m16168}{$\epsilon' = \epsilon'(\epsilon, \delta)>0$} \markbox{16169}{as} \markbox{16170}{in} \markbox{16171}{Lemma} \ref{lem:Morse close}, \markbox{16172}{with} \markbox{16173}{also} \markbox{m16174}{$\epsilon' > \epsilon$}.

There \markbox{16175}{exists} \markbox{m16176}{$E = E(\epsilon, \delta)>0$} \markbox{16177}{so} \markbox{16178}{that} \markbox{16179}{the} \markbox{m16180}{$E$}-cluster \markbox{16181}{separation} \markbox{16182}{graph} \markbox{m16183}{$\calG_{E,\epsilon'}(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{16184}{is} \markbox{16185}{an} \markbox{16186}{interval} \markbox{16187}{whose} \markbox{16188}{order} \markbox{16189}{coincides} \markbox{16190}{with} \markbox{16191}{the} \markbox{16192}{order} \markbox{16193}{of} \markbox{16194}{cluster} \markbox{16195}{shadows} \markbox{16196}{along} \markbox{m16197}{$\lambda(a,b)$}, \markbox{16198}{with} \markbox{16199}{the} \markbox{16200}{endpoint} \markbox{16201}{clusters} \markbox{16202}{containing} \markbox{m16203}{$a,b$}, \markbox{16204}{respectively.} 
\end{proposition}



\subsection{Stable intervals defined}

We \markbox{16205}{are} \markbox{16206}{now} \markbox{16207}{ready} \markbox{16208}{to} \markbox{16209}{describe} \markbox{16210}{the} \markbox{16211}{stable} intervals.

By \markbox{16212}{Proposition} \ref{prop:cluster sep graph}, \markbox{16213}{the} \markbox{16214}{cluster} \markbox{16215}{separation} \markbox{16216}{graph} \markbox{16217}{is} \markbox{16218}{an} \markbox{16219}{interval.}  \markbox{16220}{Our} \markbox{16221}{stable} \markbox{16222}{intervals} \markbox{16223}{admit} \markbox{16224}{a} \markbox{16225}{decomposition} \markbox{16226}{into} \markbox{16227}{two} \markbox{16228}{families} \markbox{16229}{of} \markbox{16230}{intervals,} \markbox{16231}{namely} \markbox{16232}{of} \markbox{16233}{\emph{edge}} \markbox{16234}{components} \markbox{16235}{and} \markbox{16236}{\emph{cluster}} \markbox{16237}{components.}  \markbox{16238}{An} \markbox{16239}{edge} \markbox{16240}{component} \markbox{16241}{connects} \markbox{16242}{adjacent} \markbox{16243}{clusters} \markbox{16244}{at} \markbox{16245}{their} \markbox{16246}{nearest} \markbox{16247}{points,} \markbox{16248}{while} \markbox{16249}{a} \markbox{16250}{cluster} \markbox{16251}{component} \markbox{16252}{connects} \markbox{16253}{the} \markbox{16254}{endpoints} \markbox{16255}{of}  \markbox{16256}{whatever} \markbox{16257}{edge} \markbox{16258}{components} \markbox{16259}{are} \markbox{16260}{connected} \markbox{16261}{to} \markbox{16262}{a} \markbox{16263}{given} cluster.

\begin{definition}[Stable interval]\label{defn:stable interval}
Let \markbox{m16264}{$\calZ$} \markbox{16265}{be} \markbox{m16266}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic, \markbox{m16267}{$a,b \in \calZ$} \markbox{16268}{with} \markbox{m16269}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{16270}{a} \markbox{16271}{geodesic} \markbox{16272}{connecting} \markbox{16273}{them,} \markbox{16274}{and} \markbox{m16275}{$\calY \subset \calZ$} \markbox{16276}{finite} \markbox{16277}{with} \markbox{m16278}{$\calY \subset \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a,b))$}.  \markbox{16279}{The} \markbox{16280}{\emph{stable interval}} \markbox{16281}{for} \markbox{16282}{this} \markbox{16283}{setup} \markbox{16284}{is} \markbox{16285}{the} \markbox{16286}{union} \markbox{16287}{of} \markbox{16288}{the} \markbox{16289}{following} \markbox{16290}{two} \markbox{16291}{families} \markbox{16292}{of} \markbox{16293}{geodesic} segments:

\begin{enumerate}
\item {} (Edge \markbox{16294}{components)} \markbox{16295}{For} \markbox{16296}{each} \markbox{16297}{adjacent} \markbox{16298}{pair} \markbox{16299}{of} \markbox{m16300}{$C, C'$} \markbox{16301}{of} \markbox{16302}{clusters} \markbox{16303}{in} \markbox{m16304}{$\calG = \calG_{E,\epsilon'}(a,b;\calY)$}, \markbox{16305}{the} \markbox{16306}{\emph{edge component}} \markbox{16307}{between} \markbox{16308}{them} \markbox{16309}{is} \markbox{m16310}{$\lambda_0(C,C')$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item {} The \markbox{16311}{edge} \markbox{16312}{components} \markbox{16313}{comprise} \markbox{16314}{the} \markbox{16315}{\emph{edge forest}}, \markbox{16316}{which} \markbox{16317}{we} \markbox{16318}{denote} \markbox{16319}{by} \markbox{m16320}{$T_e$}.
\end{itemize}
\item {} (Cluster \markbox{16321}{components)} \markbox{16322}{For} \markbox{16323}{each} \markbox{16324}{cluster} \markbox{m16325}{$C$}, \markbox{16326}{we} \markbox{16327}{let} \markbox{m16328}{$C_1,C_2$} \markbox{16329}{be} \markbox{16330}{the} \markbox{16331}{clusters} \markbox{16332}{adjacent} \markbox{16333}{to} \markbox{m16334}{$C$} \markbox{16335}{in} \markbox{m16336}{$\calG$}.  \markbox{16337}{Let} \markbox{m16338}{$r(C) = C \cap (\lambda(C_1,C) \cup \lambda(C,C_2) \cup \{a,b\})$}, \markbox{16339}{where} \markbox{m16340}{$\lambda(C_i,C) = \emptyset$} \markbox{16341}{if} \markbox{m16342}{$C$} \markbox{16343}{is} \markbox{16344}{an} \markbox{16345}{endpoint} \markbox{16346}{cluster,} \markbox{16347}{for} \markbox{16348}{the} \markbox{16349}{appropriate} \markbox{m16350}{$i \in \{1,2\}$}.  \markbox{16351}{The} \markbox{16352}{cluster} \markbox{m16353}{$C$} \markbox{16354}{then} \markbox{16355}{determines} \markbox{16356}{the} \markbox{16357}{\emph{cluster component}} \markbox{m16358}{$\mu(C) = \lambda(r(C))$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item {} The \markbox{16359}{cluster} \markbox{16360}{components} \markbox{16361}{comprise} \markbox{16362}{the} \markbox{16363}{\emph{cluster forest}}, \markbox{16364}{which} \markbox{16365}{we} \markbox{16366}{denote} \markbox{16367}{by} \markbox{m16368}{$T_c$}.
\end{itemize} 
\end{enumerate}

\begin{itemize}
\item {} The \markbox{16369}{\emph{stable interval}} \markbox{16370}{is}  \markbox{m16371}{$T(a,b; \calY) = T_e \sqcup T_c$}, \markbox{16372}{by} \markbox{16373}{which} \markbox{16374}{we} \markbox{16375}{mean} \markbox{16376}{the} \markbox{16377}{abstract} \markbox{16378}{union} \markbox{16379}{of} \markbox{16380}{these} \markbox{16381}{two} \markbox{16382}{forests,} \markbox{16383}{where} \markbox{16384}{we} \markbox{16385}{attach} \markbox{m16386}{$\lambda_0(C_1,C_2)$} \markbox{16387}{to} \markbox{16388}{the} \markbox{16389}{corresponding} \markbox{16390}{endpoints} \markbox{16391}{of} \markbox{m16392}{$\mu(C_1), \mu(C_2)$} \markbox{16393}{for} \markbox{16394}{adjacent} \markbox{m16395}{$C_1, C_2$} \markbox{16396}{as} \markbox{16397}{determined} \markbox{16398}{by} \markbox{m16399}{$\calG$}.
\item {} We \markbox{16400}{let} \markbox{m16401}{$\phi:T(a,b;\calY) \to \calZ$} \markbox{16402}{denote} \markbox{16403}{the} \markbox{16404}{map} \markbox{16405}{induced} \markbox{16406}{from} \markbox{16407}{the} \markbox{16408}{fact} \markbox{16409}{that} \markbox{16410}{its} \markbox{16411}{pieces} \markbox{16412}{are} \markbox{16413}{geodesics} \markbox{16414}{in} \markbox{m16415}{$\calZ$}. 
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}




\begin{remark}
    \markbox{16416}{We} \markbox{16417}{note} \markbox{16418}{that} \markbox{16419}{stable} \markbox{16420}{intervals} \markbox{16421}{are} \markbox{16422}{abstractly} \markbox{16423}{intervals,} \markbox{16424}{but} \markbox{16425}{not} \markbox{16426}{necessarily} \markbox{16427}{as} \markbox{16428}{subsets} \markbox{16429}{of} \markbox{m16430}{$\calZ$}.  \markbox{16431}{In} \markbox{16432}{particular,} \markbox{16433}{the} \markbox{16434}{points} \markbox{m16435}{$a,b$} \markbox{16436}{need} \markbox{16437}{not} \markbox{16438}{be} \markbox{16439}{the} \markbox{16440}{``endpoints''} \markbox{16441}{of} \markbox{16442}{the} \markbox{16443}{stable} \markbox{16444}{interval} \markbox{m16445}{$T$}, \markbox{16446}{either} \markbox{16447}{abstractly} \markbox{16448}{or} \markbox{16449}{in} \markbox{m16450}{$\calZ$}.  \markbox{16451}{However,} \markbox{16452}{their} \markbox{16453}{images} \markbox{16454}{in} \markbox{16455}{the} \markbox{16456}{collapsed} \markbox{16457}{stable} \markbox{16458}{interval} \markbox{16459}{will} \markbox{16460}{be} \markbox{16461}{the} \markbox{16462}{endpoints,} \markbox{16463}{see} \markbox{16464}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:collapsed stable intervals}.
\end{remark}


The \markbox{16465}{following} \markbox{16466}{lemma} \markbox{16467}{is} \markbox{16468}{the} \markbox{16469}{key} \markbox{16470}{to} \markbox{16471}{controlling} \markbox{16472}{the} \markbox{16473}{structure} \markbox{16474}{of} \markbox{m16475}{$T(a,b;\calY)$}.  \markbox{16476}{We} \markbox{16477}{omit} \markbox{16478}{its} \markbox{16479}{proof} \markbox{16480}{since} \markbox{16481}{it} \markbox{16482}{again} \markbox{16483}{uses} \markbox{16484}{only} \markbox{16485}{hyperbolic} \markbox{16486}{geometry,} \markbox{16487}{though} \markbox{16488}{see} \markbox{16489}{Figure} \ref{fig:cluster close} \markbox{16490}{for} \markbox{16491}{a} schematic:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:cluster close}
Let \markbox{m16492}{$C_1, C_2$} \markbox{16493}{be} \markbox{16494}{distinct} \markbox{16495}{clusters} \markbox{16496}{along} \markbox{m16497}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{16498}{Suppose} \markbox{16499}{that} \markbox{m16500}{$p_1 \in C_1$} \markbox{16501}{and} \markbox{m16502}{$p_2 \in C_2$} \markbox{16503}{are} \markbox{16504}{closest} \markbox{16505}{points,} \markbox{16506}{while} \markbox{m16507}{$x_1 \in s(C_1)$} \markbox{16508}{and} \markbox{m16509}{$x_2 \in s(C_2)$} \markbox{16510}{are} \markbox{16511}{closest} \markbox{16512}{points.}  \markbox{16513}{Then} \markbox{m16514}{$d_{\calZ}(x_i, p_i) \leq 7\epsilon$} \markbox{16515}{for} \markbox{m16516}{$i=1,2$}.

As \markbox{16517}{a} \markbox{16518}{consequence,} \markbox{16519}{the} \markbox{16520}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} For \markbox{16521}{distinct} \markbox{16522}{clusters} \markbox{m16523}{$C_1,C_2$}, \markbox{16524}{we} \markbox{16525}{have} \markbox{m16526}{$|d(C_1,C_2) - d(s(C_1),s(C_2))| < 14\epsilon.$}
\item {} For \markbox{16527}{any} \markbox{m16528}{$p \in T_e$}, \markbox{16529}{we} \markbox{16530}{have} \markbox{16531}{that} \markbox{m16532}{$d_{\calZ}(p, \calY \cup \{a,b\}) \leq d_{\calZ}(p, \partial T_e) + O(\epsilon).$}
\item {} For \markbox{16533}{any} \markbox{16534}{components} \markbox{m16535}{$V,W$} \markbox{16536}{of} \markbox{m16537}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$}, \markbox{16538}{we} \markbox{16539}{have} \markbox{m16540}{$\diam_{\calZ}(s(V)\cap s(W)) < O(\epsilon)$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{lemma}



\begin{figure}
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=.75\textwidth]{figures/cluster_close}
    \caption{Proof of Lemma \ref{lem:cluster close}: Clusters can have multiple pairs of closest points.  In this example, the red and pink points on $C_1$ are equidistant from their matching point on $C_2$, while the red and pink cluster points in $C_1$ are both within $7\epsilon$ of the endpoint of the shadow $s(C_1)$ nearest $s(C_2)$, and the same for the roles of $C_1,C_2$ switched.  In subsequent arguments, this will allow us to conclude that connecting points between clusters are close even after we alter the clusters.}
    \label{fig:cluster close}
\end{figure}




\begin{figure}
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=1\textwidth]{figures/pathologies.pdf}
    \caption{This figure, which is essentially \cite[Figure 11]{DMS_bary}, is an example of two phenomena.  First, the edge components of a stable interval can have bounded overlap in the space $\calZ$.  This can lead to a bounded multiplicative error in the quasi-isometric embedding $\phi:T(a,b;\calY) \to \calZ$; see item (3) of Proposition \ref{prop:stable interval structure}.  In the figure, the multiplicative constant is at least $\frac{102}{100}$.  Second, the image of $T(a,b;\calY)$ in $\calZ$ need not itself be an interval, as the clusters can form leaves on the image.}
    \label{fig:pathologies}
\end{figure}


With \markbox{16541}{the} \markbox{16542}{above} \markbox{16543}{lemma} \markbox{16544}{in} \markbox{16545}{hand,} \markbox{16546}{we} \markbox{16547}{can} \markbox{16548}{prove} \markbox{16549}{the} \markbox{16550}{following} \markbox{16551}{structural} \markbox{16552}{proposition:}                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
 
 \begin{proposition}\label{prop:stable interval structure}
 
There \markbox{16553}{exists} \markbox{m16554}{$L_0 = L_0(\delta, \epsilon)>0$} \markbox{16555}{so} \markbox{16556}{that} \markbox{16557}{the} \markbox{16558}{following} hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m16559}{$T(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{16560}{is} \markbox{16561}{an} \markbox{16562}{interval} \markbox{16563}{with} \markbox{16564}{endpoints} \markbox{16565}{contained} \markbox{16566}{in} \markbox{m16567}{$\calY \cup \{a,b\}$} \markbox{16568}{whose} \markbox{16569}{images} \markbox{16570}{in} \markbox{m16571}{$\calZ$} \markbox{16572}{are} \markbox{m16573}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{16574}{of} \markbox{m16575}{$a,b \in \calZ$}.
\item {} For \markbox{16576}{every} \markbox{16577}{cluster} \markbox{m16578}{$C$},we \markbox{16579}{have} \markbox{16580}{that} \markbox{m16581}{$d_{\calZ}^{Haus}(\mu(C), C) < L_0$} \markbox{16582}{and} \markbox{m16583}{$\phi(T_C) \subset \calN_{L_0}(\calY \cup \{a,b\})$}. 
\item {} The \markbox{16584}{map} \markbox{m16585}{$\phi:T(a,b;\calY) \to \calZ$} \markbox{16586}{is} \markbox{16587}{an} \markbox{m16588}{$(L_0,L_0)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{16589}{embedding} \markbox{16590}{with} \markbox{16591}{image} \markbox{m16592}{$L_0$}-Hausdorff \markbox{16593}{close} \markbox{16594}{to} \markbox{m16595}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.
\item {} Each \markbox{16596}{edge} \markbox{16597}{component} \markbox{16598}{of} \markbox{m16599}{$T$} \markbox{16600}{has} \markbox{16601}{positive} \markbox{16602}{integer} length.
\end{enumerate}
 \end{proposition}
 
 \begin{proof}
 
 \markbox{16603}{For} \markbox{16604}{(1),} \markbox{16605}{observe} \markbox{16606}{that} \markbox{m16607}{$T(a,b;\calZ)$} \markbox{16608}{is} \markbox{16609}{an} \markbox{16610}{interval} \markbox{16611}{by} \markbox{16612}{construction} \markbox{16613}{and} \markbox{16614}{Proposition} \ref{prop:cluster sep graph}, \markbox{16615}{and} \markbox{16616}{the} \markbox{16617}{end} \markbox{16618}{clusters} \markbox{16619}{contain} \markbox{m16620}{$a,b$}, \markbox{16621}{respectively,} \markbox{16622}{also} \markbox{16623}{by} \markbox{16624}{that} \markbox{16625}{proposition.}  \markbox{16626}{Since} \markbox{16627}{each} \markbox{16628}{cluster} \markbox{m16629}{$C \subset \calN_{E}(\lambda(a,b))$}, \markbox{16630}{if} \markbox{m16631}{$a \in C$}, \markbox{16632}{then} \markbox{16633}{the} \markbox{16634}{outer-most} \markbox{16635}{endpoint} \markbox{16636}{of} \markbox{m16637}{$\mu(C)$} \markbox{16638}{must} \markbox{16639}{be} \markbox{16640}{within} \markbox{m16641}{$E$} \markbox{16642}{of} \markbox{m16643}{$a$}, \markbox{16644}{as} required.
 
 \markbox{16645}{For} \markbox{16646}{(2),} \markbox{16647}{observe} \markbox{16648}{that} \markbox{16649}{each} \markbox{16650}{cluster} \markbox{m16651}{$C$} \markbox{16652}{is} \markbox{16653}{within} \markbox{16654}{Hausdorff} \markbox{16655}{distance} \markbox{m16656}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{16657}{of} \markbox{m16658}{$s(C)$}, \markbox{16659}{while} \markbox{16660}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close} \markbox{16661}{implies} \markbox{16662}{that} \markbox{m16663}{$\mu(C)$} \markbox{16664}{is} \markbox{16665}{within} \markbox{16666}{Hausdorff} \markbox{16667}{distance} \markbox{m16668}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{16669}{of} \markbox{m16670}{$s(C)$}.  \markbox{16671}{The} \markbox{16672}{conclusion} follows.
 
 \markbox{16673}{Item} \markbox{16674}{(3)} \markbox{16675}{is} \markbox{16676}{essentially} \markbox{16677}{a} \markbox{16678}{consequence} \markbox{16679}{of} \markbox{16680}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close} \markbox{16681}{and} \markbox{16682}{the} \markbox{16683}{construction} \markbox{16684}{as} \markbox{16685}{follows.}  \markbox{16686}{By} \markbox{16687}{Lemma} \ref{lem:Morse close}, \markbox{16688}{the} \markbox{16689}{image} \markbox{16690}{under} \markbox{16691}{the} \markbox{16692}{map} \markbox{m16693}{$\phi:T \to \calZ$} \markbox{16694}{of} \markbox{16695}{each} \markbox{16696}{component} \markbox{16697}{of} \markbox{m16698}{$T_e$} \markbox{16699}{and} \markbox{m16700}{$T_c$} \markbox{16701}{is} \markbox{16702}{within} \markbox{m16703}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{16704}{of} \markbox{16705}{its} \markbox{16706}{shadow} \markbox{16707}{on} \markbox{m16708}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{16709}{In} \markbox{16710}{other} \markbox{16711}{words,} \markbox{16712}{for} \markbox{16713}{any} \markbox{16714}{component} \markbox{m16715}{$V$} \markbox{16716}{of} \markbox{m16717}{$T_e$} \markbox{16718}{or} \markbox{m16719}{$T_c$}, \markbox{16720}{the} \markbox{16721}{shadow} \markbox{16722}{map} \markbox{16723}{induces} \markbox{16724}{a} \markbox{m16725}{$(1,O(\epsilon))$}-quasi-isometry \markbox{m16726}{$s:\phi(V) \to s(\phi(V))$}.  \markbox{16727}{On} \markbox{16728}{the} \markbox{16729}{other} \markbox{16730}{hand,} \markbox{16731}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close} \markbox{16732}{says} \markbox{16733}{every} \markbox{16734}{pair} \markbox{16735}{of} \markbox{16736}{components} \markbox{16737}{of} \markbox{m16738}{$T$} \markbox{16739}{have} \markbox{16740}{shadows} \markbox{16741}{on} \markbox{m16742}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{16743}{with} \markbox{m16744}{$O(\epsilon)$}-bounded \markbox{16745}{overlap.}  \markbox{16746}{It} \markbox{16747}{follows} \markbox{16748}{that} \markbox{m16749}{$\phi:T \to \calZ$} \markbox{16750}{is} \markbox{16751}{an} \markbox{m16752}{$(O(\epsilon), O(\epsilon))$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{16753}{embedding,} \markbox{16754}{as} required.
 
 \markbox{16755}{Finally,} \markbox{16756}{item} \markbox{16757}{(4)} \markbox{16758}{follows} \markbox{16759}{because} \markbox{16760}{we} \markbox{16761}{have} \markbox{16762}{used} \markbox{16763}{the} \markbox{16764}{function} \markbox{m16765}{$\lambda_0$} \markbox{16766}{as} \markbox{16767}{our} \markbox{16768}{connectors} \markbox{16769}{in} \markbox{16770}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable interval}, \markbox{16771}{which} \markbox{16772}{performs} \markbox{16773}{a} \markbox{16774}{small} \markbox{16775}{surgery} \markbox{16776}{at} \markbox{16777}{one} \markbox{16778}{of} \markbox{16779}{the} \markbox{16780}{ends} \markbox{16781}{of} \markbox{m16782}{$\lambda$} \markbox{16783}{so} \markbox{16784}{that} \markbox{16785}{the} \markbox{16786}{result} \markbox{16787}{has} \markbox{16788}{integer} \markbox{16789}{length.}  \markbox{16790}{This} \markbox{16791}{completes} \markbox{16792}{the} proof.
\end{proof}


\subsection{Stable decompositions}\label{subsec:stable decomp}

Having \markbox{16793}{defined} \markbox{16794}{stable} \markbox{16795}{intervals} \markbox{16796}{above,} \markbox{16797}{we} \markbox{16798}{are} \markbox{16799}{almost} \markbox{16800}{ready} \markbox{16801}{to} \markbox{16802}{state} \markbox{16803}{the} \markbox{16804}{Stable} \markbox{16805}{Intervals} \markbox{16806}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.  \markbox{16807}{The} \markbox{16808}{motivation} \markbox{16809}{for} \markbox{16810}{the} \markbox{16811}{definitions} \markbox{16812}{in} \markbox{16813}{this} \markbox{16814}{section} \markbox{16815}{comes} \markbox{16816}{from} \markbox{16817}{our} \markbox{16818}{desire} \markbox{16819}{to} \markbox{16820}{plug} \markbox{16821}{things} \markbox{16822}{into} \markbox{16823}{our} \markbox{16824}{cubical} \markbox{16825}{model} \markbox{16826}{machinery.}  \markbox{16827}{We} \markbox{16828}{describe} \markbox{16829}{how} \markbox{16830}{this} \markbox{16831}{works} \markbox{16832}{in} \markbox{16833}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:perturbed to stable} \markbox{16834}{below,} \markbox{16835}{and} \markbox{16836}{we} \markbox{16837}{point} \markbox{16838}{the} \markbox{16839}{reader} \markbox{16840}{to} \markbox{16841}{it} \markbox{16842}{for} \markbox{16843}{motivation} \markbox{16844}{for} \markbox{16845}{what} follows.

A \markbox{16846}{stable} \markbox{16847}{decomposition} \markbox{16848}{involves} \markbox{16849}{decomposing} \markbox{16850}{a} \markbox{16851}{pair} \markbox{16852}{of} \markbox{16853}{stable} \markbox{16854}{intervals} \markbox{16855}{for} \markbox{16856}{a} \markbox{16857}{pair} \markbox{16858}{of} \markbox{16859}{admissible} \markbox{16860}{setups} \markbox{16861}{into} \markbox{16862}{subintervals,} \markbox{16863}{with} \markbox{16864}{some} \markbox{16865}{maps} \markbox{16866}{which} \markbox{16867}{identify} \markbox{16868}{and} \markbox{16869}{organize} \markbox{16870}{the} \markbox{16871}{various} \markbox{16872}{pieces.}  \markbox{16873}{The} \markbox{16874}{purpose} \markbox{16875}{of} \markbox{16876}{the} \markbox{16877}{next} \markbox{16878}{definition} \markbox{16879}{is} \markbox{16880}{to} \markbox{16881}{give} \markbox{16882}{shorthand} \markbox{16883}{for} \markbox{16884}{requiring} \markbox{16885}{that} \markbox{16886}{the} \markbox{16887}{various} \markbox{16888}{maps} \markbox{16889}{involved} \markbox{16890}{respect} \markbox{16891}{how} \markbox{16892}{the} \markbox{16893}{various} \markbox{16894}{pieces} \markbox{16895}{are} \markbox{16896}{oriented} \markbox{16897}{towards} \markbox{16898}{the} \markbox{16899}{endpoints} \markbox{16900}{of} \markbox{16901}{the} \markbox{16902}{ambient} intervals.

\begin{definition}[Order-preserving maps]\label{defn:order preserving}
Let \markbox{m16903}{$T_1, T_2$} \markbox{16904}{be} \markbox{16905}{two} \markbox{16906}{intervals} \markbox{16907}{with} \markbox{16908}{the} \markbox{16909}{endpoints} \markbox{16910}{of} \markbox{m16911}{$T_i$} \markbox{16912}{labeled} \markbox{16913}{by} \markbox{m16914}{$a_i,b_i$}.  \markbox{16915}{Suppose} \markbox{16916}{that} \markbox{m16917}{$T_i = T_{i,1} \sqcup T_{i,2}$} \markbox{16918}{are} \markbox{16919}{subdivisions} \markbox{16920}{of} \markbox{m16921}{$T_i$} \markbox{16922}{into} \markbox{16923}{finite} \markbox{16924}{collections} \markbox{16925}{of} \markbox{16926}{subintervals} \markbox{16927}{with} \markbox{m16928}{$\# T_{1,1} = \#T_{2,1}$} \markbox{16929}{(and} \markbox{16930}{hence} \markbox{m16931}{$\#T_{1,2} = \#T_{2,2}$}).

\begin{itemize}
\item {} We \markbox{16932}{say} \markbox{16933}{an} \markbox{16934}{isometry} \markbox{m16935}{$i_{E,E'}:E \to E'$} \markbox{16936}{between} \markbox{16937}{components} \markbox{m16938}{$E \subset T_{1,1}$} \markbox{16939}{and} \markbox{m16940}{$E' \subset T_{2,1}$} \markbox{16941}{is} \markbox{16942}{\emph{order preserving}} \markbox{16943}{if} \markbox{m16944}{$i_{E,E'}$} \markbox{16945}{sends} \markbox{16946}{the} \markbox{16947}{endpoint} \markbox{16948}{of} \markbox{m16949}{$E$} \markbox{16950}{closest} \markbox{16951}{to} \markbox{m16952}{$a_1$} \markbox{16953}{to} \markbox{16954}{the} \markbox{16955}{endpoint} \markbox{16956}{of} \markbox{m16957}{$E'$} \markbox{16958}{closest} \markbox{16959}{to} \markbox{m16960}{$a_2$}.
\item {} We \markbox{16961}{say} \markbox{16962}{a} \markbox{16963}{bijection} \markbox{m16964}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_{1,1}) \to \pi_0(T_{2,1})$} \markbox{16965}{is} \markbox{16966}{\emph{order-preserving}} \markbox{16967}{if} \markbox{16968}{it} \markbox{16969}{coincides} \markbox{16970}{with} \markbox{16971}{the} \markbox{16972}{bijection} \markbox{16973}{obtained} \markbox{16974}{by} \markbox{16975}{recording} \markbox{16976}{the} \markbox{16977}{orders} \markbox{16978}{of} \markbox{16979}{appearance} \markbox{16980}{of} \markbox{16981}{the} \markbox{16982}{components} \markbox{16983}{of} \markbox{m16984}{$T_{i,1}$} \markbox{16985}{along} \markbox{m16986}{$T_i$} \markbox{16987}{from} \markbox{m16988}{$a_i$} \markbox{16989}{to} \markbox{m16990}{$b_i$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}\label{rem:order preserving}
Using \markbox{16991}{the} \markbox{16992}{above} \markbox{16993}{notation,} \markbox{16994}{note} \markbox{16995}{that} \markbox{16996}{an} \markbox{16997}{order-preserving} \markbox{16998}{bijection} \markbox{m16999}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_{1,1}) \to \pi_0(T_{2,1})$} \markbox{17000}{automatically} \markbox{17001}{induces} \markbox{17002}{an} \markbox{17003}{order-preserving} \markbox{17004}{bijection} \markbox{m17005}{$\beta:\pi_0(T_{1,2}) \to \pi_0(T_{2,2})$}.  \markbox{17006}{Moreover,} \markbox{17007}{in} \markbox{17008}{this} \markbox{17009}{paper,} \markbox{17010}{we} \markbox{17011}{will} \markbox{17012}{only} \markbox{17013}{be} \markbox{17014}{working} \markbox{17015}{with} \markbox{17016}{intervals} \markbox{17017}{between} \markbox{17018}{a} \markbox{17019}{pair} \markbox{17020}{of} \markbox{17021}{points,} \markbox{17022}{which} \markbox{17023}{are} \markbox{17024}{usually} \markbox{17025}{denoted} \markbox{17026}{by} \markbox{17027}{(some} \markbox{17028}{form} \markbox{17029}{of)} \markbox{m17030}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{17031}{We} \markbox{17032}{will} \markbox{17033}{always} \markbox{17034}{take} \markbox{17035}{order-preserving} \markbox{17036}{to} \markbox{17037}{mean} \markbox{17038}{as} \markbox{17039}{one} \markbox{17040}{moves} \markbox{17041}{from} \markbox{17042}{the} \markbox{m17043}{$a$}-side \markbox{17044}{to} \markbox{17045}{the} \markbox{m17046}{$b$}-side \markbox{17047}{of} \markbox{17048}{the} \markbox{17049}{given} intervals.
\end{remark}

We \markbox{17050}{also} \markbox{17051}{set} \markbox{17052}{one} \markbox{17053}{last} \markbox{17054}{bit} \markbox{17055}{of} \markbox{17056}{notation:} \markbox{17057}{Given} \markbox{17058}{a} \markbox{17059}{stable} \markbox{17060}{tree} \markbox{m17061}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$} \markbox{17062}{for} \markbox{17063}{an} \markbox{m17064}{$\epsilon$}-setup \markbox{m17065}{$(\calY; \{a,b\})$}, \markbox{17066}{if} \markbox{m17067}{$y \in \calY \cup \{a,b\}$}, \markbox{17068}{we} \markbox{17069}{let} \markbox{m17070}{$C_y$} \markbox{17071}{denote} \markbox{17072}{the} \markbox{17073}{cluster} \markbox{17074}{containing} \markbox{m17075}{$y$}, \markbox{17076}{and} \markbox{m17077}{$\mu(C_y)$} \markbox{17078}{the} \markbox{17079}{corresponding} \markbox{17080}{component} \markbox{17081}{of} \markbox{m17082}{$T^c$}.

The \markbox{17083}{following} \markbox{17084}{definition} \markbox{17085}{contains} \markbox{17086}{the} \markbox{17087}{stability} \markbox{17088}{properties} \markbox{17089}{we} want:

\begin{definition}[Stable decomposition] \label{defn:stable decomp}
Let \markbox{m17090}{$\calZ$} \markbox{17091}{be} \markbox{m17092}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic \markbox{17093}{and} \markbox{17094}{geodesic.}  
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} Given \markbox{m17095}{$N>0$}, \markbox{17096}{two} \markbox{m17097}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{m17098}{$(a,b; \calY)$} \markbox{17099}{and} \markbox{m17100}{$(a',b'; \calY')$} \markbox{17101}{are} \markbox{m17102}{$(N,\epsilon)$}-\markbox{17103}{\emph{admissible}} if
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m17104}{$d_{\calZ}(a,a'), d_{\calZ}(b,b') \leq \epsilon$},
\item {} \markbox{m17105}{$\calY, \calY' \subset \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a,b)) \cap \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a',b'))$},
\item {} \markbox{m17106}{$|\calY \triangle \calY'| < N$}.
\end{enumerate}
\item {} Given \markbox{17107}{an} \markbox{m17108}{$\epsilon$}-setup \markbox{m17109}{$(a,b;\calY)$}, \markbox{17110}{an} \markbox{17111}{\emph{edge decomposition}} \markbox{17112}{of} \markbox{17113}{its} \markbox{17114}{stable} \markbox{17115}{interval} \markbox{m17116}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$} \markbox{17117}{is} \markbox{17118}{a} \markbox{17119}{collection} \markbox{17120}{of} \markbox{17121}{subintervals} \markbox{m17122}{$T_s \subset T_e$}.
\item {} Given \markbox{m17123}{$L>0$}, \markbox{m17124}{$\calY_0 \subset \calY \cap \calY'$}, \markbox{17125}{and} \markbox{17126}{two} \markbox{m17127}{$(N,\epsilon)$}-admissible \markbox{17128}{setups} \markbox{m17129}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{17130}{and} \markbox{m17131}{$(a',b'; \calY')$}, \markbox{17132}{we} \markbox{17133}{say} \markbox{17134}{that} \markbox{17135}{two} \markbox{17136}{edge} \markbox{17137}{decompositions} \markbox{m17138}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{17139}{and} \markbox{m17140}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$} \markbox{17141}{are} \markbox{m17142}{$\calY_0$}-\markbox{17143}{\emph{stably}} \markbox{m17144}{$L$}-\markbox{17145}{\emph{compatible}} if
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} Each \markbox{17146}{component} \markbox{17147}{of} \markbox{m17148}{$T_s$} \markbox{17149}{and} \markbox{m17150}{$T'_s$} \markbox{17151}{has} \markbox{17152}{positive} \markbox{17153}{integer} \markbox{17154}{length} \markbox{17155}{with} \markbox{17156}{endpoints} \markbox{17157}{at} \markbox{17158}{vertices} \markbox{17159}{of} \markbox{m17160}{$T_e$} \markbox{17161}{and} \markbox{m17162}{$T'_e$}, \markbox{17163}{respectively.} \label{item:integer length}
\item {} There \markbox{17164}{is} \markbox{17165}{an} \markbox{17166}{order-preserving} \markbox{17167}{bijection} \markbox{m17168}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_s) \to \pi_0(T'_s)$} \markbox{17169}{between} \markbox{17170}{the} \markbox{17171}{sets} \markbox{17172}{of} \markbox{17173}{stable} \markbox{17174}{components.} \label{item:stable bijection}
\item {} For \markbox{17175}{each} \markbox{17176}{\emph{stable pair}} \markbox{m17177}{$(E, E')$} \markbox{17178}{identified} \markbox{17179}{by} \markbox{m17180}{$\alpha$}, \markbox{17181}{there} \markbox{17182}{exists} \markbox{17183}{an} \markbox{17184}{order-preserving} \markbox{17185}{isometry} \markbox{m17186}{$i_{E,E'}:E \to E'$}. \label{item:stable pairs}
\item {} For \markbox{17187}{all} \markbox{17188}{but} \markbox{17189}{at} \markbox{17190}{most} \markbox{m17191}{$L$} \markbox{17192}{pairs} \markbox{17193}{of} \markbox{17194}{stable} \markbox{17195}{components} \markbox{m17196}{$(E,E')$}, \markbox{17197}{we} \markbox{17198}{have} \markbox{m17199}{$\phi(E) = \phi(E')$} \markbox{17200}{are} \markbox{17201}{identical} \markbox{17202}{with} \markbox{m17203}{$\phi(x) = \phi'(i_{E,E'}(x))$} \markbox{17204}{for} \markbox{17205}{all} \markbox{m17206}{$x \in E$}. \label{item:identical pairs}
\item {} For \markbox{17207}{the} \markbox{17208}{(at} \markbox{17209}{most)} \markbox{m17210}{$L$}-many \markbox{17211}{remaining} \markbox{17212}{stable} \markbox{17213}{pairs} \markbox{m17214}{$(E,E')$}, \markbox{17215}{we} \markbox{17216}{have} \markbox{m17217}{$d_{\calZ}(\phi(x), \phi'(i_{E,E'}(x)))< L$} \markbox{17218}{for} \markbox{17219}{all} \markbox{m17220}{$x \in E$}. \label{item:close pairs}
\item {} The \markbox{17221}{complements} \markbox{m17222}{$T_{e} - T_s$} \markbox{17223}{and} \markbox{m17224}{$T'_{e} - T'_s$} \markbox{17225}{consist} \markbox{17226}{of} \markbox{17227}{at} \markbox{17228}{most} \markbox{m17229}{$L$}-many \markbox{17230}{\emph{unstable components}} \markbox{17231}{of} \markbox{17232}{diameter} \markbox{17233}{at} \markbox{17234}{most} \markbox{m17235}{$L$}.\label{item:unstable components}
\item {} The \markbox{17236}{induced} \markbox{17237}{order-preserving} \markbox{17238}{bijection} \markbox{m17239}{$\beta:\pi_0(T-T_s) \to \pi_0(T' - T'_s)$} \markbox{17240}{satisfies:} \label{item:adjacency}
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} (Endpoints) \markbox{17241}{Let} \markbox{m17242}{$D_a$} \markbox{17243}{denote} \markbox{17244}{the} \markbox{17245}{component} \markbox{17246}{of} \markbox{m17247}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17248}{containing} \markbox{m17249}{$\mu(C_a)$}, \markbox{17250}{and} \markbox{17251}{define} \markbox{m17252}{$D_b,D_{a'},D_{b'}$} \markbox{17253}{similarly.}  \markbox{17254}{Then} \markbox{m17255}{$\beta(D_a) = D_{a'}$} \markbox{17256}{and} \markbox{m17257}{$\beta(D_b) = D_{b'}$}. \label{item:endpoint condition}
\item {} (Identifying \markbox{17258}{clusters)} \markbox{17259}{For} \markbox{17260}{any} \markbox{m17261}{$y \in \calY_0$}, \markbox{17262}{let} \markbox{m17263}{$D_y, D'_y$} \markbox{17264}{denote} \markbox{17265}{the} \markbox{17266}{components} \markbox{17267}{of} \markbox{m17268}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17269}{and} \markbox{m17270}{$T' - T'_s$} \markbox{17271}{containing} \markbox{m17272}{$\mu(C_y), \mu(C'_y)$}, \markbox{17273}{respectively.}  \markbox{17274}{Then} \markbox{m17275}{$\beta(D_y) = D'_y$}. \label{item:cluster identify}
\end{enumerate}
\end{enumerate}
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}%% remark 8.13
The \markbox{17276}{above} \markbox{17277}{definition} \markbox{17278}{is} \markbox{17279}{a} \markbox{17280}{refinement} \markbox{17281}{of} \markbox{17282}{the} \markbox{17283}{properties} \markbox{17284}{contained} \markbox{17285}{in} \cite[Stable \markbox{17286}{Tree} \markbox{17287}{Theorem} 3.2]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{17288}{where} \markbox{17289}{we} \markbox{17290}{have} \markbox{17291}{set} \markbox{17292}{up} \markbox{17293}{these} \markbox{17294}{stable} \markbox{17295}{decompositions} \markbox{17296}{to} \markbox{17297}{plug} \markbox{17298}{nicely} \markbox{17299}{into} \markbox{17300}{the} \markbox{17301}{cubical} \markbox{17302}{model} \markbox{17303}{machinery} \markbox{17304}{described} \markbox{17305}{earlier} \markbox{17306}{in} \markbox{17307}{the} \markbox{17308}{paper.} \markbox{17309}{How} \markbox{17310}{this} \markbox{17311}{process} \markbox{17312}{works} \markbox{17313}{is} \markbox{17314}{described} \markbox{17315}{below} \markbox{17316}{in} \markbox{17317}{more} \markbox{17318}{detail} \markbox{17319}{in} Subsection~\ref{subsec:perturbed to stable}, \markbox{17320}{but} \markbox{17321}{for} \markbox{17322}{now} \markbox{17323}{we} \markbox{17324}{motivate} \markbox{17325}{some} \markbox{17326}{parts} \markbox{17327}{of} \markbox{17328}{the} \markbox{17329}{definition.}  \markbox{17330}{Roughly} \markbox{17331}{speaking,} \markbox{17332}{the} \markbox{17333}{points} \markbox{m17334}{$\calY$} \markbox{17335}{and} \markbox{m17336}{$\calY'$} \markbox{17337}{stand} \markbox{17338}{in} \markbox{17339}{for} \markbox{17340}{the} \markbox{17341}{relative} \markbox{17342}{projection} \markbox{17343}{data} \markbox{17344}{on} \markbox{17345}{each} \markbox{17346}{interval,} \markbox{17347}{with} \markbox{17348}{each} \markbox{17349}{component} \markbox{17350}{of} \markbox{m17351}{$T - T_s$} \markbox{17352}{and} \markbox{m17353}{$T' - T'_s$} \markbox{17354}{being} \markbox{17355}{labeled} \markbox{17356}{by} \markbox{17357}{some} \markbox{17358}{such} \markbox{17359}{point.}  \markbox{17360}{Eventually,} \markbox{17361}{we} \markbox{17362}{will} \markbox{17363}{collapse} \markbox{17364}{each} \markbox{17365}{of} \markbox{17366}{the} \markbox{17367}{components} \markbox{17368}{of} \markbox{m17369}{$T - T_s$} \markbox{17370}{and} \markbox{m17371}{$T' - T'_s$} \markbox{17372}{to} \markbox{17373}{points.}  \markbox{17374}{Item} \eqref{item:adjacency} \markbox{17375}{says} \markbox{17376}{that} \markbox{17377}{the} \markbox{17378}{common} \markbox{17379}{labels} \markbox{m17380}{$\calY \cap \calY'$} \markbox{17381}{are} \markbox{17382}{identified,} \markbox{17383}{as} \markbox{17384}{well} \markbox{17385}{as} \markbox{17386}{the} \markbox{17387}{endpoint} \markbox{17388}{pairs} \markbox{m17389}{$a,a'$} \markbox{17390}{and} \markbox{m17391}{$b,b'$}.  \markbox{17392}{The} \markbox{17393}{rest} \markbox{17394}{of} \markbox{17395}{the} \markbox{17396}{statement} \markbox{17397}{now} \markbox{17398}{says} \markbox{17399}{that} \markbox{17400}{the} \markbox{17401}{components} \markbox{17402}{of} \markbox{m17403}{$T_s$} \markbox{17404}{and} \markbox{m17405}{$T'_s$} \markbox{17406}{are} \markbox{17407}{in} \markbox{17408}{bijection} \markbox{17409}{with} \markbox{17410}{each} \markbox{17411}{other,} \markbox{17412}{where} \markbox{17413}{identified} \markbox{17414}{components} \markbox{17415}{are} \markbox{17416}{isometric,} \markbox{17417}{and} \markbox{17418}{the} \markbox{17419}{order-preserving} \markbox{17420}{properties} \markbox{17421}{explain} \markbox{17422}{how} \markbox{17423}{to} \markbox{17424}{glue} \markbox{17425}{these} \markbox{17426}{components} \markbox{17427}{to} \markbox{17428}{obtain} \markbox{17429}{an} \markbox{17430}{isometry} \markbox{17431}{between} \markbox{17432}{collapsed} \markbox{17433}{intervals.}  \markbox{17434}{Finally,} \markbox{17435}{the} \markbox{17436}{proximity} \markbox{17437}{properties} \markbox{17438}{in} \markbox{17439}{items} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{17440}{and} \eqref{item:close pairs} \markbox{17441}{are} \markbox{17442}{necessary} \markbox{17443}{for} \markbox{17444}{controlling} \markbox{17445}{the} \markbox{17446}{maps} \markbox{17447}{back} \markbox{17448}{into} \markbox{17449}{the} \markbox{17450}{ambient} \markbox{17451}{HHS;} \markbox{17452}{see} \markbox{17453}{the} \markbox{17454}{proof} \markbox{17455}{of} \markbox{17456}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}.  \markbox{17457}{A} \markbox{17458}{more} \markbox{17459}{general} \markbox{17460}{version} \markbox{17461}{can} \markbox{17462}{be} \markbox{17463}{found} \markbox{17464}{in} \cite[Definition 10.18]{DMS_FJ}. 
\end{remark}

\subsection{The stable interval theorem}

With \markbox{17465}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{17466}{in} \markbox{17467}{hand,} \markbox{17468}{we} \markbox{17469}{can} \markbox{17470}{now} \markbox{17471}{state} \markbox{17472}{the} \markbox{17473}{main} \markbox{17474}{result} \markbox{17475}{of} \markbox{17476}{this} \markbox{17477}{section,} \markbox{17478}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{17479}{below.}  \markbox{17480}{It} \markbox{17481}{says} \markbox{17482}{that} \markbox{17483}{the} \markbox{17484}{stable} \markbox{17485}{intervals} \markbox{17486}{for} \markbox{17487}{a} \markbox{17488}{pair} \markbox{17489}{of} \markbox{17490}{admissible} \markbox{m17491}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{17492}{admit} \markbox{17493}{compatible} \markbox{17494}{stable} \markbox{17495}{decompositions---that} \markbox{17496}{is,} \markbox{17497}{decompositions} \markbox{17498}{into} \markbox{17499}{subintervals} \markbox{17500}{which} \markbox{17501}{are} \markbox{17502}{in} \markbox{17503}{bijective} \markbox{17504}{correspondence} \markbox{17505}{with} \markbox{17506}{idenitified} \markbox{17507}{pairs} \markbox{17508}{uniformly} \markbox{17509}{close,} \markbox{17510}{up} \markbox{17511}{to} \markbox{17512}{ignored} \markbox{17513}{a} \markbox{17514}{bounded} \markbox{17515}{collection} \markbox{17516}{of} \markbox{17517}{bounded-length} \markbox{17518}{subintervals.}  \markbox{17519}{We} \markbox{17520}{first} \markbox{17521}{state} \markbox{17522}{this} \markbox{17523}{technical} \markbox{17524}{result,} \markbox{17525}{and} \markbox{17526}{then} \markbox{17527}{prove} \markbox{17528}{a} \markbox{17529}{corollary} \markbox{17530}{which} \markbox{17531}{gives} \markbox{17532}{the} \markbox{17533}{main} \markbox{17534}{upshot} \markbox{17535}{for} \markbox{17536}{our} \markbox{17537}{purposes} \markbox{17538}{of} \markbox{17539}{building} \markbox{17540}{stable} \markbox{17541}{cubical} \markbox{17542}{models.}  

For \markbox{17543}{a} \markbox{17544}{bit} \markbox{17545}{of} \markbox{17546}{setup,} \markbox{17547}{recall} \markbox{17548}{the} \markbox{17549}{notion} \markbox{17550}{of} \markbox{17551}{a} \markbox{17552}{thickening} \markbox{17553}{of} \markbox{17554}{an} \markbox{17555}{interval} \markbox{17556}{from} \markbox{17557}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:thickenings}.  \markbox{17558}{This} \markbox{17559}{was} \markbox{17560}{a} \markbox{17561}{way} \markbox{17562}{of} \markbox{17563}{taking} \markbox{17564}{an} \markbox{17565}{interval} \markbox{17566}{with} \markbox{17567}{a} \markbox{17568}{decomposition} \markbox{m17569}{$T = A \cup B$} \markbox{17570}{into} \markbox{17571}{collections} \markbox{17572}{of} \markbox{17573}{segments,} \markbox{17574}{and} \markbox{17575}{expanding} \markbox{17576}{and} \markbox{17577}{combining} \markbox{17578}{one} \markbox{17579}{collection} \markbox{17580}{of} \markbox{17581}{the} \markbox{17582}{segments.}  \markbox{17583}{Our} \markbox{17584}{stable} \markbox{17585}{intervals} \markbox{17586}{come} \markbox{17587}{with} \markbox{17588}{such} \markbox{17589}{a} \markbox{17590}{decomposition} \markbox{m17591}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$}, \markbox{17592}{and} \markbox{17593}{we} \markbox{17594}{will} \markbox{17595}{always} \markbox{17596}{mean} \markbox{17597}{a} \markbox{17598}{thickening} \markbox{17599}{of} \markbox{17600}{a} \markbox{17601}{stable} \markbox{17602}{interval} \markbox{m17603}{$T$} \markbox{17604}{to} \markbox{17605}{be} \markbox{17606}{a} \markbox{17607}{thickening} \markbox{17608}{of} \markbox{m17609}{$T$} \markbox{17610}{along} \markbox{17611}{the} \markbox{17612}{components} \markbox{17613}{of} \markbox{17614}{the} \markbox{17615}{cluster} \markbox{17616}{forest} \markbox{m17617}{$T_c$}.  \markbox{17618}{Finally,} \markbox{17619}{we} \markbox{17620}{denote} \markbox{17621}{the} \markbox{17622}{components} \markbox{17623}{of} \markbox{17624}{the} \markbox{17625}{resulting} \markbox{17626}{thickening} \markbox{17627}{by} \markbox{m17628}{$T = \bT_{e} \cup \bT_c$}, \markbox{17629}{and} \markbox{17630}{we} \markbox{17631}{note} \markbox{17632}{that} \markbox{m17633}{$\bT_e \subset T_e$} \markbox{17634}{and} \markbox{m17635}{$T_c \subset \bT_c$}. 

\begin{theorem}[Stable intervals]\label{thm:stable intervals}
Let \markbox{m17636}{$\calZ$} \markbox{17637}{be} \markbox{m17638}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic \markbox{17639}{and} \markbox{17640}{geodesic.}  \markbox{17641}{For} \markbox{17642}{any} \markbox{m17643}{$\epsilon, N>0$} \markbox{17644}{and} \markbox{17645}{positive} \markbox{17646}{integers} \markbox{m17647}{$r_1,r_2>0$}, \markbox{17648}{there} \markbox{17649}{exist} \markbox{m17650}{$L_1 = L_1(\delta, \epsilon, N)>0$} \markbox{17651}{and} \markbox{m17652}{$L_2 = L_2(\delta, \epsilon, N,r_1,r_2)>0$} \markbox{17653}{so} \markbox{17654}{that} \markbox{17655}{the} \markbox{17656}{following} \markbox{17657}{holds.}  \markbox{17658}{Suppose} \markbox{m17659}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{17660}{and} \markbox{m17661}{$(a',b';\calY')$} \markbox{17662}{are} \markbox{m17663}{$(N,\epsilon)$}-admissible \markbox{m17664}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{17665}{and} \markbox{17666}{let} \markbox{m17667}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$} \markbox{17668}{and} \markbox{m17669}{$T' = T'_e \cup T'_c$} \markbox{17670}{denote} \markbox{17671}{their} \markbox{17672}{stable} \markbox{17673}{intervals.}  Then
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} There \markbox{17674}{exist} \markbox{m17675}{$(\calY \cap \calY')$}-stable \markbox{m17676}{$L_1$}-compatible \markbox{17677}{decompositions} \markbox{m17678}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{17679}{and} \markbox{m17680}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$}, and
\item {} There \markbox{17681}{exist} \markbox{m17682}{$(\calY \cap \calY')$}-stable \markbox{m17683}{$L_2$}-compatible \markbox{17684}{edge} \markbox{17685}{decompositions} \markbox{m17686}{$\bT_{s} \subset \bT_{e}$} \markbox{17687}{and} \markbox{m17688}{$\bT'_{s} \subset \bT'_{e}$} \markbox{17689}{of} \markbox{17690}{the} \markbox{m17691}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{17692}{of} \markbox{m17693}{$T, T'$} \markbox{17694}{along} \markbox{m17695}{$T_c,T'_c$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item {} Moreover, \markbox{17696}{we} \markbox{17697}{have} \markbox{m17698}{$\bT_s \subset T_s$} \markbox{17699}{and} \markbox{m17700}{$\bT_s \subset T'_s$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{enumerate}

\end{theorem}

\begin{remark}
In \markbox{17701}{the} \markbox{17702}{HHS} \markbox{17703}{setting,} \markbox{17704}{we} \markbox{17705}{will} \markbox{17706}{be} \markbox{17707}{able} \markbox{17708}{to} \markbox{17709}{control} \markbox{17710}{each} \markbox{17711}{of} \markbox{17712}{the} \markbox{17713}{constants} \markbox{m17714}{$\delta, \epsilon, N, r_1,r_2$} \markbox{17715}{in} \markbox{17716}{terms} \markbox{17717}{of} \markbox{17718}{the} \markbox{17719}{ambient} \markbox{17720}{HHS} \markbox{17721}{structure.}  \markbox{17722}{We} \markbox{17723}{have} \markbox{17724}{written} \markbox{17725}{the} \markbox{17726}{statement} \markbox{17727}{with} \markbox{17728}{two} \markbox{17729}{conclusions} \markbox{17730}{because} \markbox{17731}{the} \markbox{17732}{first} \markbox{17733}{conclusion} \markbox{17734}{is} \markbox{17735}{a} \markbox{17736}{mild} \markbox{17737}{reformulation} \markbox{17738}{of} \markbox{17739}{the} \markbox{17740}{original} \markbox{17741}{theorem} \cite[Theorem 3.2]{DMS_bary}, \markbox{17742}{while} \markbox{17743}{the} \markbox{17744}{second} \markbox{17745}{is} \markbox{17746}{what} \markbox{17747}{we} \markbox{17748}{actually} \markbox{17749}{need} \markbox{17750}{for} \markbox{17751}{the} \markbox{17752}{cubulation} \markbox{17753}{machine} \markbox{17754}{discussed} \markbox{17755}{in} \markbox{17756}{this} \markbox{17757}{paper.}  \markbox{17758}{Notably,} \markbox{17759}{the} \markbox{17760}{second} \markbox{17761}{statement} \markbox{17762}{will} \markbox{17763}{be} \markbox{17764}{an} \markbox{17765}{easy} \markbox{17766}{consequence} \markbox{17767}{of} \markbox{17768}{the} first.
\end{remark}

Before \markbox{17769}{we} \markbox{17770}{move} \markbox{17771}{onto} \markbox{17772}{the} \markbox{17773}{proof,} \markbox{17774}{we} \markbox{17775}{observe} \markbox{17776}{the} \markbox{17777}{following} \markbox{17778}{corollary,} \markbox{17779}{whose} \markbox{17780}{statement} \markbox{17781}{and} \markbox{17782}{proof} \markbox{17783}{motivate} \markbox{17784}{the} \markbox{17785}{statement} \markbox{17786}{of} \markbox{17787}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.  \markbox{17788}{In} \markbox{17789}{particular,} \markbox{17790}{this} \markbox{17791}{corollary} \markbox{17792}{will} \markbox{17793}{allow} \markbox{17794}{us} \markbox{17795}{to} \markbox{17796}{verify} \markbox{17797}{the} \markbox{17798}{interval-wise} \markbox{17799}{condition} \markbox{17800}{in} \markbox{17801}{Proposition} \ref{prop:HFI isomorphism} \markbox{17802}{and} \markbox{17803}{give} \markbox{17804}{us} \markbox{17805}{the} \markbox{17806}{cubical} \markbox{17807}{isomorphism} \markbox{17808}{we} \markbox{17809}{need} \markbox{17810}{for} \markbox{17811}{the} \markbox{17812}{Stable} \markbox{17813}{Cubulations} \markbox{17814}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable cubes}; \markbox{17815}{see} \markbox{17816}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:perturbed to stable}.

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:interval isometry}
Let \markbox{m17817}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{17818}{and} \markbox{m17819}{$(a',b'; \calY')$} \markbox{17820}{be} \markbox{m17821}{$(N,\epsilon)$}-admissible \markbox{m17822}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{17823}{with} \markbox{m17824}{$(\calY \cap \calY')$}-stable \markbox{m17825}{$L$}-compatible \markbox{17826}{decompositions} \markbox{m17827}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{17828}{and} \markbox{m17829}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$}.   \markbox{17830}{Let} \markbox{m17831}{$\Delta:T \to \hT$} \markbox{17832}{and} \markbox{m17833}{$\Delta':T' \to \hT'$} \markbox{17834}{denote} \markbox{17835}{the} \markbox{17836}{quotients} \markbox{17837}{obtained} \markbox{17838}{by} \markbox{17839}{collapsing} \markbox{17840}{each} \markbox{17841}{component} \markbox{17842}{of} \markbox{m17843}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17844}{and} \markbox{m17845}{$T'-T'_s$} \markbox{17846}{to} \markbox{17847}{a} \markbox{17848}{point.}  \markbox{17849}{The} \markbox{17850}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m17851}{$\hT$} \markbox{17852}{and} \markbox{m17853}{$\hT'$} \markbox{17854}{are} \markbox{17855}{simplicial} \markbox{17856}{intervals} \markbox{17857}{where} \markbox{17858}{each} \markbox{17859}{collapsed} \markbox{17860}{component} \markbox{17861}{of} \markbox{m17862}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17863}{and} \markbox{m17864}{$T'-T'_s$} \markbox{17865}{is} \markbox{17866}{a} \markbox{17867}{vertex,} and
\item {} There \markbox{17868}{exists} \markbox{17869}{an} \markbox{17870}{isometry} \markbox{m17871}{$\Phi:\hT \to \hT'$} \markbox{17872}{which} \markbox{17873}{is} \markbox{17874}{induced} \markbox{17875}{from} \markbox{17876}{the} \markbox{17877}{bijections} \markbox{m17878}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_s) \to \pi_0(T'_s)$} \markbox{17879}{and} \markbox{m17880}{$\beta:\pi_0(T-T_s) \to \pi_0(T'-T'_s)$}, \markbox{17881}{and} \markbox{17882}{the} \markbox{17883}{isometries} \markbox{17884}{of} \markbox{17885}{pairs} \markbox{17886}{of} \markbox{17887}{stable} \markbox{17888}{components} \markbox{m17889}{$i_{E,\alpha(E)}:E \to \alpha(E)$} \markbox{17890}{for} \markbox{m17891}{$E \subset T_s$}.   \markbox{17892}{Moreover,} \markbox{17893}{we} have
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m17894}{$\Phi(\Delta(a)) = \Delta'(a')$} \markbox{17895}{and} \markbox{m17896}{$\Phi(\Delta(b)) = \Delta'(b')$},
\item {} If \markbox{m17897}{$y \in \calY \cap \calY'$} \markbox{17898}{and} \markbox{m17899}{$D_y \in \pi_0(T - T_s)$} \markbox{17900}{and} \markbox{m17901}{$D'_y \in \pi_0(T - T_s)$} \markbox{17902}{contain} \markbox{m17903}{$\mu(C_y)$} \markbox{17904}{and} \markbox{m17905}{$\mu(C'_y)$}, \markbox{17906}{respectively,} \markbox{17907}{then} \markbox{m17908}{$\Phi(\Delta(D_y)) = \Delta'(D'_y)$}. 
\end{enumerate}
\end{enumerate}
\end{corollary}


\begin{proof}
First, \markbox{17909}{observe} \markbox{17910}{that} \markbox{m17911}{$\hT$} \markbox{17912}{and} \markbox{m17913}{$\hT'$} \markbox{17914}{are} \markbox{17915}{intervals} \markbox{17916}{because} \markbox{m17917}{$T,T'$} \markbox{17918}{are} \markbox{17919}{and} \markbox{17920}{each} \markbox{17921}{component} \markbox{17922}{of} \markbox{m17923}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17924}{and} \markbox{m17925}{$T'-T'_s$} \markbox{17926}{is} \markbox{17927}{a} \markbox{17928}{subinterval.}  \markbox{17929}{They} \markbox{17930}{are} \markbox{17931}{simplicial} \markbox{17932}{intervals} \markbox{17933}{with} \markbox{17934}{the} \markbox{17935}{given} \markbox{17936}{description} \markbox{17937}{because} \markbox{17938}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{17939}{(specifically} \markbox{17940}{item} \markbox{17941}{(4a)} \markbox{17942}{of} \markbox{17943}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}) \markbox{17944}{provides} \markbox{17945}{that} \markbox{17946}{each} \markbox{17947}{component} \markbox{17948}{of} \markbox{m17949}{$T_s,T'_s$} \markbox{17950}{has} \markbox{17951}{positive} \markbox{17952}{integer} \markbox{17953}{length,} \markbox{17954}{and} \markbox{17955}{so} \markbox{17956}{the} \markbox{17957}{distance} \markbox{17958}{between} \markbox{17959}{the} \markbox{17960}{points} \markbox{17961}{corresponding} \markbox{17962}{to} \markbox{17963}{pairs} \markbox{17964}{of} \markbox{17965}{collapsed} \markbox{17966}{components} \markbox{17967}{of} \markbox{m17968}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{17969}{and} \markbox{m17970}{$T'-T'_s$} \markbox{17971}{is} \markbox{17972}{a} \markbox{17973}{positive} integer.

For \markbox{17974}{the} \markbox{17975}{second} \markbox{17976}{conclusion,} \markbox{17977}{we} \markbox{17978}{can} \markbox{17979}{define} \markbox{m17980}{$\Phi:\hT\to \hT'$} \markbox{17981}{as} \markbox{17982}{follows:} \markbox{17983}{For} \markbox{17984}{each} \markbox{17985}{vertex} \markbox{m17986}{$v \in \hT$} \markbox{17987}{corresponding} \markbox{17988}{to} \markbox{17989}{a} \markbox{17990}{component} \markbox{m17991}{$C \in \pi_0(T-T_s)$}, \markbox{17992}{we} \markbox{17993}{define} \markbox{m17994}{$\Phi(v) = v'$}, \markbox{17995}{where} \markbox{m17996}{$v'$} \markbox{17997}{is} \markbox{17998}{the} \markbox{17999}{vertex} \markbox{18000}{of} \markbox{m18001}{$\hT'$} \markbox{18002}{corresponding} \markbox{18003}{to} \markbox{m18004}{$\beta(C) \in \pi_0(T'-T'_s)$}.  \markbox{18005}{If} \markbox{18006}{now} \markbox{m18007}{$x \in \hT$} \markbox{18008}{is} \markbox{18009}{not} \markbox{18010}{such} \markbox{18011}{a} \markbox{18012}{vertex,} \markbox{18013}{then} \markbox{m18014}{$x \in \Delta(E)$} \markbox{18015}{for} \markbox{18016}{some} \markbox{18017}{component} \markbox{m18018}{$E \in \pi_0(T_s)$}.  \markbox{18019}{So} \markbox{18020}{we} \markbox{18021}{define} \markbox{m18022}{$\Phi(x) = \Delta'(i_{E, \alpha(E)}(x))$}.  \markbox{18023}{The} \markbox{18024}{fact} \markbox{18025}{that} \markbox{18026}{these} \markbox{18027}{piece-wise} \markbox{18028}{maps} \markbox{18029}{glue} \markbox{18030}{coherently} \markbox{18031}{is} \markbox{18032}{a} \markbox{18033}{direct} \markbox{18034}{consequence} \markbox{18035}{of} \markbox{18036}{the} \markbox{18037}{fact} \markbox{18038}{that} \markbox{m18039}{$\alpha$} \markbox{18040}{is} \markbox{18041}{order-preserving.}  \markbox{18042}{The} \markbox{18043}{subitems} \markbox{18044}{of} \markbox{18045}{(2)} \markbox{18046}{are} \markbox{18047}{direct} \markbox{18048}{consequences} \markbox{18049}{of} \markbox{18050}{item} \eqref{item:adjacency} \markbox{18051}{of} \markbox{18052}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}.  \markbox{18053}{This} \markbox{18054}{completes} \markbox{18055}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}
Notably, \markbox{18056}{the} \markbox{18057}{above} \markbox{18058}{corollary} \markbox{18059}{holds} \markbox{18060}{whenever} \markbox{18061}{we} \markbox{18062}{have} \markbox{18063}{a} \markbox{18064}{stable} \markbox{18065}{decomposition,} \markbox{18066}{so} \markbox{18067}{in} \markbox{18068}{particular} \markbox{18069}{when} \markbox{18070}{this} \markbox{18071}{is} \markbox{18072}{a} \markbox{18073}{stable} \markbox{18074}{decomposition} \markbox{18075}{arising} \markbox{18076}{from} \markbox{18077}{the} \markbox{18078}{thickened} \markbox{18079}{versions} \markbox{18080}{of} \markbox{18081}{our} \markbox{18082}{stable} intervals.
\end{remark}

\subsection{Detailed sketch of the proof} \label{subsec:detailed sketch}

In \markbox{18083}{lieu} \markbox{18084}{of} \markbox{18085}{a} \markbox{18086}{full} \markbox{18087}{proof} \markbox{18088}{(see} \markbox{18089}{Appendix} \ref{app:SI}), \markbox{18090}{we} \markbox{18091}{provide} \markbox{18092}{a} \markbox{18093}{detailed} \markbox{18094}{sketch} \markbox{18095}{of} \markbox{18096}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{18097}{with} \markbox{18098}{figures} \markbox{18099}{illustrating} \markbox{18100}{the} \markbox{18101}{key} \markbox{18102}{technical} \markbox{18103}{arguments,} \markbox{18104}{which} \markbox{18105}{are} \markbox{18106}{easier} \markbox{18107}{to} \markbox{18108}{understand} \markbox{18109}{at} \markbox{18110}{a} \markbox{18111}{fairly} \markbox{18112}{close} \markbox{18113}{level} \markbox{18114}{than} \markbox{18115}{to} \markbox{18116}{write} \markbox{18117}{down} \markbox{18118}{carefully.}  \markbox{18119}{Our} \markbox{18120}{proof} \markbox{18121}{strategy} \markbox{18122}{here} \markbox{18123}{follows} \markbox{18124}{more} \markbox{18125}{closely} \markbox{18126}{the} \markbox{18127}{proof} \markbox{18128}{of} \cite[Theorem 10.23]{DMS_FJ} \markbox{18129}{than} \markbox{18130}{the} \markbox{18131}{original} \cite[Theorem 3.1]{DMS_bary}.

The \markbox{18132}{goal} \markbox{18133}{is} \markbox{18134}{to} \markbox{18135}{show} \markbox{18136}{that} \markbox{18137}{the} \markbox{18138}{stable} \markbox{18139}{intervals} \markbox{18140}{(Definition} \ref{defn:stable interval}) \markbox{18141}{for} \markbox{18142}{pairs} \markbox{18143}{of} \markbox{18144}{admissible} \markbox{m18145}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{18146}{admit} \markbox{18147}{stable} \markbox{18148}{decompositions} \markbox{18149}{in} \markbox{18150}{the} \markbox{18151}{sense} \markbox{18152}{of} \markbox{18153}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}.  \markbox{18154}{Roughly,} \markbox{18155}{these} \markbox{18156}{are} \markbox{18157}{decompositions} \markbox{18158}{of} \markbox{18159}{the} \markbox{18160}{intervals} \markbox{18161}{into} \markbox{18162}{collections} \markbox{18163}{of} \markbox{18164}{subintervals,} \markbox{18165}{which} \markbox{18166}{are} \markbox{18167}{either} \markbox{18168}{identical} \markbox{18169}{(as} \markbox{18170}{in} \markbox{18171}{item} \markbox{18172}{(d)),} \markbox{18173}{or} \markbox{18174}{the} \markbox{18175}{same} \markbox{18176}{length} \markbox{18177}{and} \markbox{18178}{uniformly} \markbox{18179}{close} \markbox{18180}{(as} \markbox{18181}{in} \markbox{18182}{item} \markbox{18183}{(e)),} \markbox{18184}{or} \markbox{18185}{are} \markbox{18186}{one} \markbox{18187}{of} \markbox{18188}{boundedly-many} \markbox{18189}{unstable} \markbox{18190}{components} \markbox{18191}{we} \markbox{18192}{can} \markbox{18193}{ignore} \markbox{18194}{(as} \markbox{18195}{in} \markbox{18196}{item} \markbox{18197}{(f)).}  \markbox{18198}{We} \markbox{18199}{need} \markbox{18200}{to} \markbox{18201}{show} \markbox{18202}{how} \markbox{18203}{to} \markbox{18204}{constraints} \markbox{18205}{on} \markbox{18206}{the} \markbox{18207}{input} \markbox{18208}{data} \markbox{18209}{assumed} \markbox{18210}{in} \markbox{18211}{item} \markbox{18212}{(1)} \markbox{18213}{translates} \markbox{18214}{into} \markbox{18215}{control} \markbox{18216}{over} \markbox{18217}{the} \markbox{18218}{components} \markbox{18219}{of} \markbox{18220}{the} \markbox{18221}{stable} intervals.

To \markbox{18222}{begin} \markbox{18223}{the} \markbox{18224}{sketch,} \markbox{18225}{first} \markbox{18226}{observe} \markbox{18227}{that} \markbox{18228}{the} \markbox{18229}{two} \markbox{18230}{main} \markbox{18231}{assumptions} \markbox{18232}{of} \markbox{18233}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{18234}{on} \markbox{18235}{the} \markbox{18236}{setups} \markbox{m18237}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{18238}{and} \markbox{m18239}{$(a',b';\calY')$} \markbox{18240}{are} that
\begin{itemize}
\item {} The \markbox{18241}{sets} \markbox{18242}{of} \markbox{18243}{cluster} \markbox{18244}{points} \markbox{m18245}{$\calY, \calY'$} \markbox{18246}{are} \markbox{18247}{close} \markbox{18248}{to} \markbox{18249}{both} \markbox{m18250}{$\lambda(a,b)$} \markbox{18251}{and} \markbox{m18252}{$\lambda(a',b')$} \markbox{18253}{and} \markbox{18254}{have} \markbox{18255}{bounded} \markbox{18256}{symmetric} \markbox{18257}{difference,} \markbox{18258}{and} 
\item {} The \markbox{18259}{endpoints} \markbox{18260}{pairs} \markbox{m18261}{$(a,b)$} \markbox{18262}{and} \markbox{m18263}{$(a',b')$} \markbox{18264}{are} \markbox{18265}{within} \markbox{m18266}{$\epsilon$} \markbox{18267}{of} \markbox{18268}{each} other.
\end{itemize}

This \markbox{18269}{suggests} \markbox{18270}{the} \markbox{18271}{following} \markbox{18272}{iterated} \markbox{18273}{proof} \markbox{18274}{strategy:} 
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} First, \markbox{18275}{show} \markbox{18276}{that} \markbox{18277}{we} \markbox{18278}{can} \markbox{18279}{build} \markbox{18280}{a} \markbox{18281}{stable} \markbox{18282}{decomposition} \markbox{18283}{when} \markbox{18284}{we} \markbox{18285}{add} \markbox{18286}{a} \markbox{18287}{single} \markbox{18288}{nearby} \markbox{18289}{cluster} \markbox{18290}{point,} \markbox{18291}{while} \markbox{18292}{keeping} \markbox{18293}{the} \markbox{18294}{endpoints} \markbox{18295}{the} same.
\item {} Next, \markbox{18296}{show} \markbox{18297}{that} \markbox{18298}{we} \markbox{18299}{can} \markbox{18300}{iteratively} \markbox{18301}{combine} \markbox{18302}{stable} \markbox{18303}{decompositions} \markbox{18304}{to} \markbox{18305}{obtain} \markbox{18306}{a} \markbox{18307}{stable} decomposition.
\item {} Finally, \markbox{18308}{show} \markbox{18309}{that} \markbox{18310}{we} \markbox{18311}{can} \markbox{18312}{build} \markbox{18313}{a} \markbox{18314}{stable} \markbox{18315}{decomposition} \markbox{18316}{when} \markbox{18317}{we} \markbox{18318}{only} \markbox{18319}{wiggle} \markbox{18320}{a} \markbox{18321}{single} \markbox{18322}{endpoint} \markbox{18323}{and} \markbox{18324}{keep} \markbox{18325}{everything} \markbox{18326}{else} \markbox{18327}{(including} \markbox{18328}{the} \markbox{18329}{cluster} \markbox{18330}{sets)} \markbox{18331}{the} same.

\end{enumerate}
