Steps \markbox{18332}{(1)} \markbox{18333}{and} \markbox{18334}{(3)} \markbox{18335}{can} \markbox{18336}{be} \markbox{18337}{thought} \markbox{18338}{of} \markbox{18339}{as} \markbox{18340}{\emph{moves}}, \markbox{18341}{where} \markbox{18342}{we} \markbox{18343}{only} \markbox{18344}{change} \markbox{18345}{one} \markbox{18346}{piece} \markbox{18347}{of} \markbox{18348}{data} \markbox{18349}{at} \markbox{18350}{a} \markbox{18351}{time,} \markbox{18352}{and} \markbox{18353}{we} \markbox{18354}{will} \markbox{18355}{see} \markbox{18356}{that} \markbox{18357}{type} \markbox{18358}{(3)} \markbox{18359}{moves} \markbox{18360}{are} \markbox{18361}{basically} \markbox{18362}{type} \markbox{18363}{(1)} \markbox{18364}{moves.}  \markbox{18365}{For} \markbox{18366}{step} \markbox{18367}{(2),} \markbox{18368}{we} \markbox{18369}{will} \markbox{18370}{want} \markbox{18371}{to} \markbox{18372}{iteratively} \markbox{18373}{perform} \markbox{18374}{type} \markbox{18375}{(1)} \markbox{18376}{moves} \markbox{18377}{by} \markbox{18378}{adding} \markbox{18379}{the} \markbox{18380}{extra} \markbox{18381}{cluster} \markbox{18382}{points} \markbox{18383}{of} \markbox{m18384}{$\calY' - \calY$} \markbox{18385}{to} \markbox{18386}{the} \markbox{18387}{setup} \markbox{m18388}{$(a,b;\calY)$}, \markbox{18389}{thereby} \markbox{18390}{shifting} \markbox{18391}{from} \markbox{m18392}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{18393}{to} \markbox{m18394}{$(a,b;\calY \cup \calY')$}.  \markbox{18395}{Then} \markbox{18396}{we} \markbox{18397}{make} \markbox{18398}{two} \markbox{18399}{type} \markbox{18400}{(3)} \markbox{18401}{moves} \markbox{18402}{to} \markbox{18403}{shift} \markbox{m18404}{$(a,b;\calY \cup \calY') \to (a',b;\calY \cup \calY') \to (a',b';\calY \cup \calY')$}.  \markbox{18405}{Finally,} \markbox{18406}{we} \markbox{18407}{make} \markbox{18408}{another} \markbox{18409}{sequence} \markbox{18410}{of} \markbox{18411}{iterated} \markbox{18412}{type} \markbox{18413}{(1)} \markbox{18414}{moves} \markbox{18415}{to} \markbox{18416}{shift} \markbox{18417}{from} \markbox{m18418}{$(a',b';\calY \cup \calY')$} \markbox{18419}{down} \markbox{18420}{to} \markbox{m18421}{$(a',b';\calY')$}.  \markbox{18422}{Since} \markbox{18423}{this} \markbox{18424}{total} \markbox{18425}{sequence} \markbox{18426}{of} \markbox{18427}{moves} \markbox{18428}{is} \markbox{18429}{bounded} \markbox{18430}{by} \markbox{m18431}{$N+2$}, \markbox{18432}{we} \markbox{18433}{will} \markbox{18434}{be} done.

For \markbox{18435}{step} \markbox{18436}{(1),} \markbox{18437}{there} \markbox{18438}{are} \markbox{18439}{two} \markbox{18440}{main} \markbox{18441}{cases---the} \markbox{18442}{\emph{split cluster}} \markbox{18443}{case,} \markbox{18444}{where} \markbox{18445}{we} \markbox{18446}{add} \markbox{18447}{a} \markbox{18448}{point} \markbox{m18449}{$z$} \markbox{18450}{to} \markbox{m18451}{$\calY$} \markbox{18452}{far} \markbox{18453}{from} \markbox{18454}{all} \markbox{m18455}{$\calY$}-clusters; \markbox{18456}{and} \markbox{18457}{the} \markbox{18458}{\emph{affected cluster}} \markbox{18459}{case,} \markbox{18460}{where} \markbox{m18461}{$z$} \markbox{18462}{is} \markbox{18463}{close} \markbox{18464}{to} \markbox{18465}{some} \markbox{18466}{existing} \markbox{m18467}{$\calY$}-cluster.  \markbox{18468}{See} \markbox{18469}{Figures} \ref{fig:split cluster} \markbox{18470}{and} \ref{fig:affected cluster}, \markbox{18471}{respectively,} \markbox{18472}{for} \markbox{18473}{relevant} \markbox{18474}{schematics.}  \markbox{18475}{The} \markbox{18476}{philosophy} \markbox{18477}{here} \markbox{18478}{is} \markbox{18479}{simple:} \markbox{18480}{adding} \markbox{18481}{a} \markbox{18482}{cluster} \markbox{18483}{point} \markbox{18484}{only} \markbox{18485}{affects} \markbox{18486}{things} \markbox{18487}{locally,} \markbox{18488}{thus} \markbox{18489}{one} \markbox{18490}{only} \markbox{18491}{needs} \markbox{18492}{to} \markbox{18493}{make} \markbox{18494}{bounded} \markbox{18495}{local} modifications.


Step \markbox{18496}{(2)} \markbox{18497}{of} \markbox{18498}{the} \markbox{18499}{proof} \markbox{18500}{now} \markbox{18501}{involves} \markbox{18502}{iteratively} \markbox{18503}{applying} \markbox{18504}{step} \markbox{18505}{(1),} \markbox{18506}{and} \markbox{18507}{thus} \markbox{18508}{one} \markbox{18509}{must} \markbox{18510}{show} \markbox{18511}{that} \markbox{18512}{one} \markbox{18513}{can} \markbox{18514}{coherently} \markbox{18515}{combine} \markbox{18516}{two} \markbox{18517}{pairs} \markbox{18518}{of} \markbox{18519}{stable} \markbox{18520}{decompositions} \markbox{18521}{across} \markbox{18522}{a} \markbox{18523}{common} \markbox{18524}{setup.}  \markbox{18525}{Figure} \ref{fig:iterated stable decomp} \markbox{18526}{shows} \markbox{18527}{a} \markbox{18528}{schematic} \markbox{18529}{for} \markbox{18530}{the} \markbox{18531}{argument,} \markbox{18532}{in} \markbox{18533}{which} \markbox{18534}{one} \markbox{18535}{has} \markbox{18536}{three} \markbox{18537}{stable} \markbox{18538}{trees} \markbox{m18539}{$T_1,T_2,T_3$} \markbox{18540}{with} \markbox{18541}{associated} \markbox{18542}{stable} \markbox{18543}{decompositions,} \markbox{18544}{so} \markbox{18545}{that} \markbox{18546}{those} \markbox{18547}{for} \markbox{m18548}{$T_1,T_2$} \markbox{18549}{and} \markbox{m18550}{$T_2,T_3$} \markbox{18551}{are} \markbox{18552}{compatible.}  \markbox{18553}{The} \markbox{18554}{idea} \markbox{18555}{is} \markbox{18556}{to} \markbox{18557}{intersect} \markbox{18558}{the} \markbox{18559}{two} \markbox{18560}{decompositions} \markbox{18561}{on} \markbox{m18562}{$T_2$} \markbox{18563}{and} \markbox{18564}{pull} \markbox{18565}{them} \markbox{18566}{back} \markbox{18567}{to} \markbox{m18568}{$T_1,T_3$}.

The \markbox{18569}{associated} \markbox{18570}{stability} \markbox{18571}{constants} \markbox{18572}{increase} \markbox{18573}{a} \markbox{18574}{controlled} \markbox{18575}{amount} \markbox{18576}{with} \markbox{18577}{each} \markbox{18578}{iteration,} \markbox{18579}{but} \markbox{18580}{we} \markbox{18581}{are} \markbox{18582}{assuming} \markbox{18583}{that} \markbox{18584}{we} \markbox{18585}{only} \markbox{18586}{need} \markbox{18587}{to} \markbox{18588}{perform} \markbox{18589}{boundedly-many} \markbox{18590}{such} \markbox{18591}{iterations} \markbox{18592}{in} \markbox{18593}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.


\smallskip

Finally, \markbox{18594}{step} \markbox{18595}{(3)} \markbox{18596}{is} \markbox{18597}{an} \markbox{18598}{application} \markbox{18599}{of} \markbox{18600}{steps} \markbox{18601}{(1)} \markbox{18602}{and} \markbox{18603}{(2).}  \markbox{18604}{To} \markbox{18605}{get} \markbox{18606}{the} \markbox{18607}{idea,} \markbox{18608}{we} \markbox{18609}{can} \markbox{18610}{consider} \markbox{18611}{the} \markbox{18612}{following} \markbox{18613}{restricted} \markbox{18614}{setup,} \markbox{18615}{which} \markbox{18616}{we} \markbox{18617}{highlight} \markbox{18618}{to} \markbox{18619}{focus} \markbox{18620}{on} \markbox{18621}{what} \markbox{18622}{happens} \markbox{18623}{when} \markbox{18624}{we} \markbox{18625}{perturb} \markbox{18626}{an} \markbox{18627}{endpoint.}  \markbox{18628}{Let} \markbox{m18629}{$a,b,a' \in \calZ$} \markbox{18630}{and} \markbox{m18631}{$\calY \subset \calZ$} \markbox{18632}{be} \markbox{18633}{finite} \markbox{18634}{with} \markbox{m18635}{$\calY \subset \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a,b)) \cap \calN_{\epsilon/2}(a',b)$}.  \markbox{18636}{The} \markbox{18637}{following} \markbox{18638}{collection} \markbox{18639}{of} \markbox{18640}{setups,} \markbox{18641}{each} \markbox{18642}{of} \markbox{18643}{which} \markbox{18644}{differs} \markbox{18645}{by} \markbox{18646}{adding} \markbox{18647}{or} \markbox{18648}{deleting} \markbox{18649}{one} \markbox{18650}{cluster} \markbox{18651}{point,} \markbox{18652}{or} \markbox{18653}{by} \markbox{18654}{switching} \markbox{18655}{the} \markbox{18656}{role} \markbox{18657}{that} \markbox{m18658}{$a,a'$} \markbox{18659}{or} \markbox{m18660}{$b,b'$} \markbox{18661}{play} \markbox{18662}{between} \markbox{18663}{cluster} \markbox{18664}{or} endpoint:
\vspace{-.09in}
\begin{multicols}{3}
\begin{enumerate}
\item $(a,b;\calY)$,
\item $(a,b;\calY \cup \{a\})$,
\item $(a,b;\calY \cup \{a, a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY \cup \{a,a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY \cup \{a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY)$.
\end{enumerate}
\end{multicols}

Hence \markbox{18665}{we} \markbox{18666}{can} \markbox{18667}{use} \markbox{18668}{steps} \markbox{18669}{(1),(2),} \markbox{18670}{(3)} \markbox{18671}{plus} \markbox{18672}{iteration} \markbox{18673}{to} \markbox{18674}{change} \markbox{18675}{the} \markbox{18676}{roles} \markbox{18677}{of} \markbox{18678}{endpoints} \markbox{18679}{once} \markbox{18680}{we} \markbox{18681}{have} \markbox{18682}{added} \markbox{18683}{all} \markbox{18684}{of} \markbox{18685}{the} \markbox{18686}{necessary} \markbox{18687}{cluster} \markbox{18688}{points.}  \markbox{18689}{See} \markbox{18690}{Appendix} \ref{app:SI} \markbox{18691}{for} \markbox{18692}{the} \markbox{18693}{full} argument.


\begin{figure}[b]
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=1\textwidth]{figures/split_cluster}
    \caption{Step (1) of the proof of Theorem \ref{thm:stable intervals}, split cluster case:  In the first figure, the two edge components of the two stable intervals are shown.  The point $z$ forms an individual cluster and therefore must be inserted as a vertex in the graph $\calG$, between clusters $C_1, C_2$.  Every cluster to the left of $C_1$ is unchanged, as are all of the connecting segments (in pink), and same for those to the right of $C_2$.  The second figure shows the stable decomposition of the stable intervals.  Here, we need to include the shadow of the cluster $z$ on $\lambda(C_1,C_2)$ as an unstable component.  This cuts $\lambda(C_1,C_2)$ into two segments, which are paired with $\lambda(C_1,z)$ and $\lambda(z,C_2)$, though these need to be slightly truncated so guarantee they have the same lengths; the unstable segments accomplishing this are red.  The third figure shows the stable decomposition for their $(r_1,r_2)$-thickenings, which are subsets of the edge components $T_e \subset T$ and $T'_e \subset T$, are indicated in brown.  Note that this can result in collapsing an entire edge component if its diameter is less than $r_2-2r_1$.  These brown segments refine the stable decompositions $T_s \subset T_e$ and $T'_s \subset T'_e$.}    \label{fig:split cluster}
\end{figure}

\newpage
\begin{figure}[!htb]
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=1\textwidth]{figures/affect_cluster}
    \caption{Step (1) of the proof of Theorem \ref{thm:stable intervals}, affected cluster case.  Two phenomena are shown.  In the top figure, there are three affected clusters, $P,Q,R$, for $(a,b;\calY)$ which combine with $z$ into a new cluster $C'$ for $(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$.  By definition, $P,Q,R$ must be $O(\epsilon)$ apart, and actually are adjacent in $\calG$.  The clusters $C_1,C_2$ appear in both setups, and the subgraph of $\calG$ to the left of $C_1$ coincides with the same subgraph for $\calG'$, and similarly for $C_2$.  So the corresponding (pink) components form (stable) components of $T_s \subset T_e$ and $T'_s \subset T'_e$.  The components of $T_e$ connecting $P,Q,R$ are declared unstable and, in this example, the components $\lambda(C_1,P)$ and $\lambda(R,C_2)$ of $T_e$ coincide with the components $\lambda(C_1,C')$ and $\lambda(C',C_2)$ of $T'_e$, and hence are stable.  The second figure shows the stable decomposition for the $(r_1,r_2)$-thickenings, which are just the thickenings of the components of $T_s = T'_s$, and hence are also exactly the same.  In the second example, the same discussion applies to the outside parts.  For the middle of the graph, $z$ combines with the cluster $A$, which results in pairs of segments $\lambda(C_1,A)$ and $\lambda(C_1, C')$, and $\lambda(A,C_2)$ and $\lambda(C',C_2)$, which have $O(\epsilon)$-close endpoints and are thus $O(\epsilon)$-Hausdorff close, with the same length up to error $O(\epsilon)$.  Small surgeries provide the required stable components for the stable intervals $T, T'$, shown in the third figure.  The fourth figure shows the stable decomposition for the $(R,r)$-thickenings of this example.}
    \label{fig:affected cluster}
\end{figure}

\begin{figure}[t]
    \centering
    \includegraphics[width=1\textwidth]{figures/iterated_stabledecomp}
    \caption{The proof of Theorem \ref{thm:stable intervals}, iterating stable decompositions: The idea for the iteration argument is to intersect the stable decompositions $T^1_{s,2} \cap T^3_{s,2} \subset T_2$ for $T_1,T_3$, respectively, and then use the isometries which identify the stable pairs for $T_1, T_2$ to give a refined stable decomposition for $(T_1,T_2)$, which can be combined with a refinement for $(T_2,T_3)$ via simple composition.  In the schematic (which is \emph{not} happening in $\calZ$), we have lined up the stable intervals $T_1,T_2,T_3$ to indicate how to refine the pairwise stable decompositions for $(T_1,T_2)$ and $(T_2,T_3)$ for one for $(T_1,T_3)$.  The orange segments correspond to cluster components of the intervals, while the blue and green segments correspond to the unstable components for the pairs $(T_1,T_2)$ and $(T_2,T_3)$, respectively.  The complement of the orange, blue, and green segments on $T_2$ form the refined stable decomposition on $T_2$, and the purple squares indicate how these segments induce refined stable decompositions on $T_1$ and $T_3$.}
    \label{fig:iterated stable decomp}
\end{figure}


\newpage
\section{Stable cubical models} \label{sec:stable cubes}

In \markbox{18694}{this} \markbox{18695}{section,} \markbox{18696}{we} \markbox{18697}{explain} \markbox{18698}{how} \markbox{18699}{to} \markbox{18700}{combine} \markbox{18701}{the} \markbox{18702}{cubulation} \markbox{18703}{machinery} \markbox{18704}{described} \markbox{18705}{in} \markbox{18706}{Sections} \ref{sec:interval systems}--\ref{sec:cubulation} \markbox{18707}{with} \markbox{18708}{the} \markbox{18709}{Controlling} \markbox{18710}{Domains} \markbox{18711}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains} \markbox{18712}{established} \markbox{18713}{in} \markbox{18714}{Section} \ref{sec:controlling domains} \markbox{18715}{and} \markbox{18716}{the} \markbox{18717}{Stable} \markbox{18718}{Interval} \markbox{18719}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{18720}{from} \markbox{18721}{Section} \ref{sec:stable intervals}.  \markbox{18722}{Over} \markbox{18723}{the} \markbox{18724}{first} \markbox{18725}{two} \markbox{18726}{subsections,} \markbox{18727}{we} \markbox{18728}{prove} \markbox{18729}{that} \markbox{18730}{our} \markbox{18731}{stable} \markbox{18732}{intervals} \markbox{18733}{can} \markbox{18734}{be} \markbox{18735}{plugged} \markbox{18736}{into} \markbox{18737}{our} \markbox{18738}{interval} \markbox{18739}{system} \markbox{18740}{machinery} \markbox{18741}{to} \markbox{18742}{produce} \markbox{18743}{an} \markbox{18744}{HFI} \markbox{18745}{for} \markbox{18746}{any} \markbox{18747}{pair} \markbox{18748}{of} \markbox{18749}{points} \markbox{m18750}{$a,b \in \calX$} \markbox{18751}{in} \markbox{18752}{an} HHS.

The \markbox{18753}{heart} \markbox{18754}{of} \markbox{18755}{the} \markbox{18756}{section} \markbox{18757}{is} \markbox{18758}{then} \markbox{18759}{explaining} \markbox{18760}{how} \markbox{18761}{to} \markbox{18762}{relate} \markbox{18763}{two} \markbox{18764}{such} \markbox{18765}{HFIs} \markbox{18766}{for} \markbox{18767}{a} \markbox{18768}{pair} \markbox{18769}{of} \markbox{18770}{points} \markbox{m18771}{$a,b$} \markbox{18772}{and} \markbox{18773}{a} \markbox{18774}{perturbed} \markbox{18775}{pair} \markbox{m18776}{$a',b'$}.  \markbox{18777}{We} \markbox{18778}{explain} \markbox{18779}{this} \markbox{18780}{below} \markbox{18781}{in} \markbox{18782}{detail} \markbox{18783}{in} \markbox{18784}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:perturbed to stable}.




\subsection{Stable intervals form an interval system}

Our \markbox{18785}{first} \markbox{18786}{goal} \markbox{18787}{is} \markbox{18788}{to} \markbox{18789}{explain} \markbox{18790}{how} \markbox{18791}{to} \markbox{18792}{take} \markbox{18793}{the} \markbox{18794}{family} \markbox{18795}{of} \markbox{18796}{stable} \markbox{18797}{intervals} \markbox{18798}{associated} \markbox{18799}{to} \markbox{18800}{a} \markbox{18801}{pair} \markbox{18802}{of} \markbox{18803}{points} \markbox{m18804}{$a, b\in \calX$} \markbox{18805}{and} \markbox{18806}{produce} \markbox{18807}{a} \markbox{18808}{hierarchical} \markbox{18809}{family} \markbox{18810}{of} intervals.


First, \markbox{18811}{we} \markbox{18812}{need} \markbox{18813}{to} \markbox{18814}{induce} \markbox{18815}{a} \markbox{18816}{collection} \markbox{18817}{of} \markbox{18818}{relative} \markbox{18819}{projections} \markbox{18820}{on} \markbox{18821}{the} \markbox{18822}{stable} \markbox{18823}{intervals} \markbox{18824}{which} \markbox{18825}{turn} \markbox{18826}{them} \markbox{18827}{into} \markbox{18828}{an} \markbox{m18829}{$R$}-interval \markbox{18830}{system} \markbox{18831}{(Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms}) \markbox{18832}{for} \markbox{18833}{a} \markbox{18834}{uniform} \markbox{m18835}{$R = R(\mathfrak S)>0$}.

Let \markbox{m18836}{$U \in \calU$}.  \markbox{18837}{Recall} \markbox{18838}{that} \markbox{18839}{the} \markbox{18840}{BGIA} \ref{ax:BGIA} \markbox{18841}{says} \markbox{18842}{that} \markbox{18843}{if} \markbox{m18844}{$d_V(a,b)$} \markbox{18845}{is} \markbox{18846}{sufficiently} \markbox{18847}{large} \markbox{18848}{for} \markbox{m18849}{$V \in \mathfrak S$}, \markbox{18850}{then} \markbox{m18851}{$\rho^V_U \subset \calN_{\ES}(\lambda(a,b))$} \markbox{18852}{when} \markbox{m18853}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{18854}{and,} \markbox{18855}{even} \markbox{18856}{better,} \markbox{m18857}{$\rho^V_U \subset \calN_{\ES}(a \cup b)$} \markbox{18858}{when} \markbox{m18859}{$V \pitchfork U$}.  \markbox{18860}{If} \markbox{18861}{we} \markbox{18862}{set} \markbox{m18863}{$\calY_U= \{\rho^V_U|V \nest U \in \calU\}$}, \markbox{18864}{then} \markbox{m18865}{$(\pi_U(a), \pi_U(b); \calY_U)$} \markbox{18866}{is} \markbox{18867}{an} \markbox{m18868}{$\epsilon$}-setup \markbox{18869}{in} \markbox{m18870}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{18871}{for} \markbox{m18872}{$\epsilon = 2\ES$} \markbox{18873}{in} \markbox{18874}{the} \markbox{18875}{sense} \markbox{18876}{of} \markbox{18877}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:stable setup}.  \markbox{18878}{In} \markbox{18879}{particular,} \markbox{18880}{our} \markbox{18881}{stable} \markbox{18882}{interval} \markbox{18883}{construction} \markbox{18884}{(Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure}) applies.

For \markbox{18885}{each} \markbox{m18886}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{18887}{let} \markbox{m18888}{$T_U = T_{U,e} \cup T_{U,c}$} \markbox{18889}{denote} \markbox{18890}{the} \markbox{18891}{stable} \markbox{18892}{interval} \markbox{18893}{for} \markbox{18894}{the} \markbox{18895}{setup} \markbox{m18896}{$(a,b;\calY_U)$} \markbox{18897}{in} \markbox{m18898}{$\calC(U)$}.  \markbox{18899}{Recall} \markbox{18900}{that} \markbox{18901}{each} \markbox{18902}{component} \markbox{18903}{of} \markbox{m18904}{$T_{U,c}$} \markbox{18905}{coincides} \markbox{18906}{with} \markbox{m18907}{$\mu(C)$} \markbox{18908}{for} \markbox{18909}{some} \markbox{18910}{cluster} \markbox{m18911}{$C$} \markbox{18912}{of} \markbox{18913}{points} \markbox{18914}{in} \markbox{m18915}{$\calY_U \cup \{a,b\}$} \markbox{18916}{(Subsection} \ref{subsec:clusters}).  \markbox{18917}{Importantly,} \markbox{18918}{item} \markbox{18919}{(2)} \markbox{18920}{of} \markbox{18921}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure} \markbox{18922}{says} \markbox{18923}{that} \markbox{m18924}{$\phi_U(\mu(C))$} \markbox{18925}{is} \markbox{m18926}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{18927}{(and} \markbox{18928}{hence} \markbox{m18929}{$O(\mathfrak S)$}) \markbox{18930}{Hausdorff} \markbox{18931}{close} \markbox{18932}{to} \markbox{m18933}{$C$} \markbox{18934}{itself.}  \markbox{18935}{This} \markbox{18936}{property} \markbox{18937}{is} \markbox{18938}{what} \markbox{18939}{makes} \markbox{18940}{the} \markbox{18941}{following} \markbox{18942}{definition} work:

\begin{definition}[Stable \markbox{18943}{interval} projections]\label{defn:stable interval projections}
For \markbox{18944}{each} \markbox{m18945}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{18946}{we} \markbox{18947}{define} \markbox{18948}{the} \markbox{18949}{following} \markbox{18950}{\emph{stable interval projections}}:
\begin{itemize}
\item {} For \markbox{18951}{each} \markbox{m18952}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{18953}{with} \markbox{m18954}{$V \nest U$}, \markbox{18955}{let} \markbox{m18956}{$C$} \markbox{18957}{be} \markbox{18958}{the} \markbox{18959}{cluster} \markbox{18960}{containing} \markbox{m18961}{$\rho^V_U$}.  \markbox{18962}{Define} 
$$\delta^V_U = \phi_U^{-1}(\hull_{\mu(C)}(p_{\phi_U(\mu(C))}(\rho^V_U))) \subset \mu(C),$$where \markbox{m18963}{$p_U:\calC(U) \to \phi_U(\mu(C))$} \markbox{18964}{is} \markbox{18965}{the} \markbox{18966}{closest} \markbox{18967}{point} \markbox{18968}{projection} \markbox{18969}{to} \markbox{18970}{the} \markbox{18971}{geodesic} \markbox{18972}{segment} \markbox{m18973}{$\phi_U(\mu(C)) = \mu(C)$}.
\item {} For \markbox{18974}{each} \markbox{m18975}{$V \in \calU$} \markbox{18976}{with} \markbox{m18977}{$V \pitchfork U$}, \markbox{18978}{let} \markbox{m18979}{$f \in \{a,b\}$} \markbox{18980}{denote} \markbox{18981}{the} \markbox{18982}{point} \markbox{18983}{(provided} \markbox{18984}{by} \markbox{18985}{Definition} \ref{defn:consistency}) \markbox{18986}{for} \markbox{18987}{which} \markbox{m18988}{$d_U(\pi_U(f), \rho^V_U)<\epsilon$}, \markbox{18989}{and} \markbox{18990}{let} \markbox{m18991}{$C$} \markbox{18992}{denote} \markbox{18993}{the} \markbox{18994}{cluster} \markbox{18995}{containing} \markbox{m18996}{$f$}.  \markbox{18997}{Again} \markbox{18998}{we} \markbox{18999}{define} \markbox{m19000}{$\delta^V_U = \phi_U^{-1}(\hull_{\mu(C)}(p_{\phi_U(\mu(C)}(\rho^V_U))) \subset \mu(C)$}.
\item {} If \markbox{m19001}{$U \nest V$}, \markbox{19002}{then} \markbox{19003}{we} \markbox{19004}{define} \markbox{19005}{the} \markbox{19006}{\emph{interval projection map}} \markbox{m19007}{$\delta^V_U:T_V \to T_U$} \markbox{19008}{by} \markbox{m19009}{$\delta^V_U = \phi^{-1}_U \circ p_{T_U} \circ \rho^V_U \circ \phi_V.$}
\end{itemize}
\end{definition}

The \markbox{19010}{next} \markbox{19011}{lemma} \markbox{19012}{says} \markbox{19013}{that} \markbox{19014}{these} \markbox{19015}{projections} \markbox{19016}{turn} \markbox{19017}{the} \markbox{19018}{family} \markbox{19019}{of} \markbox{19020}{stable} \markbox{19021}{intervals} \markbox{19022}{into} \markbox{19023}{an} \markbox{19024}{interval} \markbox{19025}{system.}  \markbox{19026}{The} \markbox{19027}{proof,} \markbox{19028}{which} \markbox{19029}{we} \markbox{19030}{leave} \markbox{19031}{to} \markbox{19032}{the} \markbox{19033}{reader,} \markbox{19034}{involves} \markbox{19035}{verifying} \markbox{19036}{the} \markbox{19037}{conditions} \markbox{19038}{of} \markbox{19039}{Definition} \ref{defn:interval axioms} \markbox{19040}{(and} \markbox{19041}{hence} \markbox{19042}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control}, \markbox{19043}{and} \markbox{19044}{one} \markbox{19045}{does} \markbox{19046}{this} \markbox{19047}{via} \markbox{19048}{Lemma} \ref{lem:rho control} \markbox{19049}{and} \markbox{19050}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure}.

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:stable interval system}
There \markbox{19051}{exists} \markbox{m19052}{$R_s = R_s(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19053}{so} \markbox{19054}{that} \markbox{19055}{the} \markbox{19056}{stable} \markbox{19057}{intervals} \markbox{m19058}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19059}{endowed} \markbox{19060}{with} \markbox{19061}{the} \markbox{19062}{stable} \markbox{19063}{interval} \markbox{19064}{projections} \markbox{19065}{forms} \markbox{19066}{an} \markbox{m19067}{$R_s$}-interval \markbox{19068}{system} \markbox{19069}{for} \markbox{m19070}{$a,b$}.
\end{lemma}



\subsection{Thickenings of stable intervals, their collapses, and HFIs}\label{subsec:collapsed stable intervals}

In \markbox{19071}{this} \markbox{19072}{subsection,} \markbox{19073}{we} \markbox{19074}{explain} \markbox{19075}{why} \markbox{19076}{collapsed} \markbox{19077}{thickened} \markbox{19078}{interval} \markbox{19079}{systems} \markbox{19080}{of} \markbox{19081}{stable} \markbox{19082}{intevals} \markbox{19083}{form} HFIs.

To \markbox{19084}{begin,} \markbox{19085}{in} \markbox{19086}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:thickenings}, \markbox{19087}{we} \markbox{19088}{took} \markbox{19089}{an} \markbox{19090}{interval} \markbox{19091}{system} \markbox{m19092}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19093}{along} \markbox{19094}{with} \markbox{19095}{its} \markbox{19096}{relative} \markbox{19097}{projection} \markbox{19098}{data} \markbox{m19099}{$\delta^V_U$}, \markbox{19100}{and} \markbox{19101}{then} \markbox{19102}{thickened} \markbox{19103}{the} \markbox{19104}{intervals} \markbox{19105}{along} \markbox{19106}{the} \markbox{19107}{components} \markbox{m19108}{$B$} \markbox{19109}{of} \markbox{19110}{a} \markbox{19111}{decomposition} \markbox{m19112}{$T_U = A \cup B$}, \markbox{19113}{where} \markbox{m19114}{$B$} \markbox{19115}{consists} \markbox{19116}{of} \markbox{19117}{these} \markbox{m19118}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{19119}{along} \markbox{19120}{with} \markbox{19121}{the} \markbox{19122}{marked} \markbox{19123}{points} \markbox{m19124}{$a_U,b_U$}.  \markbox{19125}{Then} \markbox{19126}{in} \markbox{19127}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:collapsing}, \markbox{19128}{we} \markbox{19129}{collapsed} \markbox{19130}{along} \markbox{19131}{this} \markbox{19132}{thickening} \markbox{19133}{which} \markbox{19134}{induced} \markbox{19135}{collapsed} \markbox{19136}{relative} \markbox{19137}{projections} \markbox{19138}{on} \markbox{19139}{the} \markbox{19140}{collapsed} \markbox{19141}{intervals.}  \markbox{19142}{On} \markbox{19143}{the} \markbox{19144}{other} \markbox{19145}{hand,} \markbox{19146}{the} \markbox{19147}{thickenings} \markbox{19148}{of} \markbox{19149}{stable} \markbox{19150}{intervals} \markbox{19151}{we} \markbox{19152}{considered} \markbox{19153}{in} \markbox{19154}{the} \markbox{19155}{Stable} \markbox{19156}{Intervals} \markbox{19157}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{19158}{were} \markbox{19159}{thickenings} \markbox{19160}{along} \markbox{19161}{the} \markbox{19162}{cluster} components.

The \markbox{19163}{following} \markbox{19164}{lemma,} \markbox{19165}{whose} \markbox{19166}{proof} \markbox{19167}{we} \markbox{19168}{leave} \markbox{19169}{to} \markbox{19170}{the} \markbox{19171}{reader,} \markbox{19172}{says} \markbox{19173}{that} \markbox{19174}{these} \markbox{19175}{thickenings} \markbox{19176}{coincide,} \markbox{19177}{and} \markbox{19178}{hence} \markbox{19179}{that} \markbox{19180}{the} \markbox{19181}{corresponding} \markbox{19182}{collapsed} \markbox{19183}{trees} \markbox{19184}{are} identical:

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:same thickenings}
For \markbox{19185}{any} \markbox{m19186}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{19187}{let} \markbox{m19188}{$T_U = A \cup B$} \markbox{19189}{be} \markbox{19190}{the} \markbox{19191}{decomposition} \markbox{19192}{where} \markbox{m19193}{$B$} \markbox{19194}{is} \markbox{19195}{the} \markbox{19196}{union} \markbox{19197}{of} \markbox{19198}{all} \markbox{m19199}{$\delta^V_U$} \markbox{19200}{for} \markbox{m19201}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{19202}{along} \markbox{19203}{with} \markbox{m19204}{$a_U,b_U$}.  \markbox{19205}{Let} \markbox{m19206}{$T_U = T_{U,e} \cup T_{U,c}$} \markbox{19207}{denote} \markbox{19208}{the} \markbox{19209}{decomposition} \markbox{19210}{provided} \markbox{19211}{by} \markbox{19212}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure}.  \markbox{19213}{There} \markbox{19214}{exists} \markbox{m19215}{$R_3 = R_3(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19216}{so} \markbox{19217}{that} \markbox{19218}{for} \markbox{19219}{any} \markbox{m19220}{$r_1>R_3$} \markbox{19221}{and} \markbox{m19222}{$r_2>0$}, \markbox{19223}{the} \markbox{m19224}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{19225}{of} \markbox{m19226}{$T_U$} \markbox{19227}{along} \markbox{m19228}{$B$} \markbox{19229}{and} \markbox{19230}{along} \markbox{m19231}{$T_{U,c}$} \markbox{19232}{are} identical.
\end{lemma}




The \markbox{19233}{upshot} \markbox{19234}{of} \markbox{19235}{Lemmas} \ref{lem:stable interval system} \markbox{19236}{and} \ref{lem:same thickenings} \markbox{19237}{is} \markbox{19238}{that} \markbox{19239}{we} \markbox{19240}{can} \markbox{19241}{plug} \markbox{19242}{our} \markbox{19243}{stable} \markbox{19244}{intervals} \markbox{19245}{directly} \markbox{19246}{into} \markbox{19247}{our} \markbox{19248}{interval} \markbox{19249}{system} \markbox{19250}{machinery.}  \markbox{19251}{The} \markbox{19252}{next} \markbox{19253}{step} \markbox{19254}{is} \markbox{19255}{to} \markbox{19256}{explain} \markbox{19257}{how} \markbox{19258}{to} \markbox{19259}{produce} \markbox{19260}{an} \markbox{19261}{HFI} \markbox{19262}{(Definition} \ref{defn:HFI}) \markbox{19263}{from} \markbox{19264}{this} \markbox{19265}{system} \markbox{19266}{using} \markbox{19267}{the} \markbox{19268}{thickenings} \markbox{19269}{and} \markbox{19270}{collapsing} \markbox{19271}{procedures} \markbox{19272}{discussed} \markbox{19273}{in} \markbox{19274}{Subsections} \ref{subsec:thickenings} \markbox{19275}{and} \ref{subsec:collapsing}.

Continuing \markbox{19276}{with} \markbox{19277}{our} \markbox{19278}{notation,} \markbox{19279}{Lemma} \ref{lem:stable interval system} \markbox{19280}{says} \markbox{19281}{that} \markbox{19282}{the} \markbox{19283}{stable} \markbox{19284}{intervals} \markbox{m19285}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19286}{endowed} \markbox{19287}{with} \markbox{19288}{the} \markbox{19289}{interval} \markbox{19290}{projections} \markbox{19291}{via} \markbox{19292}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable interval projections} \markbox{19293}{form} \markbox{19294}{an} \markbox{m19295}{$R_s$}-interval \markbox{19296}{system} \markbox{19297}{for} \markbox{m19298}{$a,b\in \calX$}, \markbox{19299}{where} \markbox{m19300}{$R_s = R_s(\mathfrak S)>0$}.  \markbox{19301}{Since} \markbox{m19302}{$R_s= R_s(\mathfrak S)>0$}, \markbox{19303}{Proposition} \ref{prop:hPsi defined} \markbox{19304}{and} \markbox{19305}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{19306}{provide} \markbox{19307}{constants} \markbox{m19308}{$R_1 = R_1(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19309}{and} \markbox{m19310}{$R_2(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19311}{so} \markbox{19312}{that} \markbox{19313}{for} \markbox{19314}{any} \markbox{m19315}{$r_1\geq R_1$} \markbox{19316}{and} \markbox{m19317}{$r_2 \geq R_2$}, \markbox{19318}{the} \markbox{19319}{conclusions} \markbox{19320}{of} \markbox{19321}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{19322}{hold} \markbox{19323}{for} \markbox{19324}{the} \markbox{19325}{family} \markbox{19326}{of} \markbox{19327}{collapsed} \markbox{19328}{intervals} \markbox{m19329}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19330}{obtained} \markbox{19331}{from} \markbox{19332}{the} \markbox{m19333}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{19334}{of} \markbox{19335}{the} \markbox{19336}{system} \markbox{m19337}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$}.  \markbox{19338}{We} \markbox{19339}{also} \markbox{19340}{want} \markbox{19341}{to} \markbox{19342}{assume} \markbox{19343}{that} \markbox{m19344}{$r_1>R_3 = R_3(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19345}{so} \markbox{19346}{that} \markbox{19347}{Lemma} \ref{lem:same thickenings} holds.

The \markbox{19348}{next} \markbox{19349}{proposition} \markbox{19350}{states} \markbox{19351}{that} \markbox{19352}{as} \markbox{19353}{long} \markbox{19354}{as} \markbox{m19355}{$r_1$} \markbox{19356}{is} \markbox{19357}{a} \markbox{19358}{positive} \markbox{19359}{integer,} \markbox{19360}{the} \markbox{19361}{collapsed} \markbox{19362}{intervals} \markbox{m19363}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{19364}{are} \markbox{19365}{all} \markbox{19366}{simplicial} \markbox{19367}{intervals,} \markbox{19368}{where} \markbox{19369}{the} \markbox{19370}{collapsed} \markbox{19371}{points} \markbox{19372}{lie} \markbox{19373}{at} \markbox{19374}{vertices.}  \markbox{19375}{The} \markbox{19376}{proof} \markbox{19377}{is} \markbox{19378}{a} \markbox{19379}{straightforward} \markbox{19380}{application} \markbox{19381}{of} \markbox{19382}{the} \markbox{19383}{ideas} \markbox{19384}{in} \markbox{19385}{the} \markbox{19386}{preceding} \markbox{19387}{sections,} \markbox{19388}{so} \markbox{19389}{we} \markbox{19390}{leave} \markbox{19391}{it} \markbox{19392}{to} \markbox{19393}{the} reader.

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:stable HFI}
As \markbox{19394}{long} \markbox{19395}{as} \markbox{m19396}{$r_1\geq \max\{R_1,R_3\}$} \markbox{19397}{is} \markbox{19398}{a} \markbox{19399}{positive} \markbox{19400}{integer} \markbox{19401}{and} \markbox{m19402}{$r_2\geq R_2$}, \markbox{19403}{the} \markbox{19404}{family} \markbox{19405}{of} \markbox{19406}{collapsed} \markbox{19407}{stable} \markbox{19408}{intervals} \markbox{m19409}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19410}{associated} \markbox{19411}{to} \markbox{19412}{an} \markbox{m19413}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{19414}{of} \markbox{m19415}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19416}{along} \markbox{m19417}{$T_{U,c}$} \markbox{19418}{and} \markbox{19419}{endowed} \markbox{19420}{with} \markbox{19421}{their} \markbox{19422}{collapsed} \markbox{19423}{projections} \markbox{19424}{forms} \markbox{19425}{a} \markbox{19426}{hierarchical} \markbox{19427}{family} \markbox{19428}{of} intervals.
\end{proposition} 



We \markbox{19429}{note} \markbox{19430}{the} \markbox{19431}{following} \markbox{19432}{immediate} \markbox{19433}{corollary} \markbox{19434}{of} \markbox{19435}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable HFI} \markbox{19436}{and} \markbox{19437}{Theorem} \ref{thm:Q CCC}:

\begin{corollary}\label{cor:stable HFI cube}
Let \markbox{m19438}{$a,b \in \calX$}, \markbox{m19439}{$K > K_0$} \markbox{19440}{for} \markbox{m19441}{$K_0$} \markbox{19442}{as} \markbox{19443}{in} \markbox{19444}{Theorem} \ref{thm:DF} \markbox{19445}{and} \markbox{m19446}{$\calU = \Rel_K(a,b)$}.  \markbox{19447}{Let} \markbox{m19448}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19449}{be} \markbox{19450}{the} \markbox{19451}{associated} \markbox{19452}{family} \markbox{19453}{of} \markbox{19454}{stable} \markbox{19455}{intervals.}  \markbox{19456}{Then} \markbox{19457}{the} \markbox{19458}{hierarchical} \markbox{19459}{hull} \markbox{m19460}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{19461}{is} \markbox{19462}{quasi-isometric} \markbox{19463}{to} \markbox{19464}{the} \markbox{19465}{dual} \markbox{19466}{cube} \markbox{19467}{complex} \markbox{19468}{of} \markbox{19469}{the} \markbox{19470}{associated} \markbox{19471}{HFI,} \markbox{19472}{with} \markbox{19473}{constants} \markbox{19474}{depending} \markbox{19475}{only} \markbox{19476}{on} \markbox{m19477}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{19478}{and} \markbox{m19479}{$K$}.
\end{corollary}





\subsection{From a perturbed pair to a family of stable decompositions} \label{subsec:perturbed to stable}

In \markbox{19480}{this} \markbox{19481}{subsection,} \markbox{19482}{we} \markbox{19483}{explain} \markbox{19484}{how} \markbox{19485}{the} \markbox{19486}{basic} \markbox{19487}{setup} \markbox{19488}{of} \markbox{19489}{this} \markbox{19490}{paper} \markbox{19491}{can} \markbox{19492}{be} \markbox{19493}{plugged} \markbox{19494}{into} \markbox{19495}{the} \markbox{19496}{machinery} \markbox{19497}{we} \markbox{19498}{have} \markbox{19499}{built} \markbox{19500}{so} far.

For \markbox{19501}{the} \markbox{19502}{rest} \markbox{19503}{of} \markbox{19504}{this} \markbox{19505}{section,} \markbox{19506}{assume} \markbox{19507}{that} \markbox{19508}{we} \markbox{19509}{have} \markbox{19510}{a} \markbox{19511}{colorable} \markbox{19512}{HHS} \markbox{m19513}{$(\calX, \mathfrak S)$} \markbox{19514}{endowed} \markbox{19515}{with} \markbox{19516}{the} \markbox{19517}{stable} \markbox{19518}{projections} \markbox{19519}{from} \markbox{19520}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains}.  \markbox{19521}{Let} \markbox{m19522}{$K > K_0=K_0(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19523}{be} \markbox{19524}{as} \markbox{19525}{in} \markbox{19526}{item} \markbox{19527}{(2)} \markbox{19528}{of} \markbox{19529}{that} \markbox{19530}{theorem.}  



Also \markbox{19531}{for} \markbox{19532}{the} \markbox{19533}{rest} \markbox{19534}{of} \markbox{19535}{this} \markbox{19536}{section,} \markbox{19537}{fix} \markbox{m19538}{$a,b,a',b' \in \calX$} \markbox{19539}{so} \markbox{19540}{that} \markbox{m19541}{$d_{\calX}(a,a'), d_{\calX}(b,b') \leq 1$}.  \markbox{19542}{We} \markbox{19543}{refer} \markbox{19544}{to} \markbox{19545}{the} \markbox{19546}{points} \markbox{m19547}{$a',b'$} \markbox{19548}{as} \markbox{19549}{a} \markbox{19550}{\emph{perturbed pair}} \markbox{19551}{from} \markbox{m19552}{$a,b$}.  \markbox{19553}{Let} \markbox{m19554}{$\calU = \Rel_{K}(a,b)$} \markbox{19555}{and} \markbox{m19556}{$\calU' = \Rel_{K}(a',b')$}.  \markbox{19557}{Let} \markbox{m19558}{$\{T_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19559}{and} \markbox{m19560}{$\{T'_U\}_{U \in \calU'}$} \markbox{19561}{denote} \markbox{19562}{the} \markbox{19563}{families} \markbox{19564}{of} \markbox{19565}{stable} \markbox{19566}{intervals} \markbox{19567}{produced} \markbox{19568}{as} \markbox{19569}{above.} 

The \markbox{19570}{first} \markbox{19571}{thing} \markbox{19572}{to} \markbox{19573}{observe} \markbox{19574}{is} \markbox{19575}{that} \markbox{19576}{item} \markbox{19577}{(2)(a)} \markbox{19578}{of} \markbox{19579}{Controlling} \markbox{19580}{Domains} \markbox{19581}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains} \markbox{19582}{provides} \markbox{19583}{that} 
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m19584}{$|\calU \triangle \calU'|<N_0 = N_0(\mathfrak S)$}, and
\item {} Each \markbox{19585}{domain} \markbox{m19586}{$V \in \calU \triangle \calU'$} \markbox{19587}{satisfies} \markbox{m19588}{$d_V(a,b) \leq K'$} \markbox{19589}{and} \markbox{m19590}{$d_V(a',b') \leq K'$}, \markbox{19591}{where} \markbox{m19592}{$|K-K'|$} \markbox{19593}{is} \markbox{19594}{bounded} \markbox{19595}{in} \markbox{19596}{terms} \markbox{19597}{of} \markbox{m19598}{$\mathfrak S$}.
\end{enumerate}

Item \markbox{19599}{(2)} \markbox{19600}{plus} \markbox{19601}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{19602}{says} \markbox{19603}{that} \markbox{19604}{each} \markbox{19605}{of} \markbox{19606}{the} \markbox{19607}{associated} \markbox{19608}{collapsed} \markbox{19609}{intervals} \markbox{m19610}{$\hT_V$} \markbox{19611}{or} \markbox{m19612}{$\hT'_V$} \markbox{19613}{for} \markbox{m19614}{$V\in \calU \triangle \calU'$} \markbox{19615}{has} \markbox{19616}{bounded} \markbox{19617}{diameter.}  \markbox{19618}{For} \markbox{19619}{the} \markbox{19620}{rest} \markbox{19621}{of} \markbox{19622}{the} \markbox{19623}{domains,} \markbox{19624}{namely} \markbox{19625}{the} \markbox{19626}{domains} \markbox{m19627}{$U \in \calU_0 = \calU \cap \calU'$}, \markbox{19628}{we} \markbox{19629}{want} \markbox{19630}{to} \markbox{19631}{obtain} \markbox{19632}{compatible} \markbox{19633}{stable} \markbox{19634}{decompositions} \markbox{19635}{between} \markbox{19636}{the} \markbox{19637}{intervals} \markbox{m19638}{$T_U$} \markbox{19639}{and} \markbox{m19640}{$T'_U$}, \markbox{19641}{which} \markbox{19642}{we} \markbox{19643}{do} \markbox{19644}{as} follows.

First, \markbox{19645}{observe} \markbox{19646}{that} \markbox{19647}{if} \markbox{m19648}{$V \nest U \in \calU_0$}, \markbox{19649}{then} \markbox{m19650}{$d_V(a,b)\geq K>\ES$} \markbox{19651}{and} \markbox{m19652}{$d_V(a',b') \geq K> \ES$}, \markbox{19653}{so} \markbox{19654}{the} \markbox{19655}{BGIA} \ref{ax:BGIA} \markbox{19656}{implies} \markbox{19657}{that} \markbox{m19658}{$\rho^V_U \subset \calN_{\ES}(\lambda_U(a,b)) \cap \calN_{\ES}(\lambda_U(a',b'))$}, \markbox{19659}{where} \markbox{m19660}{$\lambda_U$} \markbox{19661}{is} \markbox{19662}{the} \markbox{19663}{function} \markbox{19664}{which} \markbox{19665}{assigns} \markbox{19666}{a} \markbox{19667}{geodesic} \markbox{19668}{in} \markbox{m19669}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{19670}{to} \markbox{19671}{any} \markbox{19672}{pair} \markbox{19673}{of} \markbox{19674}{points} \markbox{19675}{from} \markbox{19676}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:stable setup}.  \markbox{19677}{Hence} \markbox{19678}{taking} \markbox{m19679}{$\epsilon = 2\ES$} \markbox{19680}{in} \markbox{19681}{our} \markbox{19682}{stable} \markbox{19683}{tree} \markbox{19684}{setup} \markbox{19685}{suffices} \markbox{19686}{to} \markbox{19687}{make} \markbox{m19688}{$(\pi_U(a),\pi_U(b);\calY_U)$} \markbox{19689}{and} \markbox{m19690}{$(\pi_U(a'),\pi_U(b');\calY'_U)$} \markbox{19691}{into} \markbox{m19692}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{19693}{in} \markbox{m19694}{$\calC(U)$} \markbox{19695}{(item} \markbox{19696}{(1)} \markbox{19697}{of} \markbox{19698}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}).

Moreover, \markbox{19699}{for} \markbox{19700}{each} \markbox{m19701}{$U \in \calU_0$}, \markbox{19702}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains} \markbox{19703}{provides} \markbox{19704}{that} 
\begin{itemize}
\item[(a)]{}  \markbox{19705}{The} \markbox{m19706}{$\rho$}-sets \markbox{19707}{for} \markbox{19708}{the} \markbox{19709}{domains} \markbox{19710}{in} \markbox{m19711}{$\calU$} \markbox{19712}{and} \markbox{m19713}{$\calU'$} \markbox{19714}{which} \markbox{19715}{nest} \markbox{19716}{into} \markbox{m19717}{$U$}---namely \markbox{m19718}{$\calY_U$} \markbox{19719}{and} \markbox{m19720}{$\calY'_U$} \markbox{19721}{respectively---satisfy} \markbox{m19722}{$|\calY_U \triangle \calY'_U| < N_0 = N_0(\mathfrak S)$}, and
\item[(b)]{}  \markbox{19723}{If} \markbox{m19724}{$\calU^*_0 \subset \calU_0$} \markbox{19725}{is} \markbox{19726}{the} \markbox{19727}{set} \markbox{19728}{of} \markbox{19729}{domains} \markbox{m19730}{$U \in \calU_0$} \markbox{19731}{for} \markbox{19732}{which} \markbox{m19733}{$\calY_U \neq \calY'_U$} \markbox{19734}{or} \markbox{m19735}{$\pi_U(a) \neq \pi_U(a')$} \markbox{19736}{or} \markbox{m19737}{$\pi_U(b) \neq \pi_U(b')$}, \markbox{19738}{then} \markbox{m19739}{$\#\calU^*_0 < N_0$}.
\end{itemize}

Hence, \markbox{19740}{by} \markbox{19741}{item} \markbox{19742}{(a),} \markbox{19743}{these} \markbox{m19744}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{19745}{are} \markbox{m19746}{$(N_0, \epsilon)$}-admissible \markbox{19747}{in} \markbox{19748}{the} \markbox{19749}{sense} \markbox{19750}{of} \markbox{19751}{item} \markbox{19752}{(2)} \markbox{19753}{of} \markbox{19754}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{19755}{for} \markbox{19756}{all} \markbox{19757}{domains} \markbox{19758}{in} \markbox{m19759}{$\calU_0$}, \markbox{19760}{while} \markbox{19761}{item} \markbox{19762}{(b)} \markbox{19763}{says} \markbox{19764}{that} \markbox{19765}{for} \markbox{19766}{domains} \markbox{19767}{in} \markbox{m19768}{$\calU_0 - \calU^*_0$}, \markbox{19769}{these} \markbox{m19770}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{19771}{exactly} \markbox{19772}{coincide.}  \markbox{19773}{Thus} \markbox{19774}{item} \markbox{19775}{(2)} \markbox{19776}{of} \markbox{19777}{the} \markbox{19778}{Stable} \markbox{19779}{Intervals} \markbox{19780}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{19781}{implies} \markbox{19782}{that} \markbox{19783}{the} \markbox{m19784}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{19785}{of} \markbox{19786}{their} \markbox{19787}{stable} \markbox{19788}{intervals} \markbox{m19789}{$T_U, T'_U$} \markbox{19790}{admit} \markbox{m19791}{$L_s$}-compatible \markbox{19792}{stable} \markbox{19793}{decompositions,} \markbox{19794}{where} \markbox{m19795}{$L_s=L_s(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19796}{by} \markbox{19797}{choosing} \markbox{m19798}{$r_1 = \max\{R_1,R_3\}$} \markbox{19799}{and} \markbox{m19800}{$r_2 = R_2$}, \markbox{19801}{since} \markbox{19802}{the} \markbox{19803}{constants} \markbox{m19804}{$R_i = R_i(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{19805}{depend} \markbox{19806}{only} \markbox{19807}{on} \markbox{m19808}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{19809}{In} \markbox{19810}{particular,} \markbox{19811}{we} have:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:stable interval decomp}
For \markbox{19812}{each} \markbox{m19813}{$U \in \calU_0$}, \markbox{19814}{the} \markbox{m19815}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{19816}{of} \markbox{19817}{the} \markbox{19818}{stable} \markbox{19819}{intervals} \markbox{m19820}{$T_U = T_{U,e} \cup T_{U,c}$} \markbox{19821}{and} \markbox{m19822}{$T'_U = T'_{U,e} \cup T'_{U,c}$} \markbox{19823}{along} \markbox{m19824}{$T_{U,c}, T'_{U,c}$} \markbox{19825}{respectively} \markbox{19826}{admit} \markbox{m19827}{$L_s$}-compatible \markbox{19828}{stable} \markbox{19829}{decompositions,} \markbox{19830}{where} \markbox{m19831}{$L_s = L_s(\mathfrak S)>0$}.
\begin{itemize}
\item {} Moreover, \markbox{19832}{if} \markbox{m19833}{$U \in \calU_0 - \calU^*_0$}, \markbox{19834}{then} \markbox{m19835}{$T_U = T'_U$} \markbox{19836}{and} \markbox{19837}{these} \markbox{19838}{thickenings} \markbox{19839}{coincide} exactly.
\end{itemize}
\end{proposition}

For \markbox{19840}{each} \markbox{m19841}{$U \in \calU_0$}, \markbox{19842}{let} \markbox{m19843}{$\Delta_U:\hT_U \to \hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{19844}{and} \markbox{m19845}{$\Delta'_U:\hT'_U \to \hT'_{U,0}$} \markbox{19846}{denote} \markbox{19847}{the} \markbox{19848}{maps} \markbox{19849}{which} \markbox{19850}{collapse} \markbox{19851}{the} \markbox{19852}{unstable} \markbox{19853}{components} \markbox{19854}{these} \markbox{19855}{decompositions} \markbox{19856}{to} \markbox{19857}{points;} \markbox{19858}{we} \markbox{19859}{note} \markbox{19860}{that} \markbox{19861}{these} \markbox{19862}{maps} \markbox{19863}{are} \markbox{19864}{the} \markbox{19865}{identity} \markbox{19866}{when} \markbox{m19867}{$U \in \calU_0- \calU^*_0$}.  \markbox{19868}{By} \markbox{19869}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{19870}{of} \markbox{19871}{a} \markbox{19872}{stable} \markbox{19873}{decomposition,} \markbox{19874}{the} \markbox{19875}{subintervals} \markbox{19876}{of} \markbox{19877}{the} \markbox{m19878}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{19879}{and} \markbox{m19880}{$\hT'_U$} \markbox{19881}{being} \markbox{19882}{collapsed} \markbox{19883}{for} \markbox{m19884}{$U \in \calU_0$} \markbox{19885}{along} \markbox{19886}{with} \markbox{19887}{the} \markbox{19888}{whole} \markbox{19889}{intervals} \markbox{m19890}{$\hT_V, \hT'_V$} \markbox{19891}{(whichever} \markbox{19892}{is} \markbox{19893}{defined)} \markbox{19894}{for} \markbox{m19895}{$V \in \calU \triangle \calU'$} \markbox{19896}{collectively} \markbox{19897}{form} \markbox{m19898}{$(L_s^2+2K'N_0)$}-admissible \markbox{19899}{simplicial} \markbox{19900}{trimming} \markbox{19901}{setups} \markbox{19902}{for} \markbox{m19903}{$\{\hT_U\}_{U \in \calU}$} \markbox{19904}{and} \markbox{m19905}{$\{\hT'_U\}_{U \in \calU'}$}, \markbox{19906}{in} \markbox{19907}{the} \markbox{19908}{sense} \markbox{19909}{of} \markbox{19910}{Definition} \ref{defn:simplicial trimming setup}.  \markbox{19911}{This} \markbox{19912}{is} \markbox{19913}{because} \markbox{19914}{the} \markbox{19915}{set} \markbox{m19916}{$(\calU \cup \calU') - \calU_0$} \markbox{19917}{has} \markbox{19918}{at} \markbox{19919}{most} \markbox{m19920}{$N_0$}-many \markbox{19921}{domains} \markbox{19922}{by} \markbox{19923}{(1)} \markbox{19924}{above,} \markbox{19925}{each} \markbox{19926}{of} \markbox{19927}{which} \markbox{19928}{has} \markbox{19929}{diameter} \markbox{19930}{bounded} \markbox{19931}{by} \markbox{m19932}{$K'$}, \markbox{19933}{while} \markbox{19934}{the} \markbox{19935}{unstable} \markbox{19936}{pieces} \markbox{19937}{for} \markbox{19938}{the} \markbox{19939}{domains} \markbox{19940}{in} \markbox{m19941}{$\calU_0$} \markbox{19942}{consist} \markbox{19943}{of} \markbox{19944}{at} \markbox{19945}{most} \markbox{m19946}{$L_2$}-many \markbox{19947}{pieces} \markbox{19948}{of} \markbox{19949}{diameter} \markbox{19950}{at} \markbox{19951}{most} \markbox{m19952}{$L_2$}.

Set \markbox{m19953}{$L_2^2 + 2K'N_0 = S_0$}, \markbox{19954}{which} \markbox{19955}{we} \markbox{19956}{note} \markbox{19957}{depends} \markbox{19958}{only} \markbox{19959}{on} \markbox{m19960}{$\mathfrak S$} \markbox{19961}{and} \markbox{19962}{our} \markbox{19963}{choice} \markbox{19964}{of} \markbox{m19965}{$K$}.  \markbox{19966}{We} \markbox{19967}{now} \markbox{19968}{obtain} \markbox{19969}{the} \markbox{19970}{following} \markbox{19971}{from} \markbox{19972}{Theorem} \ref{thm:simplicial tree trimming} \markbox{19973}{and} \markbox{19974}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval decomp}:

\begin{proposition} \label{prop:stable collapse}
The \markbox{19975}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} The \markbox{19976}{collections} \markbox{m19977}{$\{\hT_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$} \markbox{19978}{and} \markbox{m19979}{$\{\hT'_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$} \markbox{19980}{are} \markbox{19981}{HFIs.}  \markbox{19982}{Let} \markbox{m19983}{$\calQ_0, \calQ'_0$} \markbox{19984}{denote} \markbox{19985}{their} \markbox{19986}{corresponding} \markbox{m19987}{$0$}-consistent subsets.
\item {} The \markbox{19988}{combined} \markbox{19989}{maps} \markbox{m19990}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ_0$} \markbox{19991}{and} \markbox{m19992}{$\Delta':\calQ' \to \calQ'_0$} \markbox{19993}{satisfy} \markbox{m19994}{$\Delta(\calQ) = \calQ_0$} \markbox{19995}{and} \markbox{m19996}{$\Delta'(\calQ') = \calQ'_0$} \markbox{19997}{and} \markbox{19998}{are} \markbox{19999}{both} \markbox{m20000}{$(1, S_0^2)$}-quasi-isometries.
\item {} There \markbox{20001}{exists} \markbox{20002}{maps} \markbox{m20003}{$\Xi:\calQ_0 \to \calQ$} \markbox{20004}{and} \markbox{m20005}{$\Xi':\calQ'_0 \to \calQ'$} \markbox{20006}{with} \markbox{m20007}{$\Delta \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ_0}$} \markbox{20008}{and} \markbox{m20009}{$\Delta' \circ \Xi' = id_{\calQ'_0}$}.
\item {} At \markbox{20010}{the} \markbox{20011}{level} \markbox{20012}{of} \markbox{20013}{cube} \markbox{20014}{complexes,} \markbox{20015}{the} \markbox{20016}{maps} \markbox{m20017}{$\Delta\calQ \to \calQ_0$} \markbox{20018}{and} \markbox{m20019}{$\Delta':\calQ' \to \calQ'_0$} \markbox{20020}{delete} \markbox{20021}{at} \markbox{20022}{most} \markbox{m20023}{$S_0^2$}-many hyperplanes.
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

Using \markbox{20024}{this} \markbox{20025}{proposition,} \markbox{20026}{we} \markbox{20027}{can} \markbox{20028}{define} \markbox{20029}{maps} \markbox{m20030}{$\hO_0:\calQ_0 \to \calX$} \markbox{20031}{and} \markbox{m20032}{$\hO'_0:\calQ'_0 \to \calX$} \markbox{20033}{by} \markbox{m20034}{$\hO_0 = \hO \circ \Xi$} \markbox{20035}{and} \markbox{m20036}{$\hO'_0 = \hO' \circ \Xi'$}, \markbox{20037}{where} \markbox{m20038}{$\hO:\calQ \to \calX$} \markbox{20039}{and} \markbox{m20040}{$\hO':\calQ \to \calX$} \markbox{20041}{are} \markbox{20042}{the} \markbox{20043}{quasi-isometric} \markbox{20044}{embeddings} \markbox{20045}{defined} \markbox{20046}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:upgrade to HHS}.

For \markbox{20047}{the} \markbox{20048}{final} \markbox{20049}{piece} \markbox{20050}{of} \markbox{20051}{setup,} \markbox{20052}{we} \markbox{20053}{want} \markbox{20054}{to} \markbox{20055}{observe} \markbox{20056}{that} \markbox{20057}{these} \markbox{20058}{HFIs} \markbox{m20059}{$\{\hT_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$} \markbox{20060}{and} \markbox{m20061}{$\{\hT'_{U,0}\}_{U \in \calU_0}$} \markbox{20062}{admit} \markbox{20063}{an} \markbox{20064}{isomorphism} \markbox{20065}{in} \markbox{20066}{the} \markbox{20067}{sense} \markbox{20068}{of} \markbox{20069}{Proposition} \ref{prop:HFI isomorphism}.  \markbox{20070}{For} \markbox{20071}{this,} \markbox{20072}{we} \markbox{20073}{require} \markbox{20074}{the} \markbox{20075}{following} \markbox{20076}{lemma,} \markbox{20077}{whose} \markbox{20078}{proof} \markbox{20079}{is} \markbox{20080}{a} \markbox{20081}{straightforward} \markbox{20082}{application} \markbox{20083}{of} \markbox{20084}{the} \markbox{20085}{definitions} \markbox{20086}{and} \markbox{20087}{Corollary} \ref{cor:interval isometry}.  

\begin{lemma}\label{lem:interval isometries}
For \markbox{20088}{each} \markbox{m20089}{$U \in \calU^*_0$}, \markbox{20090}{the} \markbox{20091}{isometry} \markbox{m20092}{$i_U:\hT_{U,0} \to \hT'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20093}{provided} \markbox{20094}{by} \markbox{20095}{Corollary} \ref{cor:interval isometry} \markbox{20096}{satisfies} \markbox{20097}{the} \markbox{20098}{conditions} \markbox{20099}{of} \markbox{20100}{Proposition} \ref{prop:HFI isomorphism}.
\begin{itemize}
\item {} Thus \markbox{20101}{these} \markbox{20102}{component-wise} \markbox{20103}{isometries} \markbox{20104}{combine} \markbox{20105}{to} \markbox{20106}{give} \markbox{20107}{an} \markbox{20108}{isometry} \markbox{m20109}{$I_0:\calQ_0 \to \calQ'_0$}. 
\end{itemize}


\end{lemma}




\subsection{Statement of the stable cubulations theorem}

We \markbox{20110}{are} \markbox{20111}{now} \markbox{20112}{ready} \markbox{20113}{to} \markbox{20114}{state} \markbox{20115}{the} \markbox{20116}{stable} \markbox{20117}{cubical} \markbox{20118}{intervals} theorem:

\begin{theorem}[Stable \markbox{20119}{cubical} intervals]\label{thm:stable cubes}
Continuing \markbox{20120}{with} \markbox{20121}{our} \markbox{20122}{standing} \markbox{20123}{notation,} \markbox{20124}{there} \markbox{20125}{exists} \markbox{m20126}{$\Sigma = \Sigma(\mathfrak S, K)>0$} \markbox{20127}{so} \markbox{20128}{that} \markbox{20129}{the} \markbox{20130}{following} \markbox{20131}{diagram} \markbox{20132}{commutes} \markbox{20133}{up} \markbox{20134}{to} \markbox{20135}{error} \markbox{m20136}{$\Sigma$}:
\begin{equation}\label{Phi diagram}
  \begin{tikzcd}
   \calQ \arrow[ddrr,"\hO", bend left=40] \arrow[dr,"\Delta_0 \hspace{.075in}" left] &  \\
    &\calQ_{0} \arrow[dr,"\hO_0 \hspace{.2in}" below]\arrow[dd, "I_0"] \\
    & & \calX\\
    & \calQ'_{0} \arrow[ur,"\hO'_0"] \\
    \calQ'\arrow[uurr,"\hspace{.2in} \vspace{.1in} \hO'" below, bend right=40] \arrow[ur,"\Delta'_0"] & \\
  \end{tikzcd}
  \end{equation}

\begin{itemize}
\item {} In \markbox{20137}{the} \markbox{20138}{above,} \markbox{m20139}{$I_0:\calQ_0 \to \calQ'_0$} \markbox{20140}{is} \markbox{20141}{the} \markbox{20142}{isomorphism} \markbox{20143}{from} \markbox{20144}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval isometries}.
\item {} In \markbox{20145}{particular,} \markbox{20146}{any} \markbox{20147}{colorable} \markbox{20148}{hierarchically} \markbox{20149}{hyperbolic} \markbox{20150}{space} \markbox{20151}{is} \markbox{m20152}{$\Sigma$}-stably \markbox{20153}{weakly} \markbox{20154}{locally} \markbox{20155}{quasi-cubical} \markbox{20156}{(Definition} \ref{defn:stable cubes}). 
\end{itemize}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}

It \markbox{20157}{remains} \markbox{20158}{to} \markbox{20159}{prove} \markbox{20160}{that} \markbox{20161}{the} \markbox{20162}{upper,} \markbox{20163}{lower,} \markbox{20164}{and} \markbox{20165}{middle} \markbox{20166}{triangles} \markbox{20167}{coarsely} \markbox{20168}{commute.}  \markbox{20169}{The} \markbox{20170}{proof} \markbox{20171}{for} \markbox{20172}{the} \markbox{20173}{upper} \markbox{20174}{(and} \markbox{20175}{hence} \markbox{20176}{the} \markbox{20177}{lower)} \markbox{20178}{is} \markbox{20179}{essentially} \markbox{20180}{automatic} \markbox{20181}{by} \markbox{20182}{construction.}  \markbox{20183}{In} \markbox{20184}{particular,} \markbox{20185}{by} \markbox{20186}{item} \markbox{20187}{(2)} \markbox{20188}{of} \markbox{20189}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable collapse}, \markbox{20190}{the} \markbox{20191}{map} \markbox{m20192}{$\Delta_0:\calQ \to \calQ_0$} \markbox{20193}{is} \markbox{20194}{a} \markbox{m20195}{$(1,S^2_0)$}-quasi-isometry \markbox{20196}{for} \markbox{m20197}{$S_0 = S_0(\mathfrak S, K)>0$}.  \markbox{20198}{On} \markbox{20199}{the} \markbox{20200}{other} \markbox{20201}{hand,} \markbox{20202}{item} \markbox{20203}{(3)} \markbox{20204}{of} \markbox{20205}{that} \markbox{20206}{proposition} \markbox{20207}{implies} \markbox{20208}{that} \markbox{m20209}{$\Delta_0 \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ_0}$} \markbox{20210}{while} \markbox{m20211}{$\hO_0:\calQ_0 \to \calX$} \markbox{20212}{is} \markbox{20213}{defined} \markbox{20214}{by} \markbox{m20215}{$\hO_0 = \hO \circ \Xi$}.  \markbox{20216}{Hence} \markbox{20217}{the} \markbox{20218}{top} \markbox{20219}{triangle} \markbox{20220}{commutes} \markbox{20221}{up} \markbox{20222}{to} \markbox{20223}{error} \markbox{m20224}{$S_0$}, \markbox{20225}{and} \markbox{20226}{the} \markbox{20227}{same} \markbox{20228}{holds} \markbox{20229}{for} \markbox{20230}{the} \markbox{20231}{bottom} triangle.

For \markbox{20232}{the} \markbox{20233}{middle} \markbox{20234}{triangle,} \markbox{20235}{we} \markbox{20236}{want} \markbox{20237}{to} \markbox{20238}{show} \markbox{20239}{that} \markbox{m20240}{$d_{\calX}(\hO_0(\hx), \hO'_0 \circ I_0(\hx))$} \markbox{20241}{is} \markbox{20242}{bounded} \markbox{20243}{in} \markbox{20244}{terms} \markbox{20245}{of} \markbox{m20246}{$\mathfrak S, K$} \markbox{20247}{for} \markbox{20248}{any} \markbox{m20249}{$\hx \in \calQ_0$}.  \markbox{20250}{However,} \markbox{20251}{we} \markbox{20252}{note} \markbox{20253}{that} \markbox{20254}{the} \markbox{20255}{maps} \markbox{m20256}{$\hO_0:\calQ_0 \to H$} \markbox{20257}{and} \markbox{m20258}{$\Delta_0 \circ \hPsi:H \to \calQ_0$} \markbox{20259}{are} \markbox{20260}{quasi-inverses} \markbox{20261}{(with} \markbox{20262}{errors} \markbox{20263}{depending} \markbox{20264}{on} \markbox{m20265}{$\mathfrak S, K$}), \markbox{20266}{and} \markbox{20267}{similarly} \markbox{20268}{for} \markbox{m20269}{$\hO'_0:\calQ'_0 \to H'$} \markbox{20270}{and} \markbox{m20271}{$\Delta_0 \circ \hPsi:H' \to \calQ'_0$}.  \markbox{20272}{Here,} \markbox{m20273}{$H = \hull_{\calX}(a,b)$} \markbox{20274}{and} \markbox{m20275}{$H' = \hull_{\calX}(a',b')$}.  \markbox{20276}{But} \markbox{20277}{since} \markbox{m20278}{$d_{\calX}(a,a')\leq 1$} \markbox{20279}{and} \markbox{m20280}{$d_{\calX}(b,b')\leq 1$}, \markbox{20281}{it} \markbox{20282}{follows} \markbox{20283}{from} \markbox{20284}{the} \markbox{20285}{Distance} \markbox{20286}{Formula} \ref{thm:DF} \markbox{20287}{and} \markbox{20288}{Definition} \ref{defn:hier hull} \markbox{20289}{that} \markbox{m20290}{$d^{Haus}_{\calX}(H,H')$} \markbox{20291}{is} \markbox{20292}{bounded} \markbox{20293}{in} \markbox{20294}{terms} \markbox{20295}{of} \markbox{m20296}{$\mathfrak S$}.

Hence \markbox{20297}{it} \markbox{20298}{suffices} \markbox{20299}{to} \markbox{20300}{show} \markbox{20301}{that} \markbox{20302}{for} \markbox{m20303}{$x \in H \cap H'$} \markbox{20304}{(so} \markbox{20305}{that} \markbox{m20306}{$\hPsi(x)$} \markbox{20307}{and} \markbox{m20308}{$\hPsi'(x)$} \markbox{20309}{are} \markbox{20310}{both} \markbox{20311}{defined),} \markbox{20312}{we} have
$$d_{\calQ'_0}(\Delta'_0 \circ \hPsi'(x), I_0 \circ \Delta_0 \circ \hPsi(x))< \Sigma,$$
for \markbox{m20313}{$\Sigma = \Sigma(\mathfrak S, K)$}.  \markbox{20314}{Set} \markbox{m20315}{$\Delta'_0 \circ \hPsi'(x) = \hx'_0 = (\hx'_{U,0})$} \markbox{20316}{and} \markbox{m20317}{$I_0 \circ \Delta_0 \circ \hPsi(x) = \hy'_0= (\hy'_{U,0})$}, \markbox{20318}{where} \markbox{20319}{we} \markbox{20320}{note} \markbox{20321}{that} \markbox{20322}{both} \markbox{m20323}{$\hx'_0,\hy'_0 \in \calQ'_0$}.  

We \markbox{20324}{argue} \markbox{20325}{component-wise} \markbox{20326}{that} \markbox{m20327}{$d_{\calQ'_0}(\hx'_0,\hy'_0)$} \markbox{20328}{is} \markbox{20329}{bounded.}  \markbox{20330}{Recall} \markbox{20331}{that} \markbox{20332}{the} \markbox{20333}{map} \markbox{m20334}{$\hPsi:H \to \calQ$} \markbox{20335}{is} \markbox{20336}{defined} \markbox{20337}{component-wise} \markbox{20338}{(over} \markbox{20339}{the} \markbox{20340}{set} \markbox{m20341}{$\calU$}) \markbox{20342}{by} \markbox{m20343}{$\hpsi_U = q_U \circ \phi_U^{-1} \circ p_U \circ \pi_U$}, \markbox{20344}{where} \markbox{m20345}{$\pi_U:\calX \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{20346}{is} \markbox{20347}{the} \markbox{20348}{HHS} \markbox{20349}{projection,} \markbox{m20350}{$p_U:\calC(U) \to \phi_U(T_U)$} \markbox{20351}{is} \markbox{20352}{closest} \markbox{20353}{point} \markbox{20354}{projection,} \markbox{m20355}{$\phi_U:T_U \to \calC(U)$} \markbox{20356}{is} \markbox{20357}{the} \markbox{m20358}{$(L_0,L_0)$}-quasi-isometric \markbox{20359}{embedding} \markbox{20360}{provided} \markbox{20361}{by} \markbox{20362}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure} \markbox{20363}{(here} \markbox{m20364}{$L_0=L_0(\mathfrak S)$}), \markbox{20365}{and} \markbox{m20366}{$q_U:T_U \to \hT_U$} \markbox{20367}{is} \markbox{20368}{the} \markbox{20369}{map} \markbox{20370}{which} \markbox{20371}{collapses} \markbox{20372}{a} \markbox{20373}{uniform} \markbox{20374}{thickening} \markbox{20375}{of} \markbox{m20376}{$T_U$} \markbox{20377}{along} \markbox{20378}{the} \markbox{20379}{cluster} \markbox{20380}{components,} \markbox{20381}{with} \markbox{20382}{constants} \markbox{20383}{depending} \markbox{20384}{only} \markbox{20385}{on} \markbox{m20386}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{20387}{The} \markbox{20388}{map} \markbox{m20389}{$\hPsi':H' \to \calQ'$} \markbox{20390}{is} \markbox{20391}{defined} similarly.

First, \markbox{20392}{we} \markbox{20393}{can} \markbox{20394}{reduce} \markbox{20395}{to} \markbox{20396}{involved} \markbox{20397}{domains} \markbox{20398}{in} \markbox{m20399}{$\calU_0 = \calU \cap \calU'$}.  \markbox{20400}{If} \markbox{m20401}{$U \in \calU \triangle \calU'$}, \markbox{20402}{then} \markbox{m20403}{$a,b$} \markbox{20404}{and} \markbox{m20405}{$a',b'$} \markbox{20406}{have} \markbox{20407}{bounded} \markbox{20408}{diameter} \markbox{20409}{projections} \markbox{20410}{to} \markbox{m20411}{$U$} \markbox{20412}{in} \markbox{20413}{terms} \markbox{20414}{of} \markbox{m20415}{$K$} \markbox{20416}{and} \markbox{m20417}{$\mathfrak S$}, \markbox{20418}{while} \markbox{20419}{also} \markbox{20420}{each} \markbox{20421}{such} \markbox{20422}{domain} \markbox{20423}{is} \markbox{20424}{involved} \markbox{20425}{in} \markbox{20426}{the} \markbox{20427}{sense} \markbox{20428}{of} \markbox{20429}{Definition} \ref{defn:involved} \markbox{20430}{and} \markbox{20431}{hence} \markbox{20432}{there} \markbox{20433}{are} \markbox{20434}{only} \markbox{20435}{boundedly-many} \markbox{20436}{by} \markbox{20437}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains}. \markbox{20438}{Next} \markbox{20439}{observe} \markbox{20440}{that} \markbox{20441}{if} \markbox{m20442}{$U \in \calU_0$} \markbox{20443}{is} \markbox{20444}{not} \markbox{20445}{involved,} \markbox{20446}{then} \markbox{20447}{the} \markbox{20448}{stable} \markbox{20449}{trees} \markbox{m20450}{$T_U, T'_U$} \markbox{20451}{for} \markbox{20452}{the} \markbox{20453}{two} \markbox{20454}{setups} \markbox{20455}{are} \markbox{20456}{exactly} \markbox{20457}{the} \markbox{20458}{same,} \markbox{20459}{and} \markbox{20460}{hence} \markbox{20461}{have} \markbox{20462}{identical} \markbox{20463}{thickenings,} \markbox{20464}{and} \markbox{20465}{thus} \markbox{20466}{the} \markbox{20467}{stable} \markbox{20468}{decompositions} \markbox{20469}{the} \markbox{20470}{pair} \markbox{20471}{are} \markbox{20472}{the} \markbox{20473}{(identical)} \markbox{20474}{collection} \markbox{20475}{of} \markbox{20476}{edge} \markbox{20477}{components} \markbox{20478}{for} \markbox{20479}{each,} \markbox{20480}{and} \markbox{20481}{their} \markbox{20482}{corresponding} \markbox{20483}{collapsed} \markbox{20484}{trees} \markbox{m20485}{$\hT_U$} \markbox{20486}{and} \markbox{m20487}{$\hT'_U$} \markbox{20488}{are} \markbox{20489}{identical.}  \markbox{20490}{Hence,} \markbox{20491}{for} \markbox{20492}{uninvolved} \markbox{m20493}{$U \in \calU_0$}, \markbox{20494}{we} \markbox{20495}{have} \markbox{m20496}{$\hx'_{U,0} = \hy'_{U,0}$}.

Let \markbox{m20497}{$U \in \calU_0$} \markbox{20498}{be} \markbox{20499}{involved.}  \markbox{20500}{Since} \markbox{20501}{there} \markbox{20502}{are} \markbox{20503}{boundedly-many} \markbox{20504}{(in} \markbox{m20505}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20506}{such} \markbox{20507}{domains} \markbox{20508}{by} \markbox{20509}{Theorem} \ref{thm:controlling domains}, \markbox{20510}{it} \markbox{20511}{suffices} \markbox{20512}{to} \markbox{20513}{bound} \markbox{20514}{the} \markbox{20515}{diameter} \markbox{m20516}{$d_{\hT'_{U,0}}(\hx'_{U,0}, \hy'_{U,0})$} \markbox{20517}{in} \markbox{20518}{terms} \markbox{20519}{of} \markbox{m20520}{$\mathfrak S$}.

  \markbox{20521}{The} \markbox{20522}{distance} \markbox{m20523}{$d_{\hT'_{U,0}}(\hx'_{U,0}, \hy'_{U,0})$} \markbox{20524}{is} \markbox{20525}{measured} \markbox{20526}{in} \markbox{20527}{the} \markbox{20528}{edge} \markbox{20529}{components} \markbox{20530}{of} \markbox{m20531}{$\hT'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20532}{which} \markbox{20533}{separate} \markbox{20534}{them,} \markbox{20535}{and} \markbox{20536}{these} \markbox{20537}{edge} \markbox{20538}{components} \markbox{20539}{are} \markbox{20540}{stable} \markbox{20541}{components} \markbox{20542}{of} \markbox{m20543}{$T'_U$}.  \markbox{20544}{This} \markbox{20545}{means} \markbox{20546}{that} \markbox{20547}{if} \markbox{20548}{the} \markbox{20549}{distance} \markbox{m20550}{$d_{\hT'_{U,0}}(\hx'_{U,0}, \hy'_{U,0})$} \markbox{20551}{is} \markbox{20552}{very} \markbox{20553}{large,} \markbox{20554}{then} \markbox{20555}{there} \markbox{20556}{must} \markbox{20557}{be} \markbox{20558}{either} 
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} some \markbox{20559}{long} \markbox{20560}{stable} \markbox{20561}{component} \markbox{m20562}{$E' \subset T'_{U,s}$} \markbox{20563}{so} \markbox{20564}{that} \markbox{20565}{some} \markbox{20566}{long} \markbox{20567}{segment} \markbox{20568}{of} \markbox{m20569}{$\Delta'_U(q'_U(E'))$} \markbox{20570}{separates} \markbox{m20571}{$\hx'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20572}{from} \markbox{m20573}{$\hy'_{U,0}$}, or
\item {} if \markbox{20574}{no} \markbox{20575}{such} \markbox{20576}{long} \markbox{20577}{component} \markbox{20578}{exists,} \markbox{20579}{there} \markbox{20580}{must} \markbox{20581}{be} \markbox{20582}{some} \markbox{20583}{large} \markbox{20584}{number} \markbox{20585}{of} \markbox{20586}{such} \markbox{20587}{stable} \markbox{20588}{components} \markbox{20589}{separating} them.
\end{enumerate}

In \markbox{20590}{case} \markbox{20591}{(1),} \markbox{20592}{let} \markbox{m20593}{$E \subset T_{U,s}$} \markbox{20594}{be} \markbox{20595}{the} \markbox{20596}{stable} \markbox{20597}{component} \markbox{20598}{paired} \markbox{20599}{with} \markbox{m20600}{$E' \subset T'_{U,s}$}.  \markbox{20601}{Note} \markbox{20602}{that} \markbox{m20603}{$\phi_U(E) \cup \phi'_U(E')$} \markbox{20604}{is} \markbox{20605}{uniformly} \markbox{20606}{quasi-convex} \markbox{20607}{(in} \markbox{m20608}{$\mathfrak S$}), \markbox{20609}{and} \markbox{20610}{hence} \markbox{m20611}{$\pi_U(x)$} \markbox{20612}{has} \markbox{20613}{a} \markbox{20614}{uniformly} \markbox{20615}{bounded} \markbox{20616}{projection} \markbox{20617}{to} \markbox{20618}{it.}  \markbox{20619}{However} \markbox{20620}{the} \markbox{20621}{fact} \markbox{20622}{that} \markbox{20623}{a} \markbox{20624}{long} \markbox{20625}{segment} \markbox{20626}{of} \markbox{m20627}{$\Delta'_U(q_U(E')) \subset \hT'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20628}{separates} \markbox{m20629}{$\hx'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20630}{from} \markbox{m20631}{$\hy'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20632}{means} \markbox{20633}{that} \markbox{20634}{some} \markbox{20635}{large} \markbox{20636}{diameter} \markbox{20637}{portion} \markbox{20638}{of} \markbox{m20639}{$\phi_U(E) \cup \phi'_U(E')$} \markbox{20640}{coarsely} \markbox{20641}{(in} \markbox{m20642}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20643}{separates} \markbox{m20644}{$p_U(\pi_U(x))$} \markbox{20645}{from} \markbox{m20646}{$p'_U(\pi_U(x))$}, \markbox{20647}{which} \markbox{20648}{is} impossible.

In \markbox{20649}{case} \markbox{20650}{(2),} \markbox{20651}{we} \markbox{20652}{can} \markbox{20653}{assume} \markbox{20654}{that} \markbox{20655}{no} \markbox{20656}{such} \markbox{20657}{long} \markbox{20658}{stable} \markbox{20659}{component} \markbox{20660}{exists,} \markbox{20661}{so} \markbox{20662}{that} \markbox{20663}{the} \markbox{20664}{distance} \markbox{m20665}{$d_{\hT'_{U,0}}(\hx'_{U,0}, \hy'_{U,0})$} \markbox{20666}{corresponds} \markbox{20667}{to} \markbox{20668}{some} \markbox{20669}{sequence} \markbox{m20670}{$E'_1, \dots, E'_n \subset T'_{U,s}$} \markbox{20671}{of} \markbox{20672}{short} \markbox{20673}{stable} \markbox{20674}{components} \markbox{20675}{of} \markbox{20676}{length} \markbox{20677}{bounded} \markbox{20678}{in} \markbox{20679}{terms} \markbox{20680}{of} \markbox{m20681}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{20682}{Let} \markbox{m20683}{$E_i \subset T_{U,s}$} \markbox{20684}{denote} \markbox{20685}{the} \markbox{20686}{stable} \markbox{20687}{component} \markbox{20688}{paired} \markbox{20689}{with} \markbox{m20690}{$E'_i$}.  \markbox{20691}{By} \markbox{20692}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable interval structure} \markbox{20693}{and} \markbox{20694}{the} \markbox{20695}{fact} \markbox{20696}{that} \markbox{m20697}{$d_{\calX}(a,a') \leq 1$} \markbox{20698}{and} \markbox{m20699}{$d_{\calX}(b,b')\leq 1$}, \markbox{20700}{we} \markbox{20701}{have} \markbox{20702}{that} \markbox{m20703}{$\phi_U(T_U)$} \markbox{20704}{and} \markbox{m20705}{$\phi'_U(T'_U)$} \markbox{20706}{are} \markbox{20707}{within} \markbox{20708}{bounded} \markbox{20709}{(in} \markbox{m20710}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20711}{Hausdorff} \markbox{20712}{distance} \markbox{20713}{in} \markbox{m20714}{$\calC(U)$}.  \markbox{20715}{Since} \markbox{20716}{each} \markbox{20717}{of} \markbox{20718}{the} \markbox{m20719}{$E'_i$} \markbox{20720}{are} \markbox{20721}{uniformly} \markbox{20722}{close} \markbox{20723}{(in} \markbox{m20724}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20725}{to} \markbox{m20726}{$E_i$} \markbox{20727}{and} \markbox{20728}{the} \markbox{20729}{bijection} \markbox{m20730}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_{U,s}) \to \pi_0(T'_{U,s})$} \markbox{20731}{is} \markbox{20732}{order-preserving,} \markbox{20733}{it} \markbox{20734}{follows} \markbox{20735}{that} \markbox{20736}{the} \markbox{20737}{hulls} \markbox{m20738}{$\hull_{\phi_U(T_U)}(E_1, E_n)$} \markbox{20739}{and} \markbox{m20740}{$\hull_{\phi'_U(T'_U)}(E'_1,E'_n)$} \markbox{20741}{are} \markbox{20742}{within} \markbox{20743}{uniform} \markbox{20744}{(in} \markbox{m20745}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20746}{Hausdorff} \markbox{20747}{distance} \markbox{20748}{of} \markbox{20749}{each} \markbox{20750}{other,} \markbox{20751}{and} \markbox{20752}{hence} \markbox{20753}{their} \markbox{20754}{union} \markbox{20755}{is} \markbox{20756}{uniformly} \markbox{20757}{quasi-convex} \markbox{20758}{(in} \markbox{m20759}{$\mathfrak S$}).  \markbox{20760}{Thus,} \markbox{20761}{if} \markbox{m20762}{$\Delta'_U(q'_U(E'_1)), \dots, \Delta'_U(q'_U(E'_n))$} \markbox{20763}{separate} \markbox{m20764}{$\hx'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20765}{from} \markbox{m20766}{$\hy'_{U,0}$} \markbox{20767}{in} \markbox{m20768}{$\hT'_{U,0}$}, \markbox{20769}{then} \markbox{20770}{the} \markbox{20771}{union} \markbox{20772}{of} \markbox{20773}{these} \markbox{20774}{hulls} \markbox{20775}{coarsely} \markbox{20776}{(in} \markbox{m20777}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20778}{separates} \markbox{m20779}{$p_U(\pi_U(x))$} \markbox{20780}{from} \markbox{m20781}{$p'_U(\pi_U(x))$}.

Since \markbox{20782}{each} \markbox{20783}{of} \markbox{20784}{the} \markbox{20785}{segments} \markbox{m20786}{$E'_i$} \markbox{20787}{is} \markbox{20788}{bounded} \markbox{20789}{length,} \markbox{20790}{the} \markbox{20791}{union} \markbox{20792}{of} \markbox{20793}{these} \markbox{20794}{hulls} \markbox{20795}{is} \markbox{20796}{long} \markbox{20797}{if} \markbox{20798}{the} \markbox{20799}{number} \markbox{20800}{of} \markbox{20801}{segments} \markbox{m20802}{$n$} \markbox{20803}{is} \markbox{20804}{very} \markbox{20805}{large.}  \markbox{20806}{Moreover,} \markbox{20807}{each} \markbox{20808}{pair} \markbox{20809}{of} \markbox{20810}{segments} \markbox{m20811}{$E'_i, E'_{i+1}$} \markbox{20812}{is} \markbox{20813}{separated} \markbox{20814}{by} \markbox{20815}{some} \markbox{20816}{complementary} \markbox{20817}{component} \markbox{m20818}{$C_i \subset T'_U - T'_{U,s}$}.  \markbox{20819}{By} \markbox{20820}{construction,} \markbox{20821}{all} \markbox{20822}{but} \markbox{20823}{boundedly-many} \markbox{20824}{(in} \markbox{m20825}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20826}{of} \markbox{20827}{these} \markbox{20828}{components} \markbox{20829}{corresponds} \markbox{20830}{to} \markbox{20831}{some} \markbox{20832}{cluster} \markbox{20833}{component} \markbox{20834}{of} \markbox{m20835}{$T'_U$}.  \markbox{20836}{Since} \markbox{20837}{there} \markbox{20838}{are} \markbox{20839}{only} \markbox{20840}{boundedly-many} \markbox{20841}{(in} \markbox{m20842}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{20843}{involved} \markbox{20844}{domains,} \markbox{20845}{by} \markbox{20846}{choosing} \markbox{m20847}{$n$} \markbox{20848}{to} \markbox{20849}{be} \markbox{20850}{sufficiently} \markbox{20851}{large,} \markbox{20852}{there} \markbox{20853}{exists} \markbox{20854}{some} \markbox{m20855}{$C_j$} \markbox{20856}{which} \markbox{20857}{contains} \markbox{20858}{a} \markbox{m20859}{$\nest_{\calU_0}$}-minimal \markbox{20860}{domain} \markbox{m20861}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{20862}{which} \markbox{20863}{is} \markbox{20864}{both} \markbox{m20865}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{20866}{and} \markbox{m20867}{$\nest_{\calU'}$}-minimal.  \markbox{20868}{But} \markbox{20869}{this} \markbox{20870}{is} \markbox{20871}{impossible,} \markbox{20872}{for} \markbox{20873}{the} \markbox{20874}{BGIA} \ref{ax:BGIA} \markbox{20875}{would} \markbox{20876}{imply} \markbox{20877}{that} \markbox{m20878}{$d_V(\rho^U_V(p_U(\pi_U(x)), \rho^U_V(p'_U(\pi_U(x)))) \succ K$}, \markbox{20879}{and} \markbox{20880}{this} \markbox{20881}{cannot} \markbox{20882}{happen} \markbox{20883}{as} \markbox{20884}{we} \markbox{20885}{can} \markbox{20886}{also} \markbox{20887}{arrange} \markbox{m20888}{$\pi_U(x)$} \markbox{20889}{to} \markbox{20890}{be} \markbox{20891}{as} \markbox{20892}{far} \markbox{20893}{from} \markbox{m20894}{$\rho^V_U$} \markbox{20895}{as} \markbox{20896}{necessary.}  \markbox{20897}{Hence} \markbox{20898}{no} \markbox{20899}{such} \markbox{20900}{long} \markbox{20901}{sequence} \markbox{m20902}{$E'_1, \dots E'_n$} \markbox{20903}{can} \markbox{20904}{exist,} \markbox{20905}{completing} \markbox{20906}{the} proof.



\end{proof}



\appendix
\section{Proof of the Tree Trimming Theorem \ref{thm:tree trimming}}\label{app:TT}

Below \markbox{20907}{is} \markbox{20908}{a} \markbox{20909}{re-statement} \markbox{20910}{of} \markbox{20911}{Theorem} \ref{thm:tree trimming}.  \markbox{20912}{See} \markbox{20913}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:tree trimming} \markbox{20914}{for} \markbox{20915}{the} \markbox{20916}{contextual} \markbox{20917}{definitions} \markbox{20918}{and} notation.

\begin{theorem}[Tree Trimming]
There \markbox{20919}{exists} \markbox{m20920}{$B_{tt} = B_{tt}(\mathfrak S, K)>0$} \markbox{20921}{so} \markbox{20922}{that} \markbox{20923}{for} \markbox{20924}{any} \markbox{m20925}{$B < B_{tt}$}, \markbox{20926}{there} \markbox{20927}{exists} \markbox{m20928}{$L =L(\mathfrak S, B)>0$} \markbox{20929}{so} \markbox{20930}{that} \markbox{20931}{the} \markbox{20932}{following} hold:

\begin{enumerate}
\item {} We \markbox{20933}{have} \markbox{m20934}{$\Delta(\calQ) \subset \calQ'$}.
\item {} There \markbox{20935}{is} \markbox{20936}{a} \markbox{20937}{map} \markbox{m20938}{$\Xi:\calQ' \to \calQ$} \markbox{20939}{so} \markbox{20940}{that} \markbox{m20941}{$\Delta \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ'}$}.  \markbox{20942}{In} \markbox{20943}{particular,} \markbox{m20944}{$\Delta(\calQ) = \calQ'$}.
\item {} The \markbox{20945}{map} \markbox{m20946}{$\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$} \markbox{20947}{is} \markbox{20948}{an} \markbox{m20949}{$(L,L)$}-quasi-isometry.
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
The \markbox{20950}{fact} \markbox{20951}{that} \markbox{m20952}{$\Delta(\calQ) \subset \calQ'$}, \markbox{20953}{namely} \markbox{20954}{that} \markbox{m20955}{$\Delta$} \markbox{20956}{preserves} \markbox{m20957}{$0$}-consistency, \markbox{20958}{is} \markbox{20959}{immediate} \markbox{20960}{from} \markbox{20961}{the} \markbox{20962}{fact} \markbox{20963}{that} \markbox{20964}{the} \markbox{m20965}{$\Delta_U$} \markbox{20966}{just} \markbox{20967}{collapse} \markbox{20968}{subintervals,} \markbox{20969}{so} \markbox{20970}{coordinates} \markbox{20971}{which} \markbox{20972}{were} \markbox{20973}{collapsed} \markbox{20974}{projections} \markbox{20975}{remain} \markbox{20976}{collapsed} \markbox{20977}{projections,} \markbox{20978}{showing} \markbox{20979}{item} \markbox{20980}{(1).}  \markbox{20981}{Items} \markbox{20982}{(2)} \markbox{20983}{and} \markbox{20984}{(3)} \markbox{20985}{require} \markbox{20986}{more} \markbox{20987}{work} \markbox{20988}{and} \markbox{20989}{we} \markbox{20990}{provide} \markbox{20991}{a} \markbox{20992}{detailed} \markbox{20993}{sketch} \markbox{20994}{of} both.
\medskip

\markbox{20995}{\textbf{\underline{Item (2): Surjectivity of $\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$}}}: \markbox{20996}{Let} \markbox{m20997}{$\hy \in \calQ'$}.  \markbox{20998}{We} \markbox{20999}{will} \markbox{21000}{construct} \markbox{21001}{a} \markbox{21002}{point} \markbox{m21003}{$\hx \in \calQ$} \markbox{21004}{with} \markbox{m21005}{$\Delta(\hx) = \hy$} \markbox{21006}{by} \markbox{21007}{a} \markbox{21008}{coordinate-wise} \markbox{21009}{argument,} \markbox{21010}{thereby} \markbox{21011}{defining} \markbox{21012}{a} \markbox{21013}{map} \markbox{m21014}{$\Xi:\calQ' \to \calQ$} \markbox{21015}{with} \markbox{m21016}{$\Delta \circ \Xi = id_{\calQ'}$}.

For \markbox{21017}{each} \markbox{m21018}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{21019}{let} \markbox{m21020}{$C_U = \Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$}.  \markbox{21021}{Our} \markbox{21022}{goal} \markbox{21023}{is} \markbox{21024}{to} \markbox{21025}{pick,} \markbox{21026}{for} \markbox{21027}{each} \markbox{m21028}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{21029}{a} \markbox{21030}{point} \markbox{m21031}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{21032}{and} \markbox{21033}{then} \markbox{21034}{prove} \markbox{m21035}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21036}{of} \markbox{21037}{the} \markbox{21038}{tuple} \markbox{m21039}{$\hx = (\hx_U)$}.  \markbox{21040}{Note} \markbox{21041}{that} \markbox{m21042}{$\Delta(\hx) =\hy$} \markbox{21043}{for} \markbox{21044}{such} \markbox{21045}{a} \markbox{21046}{tuple,} \markbox{21047}{by} \markbox{21048}{construction.}  \markbox{21049}{The} \markbox{21050}{proof} \markbox{21051}{is} \markbox{21052}{by} \markbox{21053}{induction} \markbox{21054}{on} \markbox{21055}{the} \markbox{21056}{nesting} \markbox{21057}{level} \markbox{21058}{in} \markbox{m21059}{$\calU$}, \markbox{21060}{and} \markbox{21061}{is} \markbox{21062}{similar} \markbox{21063}{to} \markbox{21064}{the} \markbox{21065}{construction} \markbox{21066}{of} \markbox{21067}{the} \markbox{21068}{map} \markbox{m21069}{$\hO:\calQ \to H$} \markbox{21070}{as} \markbox{21071}{in} \markbox{21072}{Proposition} \ref{prop:coarse surjectivity}.  \markbox{21073}{The} \markbox{21074}{main} \markbox{21075}{difference} \markbox{21076}{is} \markbox{21077}{that} \markbox{21078}{the} \markbox{21079}{collapsing} \markbox{21080}{subintervals} \markbox{21081}{are} \markbox{21082}{not} \markbox{21083}{automatically} \markbox{21084}{associated} \markbox{21085}{to} \markbox{21086}{a} \markbox{21087}{collection} \markbox{21088}{of} \markbox{21089}{domains,} \markbox{21090}{and} \markbox{21091}{this} \markbox{21092}{is} \markbox{21093}{where} \markbox{21094}{the} \markbox{21095}{work} \markbox{21096}{lies.}  \markbox{21097}{The} \markbox{21098}{proof} \markbox{21099}{is} \markbox{21100}{basically} \markbox{21101}{the} \markbox{21102}{proof} \markbox{21103}{of} \markbox{21104}{the} \markbox{21105}{analogous} \markbox{21106}{fact} \markbox{21107}{in} \cite[Theorem 10.2]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{21108}{except} \markbox{21109}{that} \markbox{21110}{our}
