\markbox{21111}{setup} \markbox{21112}{is} \markbox{21113}{much} \markbox{21114}{simpler.}  \markbox{21115}{What} \markbox{21116}{follows} \markbox{21117}{is} \markbox{21118}{a} \markbox{21119}{very} \markbox{21120}{detailed} \markbox{21121}{sketch,} \markbox{21122}{which} \markbox{21123}{leaves} \markbox{21124}{some} \markbox{21125}{small} \markbox{21126}{bits} \markbox{21127}{to} \markbox{21128}{the} reader.

For \markbox{21129}{the} \markbox{21130}{base} \markbox{21131}{case,} \markbox{21132}{let} \markbox{m21133}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{21134}{be} \markbox{m21135}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.   \markbox{21136}{If} \markbox{m21137}{$\hy_U \in \hT_{U,0}$} \markbox{21138}{is} \markbox{21139}{not} \markbox{21140}{contained} \markbox{21141}{in} \markbox{m21142}{$\Delta_U(B)$} \markbox{21143}{for} \markbox{21144}{some} \markbox{m21145}{$B \in \calB$}, \markbox{21146}{then} \markbox{m21147}{$C_U\subset \hT_U$} \markbox{21148}{is} \markbox{21149}{a} \markbox{21150}{point} \markbox{21151}{and} \markbox{21152}{we} \markbox{21153}{set} \markbox{m21154}{$\hx_U = C_U$}.  \markbox{21155}{If} \markbox{m21156}{$\hy_U \in \Delta_U(B)$} \markbox{21157}{for} \markbox{21158}{some} \markbox{m21159}{$B \in \calB$} \markbox{21160}{and} \markbox{m21161}{$B \subset \hT_U$} \markbox{21162}{does} \markbox{21163}{not} \markbox{21164}{contain} \markbox{21165}{an} \markbox{21166}{endpoint,} \markbox{21167}{then} \markbox{21168}{let} \markbox{m21169}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{21170}{be} \markbox{21171}{any} \markbox{21172}{point.}  \markbox{21173}{If} \markbox{21174}{instead} \markbox{m21175}{$C_U$} \markbox{21176}{does} \markbox{21177}{contain} \markbox{21178}{an} \markbox{21179}{endpoint,} \markbox{21180}{then} \markbox{21181}{it} \markbox{21182}{is} \markbox{21183}{possible} \markbox{21184}{that} \markbox{21185}{it} \markbox{21186}{contains} \markbox{21187}{both} \markbox{21188}{endpoints,} \markbox{21189}{and} \markbox{21190}{we} \markbox{21191}{need} \markbox{21192}{to} \markbox{21193}{choose} one.

The \markbox{21194}{following} \markbox{21195}{claim,} \markbox{21196}{which} \markbox{21197}{is} \markbox{21198}{exactly} \cite[Claim 10.3]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{21199}{does} \markbox{21200}{not} \markbox{21201}{require} \markbox{m21202}{$U$} \markbox{21203}{to} \markbox{21204}{be} \markbox{m21205}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal:

\begin{claim} \label{claim:choose one}
If \markbox{m21206}{$W, Z \in \{V \in \calU| V\pitchfork U, \hspace{.1in} \text{and} \hspace{.1in} \hy_V \neq (\hd^U_V)_0\}$}, \markbox{21207}{then} \markbox{m21208}{$\hd^W_U = \hd^Z_U$}.
\end{claim}

With \markbox{21209}{Claim} \ref{claim:choose one} \markbox{21210}{in} \markbox{21211}{hand,} \markbox{21212}{we} \markbox{21213}{can} \markbox{21214}{define} \markbox{m21215}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{21216}{for} \markbox{m21217}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{m21218}{$U$} \markbox{21219}{as} follows:

\begin{itemize}
\item {} If \markbox{m21220}{$\calW_U^{\pitchfork} = \{V \in \calU| V \pitchfork U \hspace{.1in} \mathrm{ and } \hspace{.1in} \hy_W \neq (\hd^V_U)_0\} \neq \emptyset$}, \markbox{21221}{then} \markbox{21222}{we} \markbox{21223}{set} \markbox{m21224}{$\hx_U = \hd^W_U$} \markbox{21225}{for} \markbox{21226}{any} \markbox{21227}{(and} \markbox{21228}{hence} \markbox{21229}{all,} \markbox{21230}{by} \markbox{21231}{the} \markbox{21232}{claim)} \markbox{m21233}{$W \in \calW_U^{\pitchfork}$}.
\item {} If \markbox{m21234}{$\calW_U^{\pitchfork} = \emptyset$}, \markbox{21235}{then} \markbox{21236}{we} \markbox{21237}{let} \markbox{m21238}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{21239}{be} \markbox{21240}{any} \markbox{21241}{marked} \markbox{21242}{point} \markbox{21243}{in} \markbox{m21244}{$C_U$}.
\end{itemize}

At \markbox{21245}{this} \markbox{21246}{point,} \markbox{21247}{we} \markbox{21248}{also} \markbox{21249}{want} \markbox{21250}{to} \markbox{21251}{set} \markbox{m21252}{$l_U$} \markbox{21253}{to} \markbox{21254}{be} \markbox{21255}{equal} \markbox{21256}{to} \markbox{21257}{the} \markbox{21258}{endpoint} \markbox{m21259}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{21260}{when} \markbox{m21261}{$U$} \markbox{21262}{is} \markbox{m21263}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal, \markbox{21264}{where} \markbox{m21265}{$l_U = \emptyset$} \markbox{21266}{when} \markbox{m21267}{$C_U$} \markbox{21268}{does} \markbox{21269}{not} \markbox{21270}{contain} \markbox{21271}{an} \markbox{21272}{endpoint} \markbox{21273}{of} \markbox{m21274}{$\hT_U$}.  \markbox{21275}{These} \markbox{21276}{labels} \markbox{21277}{will} \markbox{21278}{play} \markbox{21279}{a} \markbox{21280}{similar} \markbox{21281}{role} \markbox{21282}{as} \markbox{21283}{in} \markbox{21284}{the} \markbox{21285}{cluster} \markbox{21286}{honing} \markbox{21287}{process} \markbox{21288}{in} \markbox{21289}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:hO defined}.

For \markbox{21290}{the} \markbox{21291}{inductive} \markbox{21292}{step,} \markbox{21293}{suppose} \markbox{21294}{that} \markbox{m21295}{$U$} \markbox{21296}{is} \markbox{21297}{not} \markbox{m21298}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{21299}{and} \markbox{21300}{that} \markbox{21301}{we} \markbox{21302}{have} \markbox{21303}{defined} \markbox{m21304}{$\hx_V$} \markbox{21305}{for} \markbox{21306}{all} \markbox{m21307}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{21308}{and,} \markbox{21309}{in} \markbox{21310}{particular,} \markbox{21311}{for} \markbox{21312}{all} \markbox{m21313}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{m21314}{$V \in \calU$}.  \markbox{21315}{As} \markbox{21316}{before,} \markbox{21317}{if} \markbox{m21318}{$C_U$} \markbox{21319}{does} \markbox{21320}{not} \markbox{21321}{contain} \markbox{21322}{a} \markbox{21323}{marked} \markbox{21324}{or} \markbox{21325}{a} \markbox{21326}{projection} \markbox{m21327}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{21328}{for} \markbox{21329}{some} \markbox{m21330}{$V \nest U$}, \markbox{21331}{then} \markbox{21332}{we} \markbox{21333}{let} \markbox{m21334}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{21335}{be} \markbox{21336}{any} \markbox{21337}{point.}  \markbox{21338}{If} \markbox{m21339}{$C_U$} \markbox{21340}{happens} \markbox{21341}{to} \markbox{21342}{contain} \markbox{21343}{one} \markbox{21344}{of} \markbox{21345}{the} \markbox{21346}{endpoints} \markbox{21347}{but} \markbox{21348}{no} \markbox{m21349}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{21350}{for} \markbox{m21351}{$V \nest U$}, \markbox{21352}{then} \markbox{m21353}{$C_U$} \markbox{21354}{contains} \markbox{21355}{only} \markbox{21356}{that} \markbox{21357}{one} \markbox{21358}{endpoint} \markbox{21359}{(since} \markbox{m21360}{$U$} \markbox{21361}{is} \markbox{21362}{not} \markbox{m21363}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal), \markbox{21364}{and} \markbox{21365}{we} \markbox{21366}{let} \markbox{m21367}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{21368}{be} \markbox{21369}{any} point

Otherwise, \markbox{21370}{we} \markbox{21371}{set} \markbox{m21372}{$C=C_U$} \markbox{21373}{and} \markbox{21374}{let} \markbox{m21375}{$\calV_U$} \markbox{21376}{denote} \markbox{21377}{the} \markbox{21378}{set} \markbox{21379}{of} \markbox{m21380}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{21381}{domains} \markbox{m21382}{$V \nest U$} \markbox{21383}{so} \markbox{21384}{that} \markbox{m21385}{$\hd^V_U \in C$} \markbox{21386}{(or} \markbox{21387}{equivalently,} \markbox{m21388}{$(\hd^V_U)_0 = \hy_U$}).  \markbox{21389}{For} \markbox{21390}{each} \markbox{m21391}{$V \in \calV_U$}, \markbox{21392}{set} \markbox{m21393}{$C^V_U = \hull_C(\hd^V_U \cup \pi_C(\hx_V))$}, \markbox{21394}{namely} \markbox{21395}{the} \markbox{21396}{convex} \markbox{21397}{hull} \markbox{21398}{in} \markbox{m21399}{$C$} \markbox{21400}{of} \markbox{m21401}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{21402}{and} \markbox{21403}{the} \markbox{21404}{projections} \markbox{21405}{of} \markbox{21406}{the} \markbox{21407}{marked} \markbox{21408}{point} \markbox{21409}{labeled} \markbox{21410}{by} \markbox{m21411}{$l_V$} \markbox{21412}{down} \markbox{21413}{to} \markbox{21414}{the} \markbox{21415}{convex} \markbox{21416}{subset} \markbox{m21417}{$C$}.  \markbox{21418}{The} \markbox{21419}{following} \markbox{21420}{claim,} \markbox{21421}{which} \markbox{21422}{is} \markbox{21423}{exactly} \cite[Claim 10.4]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{21424}{helps} \markbox{21425}{us} \markbox{21426}{choose} \markbox{21427}{a} \markbox{21428}{point} \markbox{21429}{in} \markbox{21430}{such} \markbox{21431}{a} \markbox{m21432}{$C_U$}:

\begin{claim}\label{claim:cluster overlap}
For \markbox{21433}{every} \markbox{m21434}{$V, W \in \calV_U$}, \markbox{21435}{we} \markbox{21436}{have} \markbox{m21437}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U \neq \emptyset$}.  \markbox{21438}{Moreover,} \markbox{21439}{at} \markbox{21440}{least} \markbox{21441}{one} \markbox{21442}{of} \markbox{m21443}{$\hd^V_U \in C^W_U$} \markbox{21444}{or} \markbox{m21445}{$\hd^W_U \in C^V_U$} holds.


\end{claim}

\begin{proof}
We \markbox{21446}{may} \markbox{21447}{assume} \markbox{21448}{that} \markbox{m21449}{$\hd^V_U \neq \hd^W_U$}, \markbox{21450}{and} \markbox{21451}{hence} \markbox{21452}{that} \markbox{m21453}{$V \pitchfork W$}.  \markbox{21454}{If} \markbox{m21455}{$C^V_U \cap C^W_U = \emptyset$}, \markbox{21456}{then} \markbox{m21457}{$\hd^V_U \notin C^W_U$} \markbox{21458}{and} \markbox{m21459}{$\hd^W_U \notin C^V_U$}, \markbox{21460}{and} \markbox{21461}{it} \markbox{21462}{follows} \markbox{21463}{that} \markbox{m21464}{$l_V \neq l_W$}.  \markbox{21465}{The} \markbox{21466}{BGI} \markbox{21467}{property} \markbox{21468}{in} \markbox{21469}{(7)} \markbox{21470}{of} \markbox{21471}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{21472}{plus} \markbox{21473}{item} \markbox{21474}{(4)} \markbox{21475}{of} \markbox{21476}{Lemma} \ref{lem:interval control} \markbox{21477}{imply} \markbox{21478}{that}  \markbox{m21479}{$\hd^W_V \notin \Delta^{-1}_V(\hy_V)$} \markbox{21480}{and} \markbox{m21481}{$\hd^V_W \notin \Delta^{-1}_W(\hy_W)$}, \markbox{21482}{and} \markbox{21483}{hence} \markbox{m21484}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^W_V)_0$} \markbox{21485}{and} \markbox{m21486}{$\hy_W \neq (\hd^V_W)_0$}, \markbox{21487}{which} \markbox{21488}{is} \markbox{21489}{a} \markbox{21490}{contradiction} \markbox{21491}{of} \markbox{m21492}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21493}{of} \markbox{m21494}{$\hy$}.  \markbox{21495}{This} \markbox{21496}{proves} \markbox{21497}{the} claim.
\end{proof}

Hence \markbox{21498}{the} \markbox{21499}{Helly} \markbox{21500}{property} \markbox{21501}{for} \markbox{21502}{trees} \markbox{21503}{implies} \markbox{21504}{that} \markbox{m21505}{$\bigcap_{V \in \calV_U} C^V_U \subset \hT_U$} \markbox{21506}{is} \markbox{21507}{nonempty.}  \markbox{21508}{This} \markbox{21509}{intersection,} \markbox{21510}{nonetheless,} \markbox{21511}{may} \markbox{21512}{contain} \markbox{21513}{many} \markbox{m21514}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{21515}{for} \markbox{m21516}{$V \in \calV_U$}.  \markbox{21517}{The} \markbox{21518}{following} \markbox{21519}{claim,} \markbox{21520}{which} \markbox{21521}{is} \markbox{21522}{exactly} \cite[Claim 10.6]{Dur_infcube} \markbox{21523}{helps} \markbox{21524}{us} \markbox{21525}{make} \markbox{21526}{a} \markbox{21527}{consistent} choice:

\begin{claim}\label{claim:choose two}
Suppose \markbox{m21528}{$V, W \in \calW_U^{\nest}$}, \markbox{21529}{then} \markbox{m21530}{$\hd^V_U = \hd^W_U$}.
\end{claim}

\begin{proof}[Proof \markbox{21531}{of} \markbox{21532}{Claim} \ref{claim:choose two}]
For \markbox{21533}{a} \markbox{21534}{contradiction,} \markbox{21535}{suppose} \markbox{21536}{that} \markbox{m21537}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{21538}{so} \markbox{21539}{that} \markbox{m21540}{$V \pitchfork W$}.  \markbox{21541}{Then} \markbox{21542}{again} \markbox{21543}{the} \markbox{21544}{BGI} \markbox{21545}{property} \markbox{21546}{in} \markbox{21547}{item} \markbox{21548}{(7)} \markbox{21549}{of} \markbox{21550}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{21551}{implies} \markbox{21552}{that} \markbox{m21553}{$\hd^V_W = \hd^U_W(\hd^V_U)$} \markbox{21554}{and} \markbox{m21555}{$\hd^W_V = \hd^U_V(\hd^W_U)$}.  \markbox{21556}{But} \markbox{21557}{then} \markbox{m21558}{$\hy_W \neq (\hd^V_W)_0 = (\hd^U_W)_0((\hd^V_U)_0)$} \markbox{21559}{and} \markbox{m21560}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^W_V)_0 = (\hd^U_V)_0((\hd^W_U)_0)$}, \markbox{21561}{which} \markbox{21562}{contradicts} \markbox{m21563}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21564}{of} \markbox{m21565}{$\hy$}, \markbox{21566}{completing} \markbox{21567}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

Finally, \markbox{21568}{this} \markbox{21569}{last} \markbox{21570}{claim} \markbox{21571}{helps} \markbox{21572}{us} \markbox{21573}{make} \markbox{21574}{a} \markbox{21575}{consistent} \markbox{21576}{choice} \markbox{21577}{between} \markbox{m21578}{$\hd^V_U$} \markbox{21579}{sets} \markbox{21580}{and} \markbox{21581}{marked} \markbox{21582}{points} \markbox{21583}{when} \markbox{m21584}{$C_U$} \markbox{21585}{contains} both:

\begin{claim}\label{claim:good choice}
The \markbox{21586}{following} holds:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} If \markbox{21587}{there} \markbox{21588}{exists} \markbox{m21589}{$V \pitchfork U$} \markbox{21590}{so} \markbox{21591}{that} \markbox{m21592}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^U_V)'$}, \markbox{21593}{then} \markbox{21594}{for} \markbox{21595}{all} \markbox{m21596}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{21597}{with} \markbox{m21598}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{21599}{we} \markbox{21600}{have} \markbox{m21601}{$\hx_W = \hd^V_W$}.
\item {} If \markbox{21602}{there} \markbox{21603}{exists} \markbox{m21604}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{21605}{with} \markbox{m21606}{$\hy_W \neq (\hd^U_W)'(\hy_U)$}, \markbox{21607}{then} \markbox{21608}{for} \markbox{21609}{all} \markbox{m21610}{$V \pitchfork U$} \markbox{21611}{with} \markbox{m21612}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{21613}{we} \markbox{21614}{have} \markbox{m21615}{$\hy_V = (\hd^U_V)'$}.
\end{enumerate}
\begin{itemize}
\item {} In \markbox{21616}{particular,} \markbox{21617}{if} \markbox{m21618}{$V \in \calW_U^{\pitchfork}$} \markbox{21619}{and} \markbox{m21620}{$W \in \calW_U^{\nest}$}, \markbox{21621}{then} \markbox{m21622}{$\hd^V_U = \hd^W_U$}.
\end{itemize}
\end{claim}

\begin{proof}[Proof \markbox{21623}{of} \markbox{21624}{Claim} \ref{claim:good choice}]
Suppose \markbox{m21625}{$V \pitchfork U$} \markbox{21626}{as} \markbox{21627}{in} \markbox{21628}{item} \markbox{21629}{(1)} \markbox{21630}{of} \markbox{21631}{the} \markbox{21632}{claim,} \markbox{21633}{and} \markbox{21634}{let} \markbox{m21635}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{21636}{with} \markbox{m21637}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}.  \markbox{21638}{Then} \markbox{m21639}{$W \pitchfork V$}, \markbox{21640}{and} \markbox{21641}{since} \markbox{m21642}{$W \nest U$}, \markbox{21643}{we} \markbox{21644}{have} \markbox{m21645}{$(\hd^W_V)_0 = (\hd^U_V)_0 \neq \hy_V$}, \markbox{21646}{and} \markbox{21647}{hence} \markbox{m21648}{$\hx_W = \hd^V_W$}, \markbox{21649}{by} \markbox{21650}{definition} \markbox{21651}{of} \markbox{m21652}{$\hx_W$}.

Now \markbox{21653}{suppose} \markbox{m21654}{$W \in \calV_U$}, \markbox{21655}{as} \markbox{21656}{in} \markbox{21657}{item} \markbox{21658}{(2),} \markbox{21659}{and} \markbox{21660}{that} \markbox{m21661}{$V \pitchfork U$} \markbox{21662}{with} \markbox{m21663}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}. \markbox{21664}{Then} \markbox{m21665}{$W \pitchfork V$}.  \markbox{21666}{By} \markbox{m21667}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21668}{of} \markbox{m21669}{$\hy$}, \markbox{21670}{we} \markbox{21671}{have} \markbox{21672}{that} \markbox{m21673}{$\hy_U = (\hd^W_U)_0$}.  \markbox{21674}{But} \markbox{21675}{since} \markbox{m21676}{$\hd^V_U \neq \hd^W_U$}, \markbox{21677}{we} \markbox{21678}{have} \markbox{m21679}{$(\hd^V_U)_0 \neq (\hd^W_U)_0$}, \markbox{21680}{and} \markbox{21681}{so} \markbox{m21682}{$\hy_V = (\hd^U_V)_0 = (\hd^W_V)_0$} \markbox{21683}{since} \markbox{m21684}{$W \nest U$}.  \markbox{21685}{This} \markbox{21686}{completes} \markbox{21687}{the} proof.
\end{proof}

We \markbox{21688}{are} \markbox{21689}{finally} \markbox{21690}{ready} \markbox{21691}{to} \markbox{21692}{define} \markbox{21693}{our} \markbox{21694}{tuple} \markbox{m21695}{$\hx$}, \markbox{21696}{which} \markbox{21697}{we} \markbox{21698}{do} \markbox{21699}{domain-wise} \markbox{21700}{for} \markbox{21701}{each} \markbox{m21702}{$U \in \calU$}:

\begin{enumerate}
\item {} If \markbox{m21703}{$\hy_U$} \markbox{21704}{is} \markbox{21705}{not} \markbox{21706}{a} \markbox{21707}{marked} \markbox{21708}{or} \markbox{21709}{cluster} \markbox{21710}{point} \markbox{21711}{of} \markbox{m21712}{$\hT_{U,0}$}, \markbox{21713}{then} \markbox{21714}{we} \markbox{21715}{let} \markbox{m21716}{$\hx_U \in C_U$} \markbox{21717}{be} \markbox{21718}{any} \markbox{21719}{point} \markbox{21720}{in} \markbox{m21721}{$\Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$}.
\item {} For \markbox{21722}{any} \markbox{m21723}{$U$} \markbox{21724}{of} \markbox{21725}{type} \markbox{21726}{(1):} \markbox{21727}{If} \markbox{m21728}{$V \pitchfork U$} \markbox{21729}{or} \markbox{m21730}{$U \nest V$}, \markbox{21731}{we} \markbox{21732}{set} \markbox{m21733}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V$}, \markbox{21734}{and} \markbox{21735}{if} \markbox{m21736}{$U \nest V$}, \markbox{21737}{we} \markbox{21738}{set} \markbox{m21739}{$\hx_V = \hd^U_V(\hx_U)$}.
\item {} If \markbox{m21740}{$U$} \markbox{21741}{is} \markbox{m21742}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{21743}{and} \markbox{m21744}{$\hy_U$} \markbox{21745}{is} \markbox{21746}{a} \markbox{21747}{marked} \markbox{21748}{point} \markbox{21749}{of} \markbox{m21750}{$\hT_{U,0}$}, \markbox{21751}{then} \markbox{21752}{there} \markbox{21753}{are} \markbox{21754}{three} \markbox{21755}{subcases:} \label{item:minimal choice}
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} The \markbox{21756}{set} \markbox{m21757}{$\calW_U^{\pitchfork} = \{W \in \calU| W \pitchfork U \hspace{.1in}  \textrm{and } \hspace{.1in} (\hd^U_W)' \neq \hy_W\}$} \markbox{21758}{is} \markbox{21759}{nonempty,} \markbox{21760}{and} \markbox{21761}{we} \markbox{21762}{set} \markbox{m21763}{$\hx_U = \hd^W_U$} \markbox{21764}{for} \markbox{21765}{any} \markbox{21766}{(and} \markbox{21767}{hence} \markbox{21768}{all} \markbox{21769}{by} \markbox{21770}{Claim} \ref{claim:choose one}) \markbox{m21771}{$W \in \calW_U^{\pitchfork}$};
\item {} \markbox{m21772}{$\calW_U^{\nest} = \{V \nest U| (\hd^U_V)'(\hy_U) \neq \hy_V \hspace{.1in} \textrm{and} \hspace{.1in} (\hd^U_W)'(\hy_U) \neq \hy_W\}$} \markbox{21773}{is} \markbox{21774}{nonempty,} \markbox{21775}{and} \markbox{21776}{we} \markbox{21777}{set} \markbox{m21778}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$} \markbox{21779}{for} \markbox{21780}{any} \markbox{21781}{(and} \markbox{21782}{hence} \markbox{21783}{all} \markbox{21784}{by} \markbox{21785}{Claim} \ref{claim:choose two}) \markbox{m21786}{$V \in \calW_U^{\nest}$}; \markbox{21787}{or} 
\item {} \markbox{m21788}{$\calW_U^{\pitchfork}$} \markbox{21789}{and} \markbox{m21790}{$\calW_U^{\nest}$} \markbox{21791}{are} \markbox{21792}{both} \markbox{21793}{empty,} \markbox{21794}{and} \markbox{21795}{we} \markbox{21796}{set} \markbox{m21797}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{21798}{to} \markbox{21799}{be} \markbox{21800}{any} \markbox{21801}{point} \markbox{21802}{of} \markbox{m21803}{$\hT^e_U$} \markbox{21804}{contained} \markbox{21805}{in} \markbox{m21806}{$C_U$}, \markbox{21807}{in} \markbox{21808}{particular} \markbox{21809}{a} \markbox{21810}{point} \markbox{21811}{which} \markbox{21812}{is} \markbox{21813}{not} \markbox{21814}{a} \markbox{21815}{cluster} \markbox{21816}{or} \markbox{21817}{marked} \markbox{21818}{point.} 
\end{enumerate}
\item {} Proceeding \markbox{21819}{inductively,} \markbox{21820}{if} \markbox{m21821}{$U$} \markbox{21822}{is} \markbox{21823}{not} \markbox{21824}{in} \markbox{21825}{cases} \markbox{21826}{(1)--(3)} \markbox{21827}{above,} \markbox{21828}{then} \markbox{m21829}{$\bigcap_{V \in \calV_U} C^V_U \neq \emptyset$} \markbox{21830}{and} \markbox{21831}{has} \markbox{21832}{finite} \markbox{21833}{diameter.}  \markbox{21834}{There} \markbox{21835}{are} \markbox{21836}{three} \markbox{21837}{subcases:} \label{item:general choice}
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m21838}{$\hx_U = \hd^W_U$} \markbox{21839}{for} \markbox{21840}{any} \markbox{m21841}{$W \in \calW_U^{\pitchfork}$} \markbox{21842}{if} \markbox{m21843}{$ \calW_U^{\pitchfork} \neq \emptyset$}, \label{item:choose transverse}
\item {} \markbox{m21844}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$} \markbox{21845}{for} \markbox{21846}{any} \markbox{m21847}{$V \in \calW_U^{\nest}$} \markbox{21848}{when} \markbox{m21849}{$\calW_U^{\nest} \neq \emptyset$}, \markbox{21850}{or} \label{item:choose nested}
\item {} Otherwise, \markbox{21851}{both} \markbox{m21852}{$\calW_U^{\pitchfork}$} \markbox{21853}{and} \markbox{m21854}{$\calW_U^{\nest}$} \markbox{21855}{are} \markbox{21856}{empty,} \markbox{21857}{and} \markbox{21858}{we} \markbox{21859}{set} \markbox{m21860}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{21861}{to} \markbox{21862}{be} \markbox{21863}{any} \markbox{21864}{point} \markbox{21865}{in} \markbox{m21866}{$\hT^e_U \cap C_U$}.
\end{enumerate}

\end{enumerate}

Finally, \markbox{21867}{we} \markbox{21868}{prove} \markbox{21869}{that} \markbox{m21870}{$\hx = (\hx_U)$} \markbox{21871}{is} \markbox{m21872}{$0$}-consistent \markbox{21873}{by} \markbox{21874}{a} \markbox{21875}{case-wise} \markbox{21876}{analysis,} \markbox{21877}{similar} \markbox{21878}{to} \markbox{21879}{the} \markbox{21880}{proof} \markbox{21881}{of} \markbox{21882}{Proposition} \ref{prop:Q-consistent}.  \markbox{21883}{Showing} \markbox{21884}{this} \markbox{21885}{will} \markbox{21886}{complete} \markbox{21887}{the} \markbox{21888}{proof} \markbox{21889}{of} \markbox{21890}{surjectivity} \markbox{21891}{of} \markbox{m21892}{$\Delta: \calQ \to \calQ'$}.  \markbox{21893}{The} \markbox{21894}{proof} \markbox{21895}{closely} \markbox{21896}{follows} \markbox{21897}{the} \markbox{21898}{analogous} \markbox{21899}{part} \markbox{21900}{of} \markbox{21901}{the} \markbox{21902}{proof} \markbox{21903}{from} \cite[Theorem 10.2]{Dur_infcube}.

\vspace{.1in}

\markbox{21904}{\underline{$U \pitchfork V$:}} \markbox{21905}{We} \markbox{21906}{may} \markbox{21907}{assume} \markbox{21908}{that} \markbox{m21909}{$\hx_V \neq \hd^U_V$}, \markbox{21910}{for} \markbox{21911}{we} \markbox{21912}{are} \markbox{21913}{done} \markbox{21914}{otherwise.}  \markbox{21915}{Then} \markbox{m21916}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^U_V)_0$}, \markbox{21917}{and} \markbox{21918}{so} \markbox{m21919}{$\hy_U = (\hd^V_U)_0$} \markbox{21920}{by} \markbox{m21921}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{21922}{of} \markbox{m21923}{$\hy$}.  \markbox{21924}{It} \markbox{21925}{follows} \markbox{21926}{that} \markbox{m21927}{$\hd^V_U \in C_U = \Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$}, \markbox{21928}{and} \markbox{21929}{necessarily} \markbox{m21930}{$\hd^V_U  \in \{\ha_V, \hb_V\}$}, \markbox{21931}{so} \markbox{21932}{we} \markbox{21933}{may} \markbox{21934}{assume} \markbox{21935}{without} \markbox{21936}{loss} \markbox{21937}{of} \markbox{21938}{generality} \markbox{21939}{that} \markbox{m21940}{$\hd^V_U = \ha_V$}.  \markbox{21941}{If} \markbox{m21942}{$U$} \markbox{21943}{is} \markbox{m21944}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal, \markbox{21945}{then} \markbox{21946}{our} \markbox{21947}{choice} \markbox{21948}{of} \markbox{m21949}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{21950}{in} \eqref{item:minimal choice} \markbox{21951}{says} \markbox{21952}{that} \markbox{m21953}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$}, \markbox{21954}{as} required.

Now \markbox{21955}{suppose} \markbox{21956}{that} \markbox{m21957}{$U$} \markbox{21958}{is} \markbox{21959}{not} \markbox{m21960}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.  \markbox{21961}{Set} \markbox{m21962}{$\calV_U$} \markbox{21963}{to} \markbox{21964}{be} \markbox{21965}{the} \markbox{21966}{set} \markbox{21967}{of} \markbox{m21968}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{m21969}{$W \nest U$} \markbox{21970}{with} \markbox{m21971}{$\hd^W_U \in C_U$}.  \markbox{21972}{Let} \markbox{m21973}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{21974}{be} \markbox{21975}{so} \markbox{21976}{that} \markbox{m21977}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}.  \markbox{21978}{Then} \markbox{m21979}{$W \pitchfork V$} \markbox{21980}{and} \markbox{m21981}{$(\hd^W_V)_0 = (\hd^U_V)_0 \neq \hy_V$}, \markbox{21982}{and} \markbox{21983}{so} \markbox{m21984}{$\hx_W = \hd^V_W = \ha_W$}, \markbox{21985}{with} \markbox{21986}{the} \markbox{21987}{first} \markbox{21988}{equality} \markbox{21989}{following} \markbox{21990}{from} \markbox{21991}{our} \markbox{21992}{choice} \markbox{21993}{in} \eqref{item:minimal choice} \markbox{21994}{and} \markbox{21995}{the} \markbox{21996}{last} \markbox{21997}{equality} \markbox{21998}{by} \markbox{m21999}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{22000}{of} \markbox{m22001}{$a$}.  \markbox{22002}{But} \markbox{22003}{this} \markbox{22004}{says} \markbox{22005}{that} \markbox{m22006}{$a = l_W$}, \markbox{22007}{and} \markbox{22008}{hence} \markbox{m22009}{$\ha_U \in C^W_U$} \markbox{22010}{for} \markbox{22011}{all} \markbox{m22012}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{22013}{(including} \markbox{22014}{those} \markbox{22015}{for} \markbox{22016}{which} \markbox{m22017}{$\hd^W_U = \hd^V_U = \ha_U$}).

It \markbox{22018}{follows} \markbox{22019}{then} \markbox{22020}{that} \markbox{m22021}{$\ha_U \in \bigcap_{W \in \calV_U}C^W_U$} \markbox{22022}{and} \markbox{22023}{so} \markbox{m22024}{$\hx_U = \ha_U$} \markbox{22025}{by} \markbox{22026}{definition} \markbox{22027}{of} \markbox{m22028}{$\hx$} \markbox{22029}{in} \markbox{22030}{item} \eqref{item:choose transverse} above.

\vspace{.1in}

\markbox{22031}{\underline{$V \nest U$:}} \markbox{22032}{We} \markbox{22033}{may} \markbox{22034}{assume} \markbox{22035}{that} \markbox{m22036}{$\hx_V \neq \hd^U_V(\hx_U)$}, \markbox{22037}{for} \markbox{22038}{we} \markbox{22039}{are} \markbox{22040}{done} \markbox{22041}{otherwise.}  \markbox{22042}{Then} \markbox{m22043}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^U_V)_0(\hy_U)$}, \markbox{22044}{and} \markbox{m22045}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{22046}{of} \markbox{m22047}{$\hy$} \markbox{22048}{implies} \markbox{22049}{that} \markbox{m22050}{$\hy_U = (\hd^V_U)'$}, \markbox{22051}{and} \markbox{22052}{thus} \markbox{m22053}{$\hd^V_U \in C_U = \Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$}.  \markbox{22054}{We} \markbox{22055}{claim} \markbox{22056}{that} \markbox{22057}{for} \markbox{22058}{all} \markbox{m22059}{$W \in \calV_U$}, \markbox{22060}{we} \markbox{22061}{have} \markbox{m22062}{$\hd^V_U \in C^W_U$}.

To \markbox{22063}{see} \markbox{22064}{this,} \markbox{22065}{is} \markbox{22066}{suffices} \markbox{22067}{to} \markbox{22068}{consider} \markbox{m22069}{$W \in \calV_U$} \markbox{22070}{with} \markbox{m22071}{$\hd^W_U \neq \hd^V_U$}.  \markbox{22072}{Then} \markbox{m22073}{$W \pitchfork V$}.  \markbox{22074}{But} \markbox{m22075}{$\hx_V \neq \hd^U_V(\hx_U)$}, \markbox{22076}{so} \markbox{22077}{if} \markbox{22078}{also} \markbox{m22079}{$\hd^V_U \notin C^W_U$}, \markbox{22080}{then} \markbox{m22081}{$\hx_V \neq \hd^U_V(\hd^W_U) = \hd^W_V$}, \markbox{22082}{while} \markbox{22083}{also} \markbox{m22084}{$\hx_W \neq \hd^U_W(\hd^V_U) = \hd^V_W$}, \markbox{22085}{which} \markbox{22086}{both} \markbox{22087}{use} \markbox{22088}{the} \markbox{22089}{BGI} \markbox{22090}{property} \markbox{22091}{in} \markbox{22092}{item} \markbox{22093}{(7)} \markbox{22094}{of} \markbox{22095}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.  \markbox{22096}{But} \markbox{22097}{then} \markbox{m22098}{$\hy_V \neq (\hd^W_V)_0$} \markbox{22099}{and} \markbox{m22100}{$\hy_W \neq (\hd^V_W)_0$}, \markbox{22101}{which} \markbox{22102}{contradicts} \markbox{m22103}{$0$}-consistency \markbox{22104}{of} \markbox{m22105}{$\hy$}.

Hence \markbox{m22106}{$\hd^V_U \in C^W_U$} \markbox{22107}{for} \markbox{22108}{all} \markbox{m22109}{$W \in \calV_U$}.  \markbox{22110}{It} \markbox{22111}{follows} \markbox{22112}{that} \markbox{m22113}{$\hd^V_U \in \bigcap_{W \in \calV_U} C^W_U$}, \markbox{22114}{and} \markbox{22115}{then} \eqref{item:choose nested} \markbox{22116}{says} \markbox{22117}{that} \markbox{m22118}{$\hx_U = \hd^V_U$}.



\vspace{.1in}

Hence \markbox{m22119}{$(\hx)$} \markbox{22120}{is} \markbox{m22121}{$0$}-consistent.  \markbox{22122}{Since} \markbox{m22123}{$\Delta(\hx) = \hy$} \markbox{22124}{because} \markbox{m22125}{$\hx_U \in \Delta^{-1}_U(\hy_U)$} \markbox{22126}{for} \markbox{22127}{all} \markbox{m22128}{$U \in \calU$}, \markbox{22129}{we} \markbox{22130}{are} \markbox{22131}{done} \markbox{22132}{with} \markbox{22133}{the} \markbox{22134}{proof} \markbox{22135}{of} \markbox{22136}{surjectivity} \markbox{22137}{of} \markbox{m22138}{$\Delta: \calQ \to \calQ'$}, \markbox{22139}{and} \markbox{22140}{this} \markbox{22141}{also} \markbox{22142}{defines} \markbox{22143}{the} \markbox{22144}{map} \markbox{m22145}{$\Xi:\calQ' \to \calQ$} \markbox{22146}{by} \markbox{m22147}{$\Xi(\hy) = \hx$}, \markbox{22148}{as} \markbox{22149}{defined} \markbox{22150}{above.}  \markbox{22151}{This} \markbox{22152}{completes} \markbox{22153}{the} \markbox{22154}{proof} \markbox{22155}{of} \markbox{22156}{item} (2).

\medskip

\markbox{22157}{\textbf{\underline{Item (3): $\Delta:\calQ \to \calQ'$ is a quasi-isometry:}}} \markbox{22158}{The} \markbox{22159}{proof} \markbox{22160}{of} \markbox{22161}{this} \markbox{22162}{part} \markbox{22163}{proceeds} \markbox{22164}{similarly} \markbox{22165}{to} \markbox{22166}{its} \markbox{22167}{analogue} \markbox{22168}{in} \cite[Theorem 10.2]{Dur_infcube}, \markbox{22169}{though} \markbox{22170}{with} \markbox{22171}{some} \markbox{22172}{modest} \markbox{22173}{simplifications} \markbox{22174}{(see} \markbox{22175}{especially} \cite[Subsection 9.1]{Dur_infcube}).

Since \markbox{m22176}{$\Delta|_{\calQ}$} \markbox{22177}{is} \markbox{22178}{surjective} \markbox{22179}{and} \markbox{22180}{distance} \markbox{22181}{non-increasing,} \markbox{22182}{it} \markbox{22183}{suffices} \markbox{22184}{to} \markbox{22185}{prove} \markbox{22186}{that} \markbox{m22187}{$d_{\calQ} \prec d_{\calQ'}$}, \markbox{22188}{and} \markbox{22189}{for} \markbox{22190}{this} \markbox{22191}{it} \markbox{22192}{suffices} \markbox{22193}{to} \markbox{22194}{bound} \markbox{22195}{the} \markbox{22196}{distances} \markbox{22197}{in} \markbox{22198}{each} \markbox{m22199}{$U \in \calU$}.

Let \markbox{m22200}{$\hx, \hy \in \calQ$} \markbox{22201}{with} \markbox{m22202}{$\hx' = \Delta(\hx)$} \markbox{22203}{and} \markbox{m22204}{$\hy' = \Delta(\hy)$}.  \markbox{22205}{We} \markbox{22206}{may} \markbox{22207}{assume} \markbox{22208}{that} \markbox{m22209}{$\hx_U \neq \hy_U$} \markbox{22210}{for} \markbox{22211}{any} \markbox{m22212}{$U\in \calU$} \markbox{22213}{that} \markbox{22214}{we} \markbox{22215}{will} \markbox{22216}{consider.}  \markbox{22217}{We} \markbox{22218}{begin} \markbox{22219}{by} \markbox{22220}{making} \markbox{22221}{a} \markbox{22222}{useful} reduction.

Observe \markbox{22223}{that} \markbox{22224}{item} \markbox{22225}{(9)} \markbox{22226}{of} \markbox{22227}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{22228}{implies} \markbox{22229}{that} \markbox{22230}{there} \markbox{22231}{are} \markbox{22232}{at} \markbox{22233}{most} \markbox{22234}{boundedly-many} \markbox{22235}{domains} \markbox{m22236}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{22237}{for} \markbox{22238}{which} \markbox{m22239}{$\hx_U,\hy_U$} \markbox{22240}{are} \markbox{22241}{in} \markbox{22242}{the} \markbox{22243}{same} \markbox{22244}{component} \markbox{22245}{of} \markbox{m22246}{$\hT^e_U$}, \markbox{22247}{where} \markbox{22248}{the} \markbox{22249}{bound} \markbox{22250}{is} \markbox{22251}{controlled} \markbox{22252}{by} \markbox{m22253}{$\mathfrak S$}.  \markbox{22254}{For} \markbox{22255}{such} \markbox{m22256}{$U$}, \markbox{22257}{we} \markbox{22258}{have} \markbox{m22259}{$d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U, \hy_U) \leq d_{\hT'_U}(\hx'_U, \hy'_U) + B^2$} \markbox{22260}{because} \markbox{22261}{at} \markbox{22262}{most} \markbox{m22263}{$B$}-many \markbox{22264}{subtrees} \markbox{22265}{of} \markbox{22266}{diameter} \markbox{m22267}{$B$} \markbox{22268}{have} \markbox{22269}{been} \markbox{22270}{deleted} \markbox{22271}{from} \markbox{22272}{that} \markbox{22273}{edge.}  \markbox{22274}{Hence} \markbox{22275}{we} \markbox{22276}{may} \markbox{22277}{deal} \markbox{22278}{with} \markbox{22279}{these} \markbox{22280}{boundedly-many} \markbox{22281}{domains} \markbox{22282}{with} \markbox{22283}{an} \markbox{22284}{additive} \markbox{22285}{constant} \markbox{22286}{in} \markbox{22287}{the} \markbox{22288}{distance} \markbox{22289}{estimate} \markbox{22290}{comparing} \markbox{m22291}{$d_{\calQ}(\hx,\hy)$} \markbox{22292}{and} \markbox{m22293}{$d_{\calQ'}(\hx',\hy')$}. \markbox{22294}{Hereafter,} \markbox{22295}{we} \markbox{22296}{assume} \markbox{22297}{that} \markbox{22298}{at} \markbox{22299}{least} \markbox{22300}{one} \markbox{22301}{of} \markbox{m22302}{$\hx_U, \hy_U$} \markbox{22303}{coincides} \markbox{22304}{with} \markbox{22305}{a} \markbox{22306}{cluster,} \markbox{22307}{or} \markbox{22308}{they} \markbox{22309}{are} \markbox{22310}{separated} \markbox{22311}{by} \markbox{22312}{at} \markbox{22313}{least} \markbox{22314}{one} cluster.



\smallskip

There \markbox{22315}{are} \markbox{22316}{two} \markbox{22317}{cases,} \markbox{22318}{(1)} \markbox{m22319}{$U$} \markbox{22320}{is} \markbox{m22321}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{22322}{and} \markbox{22323}{(2)} otherwise.

\smallskip

\markbox{22324}{\underline{Case (1)}}: \markbox{22325}{Then} \markbox{m22326}{$\hT^e_U$} \markbox{22327}{has} \markbox{22328}{one} \markbox{22329}{component.}  \markbox{22330}{So} \markbox{22331}{there} \markbox{22332}{are} \markbox{22333}{at} \markbox{22334}{most} \markbox{m22335}{$B$}-many \markbox{22336}{subtrees} \markbox{22337}{of} \markbox{22338}{diameter} \markbox{22339}{at} \markbox{22340}{most} \markbox{m22341}{$B$} \markbox{22342}{in} \markbox{m22343}{$\hT^e_U$} \markbox{22344}{being} \markbox{22345}{collapsed.}  \markbox{22346}{By} \markbox{22347}{item} \markbox{22348}{(9)} \markbox{22349}{of} \markbox{22350}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control} \markbox{22351}{there} \markbox{22352}{are} \markbox{22353}{at} \markbox{22354}{most} \markbox{22355}{boundedly-many} \markbox{22356}{(in} \markbox{m22357}{$\mathfrak S$}) \markbox{22358}{such} \markbox{m22359}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{m22360}{$U$} \markbox{22361}{for} \markbox{22362}{which} \markbox{22363}{one} \markbox{22364}{of} \markbox{m22365}{$\hx_U, \hy_U$} \markbox{22366}{is} \markbox{22367}{not} \markbox{22368}{a} \markbox{22369}{cluster} \markbox{22370}{point.}  \markbox{22371}{We} \markbox{22372}{may} \markbox{22373}{deal} \markbox{22374}{with} \markbox{22375}{such} \markbox{m22376}{$U$} \markbox{22377}{by} \markbox{22378}{increasing} \markbox{22379}{the} \markbox{22380}{additive} \markbox{22381}{constant} \markbox{22382}{in} \markbox{22383}{the} \markbox{22384}{distance} estimate.

The \markbox{22385}{general} \markbox{22386}{case} \markbox{22387}{is} \markbox{22388}{where} \markbox{m22389}{$\hx_U, \hy_U$} \markbox{22390}{are} \markbox{22391}{the} \markbox{22392}{distinct} \markbox{22393}{endpoint} \markbox{22394}{clusters} \markbox{22395}{of} \markbox{22396}{the} \markbox{22397}{interval} \markbox{m22398}{$\hT_U$}.  \markbox{22399}{In} \markbox{22400}{this} \markbox{22401}{case,} 
$$d_{\hT'_U}(\hx'_U,\hy'_U)  \geq d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U) - B^2 \geq K - B^2 - 2r_1,$$ \markbox{22402}{by} \markbox{22403}{item} \markbox{22404}{(6)} \markbox{22405}{of} \markbox{22406}{Lemma} \ref{lem:collapsed interval control}.   \markbox{22407}{Hence} \markbox{22408}{by} \markbox{22409}{choosing} \markbox{m22410}{$K = K(\mathfrak S)>0$} \markbox{22411}{sufficiently} \markbox{22412}{large} \markbox{22413}{and} \markbox{22414}{requiring} \markbox{22415}{that} \markbox{m22416}{$B^2_{tt}-2r_1<K$}, \markbox{22417}{we} \markbox{22418}{can} \markbox{22419}{guarantee} \markbox{22420}{that} \markbox{m22421}{$d_{\hT'_U}(\hx'_U,\hy'_U) >1$} \markbox{22422}{allowing} \markbox{22423}{the} estimate
$$d_{\hT_U}(\hx_U,\hy_U) \leq d_{\hT'_U}(\hx'_U,\hy'_U) + B^2 \leq (1+B^2)d_{\hT'_U}(\hx'_U,\hy'_U).$$
Thus \markbox{22424}{we} \markbox{22425}{can} \markbox{22426}{account} \markbox{22427}{for} \markbox{22428}{these} \markbox{22429}{domains} \markbox{22430}{via} \markbox{22431}{a} \markbox{22432}{bounded} \markbox{22433}{multiplicative} error.


\smallskip
\markbox{22434}{\underline{Case (2)}}:  \markbox{22435}{Suppose} \markbox{22436}{that} \markbox{m22437}{$U \in \calU$} \markbox{22438}{is} \markbox{22439}{not} \markbox{m22440}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal.  \markbox{22441}{Since} \markbox{m22442}{$\hx_U \neq \hy_U$}, \markbox{22443}{there} \markbox{22444}{is} \markbox{22445}{some} \markbox{22446}{collection} \markbox{22447}{of} \markbox{22448}{edge} \markbox{22449}{components} \markbox{m22450}{$E_1, \dots, E_k\subset \hT^e_U$} \markbox{22451}{separating} \markbox{m22452}{$\hx_U$} \markbox{22453}{from} \markbox{m22454}{$\hy_U$}, \markbox{22455}{i.e.} \markbox{22456}{intersecting} \markbox{m22457}{$[\hx_U, \hy_U]_{\hT_U}$}.  \markbox{22458}{By} \markbox{22459}{assumption,} \markbox{22460}{each} \markbox{22461}{such} \markbox{22462}{component} \markbox{22463}{contains} \markbox{22464}{at} \markbox{22465}{most} \markbox{m22466}{$B$}-many \markbox{22467}{subintervals} \markbox{22468}{in} \markbox{m22469}{$\calB$} \markbox{22470}{of} \markbox{22471}{diameter} \markbox{22472}{at} \markbox{22473}{most} \markbox{m22474}{$B$} \markbox{22475}{which} \markbox{22476}{are} \markbox{22477}{collapsed} \markbox{22478}{by} \markbox{m22479}{$\Delta_U:\hT_U \to \hT'_U$}.  \markbox{22480}{Moreover,} \markbox{22481}{adjacent} \markbox{22482}{intervals} \markbox{m22483}{$E_i, E_{i+1}$} \markbox{22484}{are} \markbox{22485}{attached} \markbox{22486}{at} \markbox{22487}{some} \markbox{22488}{collapsed} \markbox{22489}{cluster} \markbox{m22490}{$C_i$}.  \markbox{22491}{For} \markbox{22492}{each} \markbox{22493}{such} \markbox{22494}{collapsed} \markbox{22495}{cluster} \markbox{m22496}{$C_i$}, \markbox{22497}{choose} \markbox{22498}{a} \markbox{m22499}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{22500}{domain} \markbox{m22501}{$V_i \nest U$} \markbox{22502}{with} \markbox{m22503}{$\hd^{V_i}_U \in C_i$}.  \markbox{22504}{Observe} that
\begin{eqnarray*}
d_{\hT_U}(C_i,C_{i+1}) &\leq& d_{\hT'_U}(\Delta_U(C_i), \Delta_U(C_{i+1})) + B^2\\
&\leq& d_{\hT'_U}(\Delta_U(C_i), \Delta_U(C_{i+1})) + B^2d_{\hT'_{V_i}}(\hx'_{V_i}, \hy'_{V_i}).
\end{eqnarray*}

Hence \markbox{22505}{we} \markbox{22506}{can} \markbox{22507}{account} \markbox{22508}{for} \markbox{22509}{the} \markbox{22510}{lost} \markbox{22511}{distance} \markbox{22512}{along} \markbox{m22513}{$[\hx_U, \hy_U]$} \markbox{22514}{between} \markbox{22515}{each} \markbox{22516}{pair} \markbox{22517}{of} \markbox{22518}{successive} \markbox{22519}{collapsed} \markbox{22520}{cluster} \markbox{22521}{points} \markbox{m22522}{$C_i, C_{i+1}$} \markbox{22523}{(i.e.,} \markbox{22524}{the} \markbox{22525}{distance} \markbox{22526}{lost} \markbox{22527}{in} \markbox{22528}{the} \markbox{22529}{edge} \markbox{m22530}{$E_i$}) \markbox{22531}{by} \markbox{22532}{distances} \markbox{22533}{in} \markbox{22534}{the} \markbox{m22535}{$\nest_{\calU}$}-minimal \markbox{22536}{domains} \markbox{m22537}{$V_i$}.  \markbox{22538}{Similarly,} \markbox{22539}{we} \markbox{22540}{can} \markbox{22541}{use} \markbox{m22542}{$V_1, V_k$} \markbox{22543}{to} \markbox{22544}{account} \markbox{22545}{for} \markbox{22546}{any} \markbox{22547}{lost} \markbox{22548}{distance} \markbox{22549}{between} \markbox{m22550}{$\hx_U, C_1$} \markbox{22551}{and} \markbox{m22552}{$C_n, \hy_U$}, \markbox{22553}{respectively.}  \markbox{22554}{Since} \markbox{22555}{each} \markbox{22556}{domain} \markbox{22557}{in} \markbox{m22558}{$\calU$} \markbox{22559}{nests} \markbox{22560}{into} \markbox{22561}{at} \markbox{22562}{most} \markbox{22563}{boundedly-many} \markbox{22564}{domains} \markbox{22565}{in} \markbox{m22566}{$\calU$} \markbox{22567}{by} \markbox{22568}{the} \markbox{22569}{Covering} \markbox{22570}{Lemma} \ref{lem:covering}, \markbox{22571}{the} \markbox{22572}{proof} \markbox{22573}{of} \markbox{22574}{case} \markbox{22575}{(2)} \markbox{22576}{is} \markbox{22577}{complete.}  \markbox{22578}{This} \markbox{22579}{completes} \markbox{22580}{the} \markbox{22581}{proof} \markbox{22582}{of} \markbox{22583}{the} theorem.
\end{proof}




\section{Proof of the Stable Intervals Theorem \ref{thm:stable intervals}} \label{app:SI}

We \markbox{22584}{will} \markbox{22585}{give} \markbox{22586}{a} \markbox{22587}{fairly} \markbox{22588}{complete} \markbox{22589}{accounting} \markbox{22590}{of} \markbox{22591}{the} \markbox{22592}{two} \markbox{22593}{main} \markbox{22594}{arguments} \markbox{22595}{involved} \markbox{22596}{in} \markbox{22597}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.  \markbox{22598}{See} \markbox{22599}{Subsection} \ref{subsec:detailed sketch} \markbox{22600}{for} \markbox{22601}{a} \markbox{22602}{detailed} \markbox{22603}{sketch} \markbox{22604}{and} \markbox{22605}{outline.}  \markbox{22606}{The} \markbox{22607}{two} \markbox{22608}{key} \markbox{22609}{arguments} \markbox{22610}{involve} \markbox{22611}{showing} \markbox{22612}{that} \markbox{22613}{we} \markbox{22614}{can} \markbox{22615}{stably} \markbox{22616}{add} \markbox{22617}{one} \markbox{22618}{cluster} \markbox{22619}{point} \markbox{22620}{and} \markbox{22621}{then} \markbox{22622}{that} \markbox{22623}{we} \markbox{22624}{can} \markbox{22625}{iterate} \markbox{22626}{this} process.

\subsection{Adding a cluster point}

In \markbox{22627}{this} \markbox{22628}{subsection,} \markbox{22629}{we} \markbox{22630}{explain} \markbox{22631}{how} \markbox{22632}{to} \markbox{22633}{build} \markbox{22634}{a} \markbox{22635}{stable} \markbox{22636}{decomposition} \markbox{22637}{when} \markbox{22638}{adding} \markbox{22639}{a} \markbox{22640}{cluster} \markbox{22641}{point} \markbox{22642}{to} \markbox{22643}{the} \markbox{22644}{setup.}  \markbox{22645}{This} \markbox{22646}{is} \markbox{22647}{the} \markbox{22648}{main} \markbox{22649}{bit} \markbox{22650}{of} \markbox{22651}{work} \markbox{22652}{for} \markbox{22653}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}.

\begin{proposition} \label{prop:add cluster}
Let \markbox{m22654}{$\calZ$} \markbox{22655}{be} \markbox{22656}{a} \markbox{22657}{geodesic} \markbox{m22658}{$\delta$}-hyperbolic \markbox{22659}{space,} \markbox{m22660}{$\epsilon>0$}, \markbox{22661}{and} \markbox{m22662}{$r_1,r_2>0$} \markbox{22663}{be} \markbox{22664}{positive} \markbox{22665}{integers.}  \markbox{22666}{Let} \markbox{m22667}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{22668}{be} \markbox{22669}{an} \markbox{m22670}{$\epsilon$}-setup \markbox{22671}{and} \markbox{22672}{further} \markbox{22673}{fix} \markbox{22674}{a} \markbox{22675}{point} \markbox{m22676}{$z \in \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a,b))$}.  Then
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} \markbox{m22677}{$(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$} \markbox{22678}{is} \markbox{22679}{an} \markbox{m22680}{$\epsilon$}-setup;
\item {} The \markbox{22681}{two} \markbox{22682}{setups} \markbox{m22683}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{22684}{and} \markbox{m22685}{$(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$} \markbox{22686}{are} \markbox{m22687}{$(1,\epsilon)$}-admissible;
\item {} There \markbox{22688}{exists} \markbox{m22689}{$L_1=L_1(\delta, \epsilon)>0$} \markbox{22690}{so} \markbox{22691}{that} \markbox{22692}{the} \markbox{22693}{stable} \markbox{22694}{intervals} \markbox{m22695}{$T$} \markbox{22696}{and} \markbox{m22697}{$T'$} \markbox{22698}{for} \markbox{22699}{the} \markbox{22700}{setups} \markbox{m22701}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{22702}{and} \markbox{m22703}{$(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$} \markbox{22704}{admit} \markbox{m22705}{$\calY$}-stable \markbox{m22706}{$L_1$}-compatible decompositions;
\item {} There \markbox{22707}{exists} \markbox{m22708}{$L_2 = L_2(\delta, \epsilon, r_1,r_2)>0$} \markbox{22709}{so} \markbox{22710}{that} \markbox{22711}{the} \markbox{m22712}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{22713}{of} \markbox{m22714}{$T,T'$} \markbox{22715}{admit} \markbox{m22716}{$\calY$}-stable \markbox{m22717}{$L_2$}-compatible decompositions.
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
Since \markbox{22718}{the} \markbox{22719}{points} \markbox{m22720}{$a,b$} \markbox{22721}{have} \markbox{22722}{not} \markbox{22723}{changed,} \markbox{22724}{the} \markbox{22725}{first} \markbox{22726}{two} \markbox{22727}{conclusions} \markbox{22728}{are} \markbox{22729}{automatic} \markbox{22730}{from} \markbox{22731}{the} assumptions.

Choosing \markbox{m22732}{$E \gg \epsilon$}, \markbox{22733}{Proposition} \ref{prop:cluster sep graph} \markbox{22734}{implies} \markbox{22735}{that} \markbox{22736}{both} \markbox{m22737}{$\calG = \calG_E(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{22738}{and} \markbox{m22739}{$\calG' = \calG_E(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$} \markbox{22740}{are} \markbox{22741}{intervals.}  \markbox{22742}{There} \markbox{22743}{are} \markbox{22744}{two} \markbox{22745}{main} \markbox{22746}{cases:} \markbox{22747}{(a)} \markbox{m22748}{$d(z,C)>E$} \markbox{22749}{for} \markbox{22750}{all} \markbox{22751}{clusters} \markbox{m22752}{$C$}, \markbox{22753}{or} \markbox{22754}{(b)} otherwise.

We \markbox{22755}{will} \markbox{22756}{deal} \markbox{22757}{with} \markbox{22758}{these} \markbox{22759}{cases} \markbox{22760}{separately,} \markbox{22761}{though} \markbox{22762}{the} \markbox{22763}{arguments} \markbox{22764}{are} \markbox{22765}{similar.}  \markbox{22766}{Moreover,} \markbox{22767}{for} \markbox{22768}{each} \markbox{22769}{case,} \markbox{22770}{we} \markbox{22771}{will} \markbox{22772}{want} \markbox{22773}{to} \markbox{22774}{deal} \markbox{22775}{both} \markbox{22776}{with} \markbox{22777}{the} \markbox{22778}{original} \markbox{22779}{decompositions} \markbox{22780}{of} \markbox{22781}{the} \markbox{22782}{stable} \markbox{22783}{tree} \markbox{m22784}{$T = T_e \cup T_c$}, \markbox{22785}{as} \markbox{22786}{well} \markbox{22787}{as} \markbox{22788}{its} \markbox{m22789}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{m22790}{$T = \bT_{e} \cup \bT_{c}$}.  \markbox{22791}{The} \markbox{22792}{compatible} \markbox{22793}{decompositions} \markbox{22794}{for} \markbox{22795}{the} \markbox{22796}{latter} \markbox{22797}{will} \markbox{22798}{be} \markbox{22799}{refined} \markbox{22800}{for} \markbox{22801}{the} \markbox{22802}{decomposition} \markbox{22803}{for} \markbox{22804}{the} \markbox{22805}{former,} \markbox{22806}{with} \markbox{22807}{possibly} \markbox{22808}{a} \markbox{22809}{slight} \markbox{22810}{increase} \markbox{22811}{in} \markbox{22812}{the} \markbox{22813}{error} \markbox{22814}{depending} \markbox{22815}{on} \markbox{m22816}{$r_1,r_2$}.

\medskip

\markbox{22817}{\underline{\textbf{Case (a), $z$ forms a split cluster}}}: \markbox{22818}{In} \markbox{22819}{this} \markbox{22820}{case,} \markbox{m22821}{$z$} \markbox{22822}{forms} \markbox{22823}{its} \markbox{22824}{own} \markbox{22825}{cluster} \markbox{22826}{and,} \markbox{22827}{in} \markbox{22828}{particular,} \markbox{22829}{does} \markbox{22830}{not} \markbox{22831}{affect} \markbox{22832}{membership} \markbox{22833}{of} \markbox{22834}{any} \markbox{22835}{other} \markbox{22836}{cluster.}  \markbox{22837}{Moreover,} \markbox{22838}{it} \markbox{22839}{cannot} \markbox{22840}{be} \markbox{22841}{an} \markbox{22842}{endpoint} \markbox{22843}{cluster} \markbox{22844}{of} \markbox{m22845}{$\calG'$}, \markbox{22846}{as} \markbox{22847}{those} \markbox{22848}{necessarily} \markbox{22849}{contain} \markbox{m22850}{$a$} \markbox{22851}{and} \markbox{m22852}{$b$}.  \markbox{22853}{Hence} \markbox{22854}{there} \markbox{22855}{exist} \markbox{22856}{two} \markbox{22857}{clusters} \markbox{m22858}{$C_1,C_2$} \markbox{22859}{which} \markbox{22860}{are} \markbox{22861}{adjacent} \markbox{22862}{in} \markbox{m22863}{$\calG$} \markbox{22864}{but} \markbox{22865}{are} \markbox{22866}{separated} \markbox{22867}{by} \markbox{m22868}{$z$} \markbox{22869}{in} \markbox{m22870}{$\calG'$}, \markbox{22871}{say} \markbox{22872}{with} \markbox{m22873}{$C_1$} \markbox{22874}{on} \markbox{22875}{the} \markbox{22876}{side} \markbox{22877}{of} \markbox{m22878}{$a$} \markbox{22879}{and} \markbox{m22880}{$C_2$} \markbox{22881}{on} \markbox{22882}{the} \markbox{22883}{side} \markbox{22884}{of} \markbox{m22885}{$b$}.  \markbox{22886}{In} \markbox{22887}{this} \markbox{22888}{sense,} \markbox{22889}{we} \markbox{22890}{think} \markbox{22891}{of} \markbox{m22892}{$z$} \markbox{22893}{as} \markbox{22894}{splitting} \markbox{22895}{the} \markbox{22896}{clusters} \markbox{m22897}{$C_1,C_2$}.

Lemma \ref{lem:cluster arrangement} \markbox{22898}{implies} \markbox{22899}{that} \markbox{m22900}{$z$} \markbox{22901}{separates} \markbox{22902}{two} \markbox{22903}{clusters} \markbox{m22904}{$C,C'$} \markbox{22905}{for} \markbox{m22906}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{22907}{if} \markbox{22908}{and} \markbox{22909}{only} \markbox{22910}{if} \markbox{m22911}{$s(z)$} \markbox{22912}{separates} \markbox{m22913}{$s(C), s(C')$} \markbox{22914}{along} \markbox{m22915}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{22916}{It} \markbox{22917}{follows} \markbox{22918}{then} \markbox{22919}{that} \markbox{22920}{the} \markbox{22921}{subgraph} \markbox{22922}{of} \markbox{m22923}{$\calG$} \markbox{22924}{connecting} \markbox{22925}{the} \markbox{22926}{cluster} \markbox{22927}{containing} \markbox{m22928}{$a$} \markbox{22929}{to} \markbox{m22930}{$C_1$} \markbox{22931}{is} \markbox{22932}{identical} \markbox{22933}{to} \markbox{22934}{the} \markbox{22935}{subgraph} \markbox{22936}{of} \markbox{m22937}{$\calG_E(a,b;\calY \cup \{z\})$}, \markbox{22938}{and} \markbox{22939}{similarly} \markbox{22940}{for} \markbox{22941}{the} \markbox{22942}{subgraphs} \markbox{22943}{connecting} \markbox{m22944}{$C_2$} \markbox{22945}{to} \markbox{22946}{the} \markbox{22947}{cluster} \markbox{22948}{containing} \markbox{m22949}{$b$}.  \markbox{22950}{This} \markbox{22951}{says} \markbox{22952}{that} \markbox{22953}{for} \markbox{22954}{any} \markbox{22955}{pair} \markbox{m22956}{$C,C'$} \markbox{22957}{on} \markbox{22958}{the} \markbox{m22959}{$a$}-side \markbox{22960}{of} \markbox{m22961}{$z$} \markbox{22962}{in} \markbox{m22963}{$\calG'$}, \markbox{m22964}{$\lambda_0(C,C')$} \markbox{22965}{is} \markbox{22966}{an} \markbox{22967}{edge} \markbox{22968}{component} \markbox{22969}{of} \markbox{22970}{both} \markbox{m22971}{$T$} \markbox{22972}{and} \markbox{m22973}{$T'$}, \markbox{22974}{and} \markbox{22975}{similarly} \markbox{22976}{for} \markbox{22977}{such} \markbox{22978}{pairs}  \markbox{22979}{on} \markbox{22980}{the} \markbox{m22981}{$b$}-side \markbox{22982}{of} \markbox{m22983}{$z$}.  \markbox{22984}{Thus} \markbox{22985}{we} \markbox{22986}{can} \markbox{22987}{include} \markbox{22988}{each} \markbox{22989}{such} \markbox{22990}{component} \markbox{22991}{of} \markbox{m22992}{$E \subset T_e$} \markbox{22993}{and} \markbox{m22994}{$E \subset T'_e$} \markbox{22995}{in} \markbox{22996}{the} \markbox{22997}{respective} \markbox{22998}{stable} \markbox{22999}{decomposition} \markbox{m23000}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{23001}{and} \markbox{m23002}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$}, \markbox{23003}{where} \markbox{23004}{the} \markbox{23005}{identity} \markbox{23006}{map} \markbox{23007}{is} \markbox{23008}{the} \markbox{23009}{map} \markbox{23010}{described} \markbox{23011}{in} \markbox{23012}{parts} \eqref{item:stable pairs} \markbox{23013}{and} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{23014}{of} \markbox{23015}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}.  \markbox{23016}{By} \markbox{23017}{construction,} \markbox{23018}{each} \markbox{23019}{of} \markbox{23020}{these} \markbox{23021}{pieces} \markbox{23022}{has} \markbox{23023}{positive} \markbox{23024}{integer} \markbox{23025}{length,} \markbox{23026}{thus} \markbox{23027}{verifying} \markbox{23028}{property} \eqref{item:integer length}.

To \markbox{23029}{construct} \markbox{23030}{the} \markbox{23031}{rest} \markbox{23032}{of} \markbox{23033}{the} \markbox{23034}{stable} \markbox{23035}{decompositions,} \markbox{23036}{namely} \markbox{23037}{stable} \markbox{23038}{pieces} \markbox{23039}{of} \markbox{23040}{type} \eqref{item:close pairs} \markbox{23041}{in} \markbox{23042}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}, \markbox{23043}{we} \markbox{23044}{need} \markbox{23045}{to} \markbox{23046}{compare} \markbox{23047}{the} \markbox{23048}{component} \markbox{m23049}{$\lambda_0(C_1, C_2) \subset T_e$} \markbox{23050}{to} \markbox{23051}{the} \markbox{23052}{two} \markbox{23053}{components} \markbox{m23054}{$\lambda_0(C_1,z) \cup \lambda_0(z, C_2) \subset T'_e$}.  \markbox{23055}{First,} \markbox{23056}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close} \markbox{23057}{says} \markbox{23058}{that} \markbox{23059}{the} \markbox{23060}{endpoints} \markbox{23061}{of} \markbox{m23062}{$\lambda(C_1,C_2)$} \markbox{23063}{and} \markbox{m23064}{$\lambda(C_1,z)$} \markbox{23065}{on} \markbox{m23066}{$C_1$} \markbox{23067}{are} \markbox{m23068}{$14\epsilon$}-close, \markbox{23069}{and} \markbox{23070}{hence} \markbox{23071}{the} \markbox{23072}{endpoints} \markbox{23073}{of} \markbox{m23074}{$\lambda_0(C_1,C_2)$} \markbox{23075}{and} \markbox{m23076}{$\lambda_0(C_1,z)$} \markbox{23077}{are} \markbox{23078}{within} \markbox{m23079}{$14\epsilon+2$}, \markbox{23080}{and} \markbox{23081}{similarly} \markbox{23082}{for} \markbox{m23083}{$C_2$}.  \markbox{23084}{It} \markbox{23085}{follows} \markbox{23086}{from} \markbox{m23087}{$\delta$}-hyperbolicity \markbox{23088}{of} \markbox{m23089}{$\calZ$} \markbox{23090}{that} \markbox{m23091}{$\lambda_0(C_1, C_2)$} \markbox{23092}{and} \markbox{m23093}{$ \lambda_0(C_1,z) \cup \lambda_0(z, C_2)$} \markbox{23094}{are} \markbox{m23095}{$O(\epsilon)$}-Hausdorff \markbox{23096}{close.}  \markbox{23097}{Now,} \markbox{23098}{unless} \markbox{m23099}{$C_1,C_2$} \markbox{23100}{are} \markbox{m23101}{$O(\epsilon)$}-close \markbox{23102}{in} \markbox{m23103}{$\calZ$}---in \markbox{23104}{which} \markbox{23105}{case} \markbox{23106}{we} \markbox{23107}{can} \markbox{23108}{declare} \markbox{23109}{all} \markbox{23110}{three} \markbox{23111}{of} \markbox{23112}{these} \markbox{23113}{geodesics} \markbox{23114}{to} \markbox{23115}{be} \markbox{23116}{unstable---then} \markbox{23117}{the} \markbox{23118}{shadow} \markbox{m23119}{$s_T(z)$} \markbox{23120}{of} \markbox{m23121}{$z$} \markbox{23122}{on} \markbox{m23123}{$T$} \markbox{23124}{will} \markbox{23125}{be} \markbox{23126}{properly} \markbox{23127}{contained} \markbox{23128}{in} \markbox{m23129}{$\lambda_0(C_1,C_2)$} \markbox{23130}{and} \markbox{23131}{have} \markbox{m23132}{$O(\epsilon)$}-bounded \markbox{23133}{diameter.}    \markbox{23134}{Hence} \markbox{23135}{we} \markbox{23136}{can} \markbox{23137}{decompose} \markbox{23138}{these} \markbox{23139}{geodesics} \markbox{23140}{into} \markbox{m23141}{$O(\epsilon)$}-close \markbox{23142}{stable} \markbox{23143}{pieces} \markbox{23144}{and} \markbox{23145}{unstable} \markbox{23146}{pieces} \markbox{23147}{labeled} \markbox{23148}{by} \markbox{m23149}{$z$}, \markbox{23150}{as} \markbox{23151}{described} \markbox{23152}{in} \markbox{23153}{property} \eqref{item:unstable components}, \markbox{23154}{while} \markbox{23155}{satisfying} \markbox{23156}{the} \markbox{23157}{length} \markbox{23158}{requirement} \markbox{23159}{of} \eqref{item:integer length} \markbox{23160}{and} \markbox{23161}{proximity} \markbox{23162}{requirements} \markbox{23163}{of} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{23164}{and} \eqref{item:close pairs}; \markbox{23165}{see} \markbox{23166}{Figure} \ref{fig:split cluster} \markbox{23167}{for} \markbox{23168}{a} \markbox{23169}{heuristic} \markbox{23170}{picture.}  \markbox{23171}{For} \markbox{23172}{the} \markbox{23173}{bijection} \markbox{m23174}{$\alpha:\pi_0(T_s) \to \pi_0(T'_s)$}, \markbox{23175}{since} \markbox{m23176}{$T_s,T'_s$} \markbox{23177}{have} \markbox{23178}{the} \markbox{23179}{same} \markbox{23180}{number} \markbox{23181}{of} \markbox{23182}{components,} \markbox{23183}{we} \markbox{23184}{can} \markbox{23185}{take} \markbox{23186}{let} \markbox{m23187}{$\alpha$} \markbox{23188}{denote} \markbox{23189}{the} \markbox{23190}{natural} \markbox{23191}{order-preserving} \markbox{23192}{bijection,} \markbox{23193}{i.e.} \markbox{23194}{the} \markbox{23195}{one} \markbox{23196}{obtained} \markbox{23197}{by} \markbox{23198}{moving} \markbox{23199}{along} \markbox{23200}{the} \markbox{23201}{geodesics} \markbox{m23202}{$[a,b]_{T}$} \markbox{23203}{and} \markbox{m23204}{$[a,b]_{T'}$}.  \markbox{23205}{By} \markbox{23206}{construction,} \markbox{23207}{this} \markbox{23208}{bijection} \markbox{23209}{identifies} \markbox{23210}{the} \markbox{23211}{components} \markbox{23212}{we} \markbox{23213}{want} \markbox{23214}{so} \markbox{23215}{that} \markbox{23216}{the} \markbox{23217}{related} \markbox{23218}{conditions} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{23219}{and} \eqref{item:close pairs} \markbox{23220}{are} satisfied.

Finally, \markbox{23221}{we} \markbox{23222}{need} \markbox{23223}{to} \markbox{23224}{confirm} \markbox{23225}{the} \markbox{23226}{properties} \markbox{23227}{in} \eqref{item:adjacency} \markbox{23228}{for} \markbox{23229}{the} \markbox{23230}{order-preserving} \markbox{23231}{bijection} \markbox{m23232}{$\beta:\pi_0(T - T_s) \to \pi_0 (T'-T'_s)$} \markbox{23233}{induced} \markbox{23234}{by} \markbox{m23235}{$\alpha$}.  \markbox{23236}{Since} \markbox{m23237}{$\beta$} \markbox{23238}{is} \markbox{23239}{order-preserving} \markbox{23240}{(with} \markbox{23241}{the} \markbox{23242}{order} \markbox{23243}{being} \markbox{23244}{``from} \markbox{m23245}{$a$} \markbox{23246}{to} \markbox{m23247}{$b$}'', \markbox{23248}{as} \markbox{23249}{in} \markbox{23250}{Definition} \ref{defn:order preserving}), \eqref{item:endpoint condition}, \markbox{23251}{i.e.} \markbox{23252}{that} \markbox{23253}{the} \markbox{23254}{components} \markbox{23255}{of} \markbox{m23256}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{23257}{and} \markbox{m23258}{$T' - T'_s$} \markbox{23259}{associated} \markbox{23260}{to} \markbox{m23261}{$a$} \markbox{23262}{and} \markbox{m23263}{$b$} \markbox{23264}{are} \markbox{23265}{identified,} \markbox{23266}{is} \markbox{23267}{automatically} \markbox{23268}{satisfied.}  \markbox{23269}{For} \eqref{item:cluster identify}, \markbox{23270}{note} \markbox{23271}{that} \markbox{m23272}{$\calY \cap (\calY \cup \{z\}) = \calY$}, \markbox{23273}{and,} \markbox{23274}{by} \markbox{23275}{construction} \markbox{23276}{again,} \markbox{23277}{if} \markbox{m23278}{$y \in \calY$}, \markbox{23279}{then} \markbox{m23280}{$\beta$} \markbox{23281}{identifies} \markbox{23282}{the} \markbox{23283}{component} \markbox{m23284}{$D_y$} \markbox{23285}{of} \markbox{m23286}{$T- T_s$} \markbox{23287}{corresponding} \markbox{23288}{to} \markbox{m23289}{$y$} \markbox{23290}{with} \markbox{m23291}{$D'_y$}, \markbox{23292}{the} \markbox{23293}{component} \markbox{23294}{of} \markbox{m23295}{$T'-T'_s$} \markbox{23296}{corresponding} \markbox{23297}{to} \markbox{m23298}{$y$}.  \markbox{23299}{In} \markbox{23300}{this} \markbox{23301}{case,} \markbox{23302}{this} \markbox{23303}{is} \markbox{23304}{because} \markbox{23305}{all} \markbox{23306}{such} \markbox{23307}{components} \markbox{23308}{are} \markbox{23309}{exactly} \markbox{23310}{the} \markbox{23311}{same.}   \markbox{23312}{This} \markbox{23313}{proves} \markbox{23314}{part} \markbox{23315}{(1)} \markbox{23316}{of} \markbox{23317}{the} statement.

For \markbox{23318}{part} \markbox{23319}{(2)} \markbox{23320}{of} \markbox{23321}{the} \markbox{23322}{statement,} \markbox{23323}{we} \markbox{23324}{want} \markbox{23325}{to} \markbox{23326}{consider} \markbox{23327}{how} \markbox{23328}{the} \markbox{m23329}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings \markbox{23330}{of} \markbox{m23331}{$T,T'$} \markbox{23332}{along} \markbox{m23333}{$T_c,T'_c$} \markbox{23334}{respectively} \markbox{23335}{affect} \markbox{23336}{the} \markbox{23337}{decompositions} \markbox{m23338}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{23339}{and} \markbox{m23340}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$}.  \markbox{23341}{First,} \markbox{23342}{observe} \markbox{23343}{that} \markbox{m23344}{$\bT_e \subset T_e$} \markbox{23345}{and} \markbox{m23346}{$\bT'_e \subset T'_e$} \markbox{23347}{by} \markbox{23348}{definition.}  \markbox{23349}{In} \markbox{23350}{particular,} \markbox{23351}{consider} \markbox{23352}{a} \markbox{23353}{component} \markbox{m23354}{$D \subset T_e$}, \markbox{23355}{where} \markbox{m23356}{$D = \lambda_0(C,C')$} \markbox{23357}{for} \markbox{23358}{adjacent} \markbox{23359}{clusters} \markbox{m23360}{$C,C'$}.  \markbox{23361}{Then} \markbox{23362}{the} \markbox{m23363}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{23364}{of} \markbox{m23365}{$D$} \markbox{23366}{either} \markbox{23367}{truncates} \markbox{m23368}{$D$} \markbox{23369}{to} \markbox{m23370}{$D_{thick} = D - (\mu_{r_1}(C) \cup \mu_{r_1}(C'))$}, \markbox{23371}{or} \markbox{23372}{possibly} \markbox{23373}{removes} \markbox{m23374}{$D$} \markbox{23375}{entirely} \markbox{23376}{from} \markbox{m23377}{$\bT_e$} \markbox{23378}{if} \markbox{m23379}{$d_T(\mu(C), \mu(C'))<r_2-2r_1$}.  \markbox{23380}{A} \markbox{23381}{similar} \markbox{23382}{statement} \markbox{23383}{holds} \markbox{23384}{for} \markbox{23385}{components} \markbox{23386}{of} \markbox{m23387}{$T'_e$}.

By \markbox{23388}{the} \markbox{23389}{above,} \markbox{23390}{most} \markbox{23391}{components} \markbox{23392}{of} \markbox{m23393}{$T_s$} \markbox{23394}{and} \markbox{m23395}{$T'_s$} \markbox{23396}{are} \markbox{23397}{identical} \markbox{23398}{components} \markbox{23399}{of} \markbox{m23400}{$T_e, T'_e$}, \markbox{23401}{and} \markbox{23402}{hence} \markbox{23403}{their} \markbox{23404}{thickenings} \markbox{23405}{are} \markbox{23406}{exactly} \markbox{23407}{the} \markbox{23408}{same} \markbox{23409}{by} \markbox{23410}{the} \markbox{23411}{above.}  \markbox{23412}{For} \markbox{23413}{the} \markbox{23414}{remaining} \markbox{23415}{components,} \markbox{23416}{namely} \markbox{m23417}{$\lambda_0(C_1,z), \lambda_0(z,C_2)$} \markbox{23418}{of} \markbox{m23419}{$T'_e$} \markbox{23420}{and} \markbox{m23421}{$\lambda_0(C_1,C_2)$} \markbox{23422}{of} \markbox{m23423}{$T_e$}, \markbox{23424}{each} \markbox{23425}{is} \markbox{23426}{either} \markbox{23427}{truncated} \markbox{23428}{or} \markbox{23429}{removed} \markbox{23430}{as} \markbox{23431}{above.}  \markbox{23432}{The} \markbox{23433}{remaining} \markbox{23434}{two} \markbox{23435}{components} \markbox{23436}{of} \markbox{23437}{the} \markbox{23438}{stable} \markbox{23439}{decomposition} \markbox{m23440}{$T_s$} \markbox{23441}{correspond} \markbox{23442}{to} \markbox{m23443}{$\lambda_0(C_1,z)$} \markbox{23444}{and} \markbox{m23445}{$\lambda_0(z,C_2)$}, \markbox{23446}{and} \markbox{23447}{so} \markbox{23448}{one} \markbox{23449}{can} \markbox{23450}{construct} \markbox{23451}{the} \markbox{23452}{corresponding} \markbox{23453}{components} \markbox{23454}{of} \markbox{m23455}{$\bT_s$} \markbox{23456}{by} \markbox{23457}{applying} \markbox{23458}{the} \markbox{23459}{same} \markbox{23460}{procedure} \markbox{23461}{to} \markbox{23462}{the} \markbox{m23463}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickening \markbox{23464}{of} \markbox{m23465}{$\lambda_0(C_1,z)$} \markbox{23466}{and} \markbox{m23467}{$\lambda_0(z,C_2)$}.  \markbox{23468}{Note} \markbox{23469}{that} \markbox{23470}{this} \markbox{23471}{can} \markbox{23472}{inflate} \markbox{23473}{the} \markbox{23474}{proximity} \markbox{23475}{constants,} \markbox{23476}{but} \markbox{23477}{only} \markbox{23478}{in} \markbox{23479}{terms} \markbox{23480}{of} \markbox{m23481}{$r_1,r_2$}.  \markbox{23482}{The} \markbox{23483}{rest} \markbox{23484}{of} \markbox{23485}{the} \markbox{23486}{proof} \markbox{23487}{goes} \markbox{23488}{through} \markbox{23489}{unchanged;} \markbox{23490}{see} \markbox{23491}{Figure} \ref{fig:split cluster}.




\medskip

\markbox{23492}{\underline{\textbf{Case (b), $z$ affects other clusters}}}: \markbox{23493}{Suppose} \markbox{23494}{now} \markbox{23495}{instead} \markbox{23496}{that} \markbox{23497}{there} \markbox{23498}{exists} \markbox{23499}{some} \markbox{23500}{cluster} \markbox{m23501}{$C$} \markbox{23502}{for} \markbox{m23503}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{23504}{so} \markbox{23505}{that} \markbox{m23506}{$d(z,C)<E$}; \markbox{23507}{we} \markbox{23508}{say} \markbox{m23509}{$C$} \markbox{23510}{is} \markbox{23511}{an}  \markbox{23512}{\emph{affected cluster}}.

\begin{claim}\label{claim:bounded affect}
If \markbox{m23513}{$3E - 56\epsilon > 2E$}, \markbox{23514}{then} \markbox{23515}{there} \markbox{23516}{are} \markbox{23517}{at} \markbox{23518}{most} \markbox{23519}{three} \markbox{23520}{affected} \markbox{23521}{clusters,} \markbox{23522}{and} \markbox{23523}{they} \markbox{23524}{are} \markbox{23525}{adjacent} \markbox{23526}{in} \markbox{m23527}{$\calG$}.
\end{claim}

\begin{proof}
Suppose \markbox{23528}{that} \markbox{m23529}{$C_1,\dots, C_4$} \markbox{23530}{are} \markbox{23531}{four} \markbox{23532}{clusters} \markbox{23533}{appearing} \markbox{23534}{in} \markbox{23535}{that} \markbox{23536}{order} \markbox{23537}{along} \markbox{m23538}{$\lambda(a,b)$}.  \markbox{23539}{By} \markbox{23540}{item} \markbox{23541}{(1)} \markbox{23542}{of} \markbox{23543}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close}, \markbox{23544}{since} \markbox{m23545}{$d(C_i, C_{i+1})\geq E$}, \markbox{23546}{we} \markbox{23547}{have} \markbox{m23548}{$d(s(C_i), s(C_{i+1}))> E - 14\epsilon$}, \markbox{23549}{for} \markbox{m23550}{$i = 1,2,3$}.

Since \markbox{23551}{the} \markbox{23552}{shadows} \markbox{23553}{are} \markbox{23554}{disjoint} \markbox{23555}{segments} \markbox{23556}{of} \markbox{23557}{the} \markbox{23558}{geodesic} \markbox{m23559}{$\lambda(a,b)$}, \markbox{23560}{we} \markbox{23561}{have} that
$$d(s(C_1), s(C_4)) \geq d(s(C_1), s(C_2)) + d(s(C_2), s(C_3))+d(s(C_3), s(C_4)) \geq 3E -42\epsilon.$$
Hence \markbox{23562}{if} \markbox{m23563}{$3E-56\epsilon \geq 2E$}, \markbox{23564}{then} \markbox{23565}{item} \markbox{23566}{(1)} \markbox{23567}{of} \markbox{23568}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close} \markbox{23569}{says} \markbox{23570}{that} 
$$d(C_1,C_4) \geq d(s(C_1),s(C_4)) - 14\epsilon \geq 3E-56\epsilon > 2E.$$

This \markbox{23571}{is} \markbox{23572}{impossible} \markbox{23573}{if} \markbox{m23574}{$z$} \markbox{23575}{is} \markbox{m23576}{$E$}-close \markbox{23577}{to} \markbox{23578}{both} \markbox{m23579}{$C_1,C_4$}.  \markbox{23580}{Hence} \markbox{23581}{there} \markbox{23582}{are} \markbox{23583}{at} \markbox{23584}{most} \markbox{23585}{three} \markbox{23586}{affected} \markbox{23587}{clusters} \markbox{23588}{and} \markbox{23589}{they} \markbox{23590}{are} \markbox{23591}{adjacent} \markbox{23592}{vertices} \markbox{23593}{in} \markbox{m23594}{$\calG$}.
\end{proof}



Let \markbox{m23595}{$C'$} \markbox{23596}{denote} \markbox{23597}{the} \markbox{23598}{cluster} \markbox{23599}{formed} \markbox{23600}{by} \markbox{m23601}{$z$} \markbox{23602}{and} \markbox{23603}{the} \markbox{23604}{affected} \markbox{23605}{clusters} \markbox{23606}{from} \markbox{m23607}{$(a,b;\calY)$}.  \markbox{23608}{Note} \markbox{23609}{that} \markbox{23610}{the} \markbox{23611}{membership} \markbox{23612}{of} \markbox{23613}{all} \markbox{23614}{other} \markbox{m23615}{$(a,b;\calY)$}-clusters \markbox{23616}{are} \markbox{23617}{unchanged} \markbox{23618}{by} \markbox{23619}{the} \markbox{23620}{addition} \markbox{23621}{of} \markbox{m23622}{$z$}.  \markbox{23623}{Let} \markbox{m23624}{$C_1$} \markbox{23625}{and} \markbox{m23626}{$C_2$} \markbox{23627}{be} \markbox{23628}{the} \markbox{23629}{clusters} \markbox{23630}{adjacent} \markbox{23631}{to} \markbox{23632}{the} \markbox{23633}{affected} \markbox{23634}{clusters} \markbox{23635}{in} \markbox{m23636}{$\calG$} \markbox{23637}{on} \markbox{23638}{the} \markbox{23639}{side} \markbox{23640}{of} \markbox{m23641}{$a$} \markbox{23642}{and} \markbox{m23643}{$b$}, \markbox{23644}{respectively.}  \markbox{23645}{As} \markbox{23646}{in} \markbox{23647}{the} \markbox{23648}{split} \markbox{23649}{cluster} \markbox{23650}{case} \markbox{23651}{above,} \markbox{23652}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster arrangement} \markbox{23653}{implies} \markbox{23654}{that} \markbox{m23655}{$C_1$} \markbox{23656}{separates} \markbox{23657}{all} \markbox{23658}{clusters} \markbox{23659}{on} \markbox{23660}{the} \markbox{m23661}{$a$}-side \markbox{23662}{of} \markbox{m23663}{$\calG$} \markbox{23664}{from} \markbox{m23665}{$C'$}, \markbox{23666}{and} \markbox{23667}{similarly} \markbox{23668}{for} \markbox{m23669}{$C_2$} \markbox{23670}{and} \markbox{23671}{clusters} \markbox{23672}{on} \markbox{23673}{the} \markbox{m23674}{$b$}-side.  \markbox{23675}{Hence} \markbox{23676}{the} \markbox{23677}{subgraph} \markbox{23678}{of} \markbox{m23679}{$\calG$} \markbox{23680}{connecting} \markbox{23681}{the} \markbox{23682}{cluster} \markbox{23683}{containing} \markbox{m23684}{$a$} \markbox{23685}{to} \markbox{m23686}{$C_1$} \markbox{23687}{is} \markbox{23688}{the} \markbox{23689}{subgraph} \markbox{23690}{of} \markbox{m23691}{$\calG'$} \markbox{23692}{connecting} \markbox{23693}{the} \markbox{23694}{(same)} \markbox{23695}{cluster} \markbox{23696}{containing} \markbox{m23697}{$a$} \markbox{23698}{to} \markbox{m23699}{$C_1$}, \markbox{23700}{and} \markbox{23701}{similarly} \markbox{23702}{for} \markbox{23703}{the} \markbox{m23704}{$b$}-side \markbox{23705}{of} \markbox{m23706}{$\calG$} \markbox{23707}{and} \markbox{m23708}{$\calG'$}.  \markbox{23709}{As} \markbox{23710}{such,} \markbox{23711}{all} \markbox{23712}{of} \markbox{23713}{the} \markbox{23714}{corresponding} \markbox{23715}{components} \markbox{23716}{of} \markbox{m23717}{$T_e$} \markbox{23718}{and} \markbox{m23719}{$T'_e$} \markbox{23720}{are} \markbox{23721}{exactly} \markbox{23722}{the} \markbox{23723}{same,} \markbox{23724}{and} \markbox{23725}{have} \markbox{23726}{positive} \markbox{23727}{integer} \markbox{23728}{length} \markbox{23729}{by} \markbox{23730}{construction,} \markbox{23731}{verifying} \markbox{23732}{properties} \eqref{item:integer length}, \eqref{item:stable pairs}, \markbox{23733}{and} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{23734}{of} \markbox{23735}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{23736}{for} \markbox{23737}{these} components.

The \markbox{23738}{forests} \markbox{m23739}{$T_e$} \markbox{23740}{and} \markbox{m23741}{$T'_e$} \markbox{23742}{have} \markbox{23743}{some} \markbox{23744}{remaining} \markbox{23745}{components} \markbox{23746}{which} \markbox{23747}{we} \markbox{23748}{need} \markbox{23749}{to} \markbox{23750}{decompose.}  \markbox{23751}{In} \markbox{m23752}{$T_e$}, \markbox{23753}{there} \markbox{23754}{are} \markbox{23755}{the} \markbox{23756}{at-most} \markbox{m23757}{$2$} \markbox{23758}{components} \markbox{23759}{of} \markbox{m23760}{$T_e$} \markbox{23761}{which} \markbox{23762}{connect} \markbox{23763}{the} \markbox{23764}{affected} \markbox{23765}{clusters.}  \markbox{23766}{By} \markbox{23767}{assumption,} \markbox{23768}{these} \markbox{23769}{segments} \markbox{23770}{are} \markbox{23771}{at} \markbox{23772}{most} \markbox{m23773}{$O(\epsilon)$} \markbox{23774}{long,} \markbox{23775}{so} \markbox{23776}{we} \markbox{23777}{can} \markbox{23778}{declare} \markbox{23779}{them} \markbox{23780}{to} \markbox{23781}{be} \markbox{23782}{unstable} components.

We \markbox{23783}{now} \markbox{23784}{explain} \markbox{23785}{how} \markbox{23786}{to} \markbox{23787}{handle} \markbox{23788}{the} \markbox{23789}{two} \markbox{23790}{remaining} \markbox{23791}{components.}  \markbox{23792}{Let} \markbox{m23793}{$A$} \markbox{23794}{be} \markbox{23795}{the} \markbox{23796}{affected} \markbox{23797}{cluster} \markbox{23798}{adjacent} \markbox{23799}{to} \markbox{m23800}{$C_1$} \markbox{23801}{in} \markbox{m23802}{$\calG$}.  \markbox{23803}{It} \markbox{23804}{is} \markbox{23805}{enough} \markbox{23806}{to} \markbox{23807}{show} \markbox{23808}{that} \markbox{23809}{the} \markbox{23810}{geodesic} \markbox{23811}{segments} \markbox{m23812}{$\lambda(C_1,A)$} \markbox{23813}{and} \markbox{m23814}{$\lambda(C_1,C')$} \markbox{23815}{are} \markbox{m23816}{$O(\epsilon)$}-Hausdorff \markbox{23817}{close,} \markbox{23818}{since} \markbox{23819}{then} \markbox{23820}{the} \markbox{23821}{lengths} \markbox{23822}{of} \markbox{m23823}{$\lambda_0(C_1,A)$} \markbox{23824}{and} \markbox{m23825}{$\lambda_0(C_1,C')$} \markbox{23826}{are} \markbox{23827}{the} \markbox{23828}{same} \markbox{23829}{up} \markbox{23830}{to} \markbox{23831}{error} \markbox{m23832}{$O(\epsilon)$}, \markbox{23833}{and} \markbox{23834}{we} \markbox{23835}{can} \markbox{23836}{declare} \markbox{23837}{a} \markbox{23838}{small} \markbox{23839}{end} \markbox{23840}{segment} \markbox{23841}{of} \markbox{23842}{each} \markbox{23843}{unstable,} \markbox{23844}{so} \markbox{23845}{that} \markbox{23846}{their} \markbox{23847}{(stable)} \markbox{23848}{complements} \markbox{23849}{have} \markbox{23850}{the} \markbox{23851}{same} \markbox{23852}{(positive} \markbox{23853}{integer)} \markbox{23854}{length} \markbox{23855}{and} \markbox{23856}{are} \markbox{m23857}{$O(\epsilon)$}-close.  \markbox{23858}{But} \markbox{23859}{this} \markbox{23860}{endpoint} \markbox{23861}{proximity} \markbox{23862}{statement} \markbox{23863}{is} \markbox{23864}{again} \markbox{23865}{a} \markbox{23866}{consequence} \markbox{23867}{of} \markbox{23868}{Lemma} \ref{lem:cluster close}, \markbox{23869}{since} \markbox{23870}{the} \markbox{23871}{endpoints} \markbox{23872}{of} \markbox{m23873}{$\lambda(C_1,A)$} \markbox{23874}{and} \markbox{m23875}{$\lambda(C_1,C')$} \markbox{23876}{are} \markbox{23877}{within} \markbox{m23878}{$7\epsilon$} \markbox{23879}{of} \markbox{23880}{the} \markbox{23881}{endpoint} \markbox{23882}{of} \markbox{m23883}{$s(C_1)$} \markbox{23884}{on} \markbox{m23885}{$\lambda(a,b)$}, \markbox{23886}{while} \markbox{m23887}{$s(C')$} \markbox{23888}{contains} \markbox{m23889}{$s(A)$} \markbox{23890}{and} \markbox{23891}{its} \markbox{23892}{endpoint} \markbox{23893}{is} \markbox{23894}{at} \markbox{23895}{most} \markbox{m23896}{$(E+\epsilon)$}-away.  \markbox{23897}{Finally,} \markbox{23898}{the} \markbox{23899}{bijection} \markbox{m23900}{$\beta:\pi_0(T-T_s) \to \pi_0(T'-T'_s)$} \markbox{23901}{required} \markbox{23902}{for} \eqref{item:adjacency} \markbox{23903}{is} \markbox{23904}{defined} \markbox{23905}{similar} \markbox{23906}{to} \markbox{23907}{the} \markbox{23908}{split} \markbox{23909}{cluster} \markbox{23910}{case} \markbox{23911}{(a),} \markbox{23912}{with} \markbox{23913}{the} \markbox{23914}{proof} \markbox{23915}{of} \markbox{23916}{condition} \eqref{item:endpoint condition} \markbox{23917}{being} \markbox{23918}{basically} \markbox{23919}{the} \markbox{23920}{same.}  \markbox{23921}{For} \markbox{23922}{condition} \eqref{item:cluster identify}, \markbox{23923}{observe} \markbox{23924}{again} \markbox{23925}{the} \markbox{m23926}{$\calY \cap (\calY \cup \{z\}) = \calY$}.  \markbox{23927}{Assuming} \markbox{23928}{that} \markbox{m23929}{$y \in \calY$} \markbox{23930}{is} \markbox{23931}{contained} \markbox{23932}{in} \markbox{23933}{an} \markbox{23934}{affected} \markbox{23935}{cluster} \markbox{23936}{in} \markbox{23937}{the} \markbox{m23938}{$(\calY; \{a,b\})$} \markbox{23939}{setup---since} \markbox{23940}{otherwise,} \markbox{23941}{it} \markbox{23942}{is} \markbox{23943}{contained} \markbox{23944}{in} \markbox{23945}{an} \markbox{23946}{identical} \markbox{23947}{cluster} \markbox{23948}{in} \markbox{23949}{the} \markbox{m23950}{$(\calY \cup \{z\};\{a,b\})$} \markbox{23951}{setup---then} \markbox{23952}{it} \markbox{23953}{corresponds} \markbox{23954}{to} \markbox{23955}{the} \markbox{23956}{single} \markbox{23957}{component} \markbox{23958}{which} \markbox{23959}{gets} \markbox{23960}{identified} \markbox{23961}{with} \markbox{23962}{the} \markbox{23963}{component} \markbox{23964}{of} \markbox{m23965}{$T'- T'_s$} \markbox{23966}{corresponding} \markbox{23967}{to} \markbox{23968}{the} \markbox{23969}{single} \markbox{23970}{cluster} \markbox{23971}{containing} \markbox{23972}{both} \markbox{m23973}{$y$} \markbox{23974}{and} \markbox{m23975}{$z$}.  \markbox{23976}{This} \markbox{23977}{completes} \markbox{23978}{the} \markbox{23979}{proof} \markbox{23980}{of} \markbox{23981}{(1)} \markbox{23982}{in} \markbox{23983}{the} \markbox{23984}{affected} \markbox{23985}{cluster} \markbox{23986}{case.}  \markbox{23987}{See} \markbox{23988}{Figure} \ref{fig:affected cluster} \markbox{23989}{for} \markbox{23990}{a} \markbox{23991}{heuristic} picture.

The \markbox{23992}{argument} \markbox{23993}{for} \markbox{23994}{(2)} \markbox{23995}{in} \markbox{23996}{the} \markbox{23997}{affected} \markbox{23998}{cluster} \markbox{23999}{case} \markbox{24000}{is} \markbox{24001}{essentially} \markbox{24002}{identical} \markbox{24003}{to} \markbox{24004}{the} \markbox{24005}{split} \markbox{24006}{cluster} \markbox{24007}{version:} \markbox{24008}{All} \markbox{24009}{but} \markbox{24010}{a} \markbox{24011}{few} \markbox{24012}{components} \markbox{24013}{of} \markbox{m24014}{$T_s \subset T_e$} \markbox{24015}{and} \markbox{m24016}{$T'_s \subset T'_e$} \markbox{24017}{are} \markbox{24018}{identical} \markbox{24019}{and} \markbox{24020}{thus} \markbox{24021}{have} \markbox{24022}{identical} \markbox{m24023}{$(r_1,r_2)$}-thickenings.  \markbox{24024}{And} \markbox{24025}{the} \markbox{24026}{remaining} \markbox{24027}{components} \markbox{24028}{of} \markbox{m24029}{$T_s, T'_s$} \markbox{24030}{are} \markbox{24031}{constructed} \markbox{24032}{by} \markbox{24033}{pairing} \markbox{24034}{the} \markbox{24035}{corresponding} \markbox{24036}{components} \markbox{24037}{of} \markbox{m24038}{$T_e, T'_e$} \markbox{24039}{adjacent} \markbox{24040}{to} \markbox{24041}{or} \markbox{24042}{connecting} \markbox{24043}{the} \markbox{24044}{affected} \markbox{24045}{clusters,} \markbox{24046}{and} \markbox{24047}{then} \markbox{24048}{either} \markbox{24049}{declaring} \markbox{24050}{them} \markbox{24051}{unstable} \markbox{24052}{or} \markbox{24053}{modifying} \markbox{24054}{them} \markbox{24055}{pairwise} \markbox{24056}{to} \markbox{24057}{achieve} \markbox{24058}{the} \markbox{24059}{length} \markbox{24060}{bound.}  \markbox{24061}{As} \markbox{24062}{above,} \markbox{24063}{this} \markbox{24064}{can} \markbox{24065}{be} \markbox{24066}{accomplished} \markbox{24067}{post-thickening;} \markbox{24068}{see} \markbox{24069}{Figure} \ref{fig:affected cluster}.  \markbox{24070}{This} \markbox{24071}{completes} \markbox{24072}{the} \markbox{24073}{proof} \markbox{24074}{of} \markbox{24075}{the} theorem.

\end{proof}

\subsection{Iterating stable decompositions}


Next \markbox{24076}{we} \markbox{24077}{move} \markbox{24078}{to} \markbox{24079}{proving} \markbox{24080}{our} \markbox{24081}{iteration} \markbox{24082}{statement} \markbox{24083}{(Proposition} \ref{prop:stable iteration}).  \markbox{24084}{The} \markbox{24085}{main} \markbox{24086}{work} \markbox{24087}{is} \markbox{24088}{the} \markbox{24089}{base} \markbox{24090}{case} \markbox{24091}{of} \markbox{24092}{combining} \markbox{24093}{two} \markbox{24094}{pairs} \markbox{24095}{of} \markbox{24096}{stable} \markbox{24097}{decompositions} \markbox{24098}{across} \markbox{24099}{a} \markbox{24100}{common} setup.
