For \markbox{24101}{this,} \markbox{24102}{suppose} \markbox{24103}{we} \markbox{24104}{have} \markbox{24105}{three} \markbox{24106}{setups} \markbox{m24107}{$(a_i,b_i;\calY_i)$} \markbox{24108}{for} \markbox{m24109}{$i=1,2,3$}, \markbox{24110}{satisfying} \markbox{24111}{that} \markbox{m24112}{$\calY_i \subset \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a_j,b_k))$} \markbox{24113}{for} \markbox{24114}{all} \markbox{m24115}{$i,j,k$}, \markbox{24116}{and} \markbox{24117}{that} \markbox{m24118}{$\calY_0 \subset \calY_i$} \markbox{24119}{for} \markbox{24120}{each} \markbox{m24121}{$i$}.  \markbox{24122}{Suppose} \markbox{24123}{that} \markbox{24124}{the} \markbox{24125}{stable} \markbox{24126}{intervals} \markbox{24127}{associated} \markbox{24128}{to} \markbox{m24129}{$(a_1,b_1;\calY_1)$} \markbox{24130}{and} \markbox{m24131}{$(a_2,b_2;\calY_2)$} \markbox{24132}{admits} \markbox{m24133}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m24134}{$L$}-compatible \markbox{24135}{decompositions,} \markbox{24136}{and} \markbox{24137}{the} \markbox{24138}{same} \markbox{24139}{for} \markbox{m24140}{$(a_2,b_2;\calY_2)$} \markbox{24141}{and} \markbox{m24142}{$(a_3,b_3;\calY_3)$}.  \markbox{24143}{Our} \markbox{24144}{goal} \markbox{24145}{is} \markbox{24146}{to} \markbox{24147}{induce} \markbox{24148}{new} \markbox{24149}{stable} \markbox{24150}{decompositions} \markbox{24151}{on} \markbox{m24152}{$T_1,T_2$} \markbox{24153}{and} \markbox{m24154}{$T_2,T_3$} \markbox{24155}{which} \markbox{24156}{encode} \markbox{24157}{the} \markbox{24158}{stable} \markbox{24159}{decompositions} \markbox{24160}{from} \markbox{m24161}{$T_2,T_3$} \markbox{24162}{and} \markbox{m24163}{$T_1,T_2$}, \markbox{24164}{respectively.}  \markbox{24165}{The} \markbox{24166}{following} \markbox{24167}{describes} \markbox{24168}{the} \markbox{24169}{properties} \markbox{24170}{we} \markbox{24171}{want} \markbox{24172}{for} \markbox{24173}{these} \markbox{24174}{induced} decompositions:

\begin{definition}[Refined \markbox{24175}{stable} decompositions]\label{defn:refined decomp}
Let \markbox{m24176}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{24177}{and} \markbox{m24178}{$(a',b';\calY')$} \markbox{24179}{denote} \markbox{24180}{two} \markbox{24181}{admissible} \markbox{m24182}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{24183}{and} \markbox{24184}{let} \markbox{m24185}{$\calY_0 = \calY \cap \calY'$}.  \markbox{24186}{Suppose} \markbox{24187}{we} \markbox{24188}{have} \markbox{24189}{two} \markbox{24190}{compatible} \markbox{m24191}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{24192}{decompositions} \markbox{m24193}{$T_s \subset T$} \markbox{24194}{and} \markbox{m24195}{$T'_s \subset T'$}.  \markbox{24196}{We} \markbox{24197}{say} \markbox{24198}{another} \markbox{24199}{pair} \markbox{24200}{of} \markbox{24201}{stable} \markbox{24202}{decompositions} \markbox{m24203}{$T_{s,0} \subset T$} \markbox{24204}{and} \markbox{m24205}{$T'_{s,0} \subset T'$} \markbox{24206}{\emph{refine}} \markbox{m24207}{$T_s \subset T$} \markbox{24208}{and} \markbox{m24209}{$T'_s \subset T'$} \markbox{24210}{if} \markbox{24211}{the} \markbox{24212}{following} hold:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} We \markbox{24213}{have} \markbox{m24214}{$T_{s,0} \subset T_s$} \markbox{24215}{and} \markbox{m24216}{$T'_{s,0} \subset T'_s$}, and
\item {} Let \markbox{m24217}{$\beta:\pi_0(T - T_s) \to \pi_0(T'-T'_s)$} \markbox{24218}{and} \markbox{m24219}{$\beta_0:\pi_0(T-T_{s,0}) \to \pi_0(T' - T'_{s,0})$} \markbox{24220}{denote} \markbox{24221}{the} \markbox{24222}{associated} \markbox{24223}{order-preserving} \markbox{24224}{bijections.}  \markbox{24225}{Suppose} \markbox{m24226}{$C_1 \in \pi_0(T - T_s)$}  \markbox{24227}{and} \markbox{24228}{let} \markbox{m24229}{$C_{1,0} \in \pi_0(T-T_{s,0})$} \markbox{24230}{denote} \markbox{24231}{the} \markbox{24232}{component} \markbox{24233}{containing} \markbox{m24234}{$C_1$} \markbox{24235}{(which} \markbox{24236}{exists} \markbox{24237}{because} \markbox{m24238}{$T_{s,0} \subset T_s$}).  \markbox{24239}{Then} \markbox{m24240}{$\beta(C_1) \subset \beta_0(C_{1,0})$}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{definition}

\begin{remark}\label{rem:purpose of refined}
Condition \markbox{24241}{(2)} \markbox{24242}{in} \markbox{24243}{particular} \markbox{24244}{is} \markbox{24245}{used} \markbox{24246}{to} \markbox{24247}{verify} \markbox{24248}{the} \markbox{24249}{properties} \markbox{24250}{in} \eqref{item:adjacency} \markbox{24251}{of} \markbox{24252}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{24253}{during} \markbox{24254}{our} \markbox{24255}{iteration} \markbox{24256}{procedure.}  \markbox{24257}{For} \markbox{24258}{item} \eqref{item:endpoint condition}, \markbox{24259}{since} \markbox{m24260}{$\beta$} \markbox{24261}{identifies} \markbox{24262}{the} \markbox{24263}{component} \markbox{24264}{of} \markbox{m24265}{$T-T_s$} \markbox{24266}{containing} \markbox{24267}{the} \markbox{24268}{cluster} \markbox{24269}{component} \markbox{24270}{associated} \markbox{24271}{to} \markbox{m24272}{$a$} \markbox{24273}{to} \markbox{24274}{the} \markbox{24275}{component} \markbox{24276}{of} \markbox{m24277}{$T' - T'_s$} \markbox{24278}{containing} \markbox{24279}{the} \markbox{24280}{cluster} \markbox{24281}{component} \markbox{24282}{associated} \markbox{24283}{to} \markbox{m24284}{$a'$}, \markbox{24285}{the} \markbox{24286}{refinement} \markbox{24287}{condition} \markbox{24288}{(2)} \markbox{24289}{forces} \markbox{24290}{the} \markbox{24291}{same} \markbox{24292}{to} \markbox{24293}{hold} \markbox{24294}{for} \markbox{m24295}{$\beta_0$}.  \markbox{24296}{A} \markbox{24297}{similar} \markbox{24298}{observation} \markbox{24299}{works} \markbox{24300}{to} \markbox{24301}{verify} \markbox{24302}{item} \eqref{item:cluster identify}.
\end{remark}

Following \markbox{24303}{our} \markbox{24304}{notation} \markbox{24305}{from} \markbox{24306}{before} \markbox{24307}{the} \markbox{24308}{above} \markbox{24309}{definition,} \markbox{24310}{let} \markbox{m24311}{$\phi_i:T_i \to \calZ$} \markbox{24312}{denote} \markbox{24313}{the} \markbox{24314}{maps} \markbox{24315}{into} \markbox{m24316}{$\calZ$}.  \markbox{24317}{Moreover,} \markbox{24318}{assume} \markbox{24319}{that} \markbox{24320}{we} have
\begin{itemize}
\item {} a \markbox{m24321}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{24322}{decomposition} \markbox{m24323}{$T^1_{s,2} \subset T_{e,2}$} \markbox{24324}{which} \markbox{24325}{is} \markbox{m24326}{$L$}-compatible \markbox{24327}{with} \markbox{m24328}{$T^2_{s,1} \subset T_{e,1} $} \markbox{24329}{for} \markbox{24330}{the} \markbox{24331}{setups} \markbox{m24332}{$(a_1,b_1;\calY_1)$} \markbox{24333}{and} \markbox{m24334}{$(a_2,b_2;\calY_2)$}, and
\item {} a \markbox{m24335}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{24336}{decomposition} \markbox{m24337}{$T^3_{s,2} \subset T_{e,2}$} \markbox{24338}{which} \markbox{24339}{is} \markbox{m24340}{$L$}-compatible \markbox{24341}{with} \markbox{m24342}{$T^2_{s,3} \subset T_{e,3}$} \markbox{24343}{for} \markbox{24344}{the} \markbox{24345}{setups} \markbox{m24346}{$(a_2,b_2;\calY_2)$} \markbox{24347}{and} \markbox{m24348}{$(a_3,b_3;\calY_3)$}.
\end{itemize}

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:stable iteration, pair}
There \markbox{24349}{exists} \markbox{m24350}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m24351}{$4L^2$}-compatible \markbox{24352}{decompositions} \markbox{m24353}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1} \subset T_{e,1}$} \markbox{24354}{and} \markbox{m24355}{$T^{2,1}_{s,3} \subset T_{e,3}$} \markbox{24356}{which} \markbox{24357}{refine} \markbox{m24358}{$T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24359}{and} \markbox{m24360}{$T^2_{s,3}$}. 
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
Note \markbox{24361}{that} \markbox{24362}{the} \markbox{24363}{stable} \markbox{24364}{decompositions} \markbox{m24365}{$T^1_{s,2}$} \markbox{24366}{and} \markbox{m24367}{$T^3_{s,2}$} \markbox{24368}{both} \markbox{24369}{live} \markbox{24370}{on} \markbox{m24371}{$T_2$}.  \markbox{24372}{Set} \markbox{m24373}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2} = T^1_{s,2} \cap T^3_{s,2}$}.  \markbox{24374}{Observe} \markbox{24375}{that} \markbox{m24376}{$T_{e,2} - T^{1,3}_{s,2} = (T_{e,2} - T^1_{s,2}) \cup (T_{e,2} - T^3_{s,2})$} \markbox{24377}{has} \markbox{24378}{at} \markbox{24379}{most} \markbox{m24380}{$2L$}-many \markbox{24381}{components} \markbox{24382}{each} \markbox{24383}{of} \markbox{24384}{diameter} \markbox{24385}{at} \markbox{24386}{most} \markbox{m24387}{$4L^2$}; \markbox{24388}{note} \markbox{24389}{that} \markbox{24390}{the} \markbox{24391}{larger} \markbox{24392}{diameter} \markbox{24393}{bound} \markbox{24394}{accounts} \markbox{24395}{for} \markbox{24396}{unstable} \markbox{24397}{components} \markbox{24398}{to} \markbox{24399}{combine,} \markbox{24400}{but} \markbox{24401}{there} \markbox{24402}{are} \markbox{24403}{at} \markbox{24404}{most} \markbox{m24405}{$2L$}-many \markbox{24406}{of} \markbox{24407}{them.}  \markbox{24408}{Moreover,} \markbox{24409}{by} \markbox{24410}{item} \eqref{item:simplicial} \markbox{24411}{of} \markbox{24412}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}, \markbox{24413}{the} \markbox{24414}{endpoints} \markbox{24415}{of} \markbox{24416}{each} \markbox{24417}{component} \markbox{24418}{of} \markbox{m24419}{$T^1_{s,2}$} \markbox{24420}{and} \markbox{m24421}{$T^3_{s,2}$} \markbox{24422}{are} \markbox{24423}{at} \markbox{24424}{vertices} \markbox{24425}{of} \markbox{24426}{the} \markbox{24427}{components} \markbox{24428}{of} \markbox{m24429}{$T_{e,2}$} \markbox{24430}{which} \markbox{24431}{contain} \markbox{24432}{them,} \markbox{24433}{and} \markbox{24434}{hence} \markbox{24435}{this} \markbox{24436}{property} \markbox{24437}{holds} \markbox{24438}{for} \markbox{24439}{each} \markbox{24440}{component} \markbox{24441}{of} \markbox{m24442}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2}$}

We \markbox{24443}{first} \markbox{24444}{produce} \markbox{24445}{refined} \markbox{24446}{decompositions} \markbox{24447}{of} \markbox{m24448}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1} \subset T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24449}{and} \markbox{m24450}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2} \subset T^1_{s,2}$}, \markbox{24451}{and} \markbox{24452}{the} \markbox{24453}{same} \markbox{24454}{argument} \markbox{24455}{produces} \markbox{24456}{the} \markbox{24457}{refined} \markbox{24458}{decompositions} \markbox{m24459}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2}  \subset T^3_{s,2}$} \markbox{24460}{and} \markbox{m24461}{$T^{2,1}_{s,3} \subset T^2_{s,3}$}.  \markbox{24462}{We} \markbox{24463}{will} \markbox{24464}{then} \markbox{24465}{see} \markbox{24466}{the} \markbox{24467}{properties} \markbox{24468}{of} \markbox{24469}{Definition} \ref{defn:refined decomp} \markbox{24470}{allow} \markbox{24471}{us} \markbox{24472}{to} \markbox{24473}{combine} \markbox{24474}{these,} \markbox{24475}{using} \markbox{m24476}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2}$} \markbox{24477}{as} \markbox{24478}{a} \markbox{24479}{bridge} \markbox{24480}{to} \markbox{24481}{connect} them.

We \markbox{24482}{can} \markbox{24483}{induce} \markbox{24484}{a} \markbox{24485}{decomposition} \markbox{m24486}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24487}{on} \markbox{m24488}{$T_1$} \markbox{24489}{by} \markbox{24490}{taking} \markbox{24491}{the} \markbox{24492}{collection} \markbox{24493}{of} \markbox{24494}{all} \markbox{m24495}{$i^{-1}_{E,E'}(E' \cap T^{1,3}_{s,2})$} \markbox{24496}{over} \markbox{24497}{all} \markbox{24498}{stable} \markbox{24499}{pairs} \markbox{m24500}{$(E,E')$} \markbox{24501}{of} \markbox{m24502}{$T_1,T_2$} \markbox{24503}{as} \markbox{24504}{identified} \markbox{24505}{by} \markbox{24506}{the} \markbox{24507}{bijection} \markbox{m24508}{$\alpha_{1,2}:\pi_0(T_{s,1}) \to \pi_0(T_{s,2})$}.  \markbox{24509}{Observe} \markbox{24510}{that} \markbox{24511}{any} \markbox{24512}{component} \markbox{m24513}{$V \subset T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24514}{is} \markbox{24515}{contained} \markbox{24516}{in} \markbox{24517}{some} \markbox{24518}{component} \markbox{m24519}{$V \subset E \subset T_{s,1} \subset T_{e,1}$}, \markbox{24520}{and} \markbox{24521}{the} \markbox{24522}{map} \markbox{m24523}{$i_{E,E'}|_V:V \to i_{E,E'}(V)$} \markbox{24524}{is} \markbox{24525}{an} \markbox{24526}{isometry,} \markbox{24527}{where} \markbox{m24528}{$E' = \alpha_{1,2}(E)$}, \markbox{24529}{and} \markbox{24530}{vice} \markbox{24531}{versa.}  \markbox{24532}{Thus} \markbox{24533}{the} \markbox{24534}{components} \markbox{24535}{of} \markbox{m24536}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24537}{are} \markbox{24538}{in} \markbox{24539}{bijective} \markbox{24540}{correspondence} \markbox{24541}{with} \markbox{24542}{the} \markbox{24543}{components} \markbox{24544}{of} \markbox{m24545}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2}$}, \markbox{24546}{with} \markbox{24547}{identified} \markbox{24548}{components} \markbox{24549}{being} \markbox{24550}{isometric.}  \markbox{24551}{Moreover,}  \markbox{24552}{the} \markbox{24553}{natural} \markbox{24554}{order-preserving} \markbox{24555}{bijection} \markbox{m24556}{$\alpha^3_{1,2}:\pi_0(T^{2,3}_{s,1}) \to \pi_0(T^{1,3}_{s,2})$} \markbox{24557}{(as} \markbox{24558}{in} \markbox{24559}{Definition} \ref{defn:order preserving}) \markbox{24560}{coincides} \markbox{24561}{with} \markbox{24562}{the} \markbox{24563}{bijective} \markbox{24564}{correspondence} \markbox{24565}{induced} \markbox{24566}{from} \markbox{m24567}{$\alpha_{1,2}$} \markbox{24568}{and} \markbox{24569}{the} \markbox{24570}{various} \markbox{24571}{order-preserving} \markbox{24572}{isometries} \markbox{m24573}{$i_{E,E'}$}.  \markbox{24574}{We} \markbox{24575}{also} \markbox{24576}{note} \markbox{24577}{that} \markbox{24578}{the} \markbox{24579}{various} \markbox{24580}{restrictions} \markbox{m24581}{$i_{E,E'}|V$} \markbox{24582}{are} \markbox{24583}{order-preserving} \markbox{24584}{since} \markbox{m24585}{$i_{E,E'}$} \markbox{24586}{is.}  \markbox{24587}{Next} \markbox{24588}{observe} \markbox{24589}{that} \markbox{24590}{the} \markbox{24591}{images} \markbox{m24592}{$\phi_1(V)$} \markbox{24593}{and} \markbox{m24594}{$\phi_2(i_{E,E'}(V))$} \markbox{24595}{are} \markbox{24596}{either} \markbox{24597}{exactly} \markbox{24598}{the} \markbox{24599}{same} \markbox{24600}{or} \markbox{24601}{are} \markbox{m24602}{$L$}-Hausdorff \markbox{24603}{close} \markbox{24604}{in} \markbox{m24605}{$\calZ$} \markbox{24606}{as} \markbox{24607}{items} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{24608}{and} \eqref{item:close pairs} \markbox{24609}{of} \markbox{24610}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}.  \markbox{24611}{Thus} \markbox{24612}{the} \markbox{24613}{decompositions} \markbox{m24614}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1} \subset T_1$} \markbox{24615}{and} \markbox{m24616}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2} \subset T_2$} \markbox{24617}{satisfy} \markbox{24618}{all} \markbox{24619}{the} \markbox{24620}{properties} \markbox{24621}{of} \markbox{24622}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{24623}{except} \markbox{24624}{possibly} \eqref{item:adjacency}.  \markbox{24625}{We} \markbox{24626}{also} \markbox{24627}{want} \markbox{24628}{to} \markbox{24629}{show} \markbox{24630}{that} \markbox{24631}{they} \markbox{24632}{give} \markbox{24633}{a} \markbox{24634}{refinement} \markbox{24635}{as} \markbox{24636}{in} \markbox{24637}{Definition} \ref{defn:refined decomp}.

To \markbox{24638}{prove} \eqref{item:adjacency}, \markbox{24639}{it} \markbox{24640}{will} \markbox{24641}{suffice} \markbox{24642}{to} \markbox{24643}{show} \markbox{24644}{the} \markbox{24645}{refinement} \markbox{24646}{property} \markbox{24647}{(Definition} \ref{defn:refined decomp}), \markbox{24648}{as} \markbox{24649}{explained} \markbox{24650}{in} \markbox{24651}{Remark} \ref{rem:purpose of refined}.  \markbox{24652}{Property} \markbox{24653}{(1),} \markbox{24654}{namely} \markbox{24655}{that} \markbox{m24656}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1} \subset T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24657}{and} \markbox{m24658}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2} \subset T^1_{s,2}$}, \markbox{24659}{of} \markbox{24660}{Definition} \ref{defn:refined decomp} \markbox{24661}{holds} \markbox{24662}{by} \markbox{24663}{construction.}  \markbox{24664}{For} \markbox{24665}{property} \markbox{24666}{(2),} \markbox{24667}{we} \markbox{24668}{argument} \markbox{24669}{one} \markbox{24670}{component} \markbox{24671}{at} \markbox{24672}{a} \markbox{24673}{time.}  \markbox{24674}{In} \markbox{24675}{particular,} \markbox{24676}{let} \markbox{m24677}{$\beta^3_{1,2}:\pi_0(T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}) \to \pi_0(T_2 - T^{1,3}_{s,2})$} \markbox{24678}{be} \markbox{24679}{the} \markbox{24680}{natural} \markbox{24681}{order-preserving} \markbox{24682}{bijections} \markbox{24683}{(which} \markbox{24684}{exists} \markbox{24685}{via} \markbox{24686}{Remark} \ref{rem:order preserving} \markbox{24687}{because} \markbox{m24688}{$\alpha^3_{1,2}$} does).

First, \markbox{24689}{since} \markbox{24690}{the} \markbox{24691}{(unstable)} \markbox{24692}{components} \markbox{24693}{of} \markbox{m24694}{$T_1 - T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24695}{only} \markbox{24696}{get} \markbox{24697}{expanded} \markbox{24698}{when} \markbox{24699}{passing} \markbox{24700}{to} \markbox{m24701}{$T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$}, \markbox{24702}{it} \markbox{24703}{follows} \markbox{24704}{that} \markbox{24705}{the} \markbox{24706}{first} \markbox{24707}{component} \markbox{m24708}{$C_0 \subset T_1 - T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24709}{one} \markbox{24710}{encounters} \markbox{24711}{when} \markbox{24712}{moving} \markbox{24713}{from} \markbox{m24714}{$a_1$} \markbox{24715}{to} \markbox{m24716}{$b_1$} \markbox{24717}{along} \markbox{24718}{the} \markbox{24719}{geodesic} \markbox{m24720}{$[a_1,b_1]_{T_1}$} \markbox{24721}{is} \markbox{24722}{contained} \markbox{24723}{in} \markbox{24724}{the} \markbox{24725}{first} \markbox{24726}{such} \markbox{24727}{component} \markbox{24728}{of} \markbox{m24729}{$C_{0,3} \subset T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$}, \markbox{24730}{and} \markbox{24731}{similarly} \markbox{24732}{for} \markbox{24733}{the} \markbox{24734}{setup} \markbox{24735}{on} \markbox{m24736}{$T_2$}.  \markbox{24737}{Hence} \markbox{24738}{these} \markbox{24739}{expanded} \markbox{24740}{clusters} \markbox{24741}{are} \markbox{24742}{identified} \markbox{24743}{by} \markbox{m24744}{$\beta^3_{1,2}$}, \markbox{24745}{which} \markbox{24746}{we} \markbox{24747}{note} \markbox{24748}{also} \markbox{24749}{confirms} \markbox{24750}{item} \eqref{item:endpoint condition} \markbox{24751}{of} \markbox{24752}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp}.

We \markbox{24753}{now} \markbox{24754}{proceed} \markbox{24755}{inductively} \markbox{24756}{along} \markbox{m24757}{$T_1$} \markbox{24758}{and} \markbox{m24759}{$T_2$}.  \markbox{24760}{Let} \markbox{m24761}{$C_1, C'_1$} \markbox{24762}{denote} \markbox{24763}{the} \markbox{24764}{second} \markbox{24765}{pairs} \markbox{24766}{of} \markbox{24767}{components} \markbox{24768}{of} \markbox{m24769}{$T_1 - T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24770}{and} \markbox{m24771}{$T_2 - T^1_{s,2}$} \markbox{24772}{encountered} \markbox{24773}{after} \markbox{m24774}{$C_0, C'_0$}.  \markbox{24775}{Let} \markbox{m24776}{$E, E'$} \markbox{24777}{denote} \markbox{24778}{the} \markbox{24779}{respective} \markbox{24780}{components} \markbox{24781}{of} \markbox{m24782}{$T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24783}{and} \markbox{m24784}{$T^1_{s,2}$} \markbox{24785}{connecting} \markbox{m24786}{$C_0,C'_0$} \markbox{24787}{to} \markbox{m24788}{$C_1,C'_1$}.  \markbox{24789}{The} \markbox{24790}{components} \markbox{24791}{of} \markbox{m24792}{$(T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}) \cap E$} \markbox{24793}{and} \markbox{m24794}{$(T_2 - T^{1,3}_{s,2}) \cap E'$} \markbox{24795}{are} \markbox{24796}{identified} \markbox{24797}{by} \markbox{24798}{the} \markbox{24799}{order-preserving} \markbox{24800}{isometry} \markbox{m24801}{$i_{E,E'}$} \markbox{24802}{in} \markbox{24803}{an} \markbox{24804}{order-preserving} \markbox{24805}{way.}  \markbox{24806}{In} \markbox{24807}{particular,} \markbox{24808}{the} \markbox{24809}{two} \markbox{24810}{sets} \markbox{24811}{of} \markbox{24812}{components} \markbox{24813}{are} \markbox{24814}{in} \markbox{24815}{bijective} \markbox{24816}{correspondence.}  \markbox{24817}{As} \markbox{24818}{a} \markbox{24819}{consequence,} \markbox{24820}{if} \markbox{m24821}{$C^3_1 \subset T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24822}{is}  \markbox{24823}{the} \markbox{24824}{component} \markbox{24825}{containing} \markbox{m24826}{$C_1$}, \markbox{24827}{then} \markbox{m24828}{$C'_1 \subset \beta^{3}_{1,2}(C^3_1)$}, \markbox{24829}{as} \markbox{24830}{required.}  \markbox{24831}{One} \markbox{24832}{can} \markbox{24833}{repeat} \markbox{24834}{this} \markbox{24835}{procedure} \markbox{24836}{on} \markbox{24837}{subsequent} \markbox{24838}{components} \markbox{24839}{of} \markbox{m24840}{$T_1 - T^2_{s,1}$} \markbox{24841}{and} \markbox{24842}{their} \markbox{24843}{paired} \markbox{24844}{components} \markbox{24845}{of} \markbox{m24846}{$T_2 - T^1_{s,2}$} \markbox{24847}{to} \markbox{24848}{see} \markbox{24849}{that} \markbox{m24850}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24851}{and} \markbox{m24852}{$T^{1,3}_{s,2}$} \markbox{24853}{refine} \markbox{m24854}{$T^{2}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24855}{and} \markbox{m24856}{$T^1_{s,2}$}, respectively.

\medskip

\markbox{24857}{\textbf{\underline{Combining the decompositions}}}: \markbox{24858}{We} \markbox{24859}{now} \markbox{24860}{want} \markbox{24861}{to} \markbox{24862}{see} \markbox{24863}{that} \markbox{m24864}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24865}{and} \markbox{m24866}{$T^{2,1}_{s,3}$} \markbox{24867}{are} \markbox{m24868}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m24869}{$4L^2$}-compatible \markbox{24870}{decompositions} \markbox{24871}{for} \markbox{m24872}{$(a_1,b_1;\calY_1)$} \markbox{24873}{and} \markbox{m24874}{$(a_3,b_3;\calY_3)$}.  \markbox{24875}{For} \markbox{24876}{this,} \markbox{24877}{define} \markbox{m24878}{$\alpha_{1,3}:\pi_0(T^{2,3}_{s,1}) \to \pi_0(T^{2,1}_{s,3})$} \markbox{24879}{to} \markbox{24880}{be} \markbox{m24881}{$\alpha_{1,3} = \alpha^{1}_{2,3} \circ \alpha^3_{1,2}$}, \markbox{24882}{and} \markbox{24883}{similarly} \markbox{24884}{set} \markbox{m24885}{$\beta_{1,3} = \beta^1_{2,3} \circ \beta^3_{1,2}$}.  \markbox{24886}{These} \markbox{24887}{compositions} \markbox{24888}{are} \markbox{24889}{order-preserving} \markbox{24890}{bijections} \markbox{24891}{because} \markbox{24892}{their} \markbox{24893}{constituent} \markbox{24894}{maps} \markbox{24895}{are,} \markbox{24896}{and} \markbox{24897}{moreover} \markbox{24898}{we} \markbox{24899}{can} \markbox{24900}{similarly} \markbox{24901}{induce} \markbox{24902}{order-preserving} \markbox{24903}{isometries} \markbox{24904}{on} \markbox{24905}{the} \markbox{24906}{components} \markbox{24907}{of} \markbox{m24908}{$T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24909}{and} \markbox{m24910}{$T^{2,1}_{s,3}$} \markbox{24911}{identified} \markbox{24912}{by} \markbox{m24913}{$\alpha_{1,3}$}, \markbox{24914}{which} \markbox{24915}{satisfy} \markbox{24916}{the} \markbox{24917}{proximity} \markbox{24918}{conditions} \markbox{24919}{of} \eqref{item:identical pairs} \markbox{24920}{and} \eqref{item:close pairs} \markbox{24921}{of} \markbox{24922}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable decomp} \markbox{24923}{with} \markbox{24924}{a} \markbox{24925}{constant} \markbox{24926}{of} \markbox{m24927}{$2L$}.  \markbox{24928}{In} \markbox{24929}{particular,} \markbox{24930}{it} \markbox{24931}{remains} \markbox{24932}{to} \markbox{24933}{show} \markbox{24934}{the} \markbox{24935}{properties} \markbox{24936}{in} \eqref{item:adjacency}.

For \markbox{24937}{this,} \markbox{24938}{we} \markbox{24939}{use} \markbox{24940}{the} \markbox{24941}{refinement} \markbox{24942}{property} \markbox{24943}{(2)} \markbox{24944}{of} \markbox{24945}{Definition} \ref{defn:refined decomp}.  \markbox{24946}{This} \markbox{24947}{is} \markbox{24948}{basically} \markbox{24949}{automatic.}  \markbox{24950}{For} \markbox{24951}{(1),} \markbox{24952}{the} \markbox{24953}{refinement} \markbox{24954}{property} \markbox{24955}{implies} \markbox{24956}{that} \markbox{m24957}{$\beta^3_{1,2}$} \markbox{24958}{identifies} \markbox{24959}{the} \markbox{24960}{component} \markbox{24961}{of} \markbox{m24962}{$T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{24963}{associated} \markbox{24964}{to} \markbox{m24965}{$a_1$} \markbox{24966}{to} \markbox{24967}{the} \markbox{24968}{component} \markbox{24969}{of} \markbox{m24970}{$T_2 - T^{1,3}_{s,2}$} \markbox{24971}{associated} \markbox{24972}{to} \markbox{m24973}{$a_2$}, \markbox{24974}{and} \markbox{24975}{similarly} \markbox{24976}{for} \markbox{m24977}{$\beta^1_{2,3}$}.  \markbox{24978}{Hence} \markbox{m24979}{$\beta_{1,3}$} \markbox{24980}{identifies} \markbox{24981}{the} \markbox{24982}{components} \markbox{24983}{associated} \markbox{24984}{to} \markbox{m24985}{$a_1, a_3$} \markbox{24986}{and} \markbox{m24987}{$b_1,b_3$}.  \markbox{24988}{Similarly,} \markbox{24989}{if} \markbox{m24990}{$y \in \calY_0 \subset \calY_1 \cap \calY_2 \cap \calY_3$}, \markbox{24991}{then} \markbox{24992}{the} \markbox{24993}{refinement} \markbox{24994}{property} \markbox{24995}{implies} \markbox{24996}{that} \markbox{m24997}{$\beta^3_{1,2}$} \markbox{24998}{identifies} \markbox{24999}{the} \markbox{25000}{component} \markbox{25001}{of} \markbox{m25002}{$T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{25003}{associated} \markbox{25004}{to} \markbox{m25005}{$y$} \markbox{25006}{to} \markbox{25007}{the} \markbox{25008}{component} \markbox{25009}{of} \markbox{m25010}{$T_2 - T^{1,3}_{s,2}$} \markbox{25011}{associated} \markbox{25012}{to} \markbox{m25013}{$y$}, \markbox{25014}{and} \markbox{25015}{similarly} \markbox{25016}{for} \markbox{m25017}{$\beta^1_{2,3}$}.  \markbox{25018}{Hence} \markbox{m25019}{$\beta_{1,3}$} \markbox{25020}{associates} \markbox{25021}{components} \markbox{25022}{associated} \markbox{25023}{to} \markbox{m25024}{$y$} \markbox{25025}{in} \markbox{25026}{both} \markbox{25027}{of} \markbox{m25028}{$T_1 - T^{2,3}_{s,1}$} \markbox{25029}{and} \markbox{m25030}{$T_3 - T^{2,1}_{s,3}$}.  \markbox{25031}{This} \markbox{25032}{completes} \markbox{25033}{the} \markbox{25034}{proof} \markbox{25035}{of} \markbox{25036}{the} proposition.



\end{proof}

The \markbox{25037}{following} \markbox{25038}{proposition} \markbox{25039}{is} \markbox{25040}{now} \markbox{25041}{a} \markbox{25042}{simple} \markbox{25043}{iterative} \markbox{25044}{application} \markbox{25045}{of} \markbox{25046}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable iteration, pair}:

\begin{proposition}\label{prop:stable iteration}
For \markbox{25047}{every} \markbox{m25048}{$n\geq 2$}, \markbox{25049}{there} \markbox{25050}{exists} \markbox{m25051}{$L_n = L_n(L,n)>0$} \markbox{25052}{so} \markbox{25053}{that} \markbox{25054}{the} \markbox{25055}{following} \markbox{25056}{holds.}  \markbox{25057}{Suppose} \markbox{m25058}{$(a_1,b_1;\calY_1), \dots, (a_n,b_n;\calY_n)$} \markbox{25059}{is} \markbox{25060}{a} \markbox{25061}{sequence} \markbox{25062}{of} \markbox{25063}{pairwise} \markbox{25064}{admissible} \markbox{m25065}{$\epsilon$}-setups \markbox{25066}{and} \markbox{25067}{suppose} \markbox{25068}{that} \markbox{m25069}{$\calY_0 \subset \bigcap_i \calY_i$}.  \markbox{25070}{If} \markbox{25071}{each} \markbox{25072}{pair} \markbox{25073}{of} \markbox{25074}{consecutive} \markbox{25075}{setups} \markbox{25076}{admits} \markbox{m25077}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m25078}{$L$}-compatible \markbox{25079}{stable} \markbox{25080}{decompositions,} \markbox{25081}{then} \markbox{m25082}{$(a_1,b_1;\calY_1)$} \markbox{25083}{and} \markbox{m25084}{$(a_n,b_n;\calY_n)$} \markbox{25085}{admit} \markbox{m25086}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m25087}{$L_n$}-compatible \markbox{25088}{stable} \markbox{25089}{decompositions.} 
\end{proposition}


\subsubsection{Completing the proof} \markbox{25090}{To} \markbox{25091}{prove} \markbox{25092}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals}, \markbox{25093}{we} \markbox{25094}{have} \markbox{25095}{two} \markbox{25096}{remaining} tasks:
\begin{enumerate}
\item {} We \markbox{25097}{need} \markbox{25098}{to} \markbox{25099}{explain} \markbox{25100}{how} \markbox{25101}{to} \markbox{25102}{build} \markbox{25103}{a} \markbox{25104}{stable} \markbox{25105}{decomposition} \markbox{25106}{when} \markbox{25107}{perturbing} \markbox{25108}{an} \markbox{25109}{endpoint} \markbox{25110}{but} \markbox{25111}{keeping} \markbox{25112}{the} \markbox{25113}{rest} \markbox{25114}{of} \markbox{25115}{the} \markbox{25116}{setup} \markbox{25117}{the} \markbox{25118}{same,} and
\item {} Show \markbox{25119}{how} \markbox{25120}{to} \markbox{25121}{stick} \markbox{25122}{this} \markbox{25123}{into} \markbox{25124}{an} \markbox{25125}{iterative} setup.
\end{enumerate}

\markbox{25126}{\textbf{\underline{Perturbing an endpoint}:}} \markbox{25127}{This} \markbox{25128}{is} \markbox{25129}{an} \markbox{25130}{iterated} \markbox{25131}{application} \markbox{25132}{of}  \markbox{25133}{Proposition} \ref{prop:add cluster}.

Consider \markbox{25134}{the} \markbox{25135}{following} \markbox{25136}{restricted} \markbox{25137}{setup,} \markbox{25138}{which} \markbox{25139}{we} \markbox{25140}{highlight} \markbox{25141}{to} \markbox{25142}{focus} \markbox{25143}{on} \markbox{25144}{what} \markbox{25145}{happens} \markbox{25146}{when} \markbox{25147}{we} \markbox{25148}{perturb} \markbox{25149}{an} \markbox{25150}{endpoint.}  \markbox{25151}{Let} \markbox{m25152}{$a,b,a' \in \calZ$} \markbox{25153}{and} \markbox{m25154}{$\calY \subset \calZ$} \markbox{25155}{be} \markbox{25156}{finite} \markbox{25157}{with} \markbox{m25158}{$\calY \subset \calN_{\epsilon/2}(\lambda(a,b)) \cap \calN_{\epsilon/2}(a',b)$}.  \markbox{25159}{Consider} \markbox{25160}{the} \markbox{25161}{following} \markbox{25162}{collection} \markbox{25163}{of} \markbox{25164}{setups,} \markbox{25165}{each} \markbox{25166}{of} \markbox{25167}{which} \markbox{25168}{differs} \markbox{25169}{by} \markbox{25170}{adding} \markbox{25171}{or} \markbox{25172}{deleting} \markbox{25173}{one} \markbox{25174}{cluster} \markbox{25175}{point,} \markbox{25176}{or} \markbox{25177}{by} \markbox{25178}{switching} \markbox{25179}{the} \markbox{25180}{role} \markbox{25181}{that} \markbox{m25182}{$a,a'$} \markbox{25183}{or} \markbox{m25184}{$b,b'$} \markbox{25185}{play} \markbox{25186}{between} \markbox{25187}{cluster} \markbox{25188}{or} endpoint:
\vspace{-.09in}
\begin{multicols}{3}
\begin{enumerate}
\item $(a,b;\calY)$,
\item $(a,b;\calY \cup \{a\})$,
\item $(a,b;\calY \cup \{a, a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY \cup \{a,a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY \cup \{a'\})$,
\item $(a',b;\calY)$.
\end{enumerate}
\end{multicols}

First \markbox{25189}{observe} \markbox{25190}{that} \markbox{m25191}{$\calY$} \markbox{25192}{is} \markbox{25193}{contained} \markbox{25194}{in} \markbox{25195}{each} \markbox{25196}{of} \markbox{25197}{the} \markbox{25198}{above} \markbox{25199}{sets} \markbox{25200}{of} \markbox{25201}{cluster} \markbox{25202}{points,} \markbox{25203}{so} \markbox{25204}{we} \markbox{25205}{want} \markbox{25206}{to} \markbox{25207}{see} \markbox{25208}{how} \markbox{25209}{to} \markbox{25210}{build} \markbox{m25211}{$\calY$}-stable \markbox{25212}{decompositions} \markbox{25213}{for} \markbox{25214}{each,} \markbox{25215}{which} \markbox{25216}{implies} \markbox{25217}{the} \markbox{25218}{existence} \markbox{25219}{of} \markbox{m25220}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{25221}{decompositions} \markbox{25222}{for} \markbox{25223}{any} \markbox{m25224}{$\calY_0 \subset \calY$}.  \markbox{25225}{Next,} \markbox{25226}{observe} \markbox{25227}{that} \markbox{25228}{in} \markbox{25229}{the} \markbox{25230}{construction} \markbox{25231}{of} \markbox{25232}{the} \markbox{25233}{stable} \markbox{25234}{interval} \markbox{m25235}{$T(a,b;\calY)$}, \markbox{25236}{the} \markbox{25237}{roles} \markbox{25238}{of} \markbox{25239}{points} \markbox{25240}{of} \markbox{25241}{the} \markbox{25242}{endpoints} \markbox{m25243}{$a,b$} \markbox{25244}{and} \markbox{25245}{the} \markbox{25246}{cluster} \markbox{25247}{points} \markbox{m25248}{$\calY$} \markbox{25249}{are} \markbox{25250}{equivalent} \markbox{25251}{in} \markbox{25252}{cluster} \markbox{25253}{formation} \markbox{25254}{process.}  \markbox{25255}{The} \markbox{25256}{only} \markbox{25257}{special} \markbox{25258}{role} \markbox{25259}{that} \markbox{25260}{endpoints} \markbox{25261}{play} \markbox{25262}{in} \markbox{25263}{the} \markbox{25264}{Definition} \ref{defn:stable interval} \markbox{25265}{of} \markbox{m25266}{$T(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{25267}{is} \markbox{25268}{in} \markbox{25269}{the} \markbox{25270}{segments} \markbox{25271}{defined} \markbox{25272}{\emph{within}} \markbox{25273}{clusters,} \markbox{25274}{namely} \markbox{25275}{the} \markbox{m25276}{$\mu(C)$} \markbox{25277}{components.}  \markbox{25278}{In} \markbox{25279}{particular,} \markbox{25280}{the} \markbox{25281}{edge} \markbox{25282}{components} \markbox{25283}{(i.e.,} \markbox{25284}{the} \markbox{25285}{components} \markbox{25286}{of} \markbox{m25287}{$T_e$}) \markbox{25288}{treat} \markbox{25289}{endpoints} \markbox{25290}{and} \markbox{25291}{cluster} \markbox{25292}{points} \markbox{25293}{equivalently.}  \markbox{25294}{As} \markbox{25295}{the} \markbox{25296}{desired} \markbox{25297}{stable} \markbox{25298}{decompositions} \markbox{25299}{from} \markbox{25300}{Theorem} \ref{thm:stable intervals} \markbox{25301}{are} \markbox{25302}{subsets} \markbox{25303}{of} \markbox{25304}{the} \markbox{25305}{edge} \markbox{25306}{components,} \markbox{25307}{we} \markbox{25308}{are} \markbox{25309}{free} \markbox{25310}{to} \markbox{25311}{treat} \markbox{25312}{the} \markbox{25313}{points} \markbox{m25314}{$a,a',b,b'$} \markbox{25315}{as} \markbox{25316}{cluster} \markbox{25317}{points} \markbox{25318}{in} \markbox{25319}{applying} \markbox{25320}{Proposition} \ref{prop:add cluster} \markbox{25321}{to} \markbox{25322}{obtain} \markbox{25323}{stable} \markbox{25324}{decompositions} \markbox{25325}{for} \markbox{25326}{each} \markbox{25327}{of} \markbox{25328}{the} \markbox{25329}{steps} \markbox{m25330}{$(1) \to (2) \to (3)$} \markbox{25331}{and} \markbox{m25332}{$(4) \to (5) \to (6)$}.  \markbox{25333}{The} \markbox{25334}{only} \markbox{25335}{exception} \markbox{25336}{is} \markbox{25337}{the} \markbox{25338}{step} \markbox{m25339}{$(3) \to (4)$}, \markbox{25340}{where} \markbox{25341}{we} \markbox{25342}{are} \markbox{25343}{switching} \markbox{25344}{the} \markbox{25345}{roles} \markbox{25346}{of} \markbox{m25347}{$a$} \markbox{25348}{and} \markbox{m25349}{$a'$}.  \markbox{25350}{Here} \markbox{25351}{Proposition} \ref{prop:add cluster} \markbox{25352}{does} \markbox{25353}{not} \markbox{25354}{directly} \markbox{25355}{apply,} \markbox{25356}{but,} \markbox{25357}{by} \markbox{25358}{the} \markbox{25359}{above} \markbox{25360}{discussion,} \markbox{25361}{these} \markbox{25362}{two} \markbox{25363}{setups} \markbox{25364}{have} \markbox{25365}{the} \markbox{25366}{exact} \markbox{25367}{same} \markbox{25368}{clusters} \markbox{25369}{and} \markbox{25370}{thus} \markbox{25371}{the} \markbox{25372}{exact} \markbox{25373}{same} \markbox{25374}{edge} \markbox{25375}{components.}  \markbox{25376}{Hence} \markbox{25377}{we} \markbox{25378}{get} \markbox{25379}{the} \markbox{25380}{desired} \markbox{25381}{bijections} \markbox{25382}{(with} \markbox{25383}{their} \markbox{25384}{proximity} \markbox{25385}{constraints)} \markbox{25386}{by} \markbox{25387}{identifying} \markbox{25388}{the} \markbox{25389}{edge} \markbox{25390}{components} \markbox{25391}{as} \markbox{25392}{stable} \markbox{25393}{components---which,} \markbox{25394}{again,} \markbox{25395}{are} \markbox{25396}{all} \markbox{25397}{exactly} \markbox{25398}{the} \markbox{25399}{same---and} \markbox{25400}{taking} \markbox{25401}{the} \markbox{25402}{bijection} \markbox{25403}{between} \markbox{25404}{the} \markbox{25405}{complementary} \markbox{25406}{components} \markbox{25407}{to} \markbox{25408}{be} \markbox{25409}{the} \markbox{25410}{obvious} map.

In \markbox{25411}{other} \markbox{25412}{words,} \markbox{25413}{provided} \markbox{25414}{an} \markbox{25415}{explanation} \markbox{25416}{for} \markbox{25417}{how} \markbox{25418}{to} \markbox{25419}{iteratively} \markbox{25420}{combine} \markbox{25421}{a} \markbox{25422}{sequence} \markbox{25423}{of} \markbox{25424}{stable} \markbox{25425}{decompositions,} \markbox{25426}{we} \markbox{25427}{can} \markbox{25428}{apply} \markbox{25429}{this} \markbox{25430}{process} \markbox{25431}{to} \markbox{25432}{move} \markbox{25433}{from} \markbox{25434}{setup} \markbox{25435}{(1)} \markbox{25436}{above} \markbox{25437}{to} \markbox{25438}{setup} (6).

\medskip

\markbox{25439}{\textbf{\underline{Putting it all together}}}: \markbox{25440}{In} \markbox{25441}{the} \markbox{25442}{more} \markbox{25443}{general} \markbox{25444}{setting} \markbox{25445}{of} \markbox{25446}{the} \markbox{25447}{theorem,} \markbox{25448}{the} \markbox{25449}{above} \markbox{25450}{sequence} \markbox{25451}{only} \markbox{25452}{appears} \markbox{25453}{in} \markbox{25454}{the} \markbox{25455}{middle} \markbox{25456}{of} \markbox{25457}{a} \markbox{25458}{longer} \markbox{25459}{sequence} \markbox{25460}{we} \markbox{25461}{need} \markbox{25462}{to} \markbox{25463}{consider.}  \markbox{25464}{In} \markbox{25465}{particular,} \markbox{25466}{let} \markbox{m25467}{$\calY' - \calY = \{x_1, \dots, x_n\}$} \markbox{25468}{and} \markbox{m25469}{$\calY - \calY' = \{z_1, \dots, z_m\}$}, \markbox{25470}{where} \markbox{m25471}{$n,m < N$} \markbox{25472}{by} \markbox{25473}{assumption.}  \markbox{25474}{Set} \markbox{m25475}{$\calY_i = \calY \cup \{x_1, \dots, x_i\}$} \markbox{25476}{and} \markbox{m25477}{$\calY'_i = \calY' \cup \{z_1, \dots, z_i\}$}, \markbox{25478}{and} \markbox{25479}{let} \markbox{m25480}{$\calY_0 = \calY \cap \calY'$} \markbox{25481}{and} \markbox{m25482}{$\calY_{all} = \calY \cup \calY'$}.  \markbox{25483}{Then,} \markbox{25484}{by} \markbox{25485}{the} \markbox{25486}{assumptions} \markbox{25487}{in} \markbox{25488}{our} \markbox{25489}{setup,} \markbox{25490}{we} \markbox{25491}{have} \markbox{25492}{two} \markbox{25493}{sequences} \markbox{25494}{of} \markbox{25495}{pairwise} \markbox{25496}{admissible} \markbox{m25497}{$\epsilon$}-setups
$$(a,b;\calY) \to (a,b;\calY_1) \to \cdots \to (a,b;\calY_{all}) \to (a,b;\calY_{all} \cup \{a'\}) \to (a,b;\calY_{all} \cup \{a',b'\})$$
and
$$(a',b';\calY') \to \cdots \to (a',b'; \calY_n) \to (a',b';\calY_{all}) \to (a',b';\calY_{all} \cup \{a\}) \to (a',b';\calY_{all} \cup \{a,b\}),$$
which \markbox{25498}{we} \markbox{25499}{note} \markbox{25500}{are} \markbox{25501}{connected} \markbox{25502}{in} \markbox{25503}{the} \markbox{25504}{middle} \markbox{25505}{by} \markbox{25506}{the} \markbox{25507}{above} \markbox{25508}{discussion,} \markbox{25509}{where} \markbox{25510}{we} \markbox{25511}{need} \markbox{25512}{to} \markbox{25513}{switch} \markbox{25514}{the} \markbox{25515}{roles} \markbox{25516}{of} \markbox{25517}{both} \markbox{m25518}{$a,a'$} \markbox{25519}{and} \markbox{m25520}{$b,b'$}.  \markbox{25521}{In} \markbox{25522}{particular,} \markbox{25523}{the} \markbox{25524}{stable} \markbox{25525}{trees} \markbox{25526}{for} \markbox{25527}{the} \markbox{25528}{setups} \markbox{m25529}{$(a,b;\calY_{all} \cup \{a',b'\})$} \markbox{25530}{and} \markbox{m25531}{$(a',b';\calY_{all} \cup \{a,b\})$} \markbox{25532}{have} \markbox{25533}{identical} \markbox{25534}{edge} components.

By \markbox{25535}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable iteration}, \markbox{25536}{we} \markbox{25537}{get} \markbox{m25538}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m25539}{$L_{n+2}$}-compatible \markbox{25540}{stable} \markbox{25541}{decompositions} \markbox{25542}{for} \markbox{m25543}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{25544}{and} \markbox{m25545}{$(a,b;\calY_{all} \cup \{a',b'\})$}, \markbox{25546}{and} \markbox{m25547}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m25548}{$L_{m+2}$}-compatible \markbox{25549}{stable} \markbox{25550}{decompositions} \markbox{25551}{for} \markbox{m25552}{$(a',b';\calY)$} \markbox{25553}{and} \markbox{m25554}{$(a',b';\calY_{all} \cup \{a,b\})$}.  \markbox{25555}{Since} \markbox{m25556}{$(a,b;\calY_{all} \cup \{a',b'\})$} \markbox{25557}{and} \markbox{m25558}{$(a',b';\calY_{all} \cup \{a,b\})$} \markbox{25559}{determine} \markbox{25560}{identical} \markbox{25561}{edge} \markbox{25562}{components,} \markbox{25563}{we} \markbox{25564}{can} \markbox{25565}{use} \markbox{25566}{an} \markbox{25567}{identical} \markbox{25568}{argument} \markbox{25569}{to} \markbox{25570}{the} \markbox{25571}{proof} \markbox{25572}{of} \markbox{25573}{Proposition} \ref{prop:stable iteration, pair} \markbox{25574}{to} \markbox{25575}{induce} \markbox{25576}{refined} \markbox{m25577}{$\calY_0$}-stable \markbox{m25578}{$(L_n \cdot L_m)$}-compatible \markbox{25579}{stable} \markbox{25580}{decompositions} \markbox{25581}{for} \markbox{m25582}{$(a,b;\calY)$} \markbox{25583}{and} \markbox{m25584}{$(a',b';\calY)$}.  \markbox{25585}{We} \markbox{25586}{leave} \markbox{25587}{the} \markbox{25588}{details} \markbox{25589}{to} \markbox{25590}{the} \markbox{25591}{reader.}  \markbox{25592}{This} \markbox{25593}{completes} \markbox{25594}{the} \markbox{25595}{proof.} \qed
